> tapasvino dānaśīlāḥ kulīnāḥ satyavādinaḥ |  
> dharmapradhānā ṛjavaḥ putravanto dhanānvitāḥ ||  
> tryavarāḥ sākṣiṇo jñeyāḥ śrautasmārtakriyāparāḥ |  
> yathājāti yathāvarṇaṃ sarve sarveṣu vā smṛtāḥ ||

gautamaḥ [13.2–4]: 'bahavaḥ syur aninditāḥ svakarmasu prātyayikā rājñām | niṣprītyabhitāpāś cānyatarasmin | api śūdrāḥ' | **[106]** **'prātyayikā rājñām'** pratyayotpādakā rājñām | **'niṣprītyabhitāpāḥ'** maitraśāstravavarjitāḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [347–348] |

> prakhyātakulaśīlāś ca lobhamohavivarjitāḥ |  
> āptāḥ śiṣṭā vibuddhā ye teṣāṃ vākyam asaṃśayam ||  
> vibhāvyo vādinā yādṛk sadṛśair eva bhāvayet |  
> notkṛṣṭaṃ cāvakṛṣṭais tu sākṣibhir bhāvayet sadā ||

śaṅkhalikkhitau: 'atha sākṣiṇaḥ | śrotriyo guṇavān rūpavān māṇavakaḥ śīlavān kṣatriyas tathā, vaiśyaḥ śūdro vā dharmavāṃś ca yaḥ śīlopapannaḥ, karmavādair vidito na tv ekaḥ' |

vyāsaḥ |

> maṇimantrauṣadhibalāt pradattaṃ vā vidhānataḥ |  
> visaṃvaded divyam api na tu sākṣī guṇānvitaḥ ||

nāradaḥ [4.155] |

> śreṇīṣu śreṇipuruṣāḥ sveṣu vargeṣu vargiṇaḥ |  
> bahirvāsiṣu bāhyāḥ syuḥ striyaḥ strīṣu ca sākṣiṇaḥ ||

**[107]** kātyāyanaḥ [3.49–350] |

> liṅginaḥ śreṇipūgāś ca vaṇigjātās tathāpare |  
> samūhasthāś ca ye cānye vargās tān abravīd bhṛguḥ ||  
> dāsacāraṇamallānāṃ hastyaśvāyudhajīvinām |  
> pratyekaikasamūhānāṃ nāyakā vargiṇaḥ smṛtāḥ ||  
> teṣāṃ vādaḥ svavargeṣu vargiṇas teṣu sākṣiṇaḥ |

manu-kātyāyanau [ma. 8.68; kā. 351] |

> strīṇāṃ sākṣyaṃ striyaḥ kuryur dvijānāṃ dvijasattamāḥ |  
> śūdrāś ca santaḥ śūdrāṇāṃ martyānāṃ martyayonayaḥ ||

**iti bhaṭṭahṛdayadharātmaja-mahāsandhivigrahika-**

**bhattaśrīmallakṣmīdharaviracite kṛtyakapatarau vyavahārakāṇḍe sākṣiprakaraṇam**

**[108]**

## 16 asākṣiṇaḥ
**16 — athāsākṣiṇaḥ**

tatra nāradaḥ [4.157–158] |

> asākṣy api hi śāstreṣu dṛṣṭaḥ pañcavidho budhaiḥ |  
> vacanād doṣato bhedāt svayamuktir bhṛtāntaraḥ ||  
> śrotriyādyā vacanataḥ stenādyā doṣadarśanāt |  
> bhedād vipratipattiaḥ syād vivāde yatra sākṣiṇām ||  
> svyamuktir anirdiṣṭaḥ svayam evaitya yo vadet |  
> mṛtāntaro 'rthini prete mumūrṣuśrāvitād ṛte ||  
> śrotriyās tāpasā vṛddhā ye ca pravrajitā narāḥ |  
> asākṣiṇas te vacanān nātra hetur udāhṛtaḥ ||  
> stenāḥ sāhasikāś caṇḍāḥ kitavā pañcakās tathā |  
> asakṣiṇas te duṣṭatvāt teṣu satyaṃ na vidyate ||

manuḥ [8.64] |

> nārthasambandhino nāptā na sahāyā na vairiṇaḥ |  
> na dṛṣṭadoṣaḥ kartavyā na vyadhyārtā na dūṣitāḥ ||

**[109]** nāradaḥ [4.178–185, 156]

> dāsanaikṛtikāśraddhavṛddhastrībālavañcakāḥ |  
> mattonmattapramattārtakitavagrāmayājakāḥ ||  
> mahāpathikasāmudravaṇikpravrajitāturāḥ |  
> vyaṅgaikaśrotriyācārahīnaklībakuśīlavāḥ ||  
> nāstikavrātyadārāgnityāgino 'yājyayājakāḥ |  
> ekasthālīsahāyāridharajñātisanābhayaḥ ||  
> prāgdṛṣṭadoṣaśailūṣaviaṣajīvyāhituṇḍikāḥ |  
> garadāgnidakīnāśaśūdrīputropapātikāḥ ||

**[110]**  
> klānta [sāhasikāśrāntanirdhūtāntyāvasāyinaḥ] |  
> bhinnavṛttāsamāvṛttajalatailikamūlikāḥ ||  
> bhūtāviṣṭanṛpadviṣṭavarṣanakṣatrasūcakāḥ |  
> aghaśaṃsyātmavikretṛhīnāṅgabhagavṛttayaḥ ||  
> kunakhī śyāvadacchvitrimitradhrukcchaṭhaśauṇḍikāḥ |  
> aindrajālilubdhograśreṇīgaṇavirodhinaḥ ||  
> vadhakaś citrakṛcchraṅkhaḥ patitaḥ kūṭakārakaḥ |  
> kuhakaḥ pratyavasitas (?) taskaro rājapūruṣaḥ ||  
> manuṣyapaśumāṃsāsthimadhukṣīrāmbusarpiṣām |  
> vikretā brāhmaṇas tv eṣāṃ dvijo vārdhuṣikaś ca yaḥ ||

**[111]**  
> cyutaḥ svadharmāt kulikaḥ sūcako hīnasevakaḥ |  
> pitrā vivadamānaś ca bhedakṛc cety asākṣiṇaḥ ||  
> śreṇyādiṣu tu vargeṣu kaścid vai dveṣyatām iyāt |  
> tasya tebhyo na sākṣyaṃ syād dveṣṭāraḥ sarva eva te ||

**'naikṛtikaḥ'** vañcakaḥ | **'aśraddhaḥ'** śraddhārahitaḥ | **'mahāpathikaḥ'** dīrghādhvanikaḥ | **'kuśīlavao'** raṅgopajīvī | **'ekasthālī'** ekapākabhojī | **'aridharaḥ'** śrastradhārī | **'āhituṇḍikaḥ'** vyālagrāhī | **'upapātikaḥ'** pātakākrāntaḥ | **'sāhasikaḥ'** sahasāvicāritakārī | **'aśrāntaḥ'** ayogyakārī | **'nirdhūtaḥ'** grāmarājakulaśreṇyādibhir niḥsāritaḥ | **'bhinnavṛttaḥ'** svadharmānavasthitaḥ | **'mūlikaḥ'** tatra mūlaṃ vipralambhas tatkārī | **'śaṅkhaḥ'** balīvardanāṭanena bhikṣāṭanaśīlaḥ | **'pratyavasitaḥ'** pravrajyācyutaḥ | **'kulikaḥ'** paricchedakatvena viyuktaḥ |

manuḥ [8.65–67] |

> na sākṣī nṛpatiḥ kāryo na kārukakuśīlavau |  
> na śrotriyo na liṅgastho na saṅgebhyo nivartakaḥ ||  
> nādhyadhīno na vaktavyo na dasyur na vikarmakṛt |  
> na vṛddho na śiśur naiko nāntyo na vikalendriyaḥ ||

**[112]**  
> nārto na matto nonmatto na kṣuttṛṣṇopapīḍitaḥ |  
> na śramārto na kāmārto na kruddho nāpi taskaraḥ ||

**'ādhyadhīno'** bandhake ghṛtaḥ |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.70–71] |

> strīvṛddhabālakitavamattonmattābhiśastakāḥ |  
> raṅgāvatārapākhaṇḍikūṭakṛdvikalendriyāḥ ||  
> patitāptārthasaṃbandhisahāyariputaskarāḥ |  
> sāhase dṛṣṭadoṣāśca nirdoṣāś cety asākṣiṇaḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [5.39–40] |

> mātuḥ pitā pitṛvyaś ca bhāryāyā bhrātṛmātulau |  
> bhrātā sakhā ca jāmātā sarvavādeṣv asākṣiṇaḥ ||  
> parastrīpānasaktāś ca kitvāḥ sarvadūṣitāḥ |  
> unmattārtāḥ sāhasikā nāstikāś ca na sākṣiṇaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [362–364] |

> tadvṛttijīvino ye ca tatsevāhitakāriṇaḥ |  
> tadbandhusuhṛdo bhṛtyāḥ āptās te tu na sākṣiṇaḥ ||

**[113]** > mātṛṣvasṛsutāś caiva pitṛṣvasṛsutās tathā |  
> mātulasya sutāś caiva sodaryāsutamātulāḥ ||  
> ete sanābhayas tūktāḥ sākṣyaṃ teṣu na yojayet \

evaṃ pitṛmātṛsanābhayo boddhavyāḥ |

> kulyāḥ sambandhinaś caiva vivāhyo bhaginīpatiḥ ||  
> pitā bandhuḥ pitṛvyaś ca śvaśuro guravas tathā |  
> nagaragrāmadeśeṣu niyuktā ye padeṣu ca ||  
> vallabhāś ca pṛccheyur uktās te rājapūruṣāḥ |  
> na kruddhair nāpi saṃsṛṣṭair nāsīnair na rujānvitaiḥ ||  
> na nindyair nāpi saṃmūḍhaiḥ sākṣibhis tu vibhāvayet |  
> viruddhā varjitāḥ syuś cet sākṣyaṃ vargasya na kvacit ||

**[114]** athāsākṣiṇa ity adhikāre śaṅkhalikhitau: 'śulkagulmādhikṛto dūto veṣṭitaśirāḥ striyaś ca sarvāḥ gurukulavāsinaḥ parivrājakavānaprasthanirgranthaśaṅkhavyālagrāhiṇaḥ' | **'śulkādhikṛtaḥ'** śuklagrahaṇasthānādhikārī | **'gulmādhikṛtaḥ'** padātisamūho gulmas tadadhikṛtaḥ | **'gurukulavāsino'** brahmacāriṇaḥ | **'nirgranthaḥ'** kṣapaṇakaḥ |

nāradaḥ [4.160, 230, 161] |

> rājñā parigṛhīteṣu sākṣiṣv ekārthaniścaye |  
> vacanaṃ yatra bhidyeta te syur bhedād asākṣiṇaḥ ||  
> smṛtimatsākṣisāmyaṃ tu vivāde yatra dṛśyate |  
> sūkṣmatvāt sākṣidharmasya sākṣyaṃ vyāvartate tataḥ ||  
> anirdiṣṭas tu sākṣitve svayam evaitya yo vadet |  
> svayam uktaḥ sa śāstreṣu na ca sākṣitvam arhati ||

**smṛtimatsākṣisāmyam** iti | smṛtimattvād dviguṇena samāḥ santo yatra sākṣiṇo bhidyante tate te vacanabhedād asākṣiṇo na punar asmās te 'pi |

kātyāyanaḥ [404, 377] |

> yaḥ sākṣī naiva nirdiṣṭo nāhūto nāpi coditaḥ |  
> brūyān mithyeti tathyaṃ vā daṇḍyaḥ so 'pi narādhamaḥ ||

**[115]** > arthī yatra vipannaḥ syāt tatra sākṣī mṛtāntaraḥ |  
> pratyarthī vā mṛto yatra tarāpy evaṃ prakalpayet ||

nāradaḥ [4.162, 94–96] |

> yo 'rthaḥ śrāvayitavyaḥ syāt tasminn asati vā 'rthini |  
> kva tad vadatu sākṣitvam ity asākṣī mṛtāntaraḥ ||  
> santo 'pi na pramāṇaṃ syur mṛte dhanini sākṣiṇaḥ |  
> anyatra śrāvitaṃ yat syāt svayam āsannamṛtyunā ||  
> na hi pratyarthini prete pramāṇaṃ sākṣināṃ vacaḥ |  
> sākṣimat kāraṇaṃ tatra pramāṇaṃ syād viniścayaḥ ||  
> śrāvitenāntareṇāpi yas tv artho dharmasaṃhitaḥ |  
> mṛto 'pi tatra sākṣyaṃ syāt ṣaṭsu cānvāhitāgniṣu ||

**yo 'rthaḥ śrāvayitavya** ityāder ayam arthaḥ —yenārthinā sākṣīkṛtaḥ so 'rthaṃ yasya sākṣiṇo mṛtottare sa mṛtāntaranāmāsau na sākṣitvam arhati | yadi mumūrṣuṇā arthinā pitrā amukaṃ dravyam iyad etayā vṛdhyā amukakāle devadattāya dattam atrārthe 'mī sākṣiṇa ity evaṃ putraḥ śrāvito bhavet | tasya sādyādivivekābhāvāt | arthinā yo 'rthaḥ śrāvayitavyaḥ sākṣiṇām asminn arthe bhavantaḥ **[116]** sākṣiṇa iti | śrāvitād ṛte tatsādhyādiviśeṣaparīkṣābhāvān nārthaṃ śrāvayituṃ śakṣiṇāṃ śaknotīty ataḥ —**'kva tad vadatu sākṣitvam iti sākṣī mṛtāntaraḥ'** iti | yadā tu mumūrṣuṇā śrāvitās tadā mṛte 'py arthini bhavanty eva sākṣiṇa iti |

kātyāyanaḥ [360] |

> anyena hi kṛaḥ sākṣī naivānyas taṃ vivādayet |  
> tadabhāve viniryukto bāndhavo vā vivādayet ||  
> bhāvayet sākṣibhiḥ kāryaṃ mṛte tv arthini bāndhavaḥ |  
> kulādīnāṃ samakṣaṃ cel likhitaṃ bhāvayet sadā ||

**ity asākṣiṇaḥ |**

**117]**

## 17 sākṣipratyuddhāraḥ
atha sākṣipratyuddhāraḥ

tatra manu-nāradau [ma. 8.72; nā. 4.189] |

> sāhaseṣu tu sarveṣu steyasaṃgrahaṇeṣu ca |  
> vāgdaṇḍayoś ca pāruṣye na parīkṣeta sākṣiṇaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [366–367] |

> vyāghāteṣu nṛpājñāyāḥ saṅgrāme sāhaseṣu ca |  
> steyapāruṣyayoś caiva na parīkṣeta sākṣiṇaḥ ||  
> antarveśmani rātrau vā bahirgrāmāc ca yo bhavet |  
> eteṣv evābhiyoge tu parīkṣā nātra sākṣiṇām ||

manuḥ [8.69–70] |

> anubhāvī tu yaḥ kaścit kuryāt sākṣyaṃ vivādinām |  
> antarveśmany araṇye vā śarīrasyāpi cātyaye ||  
> striyā vā saṃbhave kāryaṃ bālena sthavireṇa vā |  
> śiṣyena bandhunā vāpi dāsena bhṛtakena vā ||

**[118]** anubhūtam anenety **anubhāvī** |

uśanāḥ |

> dāso 'ndho badhiraḥ kuṣṭhī strībālasthavirādayaḥ |  
> ete 'py anabhisaṃbandhāḥ sāhase sākṣiṇo matāḥ ||

nāradaḥ [4.188, 190, 191] |

> asākṣiṇo ye nirdiṣṭā dāsanaikṛtikādayaḥ |  
> kāryagauravam āsādya bhaveyus te 'pi sākṣiṇaḥ ||  
> teṣām api na bālaḥ syān naiko na strī na kūṭakṛt |  
> na bāndhavo na cārātir brūyus te sākṣyam anyathā ||  
> bālo 'jñānād asatyāt strī pāpābhyāsāc ca kūṭakṛt |  
> vikriyād bāndhavaḥ snehād vairaniryātanād ariḥ ||

manuḥ [8.77] |

> eko 'lubdhas tu sākṣī syāt bahvyaś śucyo 'pi na striyaḥ |   
> strībuddher asthiratvāt tu doṣaiś cānye 'pi ye vṛtāḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [365] |

> ṛṇādiṣu parīkṣeta sākṣiṇaḥ sthirakarmasu |  
> sāhasātyayike caiva parīkṣā kutracit smṛtā ||

**[119]** manuḥ [8.71] |

> bālavṛddhāturāṇāṃ ca sākṣyeṣu vadatāṃ mṛṣā |  
> jānīyād athirāṃ vācam utsiktamanasāṃ tathā ||

**iti sākṣipratyuddhāraḥ**

**[120]**

## 18 sākṣidūṣaṇam
atha sākṣidūṣaṇam

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ [5.21] |

> sākṣiṇo 'rthisamuddiṣṭān satsu doṣeṣu dūṣayet |  
> aduṣṭān dūṣayan vādī tatsamaṃ daṇḍam arhati ||

kātyāyanaḥ [278, 275] |

> nātathyena pramāṇaṃ tu doṣeṇaiva tu dūṣayet |  
> mithyābhiyoge daṇḍyaḥ syāt so 'rthād vāpi prahīyate ||  
> pramāṇasya hi ye doṣā vaktavyās te vivādinā |  
> gūḍhās tu prakaṭāḥ sabhyaiḥ kāle śāstrapradarśanāt ||

vivādināviditatvenānudbhāvitāḥ doṣāḥ śāstrapradarśanena prakaṭīkṛtya sabhyair vaktavyā ity arthaḥ |

bṛhaspati-kātyāyanau |

> lekhyadoṣāś tu ye kecit sākṣiṇāṃ caiva ye smṛtāḥ |  
> vādakāle tu vaktavyāḥ paścād uktāṃs tu dūṣayet ||

vyāsaḥ |

> sabhāsadāṃ prasiddhaṃ yal lokasiddham athāpi vā |  
> sākṣiṇāṃ dūṣaṇaṃ grāhyam asādhyaṃ doṣavarjanāt ||

**[121]**  
> anyais tu sākṣibhiḥ sādhye dūṣaṇe pūrvasākṣiṇām |  
> anavasthā bhaved doṣaḥ teṣām apy anyasaṃbhavāt ||

**'asādhyaṃ doṣavarjanāt'** — **'asādhyam'** sādhanānarham; **'doṣavarjanāt'** anavasthādidoṣarahitatvāt |

bṛhaspatiḥ [5.29] |

> lekhyaṃ vā sākṣiṇo vāpi vivāde yasya dūṣitāḥ |  
> tasya kāryaṃ na sidhyet tu yāvan tan na viśodhayet ||

tat lekhyaṃ sākṣiṇaś ca pramāṇam iti yāvat |

tathā [5.30] |

> sākṣibhir gaditaiḥ sabhyaiḥ prakrānte nirṇaye tu yat |  
> punar vivādaṃ kurute tasya rājā vicārayet ||

vyāsaḥ |

> sākṣidoṣāḥ prayoktavyāḥ saṃsadi prativādinā |  
> patre 'bhilikhitān sarvān vācyāḥ pratyuttaraṃ tu ye |

**[122]**  
> pratipattau na sākṣitvam arhanti tu kadācana |  
> ato 'nyathā bhāvanīyāḥ kriyayā prativādinā ||  
> abhāvayan damaṃ dāpyaḥ pratyarthī sākṣiṇaḥ sphuṭam |  
> bhāvitāḥ sākṣiṇo varjyāḥ sākṣidharmanirākṛtāḥ ||  
> jitaḥ savinayaṃ dāpyaḥ śāstradṛṣṭena karmaṇā |  
> yadi vādī nirākāṅkṣaḥ sākṣisabhyeṣv avasthitaḥ ||

**'pratyuttaram'** uttaram uttaraṃ prati, te doṣā vaktavyā ity arthaḥ | **'anyathā'** asampratipattau |

kātyāyanaḥ [407, 379] |

> yena kāryasya lobhena nirdiṣṭāḥ kūṭasākṣiṇaḥ |  
> gṛhītvā tasya sarvasvaṃ kuryān nirviṣayaṃ tataḥ ||  
> ukte 'rthe sākṣiṇo yas tu dūṣayet prāgdūṣitān |  
> na ca tatkāraṇaṃ brūyāt prāpnuyāt pūrvasāhasam ||

**[123]**

## 19 sākṣiśrāvaṇam
atha sākṣiśrāvaṇam

tatra kātyāyanaḥ [339] |

> na kālaharaṇaṃ kāryaṃ rājñā sākṣiprabhāṣaṇe |  
> mahān doṣo bhavet kālād dharmavyāvṛttilakṣaṇaḥ ||

nāradaḥ [4.198] |

> āhūya sākṣiṇaḥ pṛcchen niyamya śapathair bhṛśam |  
> samastān viditācārān vijñātārthān pṛthak pṛthak ||

viṣṇuḥ [8.19]: 'sākṣiṇaś cāhūya ādityodaye kṛtaśapathān pṛccheta' |

kātyāyanaḥ [388–390] |

> arthipratyarthisāṃnidhye sādhyārthasya ca saṃnidhau |  
> pratyakṣaṃ codayet sākṣyaṃ na parokṣaṃ kathaṃcana ||  
> arthasyopari vaktavyaṃ tayor api vinā kvacit |  
> catuṣpadeṣv ayaṃ dharmo dvipadasthāvareṣu ca ||

**124]**  
> taulyagaṇimameyānām abhāve 'pi hi vādyet |  
> kriyākāreṣu sarveṣu sākṣitvaṃ na tato 'nyathā ||

**'taulyam'** suvarṇādi | **'gaṇimam'** kapardakādi | **'meyam'** vrīhyādi | **'kriyākāreṣu'** vyavahāreṣu |

manuḥ [8.87, 79–86] |

> devabrāhmaṇasāṃnidhye sākṣyaṃ pṛcched ṛtaṃ dvijān |  
> udaṅmukhān prāṅmukhān vā pūrvāhṇe vā śuciḥ śucīn ||  
> sabhāntaḥ sākṣiṇaḥ sarvān arthipratyarthisaṃnidhau |  
> prāṅvivāko 'nuyuñjīta vidhinānena sāntvayan ||  
> yad vayor anayor vettha kārye 'smiṃś ceṣṭitaṃ mithaḥ |  
> tad brūta sarvaṃ satyena yuṣmākaṃ hy atra sākṣitā ||  
> satyaṃ sākṣye bruvan sākṣī lokān āpnoti puṣkalān |

**[125]**  
> iha cānuttamāṃ kīrtiṃ vāg eṣā brahmapūjitā ||  
> sākṣye 'nṛtaṃ vadan sākṣī pāśair badhyeta vāruṇaiḥ |  
> vivaśaḥ śatam ājātīs tasmāt sākṣye vaded ṛtam ||  
> satyena pūyate sākṣī dharmaḥ satyena vardhate |  
> tasmāt satyaṃ hi vaktavyaṃ sarvavarṇeṣu sākṣibhiḥ ||  
> ātmaiva hy ātmanaḥ sākṣī gatir ātmā tathātmanaḥ |  
> māvamaṃsthāḥ svam ātmānaṃ nṛṇāṃ sākṣitvam uttamam ||  
> manyante vai pāpakṛto na kaścit paśyatīti naḥ |  
> tāṃś ca devāḥ prapaśyanti svaś caivāntarapūruṣaḥ ||  
> dyaur bhūmir āpo hṛdayaṃ candrārkāgniyamānilāḥ |  
> rātriḥ saṃdhye ca dharmaś ca vṛttajñāḥ sarvadehinām ||

'sabhāntaḥ' sabhāmadhye | 'anuyuñjīta' pṛcchet | 'śatam ājātīḥ' śataṃ janmāni |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.73–74] |

> sākṣiṇaḥ śrāvayed vādī prativādisamīpagān |  
> ye pātakakṛtāṃ lokā mahāpātakināṃ tathā ||  
> agnidānāṃ ca ye lokā ye ca strībālaghātinām |  
> tān sarvān samavāpnoti yaḥ sākṣyam anṛtaṃ vadet ||

**126]** bṛhaspatiḥ |

> satyapraśaṃsāvacanair anṛtasyāpavarjanaiḥ |  
> sabhyaiḥ saṃbodhanīyās tu dharmaśāstrapravedibhiḥ ||  
> ā janmanaś cā maraṇāt sukṛtaṃ yad upārjitam |  
> tat sarvaṃ nāśam āyāti anṛtasyābhiśaṃsanāt ||  
> kūṭasabhyaḥ kūṭasākṣī brahmahā ca samāḥ smṛtāḥ |  
> bhrūṇahā vittahā caiṣāṃ nādhikaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ ||  
> evaṃ viditvā tat sākṣī yathā bhūtaṃ vadet tataḥ |  
> teneha kīrtim āpnoti paratra ca śubhāṃ gatim ||

sākṣiśrāvaṇe viṣṇu-nāradau [vi. 8.36; nā. 4.211] |

> aśvamedhasahasraṃ ca satyaṃ ca tulayā dhṛtam |  
> aśvamedhasahasrād dhi satyam eva viśiṣyate ||

nāradaḥ [4.200–202, 206, 212–213, 226–228] |

> purāṇair dharmavacanaiḥ satyamāhātmyadarśanaiḥ |  
> anṛtasyāpavādaiś ca bhṛśam uttrāsayed api ||

**[127]**  
> nagarapratiruddhaḥ san bahir dvāre bubhukṣitaḥ |  
> amitrān bhūyaśaḥ paśyed yaḥ sākṣyam anṛtaṃ vadet ||  
> yāṃ rātrim adhivinnā strī yāṃ caivākṣaparājitaḥ |  
> yāṃ ca bhārābhitaptāṅgo durvivaktā sa tāṃ vaset ||  
> sākṣī sākṣyasamuddeśe gokarṇaśithilaṃ caran |  
> sahasraṃ vāruṇāt pāśān ātmani pratimuñcati ||  
> tasya varṣaśate pūrṇe pāśa ekaḥ pramucyate |  
> evaṃ sa bandhanāt tasmān mucyate niyataṃ kramāt ||  
> ekam evādvitīyaṃ yat prāhuḥ pāvanam ātmanaḥ |  
> satyaṃ svargasya sopānaṃ pārāvārasya naur iva ||  
> varaṃ kūpaśatād vāpī varaṃ vāpīsatāt kratuḥ |  
> varaṃ kratuśatāt putraḥ satyaṃ putraśatād varam ||  
> bhūr dhārayati satyena satyenodeti bhāskaraḥ |  
> satyena vayuḥ pavate satyenāpaḥ sravanti ca ||

**[128]**  
> satyam eva paraṃ dhāma satyam eva paraṃ tapaḥ |  
> satyam eva paro dharmo lokānām iti naḥ śrutam ||  
> satyaṃ devāḥ samāsena manuṣyās tv anṛtaṃ smṛtam |  
> ihaiva tasya devatvaṃ yasya satye sthitā matiḥ ||  
> nāsti satyāt paro dharmo nānṛtāt pātakaṃ param |  
> sākṣidharme viśeṣeṇa satyam eva vadet tataḥ ||  
> purāṇānumatau cātra dvau ślokau samudāhṛtau |  
> yau śrutvā satyam eveha sadā vācyaṃ narair budhaiḥ ||  
> yaḥ parārthe 'paharati svāṃ vācaṃ puruṣādhamaḥ |  
> ātmārthe kiṃ na kuryāt sa pāpaṃ narakanirbhayaḥ ||  
> arthā vai vāci niyatā vāṅmulā vāgviniḥsṛtāḥ |  
> yas tu tāṃ steyayed vācaṃ sa sarvasteyakṛn naraḥ ||

**'gokarṇaśithilaṃ caran'** gokarṇavac chithilaṃ vyavaharan dṛḍham abruvann ity arthaḥ |

**[129]** **baudhāyanaḥ** |

> trīn eva ca pitṝn hanti trīn eva ca pitāmahān |  
> saptajātān ajātāṃś ca sākṣī sākṣyaṃ mṛṣā bruvan ||  
> pañca paśvanṛte hanti daśa hanti gavānṛte |  
> śatam aśvānṛte hanti sahasraṃ puruṣānṛte ||  
> sarvaṃ bhūmyanṛte hanti sākṣī sākṣyaṃ mṛṣā bruvan ||

**iti śakṣiśrāvaṇam**

**[130]**

## 20 sākṣiśapathaḥ
atha sākṣiśapathaḥ

tatra gautamaḥ: 'śapathenaike satyakarma | tad devarājabrāhmaṇasaṃsadi syāt abrāhmaṇānām' |

**'satyakarma'** satye vyavasthāpanam |

śaṅkhalikhitau: 'sākṣiṇaḥ suvarṇarajataratnagodhānyasūryāgnigajaskandhāśvapṛṣṭarathopastha-śastrādibhis tathā putrapautrair yathāvarṇaṃ parigrahaviśeṣataḥ syād devabrāhmaṇasvāminām agrataḥ' |

**suvarṇā**disparśanena, **sūryā**didarśaṇena, śāpayed iti śeṣaḥ | tathā **putrapautrair** iti | putrapautraśiraḥsparśanena svalpe 'rthe śāpayed ity arthaḥ | **yathāvarṇam** iti | yasya varṇasya yaddravyasparśanena śapathā āmnātaḥ, smṛtyantare sa tenaiva kārayitavya ity arthaḥ |

**[131]** nāradaḥ [4.199] |

> satyena śrāvayed vipraṃ kṣatriyaṃ vāhanāyudhaiḥ |  
> gobījakāñcanair vaiśyaṃ śūdraṃ sarvais tu pātakaiḥ ||

**satyena śrāvayet vipram** ity apakṛṣṭabrāhmaṇaviṣayam, na brāhmaṇamātraviṣayam | tasya gautamena śapathaniṣedhāt | **'śrāvayet'** śāpayed ity arthaḥ |

manur nāradaś ca ṣaṣṭhe |

> brūhīti brāhmaṇaṃ pṛcchet satyaṃ brūhīti pārthivam |  
> gobījakāñcanair vaiśyaṃ śūdram ebhis tu pātakaiḥ ||  
> brahmaghno ye smṛtā lokā ye ca strībālaghātinām |  
> mitradruhaḥ kṛtaghnasya te te syur bruvato mṛṣā ||  
> janmaprabhṛti yat kiṃcit puṇyaṃ bhadra tvayā kṛtam |  
> tat te sarvaṃ śuno gacched yadi brūyās tvam anyathā ||  
> eko 'ham asmīty ātmānaṃ yas tvaṃ kalyāṇa manyase |  
> nityaṃ sthitas te hṛdy eṣa puṇyapāpekṣitā muniḥ ||

**[132]**  
> yamo vaivasvato devo yas tavaiṣa hṛdi sthitaḥ |  
> tena ced avivādas te mā gaṅgāṃ mā kurūn gamaḥ ||  
> nagno muṇḍaḥ kapālena bhikṣārthī kṣutpipāsitaḥ |  
> kruddhaḥ śatrugṛhaṃ gacched yaḥ sākṣyam anṛtaṃ vadet ||  
> avākśirās tamasy andhe kilbiṣī narakaṃ vrajet |  
> yaḥ praśnaṃ vitathaṃ brūyāt pṛṣṭaḥ san dharmaniścaye ||  
> andho matsyān ivāśnāti nirapekṣaḥ sakaṇṭakān |  
> yo bhāṣate 'rthavaikalyam apratyakṣaṃ sabhāṃ gataḥ ||  
> yasya vidvān hi vadataḥ kṣetrajño nābhiśaṅkate |  
> tasmān na devāḥ śreyāṃsaṃ loke 'nyaṃ puruṣaṃ viduḥ ||

manu-nāradau |

> yāvato bāndhavān yasmin hanti sākṣye 'nṛtaṃ vadan |  
> tāvataḥ saṃkhyayā tasmiñ chṛṇu saumyānupūrvaśaḥ ||

**[133]**  
> pañca paśvanṛte hanti daśa hanti gavānṛte |  
> śatam aśvānṛte hanti sahasraṃ puruṣānṛte ||  
> hanti jātān ajātāṃś ca hiraṇyārthe 'nṛtaṃ vadan |  
> sarvaṃ bhūmyanṛte hanti mā sma bhūmyanṛtaṃ vadīḥ ||

manuḥ [8.100–101] |

> apsu bhūmivad ity āhuḥ strīṇāṃ bhoge ca maithune |  
> abjeṣu caiva ratneṣu sarveṣv aśmamayeṣu ca ||  
> paśuvat kṣaudraghṛtayor yāneṣu ca tathāśvavat |  
> govad rajatavastreṣu dhānye brahmaṇi caiva hi ||  
> etān doṣān avekṣasva sarvān anṛtabhāṣaṇe |  
> yathāśrutaṃ yathādṛṣṭaṃ satyam evāñjasā vada ||

**'abjeṣu ratneṣu'** muktāpravālādiṣu (?) | **'brahmaṇi'** vede |

nāradaḥ [4.216–224] |

> satyaṃ brūhy anṛtaṃ tyaktvā satyena svargam eṣyasi |  
> uktvānṛtaṃ mahāghoraṃ narakaṃ pratipatsyase ||

**[134]**  
> narakeṣu ca te śaśvaj jihvām utkṛtya dāruṇāḥ |  
> asibhiḥ śātayiṣyanti balino yamakiṅkarāḥ ||  
> śanair bhetsyanti cākramya krośantam aparāyaṇam |  
> avākcchirasam utkṣipya kṣepsyanty agnau hradeṣu ca ||  
> anubhūya suduḥkhāṃs tāṃś ciraṃ narakavedanāḥ |  
> iha yāsyasy abhavyāsu gṛdhrakākādiyoniṣu ||  
> jñātvaitān anṛte doṣān tathā satyeṣu sadguṇān |  
> satyaṃ vadoddharātmānaṃ nātmānaṃ pātaya svayam ||  
> na bāndhavā na suhṛdo na dhanāni mahānty api |  
> alaṃ dhārayituṃ sarve tamasy ugre nimajjataḥ ||  
> pitaras tv avalambante tvayi sākṣitvam āgate |  
> tārayiṣyati kiṃ vāsmān kiṃ vāsmān pātayiṣyati ||  
> satyam ātmā manuṣyasya satye sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam |  
> sarvathaivātmanātmānaṃ śreyasy eva niyojaya ||

**[135]**  
> yāṃ rātrim ajaniṣṭhās tvaṃ yāṃ ca rātriṃ mariṣyasi |  
> vṛthā tadantaraṃ te syāt sākṣyaṃ ced anyathā vadeḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.75] |

> sukṛtaṃ yat tvayā kiṃcij janmāntaraśtaiḥ kṛtam |  
> tat sarvaṃ tasya jānīhi yaṃ parājayase mṛṣā ||

manuḥ [8.102] |

> gorakṣakān vāṇijakāṃs tathā kārukuśīlavān |  
> preṣyān vārdhuṣikāṃś caiva viprān śūdravad ācaret ||  
> ye vyapetāḥ svakarmabhyaḥ parapiṇḍopajīvinaḥ |  
> dvijatvam abhikāṅkṣanti tāṃś ca śūdravad ācaret ||

ete brāhmaṇā api santaḥ sākṣye śūdravad eva śapathaṃ kārayitavyā ity arthaḥ |

**iti sākṣiśapathaḥ**

**[136]**

## 21 sakṣyoktavidhiḥ
atha sakṣyoktavidhiḥ

tatra kātyāyanaḥ [387, 391] |

> sabhāntasthais tu vaktavyaṃ sākṣyaṃ nānyatra sākṣibhiḥ |  
> sarvasākṣyeṣv ayaṃ dharmo 'nyatra syāt sthāvareṣu ca ||  
> vadhe ca prāṇināṃ sākṣyaṃ vādayec chivasaṃnidhau |  
> tadabhāve tu cihnasya nānyatraivaṃ pravādayet ||  
> anudvignena cittena dṛṣṭaṃ samyag yadā tu yat |  
> pratyakṣaṃ tat smṛtaṃ kāryaṃ sākṣī sākṣyaṃ tu tad vadet ||

**'tadabhāve'** śivābhāve | **'cihnasya'** asthikeśādeḥ saṃnidhāv ity arthaḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ [5.42] |

> vihāyopānaduṣṇīṣaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ pāṇim uddharet |  
> hiraṇyaṃ gośakṛddarbhān samādāya ṛtaṃ vahet ||

gautamaḥ [13.6]: 'nāsamavetā apṛṣṭāḥ prabrūyuḥ' | **'asamavetāḥ'** amilitāḥ |

**[137]** kātyāyanaḥ [394–395] |

> samavetais tu yad dṛṣṭaṃ vaktavyaṃ tais tathaiva tat |  
> vibhinnair naikakārthaṃ ca vaktavyaṃ tat pṛthak pṛthak ||  
> bhinnakāle tu yat kāryaṃ vijñātaṃ tatra sākṣibhiḥ |  
> ekaikaṃ vādeyet tatra bhinnakālaṃ tu tad bhṛguḥ ||  
> nāpṛṣṭair aniyuktair vā samaṃ satyaṃ prayatnataḥ |  
> vaktavyaṃ sākṣibhiḥ sākṣyaṃ vivādasthānam āgataiḥ ||

**naikakāryam** iti | anekakāryam ity arthaḥ | **'aniyuktaiḥ'** sākṣitvena anupanyastaiḥ |

baudhāyanaḥ [1.20.29]: 'lokāḥ pratigrahārthaṃ yathādṛṣṭaṃ yathāśrutaṃ sākṣyaṃ brūyuḥ' |

manuḥ [8.74] |

> tatra satyaṃ bruvan sākṣī dharmārthābhyāṃ na hīyate |

kātyāyanaḥ [393] |

> svabhāvoktaṃ vacas teṣāṃ grāhyaṃ yad doṣavarjitam |  
> ukte tu sākṣiṇo rājñā praṣṭavyā na punaḥ punaḥ ||

**iti sākṣivādavidhiḥ**

**[138]**

## 22 sākṣiparīkṣā
atha sākṣiparīkṣā

kātyāyanaḥ [340, 409] |

> upasthitān parīkṣeta sākṣiṇo nṛpatiḥ svayam |  
> sākṣibhir bhāṣitaṃ vākyaṃ saha sabhyaiḥ parīkṣayet ||  
> yadā śuddhā kriyā pālyā tadā tadvākyaśodhanam |  
> śuddhārthavākyād yaḥ śuddhaḥ sa śuddhārtho 'nyathā na tu ||

**'kriyā'** atra sākṣirūpaṃ pramāṇam |

bṛhaspatiḥ [5.43] |

> upasthitāḥ parīkṣyāḥ syuḥ svaravarṇeṅgitādibhiḥ |

**[139] **

**tatra kūṭasākṣiṇaḥ**

śaṅkhalikhitau: 'mantribhiḥ śāstrasāmarthyād duṣṭalakṣaṇaṃ grāhyam | tiryak prekṣate, samantād evāvalokayati, akasmāt mūtrapurīṣaṃ visṛjati, deśād deśaṃ gacchati, pāṇinā pāṇiṃ pīḍayati, nakhān nikṛntati, mukham asya vivarṇatām eti, prasvidyati cāsya lalāṭam, cakṣur vācaṃ na pratipūjayati, akasmād dadāti, praśaṃsati, punaḥ punaḥ anyam apanudati, bahir nirīkṣati, śāstraṃ paraāmṛśati, [śokam upavarṇayati], bhūmiṃ vilikhati, śiraḥ prakampayati, oṣṭhau nirbhujati, sṛkkiṇī parileḍhi, avismitaḥ karmasu mahatsu bhruvau saṃharati, hasati, tūṣṇīṃ dhyāyati, pūrvāparaviruddhaṃ vyāharati, evamādi duṣṭalakṣaṇam | kruddhasya ca svāmino 'nyatra prakṛtiśīlāt | tatra rājamūlā vyavahārāḥ' |

> kruddhasya ceti krodhāviṣṭasyāpi rājño mantribhir etāny eva cihnāni gṛhītavyāni | **'anyatra prakṛtiśīlāt'** svabhāvata eva ya evaṃvidhaḥ tadvyatirekeṇaitāni duṣṭasya lakṣaṇāni | rājakrodhāvadhāraṇe prayojanam āha – **'rājamūlā vyavahārāḥ'** | yat iti śeṣaḥ | 

**[140]**

nāradaḥ [4: 193–198] |

> yas tv ātmadoṣaduṣṭatvād asvastha iva lakṣyate |  
> sthānāt sthānāntaraṃ gacched ekaikaṃ cānudhāvati ||  
> kāsaty akasmāc ca bhṛśam ābhīkṣṇaṃ niśvasaty api |  
> vilikhaty avaniṃ padbhyāṃ bāhū vāsaś ca dhūnayet ||  
> bhidyate mukhavarṇo 'sya lalāṭaṃ svidyate yathā |  
> śoṣam āgacchataś cauṣṭhau ūrdhvaṃ tiryak ca vīkṣate ||  
> tvaramāṇa ivā[viddham apṛṣṭo] bahu bhāṣate |  
> kūṭasākṣī sa vijñeyas taṃ pāpaṃ vinayed bhṛśam ||  
> śrāvayitvā tathānyebhyaḥ sākṣitvaṃ yo 'panihnute |  
> sa vineyo bhṛśataraṃ kūṭasākṣyadhiko hi saḥ ||

**'āviddham'** ākulam |

**[141]**

## 23 sākṣidaṇḍah
atha sākṣidaṇḍah

tatra kātyāyanaḥ [406] |

> uktvānyathā bruvāṇāś ca daṇḍyāḥ syur vākcchalānvitāḥ ||

manuḥ [8.118–123] |

> lobhān mohād bhayān maitrāt kāmāt krodhāt tathaiva ca |  
> ajñānād bālabhāvāc ca sākṣyaṃ vitatham ucyate ||  
> eṣām anyatamaḥ sthāne yaḥ sākṣyam anṛtaṃ vadet |  
> tasya daṇḍaviśeṣāṃs tu pravakṣyāmy anupūrvaśaḥ ||  
> lobhāt sahasraṃ daṇḍas tu mohāt pūrvaṃ tu sāhasam |  
> bhayād dvau madhyamau daṇḍyau maityāt pūrvacaturguṇam ||  
> kāmād daśaguṇaṃ proktaṃ krodhāt tu triguṇaṃ param |  
> ajñānāt dve śate pūrṇe bāliśyāc chatam eva tu ||  
> etān āhuḥ kūṭasākṣye prokto daṇḍo manīṣibhiḥ |  
> dharmasyāvyabhicārārtham adharmaniyamāya ca ||

**[142]**  
> kūṭasākṣyaṃ tu kurvāṇāṃs trīn varṇān dhārmiko nṛpaḥ |  
> pravāsayed daṇḍayitvā brāhmaṇāṃs tu vivāsayet ||

**'sahasram'** paṇānām iti śeṣaḥ | **'mohāt'** vaicitryāt, **'pūrvasāhasaḥ'** sārdhaṃ paṇaśatadvayam | **'dvau madhyamau'** sāhasāv ity arthaḥ | paṇasahasram ity uktaṃ bhavati | pūrvasāhasacaturguṇaḥ paṇasahasram ity uktaṃ bhavati | **'triguṇaṃ param'** pūrvāpekṣayā paro madhyamasāhasas tasmiṃs triguṇe pañcadaśaśatāni saṃpadyante | **'ajñānāt'** vyavahārakāla eva viparītajñānāt | **'bāliśyam'** atra prāptayauvanamātram, na bālyam, bālasya sakṣyaniṣedhāt | **'vivāsayet'** svadeśān niḥsārayet |

viṣṇuḥ [5.179]: 'kūṭasākṣiṇāṃ sarvasvahāraḥ [kāryaḥ]' |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.81–82] |

> pṛthak pṛthak daṇḍanīyāḥ kūṭakṛt sākṣiṇas tathā |  
> vivādāt dviguṇaṃ daṇḍaṃ vivāsyo brāhmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
> yaḥ sākṣye śrāvite 'nyebhyo nihnute tat tamovṛtaḥ |  
> sa dāpyo 'ṣṭaguṇaṃ daṇḍaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ tu vivāsayet ||

**[143]** manu-nāradau |

> yasya dṛśyeta saptāhād uktavākyasya sākṣiṇaḥ |  
> rogo 'gnijñātimaraṇam ṛṇaṃ dāpyo damaṃ ca saḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.76] |

> abruvan hi naraḥ sākṣyam ṛṇaṃ sadaśabandhakam |  
> rājñā sarvaṃ pradāpyaḥ ṣāṭcatvāriṃśattame 'hani ||

**'sadaśabandhakam'** daśamāṃśasahitam |

manuḥ [8.103] |

> tripakṣād abruvan sākṣyam ṛṇādiṣu naro 'gadaḥ |  
> tad ṛṇaṃ pāpnuyāt sarvaṃ daśabandhaṃ tu sarvaśaḥ ||

viṣṇuḥ [8.37] |

> pārayanto 'pi ye sākṣye tūṣṇīṃ bhūtā upāsate |  
> te kūṭasākṣiṇāṃ pāpais tulyā daṇḍena caiva hi ||

**[144]** kātyāyanaḥ [405] |

> sākṣī sākṣyaṃ na ced brūyāt samadaṇḍaṃ vahed ṛṇam | \
> ato 'nyeṣu vivādeṣu triśataṃ daṇḍamarhati ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [5.45, 47] |

> āhūto (?) yas tu nāgacchet sākṣī rāgavivarjitaḥ |  
> ṛṇaṃ damaṃ ca dāpyaḥ syāt tripakṣāt paratas tu saḥ ||  
> apṛṣṭāḥ satyavacane praśṇasyākathane tathā |  
> sākṣiṇaḥ saṃniroddhavyā garhyā daṇḍyāś ca dharmataḥ ||

guatamaḥ [13.5]: 'brāhmaṇas tv abrāhmaṇavacanād anavarodhyo 'nibaddhaś cet' |

**'aniruddhaḥ'** patrake 'anavaropitaḥ |

**[145]** kātyāyanaḥ [342] |

> samyak kriyāparijñāne deyaḥ kālas tu sākṣiṇām |  
> saṃdigdhaṃ yatra sākṣyaṃ tu sadyaḥpṛṣṭān vivādayet ||

**'samyak kriyāparijñāne'** samyak kāryajñānārtham |

manuḥ [8.75] |

> sākṣī dṛṣṭaśrutād anyad vibruvann āryasaṃsadi |  
> avāṅ narakam āpnoti pretya svargāc ca hīyate ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

> avīci narake kalpaṃ vaseyuḥ kūṭasākṣiṇaḥ |

gautamaḥ [13.7–8]: avacane doṣiṇaḥ syuḥ | svargaḥ satyavacane, viparyaye narakaḥ" |

[**146]**

## 24 satyāpavādaḥ
**24 — satyāpavādaḥ**

tatra vasiṣṭhaḥ [viṣṇuḥ 8.14–15]: 'sākṣiṇaḥ satyena pūyante | varṇināṃ yatra vadhas tatrānṛtena' |

manuḥ [8.104, 103] |

> śūdraviṭkṣatraviprāṇāṃ yatrartoktau bhaved vadhaḥ |  
> tatra vaktavyam anṛtaṃ tad dhi satyād viśiṣyate ||  
> tad vadan dharmato 'rtheṣu jānann apy anyathā naraḥ |  
> na svargāc cyavate lokād daivīṃ vācaṃ vadanti tām ||

'ṛtoktau' satyavacane |

gautamaḥ [13.24, 25]: 'nānṛtavacane doṣo jīvanaṃ cet tadadhīnam | na tu pāpīyaso jīvanam' |

**'pāpīyasaḥ'** stenādeḥ yatrānṛtavacanena jīvanaṃ saṃpadyate tatrānṛtaṃ na vaktavyam |

**[147]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.83] |

> varṇināṃ hi vadho yatra tatra sakṣy anṛtaṃ vadet |  
> tatpāvanāya nirvāpyaś caruḥ sārasvato dvijaiḥ ||

viṣṇuḥ [8.1617]: 'tatpāvanāya kūṣmāṇḍībhiḥ [dvijo 'gniṃ] juhuyāt | śūdraś caikāhṇikaṃ godaśakasya grāsaṃ dadyāt' |

manuḥ [8.105–106] |

> vāgdaivatyaiś ca carubhir yajeraṃs te sarasvatīm |  
> anṛtasyainasas tasya kurvāṇāo niṣkṛtiṃ parām ||  
> kūṣmāṇḍair vāpi juhuyād ghṛtam agnau yathāvidhi |  
> ud ity ṛcā ca vāruṇyā tṛcenābdaivatena vā ||

**[148]**

## 25 sākṣibalatvam
atha sākṣibalatvam

tatra manuḥ [8.73] |

> bahutvaṃ parigṛhṇīyāt sākṣidvaidhe narādhipaḥ |  
> sameṣu ca guṇotkṛṣṭān guṇidvaidhe dvijottamān ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [5.46] |

> sākṣidvaidhe prabhūtāḥ syur grāhyāḥ sāmye guṇānvitāḥ |  
> guṇidvaidhe kriyāyuktās tatsāmye smṛtimattarāḥ ||

nāradaḥ [4.229] |

> sākṣivipratipattau tu pramāṇaṃ bahavo yataḥ |  
> tatsāmye guṇino grāhyās tatsāmye smṛtimattarāḥ ||

**[149]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.78] |

> dvaidhe bahūnāṃ vacanaṃ sameṣu guṇināṃ tathā |  
> guṇidvaidhe tu vacanaṃ grāhyaṃ ye guṇavattarāḥ ||

tathā [2.80] |

> ukte 'pi sākṣibhiḥ sākṣye yady anye guṇavattarāḥ |  
> dviguṇā vānyathā brūyuḥ kūṭāḥ syuḥ pūrvasākṣiṇaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [408] |

> yatra vai bhāvitaṃ kāryaṃ sākṣibhir vādinā bhavet |  
> prativādī yadā tatra bhāvayet kāryam anyathā ||  
> bahubhiś ca kulīnair vā kūṭāḥ syuḥ pūrvasākṣiṇaḥ |

**[150]**

## 26 sākṣinigadaḥ
atha sākṣinigadaḥ

tatra vyāsaḥ |

> kālākṛtivayodravyadeśajātipramāṇataḥ |  
> anyūnaṃ cen nigaditaṃ siddhaṃ sādhyaṃ vinirdiśet ||

viṣṇu-yājñavalkyau |

> yasyocuḥ sākṣiṇaḥ satyāṃ pratijñāṃ sa jayī bhavet |  
> anyathāvādino yasya dhruvas tasya parājayaḥ ||

**[151]**

### anigadaḥ
**athānigadaḥ**

[tatra] nāradaḥ [4.232–234] |

> nirdiṣṭeṣv arthajāteṣu sākṣī cet sākṣyam āgataḥ |  
> na brūyād akṣarasamaṃ na tan nigaditaṃ bhavet ||  
> deśakālavayodravyapramāṇākṛtijātiṣu |  
> tatra vipratipattiḥ syāt sākṣyaṃ tad api kutsitam ||  
> nyūnam abhyadhikaṃ cārthaṃ prabrūyur yatra sākṣiṇaḥ |  
> tad apy anuktaṃ vijñeyam eṣa sākṣividhiḥ smṛtaḥ ||

**[152]**

## 27 likhitam
atha likhitam

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

> sākṣiṇām eṣa nirdiṣṭaḥ saṃkhyālakṣaṇaniścayaḥ |  
> likhitasyādhunā vacmi vidhānam anupūrvaśaḥ ||  
> ṣāṇmāsike 'pi samaye bhrāntiḥ saṃjāyate yataḥ |  
> dhātrākṣarāṇi sṛṣṭāni patrārūḍhāny ataḥ purā ||  
> rājalekhyaṃ sthānakṛtaṃ svahastalikhitaṃ tathā |  
> lekhyaṃ tu trividhaṃ proktaṃ bhinnaṃ tad bahudhā punaḥ ||  
> bhāgadānakrayādhānasaṃviddāsaṛṇādibhiḥ |  
> saptadhā laukikaṃ lekhyaṃ trividhaṃ rājaśāsanam ||

marīciḥ |

> sthāvare vikrayādhāne vibhāge dāna eva ca |  
> likhitenāpnuyāt siddhim avisaṃvādam eva ca ||  
> sidhyate vāciko 'py ādhiḥ sthāvare ca daśābdikaḥ |  
> pratigrahe ca krīte ca nālekhyā sidhyati kriyā ||

**[153]** **sthāvara** iti | kṣetrādiviṣaye vikrayādīnāṃ lekhyaṃ vinā siddhir na bhavatīty arthaḥ | **sidhyate vāciko 'pītyāḍi** | sthāvareṣu viṣaye ādhir daśavarṣaparyantam upabhuktaḥ sa tathā vāciko 'pi lekhyaṃ vināpi sidhyatīty arthaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [257, 301] |

> sīmāvivāde nirvṛtte sīmāpatraṃ vidhīyate |

nāradaḥ [4.135] |

> lekhyaṃ tu dvividhaṃ jñeyaṃ svahastānyakṛtaṃ tathā |  
> asākṣimat sākṣimac ca siddhir deśasthites tayoḥ ||

**'tayoḥ'** sasākṣikāsākṣikayor deśācārādyavasthitir ity arthaḥ |

viṣṇuḥ [7.1–3]: 'atha lekhyaṃ [tri]vidham | rājasākṣikaṃ sasākṣikam asākṣikaṃ ca' |

rājādhikaraṇe tanniyuktakāyasthakṛtaṃ tadadhyakṣakaracihnitaṃ rājasākṣikam |

kātyāyanaḥ [258] |

> rājñaḥ svahastasaṃyuktaṃ svamudrācihnitaṃ tathā |  
> rājakīyaṃ smṛtaṃ lekhyaṃ sarveṣv artheṣu sākṣimat ||

**[154]** viṣṇuḥ [7.4–5]: 'yatra kvacana yena kenacil likhitaṃ sākṣibhiḥ svahastacihnitaṃ sasākṣikam | svahastalikhitam asākṣikam' |

bṛhaspatiḥ |

> bhrātaraḥ saṃvibhaktā ye svarucyā tu parasparam |  
> vibhāgapatraṃ kurvanti bhāgalekhyaṃ tad ucyate ||  
> bhūmiṃ datvā tu yaḥ patraṃ kuryāc candrārkakālikam |  
> anācchedyam anāhāryaṃ dānalekhyaṃ tu tad viduḥ ||  
> gṛhakṣetrādikaṃ krītvā tulyamūlyākṣarānvitam |  
> patraṃ kārayate yas tu krayalekhyaṃ tad ucyate ||  
> jaṅgamaṃ sthāvaraṃ bandhaṃ datvā lekhyaṃ karoti yaḥ |  
> gopyabhogyakriyāyuktam ādhilekhyaṃ tu tat smṛtam ||  
> grāmo deśaś ca yaḥ kuryān mataṃ lekhyaṃ parasparam |  
> rājāvirodhidharmārthe saṃdhipatraṃ vadanti tat ||  
> vastrānnahīnaḥ kāntāre likhitaṃ kurute tu yaḥ |  
> karmāṇi tu kariṣyāmi dāsapatraṃ tad iṣyate ||  
> dhanaṃ vṛddhyā gṛhītvā tu svayaṃ kuryāc ca kārayet |  
> ujjāmapatraṃ tat proktam ṛṇalekhyaṃ manīṣibhiḥ ||

**[155]**  
> deśācārayutaṃ varṣamāsapakṣāhavṛddhimat |  
> ṛṇisākṣilekhakānāṃ hastāṅkaṃ lekhyam ucyate ||

'anāhāryam' abhogyam | 'kāntāre' āpadi | 'ujjāmapatram' ṛṇapatram |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.84–88] |

> yaḥ kaścid artho niṣṇātaḥ svarucyā tu parasparam |  
> lekhyaṃ vā sākṣimat kāryaṃ tasmin dhanikapūrvakam ||  
> samāmāsatadardhāharnāmajātisagotrakaiḥ |  
> sabrahmacārikātmīyapitṛnāmādicihnitam ||  
> māse varṣe ṛṇī nāma svahastena niveśayet |  
> mataṃ me 'mukaputrasya yad atropari lekhitam ||  
> sākṣiṇaś ca svahastena pitṛnāmakapūrvakam |  
> atrāham amukaḥ sākṣī likheyur iti te samāḥ ||  
> ubhayābhyarthitenaitan mayā hy amukasūnunā |  
> likhitaṃ hy amukeneti lekhako 'nte tato likhet ||

**[156]** **'niṣṇātaḥ'** nirūpitaḥ | **'sabrahmacārikam'** bahvṛcādi[śākhā]prayuktaguṇanāma | **'bahvṛcaḥ'** kaṭha iti | **'samāḥ'** samaguṇāḥ |

vyāsaḥ [yājña. 2.90] |

> alipijñaṛṇī yaḥ syāl lekhayet svamataṃ tu saḥ |  
> sākṣī vā sākṣiṇānyena sarvasākṣisamīpagaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [251] |

> utpattijātisaṃjñāṃ ca dhanasaṃjñāṃ ca lekhayet |  
> smaraty evaṃ prayuktasya naśyed arthas tv alekhitaḥ |

**smaraty evaṃ prayuktasyeti** karmaṇiṣaṣṭhī | tenaivaṃ prayuktaṃ smarati nānyad ity arthaḥ |

**[157]**

## 28 śāsanam
atha śāsanam

tatra vyāsaḥ |

> rājñā tu svayam ādiṣṭaḥ saṃdhivigrahalekhakaḥ |  
> tāmrapaṭṭe paṭe vāpi pralikhed rājaśāsanam ||  
> sthānaṃ vaṃśānupūrvī ca deśaṃ grāmam upāgatān |  
> brāhmaṇāṃś ca tathā cānyān mānyān yān adhikṛtān likhet ||  
> kuṭumbino 'tha kāyasthadūtavaidyamahattarān |  
> mlecchacāṇḍālaparyantān sarvān saṃbodhayann iti ||  
> mātāpitror ātmanaś ca puṇyāyāmukasūnave |  
> dattaṃ mayāmukīyāya dānaṃ sabrahmacāriṇe ||  
> candrārkasamakālīnaṃ putrapautrānvayāgatam |  
> anācchedyam anāhāryaṃ sarvabhāvyavivarjitam ||

**[158]**  
> dātuḥ pālayituḥ svargaṃ hartur narakam eva ca |  
> jñātaṃ mayeti likhitaṃ tadā vyaktākṣarair yutam ||  
> abdamāsatadarhāho rājamudrāṅkitaṃ tathā |  
> anena vidhinā lekhyaṃ rājaśāsanakaṃ likhet ||

**sthānam** atra rājadhānī | **'upāgatān'** tatkāla āgantukān | **'sabrahmacāriṇe'** sahādhyāyine | etac ca pātramātropalakṣaṇam | **'sarvabhāvyavivarjitam'** daivabrāhmaṇanāpitādilabhyavarjitam |

yājñavalkyaḥ [1.318–320] |

> datvā bhūmiṃ nibandhaṃ vā kṛtvā lekhyaṃ tu kārayet |  
> āgāmibhadranṛpatiparijñānāya pārthivaḥ ||  
> paṭe vā tāmrapaṭṭe vā svamudroparicihnitam |  
> abhilekhyātmano vaṃśyān ātmānaṃ ca mahīpatiḥ ||  
> pratigrahaparīmāṇaṃ dānacchedopavarṇanam |  
> svahastakālasaṃpannaṃ śāsanaṃ kārayet sthiram ||

**[159]** **'nibandha'** āyasthāne śulkaśālādau pratyahaṃ niyatavastudānam, yathā parṇabhārakaṃ prati parṇaśataṃ grāhyaṃ tvayeti ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [6.25, 27, 26] |

> vaṃśādikaṃ yasya rājā likhitena prayacchati |  
> sevāśauryādinā tuṣṭaḥ prasādalikhitaṃ tu tat ||  
> yadvṛttaṃ vyavahāre tu pūrvapakṣottarādikam |  
> kriyāvadhāraṇopetaṃ jayapatre 'khilaṃ likhet ||  
> pūrvottarakriyāyuktaṃ nirṇayāntaṃ yadā nṛpaḥ |  
> pradadyāj jayine likhyaṃ jayapatraṃ tad ucyate ||

vṛddhavasiṣṭhaḥ |

> yathopanyastasādhyārthasaṃyuktaṃ cottarakriyam |  
> sāvadhāraṇakaṃ caiva jayapatrakam iṣyate ||  
> prāḍvivākādināmāṅkaṃ mudritaṃ rājamudrayā |

**[160]** kātyāyanaḥ [259, 260(a), 263, 260(a), 261, 264] |

> arthipratyarthivākyāni pratijñā sākṣivāk tathā |  
> nirṇayaś ca yathā tasya yathā cāvadhṛtaṃ svayam ||  
> etad yathākṣaraṃ lekhye yathāpūrvaṃ niveśayet |  
> sabhāsadaś ca ye tatra smṛtiśāstravidaḥ sthitāḥ ||  
> yathālekhyavidhau tadvat svahastaṃ tatra dāpayet |  
> abhiyoktrabhiyuktānāṃ vacanaṃ prāṅ niveśayet ||  
> sabhyānāṃ prāḍvivākasya kulānāṃ vā tataḥ param |  
> niścayaṃ smṛtiśāstrasya mataṃ tatraiva lekhayet ||  
> anena vidhinā lekhyaṃ paścātkāraṃ vidur budhāḥ |  
> nirastā tu kriyā yatra pramāṇenaiva vādinā ||  
> paścātkāro bhavet tatra na sarvāsu vidhīyate ||

**'paścātkāro'** jayapatram |

**[161]**

## 29 sallekhyam
atha sallekhyam

tatra kātyāyanaḥ [252] |

> lekhyaṃ tu sākṣimat kāryam aviluptakramākṣaram |  
> deśācārasthitiyutaṃ samagraṃ sarvavastuṣu ||

nāradaḥ [3.136] |

> deśācārāviruddhaṃ yad vyaktādhividhilakṣaṇam |  
> tat pramāṇaṃ smṛtaṃ lekhyam aviluptakramākṣaram ||

**'vyaktādhividhilakṣaṇam'**(?) spaṣṭaṃ vañcakapramāṇalakṣaṇaṃ yatra tat tathā |

kātyāyanaḥ [253, 267] |

> varṇavākyakriyāyuktam asaṃdigdhaṃ sphuṭākṣaram |  
> ahīnakramacihnaṃ ca lekhyaṃ tat siddhim āpnuyāt ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.89] |

> vināpi sākṣibhir lekhyaṃ svahastalikhitaṃ tu yat |  
> tat pramāṇaṃ smṛtaṃ sarvaṃ balopadhikṛtād ṛte ||

**'upadhiś'** chalam |

**[162]** kātyāyanaḥ [272] |

> khyāpitaṃ ced dvitīye 'hni na kaścid vinivartayet |  
> tathā tu syāt pramāṇaṃ tan mattonmattakṛtād ṛte ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.91] |

> deśāntarasthe durlekhye tathonmṛṣṭe hṛte tathā |  
> bhinne dagdhe tathā chinne lekhyam anyat tu kārayet ||

kātyāyanaḥ [312] |

> malair yad bheditaṃ dagdhaṃ chidritaṃ vītam eva vā |  
> tad anyat kārayel lekhyaṃ svātmanā likhitaṃ tathā ||

**[163]**

## 30 duṣṭalekhyam
**30 — duṣṭalekhyam**

[tatra] kātyāyanaḥ [273–274] |

> sākṣidoṣād bhaved duṣṭaṃ patraṃ vai lekhakasya vā |  
> dhanikasyopadhādoṣāt tathā dāraṇikasya vā ||  
> duṣṭair duṣṭaṃ bhaved lekhyaṃ śuddhaiḥ śuddhaṃ vinirdiśet |  
> tat patram upadhāduṣṭaiḥ sākṣilekhakakārakaiḥ ||

**'upadhā'** bhāvadoṣaḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ [6.30] |

> mumūrṣuśiśubhītārtaiḥ strīmattavyasanāturaiḥ |  
> niśopadhibalātkārakṛtaṃ lekhyaṃ na sidhyati ||

nāradaḥ [4.137] |

> mattābhiyuktastrībālabalātkārakṛtaṃ ca yat |  
> tad apramāṇaṃ likhitaṃ bhītopadhikṛtaṃ tathā ||

**[164]** kātyāyanaḥ [281, 270] |

> dhanikena svahastena likhitaṃ sākṣivarjitam |  
> bhavet kūṭaṃ na cet kartā kṛtaṃ hīti vibhāvayet ||  
> deśācāraviruddhaṃ yat saṃdigdhaṃ kramavarjitam |  
> kṛtam asvāminā yac ca sādhyahīnaṃ ca duṣyati ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [6.31–32] |

> dūṣito garhitaḥ sākṣī yatraiko viniveśitaḥ |  
> kūṭalekhyaṃ tu tat proktaṃ lekhako vāpi tadvidhaḥ ||  
> yad ujjvalaṃ cirakṛtaṃ malinaṃ svalpakālikam |  
> bhagnonmṛṣṭākṣarayutaṃ lekhyaṃ kūṭatvam āpnuyāt ||

kātyāyanaḥ [269] |

> sthānabhraṣṭās tv apaṅktisthāḥ saṃdighā lakṣaṇacyutāḥ |  
> yatraivaṃ syuḥ sthitā varṇāḥ lekhyaṃ duṣṭaṃ tathā bhṛguḥ ||

vyāsaḥ [kātyāyana 311] |

> sthāvare vikriyādhāne kūṭaṃ lekhyaṃ karoti yaḥ |  
> sa samyag bhāvitaḥ kārye jihvāpāṇyaṅghrivarjitaḥ |

**[165]**

## 31 dūṣitalekhyaparīkṣā
atha dūṣitalekhyaparīkṣā

[tatra] kātyāyanaḥ [276, 323] |

> sākṣilekhyakakartāraṃ kūṭatāṃ yānti te yathā |  
> tathā doṣāḥ prayoktavyā duṣṭair lekhyaṃ praduṣyati ||  
> āhartā bhuktiyukto 'pi lekhyadoṣān viśodhayet |  
> tatsuto bhuktidoṣāṃs tu lekhyadoṣāṃs tu nāpnuyāt ||

**'āhartā'** gṛhītā |

bṛhaspatiḥ [6.39] |

> uddharel lekhyam āhartā tatsuto bhuktim eva tu |  
> abhiyuktaḥ parmītaś cet [tatputro 'pi samuddharet] ||

'yady āhartābhiyuktaḥ san mriyeta tadā putro 'pi lekhyam uddhared ity arthaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [266, 308] |

> rājājñayā samāhūya yathānyāyaṃ vicārayet |  
> lekhyācāreṇa likhitaṃ sākṣyācāreṇa sākṣiṇaḥ ||

**[166]**  
> darpaṇasthaṃ yathā bimbam asat sad iva dṛśyate |  
> tathā lekhyasya bimbāni kurvanti kuṭilā narāḥ ||

vyāsaḥ [bṛhaspatiḥ 6.41] |

> lekhyam ālekhyavat kecil likhanti kuśalā narāḥ |  
> tasmān na lekhyasāmarthyāt siddhir aikāntikī matā ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [6.40, 42–44] |

> śrutvā kālaṃ deśakāryau kuśalāḥ kūṭakārakāḥ |  
> kurvanti sadṛśaṃ lekhyaṃ tad yatnena vicārayet ||  
> strībālārtān lipyavijān vañcayanti svabāndhavāḥ |  
> lekhyaṃ kṛtvā svanāmāṅkaṃ jñeyaṃ yuktyāgamais tataḥ ||  
> trividhasyāsya lekhyasya bhrāntiḥ saṃjāyate yadā |  
> ṛṇisākṣilekhakānāṃ hastoktyā śodhayet tataḥ ||

**[167]**  
> ujjāmam udayādānād ādhānaṃ phalasaṃgrahāt |  
> pratiyogidhanāḍhyatvāj jñeye yatnopadhiḥ kṛtaḥ ||

**'ujjāmam'** ṛṇam | **'udayādānāt'** kālāntaragrahaṇāt | **'ādhānam'** ādhiḥ | **'phalasaṃgrahāt'** phalopabhogāt | **'prayogitvam'** uttamarṇatvam |

nāradaḥ [4.143–144] |

> yasmin syāt saṃśayo lekhye bhūtābhūtakṛte kvacit |  
> tat svahastakriyācihnayuktiprāptibhir uddharet ||  
> lekhyaṃ yac cānyanāmāṅkaṃ hetvantarakṛtaṃ bhavet |  
> vipratyaye parīkṣyaṃ tat saṃbandhāgamabetubhiḥ ||

**'kriyā'** tu sākṣyopanyāsaḥ | **'cihnam'** asādhāraṇaṃ svīkārādi | **'yuktiprāptiḥ'** asmin deśe asmin kāle prayujyate tasya puruṣasyedaṃ dravyam ityādirūpā | **'vipratyaye'** vipratipattau | **saṃbandho** 'trārthipratyarthinoḥ parasparaviśvāsena pūrvam api dhanagrahaṇādisaṃbandhaḥ | **'āgamaḥ'** asyaitāvato dhanasya saṃbhāvitaḥ prāpnuyād ya iti | etaiḥ svahastādibhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ saṃdigdhaṃ lekhyaṃ sādhayed ity arthaḥ |

vyāsaḥ |

> yac cānyasya kṛtaṃ lekhyam anyahasteṣu dṛśyate |  
> avaśyaṃ tena vaktavyaṃ patrasyāgamanaṃ tataḥ ||

**[168]** kātyāyanaḥ [277, 290, 285, 286] |

> na lekhakena likhitaṃ na dṛṣṭaṃ sākṣibhis tathā |  
> evaṃ pratyarthinokte tu kūṭalekhyaṃ prakīrtitam ||  
> kūṭoktau sākṣiṇāṃ vākyāl lekhakasya ca patrakam |  
> nayec chuddhiṃ na yaḥ kūṭaṃ sa dāpyo damam uttamam ||  
> atha pañcatvam āpanno lekhakaḥ saha sākṣibhiḥ |  
> tat svahastādibhis teṣāṃ viśudhyet tu na saṃśayaḥ ||  
> ṛṇisvahastasaṃdehe jīvato vā mṛtasya vā |  
> tat svahastakṛtair anyaiḥ patrais tallekhyanirṇayaḥ ||

tathā [287] |

> samudre 'pi yadā lekhye mṛtāḥ sarve 'pi tatsthitāḥ |  
> likhitaṃ tatpramāṇaṃ tu mṛteṣv api hi teṣu vai |

prajāpatiḥ |

> kāryo balena mahatā nirṇayo rājaśāsane |  
> rājñaḥ svahastato mudrālekhakākṣaradarśanāt ||

**[169]** kātyāyanaḥ [296, 294, 296] |

> mudrāśuddhaṃ kriyāśuddhaṃ pāramparyānumoditam |  
> [adūṣitaṃ ca spṛṣṭaṃ ca kriyācitraṃ vibhāvitam |]  
> īdṛśaṃ siddhim āpnoti śāsanaṃ nṛpacihnitam ||  
> paścātkāranibaddhaṃ yat tad yatnena vicāreyet |  
> yadi syād yuktiyuktaṃ tu pramāṇaṃ likhite tadā ||  
> anyathā mūlataḥ kāryaṃ punar eva vinirṇayet |  
> atathyaṃ tathyabhāvena sthāpitaṃ jñānavibhramāt |  
> nivartyaṃ tatparmāṇaṃ syād yatnenāpi kṛtaṃ nṛpaiḥ ||

**'kriyāśuddham'** sākṣyanugṛhītam | **'pāramparyānumoditam'** bahubhir anumoditam |

**[170]**

## 32 lekhyabalam
atha lekhyabalam

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ [6.49] |

> kulaśreṇigaṇādīnāṃ yathākālaṃ pradarśayet |  
> śrāvayet smārayec caiva yathā syād balavattaram ||

nāradaḥ [4.140] |

> darśitaṃ pratikālaṃ yac chrāvitaṃ smāritaṃ ca yat |  
> lekhyaṃ sidhyati sarvatra mṛteṣv api hi sākṣiṣu ||

kātyāyanaḥ [298–303] |

> dṛṣṭaṃ patre sphuṭaṃ doṣaṃ noktavān ṛṇiko yadi |  
> tato viṃśativarṣāṇi kālaṃ [śrāntaṃ] patraṃ sthiraṃ bhavet ||  
> śaktasya saṃnidhāv artho yasya lekhyena bhujyate |  
> varṣāṇi viṃśatiṃ yāvat tat patraṃ doṣavarjitam ||

**[171]**  
> atha vā viṃśatiṃ varṣāṇy ādhir bhuktas tu niścitaḥ |  
> tena lekhyena tatsiddhir lekhyadoṣavivarjitā ||  
> sīmāvivāde nirṇīte sīmāpatraṃ vidhīyate |  
> tasya doṣāḥ prayoktavyā yāvad varṣāṇi viṃśati ||  
> ādhānasahitaṃ yatra ṛṇaṃ lekhyaniveśitam |  
> mṛtasākṣipramāṇāt tu svalpabhogena tad viduḥ ||  
> prāptaṃ vānena cet kiṃcid deyaṃ cārthanirūpitam |  
> vināpi mudrayā lekhyaṃ pramāṇaṃ mṛtasākṣikam ||

vyāsaḥ |

> svahastakāj jānapadaṃ tasmāc ca nṛpaśāsanam |  
> pramāṇataram iṣṭaṃ hi vyavahārārtham āgatam ||

**[172]** > dvitrilipijñaḥ svakṛtam anyalekhyena yuktibhiḥ |  
> kuryāc ca sadṛśaṃ lekhyaṃ tasmāj jānapadaṃ śubham ||  
> aprakāśāt sākṣiyuktaṃ lekhakākṣaramudritam |  
> lokaprasiddhaṃ svakṛtād dhīnam anyakṛtaṃ śubham ||  
> deśādhyakṣādinā lekhyaṃ patraṃ jānapadaṃ kṛtam |  
> samakālaṃ paścimaṃ vā tatra rājakṛtaṃ śubham ||

**'svahastāt'** svahastakṛtāt lekhyāt |

saṃvartaḥ |

> lekhye lekhyakriyā proktā vācike vācikī matā |  
> vācikī tu na sidhyet sā lekhyasyopari yā kṛtā ||  
> lekhyasyopari yat sākṣyaṃ kūṭaṃ tad abhidhīyate |  
> ardham asya hi taddvāram ato rājā vivarjayet ||

**[173]**  
> vācikair yadi sāmarthyam akṣarāṇāṃ vihanyate |  
> kriyāṇāṃ sarvanāśaḥ syād anavasthā ca jāyate ||

**'lekhye lekhyakriyā proktā'** balīyasīti śeṣaḥ | **'vācikī'** sākṣikriyā atrāpi balīyasīti śeṣaḥ | **'lekhyasyopari'** kriyā, lekhyakriyāvirodhinī yā kriyā na sā pramāṇam ity arthaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [306–307] |

> na divyaiḥ sākṣibhir vāpi hīyate lihitaṃ kvacit |  
> lekhyadharmaḥ sadā śreṣṭho hy ato nānyena hīyate ||  
> tadyuktipratilekhyena tadviśiṣṭena vā matā |  
> lekhyakriyā nirasyeta na sākṣiśapathaiḥ kvacit ||

**174]**

## 33 lekhyadaurbalyam
atha lekhyadaurbalyam

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ [6.51, 47, 48] |

> āḍhyasya nikaṭasthasya yac chaktena na yācitam |  
> śuddharṇāśaṅkayā tat tu lekhyaṃ durbalatām iyāt ||  
> lekhyaṃ triṃśatsamātītam adṛṣṭāśrāvitaṃ ca yat |  
> na tatsiddhim avāpnoti saṃtiṣṭhatsv api sākṣiṣu ||  
> prayukte śāntalābhe tu likhitaṃ yo na darśayet |  
> na yācate ca ṛṇikaṃ tatsaṃḍeham avāpnuyāt ||

**'śuddharṇāśaṅkayā'** śuddham ṛṇam iti śaṅkayā | **'śāntalābhe'** adhamarṇāpīḍākare |

vyāsaḥ |

> adṛṣṭāśrāvitaṃ lekhyaṃ pramītadhanikarṇikam |  
> abandhalagnakaṃ caiva bahukālaṃ na sidhyati ||

**'abandhalagnakam'** bandhalagnakābhyāṃ hīnam |

bṛhaspatiḥ [6,51] |

> unmattajadabālānāṃ rājabhītapravāsinām |  
> apragalbhabhayārtānāṃ na lekhyaṃ hānim āpnuyāt ||

**[175]** nārada-kātyāyanau |

> lekhye deśāntaraṃ nīte dagdhe durlikhite kṛte |  
> samas tatkālaharaṇam asato draṣṭṛdarśanam ||

**[176]** samas tatkālaharaṇam iti, deśāntarādau vidyamāne lekhye tadānayanaṃ yāvat, avidyamāne ca tallekhyadarśitapuruṣadarśanaṃ yāvat pratīkṣaṇīyam ity arthaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ |

> yal lekhyaṃ prāḍvivākena na dṛṣṭaṃ na pratiśrutam |  
> alabdharṇe kṛte lekhye kathaṃ tat prāpnuyād dhanī ||  
> ādhānam uparuddho vā yāvat tiṣṭhati lagnakaḥ |  
> lekhyālābhāt smṛtaṃ tāvat pramāṇaṃ draṣṭṛdarśanam ||

**yal lekhyam** ityādi | yal lekhyaṃ darśanīyam iti pratiśrutaṃ tat prāḍvivākena na dṛṣṭam, tasmin kṛte katham alabdhadhano dhanaṃ prāpnuyād ity arthaḥ |

**[177]**

## 34 bhuktiḥ
atha bhuktiḥ

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ [27.22–28] |

> etad vidhānam ākhyātaṃ sākṣiṇāṃ likhitasya ca |  
> saṃprati sthāvare prāpte bhuktasya vidhir ucyate ||  
> vidyayā krayabandhena śauryabhāryānvayāgatam |  
> sapiṇḍasyāprajasyāṃśaṃ sthāvaraṃ saptadhā smṛtam ||  
> pitrye labdhakrayādhāne satvaśauryapravedanāt |  
> prāpte saptavidhe bhogaḥ sāgamaḥ siddhim āpnuyāt ||  
> kramāgataḥ śāsanikaḥ krayādhānāgamānvitaḥ |  
> evaṃvidhas tu yo bhogaḥ sa tu siddhim avāpnuyāt ||  
> saṃvibhāgakrayaprāptaṃ pitryaṃ labdhaṃ ca rājataḥ |  
> sthāvaraṃ siddhim āpnoti bhuktvā hānim upekṣayā ||  
> prāptamātraṃ yena bhuktaṃ svīkṛtyāparipanthinam |  
> tasya tatsiddhim āpnoti hāniṃ copekṣayā tathā ||

**[178]**  
> adhyāsanāt samārabhya bhuktir yasyāvighātinī |  
> triṃśadvarṣāṇy avicchinnā tasya tāṃ na vicālayet ||

**'vidyayā'** pratigrahādiprakāreṇa | **'bandhaḥ'** ādhiḥ | **'śauryāgatam'** yuddhādinā yat prāptam | **'bhāryāgatam'** bhāryayā saha labdham | **'anvayāgatam'** pitrādikrameṇāyātam | **'pravedanam'** vivāhaḥ | '**pitrya**'ityādinā pūrvoktasaptaprakārānuvādaḥ | **'aparipanthinam'** avirodhinam | **'adhyāsanam'** adhikṛtāvasthānam | **'avighātinī'** avicchinnā |

viṣṇu-kātyāyanau |

> sāgamena tu bhogena bhuktaṃ samyag yadā tu yat |  
> āhartā labhate tat tu nāpahāryaṃ tu tat kvacit ||  
> pitrā bhuktaṃ tu yad dravyaṃ bhuktyācāreṇa dharmataḥ |  
> tasmin prete na vācyo 'sau bhuktyā prāptaṃ hi tasy atat ||  
> tribhir eva tu yā bhuktā puruṣair bhūr yathāvidhi |  
> lekhyābhāve 'pi tāṃ tatra caturthaḥ samavāpnuyāt ||\

**[179]** **'bhuktyācāreṇa'** samyagbhuktyā |

nāradaḥ [4.97] |

> anyāyena tu yad bhuktaṃ pitrā pūrvatarais tribhiḥ |  
> na tacchaktyam apāhartuṃ kramāt tripuruṣāgatam ||

**'pitrā pūrvatarais tribhir'** iti pitrā saha tribhiḥ pūrvatarair anyair ity anvayaḥ |

tathā |

> ādau tu kāraṇaṃ dānaṃ madhye bhuktis tu sāmagā |  
> kāraṇaṃ bhuktir evaikā santatā yā cirantanī ||

**'kāraṇam'** pramāṇam |

kātyāyanaḥ [329, 321] |

> bhuktir balavatī śāstre santatā yā cirantanī |  
> vicchinnāpi tu sā jñeyā yā tu pūrvaprasādhitā ||  
> ādānakālād ārabhya bhuktir yā tu nirantarā|  
> āsānaṃ prāpya tasyāṃ tu prāyaḥ sākṣyaṃ pravartate ||  
> smārte kāle kriyā bhūmeḥ sāgamā bhuktir iṣyate |  
> asmārte 'nugamābhāvāt kramāt tripuruṣāgatā ||

**[180]** **'pūrvaprasādhitā'** pūrvaiḥ puruṣaiḥ kṛtā | **'nirantarā'** yā bhuktir alpakālā bhavati tasyām āhartuḥ pratigrahādikaṃ prāpya sākṣyaṃ pravartata ity arthaḥ | **'smārte'** smaraṇayogyakāle | **'kriyāṃ'** pramāṇam | **'āgamaḥ'** svatve hetuḥ krayapratigrahādi | **'anugamābhāvāt'** anugamasyānusaṃdhānasyābhāvād ity arthaḥ |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.27] |

> āgamo 'bhyadhiko bhogād vinā pūrvakramāgamāt |

kātyāyanaḥ [318] |

> mukhyā paitāmahī bhuktiḥ paitṛkī cāpi saṃmatā |  
> tribhir etair avicchinnā sthirā ṣaṣṭyābdikā matā ||

vyāsaḥ |

> pitā pitāmaho yasya jīvec ca prapitāmahaḥ |  
> trayāṇāṃ jīvanaṃ bhogo vijñāpyas tv ekapūruṣaḥ ||  
> pitāmahena bhuktasya tatputreṇāpi pālanam |  
> tau vinā yasya pitrā ca tasya bhogas tripūruṣaḥ ||

**[181]** > varṣāṇi viṃśatiṃ bhuktā svāmināvyāhatā satī |  
> bhuktiḥ sā pauruṣī bhūmer dviguṇā ca dvipauruṣī ||  
> tripauruṣī ca triguṇā na tatrānveṣya āgamaḥ ||

tathā [bṛhaspatiḥ] [8.64] |

> sāgamo dīrghakālaś ca niśchidro 'nyaravojjhitaḥ |  
> pratyarthisaṃnidhānaś ca pañcāṅgo bhoga ucyate ||

**'niśchidraḥ'** vicchedarahitaḥ | **'anyaravojjhitaḥ'** vipratipattiśūnyaḥ | **'pratyarthisaṃnidhānaḥ'** pratyarthinaḥ saṃnidhānaṃ yasya sa tathā |

bṛhaspatiḥ [7.32–35] |

> yady ekaśāsane grāmakṣetrārāmāś ca lekhitāḥ |  
> ekadeśopabhoge 'pi sarve bhuktā bhavanti te ||  
> anumānād varaḥ sākṣī sākṣibhyo likhitaṃ guru |  
> avyāhatā tripuruṣī bhuktir ebhyo garīyasī ||

**[182]** > anumānaṃ sadya eva sākṣī cā maraṇād bhavet |  
> avyāhataṃ lekhyabhogaṃ pramāṇaṃ tat tripūruṣam ||

**anumānaṃ sadya eveti** | ākāreṅgitādiliṅgaiḥ vivādakāla evānumānaṃ pravartate |

nāradaḥ [4.75–76] |

> likhitaṃ balavan nityaṃ jīvantas tv eva sākṣiṇaḥ |  
> kālātiharaṇād bhuktir iti śāstreṣu nirṇayaḥ ||  
> trividhasyāsya dṛṣṭasya pramāṇasya yathākramam |  
> pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ guru jñeyaṃ bhuktir ebhyo garīyasī ||

**ebhyas** tv alpakālabhuktisākṣilikhitebhyo bahukālīnā vā **bhuktir garīyasī** balavatī |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.28] |

> āgamas tu kṛto yena so 'bhiyuktas tam uddharet |  
> na tatsutas tatsuto vā bhuktis tatra garīyasī ||

**[183]** bṛhaspatiḥ [7.39] |

> āhartā śodhayed bhuktim āgamaṃ cāp saṃsadi |  
> tatsuto bhuktim evaikāṃ pautrādis tu na kiṃcana ||

kātyāyanaḥ [324] |

> yenopāttaṃ hi yad dravyaṃ so 'bhiyuktas tad uddharet |  
> cirakālopabhoge 'pi bhuktis tasyaiva neśyate ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [7.38] |

> yadāhartābhiyuktaḥ syāl lekhyaṃ sākṣī tadā guruḥ |  
> lekhyābhāve tu yuktis tu bhuktis tābhyāṃ garīyasī ||

tathā [? kātyāyanaḥ 316] |

> nopabhoge balaṃ kāryam āhartrā tatsutena vā |  
> paśustrīpuruṣādīnām iti dharmo vyavasthitaḥ ||

**[184]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.29] |

> yo 'bhiyuktaḥ paretaḥ syāt tasya rikthi tam uddharet |  
> na tatra kāraṇaṃ bhuktir āgamena kṛtā vinā ||

nāradaḥ [4.93, 85] |

> tathārūḍhavivādasya pretasya vyavahāriṇaḥ |  
> putreṇa so 'rthaḥ saṃśodhyo na taṃ bhogo nivartayet ||  
> āgamena viśuddhena bhogo yāti pramāṇatām |  
> aviśuddhāgamo bhogaḥ prāṃāṇyaṃ nādhigacchati ||

tathā [nārada 8.87–88, 92] |

> anāgamena bhuktaṃ yan na tad bhuktivaśān nayet |  
> etat tu kartari dhanaṃ yāti tadviṃśino matam ||

**[185]**  
> anāgamaṃ tu yo bhuṅkte bahūny abdaśatāny api |  
> cauradaṇḍena taṃ pāpaṃ daṇḍayet pṛthivīpatiḥ ||  
> anvāhitaṃ hṛtaṃ nyastaṃ balāvaṣṭabdhayācitam |  
> apratyakṣaṃ ca yad bhuktaṃ ṣaḍ etāny āgamaṃ vinā ||

### anupabhogenāsiddhiḥ
**athānupabhogenāsiddhiḥ **

tatra yājñavalkyaḥ [2.27] |

> āgame 'pi balaṃ naiva bhuktiḥ stokāpi yatra no |

nāradaḥ [4.77, 88] |

> vidyamāne 'pi likhite jīvatsv api hi sākṣiṣu |  
> viśeṣataḥ sthāvarāṇāṃ yatra bhuktaṃ na tat sthiram ||  
> bhujyamānān parair arthān yaḥ svān mohād upekṣate |  
> samakṣaṃ jīvato 'py asya tān bhuktiḥ kurute vaśe ||

vyāsaḥ |

> upekṣitā yathā dhenur vinā pālena naśyati |  
> paśyato 'nyais tathā bhuktā bhūmiḥ kālena hīyate ||

**[186]**  
> varṣāṇi viṃśatiṃ yasya bhūr bhuktā tu parair iha |  
> sati rājñi samarthasya tasya seha na sidhyati ||

nāradaḥ [4.42] |

> pratyakṣaparibhogāt tu svāmino dvidaśāḥ samāḥ |  
> ādhyādīny api jīryanti strīnarendradhād ṛte ||

'dvidaśāḥ samāḥ' viṃśativarṣāṇi | 'strīnarendradhanād ṛte' strīdhanarājadhanavyatirekeṇa |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.24] |

> paśyato 'bruvato bhūmer hānir viṃśativārṣikī |  
> pareṇa bhujyamānāyā dhanasya daśavārṣikī ||

**[187]** manu-nāradau [manu 8.143; nā. 4.79] |

> yat kiṃcid daśavarṣāṇi saṃnidhau prekṣate dhanī |  
> bhujyamānaṃ parais tūṣṇīṃ na sa tal labdhum arhati ||

gautamaḥ [12.34]: "ajaḍāpogaṇḍadhanaṃ daśavarṣabhuktaṃ paraiḥ saṃnidhau bhoktuḥ" | 'ajaḍasya' ['apogaṇḍasya'] ca dhanaṃ tatsaṃnidhāne avivādaṃ parair daśavarṣaparyantam upabhuktaṃ bhoktur evaitat svaṃ saṃpadyata ity arthaḥ |

manuḥ [8.145] |

> ādhiś copanidhiś cobhau na kālātyayam arhataḥ |  
> avahāryau bhavetāṃ tau dīrghakālam avasthitau ||

'ādhiḥ' bandhakaḥ | 'upanidhir' api prītyā bhogārthaṃ samarpitaṃ kṣetrādi | na tu 'vāsanastham anākhyāya' ityādismṛtilakṣaṇaḥ | tasya bhogānarhatvāt | 'kālātyayaḥ' uktāvadhikālātikramaḥ | tasya bhogānarhatvāt | 'kālātyayaḥ' uktāvadhikālātikramaḥ | 'na kālātyayam arhataḥ' mokṣaṇakāle 'vaśyaṃ mokṣaṇīyāv ity arthaḥ | tatra hetum āha: 'avahāryau bhavetām' ityādinā | tau hi cirakālāvasthitau bhoktur avahāryau bhavetām, bhoktā kadācid apahared apīty arthaḥ |

**[188]** bṛhaspatiḥ [7.40, 41] |

> ṛkthibhir vā parair dravyaṃ samakṣaṃ yasya dīyate |  
> anyasya bhuñjataḥ paścān na sa tal labdhum arhati ||  
> paśyann anyasya dadataḥ kṣitiṃ yo na nivārayet |  
> svāmī satāpi lekhyena na punas tāṃ samāpnuyāt ||

tathā [7.66–67] |

> bhūmer abhuktir lekhyasya yathākālam adarśanam |  
> asmāraṇaṃ sākṣiṇāṃ ca svārthahānikarāṇi tu ||  
> tasmād yatnena kartavyaṃ pramāṇaparipālanam |  
> tena kāryāṇi sidhyanti sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca ||

**[189]**
## 35 anya-bhoga-hāny-apavādaḥ
**35 — athānyabhogahānyapavādaḥ**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ [7.43, 44, 46] |

> bhuktis tripauruṣī sidhyet pareṣāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ |  
> anivṛtte sapiṇḍatve sakulyānāṃ na sidhyati ||  
> asvāminā tu yad abhuktaṃ gṛhakṣtrāpaṇādikam |  
> suhṛdbandhusakulyasya na tad bhogena hīyate ||  
> vivāhyaśrotriyair bhuktaṃ rājāmātyais tathaiva ca |  
> sudīrgheṇāpi kālena teṣāṃ sidhyan na tad dhanam ||

**''anivṛtte sapiṇḍatve'** iti | sapiṇḍatve vidyamāne saty api tripuruṣabhuktau sakulyānāṃ bhujyamānaṃ svaṃ na bhavatīty arthaḥ | **'vivāhyo'** jāmātā |

gautamaḥ [12.34–36]: 'ajaḍāpogaṇḍadhanaṃ daśavarṣaparyantam upabhuktaṃ paraiḥ saṃnidhau bhoktuḥ | na śrotriyapravrajitarājapuruṣaiḥ | paśubhūmistrīṇām anatibhogaḥ' | atibhogato hānir ity arthaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [335] |

> sanābhibhir bāndhavaiś ca bhuktaṃ yat svajanais tathā |  
> bhogāt tatra na siddhiḥ syād bhogam anyeṣu kalpayet ||

**[190]** **'anyeṣu'** asambandhiṣu bhoktṛṣu |

manu-nāradau |

> ādhiḥ sīmā bāladhanaṃ nikṣepopanidhī striyaḥ |  
> rājasvaṃ śrotriyasvaṃ ca na bhogena praṇśyati ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [7.47] |

> aśaktālasarogārtabālabhītapravāsinām |  
> śāsanārūḍham anyena bhuktaṃ bhuktyā na hīyate ||

**'śāsanārūḍham'** tāmrapaṭṭādilikhitam |

kātyāyanaḥ [330] |

> na bhogaṃ kalpayet strīṣu devarājadhaneṣu ca |  
> bālaśrotriyavitte ca mātṛtaḥ pitṛtaḥ kramāt ||

**[191]** > na strīṇām upabhogaḥ syād vinā lekhyāt kadācana |  
> śatruśrotriyarājñāṃ tu tathā bāladhane mataḥ ||

manuḥ [8.146] |

> saṃprītyā bhujyamānāni na naśyanti kadācana |  
> dhenur uṣṭro vahann aśvo yaś ca damyaḥ prayujyate ||

**'damyaḥ prayujyate'** damanārthaṃ yaḥ samarthyate |

kātyāyanaḥ |

> krayaṃ śilpiṣu nikṣiptaṃ bandhānvāhitayācitam |  
> prasahyātihanan mohād dhīno daṇḍyaḥ sa vai bhavet ||

**'krayo'** mūlyam |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.26] |

> ādhyādīnāṃ nihantāraṃ dhanine dāpayed dhanam |  
> daṇḍaṃ ca tatsamaṃ rājñe śaktyapekṣam athāpi vā ||

**'śaktyapekṣam'** yathāśakti, **'daṇḍaṃ dāpayet'** |

**192]**

## 36 vicchinnabhoganirṇayaḥ
atha vicchinnabhoganirṇayaḥ

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ [7.48–52] |

> chinnabhoge gṛhakṣetre saṃdighaṃ yatra jāyate |  
> lekhyena bhogavidbhir vā sākṣibhis tad vibhavayet ||  
> nāmaghāṭāgamaṃ saṃkhyāṃ kālaṃ digbhāgam eva vā |  
> bhogacchedanimittaṃ ca ye vidus te 'tra sākṣiṇaḥ ||  
> tadutpannāś ca sāmantā ye 'nyadeśāntrasthitāḥ |  
> maulās te tu samuddiṣṭāḥ praveṣṭavyāḥ kāryanirṇaye ||  
> aduṣṭās te tu yad brūyuḥ saṃdigdhe samadṛṣṭayaḥ |  
> tat pramāṇaṃ tu kartavyam evaṃ dharmo na hīyate ||  
> sthāvarasyaitad ākhyātaṃ lābhabhogaprasādhanam |  
> pramāṇahīne vāde tu nirdeśyā daivikī kriyā ||

**[193]**

## 37 yuktayah
atha yuktayah

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ [7.68] |

> asākṣike cirakṛte pṛcched uttarasākṣiṇaḥ |  
> śapathān vā prayuñjīyād upadhāṃ vāpi yojayet ||

**'upadhā'** yuktiḥ |

nāradaḥ [4.235–237] |

> pramādād dhanino yatra na syāl lekhyaṃ na sākṣiṇaḥ |  
> arthaṃ vāpahnute vādī tatroktas trividho vidhiḥ ||  
> codanā pratikālaṃ ca yuktileśas tathaiva ca |  
> tṛtīyaḥ śapathaḥ proktas tair enaṃ sādhayet kramāt ||

**[194]**  
> abhīkṣṇaṃ codyamāno yaḥ pratihanyān na tadvacaḥ |  
> tricatuḥpañcakṛtvo vā parato 'rthaṃ sa dāpyate ||

**'codanā pratikālam'** 'devadatta dhanaṃ dehi' iti pratikṣaṇam preraṇā |

kātyāyanaḥ [144, 336] |

> śrāvyamāṇo 'rthinā yatra yo hy artho na vighātitaḥ |  
> dānakāle 'tha vā tūṣṇīṃ sthitaḥ so 'rtho 'numoditaḥ ||  
> arthinābhyarthito tatra vighātaṃ na prayojayet |  
> tricatuḥpañcakṛtvo vā paratas tad ṛṇī vahet ||  
> svāminā nṛpatir vipraṃ krameṇoktaṃ pradāpayet |  
> tato 'nyaṃ dāpayet pūrvaṃ sakṛd yuktaṃ vighātinam ||

nāradaḥ [4.238] |

> codanāpratighāte tu yuktileśais tam anviyāt |  
> deśakālārthasambandhaparimāṇakriyādibhiḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [337–338] |

> dānaṃ prajñāpanābhedaḥ saṃpralobhakriyā ca yā |  
> cintāpanayanaṃ caiva hetavo hi vibhāvakāḥ ||

**[195]**  
> eṣām anyatamoyatra vādinā bhāvito bhavet |  
> mūlakriyā tu tatra syād bhāvite vādinihnave ||

**'eṣām anyatamaḥ'** iti | eṣāṃ hetūnām anyatamo 'pi cet pradarśitaḥ siddhaiva tadā mūlakriyā |

nāradaḥ [4.172–175] |

> asākṣipratyayās tv anye ṣaḍ vivādāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |  
> lakṣaṇāny eva sākṣitva yeṣām āhur manīṣiṇaḥ ||  
> ulkāhasto 'gnido jñeyaḥ śastrapāṇiś ca ghātakaḥ |  
> keśākeśigṛhītaś ca yugapat pāradārikaḥ ||  
> kuddālapāṇir vijñeyaḥ setubhettā samīpagaḥ |  
> tathā kuṭhārahastaś ca vanacchetā prakīrtitaḥ ||  
> pratyakṣacihnair vijñeyo daṇḍapāruṣyakṛt naraḥ |  
> asākṣiprayayā hy ete pāruṣye tu parīkṣaṇam ||

**'sākṣitve'** sākṣisthāne |

śaṅkhalikhitau: "keśākeśigrahaṇāt pāradārikaḥ | ulkāhasto 'gnidaḥ | śastrapāṇir ghātakaḥ | **[196]** loptrahastaś ca cauraḥ | kṣepe 'ṣṭaśataṃ yathānurūpaṃ vā | rudhirasrāve prahāraiś cābhivyakte na sākṣiṇaḥ | pratyakṣaliṅgābhivyakte cāṣṭaśatam" |

**iti bhaṭṭalakṣmīdharaviracite**

**kṛtyakalpatarau yuktiḥ ||**

**[197]**

## 38 divyāni
atha divyāni

**(ka) divyabhedāiḥ**

tatra nāradaḥ [4.239, 252, 253] |

> yuktiṣv apy asamarthāsu śapathair enam ardayet |  
> arthakālabalāpekṣam agnyambusukṛtādibhiḥ |  
> dhaṭo 'gnir udakaṃ caiva viṣaṃ kośaś ca pañcamaḥ |  
> uktāny etāni divyāni viśuddhyarthaṃ mahātmabhiḥ ||  
> samdighe 'rthe 'bhiyuktānāṃ parīkṣārthaṃ mahātmabhiḥ |  
> proktāni nāradeneha satyānṛtaviśuddhaye ||

**'ardayet'** pīḍayet |

śaṅkhalikhitau: "asākṣipraṇihite puruṣapratyayaḥ śāsanaṃ bhedanaṃ tāḍanam | saṃnyaste vā vivāde vā daivaṃ vā kośaviṣabhakṣaṇaśastrajalam" |

**'asākṣipraṇihite'** sākṣibhir anirṇīte | **'puruṣapratyayaḥ'** puruṣaḥ pratīyate yena mithyākāritayā, puruṣaprtyayaḥ śāsanādiḥ | **'bhedanam'** pratodādiḥ | **'saṃnyaste'** likhitādipramāṇarahite | **'daivaṃ'** divyaṃ dhatādi |

**[198]** bṛhaspatiḥ [8.3–4] |

> dhaṭo 'gnir udakaṃ caiva viṣaṃ kośaś ca pañcamam |  
> ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca taṇḍulāḥ proktaṃ saptamaṃ saptamāṣakaḥ ||  
> aṣṭamaṃ phāla ity uktaṃ navamaṃ dharmajaṃ bhavet ||  
> divyāny etāni dharmāṇi nirdiṣṭāni svayaṃbhuvā ||

tathā [8.5–6] |

> aham uddeśato vacmi saṃdighārthaviśuddhaye |  
> deśakālārthasaṃkhyābhiḥ prayuktāny anupūrvaśaḥ ||  
> aparādhānupūrveṇa sādhvasādhuvivakṣayā |  
> śāstroditena vidhinā pradātavyāni nānyathā ||

atha dravyasaṃkhyādinā divyaviśeṣaḥ | tatra viṣṇuḥ [9.1–3]: "atha śapathakriyā | rājadrohasāhaseṣu yathākramam | nikṣepasteyeṣv arthapramāṇāt" | **'śapatho'** divyam |

**[199]** daivī kriyety anuvṛttau bṛhaspatiḥ [8.7] |

> ṛṇādikeṣu kāryeṣu visaṃvāde parasparam |  
> dravyasaṃkhyānvitā deyā puruṣāpekṣayā tathā ||

kātyāyanaḥ [416] |

> dattasyāphnavo yatra pramāṇaṃ tatra kalpayet |  
> steyasāhasayor divyaṃ svalpe 'py arthe pradāpayet ||

**'pramāṇam'** apahnutadravyānusāreṇa divyādipramāṇaṃ dāpayet |

bṛhaspatiḥ [8.27–32] |

> saṃkhyā raśmirajomūlā manunā samudāhṛtā |  
> kārṣāpaṇāntā sā divye niyojyā vinaye tathā ||  
> viṣaṃ sahasre 'pahṛte pādone ca hutāśanaḥ |  
> tribhāgone ca salilam ardhe deyo dhaṭas tathā ||  
> catuḥśate 'bhiyoge tu dātavyas taptamāṣakaḥ |  
> triśate taṇḍulā deyāḥ kośaś caiva tadardhake ||  
> śate hṛte 'pahnute ca dātavyaṃ darmaśodhanam |

**[200]**  
> gocorasya pradātavyaṃ sabhyaiḥ phālaṃ prayatnataḥ ||  
> yathāsaṃkhyā nikṛṣṭānāṃ madhyānāṃ dviguṇā smṛtā |  
> caturguṇottamānāṃ ca kalpanīyā prayatnataḥ ||

**'raśmirojomūlā'** –

> raśmumūlagate bhānau yat sūkṣmaṃ dṛśyate rajaḥ |  
> prathamaṃ tat pramāṇānāṃ trasareṇuṃ pracakṣate ||

ityādikā | **'vinayo'** daṇḍaḥ | **'nikṛṣṭānāṃ'** jātikarmaguṇaiḥ | evaṃ madhyamānām uttamānāṃ ca |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.99] |

> nāsahasrād dharet phālaṃ na viṣaṃ na tulāṃ tathā |  
> nṛpārtheṣv abhiśāpe ca vaheyuḥ śucayas tadā ||

**'nāsahasrāt'** paṇasahasrād ūrdhvaṃ cāpahnave phālādikriyety arthaḥ | **'nṛpārtheṣu'** nṛpaviṣayeṣu drohādiṣu | **'abhiśāpe'** pātakābhigoye | **'śucayaḥ'** snānādinā |

viṣṇuḥ [9.4]: "sarveṣv evārthajāteṣu mūlyaṃ kanakaṃ prakalpayet" | **201]** tathā [9.10–19]: "suvarṇārdhone kośo dātavyaḥ śūdrasya | tataḥ paraṃ yathārhaṃ ghaṭāgnyudakaviṣāṇām anyatamam | dviguṇe 'rthe yathābhihitā samayakriyā vaiśyasya | triguṇātha rājanyasya | kośavarjaṃ caturguṇārthe brāhmaṇasya | na brāhmaṇasya kośaṃ dadyāt | anyatrāgāmikālasamayanibandhanakriyātaḥ | kośasthāne brāhmaṇaṃ sīroddhṛtamahīkaram eva śāpayet | prāgdṛṣṭadoṣaṃ svalpe 'py arthe divyānām anyatamam eva kārayet | satsu viditaṃ saccāritraṃ na mahaty arthe 'pi" |

**'suvarṇārdhone'** parikalpyamāne kiṃcinnyūne, suvarṇārdhamūlye | **'dviguṇe 'rthe'** pūrvārthoktasuvarṇārdharūpe dviguṇībhūte | evaṃ triguṇādāv api | 'yathabhihita**samayakriyā'** kośapānarūpā | anyatrāgāmītyādi | asmābhir militvā evaṃ kartavyam eveti samayakaraṇam, tasmād anyatra | **'sīroddhṛtamahīkaram'** halotkhātamṛttikāhastam | **'divyānām'** ghaṭādīnām | **'satsu viditam'** śiṣṭeṣu prasiddham | **'na mahaty 'rthe 'pi'** dhaṭādīnām anyatamaṃ kāreyed ity arthaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [417, prathame] |

> sarvadravyapramāṇaṃ tu jñātvā hema prakalpayet |  
> hemapramāṇayuktaṃ tu tadā divyaṃ prayojayet ||

**[202]** > śate viṣaṃ tu pādone hutabhuk tatra dṛśyate |  
> āpas tribhāgahīne tu śatārdhe tu tulā smṛtā ||  
> kośapānaṃ tadardhe vā daśapañcakasaptasu |  
> tadardhe taṇḍulā jñeyā tadardhe taptamāṣakaḥ ||

**'śate'** suvarṇasyeti śeṣaḥ |

vṛddhaḥ [kātyāyanaḥ 418–20] |

> jñātvā saṃkhyāṃ suvarṇasya śatanāśe viṣaṃ smṛtam |  
> aśītes tu vināśe vai dadyāc caiva hutāśanam ||  
> ṣaṣṭyā nāśe jalaṃ jñeyaṃ syāc catvāriṃśatā dhaṭaḥ |  
> triṃśaddaśavināśe vā kośapānaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ ||  
> pañcārdhikasya vā nāśe tadardhasya ca taṇḍulāḥ |

**'pañcārdhikasya'** pañcārdhaṃ sārdhadvayam |

**[203]**

**(kha) atha divyakālaviśeṣaḥ**

tatra pitāmahaḥ |

> yo yasya vihitaḥ kālo vidhir yasya ca yo yathā |  
> taṃ pravakṣyāmi tattvena vādinaś ca balābalam ||  
> caitro mārgaśiraś caiva vaiśākhaś ca tathaiva ca |  
> ete sādhāraṇā māsā divyānām avirodhinaḥ ||  
> dhaṭaḥ sarvartukaḥ prokto vāte vāti vivarjayet |  
> agneḥ śiśirahemantavarṣāś caiva prakīrtitāḥ ||  
> śaradgrīṣme tu salilaṃ hemante śiśire viṣam |

nāradaḥ [4.260, 254] |

> vicārya dharmanipuṇair dharmaśāstraviśāradaiḥ |  
> dharmyaṃ sarvartukaṃ proktaṃ piṇḍitair dhaṭadhāraṇam ||  
> varṣāsu samaye vahniḥ hemante śiśire tathā |  
> grīṣme salilam ity uktaṃ viṣaṃ kāle tu śītale ||

**[204]** > na śīte toyasiddhiḥ syān noṣṇakāle 'gniśodhanam |  
> na prāvṛṣi viṣaṃ dadyāt pravātu tu (na?) tulāṃ nṛpaḥ ||

pitāmahaḥ |

> avyavasthitamaryādaṃ viṣaṃ prāvṛṣi jāyate |

**(ga) atha varṇādito divyaviśeṣaḥ**

tatra nāradaḥ [4.334] |

> brāhmaṇasya ghaṭo deyaḥ kṣatriyasya hutāśanaḥ|  
> vaiśyasya salilaṃ deyaṃ śūdrasya viṣam eva tu ||  
> sādhāraṇaḥ samastānāṃ kośaḥ prokto manīṣibhiḥ |  
> viṣavarjaṃ brāhmaṇasya sarveṣāṃ vā tulā smṛtā ||

kātyāyanaḥ [422] |

> rājanye 'gnir dhaṭaṃ vipre vaiśye toyaṃ niyojayet |  
> sarveṣu sarvadivyaṃ vā viṣaṃ varjyaṃ dvijātaye ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.98] |

> tulā strībālavṛddhāndhapaṅgubrāhmaṇarogiṇām |  
> agnir jalaṃ vāśudrasya yavāḥ sapta viṣasya vā ||

**[205]** kātyāyanaḥ [423] |

> gorakṣakān vāṇijakāṃs tathā kārukuśīlavān |  
> preṣyān vārdhuṣikāṃś caiva grāhayec chūdravad dvijān ||

kālikāpurāṇe |

> vaiśyasya ca jalaṃ deyaṃ viṣaṃ śudrasa dāpayet |  
> varṇāntasya sadā deyaṃ māṣakaṃ taptahemajam ||

**'varṇāntasya'** ityantasya (?) |

nāradaḥ [4.255, 313–15] |

> klībāturān satvahīnān patitāṃś cārditān narān |  
> bālavṛddhāturān strīṃś ca parīkṣeta dhaṭe sadā ||  
> nārtānāṃ toyaśuddhiḥ syān na viṣaṃ pittarogiṇām |  
> śvitryandhakunakhīnāṃ ca nāgnikarma vidhīyate ||

**[206]**  
> na majjanīyaṃ strībālaṃ dharmaśāstravicakṣaṇaiḥ |  
> rogiṇo ye ca vṛddhaḥ syuḥ pumāṃso ye ca durbalāḥ ||  
> nirutsāhān vyādhikliṣṭān nārtān toya nimajjayet |  
> sadyo mriyante majjantaḥ svalpaprāṇā hi te smṛtāḥ ||  
> sāhase 'py āgatān etān naiva toye nimajjayet |  
> na cāpi hārayed [sādhayed?] agniṃ na viṣeṇa viśodhayet ||

kātyāyanaḥ [428] |

> na lohaśilpinām agniṃ salilaṃ nāmbusevinām |  
> mantrayogavidāṃ caiva viṣaṃ dadyāt tu na kvacit ||  
> divyaṃ tu varjayen nityam ārtānāṃ tu gadair nṛṇām |  
> taṇḍulair na niyuñjīta vratināṃ mukharogiṇām ||

viṣṇuḥ [9.25–32]: "na kuṣṭyasamarthalohakārāṇām agir deyaḥ | śaradgrīṣmayoś ca | na kuṣṭhipauttakabrāhmaṇānāṃ viṣaṃ deyam | prāvṛṣi ca | na śleṣmavyādhyarditānāṃ bhīrūṇāṃ **[207]** śvāsakāsinām ambujīvināṃ codakam | hemantiśiśirayoś ca | na nāstikebhyaḥ kośo deyaḥ, deśe vyādhimaraṇakopasṛṣṭe ca" |

nāradaḥ [4.332] |

> mahāparādhe nirdharme kṛtaghne klībakutsite |  
> nāstike dṛṣṭadoṣe ca kośadānaṃ vivarjayet ||

pitāmahaḥ |

> madyapastrīvyasinināṃ kitavānāṃ tathaiva ca |  
> kośaḥ prājñair na dātavyo ye ca nāstikavṛttayaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [436] |

> kāladeśavirodhe tu yathāyuktaṃ prakalpayet |  
> anyena hārayed divyaṃ vidhir eva viparyaye ||

nāradaḥ [4.256] |

> savratānāṃ bhṛśārtānāṃ vyādhitānāṃ tapasvinām |  
> strīṇāṃ na tu bhaved divyaṃ yadi dharmas tv avekṣyate ||

**[208]** kātyāyanaḥ [427–30] |

> mātāpitṛdvijagurubālastrīrājaghātinām |  
> mahāpātakayuktānāṃ nāstikānāṃ viśeṣataḥ ||  
> liṅgināṃ prasavānāṃ tu mantrayogakriyāvidām |  
> varṇasaṃkarajātānāṃ pāpābhyāsapravartinām ||  
> eteṣv evābhiyogeṣu ninditeṣv eva yatnataḥ |  
> divyaṃ prakalpayen naiva rājā dharmaparāyaṇaḥ ||  
> etair eva niyuktānāṃ sādhūnāṃ divyam arhati |  
> na santi sādhavo yatra tatra śodhyāḥ svakair naraiḥ (?) ||

tathā [431–32]

> mahāpātakayukteṣu nāstikeṣu viśeṣataḥ |  
> na deyaṃ teṣu divyaṃ tu pāpābhyāsarateṣu ca ||  
> eṣu vādeṣu divyāni pratiṣiddhāni yatnataḥ |  
> kārayet sajjanais tāni nābhiśastaṃ tyajen manuḥ ||

**[209]**

**(gha) athāvaṣṭambhavādaḥ **

tatra pitāmahaḥ |

> avaṣṭambhābhiyuktānāṃ dhaṭādīni vinirdiśet |  
> taṇḍulāś caiva kośaś ca śaṅkāsv etau niyojayet ||

**'avaṣṭambho'** niścayaḥ |

tathā |

> cauryaśaṅkābhiyuktānāṃ taptamāṣo vidhīyate |

kātyāyanaḥ [415] |

> śaṅkā viśvāsasaṃdhāne vibhāge rikthināṃ sadā |  
> kriyāsamūhakartṛtve kośam eva pradāpayet ||

pitāmahaḥ |

> visrambhe sarvaśṅkāsu saṃdhikārye tathaiva ca |  
> eṣu kośaḥ pradātavyo nityaṃ cittaviśuddhaye ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.95] |

> tulāgnyāpo viṣaṃ kośo dviyānīha viśuddhaye |  
> mahābhiyogeṣv etāni śrīṣakasthe 'bhiyoktari ||

**'śīrṣakam'** śiraḥ | tac ca divyagrāhiṇo jaye svayaṃ daṇḍāṅgīkāraḥ |

**[210] **pitāmahaḥ |

> śiraḥsthāyivihīnāti divyāni parivarjayet |  
> catvāri tu dhaṭādīni kośas tv evāśirāḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
> abhiyoktā śiraḥsthāyī divyeṣu parikalpayet |  
> abhiyuktāya dātavyaṃ divyaṃ smṛtinidarśanāt ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.26] |

> rucyā vāyataraḥ kuryād itaro vartayec chiraḥ |  
> vināpi śīrṣakān kuryān nṛpadrohe ca pātake ||

kālikāpurāṇe |

> paradārābhiśāpe ca caurye 'gamyāgameṣu ca |  
> mahāpātakaśasteṣu syād divyaṃ nṛpasāhase ||  
> vipratipattau vivāde cāvarṇasthāpane kṛte |  
> tatraitad dāpayed divyaṃ śiraḥpūrvaṃ mahīpatiḥ ||

**[211]**  
> paradārābhimarśe ca bahavo yatra vādinaḥ |  
> śirohīnaṃ bhaved divyam ātmanaḥ śuddhikāraṇāt ||

**'vipratipattau'** paradārābhiśāpādiviṣayāyām | **'vivāde'** ṛṇādānādiviṣaye | [**'avarṇo'** apavādaḥ] | **'paradārābhimarśe ca'** iti cauryādīnām apy upalakṣaṇam |

viṣṇuḥ [9.22] |

> rājadrohe sāhaseṣu vināśīrṣapravartanāt | iti |

pitāmahaḥ |

> rājabhiḥ śaṅkitānāṃ ca nirdiṣṭānāṃ ca dasyubhiḥ |  
> ātmaśuddhiparāṇāṃ ca divyaṃ deyaṃ śiro vinā||

nāradaḥ [4.270] |

> aśirāṃsi ca divyāni rājakṛtyeṣu dāpayet |  
> abhiyoktābhiyuktānām anyeṣāṃ ca yathākramam ||

**(ṅa) atha deśakālaḥ**

kātyāyanaḥ [434–35] |

> indrasthāne 'bhiśastānāṃ mahāpātakināṃ nṛṇām |  
> nṛpadrohapravṛttānāṃ rājadvāreṣu yojayet ||

**[212]** > prātilomyaprasūtānāṃ divyaṃ deyaṃ catuṣpathe |  
> ato 'nyeṣu [tu] kāryeṣu sabhāmadhye vidur budhāḥ ||

**'indrasthānam'** indradhvajapūjāsthānam |

bṛhaspati-kātyāyanau [bṛ. 8.15–16; kā. 439–440] |

> yathoktavidhinā deyaṃ divyaṃ divyaviśāradaiḥ |  
> ayathoktapradattaṃ ca na śakyaṃ sādhyasādhane ||  
> adeśakāladattāni bahirvādikṛtāni ca |  
> vyabhicāraṃ sadārtheṣu kurvantīha na saṃśayaḥ ||

'bahirvādinam' vādinam abhiyoktāraṃ vinā |

**(ca) atha divyavidhiḥ**

bṛhaspatiḥ [8.14] |

> snehāt krodhāl lobhato vā bhedam āyānti sākṣiṇaḥ |  
> vidhidattasya divyasya na bhedo jāyate kvacit ||

pitāmahaḥ |

> pratyakṣaṃ dāpayed divyaṃ rāja vādhikṛto 'pi vā |  
> brāhmaṇānāṃ śrutavatāṃ prakṛtīnāṃ tathaiva ca ||

**[213]** viṣṇu[yājñavalkyau] |

> sacelaṃ snātam āhūya sūryodaya upoṣitam |  
> kārayet sarvadivyāni nṛpabrāhmaṇasaṃnidhau ||

nāradaḥ [4.268] |

> ahorātroṣite snāte ārdravāsasi mānave |  
> pūrvāhṇe sarvadivyānāṃ pradānam anukīrtitam ||

pitāmahaḥ |

> trirātropoṣitāyaiva ekarātroṣitāya vā |  
> nityaṃ divyāni deyāni śucaye cādravāsase ||  
> divyeṣu sarvakāryāṇi prāḍvivākaḥ samācaret |  
> adhvareṣu yathādhvaryuḥ sopavāso nṛpājñayā ||

kātyāyanaḥ [438] |

> sādhayet tat punaḥ sādhyaṃ vyāghāte sādhanasya hi |  
> dattāny api yathoktāni rājā divyāni varjayet ||  
> mūrkhair lubdhaiś ca duṣṭaiś ca punar deyāni tāni vai |

**'dattāni'** ity asya **'mūrkhair'** ityādinānvayaḥ | **'varjayet'** na pramāṇīkuryāt |

**[214]**

## 39 dhaṭavidhiḥ
atha dhaṭavidhiḥ

tatra viṣṇuḥ [10.2–3]: "atha dhaṭaḥ | caturhastocchrito dvihastāyataḥ | tatra ca sāravṛkṣodbhavā pañcahastāyatā ubhayataḥ śikyā tulā" |

pitāmahaḥ |

> caturhastā tulā kāryā pādau kāryau tathāvidhau |  
> antaraṃ tu tayor hasto bhaved adhyardham eva vā ||  
> chitvā tu yajñiyaṃ vṛkṣaṃ yūpavan mantrapūrvakam |  
> praṇamya lokapālehyas tulā kāryā manīṣibhiḥ ||

nāradaḥ [4.264–65, 263, 261] |

> khādirāṃ kārayet tatra nivraṇāṃ śuṣkavarjitām |  
> śāṃśapīṃ tadabhāve tu sālāṃ vā koṭarair vinā ||  
> arjunas tilako 'śokas timiśo raktacandanam |  
> evaṃvidhāni kāṣṭhāni dhaṭārthaṃ parikalpayet ||

**[215]**  
> ṛjvī dhaṭatulā kāryā khādinī taindukī tathā |  
> caturasrā tribhiḥ sthānair dhaṭaḥ karkaṭakādibhiḥ |  
> hastadvayaṃ nikheyaṃ tu proktaṃ muṇḍakayos tayoḥ |  
> ṣaḍhastaṃ tu tayoḥ proktaṃ pramāṇaṃ parimāṇataḥ ||

pitāmahaḥ |

> toraṇe tu tathā kārye pārśvayor ubhayor api |  
> dhaṭād uccatare syātāṃ nityaṃ daśabhir aṅgulaiḥ ||  
> avalambau ca kartavyau toraṇābhyām adhomukhau |  
> mṛṇmayau sūtrasaṃbaddhau dhaṭamastakacumbakau ||  
> prāṅmukho niścalaḥ kāryaḥ śucau deśe dhaṭaḥ sadā |  
> indrasthāne sabhāyāṃ vā rājadvāre catuṣpathe ||

nāradaḥ [4.265–67] |

> sabhā-rājakuladvāra-surāyatanacatvare |  
> nakheyo niścalaḥ kāryo gandhamālyānulepanaiḥ ||

**[216]**  
> dadhyakṣatahavirgandhaiḥ kṛtādhyayanamaṅgalaḥ |  
> dharmarakṣārtham āhūtair lokapālair adhiṣṭhitaḥ ||

pitāmahaḥ |

> tatraiva lokapālāṃś ca sarvadikṣu niveśayet |  
> trisaṃdhyaṃ pūjayen nityaṃ dhūpamālyānulepanaiḥ ||  
> lokapālās tathādityā rudrāś ca vasavas tathā |  
> pūjāprabhāvayuktāś ca sāṃnidhyaṃ kalpayanti te ||  
> viśālām ucchritāṃ śuddhāṃ dhaṭaśālāṃ tu kārayet |  
> yatrasthā nopahanyeta śvabhiś cāṇḍālavāyasaiḥ ||  
> kavāṭabījasaṃyuktāṃ paricārakarakṣitām |  
> pānīyāgnisamāyuktām aśūnyāṃ kārayen nṛpaḥ ||  
> dhaṭaṃ tu kārayen nityaṃ patākādhvajaśobhitam |  
> vāditratūryaghoṣaiś ca dhūpamālyānulepanaiḥ ||

nāradaḥ [4.271–72] |

> śikydvayaṃ samāsādya dhaṭakarkaṭayor dṛḍham |  
> ekatra śikye puruṣam anyatra tulayec chilām ||

**[217]**  
> dhārayed uttare pārśve puruṣaṃ dakṣiṇe śilām |  
> piṭikāṃ pūrayet tasmin niṣṭakāyāṃ suloṣṭakaiḥ ||

viṣṇuḥ [10.5]: "tatraikasmin śikye puruṣam āropayet dvitīye pratimānaṃ śilādi" |

pitāmahaḥ |

> śikyadvayaṃ samāsajya pārśvayor ubhayor api |  
> prāgagrān kārayed dharbhāṃs tatra vipraḥ samāhitaḥ ||  
> ekasmin tolayen martyam anyasmin mṛttikāṃ śubhām |  
> iṣṭakābhasmapāṣāṇakapālāsthivivarjitām ||  
> parīkṣakā niyoktavyāḥ tulāmānaviśāradāḥ |  
> vaṇijo hemakārāś ca kāṃsyakārās tathaiva ca ||

tathā |

> kāryaḥ parīkṣakair nityam avalambasamodhaṭaḥ |  
> udakaṃ ca pradātavyaṃ dhaṭasyopari paṇḍitaiḥ ||

**[218]**  
> yasmin na plavate toyaṃ sa vijñeyaḥ samo dhaṭaḥ |

nāradaḥ [4.273, 275] |

> prathamāropaṇe grāhyaṃ pramāṇaṃ nipuṇaiḥ saha |  
> tulāśilābhyāṃ tulyaṃ ca toraṇaṃ nyastalakṣaṇam ||  
> tulayitvā naraṃ pūrvaṃ cihnaṃ kṛtvā dhaṭasya tu |  
> kakṣāsthāne yadā tulyam avatārya tato dhaṭāt ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.100–02] |

> tulādhāraṇavidvadbhir abhiyuktas tulāśritaḥ |  
> pratimānasamībhūto rekhāṃ kṛtvāvatāritaḥ ||  
> tvaṃ tule satyadharmāsi purā devair vinirmitā |  
> tat satyaṃ vada kalyāṇi saṃśayān māṃ vimocaya ||  
> yady asmi pāpakṛn mātas tato māṃ tvam adho naya |  
> śuddhaś ced gamayordhvaṃ māṃ tulām ity abhimantrayet ||

**[219]** **'rekhāṃ kṛtvā'** yena saṃniveśena pratīmānasamīkaraṇadaśāyāṃ yatra pādau sthitau śikyarajjavaś ca tatra pāṇḍulekhyenāṅkayitvā |

pitāmahaḥ |

> tulayitvā naraṃ pūrvaṃ tasmāt tam avatārya ca |  
> prāṅmukhaḥ prāñjalir bhūtvā prāḍvivākas tato vadet ||  
> ehy ehi bhagavan darma divyam etat samāviśa |  
> sahito lokapālais tvaṃ vasvādityamarudgaṇaiḥ ||  
> tasyārtham abhiyuktasya lekhayitvā tu patrakam |  
> mantreṇānena sahitaṃ kuryāt tasya śirogatam ||  
> ādityacandrāv anilānalau ca  
> dyaur bhūmir āpo hṛdayaṃ yamaś ca |  
> ahaś ca rātriś ca ubhe ca saṃdhye   
> dharmaś ca jānāti narasya vṛttam ||  
> imaṃ mantravidhiṃ kṛtsnaṃ sarvadivyeṣu kārayet |  
> āvāhanaṃ ca devānām athaivaṃ parikīrtayet ||

**[220]** > dhaṭa tvaṃ brahmaṇā sṛṣṭaḥ parīkṣārthaṃ durātmanām |  
> dhakārād dharmamūrtis tvaṃ ṭakārāt kuṭilaṃ naram ||  
> bhṛto dhārayase tasmād dhaṭas tenābhidhīyase |

viṣṇuḥ [10.7–11]: "dhaṭaṃ ca samayena gṛhṇīyāt | tulādharaṃ ca |

> dharmaparyāyavacanair dhaṛa ity abhidhīyase |  
> tvam eva dhaṭa jānīṣe na vidur yāni mānavāḥ ||  
> vyavahārābhiśasto 'yaṃ mānuṣas tolyate tvayi |  
> tad enaṃ saṃśayād asmād dharmatas trātum arhasi ||  
> brahmaghnāṃ ye smṛtā lokā ye lokāḥ kūṭasākṣiṇām |  
> tulādhārasya te lokās tulāṃ dhārayato mṛṣā ||  
> [samayena ca gṛhṇīyāt niyamena ca yojayet |  
> upoṣitaṃ tathā snātaṃ mṛṇmayaṃ prathamaṃ tulām ||  
> saṃtolya kārayed evam avatāryānumantrayet |

**'samayena gṛhṇīyāt'** niyamena yojayet | ]

**'tvam eva dhaṭa jānīṣa'** ityādinā **'brahmaghnāṃ ye smṛtā lokā'** ityādinā ca tulāṃ dharayan japed ity arthaḥ |

**[221]** kālikāpurāṇe |

> upoṣitaṃ tathā snātaṃ mṛṇmayaṃ prathamaṃ tulām |  
> saṃtolya kārayed evam avatāryābhimantrayet ||  
> tvaṃ tule satyadhāmāsi pūrvaṃ devena nirmitā |  
> tat satyaṃ vada kalyāṇi modayainaṃ mahāpadaḥ ||  
> yady ayaṃ pāpakṛn mātas tataś cāmum adho naya |  
> śuddhaś ced gamayordhvaṃ ca tulām ity abhimantrayet ||

nāradaḥ [4.276–78, 281, 279] |

> samayaiḥ parigṛhyātha punar āropayen naram |  
> nirvāte vṛṣṭirahite śirasy āropya patrakam ||  
> tasminn eva kṛte kakṣye kakṣāṃ kṛtvā dvijo vadet |  
> dharmaparyāyavacanair dhaṭa ity abhidhīyase ||  
> tvaṃ vetsi sarvabhūtānāṃ pāpāni sukṛtāni ca |  
> tvam eva deva jānīṣe na vidur yāni mānavāḥ ||  
> vyavahārābhiśasto 'yaṃ mānavas taulyate tvayā |  
> tad enaṃ saṃśayārūḍhaṃ dharmatas trātum arhasi ||

**[222]** > devāsuramanuṣyāṇāṃ satye tvam atiricyase |  
> satyasaṃdho 'si bhagavan śubhāśubhavibhāvane ||  
> ādityacandrāv anilānalau ca  
> dyaur bhūmir āpo hṛdayaṃ yamaś ca |  
> ahaś ca rātriś ca ubhe ca saṃdhye   
> dharmaś ca jānāti narasya vṛttam ||

**tasminn eva kṛte kakṣye** iti | kakṣāṃ tulanāṃ maryādākṛtānām eva parīkṣārtham ārohaṇasamaye 'pi kṛtvā dharmaparyāyaśabdenetyādi parīkṣakaḥ paṭhed ity arthaḥ |

pitāmahaḥ |

> tulito yadi vardheta śuddho bhavati dharmataḥ |  
> hīyamāno na śuddhaḥ syād ekeṣāṃ tu samo śuciḥ ||  
> alpapāpa samo jñeyo bahupāpas tu hīyate |  
> dharmagauravamāhātmyād atirikto viśudhyati ||

**[223]** bṛhaspatiḥ [8.49] |

> dhaṭe 'bhiyuktas tulito hīnaś ced dhānim āpnuyāt |  
> tatsamas tu punas taulye vardhito vijayī bhavet ||

vyāsaḥ |

> adhogatir na śudhyeta śudhyaty ūrdhvagatis tathā |  
> samo 'pi na ca śuddhaḥ syād eṣā śuddhir udāhṛtā ||  
> kakṣācchede tulābhaṅge dhaṭakarkaṭayos tathā |  
> rajjucchede 'kṣabhaṅge vā dadyāc chiddhiṃ punar nṛpaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [440] |

> śikyacchede tulābhaṅge tathā cāpi guṇasya vā |  
> śuddhes tu saṃśaye caiva parīkṣeta punar naram ||

**[224]**
## 40 agnividhiḥ
**40 — athāgnividhiḥ**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ [pitāmahaḥ] |

> agner vidhiṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāvac chāstracoditam |  
> kārayen maṇḍalāny aṣṭau purastān navamaṃ tathā ||  
> āgneyaṃ maṇḍalaṃ tv ādyaṃ dvitīyaṃ vāruṇaṃ smṛtam |  
> tṛtīyaṃ vāyudaivatyaṃ caturthaṃ yamadaivatam ||  
> pañcamaṃ tv indradaivatyaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ kauberam ucyate |  
> saptamaṃ somadaivatyam aṣṭamaṃ sarvadaivatam ||  
> purastān navamaṃ yat tu tat mahāpārthivaṃ viduḥ |  
> gomayena kṛtāni syur adbhiḥ paryukṣitāni ca ||  
> dvātriṃśadaṅgulāny āhur maṇḍalān maṇḍalāntaram |  
> kartuḥ samapadaṃ kāryaṃ maṇḍalaṃ tu pramāṇataḥ ||

'mahat' pūrvamaṇḍalebhyo 'dhikaparimāṇam | 'pārthivam' pṛthivīdevatākam |

**[225]** nāradaḥ [4.285–86, 299] |

> ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi vidhim agnes tathottamam |  
> dvātriṃśadaṅgulāny āhur maṇḍalān maṇḍalāntaram ||  
> aṣṭabhir maṇḍalair evam aṅgulānāṃ śatadvayam |  
> caturviṃśatir ākhyātā bhūmes tu parikalpanā ||  
> maṇḍalasy pramāṇaṃ tu kuryāt tatpadasaṃmitam |  
> [na maṇḍalam atikrāmen nāpy arvāk sthāpayet padam ||]

prathamān maṇḍalād avaraṃ ca dvātriṃśadaṅgulaparimitaṃ maṇḍalaṃ tadatiriktaṃ vā maṇḍalāntaram apy evaṃ kāryam | evaṃ gamyabhūmeḥ saptabhir maṇḍalair antarālaṃ śatadvayaṃ caturviṃśatyadhikaṃ saṃpadyate |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.106] |

> ṣoḍaśāṅgulakaṃ jñeyaṃ maṇḍalān maṇḍalāntaram |

**[226]** pitāmahaḥ |

> maṇḍale maṇḍale deyāḥ kuśāḥ śāstrapracoditāḥ |  
> vinyaset tu padaṃ kartā teṣu nityam iti sthitiḥ ||

hārītaḥ |

> prāṅmukhas tatra tiṣṭhec ca prasāritakarāṅguliḥ |  
> ārdravāsāḥ śuciś caiva śirasy āropya patrakam ||

pitāmahaḥ |

> paścime maṇḍale tiṣṭhet prāṅmukhaḥ prāñjaliḥ śuciḥ |  
> lakṣayeyuḥ kṣatādīni hastayos tasya kāriṇaḥ ||

viṣṇuḥ [11.20] |

> karau pramarditavrīhes tasyādāv eva lakṣayet |

nāradaḥ [4.301] |

> hastakṣateṣu sarveṣu kuryād dhasapadāni (?) tu |  
> tāny eva punar ālakṣet taddhastau binducitritau ||

**[227]** tathā [pitāmahaḥ] |

> saptāśvatthasya patrāṇi śamīpatrākṣatāni ca |  
> hastayor nikṣipet tasya tantūn sūtrasya sapta ca ||  
> pippalāj jāyate hy agniḥ pippalo vṛkṣarāṭ smṛtaḥ |  
> tatas tasya palāśāni niyojyāni manīṣibhiḥ ||  
> aṃsrihīnaṃ samaṃ kṛtvā aṣṭāṅgulamayomayam |  
> piṇḍaṃ tu tāpayed agnau pañcāśatpalikaṃ samam ||

**'aṃsrihīnam'** koṇarahitam |

nāradaḥ [277–295??] |

> jātyaiva lohakāro yaḥ kuśalaś cāpi karmaṇi |  
> dṛṣṭaprayogaś caivāgnau tenāgnau taṃ tu tāpayet ||  
> agnivarṇam ayaḥpiṇḍaṃ susphuliṅgaṃ suraktikam |  
> pañcāśatpalikaṃ bhūyaḥ kārayitvā śucir dvijaḥ ||  
> tṛtīyatāpataptaṃ taṃ brūyāt satyapuraskṛtaḥ |  
> śṛṇvimaṃ mānavaṃ dharmaṃ lokapālair adhiṣṭhitam ||

**[228]**
