> tvam agne sarvadevānāṃ pavitraṃ paramaṃ sukham |  
> tvam eva sarvabhūtānāṃ hṛdistho vetsi ceṣṭitam ||  
> satyānrte ca jihvāyās tvattaḥ samupalakṣyate |  
> vedādibhir idaṃ proktaṃ nānyathā kartum arhasi ||  
> anenāsāv idaṃ proktaṃ mithyā cedam asau vadet |  
> sarvathā ca yathā mithyā tathāgniṃ dhārayāmy aham ||  
> sa eṣa tvāṃ dhārayati satyenānena mānavaḥ |  
> satyavākyasya cāsya tvaṃ śīto bhava hutāśana ||  
> mṛṣāvākyasya pāpasya daha hastau ca śāpitaḥ |  
> amum arthaṃ ca patrastham abhiyuktaṃ yathārthataḥ ||  
> saṃśrāvya mūrdhni tasyaiva nyasya deyaṃ yathākramam |

pitāmahaḥ |

> tāpayitvā tataḥ paścād agnim āvāhayec chuciḥ |  
> [āvāhanantu devānāṃ kṛtvā pūrvaṃ vidhānavit ||]  
> tvam agne vedāś catvāras tvaṃ ca yajñeṣu hūyase ||  
> tvaṃ mukhaṃ sarvadevānāṃ tvaṃ mukhaṃ brahmavādinām |  
> udarastho hi bhūtānāṃ tathā vetsi śubhāśubham ||  
> pāpaṃ punāsi vai yasmāt tasmāt pāvaka ucyase |  
> pāpeṣu darśayātmānam arciṣmān bhava pāvaka ||

**[229]**  
> atha vā śuddhabhāveṣu śīto bhava mahābala |  
> āyasaṃ lelihānasya jihvayāpi samādiśet ||

**āyasaṃ lelihānasyeti **| jihvayā lelihānasyāpy āyasayoge tan mantraṃ samādiśed ity arthaḥ |

viṣṇuḥ [11.10–12] |

> abhimantryāsa karayor nyaset taṃ lohapiṇḍakam |  
> tvam agne sarvabhūtānām antaś carasi sākṣivat ||  
> tvam evāgne vijānīṣe na vidur yāni mānavāḥ |  
> vyavahārābhiśasto 'yaṃ mānuṣaḥ śuddhim icchati ||  
> tad enaṃ saṃśayād asmād dharmatas trātum arhasi |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.104–05] |

> tvam agne sarvabhūtānām antaś carasi pāvaka |  
> sākṣivat puṇyapāpebhyo brūhi satyaṃ kave mama ||  
> tasyety uktavato lohaṃ pañcāśatpalikaṃ samam |  
> agnivarṇaṃ nyaset piṇḍaṃ hastayor ubhayor api ||

**[230]** nāradaḥ |

> ity uktvā hastayos tasya pradadyāt piṇḍapāvakam |  
> suprataptaṃ susaṃyuktaṃ visphuliṅgārciruddatam ||  
> piṇḍaṃ gṛhītvā sandaṃśair vidyudjvālāsamaprabham |

pitāmahaḥ |

> tataḥ samam upādāya rājā dharmaparāyaṇaḥ |  
> sandaṃśena niyukto vā hastayos tasya nikṣipet ||

viṣṇuḥ [12.5–7): "tatas tatrāgnivarṇaṃ lohapiṇḍaṃ pañcāśatpalikaṃ dadyāt | tad ādāya nātidrutaṃ na ca vilambitaṃ maṇḍaleṣu padanyāsaṃ kurvan vrajet | tataḥ saptamaṃ maṇḍalam atītya bhūmau lohapiṇḍaṃ pātayet" |

śaṅkhalikhitau: "atha vā saptāśvatthaparṇāntaritaṃ ṣoḍaśapalam agnivarṇaṃ lohapiṇḍaṃ añjalinādāya saptapadamaryādāṃ gacchet" |

nārada (4.293–97, 299) |

> hastābhyāṃ taṃ samādāya prāḍvivākasamīritaḥ |  
> sthitvaikasmiṃs tato 'nyāni vrajet sapta tv ajihmagaḥ ||

**[231]** > asaṃbhrāntaḥ śanair gacched akruddhaḥ so 'nalaṃ prati |  
> na pātayet tām aprāpya yā bhūmiḥ parikalpitā ||  
> na maṇḍalam atikrāmen na cārvāk sthāpayet padam |  
> aṣṭamaṃ maṇḍalaṃ gatvā navame nikṣiped budhaḥ ||

pitāmahaḥ |

> tvaramāṇo na gacchet tu svastho gacchet śanaiḥ śanaiḥ |  
> na maṇḍalam atikrāmet nāntarā sthāpayet padam ||  
> aṣṭamaṃ maṇḍalaṃ gatvā navame nikṣiped budhaḥ |

kālikāpurāṇe |

> maṇḍalāni tathā sapta ṣoḍaśāṅgulamātrataḥ |  
> tāvad antarato gacchet dhṛtvā navatṛṇe kṣipet ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.207] |

> antarā patite piṇḍe saṃdehe vā punar haret |

**[232]** pitāmahaḥ |

> bhayārtaḥ pātayed yas tu vraṇaṃ ca na vibhāvyate |  
> punar ārohayel lohaṃ sthitir eṣā dṛḍhīkṛtā ||

kātyāyanaḥ [441] |

> prajvālenābhiśastaś cet sthānād anyatra dahyate |  
> adagdhaṃ taṃ vidur devās tasya bhūyo 'pi dāpayet ||

pitāmahaḥ |

> tatas taddhastayoḥ prāsyed vrīhīn vā yadi vā yavān |  
> nirviśaṅkena teṣāṃ tu hastābhyāṃ mardane kṛte ||  
> nirvikāre dinasyānte śuddhiṃ tasya vinirdiśet |

nāradaḥ [4.302–03] |

> tasyaivaṃ muktapiṇḍasya kuryāt karanirīkṣaṇam |  
> pūrvadṛṣṭeṣu cihneṣu tato 'nyatrāpi lakṣayet ||  
> maṇḍalaṃ raktasaṅkāśaṃ yatnān yad vāgnisaṃbhavam |  
> so 'viśuddhaḥ suvijñeyo 'satyadharmavyavasthitaḥ ||  
> yadā tu na vibhāvyete dagdhāv iti karau tadā |  
> vrīhīn atiprayatnena saptavārāṃs tu mardayet ||

**[233]** > mardito yadi no dagdhaḥ sabhyair eva viniścitaḥ |  
> mocyaḥ śuddhaḥ sa satkṛtya dagdho daṇḍyo yathākramam ||

viṣṇuḥ [11.8] |

> yo hastayoḥ kvacid dagdhas tam aśuddhaṃ vinirdiśet |  
> na dagdhaḥ sarvathā yas tu sa viśuddho bhaven naraḥ ||

vṛddhaḥ |

> ayas taptaṃ tu pāṇibhyām arkapatrais tu saptabhiḥ |  
> antarhitaṃ haran śuddhas tv adagdhaḥ saptame pade ||

**[234]**

## 41 toyavidhiḥ
atha toyavidhiḥ

tatra pitāmahaḥ |

> toyasyātaḥ pravakṣyāmi vidhiṃ dharmyaṃ sanātanam |  
> maṇḍalaṃ puṣpadhūpābhyāṃ kārayet tu vicakṣaṇaḥ ||  
> śarān saṃpūjayed bhaktyā vaiṣṇavaṃ ca dhanus tathā |  
> maṇḍape puṣpadhūpaiś ca tataḥ karma samācaret ||

kātyāyanaḥ [442] |

> śarāṃs tān āyasair agraiḥ prakurvīta viśuddhaye |  
> veṇukāṇḍamayāṃś caiva kṣeptā ca sudṛḍhaṃ kṣipet ||

pitāmahaḥ |

> kṣeptā ca kṣatriyaḥ kāryas tadvṛttir brāhmaṇo 'pi vā |  
> akrūrahṛdayaḥ śāntaḥ sopavāsas tathā śuciḥ ||  
> iṣūn na prakṣiped vidvān mārute cātidhāvati |  
> viṣame bhūpradeśe ca vṛkṣasthāṇusamākule ||

nāradaḥ [4.307] |

> krūraṃ dhanuḥ saptaśataṃ madhyamaṃ ṣaṭcchataṃ smṛtam |  
> mandaṃ pañcaśataṃ jñeyam eṣa jñeyo dhanur vidhiḥ ||

**[235]** **dhanuḥ saptaśatam** iti | yad dhanuḥ baddhajyaṃ saptabhir palaśataiḥ śarapūrṇaparyantaṃ namati tat tathocyate | evaṃ **ṣaṭcchatam** ityādy api |

pitāmahaḥ |

> madhyamena tu cāpena prakṣipet tu śaratrayam |  
> hastānāṃ tu śate sārdhe lakṣyaṃ kṛtvā vicakṣaṇaḥ ||  
> teṣāṃ ca preṣitānāṃ tu śarāṇāṃ śāstracodanāt |  
> madhyamas tu śaro grāhyaḥ puruṣeṇa balīyasā ||  
> śarāṇāṃ patanaṃ grāhyaṃ sarpaṇaṃ parivarjayet |  
> sarpan sarpan śaro yāti dūrād dūrataraṃ tu saḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [443] |

> kṣiptais tu majjanaṃ kāryaṃ gamanaṃ samakālikam |  
> gamane tv āgamaḥ kāryaḥ pumān anyo jale viśet ||

**kṣiptaiḥ** śaraiḥ |

viṣṇuḥ [12:3–4] | "[abhimantritam ambhaḥ praviśet |] tatsamakālaṃ ca nātikrūramṛdunā dhanuṣā puruṣo 'paraḥ śaramokṣaṃ kuryāt" |

bṛhaspatiḥ [8.62] |

> apsu praviśya puruṣaṃ preṣayet sāyakatrayam |

**[236]** pitāmahaḥ |

> sthire toye nimajjet tu na grāhiṇi na cālpake |  
> tṛṇaśaivālarahite jalaukāmatsyavarjite ||  
> devakhāteṣu yat toyaṃ tasmin kuryād viśodhanam |  
> āhāryaṃ varjayet toyaṃ śīghraveganadīṣu ca ||

**'grāhiṇi'** grāhākhyaprāṇiyukte |

nāradaḥ [4.305] |

> nadīṣu nātivegāsu taṭāgeṣu saraḥsu ca |  
> hradeṣu sthiratoyeṣu kuryāt puṃsāṃ nimajjanam ||

viṣṇuḥ [12.2–3]: "paṅkaśaivāladuṣṭagrāhamatsyajalaukādivarjite 'mbhasi | tatrānābhimagnasyārāgadveṣiṇaḥ puruṣasyānyasya jānunī gṛhītvābhimantritam ambhaḥ praviśet" |

nāradaḥ [4.308] |

> brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyo rāgadveṣavivarjitaḥ |  
> nābhimātrajale sthāpyaḥ puruṣaḥ sthāṇuvad balī ||  
> tasyoruṃ pratigṛhyātha nimajjed abhiśāpavān |

**[237]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.108] |

> satyena mābhirakṣava varuṇety abhiśāpya kam |  
> nābhidaghnodakasthasya gṛhītvoruṃ jalaṃ viśet ||

**'abhiśāpya'** śapathaṃ kārayitvā | **'kam'** pānīyam |

viṣṇuḥ [12.7–8] |

> tvam ambhaḥ sarvabhūtānām antaś carasi sākṣivat |  
> tvam evāmbho vijānīṣe na vidur yāni mānavāḥ ||  
> vyavahārābhiśasto 'yaṃ mānuṣas tvayi majjati |  
> tad enaṃ saṃśayād asmād dharmatas trātum arhasi ||

pitāmahaḥ |

> toya tvaṃ prāṇināṃ prāṇaḥ sṛṣṭer ādyaṃ tu nirmitam |  
> śuddhes tvaṃ kāraṇaṃ proktaṃ dravyāṇāṃ dehināṃ tathā ||  
> atas tvaṃ darśayātmānaṃ śubhāśubhaparīkṣaṇe |

nāradaḥ [4.316–17] |

> satyānṛtavibhāgasya toyāgnī spaṣṭakṛttamau |  
> adbhyaś cāgnir abhūd yasmāt tasmāt toye viśeṣataḥ ||  
> kriyate dharmatattvajñair dūṣitānāṃ viśodhanam |  
> tasmāt satyena bhagavan jaleśa trātum arhasi ||

**[238]** kālikāpurāṇe |

> pāhy enaṃ varuṇa tvaṃ hi asmād evābhiśāpataḥ |  
> śuddhaś ced atikāruṇyād abhimantrya jale kṣipet ||  
> nābhimātrodakasthasya puruṣasyoruṃ pragṛhya vai |  
> praṇamya devatām iṣṭāṃ tasmin magno jale viśet ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: "sad asac ca tvam eva varuṇa ubhayoḥ pratitiṣṭhataḥ | tvayi satyaṃ tv idaṃ deva, varuṇa, tvam eva tad brūhi vareṇyaṃ tad ādiśasva" iti |

pitāmaha-nāradau |

> śaraprakṣepaṇasthānād yuvā javasamanvitaḥ |  
> gacchet paramayā śaktyā yatrāsau madhyamaḥ śaraḥ ||  
> madhayamaṃ śaram ādāya puruṣo 'nyas tathāvidhaḥ |  
> pratyāgacchet tu vegena yataḥ sa puruṣo gataḥ ||  
> āgatas tu śaragrāhī na paśyati yadā jale |  
> antarjalagataṃ samyak tadā śuddhiṃ vinirdiśet ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [8.61] |

> ānīte madhyame cāpe magnāṅgaḥ śucitām iyāt |

**[239]** pitāmaha-nāradau |

> anyathā na viśuddhaḥ syād ekāṅgasyāpi darśanāt |  
> sthānād vānyatra gamanād yasmin pūrvaṃ niveśitaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [444-45] |

> śiromātraṃ tu dṛśyeta na karṇau nāpi nāsikā |  
> apsu praveśane yasya śuddhaṃ tam api nirdiśet ||  
> nimajyotplavate yas tu dṛṣṭaś cet prāṇinā naraḥ |  
> punas tatra nimajjyet sa deśacihnavibhāvitaḥ ||

**[240]**

## 42 viṣavidhiḥ
atha viṣavidhiḥ

tatra nāradaḥ [4.318–21] |

> ataḥ paraṃ pravkṣyāmi viṣasya vidhim uttamam |  
> yasmin kāle yadā deyaṃ yādṛśaṃ ca prakīrtitam ||  
> yāvanmātraṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ dharmatattvārthdarśibhiḥ |  
> tualayitvā śaratkāle deyam etad dhimāgame ||  
> nāparāhṇe na madhyāhne na saṃdhyāyāṃ ca dharmavit |  
> śaradgrīṣmavasanteṣu varṣāsu ca vivarjayet ||  
> bhagnaṃ ca dhāritaṃ caiva dhūpitaṃ miśritaṃ tathā |  
> kālakūṭam alābuṃ ca viṣaṃ yatnena varjayet ||

pitāmahaḥ |

> cāritāny atijīrṇāni kṛtrimāṇi tathaiva ca |  
> bhūmijāni ca sarvāṇi viṣāṇi parivarjayet ||  
> oṣadhīr mantrayogāṃś ca maṇīn anyaviṣāpahān |  
> kartuḥ śarīrasaṃsthāṃś ca gūḍhān anyān parīkṣayet ||

**[241]** kātyāyanaḥ [446–49] |

> ajaśaṅganibhaṃ śyāmaṃ supītaṃ śṛṅgasaṃbhavam |  
> bhaṅge ca śṛṅgaverābhaṃ khyātaṃ tac chṛṅgiṇāṃ viṣam ||  
> raktaṃ tad asitaṃ kuryāt kaṭhinaṃ caiva tatkṣaṇāt |  
> anena vidhinā jñeyaṃ viṣaṃ divyaviśāradaiḥ ||  
> vatsanābhinibhaṃ pītaṃ varṇajñānena niścayaḥ |  
> śuktiśṛṅgākṛtir bhaṅge vidyāt tad vatsanābhakam ||  
> madhukṣīrasamāyuktaṃ svacchaṃ kurvīta tatkṣaṇāt |  
> bāhyam evaṃ samākhyātaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ dharmasādhakaiḥ ||

nāradaḥ [3.322] |

> śārṅgaṃ haimavataṃ śastaṃ varṇagandharasānvitam |  
> akṛtrimam asaṃgūḍhamantropahataṃ ca yat ||

pitāmahaḥ |

> yavāḥ sapta pradātavyāḥ śuddhihetor asaṃśayam |  
> śṛṅgiṇo vatsanābhasya himajasya viṣasya vā ||

nāradaḥ [4.324] |

> varṣāsu ṣaḍyavā mātrā grīṣme pañca yavāḥ smṛtāḥ |  
> hemante vā sapta yavāḥ śarady alpās tato 'pi hi ||

**[242]** kātyāyanaḥ [450] |

> pūrvāhṇe śītale deśe viṣaṃ dadyāt tu dehinām |  
> ghṛtena yojitaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ piṣṭaṃ triṃśadguṇena tu ||

śaṅkha-nāradau |

> dadyād viṣaṃ sopavāsaḥ devabrāhmaṇasaṃnidhau |  
> dhūpopahāramantraiś ca pūjayitvā maheśvaram ||  
> dvijānāṃ saṃnidhāv eva dakṣiṇābhimukhe sthite |  
> udaṅmukhaḥ prāṅmukho vā dadyād vipraḥ samāhitaḥ ||

pitāmahaḥ |

> dīyamānaṃ kare kṛtvā viṣaṃ tu pariśodhayet |  
> viṣa tvaṃ brāhaṇā [brahmaṇā?] sṛṣṭaḥ parīkṣārthaṃ durātmanām ||  
> pāpeṣu darśayāmānaṃ śuddhānām amṛtī bhava |

viṣṇuḥ [13.6–7] |

> viṣatvād viṣamatvāc ca krūratvāt sarvadehinām |  
> tvam eva viṣa jānīṣe na vidur yāni mānavāḥ ||

**[243]** > vyavahārābhiśavto 'yaṃ mānuṣaḥ śuddhim icchati |  
> tad enaṃ saṃśayād asmād dharmatas trātum arhasi ||

nāradaḥ [4.325] |

> viṣa tvaṃ brahmaṇaḥ putraḥ satyadharmavyavasthitaḥ |  
> śodhayainaṃ naraṃ pāpāt satyenāsyāmrto bhava ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.110–11] |

> viṣa tvaṃ brahmaṇaḥ putraḥ satyadharmavyavasthitaḥ |  
> trāyasvāsmād abhīśapāt satyena bhava me 'mṛtam ||  
> evam uktvā viṣaṃ śārṅgaṃ bhakṣayed dhimaśailajam ||

nāradaḥ [4.326] |

> chāyāniveśito rakṣyo dinaśeṣam abhojanaḥ |  
> viṣavegaklamātītaḥ śuddho 'sau manur abravīt |

pitāmahaḥ |

> bhakṣite tu yadā svastho mūrcchācchardivivarjitaḥ |  
> nirvikāro dinasyānte taṃ śuddham iti nirdiśet 

**[244]** viṣṇuḥ [12.5] |

> viṣaṃ vegakramāpetaṃ sukhena yadi jīryate |  
> visuddhaṃ tam iti jñātvā divasānte visarjayet |

bṛhaspatiḥ [8.64] |

> vidhidattaṃ viṣaṃ yena jīrṇaṃ mantrauṣadhair vinā |  
> sa śuddhaḥ syād anyathā tu daṇḍyo dāpyaś ca tad dhanam ||

pitāmahaḥ |

> trirātraṃ pañcarātraṃ vā puruṣaiḥ svair adhiṣṭhitam |  
> kuhakāśaṅkayā rājā dhārayed divyakāriṇam ||

**[245]**

## 43 kośavidhiḥ
atha kośavidhiḥ

tatra nāradaḥ [4.327–28] |

> ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi kośasya vidhim uttamam |  
> śāstravidbhir yathā proktaṃ sarvakālāvirodhinam ||  
> pūrvāhṇe sopavāsasya snātasyārdrapaṭasya ca |  
> saśūkasyāvyasininaḥ kośapānaṃ vidhīyate ||  
> icchataḥ śraddadhānasya devabrāhmaṇasaṃnidhau |

**'saśūko'** 'tra satyena divyakaraṇe niḥśaṅkavān |

pitāmahaḥ |

> bhakto yo yasya devasya pāyayet tasya taj jalam |  
> samabhāve tu devānām ādityasya ca pāyayet ||  
> durgāyāḥ pāyayec corān ye ca śastropajīvinaḥ |  
> bhāskarasya ca yat toyaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ tan na pāyayet ||

**[246]** > durgāyāḥ snāpayec chūlam ādityasya ca maṇḍalam |  
> itareṣāṃ tu devānāṃ snāpayed āyudhāni tu ||  
> prāṅmukhaṃ kāriṇaṃ kṛtvā pāyayat prasṛtitrayam |  
> pūrvoktena vidhānena snātam ārdrapaṭaṃ śucim ||

**'samabhāve'** devatāviṣayakabhaktisāmya ity arthaḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ [8.66] |

> yadbhaktaḥ so 'bhiyuktaḥ syāt tad evāyudhamaṇḍalam |  
> prakṣālya pāyayet tasmāj jalāt tu prasṛtitrayam ||

viṣṇuḥ [14.2–3]: "ugrān devān samabhyarcya tatsnānodakāt prasṛtitrayaṃ pibet | idaṃ mayā na kṛtam iti vyāharan devatābhimukhaḥ" |

nāradaḥ |

> arcayitvā tu taṃ devaṃ prakṣālya salilena ca |  
> enaś ca śrāvayitvā tu pāyayet (?) prasṛtitrayam ||

kātyāyanaḥ [452] |

> svalpe 'parādhe devānāṃ snāpayitvāyudhodakam |  
> pāyyo vikāre cāśuddho niyamyaḥ śucir anyathā ||

"**pāyyaḥ**" pāyayitavyaḥ | "**niyamyo**" daṇdayitavyaḥ |

**[247]** viṣṇuḥ [14.4] |

> yasya paśyed dvisaptāhāt trisaptāhād athāpi vā |  
> rogo 'gnir jñātimaraṇaṃ rājātaṅkam athāpi vā ||  
> tam aśuddhaṃ vijānīyāt tathā śuddhaṃ viparyaye |

pitāmahaḥ |

> trirātrāt saptarātrād vā trisaptāhād athāpi vā |  
> vaikṛtaṃ yasya dṛśyeta pāpakṛ sa tu mānavaḥ ||  
> tasyaikasya na sarvasya janasya yadi tad bhavet |  
> rogo 'gnir jñātimaraṇaṃ saiva tasya vibhāvanā ||

kātyāyanaḥ [456–58] |

> atha devavisaṃvādāt trisaptāhāt tu dāpayet |  
> abhiyuktaṃ prayatnena tam arthaṃ daṇḍam eva ca ||  
> tasyaikasya na sarvasya janasya yadi tad bhavet |  
> rogo 'gnir jñātimaraṇaṃ ṛṇaṃ dadyād damaṃ ca saḥ ||

**[248]** > jvarātisāravisphoṭāḥ śūlādiparipīḍanam |  
> netraruggalarogaś ca tathonmādaḥ prajāyate ||  
> śirorug bhujabhaṅgaś ca daivikavyādhayo nṛṇām |

"**daivavisaṃvādaḥ**" daivakṛto rogajñātimaraṇādirūpo virodhaḥ |

nāradaḥ [4.331] |

> ūrdhvaṃ yasya dvisaptāhād vaikṛtaṃ sumahad bhavet |  
> nābhiyojyaḥ sa viduṣā kṛtakālavyatikramāt ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.113] |

> arvāk caturdaśād ahno yasya no rājadaivikam |  
> vyasanaṃ jāyate ghoraṃ sa viśuddho na saṃśayaḥ ||

**[249]** "**vyasanam**" āpat | "**ghoram**" atipīḍākaram |

bṛhaspatiḥ [8.65] |

> saptāhād vā dvisaptāhād yasyārtir na prajāyate |  
> putradāradhanānāṃ ca viśuddhaḥ syān na saṃśayaḥ ||

atra ca dvyahasaptāhatrisaptāhapratīkṣaṇe vyavasthā deśakālaviṣayatāratamyāpekṣayety avagantavyā |

kātyāyanaḥ [454] |

> avaṣṭambhābhiyuktasya viśuddhasyāpi kośataḥ |  
> sadaṇḍam abhiyogaṃ tu dāpayed abhiyojakam ||

viṣṇuḥ [14.5]

> divyena śuddhaṃ puruṣaṃ satkuryād dhārmiko nṛpaḥ |

nāradaḥ [4.333] |

> yathoktena vidhānena pañca divyāni kārayet |  
> tatra rājābhiśastānāṃ pretya ceha ca nandati ||

**[250]**

## 44 taṇḍulavidhiḥ
atha taṇḍulavidhiḥ

tatra pitāmahaḥ |

> taṇḍulānāṃ pravakṣyāmi vidhiṃ bhakṣaṇavarjane |  
> śūdre tu taṇḍulā deyā nānyatreti viniścayaḥ ||  
> taṇḍulān kārayec chuklān śāler nāyasya kasyacit |  
> mṛnmaye bhājane kṛtvā ādityasyāgrataḥ śuciḥ ||  
> snānodakena saṃmiśrān rātrau tatraiva vāsayet |  
> prabhāte kāriṇo deyo ādityābhimukhasya tu ||  
> taṇḍulān bhakṣayitvā tu patre niṣṭhīvayed divā |  
> bhūryasyaiva tu nānyasya abhāve pippalasya ca ||

**[251]** kātyāyanaḥ [453] |

> devatāsnānapānīyadigdhataṇḍulabhakṣaṇe |  
> śuddhaniṣṭhīvanāc chuddho niyamyo 'śucir anyathā ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [8.70] |

> sopavāsaḥ sūryagrahe taṇḍulān bhakṣayec chuciḥ |  
> śuddhaḥ syāc chuklaniṣṭhīve raktamiśre ca doṣabhāk ||

bṛhaspati-pitāmahau |

> śoṇitaṃ dṛśyate yasya hanujālaṃ ca sīdati |  
> gātraṃ ca kampate yasya tam aśuddhaṃ vinirdiśet ||

**'hanujālam'** uttarādharavāmadakṣiṇahanusamūhaḥ |

**[252]**

## 45 taptamāṣakavidhiḥ
atha taptamāṣakavidhiḥ

tatra pitāmahaḥ |

> taptamāṣasya vakṣyāmi vidhim uddhareṇe śubham |  
> kārayed āyasaṃ pātraṃ tāmraṃ vā ṣoḍaśāṅgulam ||  
> caturaṅgulakhātaṃ mṛnmayaṃ vāpi maṇḍalam |  
> pūrayed ghṛtatailābhyāṃ viṃśatyā vā palais tataḥ ||  
> sutapte nikṣipet tatra suvarṇasya tu māṣakam |  
> aṅguṣṭhāṅguliyogena taptamāṣaṃ samuddharet ||

**'maṇḍalam'** vartulam |

bṛhaspatiḥ [8.72] |

> samuddharet tailaghṛtāt sutapāt taptamāṣakam |  
> aṅguṣṭhāṅguliyogena satyam āmantrya vītabhīḥ ||

**'satyam āmantrya'** 'ehy ehi bhagavan dharma' ityādimantreṇa dharmaṃ saṃśodhya |

pitāmaha-bṛhaspatī |

> karāgraṃ na dhuned yas tu visphoṭo vā na jāyate |  
> śuddho bhavati dharmeṇa pitāmahavaco yathā ||

kālikāpurāṇe |

> na dhuned yaḥ karāgraṃ tu yasya raktaṃ na jāyate |  
> visphoṭādyais tathā doṣaiḥ sa śuddho yasya cojjhitam ||

**[253]**

## 46 phālavidhiḥ
atha phālavidhiḥ

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ [8.79–80] |

> āyasaṃ dvādaśapalaṃ ghaṭitaṃ phālam ucyate |  
> aṣṭāṅgulaṃ bhaved dīrghaṃ caturṅgulavistaram ||  
> agnivarṇaṃ tu tac coro jihvayā lehayet sakṛt |  
> na dagdhaś cec chuddhim iyād anyathā tu sa hīyate ||

**[254]**

## 47 dharmajavidhiḥ
atha dharmajavidhiḥ

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ [8.82–85] |

> patradvaye lekhanīyau dharmādharmau sitāsitau |  
> jīvadānādikair mantrair gāyatryādyaiś ca sāmabhiḥ ||  
> āmantrya pūjayed gandhaiḥ kusumaiś ca sitāsitaiḥ |  
> abhyukṣya pañcagavyena mṛtpiṇḍāntaritau tataḥ ||  
> samau kṛtvā nave kumbhe sthāpyau cānupalaṣitau |  
> tataḥ kumbhāt piṇḍam ekaṃ pragṛhṇītāvilambitaḥ ||  
> dharma gṛhīte śuddhaḥ syāt saṃpūjyaś ca parīkṣakaiḥ |

**'jīvadānādikaiḥ'** 'mā pragāmapatho vayam' ityādimantraiḥ |

**[255]**

## 48 śapathavidhiḥ
atha śapathavidhiḥ

tatra manuḥ [8.110] |

> maharṣibhiś ca devaiś ca kāryārthaṃ śapathāḥ kṛtāḥ |  
> vasiṣṭhaś cāpi śapathaṃ śepe paijavane nṛpe ||

nāradaḥ [4.243–44] |

> śapathā hy api devānām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca mahātmanām |  
> vasiṣṭhaḥ śapathaṃ śepe yātudhāne tu śabditaḥ ||  
> maharṣayas tathendrādyāḥ prastarārthe nibodhitāḥ |  
> śepuḥ śapatham avyagrāḥ parasparaviśuddhaye ||

viṣṇuḥ [9.4–14]: "sarveṣv apy arthajāteṣu mūlyaṃ kanakaṃ prakalpayet | tac ca kṛṣṇalone śūdraṃ dūrvākaraṃ śāpayet | dvikṛṣṇalone tilakaram | trikṣṭṇalone rajatakaram | catuḥkṛṣṇalone suvarṇakaram | pañcakṛṣṇalone sītoddhṛtamahīkaram | suvarṇārdhone kośo deyaḥ śūdrasya | tataḥ paraṃ yathārhaṃ dhaṭāgnyudakaviṣāṇām anyatamam | **[256]** dviguṇārthe yathābhihitā samayakriyā vaiśyasya | triguṇārthe rājanyasya | caturguṇārthe brāhmaṇasya" |

**'kṛṇalone'** kṛṣṇalāvare | evaṃ dvikṛṣṇalona ityādy api boddhavyam |

manuḥ [8.113–14] |

> satyena śāpayed vipraṃ kṣatriyaṃ vāhanāyudhaiḥ |  
> gobījakāñcanair vaiśyaṃ śūdraṃ sarvais tu pātakaiḥ ||  
> putradārasya cāpy enaṃ śirāṃsi sparśayet pṛthaṅ |

bṛhaspatiḥ [8.33–34] |

> satyaṃ vāhanaśastrāṇi gobījakanakāni ca |  
> devabrāhmaṇapādāṃs tu putradāraśirāṃsi ca ||  
> ete tu śapathāḥ proktāḥ svalpe 'rthe sukarāḥ sadā |  
> sāhaseṣv abhiśāpeṣu divyāṇy āhur viśodhanam ||

nāradaḥ [4.248–250] |

> satyaṃ vāhanaśastrāṇi gobījakanakāni ca |  
> devatāpitṛpādāṃś ca dattāni sukṛtāni ca ||  
> ity ete śapathāḥ proktā manunā svalpakāraṇe |  
> pātakeṣv abhiśāpe ca vidhir divyeṣu kīrtitaḥ ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: "iṣṭāpūrtapradānam anyāṃś ca śapathān kārayet" |

**[257]** manuḥ [8.115] |

> yam iddho na dahaty agnir āpo nonmajjayanti ca |  
> na cārtim ṛcchati kṣipraṃ sa jñeyaḥ śapathe śuciḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [463] |

> ā caturdaśakālād ahno yasya no rājadaivakam |  
> vyasanaṃjāyate ghoraṃ sa jñeyaḥ śapathe śuciḥ ||

manuḥ [8.111–12] |

> na vṛthā śapathaṃ kuryāt svalpe 'py arthe naro budhaḥ |  
> vṛthā hi śapathaṃ kurvan pretya ceha ca naśyati ||  
> kāminīṣu vivāheṣu gavāṃ bhukte tathendhane |  
> brāhmaṇābhyupapattau ca śapathe nāsti pātakam ||

yamaḥ |

> kṛtvā mṛṣā tu śapathaṃ kīṭasya vadhasaṃyutam |  
> anṛtena tu yujyeta vadhena ca tathā naraḥ ||  
> tasmān na mithāśapathaṃ naraḥ kuryād yathepsitam ||

**iti bhaṭṭahṛdayadharātmajamahāsāndhivgrahika-**

**śrīmallakṣmīdharaviracite kṛtyakalpatarau**

**vyavahārakāṇde kriyāpādaḥ ||**

**[258]**

## 49 nirṇayaprakāraḥ
atha nirṇayaprakāraḥ

tatra vyāsaḥ |

> pramāṇair hetucaritaiḥ śapathena nṛpājñayā |  
> vādisaṃpratipatyā vā nirṇayo 'ṣṭavidhaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
> likhitaṃ sākṣiṇo bhuktiḥ pramāṇaṃ trividhaṃ smṛtam |  
> anumānaṃ vidur hetus tarkaś ceti manīṣiṇaḥ ||  
> daśesthitiḥ pūrvakṛtā caritaṃ samudāhṛtam |  
> arthānurūpāḥ śapathāḥ smṛtāḥ satyadhaṭādayaḥ ||  
> teṣām abhāve rājājñā nirṇayaṃ tad vidur budhāḥ |

**anumānam** iti | tarko 'numānaṃ nirṇayahetur iti manyanta ity arthaḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ [9.1] |

> dharmeṇa vyavahāreṇa cāritreṇa nṛpājñayā |  
> catuṣprakāro 'bhihitaḥ saṃdigdhe vastunirṇayaḥ ||  
> ekaiko dvividhaḥ proktaḥ kriyābhedān maharṣibhiḥ |  
> samyag vicārya kāryaṃ tu yuktyā saṃparikalpitam ||  
> parīkṣitaṃ tu śapathaiḥ sa jñeyo dharmanirṇayaḥ |  
> prativādī prapadyeta yatra dharmaḥ sa nirṇayaḥ ||  
> divyair viśodhitaḥ samyak dvitīyaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ |

**[259]** kātyāyanaḥ [36] |

> smṛtiśāstraṃ tu yat kiṃcit kathitaṃ dharmasādhakaiḥ |  
> kāryāṇāṃ nirṇayārtheṣu vyavahāraḥ smṛto hi saḥ ||

'**smṛtiśāstra**'śabdenātra smṛtiśāstroktasākṣyādīni pramāṇāny ucyante |

bṛhaspatiḥ [9.5] |

> pramāṇaniścito yas tu vyavahāraḥ sa ucyate |  
> vākchalānuttaratvena dvitīyaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ||

**'vākchalānuttaratvena'** vākchalatvena niścito anuttaratvena ca niścito dvitīyo vyavahāra ity arthaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [37] |

> yad yad ācaryate yena dharmyaṃ vādharmyam eva vā |  
> deśasyācaraṇān nityaṃ caritraṃ tat parikīrtitam ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [9.6] |

> anumānena nirṇītaṃ caritram iti kathyate |  
> deśasthityā dvitīyas tu śāstravidbhir udāhṛtaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [38, dvitīye] |

> saṃdigdhā yena sādhyante niścitaṃ śāstrato bhṛguḥ |  
> teṣāṃ nṛpaḥ pramāṇaṃ syāt sarvasya hi nṛpaḥ prabhuḥ ||  
> nyāyaśāstrāvirodhena deśadṛṣṭais tathaiva ca |  
> yaṃ dharmyaṃ sthāpayed rājā nyāyyaṃ tad rājaśāsanam ||

**[260]** > dharmaṃ ca vyavahāraṃ ca caritraṃ vāvilopayan |  
> sthityaitat sthāpayed rājā dharmyaṃ tad rājaśāsanam ||

**'avilopayan'** aparityajann api |

bṛhaspatiḥ [9.7] |

> pramāṇasahitādyas tu rājājñā nirṇayaḥ smṛtaḥ |  
> śāstrasabhyavirodhena tathānyaḥ saṃprakīrtitaḥ ||

**'pramāṇasahitā rājājñā ādyo nirṇaya'** iti yojanā | **'sabhyaśāstravirodhe'** sabhyānāṃ śāstrāṇāṃ ca parasparavipratipattau |

nāradaḥ [1.11] |

> tatra satye sthito dharmo vyavahāraś ca sākṣiṣu |  
> caritaṃ pustakaraṇe rājājñāyāṃ tu śāsanam ||

bṛhaspatiḥ |

> yatraivaṃ vetti nṛpatiḥ nirṇayaṃ tu caturvidham |  
> so 'smiṃś loke yaśaḥ prāpya yāti śakralokatām ||

**[261]**

## 50 nirṇayabalābalam
atha nirṇayabalābalam

nāradaḥ [1.10] |

> dharmaś ca vyavahāraś ca caritraṃ rājaśāsanam |  
> catuṣpād vyavahāro 'yam uttaraḥ pūrvabādhakaḥ ||

**'uttaraḥ pūrvabādhakaḥ'** iti | dharmavyavahāracaritrarājaśāsaneṣu utattrottaraḥ pūrvasya bādhaka ity arthaḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ [1.19] |

> śāstraṃ kevalam āśritya kriyate yatra nirṇayaḥ |  
> vyavahāraḥ sa vijñeyo dharmas tenāvahīyate ||

kātyāyanaḥ [39] |

> yuktiyuktaṃ tu kāryaṃ syād divyaṃ yatra vivarjitam |  
> dharmas tu vyavahāreṇa bādhyate tatra nānyathā ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [1.20] |

> deśasthityānumānena naigamānumatena ca |  
> kriyate nirṇayas tatra vyavahāras tu bādhyate ||

**'naigamāḥ'** paurāḥ vaṇijaḥ | **'anumānena naigamānumatena'** ity saṃbandhaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [40–41] |

> pratilomaprasūteṣu tathā durganivāsiṣu |  
> viruddhaṃ niyataṃ prāhus taṃ dharmaṃ na vicālayet ||

**[262]** > nirṇayaṃ tu yadā kuryāt tena dharmeṇa pārthivaḥ |  
> vyavahāraś caritreṇa tadā tenaiva bādhyate ||

**'tena dharmeṇa'** deśācārarūpeṇa |

bṛhaspatiḥ [1.21] |

> vihāya caritācāraṃ yat tu kuryāt punar nṛpaḥ |  
> nirṇayaṃ sā tu rājājñā caritraṃ bādhyate tathā ||

**'caritācāram'** pūrvapūrvācaritam ācāram |

kātyāyanaḥ [42, 43] |

> viruddhaṃ nyāyato yat tu caritraṃ kalpyate nṛpaiḥ |  
> evaṃ tatra nirasyeta caritraṃ tu nṛpājñayā ||  
> anena vidhinā proktaṃ bādhakaṃ yad yad uttaram |  
> anyathā bādhanaṃ yatra tatra dharmo vihanyate ||

**iti nirṇayaprakāraḥ |**

**[263]**

## 51 nirṇītakṛtyam
atha nirṇītakṛtyam

tatra nāradaḥ [2.41] |

> svayam abhyupapanno 'pi sucaryāvasito 'pi san |  
> kriyāvasanno 'py arhet tu paraṃ sabhyāvadhāraṇam ||  
> sabhyair eva kṛtā paścād rājñā śāsyaḥ svaśāstravat |

**'svayam abhyupapannaḥ'** svayam aṅgīkṛtaparājayaḥ | 'sucaryāvasitaḥ' sucetṣṭayā vaivarṇyasvedakampādikayā parājitatvena jñātaḥ | **'kriyāvasannaḥ'** kriyayā sākṣidivyādikayā prāptāvasādaḥ | **'paraṃ sabhyāvadhāraṇam'** anantaraṃ sabhyānām ekasthānām anenāvasādanena parājita iti kīrtanam |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.11] |

> nirṇayaṃ bhāvito dadyād dhanaṃ rājñe ca tatsamam |  
> mithyābhiyoge dviguṇam abhiyogād dhanaṃ vahet ||

**[264]** manuḥ [8.51, 59] |

> arthe 'pavyayamānaṃ tu karaṇena vibhāvitam |  
> dāpayed dhanikasyārthaṃ daṇḍaleśaṃ ca śaktitaḥ ||  
> yo yāvan nihnuvītārthaṃ mithyāṃ yāvati vādayet |  
> tau nṛpeṇa hy adharmajñau dāpyau taddviguṇaṃ damam ||

**'apavyayamānam'** apanihnuvānam | **'karaṇena'** likhitādinā | **'yo yāvat tau'** iti | yo yāvantam apajānīte adhamarṇaḥ, mithyāṃ vā yāvati dhane abhiyuñjīta tāv ubhāv apy uttamarṇāv āśayadoṣeṇa vivādavṛttau dviguṇaṃ daṇḍaṃ dāpyāv ity arthaḥ | āśayadoṣavyatirekeṇa tu dāridryavismaraṇādināpahnavaviṣaye daṇḍaleśaṃ ca śaktitaḥ ity avagantavyam |

vyāsaḥ |

> nihnave tu yadā vādī svayaṃ tat pratipadyate |  
> jñeyā sā pratipattis tu tasyārdhavinayaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

nāradaḥ [2.37] |

> mithyābhiyogino ye syuḥ dvijānāṃ śūdrayonayaḥ |  
> teṣāṃ jihvāṃ samutkṛtya rājā śūle niveśayet ||

**[265]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.20] |

> nihnute likhitaṃ naikaṃ ekadeśavibhāvitaḥ |  
> dāpyaḥ sarvaṃ nṛpeṇārthaṃ na grāhyas tv aniveditaḥ ||

yadā naikaṃ suvarṇarajata[tāmrādilikhitam abhiyuktas san **'nihnute'** punar api tadaikadeśe suvarṇādau śāstrādibhiḥ vādī **'vibhāvitaḥ'** aṅgīkāritaḥ uddharet rājñā sarvān rajatādyarthān dāpyaḥ | tatrāpi] **'na grāhyas tv aniveditaḥ'** pūrvoddeśena deym iti yady abhiyoktrā pūrvabhāṣākāle 'nupanuyasto 'rthaḥ ekadeśavibhāvitatve 'py abhiyoktā na grāhayitavya ity arthaḥ |

nāradaḥ |

> anekārthābhiyuktena sarvārthavyapalāpinā |  
> vibhāvitaikadeśena deyaṃ yad abhiyujyate ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.18] |

> sapaṇaś ced vivādaḥ syāt tadgṛhītaṃ tu dāpayet |  
> sa daṇḍaṃ dviguṇaṃ caiva dhanine dhanam eva ca ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [9.25] |

> aparādhānurūpaś ca daṇḍo 'yaṃ parikalpitaḥ |

**[266]**

## 52 jayipratipattiḥ
atha jayīpratipattiḥ

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ [9.21] |

> pratijñābhāvanād vādī prāḍvivākādipūjanāt |  
> jayapatrasya cādānāj jayī loke nigadyate ||

kātyāyanaḥ [262] |

> siddhenārthena saṃyojyo vādī satkārapūrvakam |  
> lekhyaṃ svahastasaṃyuktaṃ tasmai dadyāt tu pārthivaḥ ||

vyāsaḥ |

> vyavahārān svayaṃ dṛṣṭvā śrutvā vā prāḍvivākataḥ |  
> jayapatraṃ tato dadyāt parijñānāya pārthivaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [264] |

> nirastaṃ likhitaṃ yat tu tat tu sadyo vināśayet |  
> paścātkārakriyā cātha nirasyet tan na saṃśayaḥ ||  
> nirastā tu kriyā yatra pramāṇenaiva vādinā |  
> paścātkāro bhavet tatra na sarvāsu vidhīyate ||  
> dāsastrībhūgṛhārāmalekhakānāṃ parājaye |  
> eteṣv eva yadā deyaḥ paścātkāras tu pārthivaiḥ ||

**'paścātkāro'** nirṇayānantarajayapatrādikā kriyā | **'pramāṇam'** sākṣyādi | **'eteṣv eva'** ity upalakṣaṇam |

**[267]**

## 53 punarnyāyaḥ
atha punarnyāyaḥ

tatra manuḥ [9.233] |

> tīritaṃ cānuśiṣṭaṃ ca yatra kvacana yad bhavet |  
> kṛtaṃ tad dharmato vidyān na tad bhūyo nivartayet ||

**'tīritam'** iti 'pāratīrakarmasamāptau' ity asya niṣṭhāpratyaye rūpam | tena nirṇīya samāpitam ity arthaḥ | **'anuśiṣṭaṃ'** sākṣibhir uktam | **'yatra kvacana'** grāmādisabhāyām |

nāradaḥ [1.65] |

> tīritaṃ cānuśiṣṭaṃ ca yo manyeta vidharmataḥ |  
> dviguṇaṃ daṇḍam āsthāya tat kāryaṃ punar uddharet ||

tathā [2.40] |

> sākṣisbhyāvasannānāṃ dūṣaṇe darśanaṃ punaḥ |  
> svacaryāvasitānāṃ tu noktaḥ paunarbhavo vidhiḥ ||

**'sākṣisabhyāvasannānām'** sākṣisabhyadvāreṇa prāptāvasādānām | **'dūṣaṇe'** sākṣiṣu sabhyeṣu cety anvayaḥ | **'darśanam'** punaḥ punar vyavahāradarśanaṃ kartavyam ity arthaḥ | **'svacaryavasitaḥ'** svavyāpāreṇa parasparaviruddhabhāṣaṇādinā parājitaḥ |

**[268]** bṛhaspatiḥ [9.22] |

> palāyanānuttaratvād anyapakṣāśrayeṇa ca |  
> hīnasya gṛhyate vado na svavākyair jitasya tu ||

bṛhaspati-kātyāyanau |

> kulādibhir nirścite 'pi na saṃtoṣaṃ gataś ca yaḥ |  
> vicārya tat kṛtaṃ rājā kukṛtaṃ punar uddharet ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [9.24] |

> niścitya bahubhiḥ sārdhaṃ brāhmaṇaiḥ śāstrapāragaiḥ |  
> daṇḍayej jayinā sākaṃ pūrvasabhyāṃs tu doṣiṇaḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.305] |

> durdṛṣṭāṃs tu punar dṛṣṭvā vyavahārān nṛpeṇa tu |  
> sabhyāḥ sajayino daṇḍyā vivādād dviguṇaṃ damam ||  
> [yo manyetājito 'smīti nyāyenāpi parājitaḥ |  
> sabhāyāṃ tat punar jitvā dāpayed dviguṇaṃ damam ||]

**[269]** nāradaḥ [2.66] |

> durdṛṣṭe vyavahāre tu sabhyās taṃ daṇḍam apnuyuḥ |  
> na hi jātu vinā daṇḍaṃ kaścin mārge 'vatiṣṭhate ||

manuḥ [9.234] |

> amātyāḥ prāḍvivāko vā ye kuryuḥ karyam anyathā |  
> tat svayaṃ nṛpatiḥ kuryāt tān sahasraṃ ca daṇḍayet ||

**[270]**

## 54 kṛtanivṛttiḥ
atha kṛtanivṛttiḥ

tatra manu-viṣṇū |

> yasmin yasmin vivāde tu kauṭasākṣyaṃ kṛtaṃ bhavet |  
> tat tat kāryaṃ nivarteta kṛtaṃ vāpy akṛtaṃ bhavet ||

nāradaḥ [1.43] |

> strīṣu rātrau bahir grāmād antarveśmany arātiṣu |  
> vyavahāraḥ kṛto 'py eṣu punaḥ kartavyatām iyāt ||

manu-nāradau [manu 8.164; nā. 2.15] |

> satyā na bhāṣā bhavati yady api syāt pratiṣṭhitā |  
> bahiś ced bhāṣyate dharmān niyatād vyāvahārikāt ||

**[271]** niyatā vyāvahārikadharmaviṣayā bhāṣocyate | sā pratiṣṭhitāpi lekhyādipramāṇavaty api na satyā | tayā yo 'rthaḥ pratipādyate sa nānuṣṭheyo yathā ********* [lacuna] kaścid anena mama sarvasvaṃ dattam ityādi |

manuḥ [8.165, 138] |

> yogādhamanavikrītaṃ yogadānapratigraham |  
> yatra vāpy upadhiṃ paśyet tat sarvaṃ vinivartayet ||  
> balād dattaṃ balād bhuktaṃ balād yac cāpi lekhitam |  
> sarvān balakṛtān arthān akṛtān manur abravīt ||

**'yogaḥ'** chadma | tena yad bandhakārpaṇādi kṛtaṃ tad rājā nivartayed ity arthaḥ | **'upadhiḥ'** chalam |

tathā [8.163] |

> mattonmattārtādhadhīnair bālena sthavireṇa vā |  
> asambaddhakṛtaś caiva vyavahāro na sidhyati ||

**[272]** **'adhvadhīno'** dāsaḥ |

nāradaḥ [4.39–42; 4.29–30] |

> yad bālaḥ kurute kāryam asvatantras tathaiva ca |  
> akṛtaṃ tad api prāhuḥ śāstre śāstravido janāḥ ||  
> svatantro 'pi hi yat kāryaṃ kuryād aprakṛtiṃ gataḥ |  
> tad apy akṛtam evāhur asvatantraḥ svahetutaḥ ||  
> kāmakrodhābhibhūtārtabhayavyasanapīḍitāḥ |  
> rāgadveṣaparītāś ca jñeyās tv aprakṛtiṃ gatāḥ ||  
> tathā dāsakṛtaṃ kāryam akṛtaṃ paricakṣate |  
> anyatra svāmisandeśān na dāsaḥ prabhur ātmanaḥ ||  
> putreṇa ca kṛtaṃ kāryaṃ yatra syāc chandataḥ pituḥ |  
> tad apy akṛtam evāhur dāsaḥ putraś ca tau samau ||

kārtyāyanaḥ [467] |

> na kṣetragṛhadāsānāṃ dānādhamanavikrayaḥ |  
> asvatantrakṛtāḥ siddhiṃ prāpnuyur nānuvarṇitāḥ ||

**'nānuvarṇitāḥ'** ananumatāḥ, svatantreṇeti śeṣaḥ |

**[273]** nāradaḥ [2.26–27, 42] |

> strīkṛtāny apramāṇāni kāryāṇy āhur anāpadi |  
> viśeṣato gṛhakṣetradānādhamanavikraye ||  
> etāny eva pramāṇāni bhartā yady anumanyate |  
> putraḥ patyur abhāve vā rājā vā patiputrayoḥ ||  
> kule jyeṣṭas tathā śreṣṭhaḥ prakṛtisthaś ca yo bhavet |  
> tatkṛtaṃ syāt kṛtaṃ kāryaṃ nāsvatantrakṛtaṃ kṛtam ||

**[274]**

## 55 svatantrāsvatantralakṣaṇam
atha svatantrāsvatantralakṣaṇam

tatra nāradaḥ [4.31, 33–37] |

> svātantryaṃ tu smṛtaṃ jyaiṣṭhyaṃ jyaiṣṭhyaṃ guṇavayaḥkṛtam |

tathā |

> svatantrāḥ prajāḥ sarvāḥ svatantraḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ |  
> asvatantraḥ smṛtaḥ śiṣya ācārye tu svatantratā ||  
> asvatantrāḥ striyaḥ sarvāḥ putrā dāsāḥ parigrahāḥ |  
> svatantras tatra tu gṛhī yasya tat syāt kramāgatam ||  
> garbhasthaiḥ sadṛśo jñeyaḥ āṣṭamād vatsarāc chiśuḥ |  
> bāla āṣoṣaśād varṣāt pogaṇḍaś ceti kīrtyate ||

**[275]** > parato vyavahārajñaḥ svatantraḥ pitarāvṛte |  
> jīvator na svatantraḥ syāj jarayāpi samanvitaḥ ||  
> tayor api pitā śreyān bījaprādhānyadarśanāt |  
> abhāve bījino mātā tadabhāve tu pūrvajaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [466] |

>  pitāsvatantraḥ pitṛmān bhrātā brātṛvya eva vā |  
> kaniṣṭho vāvibhaktasvo dāsaḥ parikaras tathā ||

**'pitāsvatantraḥ'** pitṛmān asvatantra ity arthaḥ | **'avibhaktasvaḥ'** avibhiktadhanaḥ |

hārītaḥ |

> dānārthe vā dhanārthe vā dharmārthe vā viśeṣataḥ |  
> ādāne vā visarge vā na strī svātantryam arhati ||

nāradaḥ [2.38] |

> svatantrāḥ sarva evaite paratantreṣu nityaśaḥ |  
> anuśiṣṭau visarge ca vikraye ceśvarā matāḥ ||

**'ete'** pūrvoktarājadayaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [468–69] |

> pramāṇaṃ sarva evaite paṇyānāṃ krayavikraye |  
> yadi saṃvyavahāraṃ prāk kurvanto hy anumoditāḥ ||  
> kṣetrādīnāṃ tathaiva syād bhrātā bhrātṛsutaḥ sutaḥ |  
> nisṛṣṭāḥ kṛtyakaraṇe guruṇā yadi gacchatā ||

**[276]** > nisṛṣṭārthas tu yo yasmin tasminn arthe prabhus tu saḥ |  
> tad bhartā tatkṛtaṃ kāryaṃ nānyathā kartum arhati ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [9.29, 28] |

> yaḥ svāminā niyuktas tu dhanāyavyayapālane |  
> kusīdakṛṣivāṇijye nisṛṣṭārthas tu sa smṛtaḥ ||  
> pramāṇaṃ tatkṛtaṃ sarvaṃ lābhālābhavyayodayam |  
> svadeśe vā videśe vā svāmī tan na visaṃvadet ||

kātyāyanaḥ [471] |

> sutasya sutadārāṇāṃ vaśitvaṃ tv anuśāsane |  
> vikraye caiva dāne ca vaśitvaṃ na sute prabhuḥ ||

**iti mahārājādhirājaśrīmadgovindacandradevamahāsandhivrahikeṇa**

**bhaṭṭahṛdayadharātmajena**

**bhaṭṭaśrīmallakṣmīdhareṇa viracite kṛtyakalpatarau**

**vyavahārakāṇde vyavahāramātṛkā**

**samāptā ||**

**[277]**

**atharṇādānādivyavahārapadāni**

## 56 ṛṇādānavidhiḥ
atha ṛṇādānavidhiḥ

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ [10.1–2] |

> padāṅgasahitas tv eṣa vyavahāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ |  
> vivādakāraṇāny asya padāni śṛṇutādhunā ||  
> ṛṇādānapradānāni dyūtāhvānānitkāni ca |  
> kramaśaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi kriyābhedāṃś ca tattvataḥ ||

naradaḥ [4.1, 98] |

> ṛṇaṃ deyam adeyaṃ ca yena yatra yathā ca yat |  
> dānagrahaṇadharmāś ca ṛṇādānam iti smṛtam ||  
> sthānalābhanimittaṃ yad dānagrahaṇam iṣyate |  
> tat kusīdam iti jñeyaṃ tena vṛttiḥ kusīdinām ||

**'sthanam'** atra mūladhanasthitiḥ | **'lābhaḥ'** kalādiprāptiḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.6, 5] |

> kutsitāt sīdataś caiva nirviśaṅkaiḥ pragṛhyate |  
> caturguṇaṃ vāṣṭaguṇaṃ kusīdākhyam ataḥ smṛtam ||

**[278]** > paripūrṇaṃ gṛhītvādhiṃ bandhaṃ vā sādhu lagnakam |  
> lekhyārūḍhaṃ sākṣimad vā ṛṇaṃ dadyād dhanī sadā ||

**'kutsitāt sīdataś ca'** ity adhamarṇaviśeṣaṇe |

nāradaḥ [4.117] |

> viśrambhahetū dvāv atra pratibhūr ādhir eva ca |  
> likhitaṃ sākṣiṇaś ca dve pramāṇavyaktikārake ||

kātyāyanaḥ [497] |

> na strībhyo bāladāsebhyaḥ prayacchet kiṃcid uddhṛtam |  
> dātā na labhate tat tu tebhyo dattaṃ ca yad vasu ||

**'uddhṛtam'** uddhāram |

**(ka) atha vṛddhiḥ**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ [10.28) |

> vasiṣṭhavacanaproktaṃ vṛddhiṃ vārdhuṣike śṛṇu |  
> pañca māṣās tu viṃśatyām evaṃ dharmo na hīyate ||

**'viṃśatir'** atra māṣāṇām |

gautamaḥ [12.26]: "kusīdavṛddhir dharmyā viṃśatiḥ pañcamāṣikī pratimāsam" |

**[279]** smṛtiḥ |

> māṣo viṃśatimbhāgas tu paṇasya parikīrtitaḥ |

manuḥ [8.140] |

> vasiṣṭhavihitāṃ vṛddhiṃ sṛjed vittavivardhinīm |  
> aśītibhāgaṃ gṛhṇīyān māsād vārdhuṣikaḥ śate ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.37] |

> aśītibhāgo vṛddhiḥ syān māsi māsi sabandhake |

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.22] |

> aśītibhāgo vardheta lābho dviguṇatām iyāt |  
> prayuktaṃ saptabhir varṣais tribhāgonair na saṃāśayaḥ ||

vyāsaḥ |

> sabandhe bhāge āśītaḥ sāṣṭo bhāgaḥ salagnake |  
> nirādhāne dvikaśataṃ māsalābha udāhṛtaḥ ||

**'āśītaḥ'** aśītitamaḥ | ayam eva salagnake svakīyāṣṭamabhāgasahitaḥ sāṣṭabhāgaḥ | **'nirādhāne'** bandhakarahite |

**[280]** manuḥ [8.141] |

> dvikaṃ śataṃ vā gṛhṇīyāt satāṃ dharmam anusmaran |  
> dvikaṃ śataṃ hi gṛhṇāno na bhavaty arthakilbiṣī ||

hārītaḥ: "purāṇapañcaviṃśatyāṃ māse 'ṣṭapaṇā vṛddhiḥ | evaṃ sadvimāsaiś caturbhir varṣaiḥ dviḥparyāgataṃ saṃtiṣṭhate, eṣā dharmavṛddhiḥ | nānayā dharmāc cyavate" |

**'purāṇaḥ'** ṣoḍaśa paṇāḥ | **'dviḥparyāgatam'** dviguṇībhūtam | **'saṃtiṣṭhate'** vyvatiṣṭhate, na punar vivardhata ity arthaḥ |

manuḥ [8.142] |

> dvikaṃ trikaṃ catuṣkaṃ ca pañcakaṃ ca śataṃ samam |  
> māsasya vṛddhiṃ gṛhṇīyād varṇānām anupūrvaśaḥ ||

**'dvikaṃ'** dvau [purāṇau māsi] vṛddhir dīyate yasmin mūladhane tathā | evaṃ trikādy api | **'samam'** mātrayāpy anadhikam |

**[281]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.37] |

> varṇakramāc chataṃ dvitricatuṣpañcakam anyathā |

**'anyathā'** bandhakaṃ vinā |

viṣṇuḥ [6.1–2]: "athottamarṇo 'dhamarṇakād yathādattam arthaṃ gṛhṇīyāt | dvikaṃ trikaṃ catuṣkaṃ pañcakaṃ śataṃ varṇānukrameṇa pratimāsam" |

gautamaḥ [12.27]: "nātisāṃvatsarīm eke" |

manuḥ [8.153] |

> nātisāṃvatsarīṃ vṛddhiṃ na cādṛṣṭāṃ punar haret |  
> cakravṛddiḥ kālavṛddhiḥ kāritā kāyikā ca yā ||

**[282]** **'nātisāṃvatsarīm'** iti – māsād ārabhya saṃvatsaraṃ yāvad vṛddhir niyamanīyā | na tu saṃvatsarād ūrdhvam iti yadi vṛddhyā dārayasi tad eva prayacchāmīti niyamaḥ kartavyaḥ |

nāradaḥ [4.102] |

> kāyikā kālikā caiva kāritā ca tathāparā |  
> cakravṛddhis tu śāstreṣu. tasya vṛddihś caturvidhā ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.8–9] |

> vṛddiḥ caturvidhā proktā pañcadhānyaiḥ prakīrtitā |  
> ṣaḍvidhānyaiḥ samākhyātā tatvatas tāṃ nibodhata ||  
> kāyikā kālikā caiva cakravṛddir athāparā |  
> kāritā ca śikhāvṛddhir bhogalābhas tathaiva ca ||

vyāsaḥ |

> dohyavāhyakarmayutā kāyikā samudāhṛtā |  
> kāyāvirodhinī śaśvat pañapādādi kāyikā ||

**[283]** nāradaḥ [4.104a; 103a; 104ā; 103ā] |

> kāyāvirodhinī śaśvat paṇārdhādyā tu kāyikā |  
> pratimāsaṃ sravati yā vṛddhiḥ sā kālikā matā ||  
> vṛddher api punar vṛddhiḥ cakravṛddhir udāhṛtā |  
> vṛddhiḥ sā kāritā nāma yarṇikena savyaṃ kṛtā ||

**'kāyāvirodhinī'** mūladhanāvirodhinī | **'śaśvat paṇārdhādyā tu'** pratidinaṃ deyatvena paṇatadardhādikā | prathamam ubhābhyāṃ yā kṛtā vṛddhiḥ sā tu **'kārikā'** |

kātyāyanaḥ [498] |

> ṛṇikena tu yā vṛddhir adhikā saṃprakalpitā |  
> āpatkālakṛtā nityaṃ dātavyā kāritā tu sā ||  
> anyathā kāritā vṛddhir na dātavyā kathaṃcana |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.38] |

> kāntāragās tu daśakaṃ sāmudrā viṃśakaṃ śatam |  
> dadyur vā svakṛtāṃ vṛddhiṃ sarve sarvāsu jātiṣu ||

manuḥ [8.157] |

> samudrayānakuśalā deśakālārthadarśinaḥ |  
> sthāpayanti tu yāṃ vṛddhiṃ sā tatrādhigamaṃ prati ||

**[284]** **'samudrayānakuśalā'** iti vaṇiṅmātropalakṣaṇam | **'deśakālārthadarśinaḥ'** asmin kāla iyān lābho 'sminn iyān iti ye paśyanti | **'adhigamo'** niścayaḥ |

hārītaḥ: "purāṇe paṇikaṃ māsam ity eke | tūle dviguṇaṃ dhānyaṃ triguṇam evaṃ ca vardhate, tathorṇākārpāsaḥ saṃvatsareṇa tṛṇaśalākaṃ ghṛtaguḍalavaṇam aṣṭaguṇam" |

**'paṇikaṃ māsam'** gṛhṇīyād iti śeṣaḥ | **'tūle dviguṇaṃ dhānyam'** iti, dvitryādibhir api māsair dhānyaṃ dviguṇaṃ grāhyam | **'tūle'** navadhānyāgame | yadā tu tūlāgame na dattaṃ tadā triguṇam eva | **'nādhikaṃ vardhate'** caturguṇatāṃ no bhavatīty arthaḥ | **'tathā'**, dhānyavad ūrṇākārpāsaḥ triguṇam eva saṃvatsareṇa vardhate | yadā tu saṃvatsareṇa na dīyate tadā triguṇam evāṣṭaguṇaṃ saṃvatsareṇety arthaḥ |

**[285]** nāradaḥ [4.105–106] |

> ṛṇānāṃ sārvabhaumo 'yaṃ vidhir vṛddhikaraḥ smṛtaḥ |  
> deśācārasthitis tv anyā yatrarṣam avatiṣṭhate ||  
> dviguṇaṃ triguṇaṃ caiva tathānyasmiṃś caturguṇam |  
> tathāṣṭaguṇam anyasmin deyaṃ deśe 'vatiṣṭhate ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.11, 13 ā]

> pratyahaṃ gṛhyate yā tu śikhāvṛddhis tu sā smṛtā |  
> śikheva vardhate nityaṃ śiraśchedān nivartate ||  
> mūle datte tathaivaiṣā śikhāvṛddhis tataḥ smṛtā |

kātyāyanaḥ [501] |

> ādhibhogas tv aśeṣo yo vṛddhis tu parikalpitaḥ |  
> prayogo yatra caivaṃ syād ādhibhogaḥ sa ucyate ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.14, 16] |

> gṛhāt stomaḥ sadaḥ kṣetrād bhogalābhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ |  
> śikhāvṛddhiṃ kāyikā ca bhogalābhaṃ tathaiva ca ||  
> dhanī tāvat samādadyād yāvan mūlaṃ na śodhitam |

**'stomo'** bhāṭakam | **'sadaḥ'** sasyādiphalam |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.90] |

> ādhis tu bhujyate tāvad yāvat tan na pradīyate |

**[286]** ādhim uttamarṇo dadyād ity anuvṛttau, viṣṇuḥ [6.6–8]: "antyavṛddhau praviṣṭāyām api | na sthāvaram ādhim ṛte vacanāt" |

**'ṛte vacanāt'** dviguṇe dhane praviṣṭe tatra ādhiṃ dāsyāmīti yadi pūrvam eva noktaṃ bhaved ity arthaḥ |

manuḥ [8.152] |

> kṛtānusārād adhikā vyatiriktā na sidhyati |  
> kusīdapatham āhus taṃ pañcakaṃ satam arhati ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.21] |

> bhogo yad dviguṇād ūrdhvaṃ cakravṛddhiś ca gṛhyate |  
> mūlaṃ ca sodayaṃ paścād vārdhuṣyaṃ tad vigarhitam ||

**(a) athākṛtavṛddhiḥ**

tatra kātyāyanaḥ [50] |

> kṛtvoddhāram adatvā yo yācitas tu diśaṃ vrajet |  
> ūrdhvaṃ māsatrayāt tasya tad dhanaṃ vṛddhim āpnuyāt ||

**[287]** > paṇyaṃ gṛhītvā yo mūlyam adatvaiva diśaṃ vrajet |  
> ṛtutrayasyopariṣṭāt tad dhanaṃ vṛddhim āpnuyāt ||  
> nikṣepaṃ vṛddhiśeṣaṃ ca krayaṃ vikrayam eva ca |  
> yācyamāno na dadyāc ced vardhate pañcakaṃ śatam ||  
> prītidattaṃ na vardheta yāvan na pratiyācitam |  
> yācyamānaṃ na dattaṃ ced vardhate pañcakaṃ śatam ||  
> yo yācitakam ādāya tad adatvā diśaṃ vrajet |  
> ṛtutrayasyopariṣṭāt tad dhanaṃ vṛddhim āpnuyāt ||  
> svadeśastho 'pi vā yas tu na dadyād yācito 'sakṛt |  
> sa tatra kāritāṃ vṛddhim anicchann api cāvahet ||

viṣṇuḥ [6.3]: "vṛddhiṃ dadyuḥ sarve varṇā vā svapratipannām | akṛtām api vatsarātikrameṇa yathābhihitām" |

'yathābhihitām' varṇakrameṇa dvikatrikādinā yatoktām |

nāradaḥ [4.208, 220] |

> na vṛddhiḥ prītidattānāṃ syād anākāritā kvacit |  
> anākāritam apy ūrdhvaṃ vatsarārdhād vivardhate ||  
> eṣa vṛddhividhiḥ proktaḥ prītidattasya dharmataḥ |  
> vṛddhis tu yoktā dhānyānāṃ vārdhuṣyaṃ tad udāhṛtam ||

**'anākāritam'** anudīritam |

**[288]**

**(ā) atha paramavṛddhiḥ**

tatra gautamaḥ [12.28]: 'cirasthāne dvaiguṇyaṃ prayogasya' |

kātyāyanaḥ [510] |

> maṇimuktāpravālānāṃ suvarṇarajatasya ca |  
> tiṣṭhati dviguṇā vṛddhiḥ phālakaiṭāvikasya ca ||

**'tiṣṭhati'** ciratarāvasthāne na vardhata ity arthaḥ |**'kaiṭam'** kīṭabhavaṃ trasarādi | **'āvikam'** kambalādi |

manuḥ [8.151] |

> kusīdavṛddhir dvaiguṇayaṃ nātyeti sakṛd āhṛtā |  
> dhānye sade lave vāhye nātikrāmati pañcatām ||

**'dhānyam'** vrīhiyavādi | **'lavaḥ'** ūrṇācāmarādiḥ, lūyate **'lavaḥ'** iti vyutpatyā | **'vāhyo'** balīvardādiḥ |

**[289]** gautamaḥ [12:33]: "kusīdaṃ paśūpajalomakṣetrasadavāhyeṣu nātipañcaguṇam" |

**'paśūpajam'** kṣīraghṛtādi | bṛhaspatiḥ [10.17] |

> hiraṇye dviguṇā vṛddhis triguṇā vastrakupyake |  
> dhānye caturguṇā proktā sadavāhyalaveṣu ca ||

viṣṇuḥ [6.11–15]: "hiraṇyasya parā vṛddhir dvigunā | dhānyasya triguṇā | vastrasya caturguṇā | rasasyāṣṭaguṇā | santatiḥ strīpaśūnām" |

vasiṣṭhaḥ [2.44–47]: "dviguṇaṃ hiraṇyaṃ triguṇaṃ ca dhānyam | dhānyenaiva rasā vyākhyātāḥ | puṣpamūlaphalāni ca | tulāghṛtam aṣṭaguṇam" |

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.18] |

> uktā pañcaguṇā śāke bījekṣau ṣaḍguṇā smṛtā |  
> lavaṇasnehamadyeṣu vṛddhir aṣṭaguṇā smṛtā |  
> guḍe madhuni caivoktā prayukte cirakālike ||

**[290]** kātyāyanaḥ [511] |

> tailānāṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ madyānām atha sarpiṣām |  
> vṛddhir aṣṭaguṇā jñeyā guḍasya lavaṇasya ca ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.23] |

> tṛṇakāṣṭheṣṭakāsūtrakiṇvapāṣāṇacarmaṇām |  
> hetipuṣpaphalānāṃ ca vṛddhis tu na nivartate ||

**'kiṇvam'** suraprakṛtidravyaviśeṣaḥ | **'hetiḥ'** śastram |

viṣṇuḥ [6.16–17]: "kiṇvakārpāsasūtravarmacarmāyudheṣṭakāṅgārāṇām akṣayā | anuktānāṃ dviguṇā" |

**(kha) atha vṛddhiniṣedhaḥ**

tatra nāradaḥ [2.36] |

> paṇyamūlyaṃ bhṛtir nyāso daṇḍo yac cābhihārikam |  
> vṛthādānākṣikapaṇā vardhante nāvivakṣitāḥ ||

**[291]** **'ābhihārikam'** chalādinā gṛhyamāṇam | **'ākṣikapaṇaḥ'** dyūtanimittaṃ dhanam |

kātyāyanaḥ [508] |

> carmasasyāsavadyūtapaṇyamūlye ca sarvadā |  
> strīśulkeṣu na vṛddhiḥ syāt prātibhāvyāgateṣu ca ||

**'sasyam'** kṣetrāj jātaṃ dhānyastambādi | **'āsavam'** madhu |

saṃvartaḥ |

> na vṛddhiḥ strīdhane lābhe nikṣepe ca tathā sthite |  
> saṃdigdhe prātibhāvye ca yadi na syāt svayaṃkṛtā ||

vyāsaḥ |

> prātibhāvyaṃ bhuktabandham agṛhītaṃ ca ditsatam |  
> na vardhate prapannasya damaḥ śulkaṃ pratiśrutam ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.44] |

> dīyamānaṃ na gṛhṇāti prayuktaṃ yaḥ svakaṃ dhanam |  
> madhyasthasthāpitaṃ tat syād vardhate na tataḥ param ||

**[292]**

**(ga) athādhividhiḥ**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ [10.38–39] |

> ādhir bandhaḥ samākhyātaḥ sa ca proktaś caturvidhaḥ |  
> jaṅgamaḥ sthāvaraś caiva gopyo bhogyas tathaiva ca ||  
> yādṛcchikaḥ sāvadhiko lekhyārūḍho 'tha sākṣimān |

'caturvidhaḥ' svarūpaprakārakālapramāṇaiḥ | tatra svarūpam eva dvividhaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamabhedana (?) | prakāraś ca dvividho gopyabogyabhedena | kālo dvividhaḥ avadhiniyamāniyamābhyām | pramāṇaṃ dvividhaṃ lekhyasākṣibhedena |

nāradaḥ [4.125] |

> upacāras tathaivāsya lābhahānir viparyaye |  
> pramādād dhaninas tadvad ādhau vikṛtim āgate ||

**'upacāraḥ'** rakṣaṇam | kartavyam iti śeṣaḥ | **'asya'** ādheḥ **'lābhahāniḥ'** vṛddhihāniḥ | **'viparyaye'** vināśe |

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.39–40] |

> aśāntalābhe ca ṛṇe tathā pūrṇe 'vadhau dhanī |  
> yo bhuṅkte bandhakaṃ lobhān na sa lābho bhavet punaḥ ||

**[293]** > nyāsavat paripālyo 'sau vṛddhir naśyati hāpite |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.59] |

> gopyādhibhoge no vṛddhiḥ sopakāre ca hāpite |

**'sopakāre'** balīvardādau tāmrakaṭāhādau | **'hāpite'** vyavahārākṣamatvam anuprāpite |

manuḥ [8.143] |

> na tv evādhau sopakāre kausīdīṃ vṛddhim āpnuyāt |

tathā [8.150] |

> yaḥ svāminānanujñātam ādhiṃ bhuṅkte 'vicakṣaṇaḥ |  
> tenārdhavṛddhir moktavyā tasya bhogasya niṣkṛtiḥ ||

tathā [8.144] |

> na bhoktavyo balād ādhir bhuñjāno vṛddhim utsṛjet |  
> mūlyena toṣayec cainam ādhisteno 'nyathā bhavet ||

'ardhavṛddhiḥ bhoktavyā' iti, ādher upabhuktasya vikāre 'satīti boddhavyam | vikāre tu sati sakalavṛddhityāga eveety arthaḥ |

**[294]** kātyāyanaḥ [525] |

> akāmam ananujñātam ādhiṃ yaḥ karma kārayet |  
> bhoktā karmaphalaṃ dāpyo vṛddhiṃ vā labhate na saḥ ||

'akāmam' ādhīkṛtaṃ kāmyādikarmakaraṇecchārahitam |

viṣṇuḥ [6.5–6]: "ādhyupabhoge vṛddhyabhāvaḥ | devarājopaghātād ṛte vinaṣṭam ādhim uttamarṇo dadyāt" |

nāradaḥ [4.126] |

> vinaṣṭe mūlahāniḥ syād daivarājakṛtā ṛte |

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.46] |

> bhukte cāsāratāṃ prāpte mūlahāniḥ prajāyate |  
> bahumūlyaṃ yatra naṣṭam ṛṇikaṃ tatra toṣayet ||

vyāsaḥ |

> gṛhītṛdoṣān naṣṭaś ced bandho deyādhiko bhavet |  
> ṛṇaṃ salābhaṃ saṃśodhya tanmūlyaṃ dāpyate dhanī ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.59] |

> naṣṭo deyo vinaṣṭaś ca daivarājakṛtād ṛte |

**[295]** **'vinaṣṭo'** atra vikṛtiṃ gataḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [526] |

> yas tv ādhiṃ karma kurvāṇaṃ vācā daṇḍena karmabhiḥ |  
> pīḍayed bhartsayec caiva prāpnuyāt pūrvasāhasam ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.41] |

> daivarājopaghātena yatrādhir nāśam āpnuyāt |  
> tatrānyaṃ dāpayed bandhaṃ sodayaṃ ca ṛṇaṃ dhanī ||

nāradaḥ [4.130] |

> rakṣyamāṇo 'pi yady ādhiḥ kāleneyād asāratām |  
> ādhir anyo 'tha vā kāryo deyaṃ vā dhanine dhanam ||

kātyāyanaḥ [524] |

> na ced dhanikadoṣeṇa niṣpated vā mriyeta vā |  
> ādhim anyaṃ sa kāryaḥ syād ṛṇān mucyet narṇikaḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.42, 66] |

> bandhahastasya yad deyaṃ citreṇa caritena vā |  
> adatte 'rthe 'khile bandhaṃ nākāmo dāpyete kvacit ||  
> dhanaṃ mūlīkṛtaṃ datvā yad ādhiṃ prārthayed ṛṇī |  
> tadaiva tasya moktavyas tv anyathā doṣabhāg dhanī ||

**[296]** **'citram'** lekhyam | **'caritam'** sākṣyādi |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.62–63] |

> upasthitasya moktavya ādhiḥ steno 'nyathā bhavet |  
> prayojake 'sati dhanaṃ kule nyasyādhim āpnuyāt ||  
> tatkālakṛtamūlyo vā tatra tiṣṭhed avṛddhikaḥ |

'asati' avidyamāne |

ādhim uttamarṇo dadyād ity anuvṛttau viṣṇuḥ [6.7]: "antyavṛddhau praviṣṭāyām api" |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.64] |

> yadā tu dviguṇībhūtam ṛṇam ādhau tadā khalu |  
> mocya ādhis tadutpanne praviṣṭe dviguṇe dhane ||

'etadutpanne dviguṇe dhane praviṣṭe tvayādhir moktavyā' ity uktvāyaṃ cādhir dīyate tadviṣayam idam | evaṃvidha eva loke kṣayādhir ity ucyate |

**[297] **viṣṇuḥ [6.9]: "gṛhītadhanapraveśārtham eva yat sthāvaraṃ dattaṃ tad gṛhītadhanam apraveśe dadyāt" | bṛhaspatiḥ [10.67–69] |

> kṣetrādikaṃ yadā bhuktam utpannam adhikaṃ tataḥ |  
> mūlodayaṃ praviṣṭaṃ ceet tad ādhiṃ prāpnuyād ṛṇī ||  
> paribhāvya yadā kṣetraṃ pradadyād dhanike ṛṇī |  
> tadā tac chāntalābhe 'rthe moktavyam iti niścayaḥ ||  
> praviṣṭe sodaye dravye pradātavyaṃ punar mama |  
> kusīdādividhis tv eṣa dharmyaḥ saṃparikīrtitaḥ ||

**'śāntalābhe 'rthe'** parisamāptalābhe 'rthe nimittabhūte, savṛddhikadhanapraveśo yāvad ity arthaḥ |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.58] |

> ādhiḥ praṇśyed dviguṇe dhane yadi na mokṣyate |  
> kāle kālakṛte naśyet phalabhogyo na naśyati ||

**'ādhiḥ praṇaśyet'** iti, dviguṇībhūte dhane yady ādhir adhamarṇena na mokṣyate tadā naśyati, dhanaprayoktuḥ svaṃ bhavati | **'kālakṛtaḥ'** kṛtakālaḥ | tena yaḥ kālāvadhiḥ kṛtas tasmin prāpte yadi na mokṣyate tadā naśyatīty arthaḥ |

**[298]** bṛhaspatiḥ [10.49] |

> pūrṇe 'vadhau śāntalābhe bandhasvāmī dhanī bhavet |  
> anirgate daśāhe tu ṛṇī mokṣitum arhati ||

vyāsaḥ |

> hiraṇye dviguṇībhūte pūrṇe kāle kṛtāvadheḥ|  
> bandhakasya dhanī svāmī dvisaptāhaṃ pratīkṣya tu ||  
> ato 'ntarā dhanaṃ datvā ṛṇī bandhakam āpnuyāt |  
> phalabhogyaṃ pūrṇakālaṃ datvā dravyaṃ tu sāmakam ||

samam eva **'sāmakam'** phalaśūnyamity arthaḥ |

manuḥ [8.143] |

> na tv evādhau sopakāre kausīdiṃ vṛddhim āpnuyāt |  
> na cādheḥ kālasaṃrodhān nisargo 'sti na vikrayaḥ ||

**'kālasaṃrodhaḥ'** cirakālāvasthānam | **'nisargaḥ'** anyathādhikaraṇam | tac ca bhogyādhiviṣayam | **'na tv evādhau sopakāre'** iti tasyaiva prakṛtatvāt | 'ādhiḥ praṇaśyed dviguṇe dhane' iti yājñavalkyavacanaṃ [2.58] gopyādhiviṣayam | ato nānayor virodhaḥ | **'na nisargo na vikrayaḥ'** ity atra uttamarṇena na kartavya ity śeṣaḥ |

**[299]** bṛhaspatiḥ [10.70, 71, 50, 85] |

> yatrāhitaṃ gṛhakṣetraṃ bhoge na prakarṣānvitam |  
> tatrarṇī nāpnuyād bandhaṃ dhanī caiva ṛṇaṃ tathā ||  
> pūrṇe prakarṣe tatsvāmyam ubhayoḥ parikīrtitam |  
> apūrṇe tu prakuryātāṃ parasparamate tau ||  
> gopyādhir dviguṇād ūrdhvaṃ kṛtakālas tathāvidhiḥ |  
> śodhayitvā ṛṇikule moktavyaḥ samanantaram ||  
> naṣṭe mṛte vā ṛṇike dhanī patraṃ pradarśayet |  
> tatkālāvadhisaṃyuktaṃ sthānalekhyaṃ ca kārayet ||

**'parkarṣo'** vṛddhiḥ |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.61] |

> caritraṃ bandhakakṛtaṃ savṛddhiṃ dāpayed dhanam |

**'caritram'** agnihotragaṅgāsnānādi | tad eva bandhakīkṛtya yad gṛhītaṃ tad vṛddhisahitaṃ dātavyam ity arthaḥ |

**[300]** kātyāyanaḥ [529] |

> ādhātā yatra na syāt tu dhanī bandhaṃ nivedayet |  
> rājñas tataḥ sa vikhyāto vikreya iti dhāraṇā ||  
> savṛddhikaṃ gṛhītvā tu śeṣaṃ rājany athārpayet |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.63] |

> vinā dhāraṇakād vāpi vikrīṇīta sasākṣikam |

**(gha) athādhisiddhiḥ**

tatra vyāsaḥ |

> ādhis tu dvividhaḥ prokto jaṅgamaḥ sthāvaras tathā |  
> siddhir asyobhayasyāpi bhogo yady asti nānyathā ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.53] |

> na bhuṅkte yaḥ svam ādhānaṃ na dadyān an nivedayet |  
> pramītasākṣiṛṇikaṃ tasya lekhyam apārthakam ||  
> gṛhaṃ vāryāpaṇaṃ dhānyaṃ paśustrīvāhanāni ca |  
> upekṣayā vinaśyanti yānti cāsāratāṃ tathā ||

**'svam ādhānam'** ādhim |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.60] |

> ādheḥ svīkaraṇāt siddhiḥ rakṣyamāṇo 'py asāratām |

**[301]** kātyāyanaḥ [517] |

> ādhim ekaṃ dvayor yatra kuryāt kā pratipad bhavet |  
> tayoḥ pūrvataraṃ grāhyam ādhātā cauradaṇḍabhāk ||

**'pratipat'** vyavasthā | **'pūrvataram'** karaṇam iti śeṣaḥ |

viṣṇuḥ [5.181–84]: "gocarmamātrādhikāṃ bhuvam anyasyādhīkṛtāṃ tasmād anirmocyānyasya yaḥ prayacchet sa vadhyaḥ | ūnāṃ cec choḍaśasuvarṇaṃ daṇḍyaḥ" |

> eko 'śnīyād yad utpannaṃ naraḥ sāṃvatsaraṃ phalam |  
> gocarmamātrā sā kṣoṇī stokā vā yadi vā bahu ||  
> yayor nikṣipta ādhis tau vivadetāṃ yadā narau |  
> yasya bhuktiḥ phalaṃ tasya balātkāraṃ vinā kṛtā ||

yasya bhuktir balātkāraṃ vinety arthaḥ | tasya sā bhūmir iti seṣaḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.44–45] |

> kṣetram ekaṃ dvayor bandhe dattaṃ yat samakālikam |  
> yena bhuktaṃ bhavet pūrvaṃ tasya tat siddhim āpnuyāt ||  
> tulyakālopasthitayor dvayor api samaṃ bhavet |  
> pradāne vikraye caiva vidhiḥ saṃparikīrtitaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [518, 521, 522, 519, 520]

> ādhānaṃ vikrayo dānaṃ sākṣilekhyakṛtaṃ tathā |  
> ekakriyānibandhena lekhyaṃ tatrāpahārakam ||

**[302]**  
> yas tu sarvasvam ādiśya prāk paścān nāmacihnitam |  
> ādadhyāt tat kathaṃ na syāc cihnitaṃ balavattaram ||  
> maryādācihnitaṃ kṣetraṃ gṛhaṃ vāpi yadā bhavet |  
> grāmādayaś ca likhyante tadā siddhim avāpnuyāt ||  
> anirdiṣṭaṃ ca nirdiṣṭam ekatra ca viseṣitam |  
> viśeṣalikhitaṃ jyāya iti kātyānayo 'bravīt ||  
> yo vidyamānaṃ pradhanam anirdiṣṭasvarūpakam |  
> ākāśabandham ādadhyād ādiṣṭaṃ naiva tad bhavet ||  
> yad yat tadāsya vidyeta tad ādiṣṭaṃ vinirdiśet |

**'ekakriyānibandhena'** ekajātīyadānādikriyānimittena | yas tu sarvasvam ityādi | yaḥ prathamaṃ sarvasvaṃ bandhakatvenoddiśya paścāl lekhanasamaye nāmaviśeṣeṇa lekhayati, tatrottarakālaṃ vivāde sati, yad yāvan nāmato likhitaṃ tat tāvat pramāṇam | noddiṣṭamātram ity arthaḥ | **'pradhanam'** atra prakṛṣṭaṃ dhanam |

**[303]**

**(ṅa) atha pratibhūvidhiḥ**

tatra kātyāyanaḥ [114–116] |

> na svāmī na ca vai śatruḥ svāminādhikṛtas tathā |  
> niruddho daṇḍitaś caiva saṃśayasthaś ca na kvacit ||  
> naiva rikthī na riktaś ca na caivātyantavāsinaḥ |  
> rājakāryaniyuktāś ca ye ca pravrajitā narāḥ ||  
> nāśakto dhanine dātuṃ daṇḍaṃ rājñe ca tatsamam |  
> nāvijñāto gṛhītavyaḥ pratibhūḥ svakriyāṃ prati ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.52] |

> bhrātṝṇām atha dampatyoḥ pituḥ putrasya caiva hi |  
> prātibhāvyam ṛṇaṃ sākṣyam avibhakte na tu smṛtam ||

nāradaḥ [16.39] |

> sākṣitvaṃ prātibhāvyaṃ ca dānaṃ grahaṇam eva ca |  
> vibhaktāḥ bhrātaraḥ kuryur nāvibhaktāḥ parasparam ||

**[304]** bṛhaspatiḥ [10.73, 74, 78] |

> darśane pratyaye dāne ṛṇidravyārpaṇe tathā |  
> catuṣprakāraḥ pratibhūḥ śāśtre dṛṣṭo manīṣibhiḥ ||  
> āhaiko 'haṃ darśayāmi sādhur eṣo 'paro 'bravīt |  
> dātāham etad draviṇam arpayāmy aparo vadet ||  
> ādyau tu vitathe dāpyau tatkālāveditaṃdhanam |  
> uttarau ca visaṃvāde tau vinā tatsutau tathā ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.54] |

> darśanapratibhūr yatra mṛtaḥ prātyayiko 'pi vā |  
> na tatputrā ṛṇaṃ dadyuḥ dadyur dāyāya yaḥ sthitaḥ ||

**'dadyur dānāya yaḥ sthitaḥ'** iti | yo dānapratibhūtvena sthitas tasya putrā ṛṇaṃ dadyur ity arthaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [530, 531, 533] |

> dānopasthānaviśvāsavivādaśapathāya ca |  
> lagnakaṃ dāpayed evaṃ yathāyogaṃ viparyaye ||  
> darśanapratibhūr yas tu deśe kāle na darśayet |  
> nibandham āvahet tatra daivarājakṛtād ṛte ||  
> kāle vyatīte pratibhūr yadi taṃ naiva darśayet |  
> nibandhaṃ dāpayet tatra prete caiva vidhiḥ smrtaḥ ||

**[305]** > deśakālau kriyākāre yady alpam api laṅghayet |  
> sādhitaṃ pratibhūr dāpyas tam arthaṃ sādhite vidhiḥ ||  
> parāśrayama abhavyaṃ vāpy asatsaṃsargam eva ca |  
> apakārakṣamo yaś ca dveṣāt kartumanāḥ kvacit ||  
> kārayet pratyayāyaiva tadbhayāl lagnakaṃ tu tam |  
> visaṃvāde 'tha śīlasya dāpyate pratibhūs tathā ||

**'parāśrayam'** ityādiṣu **'kartumanā'** iti sambandhaḥ | **'abhavyam'** virūpakam |

manuḥ [8.160] |

> dānapratibhuvi prete dāyādān api dāpayet |

kātyāyanaḥ [534] |

> gṛhītvā bandhakaṃ yatra darśane 'sya sthito bhavet |  
> vibhāvya vādinā tatra dāpyaḥ syāt tad ṛṇaṃ sutaḥ ||

**[306]** asyārthaḥ — bandhakaṃ gṛhītvā darśanapratibhūr abhūd iti vibhāvya yadi vādinā tasminn asati tatsutas tad ṛṇaṃ dāpya iti |

manuḥ [8.16162] |

> adātari punar dātā vijñātaprakṛtāv ṛṇam |  
> paścāt pratibhuvi prete parīpset kena hetunā ||  
> nirādiṣṭadhanaś cet tu pratibhūḥ syād alaṃdhanaḥ |  
> svadhanād eva tad dadyān nirādiṣṭa iti sthitiḥ ||

**'adātari'** dānapratibhuvo 'nyasmin pratibhuvi | **'dātā'** uttamarṇaḥ | **'vijñātaprakṛtiḥ'** vijñātaṃ prātibhāvye kāraṇaṃ bandhakādigrahaṇaṃ yasya sa tathā | **'nirādiṣṭadhanaḥ'** nirādiṣṭaṃ dhanam adhamarṇena ṛṇanistārāya yasmai sa tathā | **'alaṃdhanaḥ'** paryāptadhanaḥ | **'nirādiṣṭo'** 'tra nirādiṣṭadhanasya putro lakṣaṇayā, pitari prete tadṛṇam asau dadyād ity arthaḥ |

vyāsaḥ |

> ṛṇaṃ paitāmahaṃ pautraḥ prātibhāvyāgataṃ sutaḥ |  
> samaṃ dadyāt tatsutau tu na dāpyāv iti niścayaḥ ||

**[307]** **'samaṃ'** kalārahitam | **'tatsutau'** prapautrapautrau |

kātyāyanaḥ [561] |

> prātibhāvyāgataṃ pautrair dātavyaṃ na tu tat kvacit |  
> putreṇāpi samaṃ deyam ṛṇaṃ sarvatra paitṛkam ||

**'ṛṇaṃ'** prātibhāvyāgatam iti sambandhaḥ |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.55] |

> bahavaḥ syur yadi svāṃśair dadyuḥ pratibhuvo dhanam |  
> ekacchāyāśriteṣv eṣu dhanikasya yathāruci ||

**'ekacchāyāśritāḥ**" ekasya pratibhuvaḥ chāyāṃ sādṛśyam āśritāḥ ye pratibhuvas te tathā | yathā ekapratibhūḥ kṛtsnaṃ dravyaṃ dadyāt, evan aneke 'pi |

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.76, 84] |

> naṣṭasyānveṣaṇe kālaṃ dadyāt pratibhuve dhanī |  
> deśānurūpataḥ pakṣaṃ māsaṃ sārdham athāpi vā ||  
> nātyantaṃ pīḍanīyāḥ syur ṛṇaṃ dāpyāḥ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ |  
> svasākṣye na niyojyāḥ syur vidhiḥ pratibhuvām ayam ||

**'svasākṣye'** svayam samakṣadarśane vā |

tathā [10.82] |

> prātibhāvyaṃ tu yo dadyāt pīḍitaḥ pratibhāvitaḥ |  
> tripakṣāt parataḥ so 'rthaṃ dviguṇaṃ labdhum arhati ||

**[308]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.56] |

> pratibhūr dāpito yat tu prakāśaṃ dhanināṃ dhanam |  
> dviguṇaṃ pratidātavyam ṛṇikais tasya tad bhavet ||

kātyāyanaḥ [540] |

> yasyārthe yena yad dattaṃ vidhinābhyarthitena tu |  
> sākṣibhir bhāvitenaiva pratibhūs tat samāpnuyāt ||

**(ca) atharṇādānavidhiḥ **

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ [10.102, 103, 113] |

> parahastād gṛhītaṃ yat kusīdavidhinā ṛṇam |  
> yena yatra yathā deyam adeyaṃ vocyate 'dhunā ||  
> yācamānāya dātavyam aprakālakṛtaṃ ṛṇam |  
> pūrṇāvadhau śāntalābham abhāve ca pituḥ sutaiḥ ||

**[309]** > pitryam evāgrato deyaṃ paścād ātmīyam eva ca |  
> tayoḥ paitāmahaṃ pūrvaṃ deyam evam ṛṇaṃ sadā ||

**'prakālaḥ'** pratiniyataḥ kālo 'vadhir ity arthaḥ |

nāradaḥ [4.2] |

> pitary uparate putrā ṛṇaṃ dadyur yathāṃśataḥ |  
> vibhaktā hy avibhaktā vā yo vā tām udvahed dhuram ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.50] |

> pitari proṣite prete vyasanābhiplute 'pi vā |  
> putrapaurair ṛṇaṃ deyaṃ nihnave sākṣibhāvitam ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

> yad dṛṣṭaṃ dattaśeṣaṃ vā deyaṃ paitāmahaṃ tu tat |  
> sadoṣaṃ vyāhataṃ pitrā naiva deyam ṛṇaṃ kvacit ||  
> pitrā dṛṣṭam ṛṇaṃ yat tu kramāyātaṃ pitāmahāt |  
> nirdoṣaṃ noddhṛtaṃ putrair deyaṃ pautrais tu tad bhṛguḥ ||  
> paitāmahaṃ tu yat putrair na dattaṃ rogibhiḥ sthitaiḥ |  
> tasmād evaṃvidhaṃ pautrair deyaṃ paitāmahaṃ samam ||

**[310]** > anekārthābhiyoge 'pi yāvat saṃsādhayed dhanam |  
> sākṣibhis tāvad evāsau labhate sādhitaṃ dhanam ||  
> putrābhāve tu dātavyam ṛṇaṃ pautreṇa yatnataḥ |  
> caturthena yad ādattaṃ tat tasmād vinivartayet ||

**'sadoṣam'** dyūtamadyādiviniyuktam | **'vyāhatam'** naitad deyam iti pitrā visaṃvāditam | **'caturthena'** puruṣeṇa **'yad ādattaṃ'** yad gṛhītam **'tad vinivartayet'** na dadyād ity arthaḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.114] |

> ṛṇam ātmīyavat pitryaṃ putrair deyaṃ vibhāvitam |  
> paitāmahaṃ samaṃ deyaṃ na deyaṃ tatsutasya tu ||

**'ātmīyavat'** savṛddhikaṃ deyam ity arthaḥ |

nāradaḥ [4.4] |

> kramād avyāhataṃ prāptaṃ putrair yan narṇam uddhṛtam |  
> deyaṃ paitāmahaṃ pautrais tac caturthān nivartayet ||

**[311]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.90] |

> ṛṇaṃ lekhyakṛtaṃ deyaṃ puruṣair tribhir eva tu |  
> ādhis tu bhujyate tāvad yāvat tan na pradāpayet ||

**'ādhis tu bhujyate'** iti — ādhiṃ gṛhītvā yad ṛṇaṃ dattaṃ tad yāvan na dīyate tāvad asāv ādhir bhujyate | na caturthādipuruṣe tad ṛṇaṃ nivartata ity arthaḥ |

viṣṇuḥ [6.27–28]: "dhanagrāhiṇi prete pravrajite dvidaśa samāḥ pravasite vā tatputrapautrair dhanaṃ deyam | nātaḥ param anicchubhiḥ" |

nāradaḥ [4.24] |

> nārvāk saṃvatsarād viṃśāt pitari proṣite sutaḥ |  
> ṛṇaṃ dadyāt pitṛvye vā prete bhrātary athāpi vā ||

kātyāyanaḥ [548–49] |

> vidyamāne 'pi rogārte svadeśāt proṣite 'pi vā |  
> viṃśāt saṃvatsarād deyam ṛṇaṃ pitṛkṛtaṃ sutaiḥ ||  
> vyādhitonmattavṛddhānāṃ tathā dīrghapravāsinām |  
> ṛṇam evaṃvidhaṃ putrān jīvatām api dāpayet ||

**[312]** bṛhaspatiḥ [10.110–12] |

> sāṃnidhye 'pi pituḥ putrair ṛṇaṃ deyaṃ vibhāvitam |  
> jātyandhapatitonmattakṣayaśvitrādirogiṇaḥ ||  
> ekacchāyākṛtaṃ sarvaṃ dadyāt tu proṣite sutaḥ |  
> mṛte pitari pitraṃśaṃ pararṇaṃ na kadācana ||

nāradaḥ [4.25] |

> dāpyaḥ pararṇam eko 'pi jīvann aviyutaiḥ kṛtam |  
> mṛteṣu tu na tatputraḥ pararṇaṃ dātum arhati ||

viṣṇuḥ [6.34–36]: "avibhaktaiḥ kṛtam ṛṇaṃ yas tiṣṭhet sa dadyāt | paitṛkam avibhaktānāṃ bhrātṝṇāṃ ca | vibhaktāś ca dāyānurūpam aṃśam" |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.45] |

> avibhaktaiḥ kuṭumbārthe yad ṛṇaṃ tu kṛtaṃ bhavet |  
> dadyus tad rikthinaḥ prete proṣite vā kuṭumbini ||

nāradaḥ [4.3] |

> pitṛvyeṇāvibhaktena brātrā vā yad ṛṇaṃ kṛtam |  
> mātrā vātha kuṭumbārthe dadyus tat sarvam ṛkthinaḥ ||

**[313]** manuḥ [8.166] |

> grahītā yadi naṣṭaḥ syāt kuṭumbe ca kṛto vyayaḥ |  
> dātavyaṃ bāndhavais tat syāt pravibhaktair api svataḥ ||

nāradaḥ [4.31] |

> aprāptavyavahāraś ca svatantre 'pi hi narṇabhāk |

kātyāyanaḥ [552, 551] |

> nāprāptavyavahārais tu pitary uparate kvacit |  
> kālena vidhinā deyaṃ vaseyur narake 'nyathā ||  
> pitṝṇāṃ sūnubhir jātair dānenaivādhamād ṛṇāt |  
> vimokṣas tu yatas tasmād icchanti pitaraḥ sutam ||

nāradaḥ [4.5; vulagate 5.9] |

> icchanti pitaraḥ putrān svārthahetor yatas tataḥ |  
> uttamarṇādhamarṇābhyāṃ mām ayaṃ mokṣayiṣyati ||  
> ataḥ putreṇa jātena svārtham utsṛjya yatnataḥ |  
> ṛṇāt pitā mocanīyo yathā na narakaṃ vrajet ||  
> tapasvī cāgnihotrī ca ṛṇavān mriyate yadi |  
> tapaś caivāgnihotraṃ ca tat sarvaṃ dhanināṃ bhavet ||

**[314]** **'uttamarṇāni'** uttamānāṃ devaṛṣipitṝṇām ṛṇāni | **'adhamarṇāni'** adhamānāṃ manuṣyāṇām ṛṇāni suvarṇadhānyādīni |

bṛhasptiḥ [10.123] |

> ujjāmādikam ādāya svāmine na dadāti yaḥ |  
> sa tasya dāso bhṛtyaḥ strī paśur vā jāyate gṛhe ||

**ujjāma**śabdena ṛṇam ucyate | **ādi**śabdena nikṣepādikam ucyate |

manuḥ [8.167] |

> kuṭumbārthe 'dhyadhīno 'pi vyavahāraṃ yam ācaret |  
> svadeśe vā videśe vā taṃ vidvān na vicālayet ||

**'adhyadhīno'** dāsādiḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.121] |

> pitṛvyabhrātṛputrastrīdāsaśiṣyānujīvibhiḥ |  
> yad gṛhītaṃ kuṭumbārthe tad gṛhī dātum arhati ||

viṣṇuḥ [6.38, 39]: "vākpratipannaṃ kuṭumbinā deyam | kasyacit kuṭumbārthe kṛtaṃ vā" |

kātyāyanaḥ [542, 543, 545] |

> kuṭumbārtham aśaktena gṛhītaṃ vyādhitena vā |  
> upaplavanimittaṃ ca vidyād āpatkṛtaṃ tu tat ||

**[315]** > kanyāvaivāhikaṃ caiva pretakārye tu yat kṛtam |  
> etat sarvaṃ pradātavyaṃ kuṭumbena kṛtaṃ prabhoḥ ||  
> proṣitasyāmatenāpi kuṭumbārtham ṛṇaṃ kṛtam |  
> dāsastrīmātṛśiṣtair vā dādyāt putreṇa vā bhṛguḥ ||

nāradaḥ [4.11] |

> pitur eva niyogād vā kuṭumbabharaṇāya vā |  
> kṛtaṃ vā yad ṛṇaṃ kṛcchre dadyāt putrasya tat pitā ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.124] |

> ṛṇaṃ putrakṛtaṃ pitrā śodhyaṃ yad anumoditam |  
> sutasnehena vā dadyān nānyathā dātum arhati ||

kātyāyanaḥ [544] |

> ṛṇaṃ putrakṛtaṃ pitrā na deyam iti dharmataḥ |  
> deyaṃ pratiśrutaṃ yat syād yac ca syād anuvarṇitam ||

manuḥ [8.159, 160] |

> prātibhāvyaṃ vṛthādānam ākṣikaṃ saurikaṃ ca yat |  
> daṇḍaśulkāvaśiṣṭaṃ ca na putro dātum arhati ||  
> darśanaprātibhāvye tu vidhiḥ pūrvapracoditaḥ |  
> dānapratibhuvi prete dāyādān api dāpayet ||

**[316]** bṛhaspatiḥ [10.118] |

> saurākṣikaṃ vṛthādānaṃ kāmakrodhapratiśrutam |  
> prātibhāvyaṃ daṇḍaśulkaśeṣaṃ putraṃ na dāpayet ||

**'sauram'** madyanimittam | **'ākṣikam'** dyūtanimittam |

vyāsaḥ |

> daṇḍo vā daṇḍaśeṣo vā śulkaṃ taccheṣa eva vā |  
> na dātavyaṃ tu putreṇa yac ca na vyāvahārikam ||

**'vyāvahārikam'** vyavahārārhapuruṣakṛtam |

kātyāyanaḥ [564–565] |

> likhitaṃ muktakaṃ vāpi deyaṃ yat tu pratiśrutam |  
> parapūrvastriyai tat tu vidyāt kāmakṛtam ṛṇam ||  
> yatra hiṃsā samutpādya krodhād dravyaṃ vināśya vā |  
> uktaṃ tuṣṭikaraṃ yat tu vidyāt krodhakṛtaṃ tu tat ||

**'uktam'** pratijñātam |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.46] |

> na yoṣit patiputrābhyāṃ na putreṇa kṛtaṃ pitā |  
> dadyād ṛte kuṭumbārthān na patiḥ strīkṛtaṃ tathā ||

viṣṇuḥ [6.32]: "na strīkṛtaṃ patiputrau" |

**[317]** kātyāyanaḥ [578] |

> deyaṃ bhāryākṛtam ṛṇaṃ bhartrā putreṇa mātṛkam |  
> bhaktasyārthe kṛtaṃ yat syād abhidhāya gate diśam ||

nāradaḥ [4.18–19] |

> na ca bhāryākṛtam ṛṇaṃ kathaṃcit patyur ābhavet |  
> āpatkṛtād ṛte puṃsaḥ kuṭumbārtho hi dustaraḥ ||  
> anyatra rajakavyādhagopaśauṇḍikayoṣitām |  
> teṣāṃ tu tatparā vṛttiḥ kuṭumbaṃ ca tadāśrayam ||

**'ābhavet'** iti deyaṃ bhaved ity arthaḥ |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.48] |

> gopaśauṇḍikaśaulūṣarajakavyādhayoṣitām |  
> ṛṇaṃ dadyāt patis tāsāṃ yasmād vṛttis tadāśrayā ||

bṛhaspati-kātyāyanau |

> śauṇḍikavyādharajakagopanāvikayoṣitām |  
> adhiṣṭhātā ṛṇaṃ dāpyas tāsāṃ bhartṛkriyāsu tat ||

**[318]** **'adhiṣṭhātā'** atra patir eva | **'bhartṛkriyāsu tat'** yato bhartuḥ kartavyeṣu prayojaneṣu tad ṛṇaṃ jātaṃ tāsām ity arthaḥ |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.49] |

> pratipannaṃ striyā deyaṃ patyā vā saha yat kṛtam |  
> svyaṃ kṛtaṃ vā yad ṛṇaṃ nānyat strī dātum arhati ||

kātyāyanaḥ [546, 549?]

> bhartrā putreṇa vā sārdhaṃ kevalaṃ vātmanā kṛtam |  
> ṛṇam evaṃvidhaṃ deyaṃ nānyathā tatkṛtaṃ striyā ||  
> bhartukāmena yā bhartrā uktā deyam ṛṇaṃ tvayā |  
> aprapannāpi sā dāpyā dhanaṃ yady āśritaṃ striyā ||

**'tatkṛtam'** patiputrakṛtam | **'dhanam'** bhartṛdhanam |

nāradaḥ [4.16–17] |

> na strī patikṛtaṃ dadyād ṛṇaṃ putrakṛtaṃ tathā |  
> abhyupetād ṛte yad vā saha patyā kṛtaṃ bhavet ||  
> dadyād aputrā vidhavā niyuktā yā mumūrṣuṇā |  
> yā vā tadriktham ādadyād yato riktham ṛṇaṃ tataḥ ||

**[319]** viṣṇuḥ [6.29–30]: "saputrasya cāpy aputrasya rikthagrāhī ṛṇaṃ dadyāt | vidhanasya strīgrāhī" |

nāradaḥ [4.24, 22] |

> antimā svairiṇīnāṃ yā punarbhūḥ prathamā ca yā |  
> ṛṇaṃ tayoḥ patikṛtaṃ dadyād yas te samaśnute ||  
> adhanasya hy aputrasya mṛtasyopaiti yaḥ striyam |  
> ṛṇaṃ voḍhuḥ sa bhajate tad evāsya dhanaṃ smṛtam ||

**'svairiṇīnām antimā'** nāradenoktā yathā –

> deśadharmānavekṣya strī gurubhir yā pradīyate |  
> utpannasāhasānyasmai sāntimā svairiṇī matā || iti |

**'punarbhūḥ prathamā'** nāradenoktā [12.46] yathā –

> kanyaivākṣatayonir yā pāṇigrahaṇadūṣitā |  
> punarbhūḥ prathamā proktā punaḥ saṃskṛrakarmaṇā || iti |

atra caitayor anyasvairiṇyāpakṣayā śraiṣṭhyāt tadgrāhī tatpatikṛtam ṛṇaṃ dadyād ity arthaḥ |

**[320]** kātyāyanaḥ [567] |

> nirdhanair anapatyais tu yat kṛtaṃ śauṇḍikādibhiḥ |  
> tat strīṇām upabhoktā tu dadyāt tadṛṇam eva hi ||

nāradaḥ [4.23] |

> dhanastrīhāriputrāṇām ṛṇabhāg yo dhanaṃ haret |  
> putro 'satoḥ strīdhaninoḥ strīhārī dhaniputrayoḥ ||

**'stridhaninoḥ'** strī ca dhanaṃ ca strīdhane tadvatoḥ | strīhāridhanahāriṇor ity arthaḥ | **'strīhārī dhaniputrayor'** ity atrāsator ity anuṣaṅgaḥ | strīhāriputrayos tu vidyamānayor bāle vyasanābhibhūte draviṇānarhe ṛṇadānāsamarthe putre sati, strīhārī ṛṇaṃ dadyāt | yadā tu nirupadravo draviṇārho dhuryaś ca putro bhavati tadā sa eva ṛṇabhāk | na strīhārīty arthaḥ |

**[321]** tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ [557, 576] |

> ṛṇaṃ tu dāpayet putraṃ yadi syān nirupadravaḥ |  
> draviṇārhaś ca duryaś ca nānyathā dāpayet sutam ||  
> vyasanābhiplute putre bālo vā yatra dṛśyate |  
> dravyahṛd dāpyate tatra tasyābhāve purandhrihṛt ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.51] |

> rikthagrāha ṛṇaṃ dāpyo yoṣidgrāhas tathaiva ca |  
> putro 'nanyāśritadravyaḥ putrahīnasya rikthinaḥ ||

**'rikthagrāha ṛṇaṃ dāpyaḥ'** iti | anyādisambandhaviśeṣeṇa yo yadīyaṃ dravyaṃ gṛhṇāti sa tatkṛtam ṛṇaṃ rājñā dāpyata ity arthaḥ | **'putro 'nanyāśritadravyaḥ'** iti | na anyasmin saṃśritaṃ mātāpitroḥ sambandhi dravyaṃ yasya sa tathā | **[322]** atrāpi ṛṇaṃ dāpyata ity arthaḥ | atra ca pitṛdhanagrahaṇayogyaḥ putro vivakṣito, na tu labdhapitṛdhanaḥ | tasya rikthagrāha ity anenaiva gatārthatvāt | etac cāndhapaṅgvādeḥ pitṛdhanagrahaṇānadhikāriṇaḥ putrasya ṛṇāpakaraṇe 'dhikāro mā bhūd ity evamartham | **'rikthinaḥ'** atra rikthagrahaṇayogyāḥ pautrāḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [571–73] |

> amatenaiva putrasya pradhanā yānyam āśrayet |  
> putreṇaivāpahāryaṃ tad dhanaṃ duhitṛbhir vinā ||  
> ṛṇārtham āharet tat tu na sukhārthaṃ kathaṃcana |  
> ayukte kāreṇe yasmāt pitarau tu na dāpayet ||  
> yā svaputraṃ tu jahyāt strī samartham api putriṇī |  
> āhṛtya strīdhanaṃ tatra pitryarṇaṃ śōdhayen manuḥ ||

**[323]** **'pradhanā'** prabhūtadhanā |

nāradaḥ [4.20, 21] |

> putriṇī tu samutsṛjya putraṃ strī yānyam āśrayet |  
> tasyā ṛṇaṃ haret sarvaṃ niḥsvāyāḥ putra eva tu ||  
> yā tu sapradhanaiva strī sāpatyā vānyam āśrayet |  
> so 'syā dadyād ṛṇaṃ bhartur utsṛjed vā tathaiva tām ||

kātyāyanaḥ [574-75] |

> bālaputrādhikārthā ca bhartāraṃ yānyam āśritā |  
> āśritas tadṛṇaṃ dadyād bālaputrāvidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
> dīrghapravāsinirbandhujaḍonmattārtaliṅginām |  
> jīvatām api dātavyaṃ tat strīdravyaṃ samāśritaiḥ ||

**[324]**

**(cha) athodgrāhaṇavidhiḥ**

tatra manuḥ [8.48–49] |

> yair yair upāyair arthaṃ svaṃ prāpnuyād uttamarṇikaḥ |  
> tais tair upāyaiḥ saṃgṛhya sādhayed adhamarṇikam ||  
> dharmeṇa vyavahāreṇa chalenācaritena ca |  
> prayuktaṃ sādhayed arthaṃ pañcamena balena ca ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.87] |

> pratipannam ṛṇī dāpyaḥ sāmādibhir upakramaiḥ |  
> darmopadhibalātkārair gṛhasaṃrodhanena ca ||

kātyāyanaḥ [585–88] |

> pīḍanenoparodhena sādayed ṛṇikaṃ dhanī |  
> karmaṇā vyavahāreṇa sāntvenādau vibhāvitam ||  
> ādadītārtham evaṃ tu vyājenācaritena ca |  
> rājānaṃ svāminaṃ vipraṃ sāntvenaiva pradāpayet ||  
> rikthinaṃ suhṛdaṃ cāpi chalenaiva pradāpayet |

**[325]** tathā |

> vaṇijaḥ karṣakāś caiva śilpinaś cābravīd bhṛguḥ |  
> deśācāreṇa dāpyāḥ syur duṣṭān saṃpīḍya dāpayet ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.88, 90] |

> suhṛtsambandhisaṃdiṣṭaiḥ sāmoktyānugamena ca |  
> prāyeṇa vā ṛṇī dāpyo dharma eṣa udāhṛtaḥ ||  
> chadmanā yācitaṃ cārtham ānīya ṛṇikād dhanī |  
> anvāhitādi vāhṛtya dāpyate yatra sopadhiḥ ||  
> baddhvā svagṛham ānīya tāḍanād yair upakramaiḥ |  
> ṛṇiko dāpyate yatra balātkāraḥ sa kīrtitaḥ ||  
> dāraputrapaśūn ruddhvā kṛtvā dvāropaveśanam |  
> yatrarṇī dāpyate 'rthaṃ svaṃ tad ācaritam ucyate ||

**'suhṛtsaṃbandhisaṃdiṣṭaiḥ'** tatsuhṛdāṃ saṃbandhināṃ saṃdeśaiḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [580–84] |

> dhāryo 'varuddhas tv ṛṇikaḥ prakāśaṃ janasaṃsadi |  
> yāvan na dadyād deyaṃ ca deśācārasthithir yathā ||  
> viṇmūtraśaṅkā yasya syād dhāryamāṇasya dehinaḥ |  
> pṛṣṭhato vānugantavyaṃ nibaddhaṃ vā samutsṛjet ||  
> sa kṛtapratibhūś caiva moktavyaḥ syād dine dine |  
> āhārakāle rātrau ca nibandhe pratibhūḥ sthitaḥ ||

**[326]** > yo darśanapratibhuvaṃ nādhigacchen na cāśrayet |  
> sa cārake niroddhavyaḥ sthāpyo vāvedya rakṣiṇaḥ ||  
> na cārake niroddhavya āryaḥ prātyayikaḥ śuciḥ |  
> so 'nibaddhaḥ pramoktavyo nibaddhaḥ śapathena vā ||

**'viṇmūtraśaṅkā'** viṇmūtravegasūcanam | **'nibaddho'** niyamitaḥ | **'cārake'** kārāgṛhe |

manuḥ [8.177] |

> karmaṇāpi samaṃ kuryād dhanikasyādhamarṇikaḥ |  
> samo 'vakṛṣṭajātiś ca dadyāc chreyāṃs tu tac chanaiḥ ||

**'karmaṇāpi samaṃ kuryāt'** adhamarṇikatvenottamarṇād adharībhūtam ātmānaṃ tāvad dhanakāryakarmakaraṇenāpi samaṃ kuryād adhamarṇatvam apanayed ity arthaḥ | **'śreyān'** uttamajātīyo guṇādhikaś ca |

bṛhaspatiḥ [8.105] |

> nirdhanaṃ ṛṇikaṃ karma gṛham ānīya kārayet |  
> śauṇḍikādyaṃ brāhmaṇas tu dāpanīyaḥ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ||

**[327]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.43] |

> hīnajātiṃ parikṣīṇam ṛṇārthaṃ karma kārayet |  
> brāhmaṇas tu parikṣīṇaḥ śanair dāpyo yathodayam ||

**'yathodayam'** yathādravyotpatti |

kātyāyanaḥ [486] |

> karmaṇā kṣatraviṭchūdrān samahīnāṃs tu dāpayet |

tathā [590] |

> yadi hy ādāv anādiṣṭam aśubhaṃ karma kārayet |  
> prāpnuyāt sāhasaṃ pūrvam ṛṇān mucyeta carṇikaḥ ||

nāradaḥ [4.123] |

> atha śaktivihīnaḥ syād ṛṇī kālaviparyayāt |  
> śaktyapekṣaṃ ṛṇaṃ dāpyaḥ kāle kāle yathodayam ||

**śaktyapekṣam** ṛṇaṃ dātum | **'kālaviparyayāt'** durbhikṣādeḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.99–100] |

> pūrṇāvadhau śāntalābham ṛṇam udgrāhayed dhanī |  
> kāreyed vā ṛṇī lekhyaṃ cakravṛddhivyavasthayā ||

**[328]** **'śāntalābham'** param avṛddhiprāptam |

> dviguṇasyopari yadā cakravṛddhiḥ pragṛhyate |  
> bhogalābhas tathā tadvan mūlaṃ syāt sodayam ṛṇam ||

kātyāyanaḥ [509] |

> grāhyaṃ syād dviguṇaṃ dravyaṃ prayuktaṃ dhaninā sadā |  
> labheta cen na dviguṇaṃ punar vṛddhiṃ prakalpayet ||

manuḥ [8.154–56] |

> ṛṇaṃ dātum aśakto yaḥ kartum icchet punaḥ kriyām |  
> sa datvā nirjitāṃ vṛddhiṃ karaṇaṃ parivartayet ||  
> adarśayitvā tatraiva hiraṇyaṃ parivartayet |  
> yāvatī saṃbhaved vṛddhis tāvatīṃ dātum arhati ||  
> cakravṛddhiṃ samārūḍho deśakālavyavasthitaḥ |  
> atikrāman deśakālau na tatphalam avāpnuyāt ||

**''nirjitām'** labhyatvenātmādhīnāsaṃpannām | **'karaṇaṃ parivartayet'** anyalekhyasākṣyādi kuryāt | **'adarśayitvā'** hiraṇyaṃ dīyamānam iti śeṣaḥ | tena dhanine sarvaṃ savṛddhikaṃ hiraṇyam adatvety arthaḥ | tatraiva punaḥ karaṇaṃ parivartayet sākṣisamakṣam etad brūyāt | etāvan mūlam asmai dhārayāmi, etāvatī vṛddhir iti patre cāropayed ity arthaḥ | etac ca yāvadvṛddhi dhanaṃ dātuṃ śaknoti tāvad datvā karaṇaparivartanaṃ kāryam | **'samārūḍhaḥ'** pratipanno 'ṅgīkṛtavān iti yāvat | tatphalaṃ cakravṛddhiḥ lakṣaṇam |

**[329]** bṛhaspatiḥ [10.51, 52, 55] |

> hiraṇye dviguṇībhūte mṛte naṣṭe 'dhamarṇike |  
> dravyaṃ tadīyaṃ saṃgṛhya vikrīṇīta sasākṣikam ||  
> rakṣed vā kṛtamūlyaṃ tu daśāhaṃ janasaṃsadi |  
> ṛṇānurūpaṃ parato gṛhṇītānyat tu varjayet ||  
> svadhanaṃ ca sthirīkṛtya gaṇanākuśalair naraiḥ |  
> tadbandhujñātividitaṃ pragṛhṇan nāparādhnuyāt ||

manuḥ [8.50] |

> yaḥ svayaṃ sādhayed artham uttamarṇo 'dhamarṇikāt |  
> sa rājñā nābhiyoktavyaḥ svakaṃ saṃsādhayan dhanam ||

viṣṇuḥ [6.18]: "prayuktam arthaṃ yathā kathaṃcit saṃsādhayan na rājño vācyaḥ syāt" |

**'yathā kathaṃcit'** avarodhavañcanādinā |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.40] |

> prayuktaṃ sādhayāno 'rthaṃ na vācyo nṛpater bhavet |  
> sādhyamāno nṛpaṃ gacchan daṇḍyo dāpyaś ca tad dhanam ||

**[330]** viṣṇuḥ: "sādhyamānaś ced rājānam abhigacchet tatsamaṃ daṇḍyaḥ" |

**'tatsamam'** sādhyamānarṇasamam |

manuḥ [8.176] |

> yaḥ sādhayantaṃ chandena vedayed dhanikaṃ nṛpe |  
> sa rājñā taccaturbhāgaṃ dāpyas tasya ca tad dhanam ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.95] |

> pratipannasya dharmo 'yaṃ vyavasāyī tu saṃsadi |  
> lekhyena sākṣibhir vāpi bhāvayitvā pradāpayet ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.101] |

> anāvedya tu rājñe yaḥ saṃdigdhe 'rthe pravartate |  
> prasahya sa vineyaḥ syāt sa cāpy artho na sidhyati ||

kātyāyanaḥ [589] |

> pīḍayet tu dhanī yatra ṛṇikaṃ nyāyavādinam |  
> tasmād arthāt sa hīyeta tatsamaṃ cāpnuyād damam ||

**[331]** bṛhaspatiḥ [10.97–98] |

> nāseddhavyaḥ kriyāvādī saṃdigdhe 'rthe kathaṃcana |  
> āsedhayaṃs tv anāsedhyaṃ daṇḍyo bhavati darmataḥ ||  
> pradātavyaṃ yad bhavati nyāyatas tad dadāmy aham |  
> evaṃ yatrarṇiko brūte kriyāvādī sa ucyate ||  
> rūpasaṃkhyādilābheṣu yatra bhrāntir dvayor bhavet |  
> deyānādeyayor vāpi saṃdigdho 'rthaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||

manuḥ [8.47] |

> adhamarṇārthasiddhyartham uttamarṇena coditaḥ |  
> dāpayed dhanikasyārtham adhamarṇād vibhāvitam ||

tathā [8.55] |

> arthe 'pavyayamānaṃ tu karaṇena vibhāvitam |  
> dāpayed dhanikasyārthaṃ daṇḍaleśaṃ ca śaktitaḥ ||

tathā [8.59] |

> yo yāvan nihnuvītārthaṃ mithyā yāvati vā vadet |  
> tau nṛpeṇa hy adharmajñau dāpyau taddviguṇaṃ damam ||

**[332]** **'adhamarṇārthasiddhyartham'** adhamarṇato yo labhyo 'rthaḥ tatprāptyartham | '**uttamarṇena** **coditaḥ'** preritaḥ, atra rājā prakṛtatvāt | **'vibhāvitam'** niścitam | **'nihnuvīta'** apalapet, adhamarṇa iti sambandhaḥ | **'mithyā yāvati vā vadet'** uttamarṇa iti sambandhaḥ |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.11] |

> nihnave bhāvito dadyād dhanaṃ rājñe ca tatsamam |  
> mithyābhiyogī dviguṇam abhiyogād dhanaṃ vahet ||

vyāsaḥ |

> mithyābhiyogī dviguṇam abhiyogād dhanaṃ vahet |  
> kāraṇe vidhir eṣa syāj jitasyaikatarasya tu ||  
> prāṅnyāyavāde tu tathā yac cāsatyena yujyate |

**'abhiyogāt'** abhiyuktadhanāt | **'kāraṇe'** pratyavaskandane | **'asatyena'** mithyottareṇa |

nāradaḥ [1.55] |

> na ca mithyābhiyuñjīta doṣo mithyābhiyoginaḥ |  
> yas tatra vinayaḥ proktaḥ so 'bhiyoktāram āvrajet ||

**[333]** manuḥ [8.139] |

> ṛṇe deye pratijñāte pañcakaṃ śatam arhati |  
> apahnave taddviguṇaṃ tan manor anuśāsanam ||

yady arthaṃ vipratipadya rājasabhāyām ānīto 'dharmarṇaḥ ṛṇaṃ deyatayā pratijānīte — 'satyam asyai dhārayāmi' iti sa **pañcakaṃ śatam arhati**, daṇḍam iti śeṣaḥ | yas tu sabhāyāṃ apy apahnute — 'nāham asmai dhārayāmi' iti, sa pañcaśatād **dviguṇam**, daśakaṃ [śataṃ] daṇḍam arhati | anena saṃkalanena viṃśatitamo bhāgo daṇḍaḥ saṃpadyate | etac cāśayadoṣavyatirekeṇa bhrāntyādinā vipratipadya paścāt saṃpratipadyate tadviṣayam | yat tu 'yo yāvan nihnuvītārtham' ity atra dviguṇadamadānaṃ tadāśayadoṣeṇa tathākaraṇe 'vagantavyam | tatrādharmajñāv ity abhidhānāt |

**[334]** yamaḥ |

> ṛṇikaḥ sadhano yas tu daurātmyān na prayacchati |  
> rājñā dāpayitavyaḥ syād gṛhītvā dviguṇaṃ tataḥ ||

nāradaḥ [4.132] |

> ṛṇikaḥ sadhano yas tu daurātmyān na prayacchati |  
> rājñā dāpayitavyaḥ syād gṛhītvāṃśaṃ tu viṃśakam ||

**'viṃśakaṃ'** viṃśatitamam aṃśakam |

viṣṇuḥ [6.20–22]: "uttamarṇaś ced rājānam iyāt tadvibhāvato 'dhamarṇo rājñe dhanadaśabhāgasamaṃ daṇḍaṃ dadyāt | prāptārthaś cottamarṇo viṃśatitamam aṃśam" |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.41–42] |

> rājñādhamarṇiko dāpyaḥ sādhitād daśakaṃ śatam |  
> pañcakaṃ tu śataṃ dāpyaḥ prāptārtho 'py uttamarṇikaḥ ||

**[335]** > gṛhītānukramād dāpyo dhaninām adhamarṇikaḥ |  
> datvā tu brāhmaṇāyaiva nṛpates tadanantaram ||

kātyāyanaḥ [514, 513, 515] |

> nānarṇsamavāye tu yad yat pūrvakṛtaṃ bhavet |  
> tat tad evāgrato deyaṃ rājñaḥ syāc chrotriyād anu |  
> ekāhe likhitaṃ yac ca tatra kuryād ṛṇaṃ samam |  
> grahaṇaṃ rakṣaṇaṃ lābham anyathā tu yathākramam |

**'nānarṇasamavāye'** nānāṛṇasaṃnipāte |

**[336]** yājñavlkyaḥ [2.93] |

> lekhyasya pṛṣṭhe 'bhilikhed datvā datvā dhanaṃ ṛṇī |  
> dhanī copagataṃ dadyāt svahastaparicihnitam ||

viṣṇuḥ [6.26]: "asamagradāne lekhyāsaṃnidhāne cottamarṇaḥ svalikhitaṃ dadyāt" |

nāradaḥ [4.114] |

> gṛhītvopagataṃ dadyād ṛṇikāyodayaṃ dhanī |  
> adadad yācyamānas tu śeṣahānim avāpnuyāt ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.130] |

> dharmādinodgrāhya ṛṇaṃ yas tūpari na lekhayet |  
> na caivopagataṃ dadyāt taddvivṛddhim avāpnuyāt ||

**[337]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.94] |

> datvarṇaṃ pāṭayel lekhyaṃ śuddhyai vānyat tu kārayet |  
> sākṣimac ca bhaved yad vā tad dātavyaṃ sasākṣikam ||

viṣṇuḥ [6.24–25]: "sasakṣikam āptaṃ sasākṣikam eva dadyāt | likhitārthe praviṣṭe likhitaṃ pāṭayet" |

nāradaḥ [4.116, 112, 113] |

> lekhyaṃ dadyād viśuddharṇe tadabhāve pratiśravam |  
> dhanikarṇikayor evaṃ viśuddhiḥ syāt parasparam ||  
> brāhmaṇasya tu yad deyaṃ sānvayasya tu nāsti saḥ |  
> nikṣipet tatsakulyeṣu tadabhāve 'sya bandhuṣu ||  
> yadā tu na sakulyāḥ syuḥ na ca saṃbandhibāndhavāḥ |  
> tadā dadyād dvijātibhyas teṣv asatsv apsu nikṣipet ||

**iti bhaṭṭa[śrī]hṛdayadharātmajamahāsāṃdhivigrahika-**

**bhaṭṭaśrīmallakṣmīdharaviracite kṛtyakalpatarau**

**vyavahārakāṇde ṛṇādānādiparva**

**[338]**

## 57 nikṣepaḥ
atha nikṣepaḥ

tatra nāradaḥ [5.1] |

> svaṃ dravyaṃ yatra visrambhān nikṣipaty aviśaṅkitaḥ |  
> nikṣepo nāma tatproktaṃ vyvahārapadaṃ budhaiḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [11.13, 2] |

> ṛṇādānaṃ prayogādidāpanāntaṃ prakīrtitam |  
> nikṣepasyādhunā samyag vidhānaṃ śrūyatām iti ||  
> rājacaurādikabhayād dāyādānāṃ ca vañcanāt |  
> sthāpyate 'nyagṛhe dravyaṃ nyāsas tat parikīrtitam ||  
> anākhyātaṃ vyavahitam asaṃkhyātam adarśitam |  
> mudrāṅkitaṃ ca yad dravyaṃ tad aupanidhikaṃ smṛtam ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.65] |

> vānastham anakhyāya haste 'nyasya samarpyate |  
> dravyaṃ tad aupanidhikaṃ pratideyaṃ tathaiva tat ||

**[339]** 'vāsanam' nikṣepadravyādhārabhūtaṃ saṃpuṭādi |

kātyāyanaḥ [592, 611] |

> krayaḥ proṣitanikṣiptaṃ bandhānvāhitayācitam |  
> vaiśyavṛtyarpitaṃ caiva so 'rthas tūpanidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
> anumārgeṇa kāryeṣu amuṣmin vacanān mama |  
> dadyās tvam iti yo dattaḥ sa ihānvādhir ucyate ||

**'krayo'** 'tra krītadravyaṃ kutaścin nimittād vikretṛpārśve sthitam | **'proṣitanikṣiptaṃ'** pravasatā samarpitam | **'bandhaḥ'** ādhiḥ | **'yācitaṃ'** maṇḍanārtham ānītābharaṇādi | **'vaiśyavṛtarpitam'** vāṇijyārthaṃ yan nikṣiptam | ete sarve **'upanidhayaḥ'** [upanidhidravyavad draṣṭavyāḥ] | **'anumārgeṇa'** iti, asyārthaḥ — ekasmin yad arpitaṃ vastu, tena puruṣāntare amuṣmin svāmini tvaṃ dāsyatīti nikṣiptaṃ tad anvādhi iti |

manuḥ [8.179] |

> kulaje vṛttasampanne dharmajñe satyavādini |  
> mahāpakṣe dhaniny ārye nikṣepaṃ nikṣiped budhaḥ ||

**[340]** **'mahāpakṣe'** bahuparijane |

bṛhaspatiḥ [11.4] |

> sthānaṃ gṛhaṃ gṛhasthatvaṃ tadbalaṃ vibhavaṃ guṇān |  
> satyaṃ śaucaṃ bandhujanaṃ parīkṣya sthāpayen nidhim ||

nāradaḥ [5.2] |

> sa punar dvividhaḥ proktaḥ sākṣimān itaras tathā |  
> pratidānaṃ tathaivāsya pratyayaḥ syād viparyaye ||

**'viparyaye'** visaṃvāde | **'prayayaḥ'** śapathaḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ [11.6–9] |

> sasākṣikaṃ rahodattaṃ dvividhaṃ samudāhṛtam |  
> putravatparipālyaṃ tad vinaśyaty anavekṣayā ||  
> dadato yad bhavet puṇyaṃ hemarūpyāmbarādikam |  
> tat syāt pālayato nyāsaṃ tathā ca śaraṇāgatam ||  
> bhartṛdrohe yathā nāryāḥ puṃsaḥ putrasuhṛdvadhe |  
> doṣo bhavet tathā nyāse bhakṣitopekṣite nṛṇām ||  
> nyāsadravyaṃ na gṛhṇīyāt tannāśas tv ayaśakaraḥ |  
> gṛhītaṃ pālayed yatnāt sakṛdyācitam arpayet ||

**[341]** manuḥ [8.180, 195, 188] |

> yo yathā nikṣiped vastu yam arthaṃ yasya mānavaḥ |
