> sa tathaiva gṛhītavyo yathā dāyas tathā grahaḥ ||  
> mitho dāyaḥ kṛto yena gṛhīto mitha eva vā |  
> mitha eva pradātavyo yathā dāyas tathā grahaḥ ||  
> samudre nāpnuyāt kiṃcid yadi tasmān na saṃharet |

'dāyo' nikṣepaṇam | 'mithaḥ' anyonyam eva, asākṣikam ity arthaḥ | 'samudre' mudrāsahite nikṣepe mūṣikādinopadrute 'pi nikṣepasya dhanasya dhartā na kiṃcid dūṣaṇam āpnoti, yadi tasmān nikṣepāt pratimudrāśrāvaṇādinā nāpaharet kiṃcid ity arthaḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ [11.10] |

> sthāpitaṃ yena vidhinā yena yena yathāvidhi |  
> tathaiva tasya dātavyaṃ na deyaṃ pratyanantare ||

**[342]** **'pratyanantare'** putrādau |

manuḥ [8.185-86] |

> nikṣepopanidhī nityaṃ na deyau pratyanantare |  
> naśyato vinipāte tāv anipāte tv anāśitau ||  
> svayam eva tu yo dadyān mṛtasya pratyanantare |  
> na sa rājñā niyoktavyo na nikṣeptuś ca bandhubhiḥ ||

**'vinipāte'** deśāntaragamanādau |

atha nāradaḥ [5.9] |

> gṛhītuḥ saha yo 'rthena naṣṭo naṣṭaḥ sa dāyinaḥ |  
> daivarājakṛte tadvan na cet tajjihmakāritam ||

**'dāyinaḥ'** nikṣipetuḥ | **'tjjihmakāritam'** nikṣepagrāhikauṭilyakāritam |

manuḥ [8.189] |

> corair hataṃ jalenoṣham agninā dagdham eva ca |  
> na dadyād yadi tasmāt sa na saṃharati kiṃcana ||

**'tasmāt'** nikṣitadhanāt | **'na saṃharati'** nāparatīty arthaḥ |

'nābhyābhaveyuḥ' (GDh 12.41] ity anuvṛttau gautamaḥ [12.42]: "nidhyanvādhiyācitāvakrītādhayo naṣṭāḥ sarvān aninditān puruṣāparādhena" |

**'nidhiḥ'** nikṣepaḥ | **'avakrītaṃ'** bhāṭakagṛhītaṃ śakaṭādiḥ | **'sarvān'** putrapautrādīn rikthinaḥ | **'aninditān puruṣāparādhena'** [tena taṃ puruṣāparādham antareṇa nidhyādayaḥ pranaṣṭāḥ, **'sarvān'** putrādīn] **'nānyābhyābhaveyuḥ'** na te deyā ity arthaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [599, 600] |

> jñātvā dravyaviyogaṃ tu dātā yatra vinikṣipet |  
> sarvāpāyavināśe 'pi grahītā naiva dāpyate ||  
> grāhakasya ca yad doṣān naṣṭaṃ tadgrāhakasya tu |

**'dravyaviyogaṃ tu'** dravyasya rāṣṭre rājñaḥ upaplavādinā nāśam | **'sarvāpāyavināśe 'pi'** śaṅkitāpāyād apāyāntareṇāpi | **'grāhakasya ca'** iti, grāhakadoṣād yadi naṣṭaṃ tadgrāhakasyaiva naṣṭaṃ na tu nikṣeptuḥ | tena nikṣepagrāhiṇā na tad deyam ity arthaḥ |

**[344]** tathā [594] |

> yasya doṣeṇa yat kiṃcid vinaśyeta hriyeta vā |  
> tad dravyaṃ sodayaṃ dāpyo daivarājakṛtād vinā ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [11.12] |

> bhedenopekṣayā nyāsaṃ grahītā yadi nāśayet |  
> yācyamāno na dadyād vā dāpyas tat sodayaṃ bhavet ||

**'bhedenopekṣayā'** svadravyapṛthaktvenopekṣayā |

nāradaḥ [5.7–8] |

> yācyamānas tu yo dātur nikṣepaṃ na prayacchati |  
> daṇḍyaḥ sa rājño bhavati naṣṭe dāpyas tu tatsamam ||  
> yatrārthaṃ sādhayet tena nikṣeptur ananujñayā |  
> tatrāpi daṇḍyaḥ sa bhavet taṃ ca sodayam āvahet ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [11.13] |

> nyāsadravyeṇa yaḥ kaścit sādhayet kāryam ātmanaḥ |  
> daṇḍyaḥ sa rājño bhavati dāpyas tac cāpi sodayam ||

vyāsaḥ [kātyāyanaḥ 597] |

> bhakṣitaṃ sodayaṃ dāpyaḥ samaṃ dāpya upekṣitam |  
> kiṃcid ūnaṃ pradāpyaḥ syād dravyam ajñānanāśitam ||

**[345]** manuḥ [8.191–93] |

> yo nikṣepaṃ nārpayati yas tv anikṣipya yācate |  
> tāv ubhau coravac chāsyau dāpyau tau tatsamaṃ damam ||  
> nikṣepasyāpahartāraṃ tatsamaṃ dāpayed damam |  
> yathopanidhihartāram aviśeṣeṇa pārthivaḥ ||  
> upadhābhis tu yaḥ kaścit paradravyaṃ haren naraḥ |  
> sasahāyaḥ sa hantavyaḥ prakāśaṃ vividhari vadhaiḥ ||

matsyapurāṇe |

> yo nikṣiptaṃ nārpayati yas tv anikṣipya yācate |  
> tāv ubhau coravac chāsyau dāpyau vā dviguṇaṃ damam ||

kātyāyanaḥ [601] |

> grāhyas tūpanidhiḥ kāle kālahīnaṃ tu varjayet |  
> kālahīne dadad daṇḍaṃ dviguṇaś ca pradāpyate ||

**'grāhyaḥ'** nikṣepakāriṇā iti śeṣaḥ | **'kāle'** niratyayasamaye | **'upanidhiḥ'** ity atra 'bandhānvāhitayācitādiḥ' kātyāyanoktaḥ | **'kālahīnaṃ'** niratyayakālahīnam upanidhim | **'varjayet'** na gṛhṇīyāt | evaṃvidhe 'pi kāle nikṣepahartā pratyarpayan daṇḍya ity arthaḥ |

**[346]** bṛhaspatiḥ [11.14] |

> gṛhītvā nihnute yatra sākṣibhiḥ śapathena vā |  
> vibhāvya dāpayen nyāsaṃ tatsamaṃ vinayaṃ tathā ||

manuḥ [8.194, 187, 181–84, 196] |

> nikṣepo yaḥ kṛto yena yāvāṃś ca kulasaṃnidhau |  
> tāvān eva sa vijñeyo vibruvan daṇḍam arhati ||  
> acchalenaiva cānvicchet tam arthaṃ prītipūrvakam |  
> vicārya tasya vā vṛttaṃ sāmnaiva praiśodhayet ||  
> yo nikṣepaṃ yācamāno nikṣeptur na prayacchati |  
> sa yācyaḥ prāḍvivākena tannikṣeptur asaṃnidhau ||  
> sākṣyabhāve praṇidhibhir vayorūpasamanvitaiḥ |  
> apadeśaiś ca saṃnyasya hiraṇyaṃ tatra sārataḥ ||

**[347]** > sa yadi pratipadyeta yathānyastaṃ yathākṛtam |  
> na tatra vidyate kiṃcid yat parair abhiyujyate ||  
> teṣāṃ na dadyād yadi tu tad dhiraṇyaṃ yathāvidhi |  
> dvayaṃ nigṛhya dāpyaḥ syād iti dharmasya dhāraṇā ||  
> nikṣiptasya dhanasyaivaṃ prītyopanihitasya ca |  
> rājā vinirṇayaṃ kuryād akṣiṇvan nyāsadhāriṇam ||

**'praṇidhayaḥ'** cārāḥ | **'apadeśaiḥ saṃnyasya hiraṇyam'** ityādi, anṛtasaṃbhavān nikṣepakāriṇaṃ grāmagamanarājabhayādikam uktvātikuśalacāradvāreṇa svaṃ suvarṇādikaṃ nikṣipya kiyaty api kāle gate cārair eva yācanīya ity arthaḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ [11.15, 18] |

> rahodatte nidhau yatra visaṃvādaḥ prajāyate |  
> vibhāvakaṃ tatra dviyam ubhayor api ca smṛtam ||  
> anvāhite yācitake śilpinyāse sabandhake |  
> eṣa evodito dharmas tathā ca śaraṇāgate ||

nāradaḥ [5.14–15] |

> eṣa eva vidhir dṛṣṭo yācitānvāhitādiṣu |  
> śilpiṣūpanidhau nyāse pratinyāse tathaiva ca ||

**[348]** > pratigṛhṇāti yo daṇḍaṃ yaś ca sapradhanaṃ naraḥ |  
> tasyāpy eṣa vidhir dṛṣṭaḥ ṣaḍ ete vidhayaḥ samāḥ ||

**'pratinyāsaḥ'** parasparanyāsaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [602] |

> sarveṣūpanidhiṣv ete vidhayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ |

tathā |

> yo yācitakam ādāya na dadyāt pratiyācitaḥ |  
> sa nigṛhya balād dāpyo daṇḍyaś ca na dadāti yaḥ ||

matsyapurāṇe [242.4] |

> yo his yācitam ācāya na tad dadyāt tathā dhruvam |  
> sa nigṛhya balād dāpyo daṇḍyo vā pūrvasāhasam ||

kātyāyanaḥ [606, 609, 607] |

> yadi tat kāryam uddiśya kālaṃ pariniyamya vā |  
> yācito 'rdhakṛte tasminn aprāpte na tu dāpayet ||  
> atha kāryavipattis tu tasyaiva svāmino bhavet |  
> aprāpte vā sa kāle tu dāpyas tv ardhakṛte 'pi tat ||  
> prāptakāle kṛte kārye na dadyād yācito 'pi san |  
> tasmin naṣṭe hṛte vāpi grahītā mūlyam āvahet ||

**'tat kāryam'** vivāhādikam | **'ardhakṛte'** kārye | **'aprāpte'** kāle |

**[349]** bṛhaspatiḥ [11.20] |

> yācitaṃ svāmyam anujñātaṃ pradadan nāparādhnuyāt |

**'pradadat'** anyasmā iti śeṣaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [603, 604, 604, 596] |

> yais tu saṃskriyate nyāso divasaiḥ pariniṣṭhitaiḥ |  
> tadūrdhvaṃ sthāpayec chilpī dāpyo daivahat 'pi tam ||  
> svalpenāpi ca yat karma naṣṭaṃ ced bhṛtakasya tat |  
> paryāptaṃ ditsatas tasya vinaśyet tad agṛhṇataḥ ||  
> nyāsadoṣeṇa nāśaḥ syāc chilpinaṃ tan na dāpayet |  
> dāpayec chilpidoṣāt tat saṃskārārthaṃ yad arpitam ||  
> nyāsādikaṃ paradravyaṃ prabhakṣitam upekṣitam |  
> ajñānanāśitaṃ caiva yena dāpyaḥ sa eva tat ||

**'tam'** nyāsam | **'svalpena'** kālena | **'yat karma'** kuṇḍalādinirmāṇam | **'bhṛtakasya tat'** śilpina eva tan naṣṭam, na svāminaḥ | naitat punaḥ kartavyam | **'paryāptam'** niṣpannam | **'ditsataḥ'** śilpinaḥ | **'agṛhṇataḥ'** svāminaḥ | **'nyāsadoṣeṇa'** kuṅkumādeḥ kālavaśādidūṣaṇena |

**iti bhaṭṭahṛdayadharātmajamahāsāṃdhivigrahika-**

**bhaṭṭaśrīmallakṣmīdharaviracite kṛtyakalpatarau**

**vyavahārakāṇde nikṣepavivādaparva ||**

**[350]**
## 58 asvāmivikrayaḥ
**58 — athāsvāmivikrayaḥ**

tatra nāradaḥ [10.1] |

> nikṣiptaṃ vā paradravyaṃ naṣṭaṃ labdhvāpahṛtya vā |  
> vikrīyate 'samakṣaṃ yat sa jñeyo 'svāmivikrayaḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [12.2] |

> nikṣepānvāhitanyāsahṛtayācitabandhakam |  
> upāṃśu yena vikrītam asvāmī so 'bhidhīyate ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.169] |

> naṣṭāpahṛtam āsādya hartāraṃ grāhayen naram |  
> deśakālātipattau vā gṛhītvā svayam arpayet ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [12.6] |

> pūrvasvāmī tu tad dravyaṃ yad āgatya vicārayet |  
> tatra mūlaṃ darśanīyaṃ kretuḥ śuddhis tato bhavet ||

**[351]** 'mūlam' atra yasmāt krītam asāv ucyate |

kātyāyanaḥ [615, 617] |

> prakāśaṃ vā krayaṃ kuryān mūlaṃ vāpi samarpayet |  
> mūlānayanakālaś ca deyo yojanasaṃkhyayā ||  
> yadā mūlam upanyasya punar vādī krayaṃ vadet |  
> āharen mūlam evāsau na krayeṇa prayojanam ||

**'prakāśaṃ krayaṃ kuryāt'** krayaṃ prakāśayed ity arthaḥ |

vyāsaḥ |

> mūle samāhṛte kretā nābhiyojyaḥ kathaṃcana |  
> mūlena saha vādas tu nāṣṭikasya tadā bhavet ||

**'nāṣṭikasya'** naṣṭadhanasvāminaḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ [12.7] |

> vikretā darśito yatra hīyate vyavahārataḥ |  
> kretṛrājñor mūladamau pradadyāt svāmine dhanam ||

manuḥ [8.197–99, 201–02] |

> vikrīṇīte parasya svaṃ yo 'svāmī svāmyasaṃmataḥ |  
> na taṃ nayena sākṣyaṃ tu stenam astenamāninam ||

**[352]** > avahāryo bhavec caiṣa sānvayaḥ ṣaṭchataṃ damam |  
> niranvayo 'napasaraḥ prāptaḥ syāc caurakilbiṣam ||  
> anena vidhinā śāsyaḥ kurvann asvāmivikrayam |  
> ajñānāj jñānapūrvaṃ tu cauravad daṇḍam arhati ||  
> vikrayād yo dhanaṃ kiṃcid gṛhṇīyāt kulasaṃnidhau |  
> krayeṇa sa viśuddhas tu nyāyato labhate dhanam ||  
> atha mūlam anāhāryaṃ prakāśakrayaśodhitam |  
> adaṇḍyo mucyate rājñā nāṣṭiko labhate dhanam ||

**'na taṃ nayeta sākṣyam'** iti, na taṃ kvāpi pramāṇīkuryād ity arthaḥ | **'avahāryaḥ'** daṇḍyaḥ | **'sānvayaḥ'** saṃbandhī bhrātṛjādiḥ | **'ṣaṭcchatam'** paṇānām iti śeṣaḥ | **'anapasaraḥ'** apasaraty anena svāminaḥ sakāśād dhanam iti pratigrahādir dhanāgamopāyo 'pasaraḥ sa na vidyate yasya sa tathā |  etac ca bhāguri-medhātithi-vṛttikārāṇāṃ matam | **'vikrayāt'** āpaṇadeśāt | etac ca vikrīyate 'sminn iti vyutpattyā | **'kulasaṃnidhau'** vyavahartṛsamūhasamakṣam | **'nyāyataḥ krayeṇa'** iti sambandhaḥ | tena ucitamūlyakrayeṇety arthaḥ |

**[353]** kātyāyanaḥ [614] |

> nāṣṭikas tu prakurvīta taddhanaṃ jñātṛbhiḥ svakam |  
> adattatyaktavikrītaṃ kṛtvā svaṃ labhate dhanam ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.171] |

> āgamenopabhogena naṣṭaṃ bhāvyam ato 'nyathā |

manu-yamau [8.197] |

> asvāminā kṛto yas tu dāyo vikraya eva vā |  
> akṛtaḥ sa tu vijñeyo vyavahāre yathāsthitiḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [612] |

> asvāmivikrayaṃ dānam ādhiṃ ca vinivartayet |

**'asvāmivikrayam'** avidyamānasvāmivikrayam |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.168] |

> svaṃ labhetānyavikrītaṃ kretur doṣo 'prakāśite |

nāradaḥ [10.2] |

> dravyam asvāmivikrītaṃ prāpya svāmī samāpnuyāt |

**'prāpya'** upalabhya |

kātyāyanaḥ [620] |

> yadi svaṃ naiva kurute jñātṛbhir nāṣṭiko dhanam |  
> prasaṅgavinivṛttyarthaṃ cauravad daṇḍam arhati ||

**[354]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.171] |

> āgamenopabhogena naṣṭaṃ bhāvyam ato 'nyathā |  
> pañcabandho damas tatra rājñe tenāvibhāvite ||

**'ato 'nyathā'** nāṣṭikenāvibhāvite | **'pañcabandhaḥ'** pañcamo 'ṃśaḥ | **'tatra'** naṣṭadravya |

kātyāyanaḥ [613, 618, 616] |

> abhiyoktā dhanaṃ kuryāt prathamaṃ jñātṛbhiḥ svakam |  
> paścād ātmaviśuddhyarthaṃ krayaṃ kretā svabandhubhiḥ ||  
> asamāhāryamūlas tu krayam eva viśodhayet |  
> viśodhite kraye rājñā vaktavyaḥ sa na kiṃcana ||  
> prakāśaṃ ca krayaṃ kuryāt sādhubhir jñātibhiḥ svakaiḥ |  
> na tatrānyā kriyā proktā daivikī na ca mānuṣī ||

viṣṇuḥ [5.164]: "ajñānataḥ prakāśaṃ yaḥ paradravyaṃ krīṇīyāt tasya na doṣaḥ | kretā mūlyam avāpnoti | svāmī dravyam avāpnuyāt" |

**[355]** nāradaḥ [10.2] |

> prakāśakrayataḥ śuddhiḥ kretuḥ steyaṃ rahaḥkrayāt |

bṛhaspatiḥ [12.3,4] |

> yena krītaṃ tu mūlyena prāg adhyakṣaniveditam |  
> na tatra vidyate doṣaḥ stenaḥ syād upadhikrayāt ||  
> antargṛhe bahir grāmān niśy upāṃśv asato janāt |  
> hīnamūlyaṃ ca yat krītaṃ jñeyo 'sāv upadhikrayaḥ ||

nāradaḥ [7.3] |

> asvāmyanumatād dāsād asataś ca janād rahaḥ |  
> hīnamūlyam avelāyāṃ krīṇaṃs taddoṣabhāg bhavet ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.168] |

> svaṃ labhetānyavikrītaṃ kretur doṣo 'prakāśite |  
> hīnād raho hīnamūlye velāhīne ca taskaraḥ ||

viṣṇuḥ [5.166]: "yady aprakāśaṃ hīnamūlyaṃ ca krīṇīyāt tadā kretā vikretā ca cauravac chasyau" |

**[356]** kātyāyanaḥ [619] |

> anupasthāpayan mūlaṃ krayaṃ vāpy aviśodhayan |  
> yathābhiyogaṃ dhanine dhanaṃ dāpyo damaṃ ca saḥ ||

nāradaḥ [10.4] |

> na gūhetāgamaṃ kretā śuddhis tasya tadāgatāt |  
> viparyaye tulyadoṣaḥ sarvaṃ taddaṇḍam arhati ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [12.9] |

> pramāṇahīnavāde tu puruṣāpekṣayā nṛpaḥ |  
> samanyūnādhikatvena svayaṃ kuryād vinirṇayam ||

nikṣepoktaprakāreṇa gūḍhacāraprayogaṃ kṛtvā puruṣāṇāṃ dharmādharmayoḥ samanyūnādhikabhāvaṃ niścitya svayam eva rājā nirṇayed ity arthaḥ |

tathā [12.10–12] |

> vaṇigvīthīparigataṃ vijñātaṃ rājapūruṣaiḥ |  
> avijñātāśrayāt krītaṃ vikretā yatra vā mṛtaḥ ||  
> svāmī datvārdhamūlaṃ tu pragṛhṇīta svakaṃ dhanam |  
> ardhaṃ dvayor api hṛtaṃ tatra syāt dvyavahārataḥ ||  
> avijñātakrayo doṣas tathā cāparipālanam |  
> etad dvayaṃ samākhyātaṃ dravyahānikaraṃ buddhaiḥ ||

**[357]** marīciḥ |

> vaṇigvīthīparigataṃ vijñātaṃ rājapūruṣaiḥ |  
> divā gṛhītaṃ yat kretā sa śuddho labhate dhanam ||  
> avijñātaniveśatvād yatra mūlyaṃ na labhyate |  
> hānis tatra samā kalpyā kretṛnāṣṭikayor dvayoḥ ||

yājñavlkyaḥ [2.172] |

> hṛtaṃ praṇaṣṭaṃ yad dravyaṃ parahastā avāpnuyāt |  
> anivedya nṛpe daṇḍyaḥ sa tu ṣaṇṇavatiṃ paṇān ||

**'hṛtaṃ praṇaṣṭaṃ'** vā caurādihastasthaṃ **'dravyaṃ'** madīyam anenāpahṛtam iti nṛpasyānivedyaiva yo gṛhṇāti **'sa daṇḍyaḥ'** taskarapracchādakatvena duṣṭatvāt |

**vyavahārakāṇḍe kṛtyakapatarāv asvāmivikrayaḥ |**

**[358]**

## 59 saṃbhūyasamuttthānam
atha saṃbhūyasamuttthānam

tatra nāradaḥ [6.1] |

> vaṇikprabhṛtayo yatra karma saṃbhūya kurvate |  
> tatsaṃbhūyasamutthānaṃ vyavahārapadaṃ smṛtam ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [13.3, 1] |

> aśaktālasarogārtamandabhāgyanirāśrayaiḥ |  
> vāṇijyādyāḥ sahaitais tu na kartavyāḥ budhaiḥ kriyāḥ ||  
> kulīnadakṣānalasaiḥ prājñair nānṛtavādibhiḥ |  
> āyavyayajñaiḥ śucibhiḥ śūraiḥ kuryāt saha kriyām ||

nāradaḥ [6.2] |

> phalahetor upāyena karma saṃbhūya kurvatām |  
> ādhārabhūtaḥ prakṣepas tenottiṣṭheyur aṃśataḥ ||

**[359]** bṛhaspatiḥ [13.5] |

> samo nyūno 'dhiko vāṃśo yena kṣiptas tathaiva ca |  
> vyayaṃ dadyāt karma kuryāl lābhaṃ gṛhṇīta caiva hi ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.259] |

> samavāyena vaṇijāṃ lābhārthaṃ karma kurvatām |  
> lābhālābhau yathādravyaṃ yathā vā saṃvidā kṛtau ||

kātyāyanaḥ [624] |

> samavetās tu ye kecic chilpino vaṇijo 'pi vā |  
> avibhajya pṛthagbhūtaiḥ prāptaṃ tatra samaṃ phalam ||

nāradaḥ [6.4] |

> bhāṇḍapiṇḍavyayoddhārabhārasārānvavekṣaṇe |  
> kuryus te 'vyabhicāreṇa samaye sve vyavasthitāḥ ||

**'bhāṇḍam'** vikreyadravyam | **'piṇḍam'** pātheyam |

vyāsaḥ |

> samakṣaṃ asamakṣaṃ vāvañcayantaḥ parasparam |  
> nānāpaṇyānusāreṇa prakuryur krayavikrayau ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [13.6–9] |

> parīkṣakāḥ sākṣiṇaś ca ta evoktāḥ parasparam |  
> saṃdigdhe 'rthe pañcanārthā na ced vidveṣasaṃyutāḥ ||

**[360]** > yaḥ kaścid vañcakas teṣāṃ vijñātaḥ krayavikraye |  
> śapathaiḥ sa viśodhyaḥ syāt sarvavādeṣv ayaṃ vidhiḥ ||  
> kṣayo hānir yadā tatra daivarājakṛto bhavet |  
> sarveṣām eva sā proktā kalpanīyā yathāṃśataḥ ||  
> anirdiṣṭo vāryamāṇaḥ pramādād yas tu nāśayet |  
> tenaiva tad bhaved deyaṃ sarveṣāṃ samavāyinām ||

nāradaḥ [6.5] |

> pramādān nāśitaṃ dapyaḥ pratiṣiddhaṃ ca yad bhavet |  
> asaṃdiṣṭaṃ ca yat kuryāt sarvaiḥ saṃbhūyakāribhiḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.260] |

> pratiṣiddham anādiṣṭaṃ pramādād yac ca nāśitam |  
> sa tad dadyād viplavāc ca rakṣitā daśamāṃśabhāk ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [13.11] |

> rājadaivabhayād yas tu svaśaktyā paripālayet |  
> tasyāṃśaṃ daśamaṃ datvā gṛhṇīyuḥ svāṃśato 'pare ||

**[361]** nāradaḥ [6.6] |

> daivataspararājāgnivyasane samupasthite |  
> yas tu svaśaktyā rakṣet tu tasyāṃśo daśamaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [631] |

> caurataḥ salilād agner dravyaṃ yas tu samāharet |  
> tasyāṃśo daśamo dāpyaḥ sarvadravyeṣv ayaṃ vidhiḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.265] |

> jihmaṃ tyajeyur nirlābam aśakto 'nyena kāreyet |

**'jihmam'** vañcakam | **'nirlābham'** lābham ācchidya | **'tyajeyuḥ'** saṃbhūyakāriṇaḥ | **'aśaktaḥ'** [asamarthaḥ] bhāṇḍapiṇḍavyayādyavekṣaṇe |

nāradaḥ [6.4] |

> bhāṇḍapiṇḍavyayoddhārabhārasārānvavekṣaṇam |  
> kuryus te 'vyabhicāreṇa samaye sve vyavasthitāḥ ||

nāradaḥ [6.7] |

> ekasya cet syād dvyasanaṃ dāyādo 'sya tad āpnuyāt |  
> anyo vāsati dāyāde śaktaś cet sarva eva vā ||

**[362]** tathā [6.16] |

> kaścic cet saṃcaran deśān preyād abhyāgato vaṇik |  
> rājāsya bhāṇḍaṃ tad rakṣed yāvad dāyādadarśanam ||

**'vyasanam'** maraṇarūpam | **'anyo vā'** ityādi | **'asati dāyāde'** saṃbhūyakāriṇāṃ madhye yaḥ **'śaktaḥ'** pradhānībhūto 'sau tad dravyaṃ gṛhṇīyāt | ata **'sarva eva'** tulyās tadā sarva eva tad dravyaṃ gṛhṇīyur ity arthaḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ [13.14, 15] |

> yadā tatra vaṇik kaścit pramīyet pramādataḥ |  
> tasya bhāṇḍaṃ darśanīyaṃ niyuktai rājapūruṣaiḥ ||  
> yadā kaścit samāgacchet tatra rikthaharo naraḥ |  
> svāmyaṃ vibhāvayed anyaiḥ sa tadā labdhum arhati ||

nāradaḥ [6.17] |

> dāyāde 'sati bandhubhyo jñātibhyo vā tad arpayet |  
> tad abhāve suguptaṃ tad dhārayed daśavatsarān ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [13.16, 17] |

> rājādadīta ṣaḍbhāgaṃ navamaṃ daśamaṃ tathā |  
> śūdraviṭkṣatrajātīnāṃ viprād gṛhṇīta viṃśakam ||  
> tryabdād ūrdhvaṃ tu nāgacched yatra svāmī kathaṃcana |  
> tadā gṛhṇīta tad rājā brahmasvaṃ brāhmaṇān śrayet ||

**[363]** baudhāyanaḥ [1.18.16]: "abrāhmaṇasya praṇaṣṭasvāmikaṃ rikthaṃ saṃvatsaraṃ paripālya rājā haret" |

atra ca praṇaṣṭasvāmikadravye ekavarṣatrivarṣadaśavarṣadhāraṇavikalpānāṃ vyavasthā tat paradeśavartidūrataradūratamadeśavartitadīyaputrādidāyādavārtāyāṃ satyāṃ nānāvidhānekagamanapratibandhasaṃbhave cāvagantavyam |

nāradaḥ [6.18, 8] |

> asvāmikam adāyādaṃ daśavarṣasthitaṃ tataḥ |  
> rājā tad ātmasāt kuryād evaṃ dharmo na hīyate ||  
> ṛtvijāṃ vyasane 'py evam anyas tat karma nistaret |  
> labhate dakṣiṇābhāgaṃ sa ca tasmāt prakalpitam ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [13.18] |

> evaṃ kriyāprapannānāṃ yadā kaścid vipadyate |  
> tadbandhunā kriyā kāryā sarvair vā sahakāribhiḥ ||

**'kriyā'** atra tasya kartavyārtvijyādikā |

śaṅkhalikhitau: "tatra ced anuprāpte savane ṛtviṅ mriyeta tatra kiṃ kāryam iti jijñāsā tasya sagotro 'tha śiṣyo vā tat kāryam anupūrayet | atha ced abāndhavas tato 'nyam ṛtvijaṃ vṛṇuyāt" |

**[364]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.265] |

> jihmaṃ tyajeyur nirlābham aśakto 'nyena kārayet |  
> anena vidhinākhyāta ṛtvikkarṣakakarmiṇām ||

manuḥ [8.206–07] |

> ṛtvig yadi vṛto yajñe savakarma parihāpayet |  
> tasya karmānurūpeṇa deyo 'ṃśaḥ sahakartṛbhiḥ ||  
> dakṣiṇāsu ca dattāsu svakarma parihāpayet |  
> kṛtsnam eva labhetāṃśam anyenaiva ca kārayet ||

manu-bṛhaspatī [m. 8.210; bṛ. 13.20] |

> sarveṣām ardhino mukhyās tadardhenārdhino 'pare |  
> tṛtīyinas tṛtīyāṃśāś caturthāṃśās tu pādinaḥ ||

**'sarveṣām'** ṣoḍaśānām ṛtvijām, yā samuditā dakṣiṇā tasyām ardhaṃ gṛhṇanti **'mukhyāḥ'** hotṛbrāhmādhvaryūdgātāraḥ | īṣannyūnārdhagrahaṇe 'pi sāmīpyena **'ardhina'** ucyante | **'apare'** maitrāvaruṇabrāhmaṇācchaṃsipratiprasthātṛprastotāraḥ, te **[365]** mukhyaṛtviggṛhītadakṣiṇārdhagrahaṇenārdhina ucyante | ye **'tṛtīyinaḥ'** acchāvākaneṣṭragnīdhrapratihartāras te mukhyārthagṛhītasya tṛtīyam aṃśaṃ labhante | **'pādinaḥ'** grāvastotṛpotṛnetṛsubrahmaṇyāḥ | ete mukhartviggṛhītasya caturtham aṃśaṃ labhante |

manuḥ [8.211, 208] |

> saṃbhūya svāni karmāṇi kurvadbhir iha mānavaiḥ |  
> anena kramayogena kartavyāṃśaprakalpanā ||  
> yasya karmaṇi yās tu syur uktāḥ pratyaṃśadakṣiṇāḥ |  
> sa eva tā ādadīta bhajeran sarva eva vā ||

**[365]** **'pratyaṃśadakṣiṇāḥ'** aṃśam aṃśaṃ prati ṛtvigviśeṣasaṃbandhena samāmnātā dakṣiṇāḥ | tāḥ kiṃ yas karmaṇi yatsaṃbandhena samāmnātāḥ — yathā abhiṣecanīye 'hiraṇmayau prākāśāv adhvaryave dadāti' iti tenaivādhvaryuṇā gṛhītavyā, utādhvaryur dvāramātram, sarve vibhajya gṛhṇīrann iti saṃśayaḥ |

manu-bṛhaspatī [ma. 8.209; bṛ. 13.19] |

> rathaṃ hared athādhvaryur brahmādhāne ca vājinam |  
> hotā cāpi hared aśvam udgātā cāpy anaḥ kraye ||

pūrvoktasaṃśaye 'yaṃ nirṇayaḥ | keṣāṃcic chāśinām ādhāne adhavaryave rathaḥ āmnāyate, brahmaṇe ca veganān aśvaḥ, hotra cāśvaḥ, udgātre somakraye somavāhakaṃ **'anaḥ'** śakaṭam | evaṃ vyavasthāyāṃ dadātir mukhyārtho bhavet | puruṣasaṃyogaś ca nādṛṣṭārthaḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ [13.21] |

> āgantukāḥ kramāyātās tathā caiva svayaṃ kṛtāḥ |  
> trividhās te samākhyātā vartitavyaṃ tathaiva taiḥ ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: "athartviji vṛttte paścād anyaṃ vṛṇuyāt | pūrvāhūtasyaiva dakṣiṇā | paścād āhūtaḥ kiṃcil labheta | pravasec cet tatkālaṃ nimittaṃ cāpekṣya yakṣyamāṇas tatkālam udīkṣeta | **[367]** nāntarā yajeta | syād ātyayiko vā | taṃ kratuṃ sampādayeta | proṣya pratyāgataś ca kiṃcil labheta | atha cet pratiṣiddhaḥ pravaset kāmād anuprāpte savane ṛtvik cchataṃ daṇḍyaḥ | sa eva cāduṣṭas tasya ṛtvikkulopādhyāyaḥ | evaṃ vyādhitapatitonmattaprahīṇapradhvasteṣu saṃprasādhakaraṇam ṛtvikṣu | kāmāc ced apatitaṃ yājyaṃ tyajed ṛtvik prāpnuyād dviśataṃ damam | yājyaś caiva tad evāpnuyāt tyāge ṛtvijo 'patitasya | kāmaṃ patitam aśrotriyaṃ tyajed yājyaṃ cābhiśastam adātāram" |

**'pūrvāhutasyaiva dakṣiṇā'** iti, pūrvāhūtasya dāyādānāṃ sā dakṣiṇā | **'kālaṃ nimittaṃ cāvekṣya'** **'kālaṃ'** pakṣam āsādikam, **'nimittaṃ'** vivāhādiprayojanaṃ buddhvā | atyaya eva **'ātyayikaḥ'** | tena yadi tatpratīkṣaṇe yajñātyayo bādhaḥ saṃbhāvyeta tadā ṛtvigantareṇa taṃ yajñaṃ niṣpādayed ity arthaḥ | **'anuprāpte savane'** savanakāla upasthite | **'sa eva vāduṣṭaḥ'** tasya yajamānasya yaḥ kulopādhyāyaḥ sa proṣito 'py aduṣṭa eva | **'prahīṇaḥ'** abhiśāpādinā tyaktaḥ | **'pradhvastaḥ'** ativṛddhaḥ | **'saṃprasādakaraṇaṃ'** ṛtvigantaragrahaṇe 'py anujñāgrahaṇam |

**[368]** manuḥ [8.388] |

> ṛtvijaṃ yas tyajed yājyo yājyaṃ cartvik tyajed yadi |  
> śaktaṃ karmaṇy aduṣṭaṃ ca tayor daṇḍaḥ śataṃ śatam ||

dviśataikaśatadaṇḍayoḥ kāmākāmakṛtā vyavasthā |

nāradaḥ [6.10, 9, 11] |

> ṛtvik ca trividho dṛṣṭaḥ pūrvair juṣṭaḥ svayaṃkṛtaḥ |  
> yadṛcchayā ca yaḥ kuryād ārtvijyaṃ prītipūrvakam ||  
> ṛtvigyājyam aduṣṭaṃ yas tyajed anapakāriṇam |  
> aduṣṭaṃ cartvijaṃ yājyo vineyau tāv ubhāv api ||  
> kramāyāte hy eṣa dharmo mṛteṣv ṛtvikṣu ca svayam |  
> yādṛcchake tu saṃyājye tyakte nāsty eva kilbiṣam ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [13.4, 22] |

> prayogaṃ kurvate ye tu hemadhānyarasādinā |  
> samanyūnādhikair aṃśair lābhas teṣāṃ tathāvidhaḥ ||  
> bahūnāṃ saṃmato yas tu dadyād eko dhanaṃ naraḥ |  
> karaṇaṃ kārayed vāpi sarvair eva kṛtaṃ bhavet ||

**[369]** [**'prayogaṃ'** lābhārtham ] **'karaṇaṃ'** lekhyādi | ]

tathā [13.23–27, 29–31, 27, 32–34 ??] |

> jñātisambandhisuhṛdām ṛṇaṃ deyaṃ sabandhakam |  
> anyeṣāṃ lagnakopetaṃ lekhyasākṣiyutaṃ tathā ||  
> svecchādeyaṃ hiraṇyaṃ tu rasadhānyaṃ tu sāvadhi |  
> deśasthityā pradātavyaṃ gṛhītavyaṃ tathaiva tat ||  
> samavetais tu yad dattaṃ prārthanīyaṃ tathaiva tat |  
> na yācate ca yaḥ kaścil lābāt sa parihīyate ||  
> prayogaḥ pūrvam ākhyātaḥ samāsenodito 'dhunā |  
> śrūyatāṃ karṣakādīnāṃ vidhānam idam ucyate ||  
> bāhyakarṣakabījādyaiḥ kṣetrāpakaraṇena ca |  
> ye samānās tu taiḥ sārdhaṃ kṛṣiḥ kāryā vijānatā ||  
> vivītanagarābhyāse tathā rājapathasya ca |  
> ūṣaraṃ mūṣikavyāptaṃ kṣetraṃ yatnena varjayet ||

**[370]** > gartānūpam susekaṃ ca samantāt kṣetrasaṃyutam |  
> prakṛṣṭaṃ ca kṛtaṃ kāle vāpayan phalam aśnute ||  
> kṛśātivṛddhaṃ kudraṃ ca rogiṇaṃ prapalāyinam |  
> kāṇaṃ khañjaraṃ ca nādadyād vāhyaṃ prājñaḥ kṛṣīvalaḥ ||  
> vāhyabījātyayād yasya kṣetrahāniḥ prajāyate |  
> tenaiva sā pradātavyā sarveṣāṃ kṛṣijīvinām ||  
> eṣa dharmaḥ samākhyātaḥ kīnāśānāṃ sanātanaḥ |  
> hiraṇyarūpyasūrāṇāṃ kāṣṭapāṣāṇacarmaṇām ||  
> saṃskartā ca kalābhijñaḥ śilpī cokto manīṣibhiḥ |  
> hemakārādayo yatra śilpaṃ sambhūya kurvate ||  
> karmānurūpaṃ nirveśaṃ labheraṃs tu yathāṃśataḥ |

'**vivīta**'śabdena yavasādhyarthaṃ rakṣito bhūpradeśa ucyate | **'kīnāśāḥ'** kṛṣīvalāḥ | **'nirveśo'** atra bhṛtiḥ |

**[371]** kātyāyanaḥ [632] |

> śikṣakābhijñakuśalā ācāryāś ceti śilpinaḥ |  
> ekadvitricaturbhāgāt vaheyus te yathottaram ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [13.36–39] |

> harmyaṃ devagṛhaṃ vāpi dhārmikopaskarāṇi ca |  
> saṃbhūya kurvatāṃ caiṣāṃ pramukho dvyaṃśam arhati ||  
> nartakānām eṣa eva sadbhir udāhṛtaḥ |  
> tālajño labhate 'dhyardhaṃ gāyanās tu samāṃśinaḥ ||  
> svāmyājñayā tu yac coraiḥ paradeśāt samāhṛtam |  
> rājñe datvā tu ṣaḍbhāgaṃ bhajeyus te yathāṃśataḥ ||  
> caturo 'ṃśān tathā mukhyaḥ śūras tryaṃśam avāpnuyāt |  
> samarthas tu hared dvyaṃśaṃ śeṣās tv anye samāṃśinaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [633–35, 637] |

> pararāṣṭrād dhanaṃ yat syāc coraiḥ svāmyājñayā hṛtam |  
> rājñe daśāṃśam āhṛtya vibhajeran yathāvidhi ||

**[372]** > corāṇāṃ mukhyabhūtas tu caturo 'ṃśāṃs tato haret |  
> śūro 'ṃśāṃs trīn samartho dvau śiṣṭās tv ekaikam eva ca ||  
> teṣāṃ ca prasṛtānāṃ yo grahaṇaṃ samavāpnuyāt |  
> tanmokṣaṇārthaṃ yad dattaṃ tasya kāryā samakriyā ||  
> vaṇijāṃ karṣakāṇāṃ ca corāṇāṃ śilpināṃ tathā |  
> aniyamyāṃśakartṝṇāṃ sarveṣām eṣa nirṇayaḥ ||

**iti vyavahārakāṇḍe kṛtyakalpatarau sambhūyasamutthānam |**

**[373]**

## 60 dattāpradānikam
atha dattāpradānikam

tatra nāradaḥ [7.1–3] |

> datvā dravyam asamyag yaḥ punar ādātum icchati |  
> dattāpradānikaṃ nāma vyavahārapadaṃ hi tat ||  
> adeyam atha deyaṃ ca dattaṃ cadattam eva ca |  
> vyavahāreṣu vijñeyo dānamārgaś caturvidhaḥ ||  
> tatrehāṣṭāv adeyāni deyam ekavidhaṃ smṛtam |  
> dattaṃ saptavidhaṃ dadyād adattaṃ dvādaśātmakam ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [14.2] |

> sāmānyaṃ putradārādhisarvasvanyāsayācitam |  
> pratiśrutaṃ tathānyasya na deyam iti saṃmatam ||

nāradaḥ [7.4–5] |

> anvāhitaṃ yācitakam ādhiḥ sāmānyakaṃ ca yat |  
> nikṣepaḥ putradāraṃ ca sarvasvaṃ cānvaye sati ||

**[374]** > āpatsv api hi kaṣṭāsu vartamānena dehinā |  
> adeyāny āhur ācāryā yac cānyasmai pratiśrutam ||

dakṣaḥ |

> sāmānyaṃ yācitaṃ nyāsa ādhir dārāś ca taddhanam |  
> anvāhitaṃ ca nikṣepaḥ sarvasvaṃ cānvaye sati ||  
> āpatsv api na deyāni nava vastūni paṇḍitaiḥ |  
> yo dadāti sa mūḍhātmā prāyaścittīyate naraḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.175] |

> svakuṭumbāvarodhena deyaṃ dārasutād ṛte |  
> nānvaye sati sarvasvaṃ yac cānyasmai pratiśrutam ||

kātyāyanaḥ [638–39] |

> vikrayaṃ caiva dānaṃ ca na deyāḥ syur anicchavaḥ |  
> dārāḥ putrāś ca sarvasvam ātmanaiva tu yojayet ||

**[375]** > āpatkāle tu kartavyaṃ dānaṃ vikraya eva vā |  
> anyathā na pravarteta iti śāstraviniścayaḥ ||

vasiṣṭhaḥ [15.1–5]: "śukraśoṇitasaṃbhavaḥ puruṣo mātṛpitṛnimittakaḥ | tasya pradānavikrayaparityāgeṣu mātāpitarau prabhavataḥ | na caikaṃ putraṃ dadyāt pratigṛhṇīyād vā | sa hi saṃtānāya pūrveṣām | na tu strī putraṃ dadyāt pratigṛhṇīyād vā, anyatrānujñānād bhartuḥ" |

bṛhaspatiḥ [14.3] |

> kuṭumbabhaktavasanād dayeṃ yad atiricyate |  
> madhvāsvādo viṣaṃ paścād dātur dharmo 'nyathā bhavet ||

kātyāyanaḥ [640] |

> sarvasvaṃ gṛhavarjaṃ tu kuṭumbabharaṇādhikam |  
> yad dravyaṃ tat svakaṃ deyam adeyaṃ syād ato 'nyathā ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [14.4–6, 8] |

> saptāgamād gṛhakṣetrād yad yat kṣetraṃ pradīyate |  
> pitryaṃ vātha svayaṃ prāptaṃ tad dātavyaṃ vivakṣitam ||  
> svecchādeyaṃ svayaṃ prāptaṃ bandhācāraṇabandhakam |  
> vaivāhike kramāyāte sarvadānaṃ na vidyate ||

**[376]** > saudāyikaṃ kramāyātaṃ śauryaprāptaṃ ca yad bhavet |  
> strījñātisvāmyanujñātaṃ dattaṃ siddhim āpnuyāt ||  
> vibhaktā vāvibhaktā vā dāyādāḥ sthāvare samāḥ |  
> eko hy anīśaḥ sarvatra dānādhamanavikraye ||

**'saptāgamāt'** —

> saptavittāgamāḥ dharmyā dāyo lābhaḥ krayo jayaḥ |  
> prayogaḥ karmayogaś ca satpratigraha eva ca ||

iti manūkteḥ [10.115] saptavidhaśauryādyāgamalabdhadhanād uddhṛtya tad dhanam āśritya gṛhakṣetrādi dātavyam | na tv anāgamam ity arthaḥ |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.176] |

> pratigrahaḥ prakāśaḥ syāt sthāvarasya viśeṣataḥ |  
> deyaṃ pratiśrutaṃ caiva datvā nāpaharet punaḥ ||

**[377]** kātyāyanaḥ [642] |

> svecchayā yaḥ pratiśrutya brāhmaṇāya pratigraham |  
> na dadyād ṛṇavad dāpyaḥ prāpnuyāt pūrvasāhasam ||

matsyapurāṇe [227.4] |

> pratiśrutyāpradātāraṃ suvarṇaṃ daṇḍayen nṛpaḥ |

hārītaḥ |

> pratiśrutārthadāne tu dattasyocchedanena ca |  
> vividhān narakān yāti tiryagyonau ca jāyate ||  
> vācā ca yat pratijñātaṃ karmaṇā nopapāditam |  
> ṛṇaṃ tad dharmasaṃyuktam iha loke paratra ca ||

gautamaḥ [5.24]: "pratiśrutyāpy adharmasaṃyuktāya na dadyāt" |

bṛhaspatiḥ [14.9] |

> bhṛtis tuṣṭyā paṇyamūlyaṃ strīśulkam upakāriṇe |  
> śraddhānugrahasaṃprītyā dattam aṣṭavidhaṃ viduḥ ||

dattasya saptavidhatvam abhidhāya vibhāge —

**[378]** nāradaḥ [4.7] |

> paṇyamūlyaṃ bhṛtis tuṣṭyā snehāt pratyupakārataḥ |  
> strīśulkānugrahārthaṃ ca dattaṃ dānavido viduḥ ||

**'paṇyamūlyam'** krītamūlyam | **'bhṛtiḥ'** vetanam, kṛtakarmaṇe dattam | **'tuṣṭyā'** bandicāraṇādibhyo dattam |

dakṣaḥ |

> mātāpitror gurau mitre vinīte copakāriṇi |  
> dīnānāthaviśiṣṭebhyo dattaṃ tu saphalaṃ bhavet ||

kātyāyanaḥ [645, 644, 646] |

> bhayatrāṇāya rakṣārthaṃ tathā kāryaprasādhanāt |  
> anena vidhinā dattaṃ vidyāt pratyupakārikam ||  
> avijñātopalabdhyarthaṃ dānaṃ yatra nirūpitam |  
> upalabdhikriyālabdhaṃ sā bhṛtiḥ parikīrtitā ||  
> prāṇasaṃśayam āpannaṃ yo mām uttārayed itaḥ |  
> sarvasvaṃ tasya dāsyāmīty ukte 'pi na tathā bhavet ||

nāradaḥ |

> adattaṃ tu bhayakrodhaśokavegaruganvitaiḥ |  
> tathotkocaparīhāsavyatyāsacchalayogataḥ ||

**[379]** > bālamūḍhasvatantraiś ca mattonmattāpavarjitaiḥ |  
> kartā mamāyaṃ karmeti pratilābhecchayā tu yat ||

kātyāyanaḥ [647, 649] |

> kāmakrodhāsvatantrārtaklībonmattapramohitaiḥ |  
> vyatyāsaparihāsāc ca yad dattaṃ tat punar haret ||  
> yadi kāryasya siddhyartham utkocā syāt pratiśrutā |  
> tasminn api prasiddhe 'rthe na deyā syāt kathaṃcana ||  
> atha prāg eva dattā syāt pratidāpyaḥ sa tāṃ balāt |  
> daṇḍaṃ caikādaśaguṇam āhur gārgīyamānavāḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [14.15–17] |

> kruddhahṛṣṭapramattārtabālonmattabhayāturaiḥ |  
> mattātivṛddhanirdhūtaiḥ pramūḍhaiḥ śokavegibhiḥ ||  
> narmadattaṃ tathaitair yat tad adattaṃ prakīrtitam |  
> pratilābhecchayā dattam apātre pātraśaṅkayā ||  
> kārye cādharmasaṃyukte svāmī tat punar āpnuyāt ||

**Amia Srinivasan**

**[380]** nāradaḥ [4.11] |

> apātre pātram ity ukte kārye cādharmasaṃhite |  
> yad dattaṃ syād avijñānād adattaṃ tad api smṛtam ||

manuḥ [8.212-13] |

> dharmārthaṃ yena dattaṃ syāt kasmaicid yācate dhanam |  
> paścāc ca na tathā tat syān na deyaṃ tena tad bhavet ||  
> yadi saṃsādhayet tat tu darpāl lobhena vā punaḥ |  
> rājñā dāpyaḥ suvarṇaṃ syāt tasya steyasya niṣkṛtiḥ ||

nāradaḥ [4.12] |

> gṛhnāty adattaṃ yo mohād yaś cādeyaṃ prayacchati |  
> daṇḍanīyāv ubhāv etau dharmajñena mahīkṣitā ||

kātyāyanaḥ [654, 650, 651] |

> svasthenārtena vā deyaṃ śrāvitaṃ dharmakāraṇāt |  
> adatvā tu mṛte dāpyas tatsuto nātra saṃśayaḥ ||

**[381]** > stenasāhasikodvṛttapārajāyikaśaṃsanāt |  
> darśanād vṛttanaṣṭasya tathāsatyapravartanāt ||  
> prāptam etais tu yat kiṃcit tad utkocākhyam ucyate |  
> na dātā tatra daṇḍyaḥ syān madhyasthaś caiva doṣabhāk ||

**iti mahārājādhirājaśrīgovindacandradevamahāsandhivigrahikeṇa**

**bhaṭṭaśrīhṛdayadharātmajena**

**śrīmallakṣmīdhareṇa viracite kṛtyakalpatarau**

**vyavahārakāṇde dattāpradānikam ||**

**[382]**

## 61 bhṛtividhiḥ
atha bhṛtividhiḥ

**tatrābhyupetyāśuśrūṣā**

bṛhaspatiḥ [15.1–3] |

> adeyādikam ākhyātaṃ bhṛtānām ucyate vidhiḥ |  
> aśuśrūṣābhyupetyaitad vivādapadam ucyate ||  
> vetanasyānapākarma tad anu svāmipālayoḥ |  
> kramaśaḥ kathyate vādo bhṛtabhedatrayaṃ tv idam ||

nāradaḥ [8.1–2] |

> abhyupetya tu śuśrūṣāṃ yas tāṃ na pratipadyate |  
> aśuśrūṣābhyupetyaitad vivādapadam ucyate ||  
> śuśrūṣakaḥ pañcavidhaḥ śāstre dṛṣṭo manīṣibhiḥ |  
> caturvidhaḥ karmakaraḥ śeṣā dāsās tripañcakāḥ ||

bhṛtyā ity anuvṛttau bṛhaspatiḥ [15.4–5] |

> anekadhā tv abhihitā jātikarmānurūpataḥ |  
> vidyāvijñānakarmārthanimittena caturvidhāḥ ||  
> ekaikaḥ punar eteṣāṃ kriyābhedāt prabhidyate |

**[383]** nāradaḥ [8.3–4] |

> śiṣyāntevāsibhṛtakāś caturthas tv adhikarmakṛt |  
> ete karmakarā jñeyā dāsās tu gṛhajādayaḥ ||  
> sāmānyam asvatantratvam eṣām āhur manīṣiṇaḥ |  
> jātikarmakṛtas tūkto viśeṣo vṛttitas tathā ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [15.6] |

> vidyā trayī samākhyātā ṛgyajuḥsāmalakṣaṇā |  
> tadarthaṃ guruśuśrūṣāṃ prakuryāc chāstracoditām ||

nāradaḥ [8.8] |

> ā vidyāgrahaṇāc chiṣyaḥ śuśrūṣet prayato gurum |  
> tadvṛttir gurudāreṣu guruputre tathaiva ca ||

tathā [8.15] |

> samāvṛttaś ca gurave pradāya gurudakṣiṇām |  
> pratīyāt svagṛhān eṣā śiṣyavṛttir udāhṛtā ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [15.7] |

> vijñānam ucyate śilpaṃ hemakupyādisaṃskṛtiḥ |  
> nṛtyādikaṃ ca tac chikṣan kuryāt karma guror gṛhe ||

**[384]** nāradaḥ [8.16–17] |

> svaṃ śilpam icchann āhartuṃ bāndhavānām anujñayā |  
> ācāryasya vased ante kālaṃ kṛtvā suniścitam ||  
> ācāryaḥ śikṣayed enaṃ svagṛhe dattabhojanam |  
> na cānyat kārayet karma putravac cainam ācaret ||

kātyāyanaḥ [716] |

> yas tu na grāhayec chilpaṃ karmāṇy ākhyāti kārayet |  
> prāpnuyāt sāhasaṃ pūrvaṃ tasmāc chiṣyo nivartate ||

nāradaḥ [7.18–19] |

> śikṣayantam aduṣtaṃ ca yas tv ācāryaṃ parityajet |  
> balād vāsayitavyaḥ syād vadhabandhau ca so 'rhati ||  
> śikṣito 'pi kṛtaṃ kālam antevāsī samāpayet |  
> tatra karma ca yat kuryād ācāryasyaiva tat phalam ||

**'vadho'** 'tra veṇudaṇḍādinā tādanamātram | **'bandho'** bandhanam | yantraṇam iti kaścit | **'kṛtaṃ kālam'** vyavasthāpitaṃ samayam | **'tat phalam'** karmaphalaṃ bhṛtirūpam |

**[375]** tathā [7.20] |

> gṛhītaśilpaḥ samaye kṛtvācāryaṃ pradakṣiṇam |  
> śaktitaś cānumānyainam antevāsī nivartate ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [15.8–12] |

> yo bhuṅkte paradāsīm tu sa jñeyo vanitābhṛtaḥ |  
> karma tatsvāminaḥ kuryād yathānyo 'rthabhṛto naraḥ ||  
> bahudhārthabhṛtaḥ proktas tathā bhāgabhṛto 'paraḥ |  
> hīnamadhyottamatvaṃ ca sarveṣām eva coditam ||  
> dinamāsārdhaṣaṇmāsatrimāsābdabhṛtas tathā |  
> karma kuryāt pratijñātaṃ labhate paribhāṣitam ||

**[376]** > bhṛtakas trividho jñeya uttamo madhyamo 'dhamaḥ |  
> śaktibhaktyanurūpā syād eṣāṃ karmāśrayā bhṛtiḥ ||  
> uttamas tv āyudhīyo 'tra madhyamas tu kṛṣīvalaḥ |  
> adhamo bhāravāhaḥ syād ity eṣa trividho bhṛtaḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [15.13–14] |

> āyudhīyottamas teṣāṃ madhyamaḥ sīravāhakaḥ |  
> bhāravāho 'dhamaḥ proktas tathā ca gṛhakarmakṛt ||  
> dviprakāro bhāgabhṛtaḥ kṛṣigojīvināṃ smṛtaḥ |  
> jātasasyāt tathā kṣīrāt sa labheta na saṃśayaḥ ||

nāradaḥ [8.23, 25, 8, 5,7] |

> artheṣv adhikṛto yaḥ syāt kuṭumbasya tathopari |  
> so 'dhikarmakaro jñeyaḥ sa ca kauṭumbikaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
> śubhakarmakarā hy ete catvāraḥ samudāhṛtāḥ |  
> jaghanyakarmabhājas tu śeṣā dāsās tripañcakāḥ ||  
> karmāpi dvividhaṃ proktam aśubhaṃ śubham eva ca |  
> aśubhaṃ dāsakarmoktaṃ subhaṃ karmabhṛtaḥ smṛtam ||  
> gṛhadvārāśucisthānarathyāvaskaraśodhanam |  
> guhyāṅgasparśanocchiṣṭaviṇmūtragrahaṇojjhanam ||

**[387]** > icchataḥ svāminaś cāṅgair upasthānam athāntataḥ |  
> aśubhaṃ karma vijñeyaṃ śubham anyat tataḥ param ||

kātyāyanaḥ [720] |

> viṇmūtronmārjanaṃ caiva nagnatvaparimardanam |  
> prāyo dāsīsutāḥ kuryur gavādigrahaṇaṃ ca yat ||

nāradaḥ [8.26–29, 31] |

> gṛhajātas tathā krīto labdho dāyād upāgataḥ |  
> anākālabhṛtas tadvad āhitaḥ svāminā ca yaḥ ||

**[388]** > mokṣito mahataś carṇād yuddhe prāptaḥ paṇe jitaḥ |  
> tavāham ity upagataḥ pravrajyāvasitaḥ kṛtaḥ ||  
> bhaktadāsaś ca vijñeyas tathaiva vaḍavāhṛtaḥ |  
> vikretā vātmahaṇ śāstre dāsāḥ pañcadaśa smṛtāḥ ||  
> tatra pūrvaś caturvargo dāsatvān na vimucyate |  
> prasādāt svāmino 'nyatra dāsyam eṣāṃ kramāgatam ||  
> vikrīṇīte svatantraḥ san yatrātmānaṃ narādhamaḥ |  
> sa jaghanyatamas teṣām so 'pi dāsyān na mucyate ||

**'anākāle bhṛtaḥ'** durbhikṣakāle bhṛtaḥ |

**[389]** mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe [18.216] caṇḍāladāsyaṃ prāptasya putraśokārtasya hariścandrasya vākyam |

> caṇḍālenānanujñātaḥ pravekṣye jvalanaṃ yadi |   
> caṇḍāladāsatāṃ prāpsye punar anyatra janmani ||

manuḥ [8.414] |

> na svāminā nisṛṣṭo 'pi śūdro dāsyāt pramucyate |  
> nisargajaṃ hi tat tasya kas tasmāt taṃ vyapohati ||

nāradaḥ [8.36] |

> rājña eva tu dāsaḥ syāt pravrajyāvasito naraḥ |  
> na tasya pratimokṣo 'sti na viśuddhiḥ kathaṃcana ||

**[390]** kātyāyanaḥ [721] |

> pravrajyāvasitaḥ yatra trayo varṇā dvijātayaḥ |  
> nirvāsaṃ kārayed vipraṃ dāsatvaṃ kṣatraviṇ nṛpaḥ ||

dakṣaḥ [7.33] |

> pārivrājyaṃ gṛhītvā tu yaḥ svadharme na tiṣṭhati |  
> śvapadenāṅkayitvā taṃ rājā śīghraṃ pravāsayet ||

**(a) atha dāsyavimokṣaḥ**

tatra nāradaḥ [8.40, 30–34, 36] |

> tavāham iti cātmānaṃ yo 'svatantraḥ prayacchati |  
> na sa taṃ prāpnuyāt kāmaṃ pūrvasvāmī labheta tam ||

**[391]**  
> caurāpahṛtavikrītā ye ca dāsīkṛtā balāt |  
> rājñā mocayitavyās te dāsatvaṃ teṣu neṣyate ||  
> yaś caiṣāṃ svāminaṃ kaścin mocayet prāṇasaṃśayāt |  
> dāsatvāt sa vimucyeta putrabhāgaṃ labheta ca ||  
> anākāle bhṛto dāsyān mucyate goyugaṃ dadat |  
> bhakṣitaṃ cāpi yad durge na tac chudhyati karmaṇā ||  
> āhito 'pi dhanaṃ datvā svāmī yady enam uddharet |  
> athopagamayed enaṃ so 'pi krītād anantaraḥ ||  
> ṛṇaṃ tu sodayaṃ datvā ṛṇī dāsyāt pramucyate |  
> kṛtakālavyuparamāt kṛtako 'pi vimucyate ||   
> tavāham ity upagato yuddhe prāptaḥ paṇe jitaḥ |  
> pratiśīrṣapradānena mucyate tulyakarmaṇā ||  
> bhaktasyopekṣaṇāt sadyo bhaktadāsaḥ pramucyate |  
> nigrahād vaḍavāyāṃ ca mucyate vaḍavābhṛtaḥ ||

**'asvatantraḥ'** asvāmikaḥ | **'durge'** durbhikṣe | **'upagamayet'** ityādi (?) | yasminn āhito dāsas tam eva yadi grāhayen na mocayet tadā tasyāsau 'krītānantaraḥ' **[392]** krītād avaśiṣṭaḥ saṃpadyata ity arthaḥ | **'pratiśīrṣapradānena'** tulyadāsadānenety arthaḥ | **'nigrahāt'** ācchādanāt | **'vaḍavā'** dāsī |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.182] |

> balād dāsīkṛtaś caurair vikrītaś cāpi mucyate |  
> svāmiprāṇaprado bhaktatyāgāt tanniṣkrayād api ||

kātyāyanaḥ [723] |

> svadāsīṃ yas tu saṃgacchet prasūtā ca bhavet tataḥ |  
> avekṣya bījaṃ kāryā syād adāsī sānvayā tu sā ||

**[393]** nāradaḥ [8.42, 43, 41] |

> svaṃ dāsam icched yaḥ kartum adāsaṃ prītamānasaḥ |  
> skandhād ādāya tasyāsau bhindyāt kumbhaṃ sahāmbhasā ||  
> sākṣātābhiḥ sapuṣpābhir mūrdhanyadbhir avākiran |  
> adāsa iti coktvā triḥ prāṅmukhaṃ tam athotsṛjet ||  
> tataḥ prabhrti vaktavyaḥ svāmyanugrahapālitaḥ |  
> bhojyānnaś ca pratigrāhyo bhavaty abhimataḥ satām ||  
> adhanās traya evoktā bhāryā dāsas tathā sutaḥ |  
> yat te samadhigacchanti yasyaite tasya tad dhanam ||

**'samadhigacchanti'** samārjayanti |

devalaḥ |

> pitary uparate putrā vibhajeyur dhanaṃ pituḥ |  
> asvāmyaṃ hi bhavet teṣāṃ nirdoṣe pitari sthite ||  
> patyau jīvati nārīṇāṃ dāsānāṃ svāmini sthite |  
> tadvan niyatam asvāmyaṃ sarvārtheṣv abravīn manuḥ ||

manuḥ [8.147] |

> visrabdhaṃ brāhmaṇaḥ śūdrād dravyopādānam ācaret |  
> na hi tasyāsti kiṃcit svaṃ bhartṛhāryadhano hi saḥ ||

**[394]** kātyāyanaḥ [724, 725] |

> dāsasya tu dhanaṃ yat syāt svāmī tasya prabhuḥ smṛtaḥ |  
> prakāśavikrayād yat tu tat svāmī dhanam arhati ||

**[395]** tathā |

> dāsenoḍhā ca dāsī yā sāpi dāsītvam āpnuyāt |  
> yasmād bhartā prabhus tasyāḥ svāmyadhīnaḥ patir yataḥ ||

**[395]**

**atha dāsyādhikāriṇaḥ**

tatra nāradaḥ [8.39] |

> varṇānāṃ prātilomyena dāsatvaṃ na vidhīyate |  
> svadharmatyāgino 'nyatra dāravad dāsatā matā ||

kātyāyanaḥ [715–16, 719, 718] |

> svatantrasyātmano dānād dāsatvaṃ dāravad bhṛguḥ |  
> triṣu varṇeṣu vijñeyaṃ dāsyaṃ viprasya na kvacit ||  
> varṇānām ānulomyena dāsyaṃ na pratilomataḥ |  
> rājanyavaiśyaśūdrāṇāṃ tyajatāṃ ca svatantratām ||  
> samavarṇo 'pi vipraṃ tu dāsatvaṃ naiva kārayet |  
> śīlādhyayanasaṃpannas tadūnaṃ karma kāmataḥ ||  
> tatrāpi nāśubhaṃ kiṃcit prakurvīta dvijottamaḥ |  
> brāhmaṇasya hi dāsatvān nṛpatejo vihanyate ||  
> kṣatraviṭśūdradharmas tu samavarṇaṃ kadācana |  
> kārayed dāsakarmāṇi brāhmaṇaṃ na bṛhaspatiḥ ||

**'tadūnaṃ'** ity atra śīlādhayananyūnaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ śīlādhyayanasaṃpanno brāhmaṇaḥ karma kārayed iti yojanā | **'kāmataḥ'** tadicchayā | **'aśubhaṃ'** viṇmūtraśodhanādi | **[397]** **'kṣatraviṭśūdradharma'** ityādi, kṣatrādidharmaḥ brāhmaṇaṃ dāsakarmāṇi na kārayed iti bṛhaspatir manyata ity arthaḥ |

manuḥ [8.411–13] |

> kṣatriyaṃ caiva vaiśyaṃ ca brāhmaṇo vṛttikarṣitau |  
> bibhṛyād ānṛśaṃsyena svāni kārmāṇi kārayet ||

**[398]** > dāsyaṃ tu kārayen mohād brāhmaṇaḥ saṃskṛtān dvijān |  
> anicchataḥ prābhavatvād rājñā dāpyaḥ śatāni ṣaṭ ||  
> śūdraṃ tu kārayed dāsyaṃ krītam akrītam eva vā |  
> dāyāyaiva hi sṛṣṭo 'sau svayam eva svayaṃbhuvā ||

**'prābhavatvāt'** prabhutvāt |

viṣṇuḥ [5.151]: "yas tūttamavarṇaṃ dāsye niyojayati tasyottamasāhaso daṇḍaḥ" |

kātyāyanaḥ [726–29] |

> ādadyād brāhmaṇīṃ yas tu vikrīṇīyāt tathaiva ca |  
> rājñe tad akṛtaṃ kāryaṃ daṇḍyāḥ syuḥ sarva eva te ||  
> kāmāt tu saṃśritāṃ yaś ca dāsīṃ kuryāt kulastriyam |  
> saṃkrāmayet tathānyatra daṇḍyas tac cākṛtaṃ bhavet ||

**[399]** > bālaghātrīm adāsīṃ ca dāsīm eva bhunakti yaḥ |  
> paricārakapatnīṃ vā prāpnuyāt pūrvasāhasam ||  
> vikrośamānāṃ yo bhaktāṃ dāsīṃ vikretumicchati |  
> anāpadisthaḥ śaktaḥ san prāpnuyād dviśataṃ damam ||

**iti mahārājādhirājaśrīgovindacandradevamahāsandhivigrahikeṇa**

**bhaṭṭahṛdayadharātmajena**

**bhaṭṭaśrīlakṣmīdhareṇa viracite kṛtyakalpatarau**

**vyavahārakāṇde dāsyādhikāraparva ||**

**[400]**

## 62 vetanasyānapākriyā
atha vetanasyānapākriyā

tatra nāradaḥ [9.1–3] |

> bhṛtānāṃ vetanasyoktir dānādhādhamanavikrame |  
> vetanasyānapākarma tad vivādapadaṃ smṛtam ||  
> bhṛtāya vetanaṃ dadyāt karmasvāmī yathākṛtam |  
> ādau madhye 'vasāne vā karmaṇo yad viniścitam ||  
> bhṛtāv aniścitāyāṃ tu daśabhāgam avāpnuyuḥ |  
> lābhagovīryasasyānāṃ vaṇiggopakṛṣīvalāḥ ||

**'govīryam'** gavāṃ sārabhūtaṃ kṣīram ity arthaḥ |

**[401]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.194–96] |

> dāpyas tu daśamaṃ bhāgaṃ vāṇijyapaśusasyataḥ |  
> aniścitya bhṛtiṃ yas tu kārayet sa mahīkṣitā ||  
> deśaṃ kālaṃ ca yo 'tīyāt karma kuryāc ca yo 'nyathā |  
> tatra tu svāminaś chando 'dhikaṃ deyaṃ kṛte 'dhike ||  
> yo yāvat kurute karma tāvat tasya tu vetanam |  
> ubhayor apy asādhyaṃ cet sādhyaṃ kuryād yathāśrutam ||

**'tatra'** bhṛtidāne | **'svāminaś chandaḥ'** icchā |

bṛhaspatiḥ [16.1–2] |

> tribhāgaṃ pañcabhāgaṃ vā gṛhṇīyāt sīravāhakaḥ |

**[402]** tathā |

> bhāktācchādabhrtaḥ sīrād bhāgaṃ gṛhṇīta pañcamam |  
> jātasasyāt tribhāgaṃ tu pragṛhṇītopadhābhṛtaḥ ||

**'upadhā'** vyāpāraphalam |

āpastambaḥ [2.28.2–4]: "udvasataḥ kīnāśasya karmanyāse daṇḍatāḍanam | tathā paśupasya | avarodhanaṃ cāsya paśūnām" |

vṛddhamanuḥ [manusmṛti, pūrvārdhṃ, 8.157] |

> samudrayānakuśalā deśakālārthadarśinaḥ |  
> niyaccheyur bhṛtiṃ yāṃ tu sā syāt prāg akṛtā yadi ||

nāradaḥ [9.4] |

> karmopakaraṇaṃ caiṣāṃ kriyāṃ prati yad adhitam |  
> āptabhāvena tad rakṣyaṃ na jaihmyena kadācana ||

**[403]** bṛhaspatiḥ [16.3, 5] |

> bhṛtakas tu na kurvīta svāminā śāṭhyam anv api |  
> bhṛtihānim avāpnoti tato vādaḥ pravartate ||  
> gṛhītavetanaḥ karma na karoti yadā bhṛtaḥ |  
> samarthaś ced damaṃ dāpyo dviguṇaṃ tac ca vetanam ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.193] |

> gṛhītavetanaḥ karma tyajan dviguṇam āvahet |  
> agṛhīte samaṃ dāpyo bhṛtyai rakṣya upaskaraḥ ||

**'bhṛtyaiḥ'** bhṛtakaiḥ | **'upaskaraḥ'** upakaraṇam, lāṅgalādīnāṃ yoktrādi |

nāradaḥ [9.5] |

> karmākurvan pratiśrutya kāryo datvā bhṛtiṃ balāt |  
> bhṛtiṃ gṛhītvākurvāṇo dviguṇāṃ bhṛtim āvahet ||

kātyāyanaḥ [657] |

> karmārambhaṃ tu yaḥ kṛtvā siddhiṃ naiva tu kārayet |  
> balātkārayitavyo 'sāv akurvan daṇḍam arhati ||

**[404]** bṛhaspatiḥ [16.7] |

> pratiśrutya na kuryād yaḥ sa kāryaḥ syād balād api |  
> sa cen na kuryāt tat karma prāpnuyād dviśataṃ damam ||

manuḥ [8.215] |

> bhṛto 'nārto na kuryād yo darpāt karma yathoditam |  
> sa daṇḍyaḥ kṛṣṇalāny aṣṭau na deyaṃ cāsya vetanam ||

[tathā; manuḥ 8.217, 216]

> yathoktam ārtaḥ svastho vā yas tat karma na kārayet |  
> na tasya vetanaṃ deyam alponasyāpi karmaṇaḥ ||  
> ārtas tu kuryāt svasthaḥ san yathābhāṣitam āditaḥ |  
> sudīrthasyāpi kālasya tal labhetaiva vetanam ||

**'anārtaḥ'** anāpannaḥ | **'alponasya'** alpāvaśiṣṭasya |

**[405]** nāradaḥ [nāradīyam saṃhitā 7.7] |

> kāle pūrṇe tyajan karma bhṛter nāśam avāpnuyāt |  
> svāmidoṣād akaraṇe yāvad bhṛtim avāpnuyāt ||

viṣnuḥ [5.153–59]: "bhṛtakaś cāpūrṇe kāle bhṛtiṃ tyajan sakalam eva mūlyaṃ jahyāt | rājñe ca paṇaśataṃ dadyāt | taddoṣeṇa [ca] yad vinaśyet tat svāmine [deyam] | anyatra daivopaghātāt | svāmī ced bhṛtakarmapūrṇe kāle jahyāt tasya sarvam eva mūlyaṃ dadyāt | paṇaśataṃ ca rājani | anyatra bhṛtakadoṣāt" |

nāradaḥ [9.9] |

> bhāṇḍaṃ vyasanam āgacched yadi vāhakadoṣataḥ |  
> dāpyo yat tatra naṣṭaṃ syād daivarājakṛtād ṛte ||

vṛddhamanuḥ |

> pramādān nāśitaṃ dāpyaḥ samaṃ dvirdohanāśitam |  
> na tu dāpyo hṛtaṃ caurair dagdham ūḍhaṃ jalena vā ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [16.9] |

> prabhuṇā viniyuktaḥ san bhṛtako vidadhāti yat |  
> tadartham aśubhaṃ karma svāmī tatrāparādhnuyāt ||

**[406]** **'tadartham'** svāmyartham | **'aśubhaṃ'** cauryādi | 'aparādhnuyāt' daṇḍādibhāg bhavet |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.197] |

> arājadaivikaṃ naṣṭaṃ bhāṇḍaṃ dāpyas tu vāhakaḥ |  
> prasthānavighnakṛc caiva dāpyaḥ syād dviguṇaṃ bhṛtim ||

vṛddhamanuḥ |

> yaḥ karmakāle saṃprāpte na kuryād vighnam ācaret |  
> uddhṛtyānyas tu kāryaḥ syāt sa dāpyo dviguṇāṃ bhṛtim ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.198] |

> prakrānte saptamaṃ bhāgaṃ caturthaṃ pathi saṃtyajan |  
> bhṛtim ardhapathe sarvāṃ pradāpyas tyājako 'pi ca ||

matsyapurāṇe [227.6] |

> mūlyam ādāya yo vidyāṃ śilpaṃ vā na prayacchati |  
> daṇḍyaḥ sa mūlyaṃ sakalaṃ dharmajñena mahīkṣitā ||

**[407]** nāradaḥ [9.8, 7–8?] |

> anayan bhāṭayitvā tu bhāṇḍavān yānavāhane |  
> dāpyo bhṛticaturbhāgaṃ samaṃ dharmapathe tyajan ||  
> anayan vāhako 'py evaṃ bhṛtihāniṃ samāpnuyāt |

vṛddhamanuḥ |

> pathi vikrīya tad bhāṇḍaṃ vaṇig bhṛtyam tyajed yadi |  
> agatasyāpi deyaṃ syād bhṛter ardhaṃ labhet saḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [661] |

> yathā sa pathi tad bhāṇḍam āsidhyeta hriyeta vā |  
> yāvān adhvā gatas tena tāvatīṃ labhate bhṛtim ||

**'āsidhyeta'** avarudhyet |

nāradaḥ [9.6] |

> bhṛtiṣaḍbhāgam ābhāṣya pathi yugyabhṛtaṃ tyajan |  
> adadat kārayitvā tu sodayāṃ bhṛtim āvahet ||

**'bhṛtiṣaḍbhāgam'** ityādi — yo bhṛtakaḥ **'ābhāṣya'** gacchāmīti saṃpratipadya paścād gamanopakrame pathi sthitaṃ yugyabhṛtaṃ tyajati, asau uktabhṛteḥ ṣaḍbhāgaṃ dāpya ity arthaḥ |

**[408]** bṛhaspatiḥ [16.11] |

> kṛte karmaṇi yaḥ svāmī na dadyād vetanaṃ bhṛteḥ |  
> rājñā dāpayitavyaḥ syād vinayaṃ cānurūpataḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [660] |

> tyajet pathi sahāyaṃ yaḥ śrāntaṃ rogārtam eva vā |  
> prāpnuyāt sāhasaṃ pūrvaṃ grāme tryaham apālayan ||

**62 — (a) atha paṇyastrīvidhiḥ**

tatra nāradaḥ [9.19, pūrvārdham] |

> śulkaṃ gṛhītvā paṇyastrī necchantī dviguṇaṃ vahet |  
> anicchan śulkadātāpi śulkahānim avāpnuyāt ||

smṛtiḥ [bṛhaspatiḥ 16.13] |

> vyādhitā saśramā vyagrā rājakāryaparāyaṇā |  
> āmantritā ca nāgacched avācyā vaḍavā smṛtā ||

**[409]** matsyapurāṇe [227.145] |

> gṛhītvā vetanaṃ veśyā lobhād anyatra gacchati |  
> bhāṭaṃ na dadyād dāpyā syād anūḍhasyāpi bhāṭatam ||

nāradaḥ [9.18 uttarārdhaḥ, 19] |

> aprayacchaṃs tathā śulkam anubhūya pumān striyam |  
> akrameṇa tu saṃgacchan ghātadantanakhādibhiḥ ||  
> ayonau yaḥ samākrāmed bahubhir vāpi vāsayet |  
> śulkaṃ so 'ṣṭaguṇaṃ dāpyo vinayaṃ tāvad eva tu ||

matsyapurāṇe [227.146–48] |

> anyam uddiśya yo veśyāṃ nayed anyasya kāraṇāt |  
> tasya daṇḍo bhaved rājñaḥ suvarṇasya ca māṣakam ||

**[410]** > nītvā bhogaṃ na yo dadyād dāpyo dviguṇavetanam |  
> rājñaś ca dviguṇaṃ daṇḍaṃ tathā dharmo na hīyate ||  
> bahūnāṃ vrajtām ekāṃ sarve te dviguṇaṃ damam |  
> tasyai dadyuḥ pṛthag rājñe daṇḍaṃ ca dviguṇaṃ param ||

nāradaḥ |

> veśyāḥ pradhānā yās tatra kāmukās tadgṛhoṣitāḥ |  
> tatsamuttheṣu karyeṣu nirṇayaṃ saṃśaye viduḥ ||

**[iti paṇyastrīvidhiparva]**

**62 — (ā) atha grahādibhāṭakavidhiḥ**

nāradaḥ |

> parabhūmau gṛhaṃ kṛtvā stomaṃ datvā vaset tu yaḥ |  
> sa tad gṛhītvā nirgacchet tṛṇakāṣṭheṣṭakādikam ||  
> stomād vinā hy uṣitvā tu parabhūmāv aniścitaḥ |  
> nirgacchaṃs tṛṇakāṣṭhāni na gṛhṇīyāt kathaṃcana ||  
> nānyena tṛṇakāṣṭhāni tv iṣṭakā viniveśitāḥ |  
> vinirgacchaṃs tu tat sarvaṃ bhūsvāmini niveśayet ||

vyāsaḥ |

> snehena tu ciraṃ bhuktvā mandiraṃ kurute tu yaḥ |  
> nirgacchatas tasya dāru dattastomasya nānyathā ||

kātyāyanaḥ [663, 662] |

> gṛhavāryāpaṇādīni gṛhītvā bhāṭakena yaḥ |  
> svāmine nārpayed yāvat tāvad dāpyaḥ sa bhāṭakam ||

**[412]**  
> hastyaśvagokharoṣṭrādīn gṛhītvā bhāṭakena yaḥ |  
> nārpayet kṛtakṛtyaḥ san tāvad dāpyaḥ sa bhāṭakam ||

vṛddhamanuḥ |

> yo bhāṭayitvā śakaṭaṃ nītvā cānyatra gacchati |  
> bhāṭaṃ na dadyād dāpyaḥ syād anūḍhasyāpi bhāṭakam ||

nāradaḥ [9.22] |

> stomavāhīni bhāṇḍāni pūrṇakālāny upānayet |  
> grahītur ābhaved bhagnaṃ naṣṭaṃ cānyatra saṃplavāt ||

**iti kalpatarau vetanānapakriyā |**

**[413]**

## 63 svāmipālavivādaḥ
atha svāmipālavivādaḥ

tatra manuḥ [8.229, 231] |

> paśuṣu svāmināṃ caiva pālānāṃ ca yathāvidhi |  
> vivādaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi yathāvad dharmatattvataḥ ||  
> gavāṃ kṣīrabhṛto yas tu sa duhyād daśato varām |  
> gosvāmyanumate bhṛtyaḥ sā syāt pāle 'bhṛte bhṛtiḥ ||

**'kṣīrabhṛtaḥ'** kṣīram eva bhṛtir yasya sa tathā | **'duhyād daśato varām'** iti | daśasu goṣu madhye ekāṃ śreṣṭhāṃ gāṃ duhyād ity arthaḥ | **'sā'** ekagodohanarūpā | **'pāle'** gopāle | **'abhṛte'** grāsācchādaneneti śeṣaḥ |

nāradaḥ [9.10] |

> gavāṃ śatād vatsatarī dhenuḥ syād dviśatād bhṛtiḥ |  
> pratisaṃvatsaraṃ gope saṃdohaś cāṣṭame 'hani ||

**[414]** bṛhaspatiḥ [16.14] |

> tathā dhenubhṛtaḥ kṣīraṃ labheta hy aṣṭame 'khilam |

**'dhenubhṛto'** gopaḥ |

āpastambaḥ [2.28.2–4]: "udvasataḥ kīnāśasya karmanyāse daṇḍena tāḍanam | tathā paśupasya | avarodhanaṃ cāsya paśūnām" |

nāradaḥ [9.11] |

> upānayed araṇyāya pratyahaṃ rajanīkṣaye |  
> cīrṇāḥ pītāś ca tā gopaḥ sāyāhne pratyupānayet ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.164] |

> yathārpitān paśūn gopaḥ sāyaṃ pratyarpayet tathā |  
> pramādahṛtanaṣṭāṃś ca pradāpyaḥ kṛtavetanaḥ ||

**[415]** manuḥ [8.230] |

> divā vaktavyatā pāle rātrau svāmini tadgṛhe |  
> yogakṣemāv anyathā cet pālo vaktavyatām iyāt ||

manu-nāradau [manu 8.233; nā. 9.16] |

> vighuṣya tu hṛtaṃ caurair na pālo daṇḍam arhati |  
> yadi deśe ca kāle ca svāminaḥ svasya śaṃsati ||

vyāsaḥ |

> pālagrāhe grāmaghāte tathā rāṣṭrasya vibhrame |  
> yat pranaṣṭaṃ hṛtaṃ vā syān na pālas tatra kilbiṣī ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [16.16] |

> kṛmicauravyāghrabhād darīśvabhrāc ca pālayet |  
> vyāyacchec chaktitaḥ krośet svāmine vā nivedayet ||

nāradaḥ [9.12–13] |

> sā ced gaur vyasanaṃ gacched vyāyacchet tatra śaktitaḥ |  
> aśaktas tūrṇam āgatya svāmine tan nivedayet ||

**[416]** > avyāyacchann avikrośan svāmine vānivedayan |  
> voḍhum arhati gopas tāṃ vinayañ caiva rājani ||

manu-nāradau [manu 8.232; nā. 9.14] |

> naṣṭaṃ vijagdhaṃ kṛmibhiḥ śvahataṃ viṣame mṛtam |  
> hīnaṃ puruṣakāreṇa pradadyād gopa eva tu ||

**'śvahatam'** ity atra śvapadaṃ śvāpadādyupalakṣaṇārtham |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.165] |

> pāladoṣavināśe tu pāle daṇḍo vidhīyate |  
> ardhatrayodaśapaṇāḥ svāmino dravyam eva ca ||

viṣṇuḥ [5.137–39]: "divā paśūnāṃ vṛkādyupaghāte pāle tv anāpadi pālakadoṣaḥ | vinaṣṭapaśumūlyaṃ ca svāmine dadyāt | ananujñātāṃ duhan pañcaviṃśati kārṣāpaṇān" ||

brahmapurāṇe |

> gṛhītamūlyo gopālas tās tyaktvā nirjane vane |  
> grāmacārī nṛpair vadhyaḥ śalākīva vanecaraḥ ||

**[417]** > gopālahaste saṃsthā gaus taddoṣān mriyate yadi |  
> tadā sa eva daṇḍyas tu śulkaṃ dāpyas tu gopateḥ ||  
> yadā rogādidoṣeṇa mriyate gaur gṛhe kvacit |  
> tadā sa gopatir daṇḍyo datvā gopālavetanam ||

**'śalākī'** nāpitaḥ | **'rogādidoṣeṇa'** svāminaḥ pratīkārakaraṇavyatirekeṇeti śeṣaḥ |

manu-nāradau |

> ajāvike tu saṃruddhe vṛkaiḥ pāle tv anāpadi |  
> yāṃ prasahya vṛko hanyāt pāle tat kilbiṣaṃ bhavet ||  
> tāsāṃ caivāvaruddhānāṃ carantīnāṃ mitho vane |  
> yām utplutya vṛho hanyāt pālas tatra na kilbiṣī ||

**'mitho'** rahasi |

nāradaḥ [9.17] |

> anena sarvapālānāṃ vivādaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ |  
> mṛteṣu ca viśuddhiḥ syād vālaśṛṅgādidarśanāt ||

**[418]** manuḥ [8.234, 244] |

> karṇau carma ca vālāṃś ca basti snāyuṃ ca rocanam |  
> paśusvāmini dadyāt tu mṛteṣv aṅkādi darśayet ||  
> etad vidhānam ātiṣṭhed dhārmikaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ |  
> svāmināṃ ca paśūnāṃ ca pālānāṃ ca vyatikrame ||

**iti mahārājādhirājaśrīgovindacandradevamahāsandhivigrahikeṇa**

**bhaṭṭahṛdayadharātmajena**

**bhaṭṭaśrīlakṣmīdhareṇa viracite kṛtyakalpatarau**

**vyavahārakāṇde svāmipālavivādaḥ ||**

**[419]**

## 64 saṃvidvyatikarmaḥ
atha saṃvidvyatikarmaḥ

tatra nāradaḥ [13.1] |

> pākhaṇḍanaigamādīnāṃ sthitiḥ samaya ucyate |  
> samayasyānapākarma tad vivādapadaṃ smṛtam ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.185] |

> rājā kṛtvā pure sthānaṃ brāhmaṇān nyasya tatra tu |  
> traividyān vṛttimad brūyāt svadharmaḥ pālyatām iti ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [17.2–10] |

> vedavidyāvido viprān śrotriyān agnihotriṇaḥ |  
> āhṛtya sthāpayet tatra teṣāṃ vṛttiṃ prakalpayet ||  
> anācchedyakarās tebhyaḥ pradadyād gṛhabhūmikāḥ |  
> muktabhāvyāś ca nṛpatir lekhayitvā svaśāsane ||

**[420]**  
> nityaṃ naimittikaṃ kāmyaṃ śāntikaṃ pauṣṭikaṃ tathā |  
> paurāṇāṃ karma kuryus te saṃdigdhe nirṇayaṃ tathā ||  
> grāmaśreṇigaṇānāṃ ca saṅketaḥ samayakriyā |  
> bādhākāle tu sā kāryā dharmakārye tathaiva ca ||  
> cāṭacaurabhaye bādhā sarvasādhāraṇī smṛtā |  
> tatropaśamanaṃ kāryaṃ sarvair naikena kenacit ||  
> kośena lekhyakriyayā madhyasthair vā parasparam |  
> viśvāsaṃ prathamaṃ kṛtvā kuryuḥ kāryāṇy anantaram ||  
> vidveśiṇo vyasanino janasaṃtrāsabhīravaḥ |  
> lubdhātivṛddhā bālāś ca na kāryāḥ kāryacintakāḥ ||  
> śucayo vedadharmajñā dakṣā dāntāḥ kulodbhavāḥ |  
> sarvakāryapravīṇāś ca kartavyāś ca mahattarāḥ ||  
> sapta vā pañca vā kāryāḥ samūhahitavādinaḥ |  
> kartavyaṃ vacanaṃ teṣāṃ grāmaśreṇigaṇādibhiḥ ||

**[421]** **'bhāvyam'** rājña āyaviśeṣaḥ |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.188] |

> kartavyaṃ vacanaṃ teṣāṃ samūhahitavadinām |  
> yas tatra viparītaḥ syāt sa dāpyaḥ prathamaṃ damam ||

kātyāyanaḥ [671] |

> yuktiyuktaṃ tu yo hanyād vaktur yo nāvakāśadaḥ |  
> ayuktaṃ caiva yo brūyād dāpya uttamasāhasam ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.192] |

> śreṇinaigamapākhaṇḍagaṇānām apy ayaṃ vidhiḥ |  
> bhedaṃ caiṣāṃ nṛpo rakṣet pūrvavṛttiṃ ca palayet ||

**'śreṇayaḥ'** samānakarmaśilpopajīvinaḥ kāravaḥ | **'naigamaḥ'** nānāpaurasamūhaḥ | **'pākhaṇḍaḥ'** pravrajyāvasitaḥ | **'gaṇo'** brāhmaṇasamūhaḥ |

**[422]** nāradaḥ [13.22] |

> pākhaṇḍanaigamaśreṇipūgavrātagaṇādiṣu |  
> saṃrakṣet samayaṃ rājā durge janapade tathā ||  
> yo dharmaḥ samayaś caiṣām upasthānavidhiś ca yaḥ |  
> yaś caiṣāṃ vṛttyupādānam anumanyeta tat tathā ||

**'pūgo'** vaṇigādisamūhaḥ | **'vrātaḥ'** nānāyudhadharasamūhaḥ | ādiśabdenātra saṅgagulmavargā ucyante |

kātyāyanaḥ [668] |

> samūhānāṃ tu yo dharmas tena dharmeṇa te sadā |  
> prakuryuḥ sarvakarmāṇi svadharmeṣu vyavasthitāḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.185] |

> nijadharmāvirodhena yas tu sāmayiko bhavet |  
> so 'pi yatnena saṃrakṣyo dharmo rājakṛtaś ca yaḥ ||

**[423]** kātyāyanaḥ [669, 670] |

> avirodhena dharmasya nirgataṃ rājaśāsanam |  
> tasyaivācaraṇaṃ pūrvaṃ kartavyaṃ tu nṛpājñayā ||  
> rājñā pravartitān dharmān yo naro nānupālayet |  
> garhyaḥ sa pāpī daṇḍyaś ca lopayan rājaśāsanam ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [17.11–14] |

> sabhāprapādevagṛhataṭākārāmasaṃskṛtiḥ |  
> tathānāthadaridrāṇāṃ saṃskāro yajanakriyā ||  
> kulyāyananirodhaś ca kāryam asmābhir aṃśataḥ |  
> yatra tal likhitaṃ patre dharmyā sā samayakriyā ||  
> pālanīyā samas tais tair yaḥ samartho visaṃvadet |  
> sarvasvaharaṇaṃ daṇḍas tasya nirvāsanaṃ purāt ||  
> tatra bhedam upekṣāṃ vā yaḥ kaścit kurute naraḥ |  
> catuḥsuvarṇāḥ ṣaṇṇiṣkās tasya daṇḍo vidhīyate ||

**[424]** manuḥ [8.219, 221] |

> yo grāmadeśasaṅghānāṃ kṛtvā satyena saṃvidam |  
> visaṃvaden naro lobhāt taṃ rāṣtrād vipravāsayet ||  
> nigṛhya dāpayec cainaṃ samayavyabhicāriṇam |  
> catuḥsuvarṇān ṣaṇṇiṣkāṃś chatamānaṃ ca rājatam ||  
> evaṃ daṇḍavidhiṃ kuryād dhārmikaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ |  
> grāmajātisamūheṣu samayavyabhicāriṇām ||

'śatamānaṃ ca' viṃśatyadhikaraktikā śatatrayeṇa saṃpadyate |

nāradaḥ [13.6] |

> pṛthaggaṇāṃś ca ye bhindyus te vineyā viśeṣataḥ |  
> āvaheyur bhayaṃ ghoraṃ vyādhivat te hy upekṣitāḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.187] |

> gaṇadravyaṃ hared yas tu saṃvidaṃ laṅghayec ca yaḥ |  
> sarvasvaharaṇaṃ kṛtvā taṃ rāṣṭrād vipravāsayet ||

**[425]** kātyāyanaḥ [672] |

> sāhasī bhedakārī ca gaṇadravyavināśakaḥ |  
> ucchedyāḥ sarva evaite vikhyāpyaivaṃ nṛpair bhṛguḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [17.15–20] |

> yas tu sādhāraṇaṃ hiṃsyāt kṣipet traividyam eva ca |  
> saṃvitkriyāṃ vihanyāc ca sa nirvāsyas tataḥ purāt ||  
> aruntudaḥ sūcakaś ca bhedakṛt sāhasī tathā |  
> śreṇīpūganṛpadviṣṭaḥ kṣipraṃ nirvāsyate tataḥ ||  
> kulaśreṇigaṇādhyakṣāḥ puradurganivāsinaḥ |  
> vāgdigdamaṃ parityāgaṃ prakuryuḥ pāpakarmaṇām ||  
> taiḥ kṛtaṃ yat svadharmeṇa nigrahānugrahaṃ nṛṇām |  
> tad rājñāpy anumantavyaṃ nisṛṣṭārthā hi te smṛtāḥ ||  
> bādhāṃ kuryur yadaikasya saṃbhūtā dveṣasaṃyutāḥ |  
> rājñā tu vinivāryās te śāsyāś caivānubandhinaḥ ||  
> mukhyaiḥ saha samūhānāṃ visaṃvādo yadā bhavet |  
> tadā vicārayed rājā svamārge sthāpayec ca tān ||

**[426]** nāradaḥ [13.5] |

> mithaḥ saṅghātakaraṇam ahetau(?) śastracāraṇam |  
> parasparopaghātaṃ ca teṣāṃ rājā na marṣayet ||

kātyāyanaḥ [673] |

> ekapātre 'tha paṅktyāṃ vā saṃbhoktā yena yo bhavet |  
> akurvan sa tathā daṇḍyas tasya doṣam adarśayan ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [17.22] |

> saṃbhūyaikamatiṃ kṛtvā rājabhāvyaṃ haranti ye |  
> te tadaṣṭaguṇaṃ dāpyā vaṇijaś ca palāyinaḥ ||

nāradaḥ [13.4, 7] |

> pratikūlaṃ ca yad rājñaḥ prakṛtyavamataṃ ca yat |  
> bādhakaṃ ca yad arthānāṃ tat tebhyo vinivartayet ||  
> doṣavat karaṇaṃ yat syād anāmnāyaprakalpitam |  
> pravṛttam api tad rājā śreyaskāmo nivartayet ||

**[427]** **'doṣavatkaraṇaṃ'** duṣṭā kriyā | **'anāmnāyaprakalpitaṃ'** pāramparyasiddhaṃ yan na bhavati |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.189–90] |

> samūhakārya āyātān kṛtakāryān visarjayet |  
> sa dānamānasatkāraiḥ pūjayitvā mahīpatiḥ ||  
> samūhakāryaprahito yal labhet tat tad arpayet |  
> ekādaśaguṇaṃ dāpyo yady asau nārpayet svayam ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [17.13–15] |

> tato labheta yat kiṃcit sarveṣām eva tat samam |  
> ṣāṇmāsikaṃ māsikaṃ vā vibhaktavyaṃ yathāṃśataḥ ||  
> deyaṃ vā niḥsvavṛddhāndhastrībālāturarogiṣu |  
> sāṃtānikādiṣu tathā dharma eṣa sanātanaḥ ||  
> yat taiḥ prāptaṃ rakṣitaṃ vā gaṇārthe vāpy ṛṇaṃ kṛtam |  
> rājaprasādalabdhaṃ ca sarveṣām eva tat samam ||

**[428]** kātyāyanaḥ [674–76] |

> gaṇam uddiśya yaiḥ kiṃcit kṛtvarṇaṃ bhakṣitaṃ bhavet |  
> ātmārthaṃ viniyuktaṃ vā deyaṃ tair eva tad bhavet ||  
> gaṇānāṃ śreṇivargāṇāṃ gatāḥ syur ye 'pi madhyatām |  
> prāktanasya dhanarṇasya samāṃśāḥ sarva eva te ||  
> tathaiva bhojyavaibhājyadānadharmakriyāsu ca |  
> samūhastho 'ṃśabhāgī syāt pragatas tv aṃśabhāg na tu ||

**iti mahārājādhirājaśrīmadgovindacandradevamahāsandhivigrahikeṇa**

**bhaṭṭahṛdayadharātmajena**

**bhaṭṭaśrīlakṣmīdhareṇa viracite kṛtyakalpatarau**

**vyavahārakāṇde saṃvidvyatikramaparva ||**

**[429]**

## 65 vikrīyāsaṃpradānam
atha vikrīyāsaṃpradānam

tatra nāradaḥ [11.1–5] |

> vikrīya paṇyaṃ mūlyena kretur yan na pradīyate |  
> vikrīyāsaṃpradānaṃ tad vivādapadam ucyate ||  
> loke 'smin dvividhaṃ dravyaṃ sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ tathā |  
> krayavikrayadharmeṣu sarvaṃ tat paṇyam ucyate ||  
> ṣaḍvidhas tasya vibudhair dānādānavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ |  
> gaṇimaṃ tulimaṃ meyaṃ kriyayā rūpataḥ śriyā ||  
> vikrīya paṇyaṃ mūlyena kretur yo na prayacchati |  
> sthāvarasya kṣayaṃ dāpyo jaṅgamasya kriyāphalam ||  
> ardhaś ced apacīyeta sodayaṃ paṇyam āvahet |  
> sthāyinām eṣa niyamo diglābho digvicāriṇām ||

**[430]** **'gaṇimaṃ'** kramukaphalādi | **'tulimam'** kuṅkumādi | **'meyam'** śālyādi | **'kriyayā'** vāhanadohanādikayā | **'rūpataḥ'** stryādi | **'śriyā'** padmarāgādi | **'sthāvarasya'** grāmakṣetrādeḥ | **'jaṅgamasya'** gavāśvādeḥ | **'kṣayaḥ'** śasyādyupaghātenopakṣayaḥ | **'phalaṃ'** kṣīrādi |

viṣṇuḥ [5.127–28]: "gṛhītamūlyaṃ yaḥ kretur naiva dadyāt tasyāsau sodayaṃ dāpyaḥ | rājñā ca paṇaśataṃ daṇḍyaḥ" |

manuḥ [8.222, 223, 228] |

> krītvā vikrīya vā kiṃcid yasyehānuśayo bhavet |  
> so 'ntardaśāhāt tad dravyaṃ dadyāc caivādadīta vā ||  
> pareṇa tu daśāhasya nādadyān naiva dāpayet |  
> ādadāno dadac caiva rājñā daṇḍyaḥ śatāni ṣaṭ ||

**[431]** > yasmin yasmin kṛte kārye yasyehānuśayo bhavet |  
> tam anena vidhānena dharmye pathi niveśayet ||

kātyāyanaḥ [683–84] |

> krītvā prāptaṃ na gṛhṇīyād yo na dadyād adūṣitam |  
> sa mūlyād daśabhāgaṃ tu datvā svaṃ dravyam āpnuyāt ||  
> aprāpte 'rthe kriyākāre kṛte naiva pradāpayet |  
> evaṃ dharmo daśāhāt tu parato 'nuśayo na tu ||

**'kriyākāre'** sākṣilekhyādike |

nāradaḥ [11.6] |

> upahanyeta vā paṇyaṃ dahyetāpahriyeta vā |  
> vikretur eva so 'nartho vikrīyāsaṃprayacchataḥ ||

**[432]** nāradaḥ [11.7] |

> nirdoṣaṃ darśayitvā tu sadoṣaṃ yaḥ prayacchati |  
> mūlyaṃ tu dviguṇaṃ dāpyo vinayaṃ tāvad eva tu ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [18.3,4] |

> jñātvā sadoṣaṃ yaḥ paṇyaṃ vikrīṇītāvicakṣaṇaḥ |  
> tad evaṃ dviguṇaṃ dāpyas tatsamaṃ vinayaṃ tathā ||  
> mattonmattena vikrītaṃ hīnamūlyaṃ tu yad bhavet |  
> asvatantreṇa mūḍhena tyājyaṃ tasya punar haret ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.257] |

> anyahastena vikrītaṃ duṣṭaṃ vāduṣṭavad yadi |  
> vikrīyate damas tatra mūlyāt tu dviguṇo bhavet ||

nāradaḥ [11.8] |

> tathānyahaste vikrīya yo 'nyasmai tat prayacchati |  
> so 'pi taddviguṇaṃ dāpyo vinayaṃ tāvad eva tu ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.61] |

> satyaṃkārakṛtaṃ dravyaṃ dviguṇaṃ pratidāpayet |

**[433]** **'satyaṃkāraḥ'** krayavikrayasatyāpanārthaṃ yad dravyaṃ dīyate tad ucyate |

vyāsaḥ |

> satyaṃkāraṃ ca yo datvā yathākālaṃ na dṛśyate |  
> paṇyaṃ bhaven nisṛṣṭaṃ taddīyamānam agṛhṇataḥ ||

**'nisṛṣṭaṃ'** dattam |

nāradaḥ [11.9] |

> dīyamānaṃ na gṛhṇāti krītvā paṇyaṃ ca yaḥ krayī |  
> vikrīṇānas tad anyatra vikretā nāparādhnuyāt ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.255] |

> vikrītam api vikreyaṃ pūrvakretary agṛhṇati |  
> hāniś cet kretṛdoṣeṇa kretur eva hi sā bhavet ||

nāradaḥ |

> dīyamānaṃ na gṛhṇāti krītaṃ paṇyaṃ tu yaḥ krayī |  
> sa evāsya bhaved doṣo vikretur yo 'prayacchataḥ ||

**[434]** tathā [nā. 11.10–12] |

> dattamūlyasya paṇyasya vidhir eṣa prakīrtitaḥ |  
> adatte 'nyatra samayān na vikretur atikramaḥ ||  
> lābhārthaṃ vaṇijāṃ sarvapaṇyeṣu krayavikrayaḥ |  
> sa ca lābho 'rgham āsādya mahān bhavati vā na vā ||  
> tasmād deśe ca kāle ca vaṇig arghaṃ samāśrayet |  
> na jaihmena pravarteta śreyān evaṃ vaṇikpathaḥ ||

**iti mahārājādhirājaśrīmadgovindacandradevamahāsāndhivigrahikeṇa**

**bhaṭṭahṛdayadharātmajena**

**bhaṭṭaśrīmallakṣmīdhareṇa viracite kṛtyakalpatarau**

**vyavahārakāṇde vikrīyāsaṃpradānam ||**

**[435]**

## 66 krītvānuśayaḥ
atha krītvānuśayaḥ

tatra nāradaḥ [12.1–3] |

> krītvā mūlyena yaḥ paṇyaṃ krītaṃ na bahu manyate |  
> krītānuśaya ity etad vivādapadam ucyate ||  
> krītvā mūlyena yaḥ paṇyaṃ duṣkrītaṃ manyate krayī |  
> vikretuḥ pratideyaṃ tat tasminn evāhny avikṣatam ||  
> dvitīye 'hni dadat kretā mūlyaṃ triṃśāṃśam āvahet |  
> dviguṇaṃ tu tṛtīye 'hni parataḥ kretur eva tat ||

kātyāyanaḥ [686, 687] |

> krītvā tv anuśayāt paṇyaṃ tyajed dohyādi yo naraḥ |  
> aduṣtam eva kāle tu mūlyād daśamaṃ vahet ||  
> krītvā gacchann anuśayaṃ krayī hastam upāgate |  
> ṣaḍbhāgaṃ tatra mūlyasya datvā krītaṃ tyajed bhṛguḥ ||

**[436]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.258] |

> kṣayaṃ vṛddhiś ca vaṇijā paṇyāṇām avijānatā |  
> krītvā nānuśayaḥ kāryaḥ kurvan ṣaḍbhāgadaṇḍabhāk ||

nāradaḥ [12.16, 12, 8] |

> krītvā nānusayaṃ kuryād vaṇik paṇyavicakṣaṇaḥ |  
> kṣayaṃ vṛddhiṃ ca jānīyāt paṇyānāṃ yasya yādṛśī ||  
> kretā paṇyaṃ parīkṣeta prāk svayaṃ guṇadoṣataḥ |  
> parīkṣyābhimataṃ krītaṃ vikretur na bhavet punaḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [18.9] |

> parīkṣeta svayaṃ paṇyam anyeṣāṃ ca pardarśayet |  
> parīkṣitaṃ bahumataṃ gṛhītvā na punas tyajet ||

vyāsaḥ |

> carmakāṣṭheṣṭakāsūtradhānyāsavarasasya ca |  
> vastrakupyahiraṇyānāṃ sadya eva parīkṣaṇam ||

nāradaḥ [12.5,6] |

> tryahād dohyaṃ parīkṣeta pañcāhād vāhyam eva tu |  
> muktāvajrapravālānāṃ saptāhaṃ syāt parīkṣaṇam ||

**[437]** > dvipadām ardhamāsaṃ tu puṃsāṃ taddviguṇaṃ striyaḥ |  
> daśāhaḥ sarvabījānām ekāho lohavāsasām ||

nāradoktakrameṇa parīkṣākālam abhidhāya —

bṛhaspatiḥ [18.7] |

> ato 'rvāk paṇyadoṣas tu yadi saṃjāyate kvacit |  
> vikretuḥ pratideyaṃ tat kretā mūlyam avāpnuyāt ||

kātyāyanaḥ [688] |

> avijñātaṃ tu yat krītaṃ duṣṭaṃ paścād vibhāvitam |  
> krītaṃ tat svāmine deyaṃ paṇyaṃ kāle 'nyathā na tu ||

manuḥ [8.203] |

> nānyad anyena saṃsṛṣṭaṃ rūpaṃ vikrayam arhati |  
> na sāvadyaṃ na ca nyūnaṃ na dūre na tirohitam ||

nāradaḥ [12.7] |

> paribhuktaṃ tu yad vāsaḥ kliṣṭarūpaṃ malīmasam |  
> sadoṣaṃ api tat krītaṃ vikretur na bhavet punaḥ ||

**iti mahārājādhirājaśrīgovindacandradevamahāsandhivigrahikeṇa**

**bhaṭṭahṛdayadharātmajena**

**bhaṭṭaśrīmallakṣmīdhareṇa viracite kṛtyakalpatarau**

**vyavahārakāṇde krītvānuśayaḥ ||**

**[438]**

## 67 sīmāvivādaḥ
atha sīmāvivādaḥ

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ [19.1] |

> krayavikrayānuśaye vidhir eṣa udāhṛtaḥ |  
> grāmakṣetragṛhādīnāṃ sīmāvādaṃ vibodhata ||

nāradaḥ [14.1] |

> setukedāramaryādāvikṛṣṭākṛṣṭaniścaye |  
> kṣetrādhikāro yatra syād vivādaḥ kṣetrajas tu saḥ ||

asyārthaḥ — setukedārādimaryādādūratvasaṃnihitatvaniścaye kartavye kṣetraviṣayo vivādo 'sau **'kṣetraja'** ucyata iti |

kātyāyanaḥ [732] |

> ādhikyaṃ nyūnatā hy aṃśe astināstitvam eva ca |  
> abhogabhuktiḥ sīmā ca ṣaḍ vivādasya hetavaḥ ||

**[439]** **'abhogabhuktiḥ'** prāg avidyamānasya kṣetrāder bhuktiḥ |

manuḥ [8.245] |

> sīmāṃ prati samutpanne vivāde grāmayor dvayoḥ |  
> jyeṣṭhe māsi nayed enāṃ saṃprakāśeṣu setuṣu ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [19.2] |

> niveśakāle kartavyaḥ sīmāvidhiviniścayaḥ |  
> prakāśopāṃśucihnaiś ca lakṣitaḥ saṃśayāpahaḥ ||

manuḥ [8.246–48] |

> sīmāvṛkṣāṃś ca kurvīran nyagrodhāśvatthakiṃśukān |  
> śālmalīsālatālāṃś ca kṣīriṇaś caiva pādapān ||

**[440]** > gulmān veṇūṃś ca vividhān śamīvallīsthalāni ca |  
> śarān kubjakagulmāṃś ca tathā sīmā na naśyati ||  
> taḍāgāny udapānāni saritprasavaṇāni ca |  
> sīmāsandhiṣu kāryāṇi devatāyatanāni ca ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [19.8–9] |

> vāpīkūpataḍākāni caityārāmasurālayāḥ |  
> sthalanimnanadīstrotaḥśaragulmāśmarāśayaḥ ||  
> prakāśacihnāny etāni sīmāyāṃ kārayet sadā |  
> nihitāni tathānyāni yāni bhūmir na bhakṣayet ||

manuḥ [8.249–51] |

> upacchannāni cānyāni sīmāliṅgāni kārayet |  
> sīmājñāne nṛṇāṃ vīkṣya loke nityaviparyayam ||  
> aśmano 'sthīni govālāṃs tathā bhasmakapālikāḥ |  
> karīṣam iṣṭakāṅgārāṃś charkarā vālukāś ca ha ||

**[441]** > yāni caivaṃprakārāṇi kālād bhūmir na bhakṣayet |  
> tāni sandhiṣu sīmāyām aprakāśāni kārayet ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [19.20–21] |

> karīṣāsthituṣāṅgāraśarkarāśmakapālikāḥ |  
> sikateṣṭakagovālakārpāsāsthīni bhasma ca ||  
> prakṣipya kumbheṣv etāni sīmānteṣu nidhāpayet |  
> tataḥ paugaṇḍabālānāṃ prayatnena pradarśaye t||  
> vārdhakye ca śiśūnāṃ tu darśayeyus tathaiva ca |  
> evaṃ paramparājñāne sīmābhrāntir na jāyate ||

manuḥ [8.252] |

> etair liṅgair nayet sīmāṃ rājā vivadatāṃ nṛṇām |  
> pūrvabhuktyā ca satatam udakasyāgamena ca ||

'samunnayeyuḥ sīmānam' ity anuvṛttau nāradaḥ [14.6] |

> nimnagāpahṛtotsṛṣṭanaṣṭacihnāsu bhūmiṣu |  
> tatpradeśānumānaiś ca pramāṇair liṅgadarśanaiḥ ||

**[442]** manuḥ [8.253] |

> yadi saṃśaya eva syāl liṅgānām api darśane |  
> sākṣipratyaya eva syād vivāde sīmaniścayaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [733] |

> tasmin bhogaḥ prayoktavyaḥ sa ca sākṣiṣu tiṣṭhati |  
> lekhyārūḍhaś cetaraś ca sākṣī mārgadvayānvitaḥ ||

manuḥ [8.254–55, 258] |

> grāmeyakakulānāṃ ca samakṣaṃ sīmasākṣiṇaḥ |  
> praṣṭavyāḥ sīmaliṅgāni tayoś caiva vivādinoḥ ||  
> te pṛṣṭās tu yathā brūyuḥ samastāḥ sīmni niścayam |  
> tathā taṃ ca nibadhnīyāt samastāṃś caiva nāmataḥ ||  
> sākṣyabhāve tu catvāro grāmāḥ sīmantavāsinaḥ |  
> sīmāvinirṇayaṃ kuryuḥ prayatā rājasaṃnidhau ||

**'grāmeyakaḥ'** grāmyaḥ |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.152] |

> sāmāntā vā samagrāmāś catvāro 'ṣṭau daśāpi ca |  
> raktasragvasanāḥ sīmāṃ nayeyuḥ kṣitidhāriṇaḥ ||

**[443]** kātyāyanaḥ |

> teṣām abhāve sāmantā maulavṛddhoddhṛtādayaḥ |  
> sthāvare ṣaṭprakāre 'pi kāryā nātra vicāraṇā ||  
> kṣetravāstutaḍāgeṣu kūpopavanasetuṣu |  
> dvayor vivāde sāmantaiḥ prayayaḥ sarvavastuṣu ||  
> sāmantabhāvāt sāmantaiḥ kuryāt kṣetravinirṇayam |  
> grāmasīmāsu ca tathā tadvan nagaradeśayoḥ ||  
> svārthasiddhau praduṣṭeṣu sāmanteṣv arthagauravāt |  
> tatsaṃsaktais tu kartavya uddhāro nātra saṃśayaḥ ||  
> saṃsaktasaktaduṣṭeṣu tatsaṃsaktāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |  
> kartavyā na praduṣṭās tu rājñā dharmaṃ vijānatā ||  
> tyaktvā duṣṭāṃs tu sāmantān anyān maulādibhiḥ saha |  
> saṃmiśrya kārayet sīmām evaṃ dharmavido viduḥ ||  
> sāmantāḥ sādhanaṃ pūrvam aniṣṭoktau guṇānvitāḥ |  
> dviguṇās tūttarā jñeyās tato 'nye triguṇā matāḥ ||

**'tatsaṃsaktāḥ'** sāmantapratyāsannāḥ |

**[444]** śaṅkhalikhitau: "gṛhakṣetrayor virodhe sāmantapratyayaḥ | sāmantavirodhe [abhilekhyapratyayaḥ | abhi]lekhya virodhe grāmanagaravṛddhaśreṇipratyayaḥ | grāmanagaravṛddhaśreṇivirodhe daśavarṣānubhuktam anyatra rājaviprasvāt" |

nāradaḥ [14.2,3] |

> kṣetrasīmāvirodhe tu sāmantebhyo viniścayaḥ |  
> nagaragrāmagaṇino ye ca vṛddhatamā narāḥ ||  
> grāmasīmāsu ca bahir ye syus tatkṛṣijīvinaḥ |  
> gopāḥ śākunikā vyādhā ye cānye vanagocarāḥ ||

manuḥ [8.259–60] |

> sāmantānām abhāve tu maulānāṃ sīmasākṣiṇām |  
> imān apy anuyuñjīta puruṣān vanagocarān ||  
> vyādhāṃś chākunikān gopān kaivartān mūlakhānakān |  
> vyālagrāhān uñchavṛttīn anyāṃś ca vanagocarān ||

nāradaḥ [14.4–5] |

> samunnayeyuḥ sīmānaṃ lakṣaṇair upalikṣitām |  
> tuṣāṅgārakapālāsthikūpair āyatanair drumaiḥ ||

**[445]** > abhijñānaiś ca valmīkaiḥ sthalanimnonnatādibhiḥ |  
> kedārārāmamārgaiś ca purāṇaiḥ setubhis tathā ||

manuḥ [8.261] |

> te pṛṣṭās tu yathā brūyuḥ sīmāsandhiṣu lakṣaṇam |  
> tat tathā sthāpayed rājā dharmeṇa grāmayor dvayoḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [19.31] |

> śapathaiḥ śāpitāḥ svaiḥ svair brūyuḥ sīmni viniścayam |  
> darśayeyur nidhānāni tatpramāṇam iti sthitiḥ ||

manuḥ [8.256] |

> śirobhis te gṛhītvorvīṃ sragviṇo raktavāsasaḥ |  
> sukṛtaiḥ śāpitāḥ svaiḥ svair nayeyus te samañjasam ||

nāradaḥ [14.9–10] |

> naikaḥ samunnayet sīmāṃ naraḥ pratyayavān api |  
> gurutvād asya kāryasya kriyaiṣā bahuṣu sthitā ||  
> ekaś ced unnayet sīmāṃ sopavāsaḥ samunnayet |  
> raktamālyāmbaradharaḥ kṣitim āropya mūrdhani ||

bṛhaspatiḥ |

> jñātṛcihnavināśe 'pi eko 'py ubhayasaṃmataḥ |  
> raktamālyāmbaradharo mṛdam ādāya mūrdhani ||

**[446]** > satyavrataḥ sopavāsaḥ sīmāṃ saṃdarśayen naraḥ |

manuḥ [8.257, 263] |

> yathoktena nayantas te pūyante satyasākṣiṇaḥ |  
> viparītaṃ nayantas tu dāpyāḥ syur dviśataṃ damam ||  
> sāmantāś cen mṛṣā brūyuḥ setau vivadatāṃ nṛṇām |  
> sarve te ca pṛthag daṇḍyā rājñā madhyamasāhasam ||

**'setau'** sīmāyām |

katyāyanaḥ [750, 741] |

> bahūnāṃ tu gṛhītānāṃ na sarve nirṇayaṃ yadi |  
> kuryur bhayād vā lobhād vā dāpyās tūttamasāhasam ||  
> nājñānena hi mucyante sāmantā nirṇayaṃ prati |  
> ajñānoktau daṇḍayitvā punaḥ sīmāṃ vicārayet ||  
> kīrtite yadi bhedaḥ syād daṇḍyās tūttamasāhasam ||

nāradaḥ |

> śeṣāś ced anṛtaṃ brūyur niyuktā bhūmikarmaṇi |  
> jaghanyās te 'pi pratyekaṃ vineyāḥ pūrvasāhasam ||

**[447]** > gaṇavṛddhādayas tv anye daṇḍaṃ dadyuḥ pṛthak pṛthak |  
> vineyāḥ prathamenaiva sāhasenānṛte sthitāḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [738, 736, 743] |

> saṃsaktakās tu sāmāntās tatsaṃsaktās tathottarāḥ |  
> saṃsaktasaktasaktāntāḥ padmākārāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||  
> grāmo grāmasya sāmantaḥ kṣetraṃ kṣetrasya kīrtitam |  
> gṛhaṃ gṛhasya nirdiṣṭaṃ samantāt parirabhya ca ||  
> ye tatra pūrvasāmantāḥ paścād deśāntaraṃ gatāḥ |  
> tanmūlatvāt tu maulās te ṛṣibhiḥ saṃprakīrtitāḥ ||

'grāmo grāmasya sāmantaḥ' iti | grāmajano grāmajanasya vivāde sāmanto na punas tadgrāmīṇa eva tatra sāmanta ity arthaḥ | evaṃ kṣetram ityādy api | kṣetragṛhaśabdābhyāṃ tatsvāminau lakṣyete |

bṛhaspatiḥ [19.38–39] |

> tadutapnnāś ca sāmantā ye 'nye deśāntarasthitāḥ |  
> maulās te tu samādiṣṭāḥ praṣṭavyāḥ kāryanirṇaye ||  
> aduṣṭās te tu yad brūyuḥ saṃdigdhau amavṛttayaḥ |  
> tatpramāṇaṃ tu kartavyam evaṃ dharmo na hīyate ||

**[448]** kātyāyanaḥ [744–45] |

> niṣpādyamānaṃ yair dṛṣṭaṃ tat kāryaṃ nṛguṇānvitaiḥ |  
> vṛddhā vā yadi vāvṛddhās te vṛddhāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ||  
> upaśavaṇasaṃbhogakāryākhyānopacihnitāḥ |  
> uddharanti tato yasmād uddhṛtās te tataḥ smṛtāḥ ||

**'upaśravaṇam'** paramparāprasiddhiḥ | **'saṃbhogo'** bhuktiḥ | **'kāryākhyānaṃ'** tatphalakaragrahaṇavārtā |

nāradaḥ |

> dhvajinī sandhinī caiva naidhānī bhayavarjitā |  
> rājaśāsananītā ca sīmā pañcavidhā smṛtā ||

vyāsaḥ |

> nimnonnatā ca dhvajinī naidhānī rājakāritā |  
> sthirā pañcavidhā sīmā matsyinī tu chalā smṛtā ||

**[449]** > grāmayor ubhayor yatra gartaḥ sīmāpravartakaḥ |  
> nimnopalakṣitā sā tu śāstravidbhir udāhṛtā ||  
> śarakuñjakavalmīkā yatra devagṛhāṇi ca |  
> aśmakūṭāś ca dṛśyante jñeyā sā tu samunnatā ||  
> grāmayor ubhayoḥ sīmni vṛkṣā yatra samunnatāḥ |  
> samucchritā dhvajākārā dvajinī sā prakīrtitā ||  
> iṣtakāṅgārasikatāḥ śarkarāsthikapālikāḥ |  
> nihitā yatra dṛśyante naidhānī sā prakīrtitā ||  
> sākṣyabhāve dvayor yatra prabhuṇā parikalpitā |  
> sāmantānumatā sīmā jñeyā sā rājakāritā ||

kātyāyanaḥ [747] |

> bhayavarjitabhūpena sarvābhāve svayaṃkrtā |

nāradaḥ [14.11] |

> yadā tu na syur jñātāraḥ sīmāyā na ca lakṣaṇam |  
> tadā rājā dvayoḥ sīmām unnayed iṣṭataḥ svayam ||

vyāsaḥ |

> svacchandagā bahujalā jhaṣakūrmaiḥ samanvitā |  
> nityapravāhinī yatra sīmā sā matsyinī matā ||

**[450]** manuḥ [8.265] |

> sīmāyām aviṣahyāyāṃ svayaṃ rājaiva dharmavit |  
> pradiśed bhūmim eteṣām upakārād iti sthitiḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ, vyāsaś ca [prathame bṛh. 19.40] |

> anyagrāmāt samāśritya dattānyasya yadā mahī | 1  
> mahānadyātha vā rājñā kathaṃ tatra vicāraṇā || 2  
> nadyotsṛṣṭā rājadattā yasya tasyaiva sā mahī | 3  
> anyathā na bhavel lābho narāṇāṃ rājadaivikaḥ || 4  
> kṣayodayau jīvanaṃ ca daivarājavaśān nṛṇām | 5  
> tasmāt sarveṣu kāryeṣu tat kṛtaṃ na vicālayet || 6

**[451]**  
> grāmayor ubhayor yatra maryādā kalpitā nadī | 7  
> kṣayodayena cālpā sā cālayan daṇḍam arhati || 8  
> kurute dānaharaṇaṃ bhāgyābhāgyavaśān nṛṇām | 9  
> ekatra kūlapātaṃ tu bhūmer anyatra saṃsthitam || 10  
> nadī tīre prakurute tasya tāṃ na vicālayet | 11  
> kṣetraṃ sasasyam ullaṅghya bhūmiś chinnā yadā bhavet || 12  
> nadīsrotaḥpravāheṇa pūrvasvāmī labheta tām || 13  
> yā rājñā krodhalobhena chalanyāyena vā hṛtā | 14  
> pradattānyasya tuṣṭena na sā siddhim avāpnuyāt || 15   
> pramāṇarahitāṃ bhūmiṃ bhuñjāno yasya yā hṛtā | 16  
> guṇādhikāya vā dattā tasya tāṃ na vicālayet || 17

**[452]**

**67 (ka) — athatideśāḥ**

tatra kātyāyanaḥ |

> daśagrāmaśatagrāmasahasragrāmalakṣaṇāt |  
> viṣayān nṛpatiḥ kuryāc cihnaiḥ sīmāviniścitān ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.154] |

> ārāmāyatanagrāmanipānodyānaveśmasu |  
> eṣa eva vidhir jñeyo varṣāmbupravahādiṣu ||

ayam eva sāmantasākṣyādilakṣaṇo vidhir jñātavyaḥ |

manuḥ [8.262] |

> kṣetrakūpataḍāgānām ārāmasya gṛhasya ca |  
> sāmantapratyayo jñeyaḥ sīmāsandhivinirṇayaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [749] |

> kṣetrakūpataḍāgānāṃ kedārārāmayor api |  
> gṛhaprāsādāvasatheṣv evaṃ devagṛheṣu ca ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [19.45–46] |

> niveśakālād ārabhya gṛhavāryāpaṇādikam |  
> yena yāvad yathā bhuktaṃ tasya tan naiva cālayet ||

**[453]** > vātāyanaṃ praṇālīś ca tathā niryūhavedikāḥ |  
> catuḥśālaṃ syandanikāḥ prāṅniviṣṭā na cālayet ||

**'niryūho'** dvāranirgataḥ kāṣṭhaviseṣaḥ | **'vedikā'** pratolyādideśe saṃskṛtonnatā bhūmiḥ | **'catuḥśālaṃ'** caturdvāragṛham | **'syandanikā'** paṭalaprāntaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [752–53] |

> mekhalābhramaniṣkāsagavākṣān noparodhayet |  
> praṇālīṃ gṛhavāstuṃ ca pīḍayan daṇḍabhāg bhavet ||  
> niveśasamayād ūrdhvaṃ naite yojyāḥ kadācana |  
> dṛṣṭipātaṃ praṇālīṃ ca na kuryāt paraveśvasu ||

**'mekhalā'** kuḍyamūlabandhaḥ | **'bhramaḥ'** jalanirgamaḥ | **'niṣkāsaḥ'** harmyādibhittiṣu nirgataṃ kāṣṭhādinirmitam aspṛṣṭabhūmikam upaveśasthānam | **'noparodhayet'** na nirundhyāt | **'gṛhavāstu'** vāsabhūmiḥ | **'dṛṣṭipāto'** gavākṣaḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ [19.49] |

> varcaḥsthānaṃ vahnicayaṃ gartocchiṣṭāmbusecanam |  
> atyārāt parakuḍyasya na kartavyaṃ kadācana ||

**'atyārāt'** atisamīme |

**[454]** kātyāyanaḥ [754] |

> viṇmūtrodakacakraṃ ca vahiniśvabhraniveśanam |  
> aratnidvayam utsṛjya parakuḍyān niveśayet ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [19.51] |

> yānty āyānti janā yena paśavaś cānivāritāḥ |  
> tad ucyate saṃsaraṇaṃ na roddhavyaṃ tu kenacit ||

nāradaḥ [14.15] |

> avaskarasthalaśvabhrabhramasyandanikādibhiḥ |  
> catuṣpathasurasthānarathyāmārgān na rodhayet ||

**'rathyā'** catvaraḥ |

śaṅkhalikhitau: "mārgakṣetre pathi visargo, rājamārge rathaparivarthanam, pūrvamaryādāsthāpanam, toraṇagṛharathyāntareṣu tripadam, devarājāyataneṣu yatheṣṭam" |

**'mārgakṣetre'** mārge yat kṣetraṃ tatra | **'pathi visargo'** vartma nāvaroddhavyam ity arthaḥ | **'rājamārge rathaparivartanam'** yāvatā deśena rathaḥ parivartane tāvān deśo rājamārge tyaktavya ity arthaḥ | **'toraṇagṛharathyāntareṣu tripadam'** toraṇagṛharathyāsamīpe padatrayaparimitaṃ deśaṃ parityajed ity arthaḥ |

**[455]** kātyāyanaḥ [655–57] |

> sarve janāḥ sadā yena prayānti sa catuṣpathaḥ |  
> aniṣiddhā yathākālaṃ rājamārgaḥ sa ucyate ||  
> na tatra ropayet kiṃcin nopahanyāt tu kenacit |  
> gurvācāryanṛpādīnāṃ mārgādānāt tu daṇḍabhāk ||  
> yas tatra saṅkaraśvabhrān vṛkṣāropaṇam eva ca |  
> kāmāt purīṣaṃ kuryāc ca tasya daṇḍas tu māṣakaḥ ||

**'saṅkaro'** avakaraḥ |

manuḥ [9.282–83] |

> samutsṛjed rājamārge yas tv amedhyam anāpadi |  
> sa dvau kārṣāpaṇau dadyād amedhyaṃ sa ca śodhayet ||  
> āpadgatas tathā vṛddho garbhiṇī bāla eva vā |  
> paribhāṣaṇam arhanti tac ca śodhyam iti sthitiḥ ||

'daṇḍyaḥ' ity anuvṛttau viṣṇuḥ [5.105: "pathyudyānodakasamīpeṣv aśucyutkarādityāge paṇaśatam" iti |

kātyāyanaḥ [758–59] |

> taḍāgodyānatīrthāni [yo 'medhyena vināśayet |  
> amedhyaṃ śodhayitvā tu daṇḍayet pūrvasāhasam ||

**[456]**  
> dūṣayet siddhatīrthāni] sthāpitāni mahātmabhiḥ |  
> purāṇāni pavitrāṇi prāpnuyāt pūrvasāhasam ||

manuḥ [8.264] |

> gṛhaṃ taḍāgam ārāmaṃ kṣetraṃ vā bhīṣayā haran |  
> śatāni pañca daṇḍyaḥ syād ajñānād dviśato damaḥ ||

**'bhīṣayā'** bhayotpādanena |

vṛddhamanuḥ |

> sthāpitāṃ caiva maryādām ubhayor grāmayos tathā |  
> atikrāmanti ye pāpās te daṇḍyā dviśataṃ damam ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.155] |

> maryādāyāḥ prabhede tu sīmātikrameṇe tathā |  
> kṣetrasya haraṇe daṇḍā adhamottamamadhyamāḥ ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: "kṣetramaryādābhede 'ṣṭaśatam, sīmāvyatikrame 'ṣṭasahasram, kṣetrodakāpaharaṇe 'ṣṭaśatam" |

viṣṇuḥ [5.172]: "sīmābhettāram uttamaṃ sāhasaṃ daṇḍayitvā punaḥ sīmāṃ kārayet" |

kātyāyanaḥ [760–61] |

> sīmāmadhye tu jātānāṃ vṛkṣāṇāṃ kṣetrayor dvayoḥ |  
> phalaṃ puṣpaṃ ca sāmānyaṃ kṣetrasvāmiṣu nirdiśet ||

**[457]** > anyakṣetreṣu jātānāṃ śākhā yatrānyasaṃsthitāḥ |  
> svāminaṃ tu vijānīyād yatra kṣetre tu saṃsthitāḥ ||

**iti saprakriyamahāsāndhivigrahikabhaṭṭahṛdayadharātmaja-**

**bhaṭṭaśrīmallakṣmīdharaviracite kṛtyakalpatarau**

**vyavahārakāṇde sīmāvivādākhyaṃ parva ||**

**67 — (kha) atha setuḥ**

tatra nāradaḥ [14.17] |

> parakṣetrasya madhye tu setur na pratiṣidhyate |  
> mahāguṇo 'lpabādhaś ced vṛddhir iṣṭā kṣaye sati ||

asyārthaḥ — anyakṣetre 'nyena kriyamāṇaḥ setur yadi bahūpakārakaḥ kṣetrasvāminaś cālpabādhākaras tadā nāsau nivartyaḥ | yato 'lpopakṣaye saty api vṛddhiḥ sasyādyupacayalakṣaṇā sarvasyeṣṭā bhavati |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.156–57] |

> na niṣedhyo 'lpabādhas tu setuḥ kalyāṇakārakaḥ |  
> parabhūmiṃ haran kūpaḥ svalpakṣetro bahūdakaḥ ||  
> svāmine yo 'nivedyaiva kṣetre setuṃ pravartayet |  
> utpanne svāmine bhogas tadabhāve mahīpateḥ ||

**[458]** nāradaḥ [14.20–22] |

> pūrvapravṛttam utsannam apṛṣṭvā svāminaṃ tu yaḥ |  
> setuṃ pravartayet kaścin na sa tatphalabhāg bhavet ||  
> mṛte tu svāmini punas tadvaṃśye vāpi mānave |  
> rājānam āmantrya tataḥ kuryāt steupravartanam ||  
> ato 'nyathā kleśabhāk syān mṛgavyādhānudarśanāt |  
> iṣavas tasya naśyanti yo viddham anuvidhyati ||

**'svāminam'** setusvāminam |

kātyāyanaḥ [762–63] |

> asvāmyanumatenaiva saṃskāraṃ kurute tu yaḥ |  
> gṛhodyānataḍāgānāṃ saṃskartā labhate na tu ||  
> deyaṃ svāmini cāyāte na nivedya nṛpe yadi |  
> athāvedya prayuktas tu tatkṛtaṃ labhate vyayam ||

nāradaḥ [14.17, 18] |

> setus tu dvividhaḥ proktaḥ kheyo bandhyas tathaiva ca |  
> toyapravartanāt kheyo bandhyaḥ syād vinivartanāt ||  
> nāntareṇodakaṃ sasyaṃ nāśaś cābhyadhike sati |  
> ya evānudake doṣaḥ sa evātyudake bhavet ||

**iti mahāsāndhivigrahikasaprakriyabhaṭṭahṛdayadharātmaja-**

**bhaṭṭalakṣmīdharaviracite kṛtyakalpatarau**

**vivādakāṇde setuparva ||**

**[459]**

**67 (ga) — atha vikṛṣṭākṛṣṭe**

tatra nāradaḥ [14.23–24] |

> aśaktapretanaṣṭeṣu kṣetrikeṣv anivāritaḥ |  
> kṣetraṃ ced vikṛṣet kaścid aśnuvīta sa tatphalam ||  
> vikṛṣyamāṇe kṣetre tu kṣetrikaḥ punar āvrajet |  
> khilopacāraṃ tat sarvaṃ datvā kṣetram avāpnuyāt ||

kātyāyanaḥ [764] |

> aśaktito na dadyāc cet khilārthe yaḥ kṛto vyayaḥ |  
> tadaṣṭabhāgahīnaṃ tu karṣakaḥ phalam āpnuyāt ||  
> varṣāṇy aṣṭau sa bhoktā syāt parataḥ svāminas tu tat |

nāradaḥ [14.26, 27, 42, 43] |

> saṃvatsareṇārdhakhilaṃ khilaṃ syād vatsarais tribhiḥ |  
> pañcavarṣāvasannaṃ tu kṣetraṃ syād aṭavīsamam ||  
> kṣetraṃ tripuruṣaṃ yat syād gṛhaṃ vā syāt kramāgatam |  
> rājaprasādād anyatra na tadbhogaḥ param nayet ||

**[460]**  
> gṛhaṃ kṣetraṃ ca dṛṣṭe dve vāsahetū kuṭumbinām |
