> tasmāt te nākṣiped rājā tad dhi mūlaṃ kuṭumbinām ||  
> vṛddhe janapade rājño dharmaḥ kośaś ca vardhate |  
> hīyate hīyamāne tu vṛddhihetum ataḥ śrayet ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.158] |

> phālāhatam api kṣetraṃ yo na kuryān na kārayet |  
> taṃ pradāpyākṛṣṭasadaṃ kṣetram anyena kārayet ||

**'akṛṣṭasadam'** iti — akṛṣṭasya kṣetrasya **'sadam'** sasyādiphalam, kṛṣṭakṣetrānusāreṇa dāpayitvā ity arthaḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ |

> hṛhītvā vahayet kāle vāpagopanasaṃgrahān |  
> akurvaṇ svāmine dāpyo madhyaṃ kṛṣṭasadaṃ tu yaḥ ||

**'madhyaṃ kṛṣṭasadam'** notkṛṣṭaṃ nāpakṛṣṭaṃ yat kṛṣṭakṣetraphalaṃ tadanusāreṇa dāpayitavyaḥ ity arthaḥ

**[461]** vyāsaḥ |

> kṣetraṃ gṛhītvā yaḥ kaścin na kuryān na ca kārayet |  
> svāmine sa sadaṃ dāpyo rājñā daṇḍyas ca tatsamam ||  
> cirāvasanne daśamaṃ kṛṣyamāṇe tathāṣṭamam |  
> susaṃskṛte tu ṣaṣṭhaṃ syāt parikalpya yathāsthiti ||

**[iti kṛṣṭākṛṣṭaparva]**

**67 — (gha) atha sasyarakṣā**

tatra yājñavalkyaḥ [2.166] |

> grāmecchayā gopracāro bhūmī rājavaśena vā |

tathā [2.167] |

> dhanuḥśataṃ parīṇāho grāmakṣetrāntaraṃ bhavet |  
> dve śate kharvaṭasya syān nagarasya catuḥśatam ||

**'kharvaṭaḥ'** bahukārukṛṣīvalo grāmaḥ |

**[462]** manuḥ [8.237–38] |

> dhanuḥśataṃ parīhāro grāmasya syāt samantataḥ |  
> śamyāpātās trayo vāpi triguṇo nagarasya tu ||  
> tatrāparivṛtaṃ dhānyaṃ vihiṃsyuḥ paśavo yadi |  
> na tatra praṇayed daṇḍaṃ nṛpatiḥ paśurakṣiṇām ||

nāradaḥ [14.40] |

> grāmopānte ca yat kṣetraṃ vivītānte mahāpathe |  
> anāvṛtaṃ cet tannāśe na pālasya vyatikramaḥ ||

viṣṇuḥ [5.148–49]: "pathi grāme vivītānte na doṣo 'nāvṛte cālpakālam" |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.162] |

> pathi grāme vivītānte kṣetre doṣo na vidyate |  
> akāmataḥ kāmacāre cauravad daṇḍam arhati |

**[463]** '**vivīta**'śabdena yavasādyarthaṃ rakṣito bhūpradeśa ucyate |

manuḥ [8.240] |

> pathi kṣetre parivṛte grāmāntīye 'tha vā punaḥ |  
> sapālaḥ śatadaṇḍārho vipālaṃ dhārayet paśum ||

**'grāmāntīye'** grāmasamīpe kṣetre | **'vipālam'** rakṣakaśūnyam |

nāradaḥ [14.28] |

> utkramya tu vṛtiṃ yaḥ syāt sasyaghāto gavādibhiḥ |  
> pālaḥ śāsyo bhavet tatra na cec chakto nivāreyet |

**'vṛtiḥ'** āvaraṇam |

uśanā |

> gobhir vināśitaṃ dhānyaṃ yo naraḥ pratiyācate |  
> pitaras tasya nāśnanti nāśnanti ca divaukasaḥ ||

nāradaḥ [14.41] |

> pathi kṣetre vṛtiḥ kāryā yām uṣṭro nāvalokayet |  
> na laṅghayet paśur nāśvo na bhindyād yāṃ tu sūkaraḥ ||

śaṅkhalikhitau |

> mārgakṣetre vṛtiḥ kāryā yām uṣṭro nāvalokayet |

**[464]** nāśvasūkarāv antaraṃ vindetām |

kātyāyanaḥ [666] |

> ajāteṣv api sasyeṣu kuryād āvaraṇaṃ mahat |  
> duḥkhena hi nivāryante labdhasvādurasā mṛgāḥ ||

**iti sasyarakṣā**

**67 — (ṅa) atha sasyaghātadaṇḍaḥ**

tatra manuḥ [8.241] |

> kṣetreṣv anyeṣu tu paśuḥ sapādaṃ daṇḍam arhati |

**'anyeṣu'** iti — pathikṣetragrāmāntīyebhya ity avagantavyam |

śaṅkhalikhitau: "rātrau carantī gauḥ pañca māṣān | divā trīn | muhūrte māṣam | grāse tv adaṇḍyaḥ" |

kātyāyanaḥ [667] |

> dāpayet paṇapādaṃ gāṃ dvau pādau mahiṣīṃ tathā |  
> athājāvikavatsānāṃ pādo daṇḍaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||

**[465]** gautamaḥ [12.19–22]: "pañca māṣā gavi | ṣaḍ uṣṭrakhare | aśvamahiṣyor daśa | ajāviṣu dvau dvau" |

"daṇḍaṃ prāpnuyād" ity anuvṛttau śaṅkhalikhitau: "sarveṣām eva vatso māṣam, ahiṣī daśa, kharoṣṭraṃ ṣoḍaśa, ajāvikaṃ caturaḥ" |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.159] |

> māṣān aṣṭau tu mahiṣī sasyaghatasya kāriṇī |  
> daṇḍanīyā tadardhaṃ tu gaus tadardham ajāvikam ||

nāradaḥ [14.29] |

> samūlasasyanāśe tu svāmī sadam avāpnuyāt |  
> vadhena gopo mucyeta daṇḍaṃ svāmini pātayet ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.160] |

> bhakṣayitvopaviṣṭānāṃ yathoktād dviguṇo damaḥ |  
> samam eṣāṃ vivīte 'pi kharoṣṭraṃ mahiṣīsamam ||

**[466]** nāradaḥ [14.31, 34] |

> gāvaḥ pādaṃ pradaṇḍyāḥ syur mahiṣyo dviguṇaṃ tataḥ |  
> ajāvike savatse tu māṣo daṇḍaḥ paraḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
> sannānāṃ dviguṇo daṇḍo vasatāṃ ca caturguṇaḥ |  
> pratyakṣacārakāṇāṃ tu cauradaṇḍaḥ smṛto budhaiḥ ||

viṣṇuḥ [5.140–45]: "mahiṣī cet sasyanāśaṃ kuryāt pālakas tv aṣṭau māṣān daṇḍyaḥ | apālakāyāḥ svāmī | aśvas tūṣṭro gardabho vā | goś cet tadardham | tadardham ajāvikaṃ cet | bhakṣayitvopaviṣṭeṣu dviguṇam" |

**'aśvas tūṣṭro gardabho vā'** sasyanāśaṃ kuryād ity anvayaḥ |

nāradaḥ [14.35] |

> naṣṭā yā pāladoṣeṇa gauḥ kṣetraṃ tu vināśayet |  
> na tatra svāmino doṣaḥ pālas tāḍanam arhati ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [16.17] |

> sasyān nivārayed gās tu cīrṇe doṣo dvayor bhavet |  
> svāmī sadadamaṃ dāpyaḥ pālas tāḍanam arhati ||

**[467]** **'sadadamam'** bhakṣitakṣetre phalānurūpaṃ damam |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.161] |

> yāvat sasyaṃ vinaśyet tu tāvat syāt kṣetriṇāṃ phalam |  
> gopas tāḍyaś ca gomī tu pūrvoktaṃ daṇḍam arhati ||

**'gomī'** gosvāmī |

viṣṇuḥ [5.146]: "sarvatra svāmine vinaṣtasasyamūlyaṃ ca" |

nāradaḥ [14.38-39] |

> gobhis tu bhakṣitaṃ sasyaṃ yo naraḥ pratiyācate |  
> sāmantānumataṃ deyaṃ dhānyaṃ yat tatra vāpitam ||  
> gavatraṃ gominā deyaṃ dhānyaṃ vai karṣakāya ca |  
> evaṃ hi vinayaḥ prokto gavāṃ sasyāvamardane ||

**'gavatram'** yavasam |

**iti sasyaghātakaparma |**

**[468]**

**67 — (c) athādaṇḍyāḥ**

"tatra pāla" ity anvartamāne naradaḥ [14.36, 37] |

> rājagrāhagṛhīto vā vajrāśanihato 'pi vā |  
> atha sarpeṇa vā daṣṭo vṛkṣād vā patito bhavet ||  
> vyāghādibhir hato vāpi vyādhibhir vāpy upadrutaḥ |  
> na tatra doṣaḥ pālasya na ca doṣo 'sti gominām ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.163] |

> mahokṣotsṛṣṭapaśavaḥ sūtkāgantukādayaḥ |  
> pālo yeṣāṃ na te mocyā daivarājapariplutāḥ ||

manuḥ [8.242] |

> anirdaśāhāṃ gāṃ sūtāṃ vṛṣān devapaśūṃs tathā |  
> sapālān vā vipālān vā na daṇḍyān manur abravīt ||

śaṅkhaḥ: "chāgavṛṣabhā anirdaśāhā gāvaḥ sasyāparādhe na daṇḍam āpnuyuḥ" |

**[469]** nāradaḥ [14.30] |

> gauḥ prasūtā daśāhaṃ tu mahokṣo vājikuñjarāḥ |  
> nivāryāḥ syuḥ prayatnena teṣāṃ svāmī na daṇḍabhāk ||

uśanā |

> adaṇḍyā hastino 'śvāś ca prajāpālā hi te smṛtāḥ |  
> adaṇḍyāḥ kāṇakūṭāś ca vṛṣaś ca kṛtalakṣaṇaḥ ||  
> adaṇḍyāgantukā gauś ca sūtikā cābhisāriṇī |  
> adaṇḍyāś cotsave gāvaḥ śrāddhakāle tathaiva ca ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: "kṣudrapaśavaḥ sarvathānivāryāḥ | aśvataragajavājinaś cādaṇḍyāḥ | avaśyāś ca śanair apavāryāḥ" |

kātyāyanaḥ [665, 664] |

> adhamottamamadhyānāṃ paśūnāṃ caiva tāḍane |  
> svāmī tu vivaded yatra tatra daṇḍaṃ prakalpayet ||

**[470]** > kṣetrārāmavivīteṣu gṛheṣu paśukādiṣu |  
> garhaṇaṃ tatpraviṣṭānāṃ tāḍanaṃ ca bṛhaspatiḥ ||

**[ity adaṇḍyaparva]**

**iti mahārājādhirājaśrīmadgovindcandradevamahāsāndhivigrahika-**

**bhaṭṭahṛdayadharātmajabhaṭṭaśrīlakṣmīdharaviracite **

**kṛtyakalpatarau vyavahārakāṇde sīmāvivādah ||**

**[471]**

## 68 vākpāruṣyam
atha vākpāruṣyam

tatra nāradaḥ [18.1] |

> deśajātikulādīnām ākrośanyaṅgasaṃjñitam |  
> yad vacaḥ pratikūlārthaṃ vākpāruṣyaṃ tad ucyate ||

**'ākrośo'** nindā | tatra **'deśākrośo'** yathā gauḍaṃ prati "kalahapriyā gauḍāḥ" iti | **'jātyākrośo'** yathā vipraṃ prati "nitāntalolupā viprāḥ" iti | **'kulākrośo'** yathā "krūracaritā vaiśvāmitrāḥ" iti | '**ādi**'śabdena vidyāder upādānam | **'nyaṅgasaṃjñitam'** aślīlam |

kātyāyanaḥ [768] |

> huṅkāraṃ kāsanaṃ caiva loke yac ca vigarhitam |  
> anukuryād anubrūyād vākpāruṣyaṃ tad ucyate ||

nāradaḥ [18.2–3] |

> niṣṭhurāślilatīvratvād tad api trividhaṃ smṛtam |  
> gauravānukramād asya daṇḍo yuktaḥ kramād guruḥ ||

**[472]** > sākṣepaṃ niṣṭhuraṃ jñeyam aślīlaṃ nyaṅgasaṃjñitam |  
> patanīyair upakrośais tīvram āhur manīṣiṇaḥ ||

**'gauravānukramāt'** anukrameṇa gurutaratvāt |

kātyāyanaḥ [770–72] |

> yat tv asatsaṃjñair aṅgaiḥ param ākṣipati kvacit |  
> abhūtair vātha bhūtair vā niṣṭhurā vāk smṛtā tu sā ||  
> nyaṅgāvagūraṇaṃ vācā krodhāt tu kurute yadā |  
> vṛttadeśakulānāṃ ca aślīlā sā budhaiḥ smṛtā ||  
> mahāpātakayoktrī ca rājadveśakarī ca yā |  
> jātibhraṃśakarī vātha tīvrā sā prathitā tu vāk ||

**'nyaṅgāvagūraṇam'** nikṛṣṭāṅgaprakāśena tiraskaraṇam |

bṛhaspatiḥ |

> apriyoktis tāḍanaṃ ca pāruṣyaṃ dvividhaṃ smṛtam |  
> ekaikaṃ tu tridhā bhinnaṃ damaś coktas trialakṣaṇam ||  
> deśagrāmakulādīnāṃ kṣepaḥ pāpe niyojanam |  
> dravyaṃ vinā tu prathamaṃ vākpāruṣyaṃ tad ucyate ||

**[473]** > bhaginīmātṛsaṃbandham upapātakaśaṃsanam |  
> pāruṣyaṃ madhyamaṃ proktaṃ vācikaṃ śāstravedibhiḥ ||  
> abhakṣyāpeyakathanaṃ mahāpātakadūṣaṇam |  
> pāruṣyam uttamaṃ proktaṃ tīvraṃ marmābhighaṭṭanam ||

**'dravyaṃ vinā'** ity atra dravyaśabdo 'bhidheyaparaḥ | tenocyamānārthavyatirekeṇaivaṃvidham abhidhānaṃ vākpāruṣyam ity arthaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [773–74] |

> yo 'guṇān kīrtayet krodhān nirguṇe vā guṇajñatām |  
> anyasaṃjñānuyogī ca vāgduṣṭaṃ taṃ naraṃ viduḥ ||  
> duṣṭasyaiva hi yān doṣān kīrtayet krodhakāraṇāt |  
> anyāpadeśavādī ca vāgduṣṭaṃ taṃ naraṃ viduḥ ||

**[474]** bṛhaspatiḥ [20.8] |

> samānayoḥ samo daṇḍo nyūnasya dviguṇas tu saḥ |  
> uttamasyārdhikāḥ prokto vākpāruṣye parasparam ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.206–07] |

> ardho 'dhameṣu dviguṇaḥ parastrīṣūttameṣu ca |  
> daṇḍapraṇayanaṃ kāryaṃ varṇajātyuttarādharaiḥ ||  
> pratilomāpavādeṣu dviguṇatriguṇā damāḥ |  
> varṇānām ānulomyena tasmād ardhārdhahānitaḥ ||

**'ardho'** pañcaviṃśateḥ | 'pañcaviṃśatiko damaḥ' iti pūrvam uktatvāt | **'adhameṣu'** ākṣeptrapekṣayā nikṛṣṭaguṇādiṣu ākṣipteṣv ākṣeptur uttamād ardhadaṇḍo rājñā grāhya ity arthaḥ | evam uttaratrāpi | **'varṇāḥ'** kṣatraviprādayaḥ | **'jātayo'** 'tra mūrdhāvasiktamlecchādayaḥ |

**[475]** kātyāyana-uśanasau [775] |

> mohāt pramādāt saṃharṣāt prītyā coktaṃ mayeti yaḥ |  
> nāham evaṃ punar vakṣye daṇḍārdhaṃ tasya kalpayet ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.204] |

> satyāsatānyathāstotrair nyūnāṅgendriyarogiṇām |  
> kṣepaṃ karoti ced daṇḍyaḥ paṇān ardhatrayodaśa ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [20.5] |

> samajātiguṇānāṃ ca vākpāruṣyo parasparam |  
> vinayo 'bhihitaḥ śāstre paṇān ardhatrayodaśa ||

viṣṇuḥ [5.35–36]: "samavarākrośane dvādaśapaṇān daṇḍyaḥ | hīnavarṇākrośane ṣaṭ" |

manu-nāradau [ma. 8.274; nā. 18.18] |

> kāṇaṃ vāpy atha vā khañjam anyaṃ vāpi tathāvidham |  
> tathyenāpi bruvan dāpyo daṇḍaṃ kārṣapaṇāvaram ||

viṣṇu [5.27]: "daṇḍyaḥ kāṇakhañjādīnāṃ tathāvādy api kārṣāpaṇadvayam" |

**[476]** śaṅkhalikhitau: "yathākālam uttamavarṇākṣepe tatpramādo daṇḍyas trayo vā kārṣapaṇāḥ | śuktavākyābhidhāne 'py evam eva" |

tathā: "savarṇavyatikrame dvādaś kārṣapaṇāḥ | yathārūpaviśiṣṭākṣepe 'viśiṣṭasya caturviṃśati | aviśiṣṭasyātikrame viśiṣṭasya tato 'rdham" |

manu-nāradau [ma. 8.269; nā. 18.17] |

> savarṇe hi dvijātīnāṃ dvādaśaiva vyatikrame |  
> vādeṣv avacanīyeṣu tad eva dviguṇaṃ bhavet ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.205, 208–09] |

> abhigantāsmi bhaginīṃ mātaraṃ ca taveti ha |  
> śapantaṃ dāpayed rājā pañcaviṃśatikaṃ damam ||

**[477]** > bāhugrīvānetrasakthivināśe vācike damaḥ |  
> śatyas tato 'rdhikaḥ pādanāsākarṇakarādiṣu ||  
> aśaktas tu vadann evaṃ daṇḍanīyaḥ paṇān daśa |  
> tathā śaktaḥ pratibhuvaṃ dāpyaḥ kṣemāya tasya tu ||

**'vācike vināśe'** bāhuṃ chetsyāmītyādirūpataḥ | **'śatyaḥ'** śataparimito daṇḍaḥ | **'pādanāsākarṇakarādiṣu vināśe vācike'** ity anuṣaṅgaḥ | **'aśaktaḥ'** vināśakaraṇāsamarthaḥ | **'pratibhuvaṃ dāpyaḥ'** śataṃ daṇḍayitvā aśaktasya kṣemārthaṃ lagnakaṃ dāpayitavya ity arthaḥ |

"daṇḍya" ity anuvṛttau viṣṇuḥ [5.33]: "vyaṅgatāyukte kṣepe kārṣāpaṇaśatam" |

manuḥ [8.275] |

> mātaraṃ pitaraṃ jāyāṃ bhrātaraṃ tanayaṃ gurum |  
> ākṣārayan śataṃ dāpyaḥ panthānaṃ vādadad guroḥ ||

**'ākṣārayan'** tiraskurvāṇaḥ |

"krośata" ity anuvṛttau śaṅkhalikhitau: "tathādhikṛtān viprān gurūṃś ca nirbhartsanaṃ muṇḍanaṃ tāḍanam, gomayānulepanaṃ kharārohaṇaṃ darpaharo daṇḍo vā" |

**[478]** 'daṇḍya' ity anuvṛttau viṣṇuḥ [5.28]: "gurūn ākṣārayan kārṣāpaṇaśatam" |

bṛhaspatiḥ [20.9] |

> kṣipan svasrādikaṃ dadyāt pañcāśat paṇikaṃ damam |

manu-nāradau [ma. 8.267; nā. 18.15] |

> śataṃ brāhmaṇam ākruśya kṣatriyo daṇḍam arhati |  
> vaiśyo 'dhyardhaśataṃ dve vā śūdras tu vadham arhati ||

'daṇḍa' iti śeṣe hārītaḥ: "adhovarṇānām uttamavarṇākrośākṣepābhibhave hy aṣṭau purāṇāḥ" |

śaṅkhalikhitau: "ākrośe brāhmaṇasya kṣatriyaḥ śataṃ daṇḍyaḥ | śatārdhaṃ vaiśyasya | pañcaviṃśtiṃ śūdrasya" |

manu-nāradau [ma. 8.268] |

> vipraḥ pañcāśataṃ daṇḍyaḥ kṣatriyasyābhiśaṃsane |  
> vaiśyasya vārdhapañcāśat śūdre dvādaśako damaḥ ||

**[479]** bṛhaspatiḥ [20.12–16] |

> vipre śatārdhaṃ daṇḍas tu kṣatriyasyābhiśaṃsane |  
> viśas tathārdhapañcāśat śūdrasyārdhatrayodaśa ||  
> sacchūdrasyāyam udito vinayo 'naparādhinaḥ |  
> guṇahīnasya pāruṣye brāhmaṇo nāparādhnuyāt ||  
> vaiśyas tu kṣatriyākrośe daṇḍanīyaḥ śataṃ bhavet |  
> tadardhaṃ kṣatriyo. vaiśyaṃ kṣipan vinayam arhati ||  
> śūdrākrośe kṣatriyasya pañcaviṃśatiko damaḥ |  
> vaiśyasya caitad dviguṇaṃ śāstravidbhir udāhṛtam ||  
> vaiśyam ākṣārayan śūdro dāpyaḥ syāt prathamaṃ damam |  
> kṣatriyaṃ madhyamaṃ caiva vipram uttamasāhasam ||

viṣṇuḥ [5.34]: "mātṛyukta tūttamasāhasam" |

**'mātṛyukte'** ākrośe **'uttamasāhasam'** daṇḍanīya ity arthaḥ |

"śūdrasya" ity anuvṛttau, bṛhaspatiḥ |

> dharmopadeśakartā ca vedodāharaṇānvitaḥ |  
> ākrośakas tu viprāṇāṃ jihvācchedena daṇḍyate ||

**[480]** gautamaḥ [12.1]: "śūdro dvijātīn abhisandhāyābhihatya ca vāgdaṇḍapāruṣyābhyām aṅgaṃ mocyo yenopahanyāt" |

**'abhisandhāya'** buddhipūrvaṃ vācātikramya | **'abhihatya'** tāḍayitvā buddhipūrvam ugreṇa daṇḍena tāḍayitvā | **'aṅgaṃ mocyo'** tenāṅgena viyojanīyaḥ |

āpastambaḥ [2.27.14]: "jihvācchedanaṃ śūdrasya āryaṃ dhārmikam ākrośataḥ" |

purāṇādhikāre 'adhamavarṇānām uttamavarṇasya' ity anuvartamāne, hārītaḥ: "anṛtābhiśaṃsane tadaṅgacchedaḥ pañcaśataṃ vā | ādyeṣu pādo na vā | svāmitvād ādivarṇatvāc cottamānām" |

**'ādyeṣu'** brāhmaṇādivarṇeṣu | **'pādo'** aṣṭau purāṇāḥ pūrvam uktās teṣāṃ caturtho bhāgaḥ | **'na vā'** pādo daṇḍa ity anvayaḥ |

manu-nāradau [ma. 8.270–72; nā. 18.22–24] |

> ekajātir dvijātīṃs tu vācā dāruṇayā kṣipan |  
> jihvāyāḥ prāpnuyāc chedaṃ jaghanyaprabhavo hi saḥ ||

**[481]** > nāmajātigrahaṃ tv eṣām abhidroheṇa kurvataḥ |  
> nikheyo 'yomayaḥ śaṅkur jvalann āsye daśāṅgulaḥ ||  
> dharmopadeśaṃ darpeṇa dvijānām asya kurvataḥ |  
> taptam āsecayet tailaṃ vaktre śrotre ca pārthivaḥ ||

"śūdra" ity anuvṛttau, gautamaḥ [12.4]: "atha [hā]sya vedam upaśṛṇvatas trapujatubhyāṃ śrotrapūraṇam udāharaṇe jihvācchedo dhāraṇe śarīrabhedaḥ" |

manuḥ [8.273] |

> śrutaṃ deśaṃ ca jātiṃ ca karma śārīram eva ca |  
> vitathena bruvan darpād dāpyaḥ syād dviśataṃ damam ||

viṣṇuḥ [5.26]: "śrutadeśajātikarmanām anyathāvādī kārṣāpaṇaśatadvayaṃ daṇḍyaḥ" |

nāradaḥ [18.19] |

> na kilbiṣeṇāpavadec chāstrataḥ kṛtapāvanam |  
> na rājño dhṛtadaṇḍaṃ ca daṇḍabhāk tadvyatikramāt ||

**[482]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.210] |

> patanīyakṛte kṣepe daṇḍo madhyamasāhasaḥ |  
> upapātakayukte tu. dāpyaḥ prathamasāhasam ||

manuḥ [8.276–77] |

> brāhmaṇakṣatriyābhyāṃ tu daṇḍaḥ kāryo vijānatā |  
> brāhmaṇe sāhasaḥ pūrvaḥ kṣatriye tv eva madhyamaḥ ||  
> viṭśūdrayos tv evam eva svajātiṃ prati tatvataḥ |  
> chedavarjapraṇayanaṃ daṇḍasyeti viniścayaḥ ||

vyāsaḥ |

> pāpopapāpavaktāro mahāpātakaśaṃsakaḥ |  
> ādyamadhyottamān daṇḍān daṇḍyās te te yathākramam ||

viṣṇuḥ [5.29–32]: "parasya patanīye kṣepe kṛte tūttamasāhasam | upapātakayukte madhyayam | traividyavṛddhānāṃ kṣepe jātipūgānāṃ ca | grāmadeśayoḥ prathamam" |

**[483]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.211] |

> traividyanṛpadevānāṃ kṣepa uttamasāhasaḥ |  
> madhyamo jātipūgānāṃ prathamo grāmadeśayoḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [10.17, 19] |

> deśādikaṃ kṣipan dāpyaḥ paṇān ardhatrayodaśa |  
> pāpena yojayan darpād dāpyaḥ prathamasāhasam ||  
> eṣa daṇḍaḥ samākhyātaḥ puruṣāpekṣayā mayā |  
> samanyūnādhikatvena kalpanīyo manīṣibhiḥ ||

nāradaḥ [18.30] |

> avakruśya ca rājānaṃ vartmani sve vyavasthitam |  
> jihvācchedād bhavec chuddhiḥ sarvasvaharaṇena vā ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.302] |

> rājño 'niṣṭapravaktāraṃ tasyaivākrośakaṃ tathā |  
> tanmantrasya ca bhettāraṃ chitvā jihvāṃ pravāsayet ||

nāradaḥ [18.20] |

> loke 'smin dvāv avaktavyāv avadhyau ca prakīrtitau |  
> brāhmaṇaś caiva rājā ca tau hīdaṃ bibhrato jagat ||

**[484]**  
> patitaṃ patitety uktvā cauraṃ caureti vā punaḥ |  
> vacanāt tulyadoṣaḥ syān mithyā dvirdoṣatāṃ vrajet ||

kātyāyanaḥ [776–778] |

> yatra syāt parihārārthaṃ patitas tena kīrtitaḥ |  
> vacanāt tatra na syāt tu doṣo yatra vibhāvayet ||  
> anyathā tulyadoṣaḥ syān mithyoktau tūttamo damaḥ |  
> mahatā tu prayatnena vāgduṣṭaṃ sādhayen naram ||  
> atathyaṃ śrāvitaṃ rājā prayatnena vicārayet |  
> anṛtākhyānaśīlānāṃ jihvācchedād viśodhanam ||

hārītaḥ: "mithyādūṣiṇāṃ melakānāṃ rājā jihvāṃ chindyāt | daṇḍayed vā sahasram | kaṇān bhakṣayed abdam" |

**'melako'** bhakṣakaḥ |

uśanā |

> yatra nokto damaḥ pūrvair ānantyāt tu mahātmabhiḥ |  
> tatra kāryaṃ parijñāya kartavyaṃ daṇḍadhāraṇam ||

**kalpatarau vyavahārakāṇḍe vākpāruṣyam**

**[485]**

## 69 daṇḍapāruṣyam
atha daṇḍapāruṣyam

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ [21.1] |

> hastapāṣāṇalaguḍair bhasmakardamapāṃsubhiḥ |  
> āyudhaiś ca praharaṇaṃ daṇḍapāruṣyam ucyate ||

vyāsaḥ |

> bhasmādīnāṃ prakṣepaṇaṃ tāḍanaṃ ca karādinā |  
> āveṣṭanaṃ cāṃśukādyair daṇḍapāruṣyam ucyate ||

nāradaḥ [18.4–6] |

> paragātreṣv abhidroho hastapādāyudhādibhiḥ |  
> bhasmādibhiś copaghāto daṇḍāpāruṣyam ucyate ||  
> tatrāpi dṛṣṭaṃ traividhyaṃ mṛdumadhyottamakramāt |  
> avagūraṇaniḥsaṅgapīḍanākṣatadarśanaiḥ ||  
> hīnamadhyottamānāṃ tu trayāṇāṃ samatikramāt |  
> trīṇy eva sādhanāny āhuḥ tatra kaṇṭakamocane ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [19.6–7] |

> bhasmādīnāṃ prakṣepaṇaṃ tāḍanaṃ ca karādinā |  
> prathamaṃ daṇḍapāruṣyaṃ damaḥ kāryo 'tra māṣakaḥ ||

**[486]**  
> eṣa daṇḍaḥ sameṣūktaḥ parastrīṣv adhikeṣu ca |  
> dviguṇas triguṇo jñeyaḥ prādhānyāpekṣayā budhaiḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.213–14] |

> bhasmapaṅkarajaḥsparśe daṇḍo daśapaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ |  
> amedhyapārṣṇiniṣṭhyūtasparśane dviguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
> sameṣv evaṃ parastrīṣu dviguṇas tūttameṣu ca |  
> hīneṣv ardhadamo mohamadādibhir adaṇḍanam ||

kātyāyanaḥ [784] |

> chardimūtrapurīṣādyair āpādyaḥ sa caturguṇaḥ |  
> ṣaḍguṇaḥ kāyamadhye tu mūrdhni tv aṣṭaguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.217] |

> pādakeśāṃśukakarolluñchaneṣu paṇān daśa |  
> pīḍākarṣāṃsukāveṣṭapādādhyāse śataṃ damaḥ ||

pīḍā cākarṣaś cāṃśukāveṣṭaś ca pādādhyāsaś ceti samāhāradvandvaḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati | aṃśukenāveṣṭya gāḍham āpīḍyākṛṣya yaḥ pādenādhyāste tasya paṇaśataṃ daṇḍaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [785] |

> udgūraṇe tu hastasya kāryo dvādaśako damaḥ |  
> sa eva dviguṇaḥ proktaḥ pātaneṣu sajātiṣu ||

**[487]** bṛhaspatiḥ [21.8] |

> udyate 'śmaśilākāṣṭhe kartavyaḥ prathamo damaḥ |  
> [parasparaṃ hastapāde pañcaviṃśatikas tathā || ]

'daṇḍya' ity anuvṛttau viṣṇuḥ [5.60–62, 64]: "hastenodgūrayitā daśakārṣāpaṇān | pādena viṃśatim | kāṣṭhena prathamasāhasam | śastreṇottamam" |

adhamo yadā śastreṇottamasyodgūraṇaṃ karoti tadāsāv uttamasāhasaṃ daṇḍya ity arthaḥ |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.216] |

> udgūrṇe hastapāde tu daśaviṃśatikau damau |  
> parasparasya sarveṣāṃ śastre madhyamasāhasam ||

etac ca samānajātīyānām avagantavyam | asamānajātīyānāṃ daṇḍāntaraśravaṇāt |

paṇānuvṛttau śaṅkhalikhitau: "prahārodyame ṣaṭpañcāśan nipātane taddviguṇam" |

**[488]** bṛhaspatiḥ [21.9–10] |

> madhyamaḥ śastrasaṃdhāne saṃyojyaḥ kruddhayor dvayoḥ |  
> kāryaḥ kṣatānurūpas tu lagne ghāte damo budhaiḥ ||  
> iṣṭakopalakāṣṭhais tu tāḍane tu dvimāṣakaḥ |  
> dviguṇaḥ śoṇitodbhede daṇḍaḥ kāryo manīṣibhiḥ ||

viṣṇuḥ [5.66, 67]: "[daṇḍyaḥ] śoṇitena vinā duḥkham utpādayitā dvātriṃśat paṇān | saha śoṇitena catuḥṣaṣṭim" |

manuḥ [8.284] |

> tvagbhedakaḥ śataṃ daṇḍyo lohitasya ca darśakaḥ |  
> māṃsabhettā tu ṣaṇṇiṣkān pravāsyas tv asthibhedakaḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [21.11–12] |

> tvagbhede prathamo daṇḍo māṃsabhede tu madhyamaḥ |  
> uttamaś cāsthibhede tu ghātane ca pramāpaṇam ||  
> karṇanāsākaracchede dantabhede 'ṅghribhedane |  
> kartavyo madhyamo daṇḍo dviguṇaḥ patiteṣu ca ||

kātyāyanaḥ [781] |

> karṇauṣṭhaghrāṇapādākṣijihvāśiśnakarasya ca |  
> chedane cottamo daṇḍo bhedane madhyamo bhṛguḥ ||

**[489]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.219–20] |

> karapādadantabhaṅge chedane karṇanasayoḥ |  
> madhyo daṇḍo vraṇodbhede mṛtakalpahate tathā ||  
> ceṣṭābhojanavāgrodhe netrādipratibhedane |  
> kandharābāhusakthnāṃ ca bhaṅge madhyamasāhasaḥ ||

daṇḍa ity anvartamāne viṣṇuḥ [5.70–72]: "netrakandharābāhusakthyaṃsabhaṅge cottamam | ubhayanetrabhedinaṃ rājā yāvajjīvaṃ bandhanān na muñcet | tādṛśam eva vā kuryāt |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.308] |

> dvinetrabhedano rājadviṣṭādeśakṛtas tathā |  
> vipratvena tu śūdrasya jīvato 'ṣṭaśato damaḥ ||

manuḥ [8.286] |

> manuṣyāṇāṃ paśūnāṃ ca duḥkhāya prahṛte sati |  
> yathā yathā mahadduḥkhaṃ daṇḍaṃ kuryāt tathā tathā ||

**[490]** hārītaḥ: "adhovarṇānām uttamavarṇākrośābhibhavākṣepeṣv aṣṭau purāṇāḥ | grīvābhañjanagalastanakacavaktragrahaṇeṣu triṃśat | romotpāṭanatarjanāvagūraṇeṣu triṣaṣṭiḥ | śikhākarṇāṅgabhaṅgacchedeṣu dviśatam | pādatāḍane 'nṛtābhiśaṃsane tadaṅgacchedaḥ | pañcaśataṃ vā | ādyeṣu pādonaṃ vā | svāmitvād ādyavarṇatvāc cottamavarṇānām īśānatamo brāhmaṇaḥ" |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.215] |

> viprapīḍākaraṃ chedyam aṅgam abrāhmaṇasya tu |  
> udgūrṇe prathamo daṇḍaḥ saṃsparśe tu tadardhikaḥ ||

**'saṃsparśe'** vadhodyamanārthaṃ śastrādisaṃsparśane |

nāradaḥ [18.25, 31] |

> yenāṅgenāvaro varṇo brāhmaṇasyāparādhnuyāt |  
> tadaṅgaṃ tasya chettavyam evaṃ śuddhim avāpnuyāt ||  
> rājani prahared yas tu kṛtāgasy api durmatiḥ |  
> śūlyaṃ tam agnau vipaced brahmahatyāsamātigam ||

**[491]** **'kṛtāgasi'** kṛtāparādhe | śūlam āropya yat saṃskriyate tat **'śūlyam'** |

manuḥ [8.279–80] |

> yena kenacid aṅgena hiṃsyāc chreyāṃsam antyajaḥ |  
> chettavyaṃ tat tad evāsya tan manor anuśāsanam ||  
> pāṇim udyamya daṇḍaṃ vā pāṇicchedanam arhati |  
> pādena praharet kopāt padacchedanam arhati ||

manu-nāradau [ma. 8.281–83] |

> sahāsanam abhiprepsur utkṛṣṭasyāpakṛṣṭajaḥ |  
> kaṭhyāṃ kṛtāṅko nirvāsyaḥ sphicaṃ vāsya prakartayet ||  
> avaniṣṭhīvato darpād dvāv oṣṭhau chedayen nṛpaḥ |  
> avamūtrayato meḍhram avaśardhayato gudam ||  
> keśeṣu gṛhṇato hastau chedayed avicārayan |  
> padayor dāḍhikāyāṃ ca grīvāyāṃ vṛṣaṇeṣu ca ||

**'sahāsanam abhiprepsuḥ'** ekāsanopaveśābhimataḥ | 'ekāsanopaveśī kaṭhyāṃ kṛtāṅko nirvāsyaḥ' iti viṣṇuvacanāt | **'dāḍhikā'** śmaśruḥ |

**[492]** gautamaḥ [12.5]: "āsanaśayanavākpathiṣu samaprepsur daṇḍyaḥ" |

śūdrasyety anuvartamāne āpastambaḥ [2.27.15]: "vāci pathi śayyāyām āsana iti samībhavato daṇḍatāḍanam" |

kātyāyanaḥ [786] |

> vākpāruṣye yathaivoktāḥ pratilomānulomataḥ |  
> tathaiva daṇḍapāruṣye pātyā daṇḍā yathākramam ||

viṣṇuḥ [5.73–74]: "evaṃ bahūnāṃ nighnatāṃ pratyekaśa ukto daṇḍo dviguṇaḥ | utkrośantam anabhidhāvatāṃ tatsamīpavartināṃ saṃsaratāṃ ca" |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.221] |

> ekaṃ ghnatāṃ bahūnāṃ tu yathokād dviguṇo damaḥ |  
> kalahāpahṛtaṃ deyaṃ daṇḍaṃ ca dviguṇaṃ tataḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [788] |

> vāgdaṇḍas tāḍanaṃ caiva yeṣūktam aparādiṣu |  
> hṛtabhagnaṃ pradāpyās te śodhyaṃ niḥsvais tu karmaṇā ||

karmakaraṇena **'śodhyaṃ'** taddhanaṃ paripūraṇīyam ity arthaḥ |

**[493]** bṛhaspatiḥ [21.15] |

> aṅgāvapīḍane caiva bhedane chedane tathā |  
> samutthānavyayaṃ dāpyaḥ kalahāya kṛtaṃ ca yat ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.222] |

> duḥkham utpādayed yas tu sasamutthānajaṃ vyayam |  
> dāpyo daṇḍaṃ ca yo yasmin kalahe samudīritaḥ ||

manuḥ [8.287] |

> aṅgāvapīḍanāyāṃ ca prāṇaśōṇitayos tathā |  
> samutthānavyayaṃ dāpyaḥ sarvadaṇḍam athāpi vā ||

'aṅgāvapīḍanāyāṃ' aṅgānāṃ karacaraṇādīnāṃ pīḍanāyām | 'prāṇaśoṇitayoś' ca pīḍanāyāṃ satyām | 'samutthānavyayaṃ' yāvatkālena samutthānasamartho bhavati tāvatkālena pathyauṣadhyādinā yāvad dhanavyayo bhavati tam asau dāpayitavyaḥ | atha tasya yady asau na vyayaṃ dātum icchati tadā yaḥ samutthānavyayo yaś ca daṇḍaḥ, tat sarvaṃ daṇḍatvena dāpya ity arthaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [787] |

> dehendriyavināśe tu yathā daṇḍaṃ prakalpayet |  
> tathā tuṣṭikaraṃ deyaṃ samutthānaṃ ca paṇḍitaiḥ ||  
> samutthānavyayaṃ cāsau dadyād ā vraṇaropaṇam ||

**[494]** viṣṇuḥ [5.75–76]: "sarve ca puruṣapīḍākarās tadutthānavyayaṃ dadyuḥ | grāmyapaśupīḍākarāś ca" |

manuḥ [8.299–300] |

> bhāryā putraś ca dāsaś ca śiṣyo bhrātā ca sodaraḥ |  
> prāptāparādhās tāḍyās syū rajvā veṇudalena vā ||  
> pṛṣṭhatas tu śarīrasya nottamāṅge kathaṃcana |  
> ato 'nyathā tu praharan prāptaḥ syāc caurakilbiṣam ||

yamaḥ |

> bhāryā putraś ca dāsaś ca dāsī śiṣyaś ca pañcamaḥ |  
> prāptāparādhās tāḍyās tu rajvā veṇudalena vā ||  
> adhastāt tu prahartavyaṃ nottamāṅga kathaṃcana |  
> ato'nyathā pravṛttas tu yathoktaṃ daṇḍam arhati ||

brahmacārīty anuvṛttau nāradaḥ [8.13–14] |

> anuśāsyaḥ sa guruṇā na ced anuvidhīyate |  
> avadhenātha vā tanvā rajvā veṇudalena vā ||  
> bhṛśaṃ na tāḍayed enaṃ nottamāṅge na vakṣasi |  
> anuśāsya ca viśvāsyaḥ śasyo rājñānyathā guruḥ ||

**'avadhena'** atāḍanena |

**[495]** gautamaḥ [2.49–51]: "śiṣyaśiṣṭir avadhena | aśaktau rajjuveṇuvidalābhyāṃ tanubhyām | anyena ghnan rājñā śāsyaḥ" |

śiṣyānuvṛttau āpastambaḥ [1.8.29]: "aparādheṣu cainaṃ satatam upālabheta | abhitrāsa upavāsa udakopasparśanm adarśanam iti daṇḍā yathāmātram ā nivṛtteḥ" iti |

aparādhānurūpaṃ daṇḍapātanaṃ kartavyam aparādhanivṛttiparyantam ity arthaḥ |

nāradaḥ [18.32] |

> putrāparādhe na pitā nāśve na śuni daṇḍabhāk |  
> na markaṭe ca tatsvāmī tenaiva prahitā na cet ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.300] |

> śakto hy amokṣayan svāmī daṃṣṭriṇāṃ śṛṅgiṇāṃ tathā |  
> prathamaṃ sāhasaṃ dadyād vikruṣṭe dviguṇaṃ tathā ||

**'vikruṣṭe'** svakīyaṃ śṛṅginam apasārayety asakṛ ākrośe kṛte |

bṛhaspatiḥ [21.16–17] |

> vivikte tāḍito yas tu hato 'dṛśyena vā bhavet |  
> hantā tad ānumānena vijñeyaḥ śapathena vā ||  
> antarveśmany araṇye vā niśāyāṃ yatra tāḍitaḥ |  
> śoṇitaṃ yatra dṛśyeta na pṛcchet tatra sākṣiṇaḥ ||

**'adṛśyena'** adṛśyamānena ghatakena |

**[496]** nārada-bṛhaspatī [nā. 4.176; bṛ. 21.18] |

> kaścit kṛtvātmanaś cihnaṃ dveṣāt param abhidravet |  
> hetvarthagatisāmarthyais tatra yuktaṃ parīkṣaṇam ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.212] |

> asākṣikahate cihnair yuktibhiś cāgamena vā |  
> draṣṭavyo vyavahāras tu kūṭacihnakṛtād bhayāt ||

kātyāyanaḥ [779] |

> hetvādibhir na paśyec ced daṇḍapāruṣyakāraṇam |  
> tad asākṣikṛtaṃ tatra divyaṃ vātha niyojayet ||

atha vāgdaṇḍapāruṣyādhikāre —

nāradaḥ |

> vidhiḥ pañcavidhas tūkta etayor ubhayor api |  
> viśuddhir daṇḍabhāktvaṃ ca tatra saṃbadhyate yathā ||  
> pāruṣye sati saṃrambhād utpanne kṣubdhayor dvayoḥ |  
> sa mānyate yaḥ kṣamate daṇḍabhāg yo 'tivartate ||

**[497]** > pāruṣyadoṣāvṛtayor yugapatsaṃpravṛttayoḥ |  
> viśeṣaś cen na dṛśyeta vinayaḥ syāt samastayoḥ ||  
> dvayor āpannayos tulyam anubadhnāti yaḥ punaḥ |  
> sa tayor daṇḍam āpnoti pūrvo vā yadi vottaraḥ ||  
> pūrvam ākṣārayed yas tu niyataṃ syāt sa doṣabhāk |  
> paścād yaḥ so 'py asatkārī pūrve tu vinayo guruḥ ||

**'āpannayos tulyam'** iti pāruṣye tulyavṛttayor ity arthaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [780] |

> ābhīṣaṇena daṇḍena prahared yas tu mānavaḥ |  
> pūrvaṃ vā pīḍito vātha sa daṇḍyaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [21.19, 5] |

> ākruṣṭas tu samākrośaṃs tāḍitaḥ pratitāḍayan |  
> hatvātatāyinaṃ caiva nāparādhī bhaven naraḥ ||  
> vākpāruṣyādinā nīco yaḥ santam abhilaṅghayet |  
> sa eva tāḍayaṃs tasya nānveṣṭavyo mahībhujā ||

**[498]** **'sa eva'** uttama eva | **'tāḍayaṃs tasya'** tasya nīcasya tāḍanaṃ kurvan nṛpeṇa daṇḍe **'nānveṣtavyaḥ'** ity arthaḥ |

nāradaḥ [18.11–14] |

> śvapākapaśucāṇḍālaveśyāsu bakavṛttiṣu |  
> hastipavrātyadāseṣu gurvācāryātigeṣu ca ||  
> maryādātikrame sadyoghāta evānuśāsanam |  
> na ca tad daṇḍapāruṣye doṣam āhur manīṣiṇaḥ ||  
> yam eva hy ativarterann ete santaṃ janaṃ nṛṣu |  
> sa eva vinayaṃ kuryān na tadvinayabhāṅ nṛpaḥ ||  
> malā hy ete manuṣyāṇāṃ dhanam eṣāṃ malātmakam |  
> api tān ghātayed rājā nārthadaṇḍena daṇḍayet ||

'sadyoghātaḥ' sadyastāḍanam |

**[499]** bṛhaspatiḥ [21.20] |

> pratilomās tathā cāntyāḥ puruṣāṇāṃ malāḥ smṛtāḥ |  
> brāhmaṇātikrame vadhyā na dātavyā damaṃ kvacit ||

kātyāyanaḥ [783] |

> aspṛśyadhūrtadāsānāṃ mlecchānāṃ pāpakāriṇām |  
> prātilomyaprasūtānāṃ tāḍanaṃ nārthato damaḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.225–26] |

> duḥkhite śoṇitotpāde śākhāṅgacchedane tathā |  
> daṇḍaḥ kṣudrapaśūnāṃ tu dvipaṇād dviguṇaḥ kramāt ||  
> liṅgasya chedane mṛtyau madhayamo mūlyam eva ca |  
> mahāpaśūnām eteṣu sthāneṣu dviguṇo damaḥ ||

**'śākhā'** atra śṛṅgādikā | **'aṅgam'** caraṇādi | **'dviguṇaḥ'** paṇadvayād ārabhya yathākramaṃ dviguṇo daṇḍa ity arthaḥ |

'kārṣāpaṇaśataṃ daṇḍa' ity anuvṛttau viṣṇuḥ [5.119]: "paśūnāṃ puṃstvopaghātakārī" |

punar viṣṇuḥ [5.48–54]: "gajāśvoṣṭragoghātī hy ekakarapādaḥ kāryaḥ | vimāṃsavikrayī ca | grāmyapaśughātī ca kārṣāpaṇaśataṃ daṇḍyaḥ | paśusvāmine ca tanmūlyaṃ dadyāt | **[500]** āraṇyapaśughātī pañcāśat kārṣāpaṇān | pakṣighātī matsyaghātī ca daśakārṣāpaṇān | kīṭopaghātī kārṣāpaṇam" |

**'vimāṃsam'** śvasṛgālādimāṃsam |

kātyāyanaḥ [790] |

> tripaṇo dvādaśapaṇo vadhe tu mṛgapakṣiṇām |  
> sarpamārjāranakulaśvasūkaravadhe nṛṇām ||

manuḥ |

> gokumārīdevapaśūn ukṣāṇaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ tathā |  
> vāhayan sāhasaṃ pūrvaṃ prāpnuyād uttamaṃ vadhe ||

śvavṛṣādhikāre bṛhaspatiḥ [21.21] |

> śrāntān kṣudhārtāṃs tṛṣitān akāle vāhayeta yaḥ |  
> sa goghno niṣkṛtiṃ kāryo dāpyo vā prathamaṃ damam ||

kātyāyanaḥ [789] |

> śrāntāṃs tṛṣārtān kṣidhitān akāle vāhayen naraḥ |  
> kharagomahiṣoṣṭrādīn prāpnuyāt pūrvasāhasam ||

**[501]** manuḥ [8.290–92] |

> yānasya caiva yantuś ca yānasvāmini eva ca |  
> daśātivartanāny āhuḥ śeṣe daṇḍo vidhīyate ||  
> chinnanāsye bhinnayuge tiryakpratimukhāgate |  
> akṣabhaṅge ca yānasya cakrabhaṅge tathaiva ca ||  
> chedane caiva yantrāṇāṃ yoktraraśmyos tathaiva ca |  
> ākrande cāpy apaihīti na daṇḍaṃ manur abravīt ||

**'yantuḥ'** sāratheḥ | **'ativartanāni'** chinnanāsādīni, daṇḍam atikramya vartata ity vyutpatyā |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.298] |

> catuṣpādakṛte doṣo nāpaihīti prabhāṣataḥ |  
> kāṣṭhaloṣṭeṣṭapāṣāṇabāhuyugyakṛtas tathā ||

kāṣṭhaloṣṭapāṣāṇabāhubhir abhyāsakāraṇe yaḥ paropaghātād daṇḍārhatālakṣaṇo doṣa āpadyate 'sau prathamata evāpaihīti bhāṣamāṇasya na bhavatīty ārthaḥ |

**[502]** tathā [2.299] |

> chinnanāsyena yānena tathā bhagnayugādinā |  
> paścāc caivāpasaratāṃ hiṃsane svāmy adoṣabhāk ||

manuḥ [8.293–98] |

> yatrāpavartate yugyaṃ vaiguṇyāt prājakasya tu |  
> tatra svāmī bhaved daṇḍyo hiṃsāyāṃ dviśato damaḥ ||  
> prājakaś ca bhaved āptaḥ prājako daṇḍam arhati |  
> yugyasthāḥ prājake 'nāpte sarve daṇḍyāḥ śataṃ śatam ||  
> sa cet tu pathi saṃruddhaḥ paśubhir vā rathena vā |  
> pramāpayet prāṇabhṛtas tasya daṇḍo 'vicārataḥ ||  
> manuṣyamāraṇe kṣipraṃ cauravat kilbiṣaṃ bhavet |  
> prāṇabhṛtsu mahatsv ardhaṃ gogajoṣṭrahayādiṣu ||  
> kṣudrakāṇāṃ paśūnāṃ ca hiṃsāyāṃ dviśato damaḥ |  
> pañcāśat tu bhaved daṇḍaḥ śubheṣu mṛgapakṣiṣu ||  
> gardabhājāvikānāṃ tu daṇḍaḥ syāt pañcamāṣakaḥ |  
> māṣakas tu bhaved daṇḍaḥ śvasūkaranipātane ||

**[503]** 'prājakaḥ' prerakaḥ sārathyādiḥ | 'āpto' atra kuśalaḥ | 'sa cet tu' iti sa ca prājakaḥ | pathi paśvādibhir avaruddho 'pi rathapreraṇena tān pramāpayati tadā tasyāvicārato daṇḍa ity arthaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [792] |

> pramāpaṇe prāṇabhṛtāṃ pratirūpaṃ tu dāpayet |  
> tasyānurūpamūlyaṃ vā dāpya ity abravīn manuḥ ||

manuḥ [8.285] |

> vanaspatīnāṃ sarveṣām upabhogo yathā yathā |  
> tathā tathā damaḥ kāryo hiṃsāyām iti dhāraṇā ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.227–29] |

> prarohiśākhināṃ śākhāskandhaparvavidāraṇe |  
> upajīvyadrumāṇāṃ tu viṃśater dviguṇā damāḥ ||  
> caityaśmaśānasīmāsu puṇyasthāne surālaye |  
> jātadrumāṇāṃ dviguṇo damo vṛkṣo 'tha viśrute ||  
> gulamgucchakṣupalatāpratānauṣadhivīrudhām |  
> pūrvasmṛtād ardhadaṇḍaḥ sthāneṣūkteṣu kṛntane ||

'prarohiśākhinām'' vaṭādīnām | 'skandhaḥ' yataḥ śākhāḥ prabhavanti | 'upajīvyadrumāṇām' āmrādīnām | 'viṃśater dviguṇā damāḥ' śākhācchedane skandhacchedane samūlacchedane ca yathākramaṃ viṃśatipaṇād daṇḍād ārabhya pūrvasmād uttarottaro dviguṇo dama ity ārthaḥ | 'gumāḥ' mālatyādayaḥ | 'gucchāḥ' avallīrūpāḥ **[504]** kuraṇṭakādayaḥ | 'kṣupāḥ' karavīrādayaḥ | 'latāḥ' drākṣāprabhṛtayaḥ | 'pratānāḥ' kāṇḍapraroharahitāḥ saralayāyinyāḥ sārivādayaḥ | 'oṣadhayaḥ' phalapākāvasānāḥ śālyādayaḥ | 'vīrudhaḥ' chinnā api yā vividhaṃ prarohanti guḍūcyādayaḥ |

'daṇḍa' ity anuvṛttau viṣṇuḥ [5.65–59]: "phalopagadrumacchedī tūttamasāhasam | puṣpopagamadrumacchedī madhyamam | vallīgulmalatācchedī kārṣāpaṇam | tṛṇacchedy ekam | sarve ca tatsvāmināṃ tadutpattim" | dadyur iti śeṣaḥ |

vasiṣṭhaḥ [19.11–13]: "phalapuṣpopagān pādapān na hiṃsyāt | karṣaṇakaraṇārthaṃ copahanyāt | gārhasthyāṃśe ca" |

**iti daṇḍapāruṣyam |**

**[505]**

## 70 steyam
atha steyam

tatra manuḥ [8.301–02] |

> eṣo 'khilenābhihito daṇḍapāruṣyanirṇayaḥ |  
> steyasyātha pravakṣyāmi vidhiṃ daṇḍavinirṇaye ||  
> syāt sāhasaṃ tv anvayavat prasabhaṃ karma yat kṛtam |  
> niranvayaṃ bhavet steyaṃ kṛtvāpavyayate ca yat ||

'anvayavat' rakṣakapuruṣasamakṣam | 'prasabham' balātkāreṇa sānvayaṃ karaṇam ity arthaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [796] |

> sānvayas tv apahāro yaḥ prasahya karaṇaṃ ca yat |  
> sāhasaṃ ca bhaved evaṃ steyam uktaṃ vinihnavaḥ ||

sāhasāntaraṃ nāradaḥ |

> tasyaiva bhedaḥ syāt steyaṃ viśeṣas tatra tūcyate |

**[506]** > ādhiḥ sāhasam ākramya steyam ādhiś chalena ca ||  
> tad api trividhaṃ proktaṃ dravyāpekṣaṃ manīṣibhiḥ |  
> kṣudramadhyottamānāṃ tu dravyāṇām apakarṣaṇāt ||  
> mṛdbhāṇḍāsanakhaṭvāsthidārucarmatṛṇādi yat |  
> śamīdhānyaṃ kṛtānnaṃ na kṣudraṃ dravyam udāhṛtam ||  
> vāsaḥ kauśeyavarjaṃ ca govarjaṃ paśavas tathā |  
> hiraṇyavarjaṃ lohaṃ ca madyaṃ vrīhiyavā api ||  
> hiraṇyaratnakauśeyaṃ strīpuṃso gajavājinaḥ |  
> devabrāhmaṇarājñāṃ ca vijñeyaṃ dravyam uttamam ||  
> upāyair vividhair eṣāṃ chalayitvāpakarṣaṇam |  
> suptamattapramatteṣu steyam āhur manīṣiṇaḥ ||

**[507]** **'ādhiḥ'** pīḍā, sā yatrātikramya kriyate tat **'sāhasam'** | chelena tv ādhikaraṇe cauryam |

**iti steyam**

**70 — (ka) atha stenāḥ**

tatra manuḥ [9.256] |

> dvividhāṃs taskarān vidyāt paradravyāpahāriṇaḥ |  
> prakāśāṃś cāprakāśāṃś ca cāracakṣur mahīpatiḥ ||

vyāsaḥ |

> prakāśāś cāprakāśāś ca taskarā dvividhāḥ smṛtāḥ |  
> sucihnair eva vijñeyāś cārais taskaravedibhiḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [22.1–3] |

> prakāśāś cāprakāśāś ca taskarā dvividhā smṛtāḥ |  
> prajñāsāmarthyamāyābhiḥ prabhinnās te sahasradhā ||  
> naigamā vaidyakitavāḥ sadyotkocakavañcakāḥ |  
> daivotpādavido bhadrāḥ śilpajñāḥ pratirūpakāḥ ||

**[508]** > akriyākāriṇaś caiva madhyasthāḥ kūṭasākṣiṇaḥ |  
> prakāśataskarā hy ete tathā kuhakajīvinaḥ ||

nāradaḥ [21.2–3] |

> prakāśavañcakās tatra kūṭamānatulāśritāḥ |  
> utkocakāḥ sopadhikāḥ vañcakāḥ paṇyayoṣitaḥ ||  
> partirūpakarāś caiva maṅgalādeśavṛttayaḥ |  
> ity evamādayo jñeyāḥ prakāśās taskarā bhuvi ||

vyāsaḥ |

> prakāśāpaṇasaṃsthāś ca nānāpaṇyopajīvinaḥ |  
> prakāśavañcakā jñeyā bhiṣakprabhṛtayo 'pare ||

**'āpaṇaḥ'** paṇyajīvī |

manuḥ [9.258–60] |

> utkocakāḥ sopadhikāḥ kitavā vañcakās tathā |  
> maṅgalādeśavṛttāś ca bhadrāś cekṣaṇikaiḥ saha ||  
> asabhyakāriṇaś caiva mahāmātrāś cikitsakāḥ |  
> śilpopacārayuktāś ca nipuṇāḥ paṇyayoṣitaḥ ||

**[509]** > evamādīn vijānīyāt prakāśāṃl lokakaṇṭakān |  
> nigūḍhacāriṇaś cānyān anāryān āryaliṅginaḥ ||

tathā [9.257] |

> pracchannavañcakā jñeyā ye stenaāṭavikādayaḥ |

nāradaḥ [nā. m. saṃhi. prakīrṇaka, 56] |

> aprakāśās tu vijñeyā bahirabhyantarāśritāḥ |  
> suptamattapramattāṃś ca muṣṇanty ākramya ye narāḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [22.4] |

> sandhicchidaḥ pānthamuṣo dvicatuṣpadahāriṇaḥ |  
> utkṣepakāḥ sasyaharā jñeyāḥ pracchannataskarāḥ ||

vyāsaḥ |

> sādhanāṅgānvitā rātrau vicaranty avibhāvitāḥ |  
> avijñātaviśeṣāś ca jñeyāḥ pracchannavañcakāḥ ||

**[510]** > utkṣepakaḥ sandhibhettā pānthamuṭ granthibhedakaḥ |  
> strīpuṃgo'śvapuśusteyī cauro navavidhaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

**'sādhanāṅgānvitāḥ'** steyasādhanakhanitraśastrādiyuktāḥ | **'avijñātaviśeṣāḥ'** avijñātapraveśāḥ | **'utkṣepakaḥ'** iti, agrata eva anavahitasya dṛṣṭivañcanenotkṣepe yo apaharaty asau ucyate |

caurānantaraṃ nāradaḥ |

> tān viditvā tu kuśalaiś cārais tatkarmavedibhiḥ |  
> anusṛtya tu gṛhṇīyād gūḍhapraṇihitair naraiḥ ||

caurānantaraṃ manuḥ [9.261–62] |

> tān viditvā tu caritair gūḍhais tatkarmavedibhiḥ |  
> cāraiś cānekasaṃsthānaiḥ protsāhya vaśam ānayet ||  
> teṣāṃ doṣam abhikhyāpya sve sve karmaṇi tatvataḥ |  
> kurvīta śāsanaṃ rājā samyak sārāparādhataḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [22.5] |

> saṃsargacihnaloptraiś ca vijñātā rājapūruṣaiḥ |  
> pradāpyāpahṛtaṃ śāsyā damaiḥ śāstrapracoditaiḥ ||

**[511]** manuḥ |

> na hi daṇḍād ṛte śakyaḥ kartuṃ nyāyavinigrahaḥ |  
> stenānāṃ pāpabuddhīnāṃ nibhṛtaṃ caratāṃ kṣitau ||  
> paramaṃ yatnam ātiṣṭhet stenānāṃ nigrahe nṛpaḥ |  
> stenānāṃ nigrāhād asya yaśo rāṣṭraṃ vivardhate ||  
> abhayasya hi yo dātā sa pūjyaḥ satataṃ nṛpaḥ |  
> satraṃ hi vardhate tasya sadaivābhayadakṣiṇam ||  
> nibhayaṃ vā bhaved yasya rāṣṭraṃ bāhubalāśritam |  
> tasya tad vardhate nityaṃ sicyamāna iva drumaḥ ||

āpastambaḥ [2.25.15]: "kṣemakṛd rājā yasya viṣaye grāme 'raṇye vā taskarabhayaṃ na vidyate" |

manuḥ [7.143] |

> vikrośantyo yasya rāṣṭrād dhriyante dasyubhiḥ prajāḥ |  
> saṃpaśyataḥ sabhṛtyaś ca mṛtaḥ sa ca na jīvati ||

**[512]** [tathā] |

> aśāsaṃs taskarān yas tu baliṃ gṛhṇāti pārthivaḥ |  
> tasya prakṣubhyate rāṣṭraṃ svargāc ca parihīyate ||

hārītaḥ |

> pāpās tu yasya rāṣṭrād vai vardhante dasyavaḥ sadā |  
> tat pāpam ativṛddhaṃ hi rājño mūlaṃ nikṛntati ||

**[iti kṛtyakalpatarau vyavahārakāṇḍe vivādaprakaraṇe stenākhyaṃ parva]**

**70 — (kha) atha prakāśataskaradaṇḍāḥ**

tatra vyāsaḥ |

> tulāmānaviśeṣeṇa lekhyena gaṇanena ca |  
> ardhasya vṛddhihrāsena muṣṇanti vaṇijo narān ||  
> taddravyasadṛśair anyair hīnamūlyair vimiśraṇam |  
> kurvanty aupādhikāś cānye paṇyānāṃ parivartane ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.244] |

> mānena tulayā vāpi yo yo 'ṃśam aṣṭamaṃ haret |  
> daṇḍaṃ sa dāpyo dviśataṃ vṛddhau hānau ca kalpitam ||

**[513]** apahṛtadravyasya **'vṛddhau hānau ca'** daṇḍasyāpi vṛddhihānī kalpya ity arthaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [812] |

> tulāmānapratīmānapratirūpakalakṣitaiḥ |  
> carann alakṣitair vāpi prāpnuyāt pūrvasāhasam ||

manuḥ [9.287, 291] |

> samair hi viṣamaṃ yas tu cared vai mūlyato 'pi vā |  
> sa prāpnuyād damaṃ pūrvaṃ naro madhyamam eva vā ||  
> abījavikrayī yaś ca bījotkraṣṭā tathaiva ca |  
> maryādābhedakaś caiva vikṛtaṃ prāpnuyād vadham ||

**'samair viṣamam'** ityādi — **'samaiḥ'** samamūlyadātṛbhiḥ saha utkṛṣṭāpakṛṣṭaviṣamadravyadānena yo vyavaharaty asau pūrvasāhasaṃ prāpnoti | same ca dravye bahvalpaṃ ca mūlyam ādadāno madhyamasāhasam ity arthaḥ | **'abījavikrayī'** abījaṃ bījatvena yo vikrīṇāti | **'bījotkraṣṭā'** uptaṃ bījam utkhananena yo gṛhṇāti |

**[514]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.245] |

> bheṣaja-sneha-lavaṇa-gandha-dhānya-guḍādiṣu |  
> paṇyeṣu hīnaṃ kṣipataḥ paṇā daṇḍas trayodaśa ||

nārado manuś ca dvitīye |

> śulkasthānaṃ vaṇik prāptaḥ śulkaṃ dadyād yathocitam |  
> na tad vyabhicared rājñāṃ balir eṣa prakīrtitaḥ ||  
> śulkasthānaṃ pariharann akāle krayavikrayau |  
> mithyāvācī ca saṃsthāne dāpyo 'ṣṭaguṇam atyayam ||

**'aṣṭaguṇam atyayam'** apahṛtadravyāpekṣayāṣṭaguṇaṃ daṇḍaṃ dāpya ity arthaḥ |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.262] |

> mithyā vadan parīmāṇaṃ śulkasthānād apākraman |  
> dāpyas tv aṣṭaguṇaṃ yaś ca sa vyājakrayavikrayī ||

**[515]** viṣṇuḥ [3.31] |

> śulkasthānād apākrāman sarvāpahāram āpnuyāt |

śaṅkhalikhitau: "kūṭatulāmānapratimānavyavahāre śārīro 'ṅgacchedo vā" |

**'śārīraḥ'** atra muṇḍanādidaṇḍaḥ |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.240–41] |

> tulāśāsanamānānāṃ kūṭakṛn nāṇakasya ca |  
> ebhiś ca vyavahartā yaḥ sa dāpyo damam uttamam ||  
> akūṭaṃ kūṭaṃ brūte kūṭaṃ yaś cāpy akūṭakam |  
> sa nāṇakaparīkṣī tu dāpya uttamasāhasam ||

"daṇḍasāhasam" ity anuvṛttau viṣṇuḥ [5.122–26]: "tulānāṇakakūṭakartuś ca | tadakūṭakūṭavādinaś ca | dravyāṇāṃ pratirūpavikrayakasya ca | sambhūya vaṇijāṃ paṇyam argheṇoparundhatā | pratyekasya vikrīṇatāṃ ca" |

**[516]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.249–50] |

> saṃbhūya kurvatām arghaṃ sabādhaṃ kāruśilpinām |  
> arghasya hāniṃ vṛddhiṃ ca sāhasro daṇḍa ucyate ||  
> saṃbhūya vaṇijāṃ paṇyam anargheṇoparundhatām |  
> vaikrīṇatāṃ ca vihito daṇḍa uttamasāhasaḥ ||

**'sabādham'** pīḍākaram | **'arghasya'** rājakṛtasya | **'nargheṇoparundhatām'** deśāntarād āgataṃ paṇyam ucitamūlyaprārthanenoparundhatām | **'vikrīṇatām'** anargheṇty anvayaḥ |

manuḥ [8.399] |

> rājñaḥ prakhyātabhāṇḍāni pratiṣiddhāni yāni ca |  
> tāni nirharato lobhāt sarvahāraṃ haren nṛpaḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.261] |

> vyāsiddhaṃ rājayogyaṃ yad vikrītaṃ rājagāmi tat |

'śārīro 'ṅgacchedo vā daṇḍaḥ' ity anuvṛttau, śaṅkhalikhitau: "pratiṣiddhabhāṇḍanirhāre" |

manuḥ [8.401–03] |

> āgamaṃ nirgamaṃ sthānaṃ tathā vṛddhikṣayāv ubhau |  
> vicārya sarvapaṇyānāṃ kārayan krayavikrayau ||

**[517]** > pañcarātre pañcarātre pakṣe pakṣe 'tha vā gatau |  
> kurvīta caiṣāṃ pratyakṣam arghasaṃsthāpanaṃ nṛpaḥ ||  
> tulāmānaṃ pratīmānaṃ sarvaṃ tat syāt surakṣitam |  
> ṣaṭsu ṣaṭsu ca māseṣu punar eva parīkṣayet ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: "tulāmānapratīmānavyavahārārghasaṃsthāpanaṃ deśadravyānurūpaṃ pratyayitapuruṣādhiṣṭhitam" |

rājñātra kartavyam iti śeṣaḥ |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.253, 251, 252] |

> paṇyasyopari saṃsthāpya vyayaṃ paṇyasamudbhavam |  
> argho 'nugrahakṛt kāryaḥ kretur vikretur eva ca ||  
> rājani sthāpyate yo 'rghaḥ pratyahaṃ tena vikrayaḥ |  
> krayo vā niḥsravas tasmād vaṇijo lābhakṛt smṛtaḥ ||  
> svadeśapaṇye tu śataṃ vaṇig gṛhṇīta pañcakam |  
> daśakaṃ pāradeśye tu yaḥ sadyaḥ krayavikrayī ||

**'niḥsravaḥ'** paṇyavikrayeṇa yad utpannam ā mūladhanād adhikaṃ dhanam |

'rājñaḥ' ity anuvṛttau gautamaḥ [10.34]: "paṇyaṃ vaṇigbhir arghāpacayena deyam" |

**[518]** vasiṣṭhaḥ [19.14–16]: "adhiṣṭhānān nirhāraḥ sārthānām | arghamānamūlyamātraṃ nairhārikaṃ syāt | mahāmahayos tv anatyayaḥ syāt | abhayaṃ ca" |

viṣṇuḥ [3.29–30]: "svadeśapaṇyāt śulkāṃśaṃ daśamam| paradeśapaṇyāc ca viṃśatitamam" |

**'śulkāṃśaṃ daśamam'** daśamam aṃśaṃ gṛhṇīyād ity arthaḥ |

manuḥ [8.398] |

> śulkasthāneṣu kuśalāḥ sarvapaṇyaviśāradāḥ |  
> kuryur arghaṃ yathāpaṇyaṃ tato viṃśaṃ nṛpo haret ||

'rājña' ity anuvṛttau gautamaḥ [10.2–27]: "viṃśatibhāgaḥ śulkaḥ paṇye | mūlaphalapuṣpauṣadhamadhumāṃsatṛṇendhanānāṃ ṣāṣṭaḥ | tadrakṣaṇadharmitvā | teṣu ca nityayuktaḥ syāt" |

**'ṣāṣṭaḥ'** ṣaṣṭitamo bhāgaḥ |

**[519]** baudhāyanaḥ [1.18, 13–15]: "sāmudraś śulkaḥ | varaṃ rūpam uddhṛtya daśapaṇaṃ śatam | anyeṣām api sārānurūpeṇānupahatya dharmaṃ prakalpayet" |

**'sāmudraḥ'** samudrasambandhī | **'varaṃ rūpam uddhṛtya daśapaṇaṃ śatam'** iti, muktāphalādiṣu madhye ekaṃ vastu pṛthakkṛtvānyatra vastuni daśamāṃśaṃ śulkaṃ gṛhṇīyād ity arthaḥ |

vasiṣṭhaḥ [19.37]: "śulke cāpi mānavaṃ ślokam udāharanti —

> na bhinnakārṣāpaṇam asti śulkaṃ na śilpavṛttau na śiśau na dūte |  
> na bhaikṣyalabdhe na kṛtāvaśeṣe na śrotriye pravrajite na yajñe || iti"

**'na bhinnakārṣāpaṇam asti śulkam'** iti —bhinno nyūnaḥ kārṣāpaṇo mūlyaṃ yasya vastunas tat tathā | tannirmitaḥ śulko 'pi **'bhinnakārṣāpaṇaḥ'** | tena kārṣāpaṇād arvāg yas mūlyaṃ tatra śulko na grāhya ity arthaḥ |

**[520]** bṛhaspatiḥ [22.10] |

> ajñātauṣadhimantras tu yasya vyadher atattvavit |  
> rogibhyo 'rthaṃ samādatte sa daṇḍyaś cauravad bhiṣak ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.242] |

> bhiṣaṅ mithyācaran dāpyas tiryakṣu prathamaṃ damam |  
> mānuṣe madhyamaṃ rājamānuṣeṣūttamaṃ tathā ||

viṣṇuḥ [5.175–77]: "uttamasāhasaṃ daṇḍanīyo bhiṣaṅ mithyācarann uttameṣu puruṣeṣu | madhyamaṃ madhyameṣu | tiryakṣu prathamam" |

vyāsaḥ |

> kūṭākṣadevinaḥ pāpān nirhared dyūtamaṇḍalāt |  
> kaṇṭhe 'kṣamālām āsajya sa hy eṣāṃ vinayaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [22.11] |

> glahaḥ prakāśaḥ kartavyo nirvāsyāḥ kūṭadevinaḥ |

**'glahaḥ'** dyūte ya pātaḥ kriyate |

**[521]** tathā [22.12] |

> kūṭākṣadevinaḥ kṣudrā rājabhāgaharāś ca ye |  
> gaṇānāṃ vañcakāś caiva daṇḍyās te kitavāḥ smṛtāḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.202] |

> rājñā sacihnaṃ nirvāsyāḥ kūṭākṣopadhidevinaḥ |

viṣṇuḥ [5.134–35]: "dyūte ca kūṭākṣadevināṃ karacchedaḥ | upadhidevināṃ saṃdaṃśacchedaḥ" | [**'saṃdaṃśacchedaḥ'**] aṅguṣṭhatarjanīcchedaḥ |

atha vyāsaḥ |

> nyāyasthāne ye 'dhikṛtā gṛhītvārthaṃ vinirṇayam |  
> kurvanty utkocakās te tu rājadravyavināśakāḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [22.14] |

> anyāyavādinaḥ sabhyās tathaivotkocajīvinaḥ |  
> viśvastavañcakāś caiva nirvāsyāḥ sarva eva te ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [1.339] |

> utkocajīvino dravyahīnān kṛtvā vivāsayet |

vyāsaḥ |

> strīpuṃsau vañcayantīha maṅgalādeśavṛttayaḥ |  
> gṛhṇanti chadmanā cārtham anāryāś cāryaliṅginaḥ ||

**[522]** bṛhaspatiḥ [22.15–16] |

> jyotirjñānaṃ tathotpātam aviditvā tu ye nṛṇām |  
> śrāvayanty arthalobhena vineyās te prayatnataḥ ||  
> daṇḍājinādinā yuktam ātmānaṃ darśayanti yet |  
> hiṃsanti chadmanā naṝṇāṃ vadhyās te rājapūruṣaiḥ ||

manuḥ [9.292] |

> sarvakaṇṭakapāpiṣṭhaṃ hemakāraṃ tu pārthivaḥ |  
> pravartamānam anyāye chedayel lavaśaḥ kṣuraiḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.297] |

> kūṭasvarṇavyavahārī vimāṃsasya ca vikrayī |  
> aṅgahīnās tu kartavyā dāpyāś cottamasāhasam ||

tathā [2.246–48] |

> mṛccarmamaṇisūtrāyaḥkāṣṭhavalkalavāsasām |  
> ajātau jātikaraṇe vikraye 'ṣṭaguṇo damaḥ ||  
> samudraparivartaṃ ca sārabhāṇḍaṃ ca kṛtrimam |  
> ādhānaṃ vikrayaṃ cāpi nayato daṇḍakalpanā ||

**[523]** > bhinne paṇe tu pañcāśat paṇe tu śatam ucyate |  
> dvipaṇe dviśate daṇḍo mūlyavṛddhau ca vṛddhimān ||

**'aṅgahīnāḥ'** nāsākarṇakarair hīnāḥ | **'mṛccarma'** ityādi | mṛdādīnām alpamūlyāpakṛṣṭajātīnāṃ bahumūlyalābhārtham utkṛṣṭajātikaraṇena gṛhītamūlyād aṣṭaguṇo damaḥ | apakṛṣṭajāter utkṛṣṭajātikaraṇaṃ yathā — mṛdaḥ mallikāmodasaṃcaraṇena sugandhāmalakam iti; mārjāracarmaṇi varṇotkarṣāpādanena vyāghracarmeti; sphaṭike lauhityakaraṇena padmarāga iti; kārpāsike sūtre guṇotkarṣādhānena paṭṭasūtram iti; kārṣṇāyase varṇotkarṣādhānena [rajatam iti] | **'samudram'** sampuṭakam | **'sārabhāṇḍam'** kuṅkumakarpūramuktāphalādi | **'bhinne paṇe'** nyūne paṇe |

bṛhaspatiḥ [22.17–18] |

> alpamūlyaṃ tu saṃskṛtya nayanti bahumūlyatām |  
> strībālakān pañcayanti daṇḍyās te 'rthānurūpataḥ ||

**[524]** > hemamuktāpravālādyaṃ kṛtrimaṃ kurvate tu ye |  
> kretre mūlyaṃ pradāpyās te rājñā taddviguṇaṃ damam ||

nāradaḥ |

> lohānām api sarveṣām hetur agnikriyāvidhau |  
> kṣayaḥ saṃskriyamāṇānāṃ teṣāṃ dṛṣṭo 'gnisaṃgamāt ||  
> suvarṇeṣu kṣayo nāsti rajate dvipalaṃ śatam |  
> śatam aṣṭapalam jñeyaṃ kṣayas tu trapusīsayoḥ ||  
> tāmraṃ pañcapalaṃ vidyād vikārā ye ca mṛnmayāḥ |  
> taddhātūnām anekatvād ayaso 'niyamaḥ kṣaye ||

**'kriyāvidhau'** ghaṭanakarmaṇi | **'tadvikārāḥ'** kāṃsyarītyadayaḥ | uktādhikakṣaye suvarṇakārādayo dāpyā daṇḍyāś ca |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.178] |

> agnau suvarṇam akṣīṇaṃ dvipalaṃ rajate śatam |  
> aṣṭau tu trapusīseṣu tāmre pañca daśāyasi ||

manuḥ [8.397] |

> tantuvāyo daśapalaṃ dadyād ekapalādhikam |  
> ato 'nyathā vartamāno dāpyo dvādaśakaṃ damam ||

**[525]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.179] |

> śate daśapalā vṛdddhir aurṇe kārpāsike tathā |  
> madhye pañcapalā sautre sūkṣme tu tripalā matā ||

nāradaḥ [12.13–14] |

> tāntavasya tu saṃskāre kṣayavṛddhī udāhṛte |  
> tatra kārpāsikorṇānāṃ vṛddhir daśapalā śate ||  
> sthūlasūtravatām eṣāṃ madhyānāṃ pañcakaṃ śatam |  
> tripalaṃ tu susūkṣmāṇām ataḥ kṣaya udāhṛtaḥ ||  
> triṃśāṃśo romabaddhasya kṣayaḥ karmakṛtasya tu |  
> kauśeyavalkalādīṃ naiva vṛddhir na ca kṣayaḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.180] |

> kārmike romabaddhe ca triṃśadbhāgaḥ kṣayo mataḥ |  
> na kṣayo na ca vṛddhiḥ syāt kauśeye valkaleṣu ca ||

**'kārmikam'** yatra niṣpanne paṭādau rucakasvastikādikaṃ citraṃ sūtraiḥ sūcyā kriyate tad ucyate | yatra prāvārādau romāṇi badhyante sa **'romabaddho'** nepālakambalādiḥ |

**[526]** manuḥ [8.396] |

> śālmale phalake ślakṣṇe nenijyān nejakaḥ sanaiḥ |  
> na ca vāsāṃsi vāsobhir nirharen na vivāsayet ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.238, 281] |

> vasānas trīn paṇān dāpyo nejakas tu parāṃśukam |  
> vikrayāvakrayādhānayāciteṣu paṇān daśa ||  
> deśaṃ kālaṃ ca bhogaṃ ca jñātvā naṣṭe balābalam |  
> dravyāṇāṃ kuśalā brūyur yat tad dāpyam asaṃśayam ||

**'avakrayo'** bhāṭakaḥ |

nāradaḥ [12.8–9] |

> mūlyāṣṭabhāgo hīyeta sakṛddhautasya vāsasaḥ |  
> dviḥ pādas tris tribhāgas tu catuḥkṛvo 'rdham eva tu ||  
> ardhakṣayāt tu parataḥ pādaśo 'pacayaḥ kramāt |  
> yāvat kṣīṇadaśaṃ vastraṃ jīrṇasyāniyamaḥ kṣaye ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [22.19–20] |

> madhyasthā vañcayanty ekaṃ snehalobhādinā yadā |  
> sākṣiṇaś cānyathā brūyur dāpyās te dviguṇaṃ damam ||

**[527]** > mantrauṣadhibalāt kiṃcit saṃprāptaṃ darśayanti ye |  
> mūlakarma ca kurvanti nirvāsyās te mahībhujā ||

manuḥ [9.225–26] |

> kitavān kuśīlavān kerān pāṣaṇḍasthāṃś ca mānavān |  
> vikarmasthān śauṇḍikāṃś ca kṣipraṃ nirvāsayet purāt ||  
> ete rāṣṭre vartamānā rājñaḥ pracchannataskarāḥ |  
> vikarmakriyayā nityaṃ bādhante bhadrikāḥ prajāḥ ||

vyāsaḥ |

> naigamādyā bhūridhanā daṇḍyā doṣānurūpataḥ |  
> yathā te nātivartante tiṣṭhanti samaye yathā ||

**[iti prakāśataskaradaṇḍāḥ]**

**70 — (ga) athāprakāśataskaradaṇḍāḥ**

tatra manuḥ [9.276] |

> sandhiṃ kṛtvā tu ye cauryaṃ rātrau kurvanti taskarāḥ |  
> teṣāṃ chitvā nṛpo hastau tīkṣṇe śūle niveśayet ||

vyāsaḥ |

> sandhicchettānekavidhaṃ dhanaṃ prāpnoti vai gṛhāt |  
> pradāpyaḥ svāmine sarvaṃ tīkṣṇe śūle niveṣayet ||

**[528]** bṛhaspatiḥ |

> sandhicchido hṛtaṃ tyājyāḥ śūlam āropayet tu tān |  
> tathā pānthamuṣo vṛkṣe gale baddhvāvalambayet ||

nārada-kātyāyanau |

> svadeśaghātino ye syus tathā mārganirodhinaḥ |  
> teṣāṃ sarvasvam ādāya rājā śūle niveśayet ||

manuḥ [8.323] |

> puruṣāṇāṃ kulīnānāṃ nārīṇāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ |  
> mukhyānāṃ caiva ratnānāṃ haraṇe vadham arhati ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [22.22] |

> manuṣyahāriṇo rājñā dagdhavyās tu kaṭāgninā |

vyāsaḥ |

> strīhartā lohaśayane dagdhavyo vai kaṭāgninā |  
> narahartā hastapādau chittvā sthāpyaś catuṣpathe ||

**[529]** nāradaḥ [21.28] |

> puruṣaṃ harato hastau daṇḍa uttamasāhasaḥ |  
> sarvasvaṃ harato nārīṃ kanyāṃ tu harato vadhaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

> sarvasvaṃ harataḥ strīṃ tu kanyāyā haraṇe vadhaḥ |  
> vājivāraṇabālānāṃ cādadīta bṛhaspatiḥ ||

**'ādadīta'** sarvasvam iti |

śaṅkhalikhitau: "rājaputrāpahāreṣu sahasraṃ śārīro vā daṇḍaḥ | tatkulīneṣv ardham | strīpuruṣayoś ca | hastyaśvagorathavṛṣayāneṣu rājaputrāpahāravad daṇḍaḥ" |

tathā: "ajāvike 'rdhatrayodaśam | nakulabiṣālāpaharaṇe trayaḥ kārṣāpaṇāḥ" |

manuḥ [8.342] |

> asanditānāṃ sandātā sanditānāṃ ca mokṣakaḥ |  
> dāsāśvarathahartā ca prāptāḥ syāc caurakilbiṣam ||

**'sanditānām'** caraṇabaddhānām |

**[530]** nāradaḥ [21.33] |

> goṣu brāhmaṇasaṃsthāsu [sthūrāyā]ś chedanaṃ bhavet |  
> dāsīṃ ca harato madhyas tathā pādasya chedanam ||

**'sthūrā'** pārṣṇer uparibhāgaḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ |

> mohartur nāsikāṃ chittvā baddhvā cāmbhasi majjayet |

manuḥ [8.325, 328] |

> goṣu brāhmaṇasaṃsthāsu churikāyāś ca bhedane |  
> paśūnāṃ caiva haraṇe sadyaḥ kāryo 'rdhapādikaḥ ||  
> mahāpaśūnāṃ haraṇe śastrāṇām auṣadhasya ca   
> kālam āsādya kāryaṃ ca rājā daṇḍaṃ prakalpayet ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.273] |

> bandigrāhāṃs tathā vājikuñjarāṇāṃ ca hāriṇaḥ |  
> prasahya ghātinaś caiva śūlam āropayen narān ||

manuḥ [9.280] |

> koṣṭhāgārāyudhāgāradevatāgārabhedinaḥ |  
> hastyaśvarathahartṝṃś ca hanyād evāvicārayan ||

**[531]** **'avicārayan'** avilambayan |

viṣṇuḥ [5.76–77]: "go'śvakharoṣṭragajāpahāry ekakarapādikaḥ kāryaḥ | ajāpahāry ekakaraś ca" |

vyāsaḥ |

> aśvahartā hastapādau kaṭiṃ chittvā pramāpyate |  
> paśuhartuś cārdhapādaṃ tīkṣṇaśastreṇa kartayet ||

nāradaḥ [21.29] |

> mahāpaśūn stenayato daṇḍa uttamasāhasam |  
> madhyamaṃ madhyamapaśūn pūrvaṃ kṣudrapaśau hṛte ||

tathā vyāsaḥ |

> utkṣepakagranthibhedau saṃsaṃśena viyojayet |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.274] |

> utkṣepakagranthibhedau karanāsāviḥinakau |  
> karyau dvitīyāparādhe karapādaikahīnakau ||

**[532]** manuḥ [9.277] |

> aṅgulī granthibhedasya chedayet prathamagrahe |  
> dvitīye hastacaraṇau tṛtīye vadham arhati ||

nāradaḥ [21.32] |

> prathame granthibhedaś ca aṅgulyaṅguṣṭhayor vadhaḥ |  
> dvitīye naiva tajjñeyaṃ tṛtīye vadham arhati ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [22.24] |

> dānyahārī daśaguṇaṃ dāpyas tu dviguṇaṃ damam |

manuḥ [8.320, 243] |

> dhānyaṃ daśabhyaḥ kumbhebhyo harato hy adhiko vadhaḥ |  
> śeṣe 'py ekādaśaguṇaṃ dāpyas tasya ca tad dhanam ||  
> kṣetrikasyātyaye daṇḍo bhāgād daśaguṇo bhavet |  
> tato 'rdhadaṇḍo bhṛtyānām ajñānāt kṣetrikasya tu ||

**'śeṣe'** nyūte | **'kṣetrikasyātyaye'** kṛṣīvalasyātikrame bhāgāpahāralakṣaṇe |

**[533]** viṣṇuḥ [5.79–80]: "dhānyāpahāry ekādaśaguṇaṃ daṇḍyaḥ | sasyāpahārī ca" |

"kāṣṭhabhāṇḍa"ityādiślokatrayānantaraṃ 19.21–31; =p. 536] nāradaḥ [19,32] |

> tulādharmameyānāṃ gaṇimānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ |  
> ebhis tūtkṛṣṭamūlyānāṃ mūlyād daśaguṇo damaḥ ||

manuḥ [8.321–22] |

> tathā dharimameyānāṃ śatād abhyadhike vadhaḥ |  
> suvarṇarajatādīnām uttamānāṃ ca vāsasām ||  
> pañcāśatas tv abhyadhike hastacchedanam iṣyate |  
> śeṣe 'py ekādaśaguṇaṃ mūlyād daṇḍaṃ prakalpayet ||

"harataḥ" ity anuvṛttau nāradaḥ [21.27] |

> suvarṇarajatādīnām uttamānāṃ ca vāsasām |  
> ratnānāṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ śatād abhyadhike vadhaḥ ||

śārīro 'ṅgacchedo veti daṇḍe śaṅkhalikhitau: "suvarṇaratnāpaharaṇe" |

**[534]** daṇḍa ity anuvṛttau viṣṇuḥ [5.87]: "ratnāpahāry uttamasāhasam" |

manuḥ [8.323] |

> mukhyānāṃ caiva ratnānāṃ haraṇe vadham arhati |

śaṅkhalikhitau: "aṣṭaśataṃ sītādravyāpahāre ca" |

manu-yamau [8.331] |

> paripūteṣu dhānyeṣu śākamūlaphaleṣu ca |  
> niranvaye śataṃ daṇḍyaḥ sānvaye 'rdhaśataṃ damaḥ ||

**'paripūteṣu'** apākṛtabudeṣu | **'niranvaye'** rakṣakarahite |

manuḥ [8.330] |

> puṣpeṣu harite dhānye gulmavallīnageṣu ca |  
> alpeṣv aparipūteṣu daṇḍaḥ syāt pañcakṛṣṇalaḥ ||

**'alpeṣu aparipūteṣu'** dhānyeṣu iti sambandhaḥ |

**[535]** yamaḥ |

> phaleṣu harite dhānye śākamūlasasigruje |  
> alpeṣv aparipūteṣu daṇḍaḥ syāt pañcakṛṣṇalaḥ ||

vyāsaḥ |

> madhyahīnadravyahārī puṣpamūlaphalasya ca |  
> dāpyas tu dviguṇaṃ daṇḍaṃ atha vā pañca kṛṣṇalān ||

gautamaḥ [12.15]: "phalaharitadhānyaśākādāne pañca kṛṣṇalam alpe" |

dāṇḍa iti śeṣaḥ |

manuḥ [8.326–29, 333] |

> sūtrakārpāsabilvānāṃ gomayasya guḍasya ca |  
> dadhnaḥ kṣīrasya takrasya pānīyasya tṛṇasya ca ||  
> veṇuvaiṇavabhāṇḍānāṃ lavaṇānāṃ tathaiva ca |  
> mṛnmayānāṃ ca haraṇe mṛdo bhasmana eva ca ||  
> matsyānāṃ pakṣiṇāṃ caiva tailasya ca ghṛtasya ca |  
> māṃsasya madhunaś caiva yac cānyat paśusaṃbhavam ||  
> anyeṣām evamādīnāṃ madyānām odanasya ca |  
> pakvānnānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ tanmūlyād dviguṇo damaḥ ||

**[536]** > yas tv etāny upakḷptāni dravyāṇi stenayen naraḥ |  
> taṃ śataṃ daṇḍayed rājā yaś cāgniṃ corayed gṛhāt ||

**'upakḷptāni'** upayogayogyatāṃ nītāni |

viṣṇuḥ [5.83–84]: "sūtrakārpāsagomayadadhikṣīratakraguḍatṛṇalavaṇamṛdbhasmamatsya-pakṣighṛtatailamāṃsamadhuvaidalaveṇumṛnmayalohabhāṇḍānām apahartā mūlyāt triguṇaṃ daṇḍyaḥ | pakvānnānāṃ ca" |

śaṅkhalikhitau: "kṛtakāṣṭhāśmakaulālacarmavetravidalabhāṇḍeṣu mūlyāt pañcaguṇaḥ | trayo vā kārṣāpaṇāḥ | ekacakrāpaharaṇe catvāriṃśat | śakaṭe tv aśītitamaḥ" |

nāradaḥ [21.22–24] |

> kāṣṭhabhāṇḍatṛṇādīnāṃ mṛnmayānāṃ tathaiva ca |  
> veṇuvaiṇavabhāṇḍānāṃ tathā snāyvasthicarmaṇām ||  
> śākānām ārdramūlānāṃ haraṇe phalapuṣpayoḥ |  
> gorasekṣuvikārāṇāṃ tathā lavaṇatailayoḥ ||  
> pakvānnānāṃ kṛtānnānāṃ madyānām odanasya ca |  
> sarveṣām alpamūlyānāṃ mūlyāt pañcaguṇo damaḥ ||

**[537]** vyāsaḥ |

> alpadhānyāpaharaṇe kṣīre tadvikṛtau tathā |  
> svāmine tatsamaṃ dāpyo daṇḍaṃ vā dviguṇaṃ nṛpe ||

manuḥ [8.319] |

> yas tu rajjuṃ ghaṭaṃ kūpād dhared bhindyāc ca yaḥ prapām |  
> sa daṇḍaṃ prāpnuyān māṣaṃ tac ca tasmin samāharet ||

daṇda ity anuvṛttau viṣṇuḥ [5.88]: "anuktadravyāṇām apahartā mūlyasamam" |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.275] |

> kṣudramadhyamahādravyaharaṇe sārato damaḥ |  
> deśakālavapuḥśakti saṃcintyaṃ daṇḍakarmaṇi ||

nāradaḥ [17.21] |

> sāhaseṣu ya evoktas triṣu daṇḍo manīṣibhiḥ |  
> sa eva daṇḍaḥ steye 'pi dravyeṣu triṣv anukramāt ||

kātyāyanaḥ [822] |

> yena yena paradrohaṃ karoty aṅgena taskaraḥ |  
> chindyāt tat tan nṛpas tasya na karoti tathā punaḥ ||

**[538]** nāradaḥ [21.34] |

> yena yena yathāṅgena steno nṛṣu viceṣṭate |  
> tat tad evāsya chettavyaṃ tan manor anuśāsanam ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [22.25] |

> tṛṇaṃ vā yadi vā kāṣṭhaṃ puṣpaṃ vā yadi vā phalam |  
> anāpṛcchya tu gṛhṇāno hastacchedanam arhati ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: "brāhmaṇo brāhmaṇasya samidājyedhmāgnikāṣṭhatṛṇolapapuṣpaphalamūlāny apaharan balād avijñāto vā hastacchedam āpnuyāt | kuśakarakāginotradravyāṇy **[539]** apaharataḥ pratyakṣato 'ṅgacchedaḥ syāt | apratyakṣaṃ yadā viditoyaṃ kilbiṣīti brāhmaṇaḥ kharayānam āpnuyāt | mūtramauṇḍyam itareṣām kharayānam eva tu" |

cauryādhikāre gautamaḥ [12.43–45]: "na śārīro brāhmaṇadaṇḍaḥ | karmaviyogavikhyāpanavivāsanāṅkakaraṇāni | avṛttau prāyaścittī saḥ" |

**'śārīraḥ'** tāḍanāṅgacchedādirūpaḥ | kas tarhi daṇḍa ity āha — **karmaviyoge**tyādi | **'karmavirogaḥ'** tena saha sarvakriyānārambhaḥ | **'vikhyāpanam'** ḍiṇḍimakena paribhramaṇaṃ steyalakṣaṇaprakāśanārtham | **'vivāsanam'** deśān niṣkāsanam | **'aṅkakaraṇam'** śvapadenāṅkanam | **'avṛttau prāyaścittī saḥ'**, anyena prakāreṇa jīvanāsambhave yadi steyaṃ karoti tadāsya prāyaścittamātraṃ bhavati na daṇḍa ity arthaḥ |

**[540]** āpastambaḥ [2.27.16–17]: "puruṣavadhe steye bhūmyādāna iti svāny ādāya vadhyaḥ | cakṣurnirodhaś caiteṣu brāhmaṇasya" |

**'svāni'** vastūni |

bṛhaspatiḥ [22.26] |

> vṛttasvādhyāyavān steyī bandhane kliśyate ciram |  
> svāmine tad dhanaṃ dāpyaḥ prāyaścittaṃ ca kāryate ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.270] |

> cauraṃ pradāpyāpahṛtaṃ ghātayed vividhair vadhaiḥ |  
> sacihnaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ kṛtvā svarāṣṭrād vipravāsayet ||

viṣṇuḥ [5.89–90]: "[stenāḥ] sarva evāpahṛtaṃ dhanikasya dāpyāḥ | tatas teṣām abhihitadaṇḍaprayogaḥ" |

**[541]** nāradaḥ [21.6] |

> na tv ahoḍhānvitāś corā vadhyā rājñā hy anāgamāḥ |  
> sahoḍhān sopakaraṇān kṣipraṃ rājā pramāpayet ||

**'hoḍhaś'** coraliṅgaṃ loptrādiḥ |

vṛddhaḥ |

> anyāyopāttavittatvād dhanam eṣāṃ malātmakam |  
> atas tān ghātayed rājā nārthadaṇḍena daṇḍayet ||

kātyāyanaḥ [823–26] |

> mānavāḥ sadya evāhuḥ sahoḍhānāṃ pravāsanam |  
> gautamānām aniṣṭaṃ tat prāṇacchedād vigarhitam ||  
> sahoḍham asahoḍhaṃ vā tattvāgamitasāhasam |  
> pragṛhya cihnam āvedya sarvasvair viprayojayet ||

**[542]**  
> ayaḥsandānaguptās tu mandabhaktā balānvitāḥ |  
> kuryuḥ karmāṇi nṛpater ā mṛtyor iti kauśikaḥ ||  
> paradeśād dhṛtaṃ dravyaṃ vaideśyena yadā bhavet |  
> gṛhītvā tasya tad dravyam adaṇḍaṃ tam visarjayet ||

**'tattvāgamitasāhasaḥ'** tattvena jñāpitaṃ sāhasaṃ yasya sa tathā | **'ayaḥsandānaguptāḥ'** nigaḍabaddhāḥ | ye **'balānvitāḥ'** te nigaḍabaddhā alpabhaktā santaḥ yāvadāyur **nṛpateḥ karmāṇi kuryur** iti yojanā |

vasiṣṭhaḥ [19.38–39]: "steno 'nupraveśān na duṣyati | śastradhārī sahoḍho vraṇasaṃpannaś ca vyapadiṣṭas tv ekeṣām" |

asyārthaḥ — nānupraveśamātreṇa steno bhavati | kiṃ tu śastradhāraṇanimittam antareṇa śastradhārī sahoḍhaḥ kṛtavraṇaś ca duṣyatīti |

**[543]**

**70 — (gha) atha corānveṣaṇam**

tatra nāradaḥ [17.18; 21.8–11] |

> sahoḍhagrahaṇāt steyaṃ hoṣhe 'saty upabhogataḥ |  
> śaṅkhā tv asajjanaikārthyād anāyavyayatas tathā ||  
> sahoḍhān vimṛśec caurān gṛhītapariśaṅkayā |  
> nayopadhābhiś citrābhir brūyus tathyaṃ yathā hi te ||  
> deśaṃ grāmaṃ diśaṃ nāma jātiṃ vāsaṃ pratiśrayam |  
> kṛtakāryasahāyāś ca praṣṭavyāḥ syur nigṛhya te ||  
> varṇasvarākārabhedāt sasandigdhaniveditāt |  
> adeśakāladṛṣṭatvān nivāsasya viśodhanāt ||  
> asadvyayāt pūrvacauryād asatsaṃsargakāraṇāt |  
> leśair apy anugantavyā na hoḍhenaiva kevalam || **[544]**

**'hoḍhaḥ'** loptram | **'upabhogataḥ** asati tu hoḍhe' apahṛtadravyasyāsādhāraṇasya prakārāntareṇāsaṃbhavat prāpteḥ karpūrāder upabhogadarśanena steyaṃ jñeyam | **'asajjanaikārthyāt**" — **'asajjjanaiḥ'** dyūtamadyapānādyāsaktaiḥ sahaikakāryātvāt | **'upādhibhiḥ citrābhiḥ'** upāyaiḥ nānāvidhaiḥ |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.226–28] |

> grāhakair gṛhyate cauro loptreṇātha padena vā |  
> pūrvakarmāparādhī ca tathā cāśuddhavāsakaḥ ||  
> anye 'pi śaṅkayā grāhyā nāmajātyādinihnavaiḥ |  
> dyūtastrīpānasaktāś ca bhinnaśuṣkamukhasvarāḥ ||  
> paradravyagṛhāṇāṃ ca pṛcchakā gūḍhacāriṇaḥ |  
> nirāyā vyayavantaś ca vinaṣṭadravyavikrayāḥ ||

**'grāhakair gṛhyate cauraḥ'** iti | grāhakair cauro 'yam iti nirdiṣṭaḥ san gṛhītavya ity arthaḥ | **'padena'** nāśadeśād ārabhya caurādipādabimbānusāreṇa | **'aśuddhavāsakaḥ'** avijñātavāsasthānaḥ | **'vinaṣṭadravyavikrayāḥ'** bhagnasya kuṇḍalāder vikrayakāriṇaḥ |

nāradaḥ [17.22–26] |

> gavādiṣu praṇaṣṭeṣu dravyeṣūpahateṣu ca |  
> pādenānveṣaṇaṃ kuryur āmūlāt tadvido janāḥ ||

**[545]**  
> grāme vraje vivīte vā yatra tan nipatat padam |  
> voḍhavyaṃ tad bhavet tena na cet so 'nyatra tan nayet ||  
> pāde pramūḍhe bhagne vā viṣamatvāj janāntike |  
> yas tv āsannataro grāmo vrajo vā tatra pātayet ||  
> same 'dhvani dvayor yatra stenaprāyo 'śucir janaḥ |  
> pūrvāparādhair duṣto vā saṃsṛṣṭo vā durātmabhiḥ ||  
> naivāntarikṣān na divo na samudrān na cānyataḥ |  
> dasyavaḥ saṃpravartante tasmād evaṃ prakalpayet ||  
> grāmeṣv anveṣaṇaṃ kuryuś caṇḍālavadhakādayaḥ |  
> rātrisaṃcāriṇo ye ca bahiḥ kuryur bahiś carāḥ ||

**'same 'dhvani'** tulyamārge | **'dvayoḥ'** grāmayoḥ | **'stenaprāyaḥ'** caurabahulaḥ |

manuḥ [9.234–36] |

> sabhāprapāpūpaśālāveśamadyānnavikrayāḥ |  
> catuṣpathāś caityavṛkṣāḥ samājāḥ prekṣaṇāni ca ||  
> jīrṇodyānāny araṇyāni kārukāveśanāni ca |  
> śūnyāni cāpy agārāṇi vanāny upavanāni ca ||

**[546]** > evaṃvidhān nṛpo veśān gulmaiḥ sthāvarajaṅgamaiḥ |  
> taskarapratiṣedhārthaṃ caraiś cāpy anucārayet ||

**'apūpaśālā'** kandukagṛham | **'veśaḥ'** veśyāgṛham | **'kārukāveśanāni'** śilpaśālāḥ | **'gulmaiḥ'** padātisamūhaiḥ | ‘**sthāvarajaṅgamaiḥ’** ekasthānasthitaiḥ pracāribhiḥ |

nāradaḥ |

> vicitraiś cārayec cāraiś cauragrahaṇatatparaiḥ |  
> tathā cānye praṇihitāḥ śraddheyāś citravādinaḥ ||  
> cārā hy utsāhayeyus tān taskarān pūrvataskarāḥ |  
> annapānamahādānaiḥ samājotsavadarśanaiḥ ||  
> tathā śauryāpadeśaiś ca kuryus teṣāṃ samāgamam |  
> yatra te nopasarpanti cāraiḥ praṇihitair api ||  
> te ‘pi syuḥ saṃgṛhītavyāḥ saputrajñātibāndhavāḥ |  
> yāṃs tatra caurān gṛhṇīyāt tān vitāḍya nibadhya ca ||

**[547]** > avaghuṣya ca sarvatra hanyāc citravadhena tu |  
> acaurā api dṛśyante cauraiḥ saha samāgatāḥ ||  
> yadṛcchayā naiva tu tān nṛpo daṇḍena saṃspṛśet |

kātyāyanaḥ [811] |

> anyahastāt paribhraṣṭam akāmād uddhṛtaṃ bhuvi |  
> caureṇa vā parikṣiptaṃ yatnāl loptraṃ parīkṣayet ||

nāradaḥ |

> dasyuvṛtte yadi nare śaṅkā syāt taskare ’pi vā |  
> yadi spṛśyeta leśena kāryaḥ syāc chapathaṃ tataḥ ||

‘**leśena’** yuktileśena mukhaśotrādinā |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.269] |

> gṛhītaḥ śaṅkayā caurya ātmānaṃ cen na śodhayet |  
> dāpayitvā hṛtaṃ dravyaṃ cauradaṇḍena daṇḍayet ||

kātyāyanaḥ [821] |

> acaurāhāpitaṃ dravyaṃ caurānveṣaṇatatparaiḥ |  
> upalabdhe labheraṃs te dviguṇaṃ tatra dāpayet ||

**[548]**

**70 — (ṅa) atha stenātideśāḥ**

tatra manuḥ [9.271, 278] |

> grāmeṣv api ca ye kecic caurāṇāṃ bhakṣyadāyakāḥ |  
> bhāṇḍāvakāśadāś caiva sarvāṃs tān abhighātayet ||  
> agnidān bhaktadāṃś caiva tathā śastrāvakāśadān |  
> saṃnidhātṝṃś ca moṣasya hanyāc caurān iveśvaraḥ ||

‘**moṣasya’** apahṛtadravyasya |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.276] |

> bhaktāvakāśāgnyudakamantropakaraṇavyayān |  
> kṛtvā caurasya hantur vā jānato daṇḍa uttamaḥ ||

‘**bhaktam’** aśanam | ‘**avakāśo’** nivāsasthānam | ‘**agniḥ’** śītāpanodādyarthaḥ | ‘**udakam’** tṛṣitasya | ‘**mantraḥ’** cauryaprakāropadeśaḥ | ‘**upakaraṇam’** cauryasādhanam | ‘**vyayaḥ’** apahārārthaṃ deśāntaraṃ gacchataḥ pātheyam |

nāradaḥ [17.19; 21.14] |

> bhaktāvakāśadātāraḥ stenānāṃ ye samarpatām |

**[549]** > śaktāś ca ya upekṣante te ‘pi taddoṣabhāginaḥ ||  
> samadaṇḍāḥ smṛtāḥ sarve ye ca pracchādayanti tān |

kātyāyanaḥ [827] |

> caurāṇāṃ bhaktadā ye syus tathāgnyudakadāyakāḥ |  
> kretāraś caiva bhāṇḍānāṃ pratigrahaṇa eva ca ||  
> samadaṇḍāḥ smṛtā hy ete ye ca pracchādayanti tān ||

hanyād ity anuvṛttau viṣṇuḥ [5.16–17]: “prasahya taskarāṇāṃ cāvakāśabhaktapradāṃś ca | anyatra rājāśakteḥ” |

manuḥ [8.340; 9.272, 274] |

> yo ‘dattādāyino hastāl lapsyete brāhmaṇo dhanam |

**[550]** > yājanādhyāpanenāpi yathā stenas tathaiva saḥ ||  
> rāṣṭreṣu rāṣṭrādhikṛtān sāmantāṃś caiva coditān |  
> upaghāteṣu madhyasthāṃś chiṣyāṃś corān iva druvam ||  
> grāmaghāte hilābhaṅge pathi moṣādidarśane |  
> śaktito nābhidhāvanto nirvāsyāḥ saparicchadāḥ ||

‘**adattādāyinaḥ’** caurasya | **rāṣṭra** ityādi — **rāṣṭrādhikṛtān** grāmavāsinaś ca prajānāṃ caurādibhiḥ **upaghāteṣu** kriyamāṇeṣu **madhyasthān** upakṣakān **caurān iva** daṇḍayed ity arthaḥ | ‘**hilābhaṅgaḥ’** ‘parakṣetrotpannasasyanāśanam’ iti medhātithiḥ | ‘**moṣādidarśane’** apahṛtadravyadarśane |

**[551]**

**atha varṇataḥ steyaviśeṣaḥ**

tatra manuḥ [8.337–38] |

> aṣṭāpādyaṃ hi śūdrasya steyo bhavati kilbiṣam |  
> ṣoḍaśaiva tu vaiśyasya dvātriṃśat kṣatriyasya tu ||  
> brāhmaṇasya catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ pūrvaṃ vāpi śataṃ bhavet |  
> dviguṇā vā catuḥṣaṣṭis taddoṣaguṇavidviṣaḥ (?) ||

kātyāyanaḥ [485] |

> yena doṣeṇa śūdrasya daṇḍo bhavati dharmataḥ |  
> tena viṭkṣatraviprāṇāṃ dviguṇo dviguṇo bhavet ||

**70 — (ca) atha stenālābhe hṛtadānam**

tatra āpastambaḥ [2.26.4–8]: “grāmeṣu nagareṣu cāryān śucīn satyaśīlān prajāguptaye nidadhyāt | teṣāṃ puruṣās tathāguṇā eva syuḥ | sarvato yojanaṃ nagaraṃ taskarebhyo rakṣyam | krośo grāmebhyaḥ | tatra yan mucyate tais tat pratidāpyam” |

**[552]** kātyāyana-nāradau [kā. 813; nā. 21.18] |

> gṛheṣu muṣitaṃ rājā cauragrāhāṃs tu dāpayet |  
> ārakṣakāṃs tu dikpālān yadi cauro na labhyate ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.271–72] |

> ghātite ’pahṛte doṣo grāmabhartur anirgate |  
> vivītabhartus tu pathi cauroddhartur avītake ||  
> svasīmni dadyād grāmas tu padaṃ vā yatra gacchati |  
> pañcagrāmī bahiḥ kṛṣṭād daśagrāmy atha vā punaḥ ||

‘cauroddhartuḥ’ caurarakṣāniyuktasya | ‘avītake’ vivītavyatirikte kṣetrādau | ‘bahiḥ kṛṣṭāt’ karṣaṇapradeśād anyatra yad apahṛtaṃ tat pañcagrāmamilitā dadyuḥ | saṃnidhānāpekṣayā daśagrāmīti vikalpaḥ |

nāradaḥ [21.16–17] |

> gocare yasya muṣyeta tena cauraḥ prayatnataḥ |  
> mṛgyo dāpyo ‘nyathā moṣaṃ padaṃ yadi na nirgatam ||  
> nirgate tu yad etasmān na ced anyatra pātitam |  
> sāmantān mārgapālāṃś ca dikpālāṃś caiva dāpayet ||

**[553]** kātyāyanaḥ [814] |

> grāmānte tu hṛtaṃ dravyaṃ grāmādhyakṣaṃ pradāpayet |  
> vivīte svāminā deyaṃ cauroddhartrāvivītake ||

viṣṇuḥ [3.66–67]: “caurāpahṛtaṃ dhanam avāpya sarvam eva sarvavarṇebhyo dadyāt | anavāpya svakośād eva dadyāt” |

kātyāyanaḥ [815] |

> svadeśe yasya yat kiṃcit hṛtaṃ deyaṃ nṛpeṇa tat |  
> gṛhṇīyāt tat svayaṃ naṣṭaṃ prāptam anviṣya pārthivaḥ ||

nārada-kātyāyanau [nā. 21.21; kā. 816] |

> caurair hṛtaṃ prayatnena svarūpaṃ pratipādayet |  
> tadabhāve tu mūlyaṃ syād anyathā kilbiṣī nṛpaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [817] |

> labdhe tu caure yadi vā moṣas tasmān na labhyate |  
> dadyāt tam atha vā cauraṃ dāpayet tu yatheṣṭataḥ ||

**[554]** vṛddhamanuḥ |

> tasmiṃś ced dāpyamānānāṃ bhaven moṣe tu saṃśayaṃ |  
> muṣitaḥ śapathān dāpyo bandhubhir vāpi śodhayet ||  
> yasmād apahṛtāl labdhaṃ dravyāt svalpaṃ tu svāminā |  
> taccheṣam āpnuyāt tasmād pratyaye svāminā kṛte ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.173–74] |

> śaulikaiḥ sthānapālair vā naṣṭāpahṛtam āhṛtam |  
> ardhāt tu vatsarāt svāmī hareta parato nṛpaḥ ||  
> paṇān ekaśaphe dadyāc caturaḥ pañca mānuṣe |  
> mahiṣoṣṭragavāṃ dvau dvau pādaṃ pādam ajāvike ||

‘**ekaśaphe’** aśvādau praṇaṣṭādhigate svāmī rājñe rakṣaṇanimittaṃ ‘**caturaḥ paṇān’** dadyāt |

gautamaḥ [10.35–37]: “praṇaṣṭam asvāmikam adhigamya rājñe prabrūyuḥ | vikhyāpya saṃvatsaraṃ rājñā rakṣyam | ūrdhvam adhigantuś caturthaṃ rājñaḥ śeṣam” |

**[555]** manuḥ [8.31–34] |

> mamedam iti yo brūyāt so ‘nuyojyo yathāvidhi |  
> saṃvādya rūpasaṃkhyādīn svāmī tad dravyam arhati ||  
> avedayaṃs tu naṣṭasya deśaṃ kālaṃ ca tattvataḥ |  
> varṇaṃ rūpaṃ pramāṇaṃ ca tatsamaṃ daṇḍam arhati ||  
> ādadītātha ṣaḍbhāgaṃ praṇaṣṭādhigatān nṛpaḥ |  
> daśamaṃ dvādaśaṃ vāpi satāṃ dharmam anusmaran ||  
> praṇaṣṭādhitataṃ dravyaṃ tiṣṭhed yuktair adhiṣṭhitam |  
> yāṃs tatra caurān gṛhṇīyāt tān rājebhena ghātayet ||

‘**ibhena’** hastinā \

āpastambaḥ [2.28.8–10]: “pramādād araṇye paśūn utsṛṣṭān grāmam ānīya svāmibhyo visṛjet | punaḥ pramāde sakṛd avarudhya | tadūrdhvaṃ na sūrkṣet” |

‘**na sūrkṣyet’** nāharaṇaṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ |

**iti kṛtyakalpatarau vyavahārakāṇḍe steyaparva |**

**[556]**

## 71 sāhasam
atha sāhasam

tatra nāradaḥ |

> manuṣyamāraṇaṃ cauryaṃ paradārābhimarśanam |  
> pāruṣyam ubhayaṃ ceti sāhasaṃ pañcadhā smṛtam ||  
> sahasā kriyate karma yat kiṃcid baladarpitaiḥ |  
> tat sāhasam iti proktaṃ saho balam ihocyate ||  
> tasyaiva bhedaḥ steyaṃ syād viśeṣas tatra dṛśyate |  
> ādhiḥ sāhasam ākramya steyam ādhiś chalena tu ||  
> tat punas trividhaṃ proktaṃ prathamaṃ madhyamaṃ tathā |  
> uttamaṃ ceti śāstreṣu tasyoktaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ pṛthak ||  
> phalamūlodakādīnāṃ kṣetropakaraṇasya ca |  
> bhaṅgākṣepāvamardādyaiḥ prathamaṃ sāhasaṃ smṛtam ||

**[557]** > vāsaḥpaśvannapānānāṃ gṛhopakaraṇasya ca |  
> etenaiva prakāreṇa madhyamaṃ sāhasaṃ smṛtam ||  
> vyāpādo viśaśastrādyaiḥ paradārapradharṣaṇam |  
> prāṇoparodhi yac cānyad uktam uttamasāhasam ||

manuḥ [8.332] |

> syāt sāhasaṃ tv anvayavat prasabhaṃ karma yat kṛtam |

bṛhaspatiḥ [23.3; 8–8??] |

> hīnamadhyottamatvena trividhaṃ tatprakīrtitam |  
> dravyāpekṣo damas tatra prathamo madhya uttamaḥ ||  
> kṣetropakaraṇaṃ setuṃ puṣpamūlaphalāni ca |  
> vināśayan haran daṇḍyaḥ śatādyam anurūpataḥ ||  
> paśuvastrānnapānāni gṛhopakaraṇaṃ tathā |  
> hiṃsayan coravad dāpyo dviśatādyaṃ damaṃ tathā ||  
> strīpuṃsau hemaratnāni devavipradhanaṃ tathā |  
> kauśeyaṃ cottamadravyam eṣāṃ mūlyasamo damaḥ ||  
> dviguṇo vā kalpanīyaḥ puruṣāpekṣayā nṛpaiḥ |  
> hantā ca ghātanīyaḥ syāt prasaṅgavinivṛttaye ||

**[558]** sāhasānuvṛttau nāradaḥ [17.7–8] |

> tasya daṇḍaḥ kriyāpekṣaḥ prathamasya śatāvaraḥ |  
> madhyamasya tu śāstrajñair dṛṣṭaḥ pañcaśatāvaraḥ ||  
> vadhaḥ sarvasvaharaṇaṃ purān nirvāsanāṅkane |  
> tadaṅgaccheda ity ukto daṇḍa uttamasāhasaḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.230, 223] |

> sāmānyadravyaprasabhaharaṇāt sāhasaṃ smṛtam |  
> tanmūlyād dviguṇo daṇḍo nihnave ca caturguṇaḥ ||  
> abhighāte tathā bhede chede kuḍyāvapātane |  
> paṇān dāpyaḥ pañcadaś viṃśatiṃ tadvyayaṃ tathā ||

‘**sāmānyam’** nānāsvāmikaṃ ‘**dravyam’** |

manuḥ [8.288–89] |

> dravyāṇi hiṃsyād yo yasya jñānato ‘jñānato ‘pi vā |  
> sa tasyotpādayet tuṣṭiṃ rājñā daṇḍyaś ca tatsamam ||

**[559]** > carmacārmikabhāṇḍeṣu kāṣṭhaloṣṭamayeṣu ca |  
> mūlyāt pañcaguṇo daṇḍaḥ puṣpamūlaphaleṣu ca ||

kātyāyanaḥ [807] |

> śataṃ bhaṅgopamārdau vā kuryād dravyeṣu yo naraḥ |  
> prāpnuyāt sāhasaṃ pūrvaṃ dravyabhāk svāmy udāhṛtaḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.224] |

> duḥkhotpādi gṛhe dravyaṃ kṣipan prāṇaharaṃ tathā |  
> ṣoḍaśādyaḥ paṇān dāpyo dvitīyo madhyamaṃ damam ||

‘**duḥkhotpādi’** kaṇṭakādi | ‘**prāṇaharam’** sarpādi |

daṇḍa ity anuvṛttau viṣṇuḥ [5.108–19]: “gṛhakuḍyādyupabhettā madhyamasāhasam | tac ca yojayet | gṛhe pīḍākaraṃ dravyaṃ prakṣipan paṇaśatam | sādhāraṇyāpalāpī ca | preṣitasyāpradātā ca | pitṛputrācāryayājyartvijām anyonyāpatitatyāgī ca | na ca tān jahyāt | **[560]** śūdrapravrajitānāṃ daive pitrye bhojakasya | ayogyakarmakārī ca | samudragṛhabhedakaś ca | aniyuktaḥ śapathakārī | paśūnāṃ puṃstvopaghātakārī ca” |

punar viṣṇuḥ [5.104–05]: “aspṛśyaiḥ kāmakāreṇa spṛśyaṃ spṛśan vadhyaḥ | rajasvalāṃ śiphābhis tāḍayet” |

‘**śiphābhiḥ’** vṛkṣajaṭābhiḥ |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.232–37] |

> arghyākroṣātikramakṛd bhrātṛbhāryāprahārakaḥ |  
> saṃdiṣṭasyāpradātā ca samudragṛhabhedakaḥ ||  
> sāmantakulikādīnām apakārasya kārakaḥ |  
> pañcāśatpaṇiko daṇḍa eṣām iti viniścayaḥ ||  
> svacchandavidhavāgāmī vikruṣṭe nābhidhāvakaḥ |  
> akāraṇe ca vikroṣṭā cāṇḍālaś cottamān spṛśan ||

**[561]** > śūdrapravrajitānāṃ ca daive pitrye ca bhojakaḥ |  
> ayuktaṃ śapathaṃ kurvann ayogyo yogyakarmakṛt ||  
> vṛṣakṣudrapaśūnāṃ ca puṃstvasya pratighātakaḥ |  
> sādhāraṇasyāpalāpī dāsīgarbhavināśakṛt ||  
> pitāputrasvasṛbhrātṛdampatyācāryasiṣyakāḥ |  
> eṣām apatitānyonyatyāgī ca śatadaṇḍabhāk ||

manuḥ [8.389] |

> na mātā na pitā na strī na putras tyāgam arhati |  
> tyajann apatitān etān rājñā dāpyaḥ śatāni ṣaṭ ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: “na mātāpitror antaraṃ gaccheta putraḥ | kāmaṃ mātur evānuyāyāt | sā hi dhāriṇī poṣaṇī ca | na putraḥ pratimucyetānyatra sautrāmaṇīyāgāj jīvannṛṇānmātuḥ | evam atyājyā mātā | tathā pitā | sapiṇḍā guṇavantaḥ sarva evātyājyāḥ | yas tyajet kāmād apatitān sa daṇḍaṃ prāpnuyād dviśatam | na mātāpitarāv atikramet | na gurum | trayāṇām atikrame ‘ṅgacchedaḥ” |

**[562]** viṣṇuḥ [5.91–97]: “yeṣāṃ deyaḥ panthās teṣām apathadāyī kārṣāpaṇapañcaviṃśatiṃ daṇḍyaḥ | āsanārhasyāsanam adadañ ca | pūrvārham apūjayaṃś ca | prātiveśyabrāhmaṇe nimantraṇātikrame ca | nimantrayitvā bhojanādāyinaś ca | nimantritas tathety uktvā cābhuñjānāḥ suvarṇamāṣakam | niketayituś ca dviguṇam annam” |

manuḥ [8.392–93] |

> prātiveśyānuveśyau ca kalyāṇe viṃśatidvije |  
> arhāv abhojayan viprau daṇḍam arhati māṣakam ||  
> śrotriyaḥ śrotriyaṃ sādhuṃ bhūtikṛtyeṣv abhojayan |  
> tad annaṃ dviguṇaṃ dāpyo hairaṇyaṃ caiva māṣakam ||

‘**kalyāṇe viṃśatidvije’** iti — yatra kalyāṇe viṃśatidvijā bhuñjata iti |

matsyapurāṇe [227.8] |

> āmantrito dvijo yas tu vartamānaḥ pratigrahe |  
> niṣkāraṇaṃ na gacchet tu sa dāpyo ‘ṣṭaśataṃ damam ||

**[563]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.263] |

> tarikaḥ sthalajaṃ śulkaṃ gṛhṇan dāpyaḥ paṇān daśa |  
> brāhmaṇaḥ prātiveśyāṃś ca tadvad evānimantrayan ||

‘tarikaḥ’ nadyādeḥ saṃtāraṇaśulkādhikṛtaḥ |

viṣṇuḥ [5.120–21]: “pitāputravirodhe tu sākṣiṇāṃ daśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ | yas tayoś cāntare syāt tasyottamasāhasam” |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.239] |

> pitāputravirodhe tu sākṣiṇāṃ tripaṇo damaḥ |  
> antare tu tayor yaḥ syāt tasyāpy aṣṭaśato damaḥ ||

daṇḍa ity anuvṛttau viṣnuḥ [5.98–103]: “abhakṣyeṇa brāhmaṇaṃ dūṣayitvā ṣoḍaśsuvarṇān | jātyapahāriṇā śatam | surayā vadhyaḥ | kṣatriyaṃ dūṣayitus tadardham | vaiśyaṃ dūṣayitus tadardham api | śūdraṃ dūṣayituḥ prathamasāhasam” |

‘**abhakṣyeṇa’** viṣṭhādina | ‘**jātyapahāriṇā’** abhakṣyeṇa laśunādinā | śūdrasyābhakṣyaṃ pañcanakhamāṃsādi |

**[564]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.296] |

> dvijaṃ pradūṣyabhakṣyeṇa daṇḍya uttamasāhasam |  
> kṣatriyaṃ madhyamaṃ vaiśyaṃ prathamaṃ śūdram ardhikam ||

manuḥ |

> abhakṣyam atha cāpeyaṃ vaiśyādīn āśayan dvijān |  
> jaghanyamadhyamotkṛṣṭān daṇḍān arhed yathākramam ||  
> paṇāḥ śūdre bhaved daṇḍaś catuḥpañcāśad eva tu |  
> grasitāraḥ svayaṃ kāryā rājñā nirviṣayās tu te ||

viṣṇuḥ [5.173]: “jātibhraṃśakarasyābhakṣyasya bhakṣayitā vivāsyaḥ” |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.301, 303] |

> jāraṃ corety abhivadan dāpyaḥ pañcaśataṃ damam |  
> upajīvya dhanaṃ muñcaṃs tad evāṣṭaguṇīkṛtam ||  
> mṛtāṅgalagnavikretur guros tāḍayitus tathā |  
> rājayānāsanāroḍhur daṇḍo madhyamasāhasaḥ ||

**[565]** ‘**jāraṃ corety abhivadan’** svavaṃśakalaṅkaśaṅkayā svastrīdoṣam apahnuvāno jāraṃ coro ‘yaṃ nirgacchatīti bruvan | ‘**upajīvya dhanaṃ muñcan’** dhanaṃ gṛhītvā jāraṃ parityajan |

manuḥ [9.290, 286] |

> abhicāreṣu sarveṣu kartavyo dviśato damaḥ |  
> mūlakarmaṇi cānāptaiḥ kṛtyāsu vividhāsu ca ||  
> adūṣitānāṃ dravyāṇāṃ dūṣaṇe bhedane tathā |  
> maṇīnām avabādheṣu daṇḍaḥ prathamasāhasaḥ ||

tathā [10.96] |

> yo lobhād adhamo jātyā jīved utkṛṣṭakarmabhiḥ |  
> taṃ rājā nirdhanaṃ kṛtvā kṣipram eva pravāsayet ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.304] |

> vipratvena tu śūdrasya jīvato ‘ṣṭaśato damaḥ ||

manuḥ [9.285] |

> saṃkramadhvajayaṣṭīnāṃ pratimānāṃ ca bhedakaḥ \  
> pratikuryāc ca tat sarvaṃ pañca dadyāc chatāni ca ||

**[566]** kātyāyanaḥ |

> hared bhindyād dahed vāpi devānāṃ pratimāṃ yadi |  
> tadgṛhaṃ caiva yo bhindyāt prāpnuyāt pūrvasāhasam 

viṣṇuḥ [5.174]: “abhakṣyasyāvikreyasya vikrayī devapratimābhedakaś cottamasāhasaṃ daṇḍanīyaḥ” |

nāradaḥ [4.67] |

> avikreyāṇi vikrīṇān brāhmaṇaḥ pracyutaḥ pathaḥ |  
> mārge punar avasthāpyo rājñā daṇḍena bhūyasā ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: “pratimārāmakūpasaṅkramadhvajasetunipānadvijāyatanabhaṅgeṣu tatsamupasthānaṃ pratisaṃskāro ‘ṣṭaśataṃ damaṃ ca” |

manuḥ [9.281, 279] |

> yas tu pūrvaniviṣṭasya taḍāgasyodakaṃ haret |  
> āgamaṃ cāpy apāṃ bhindyāt sa dāpyaḥ pūrvasāhasam ||  
> taḍāgabhedakaṃ hanyād apsu śuddhavadhena vā |  
> tad vāpi pratisaṃskuryād dadyāc cottamasāhasam ||

hanyād ity anuvṛttau viṣṇuḥ [5.15]: “setubhedakṛtaś ca” |

‘śārīro ‘ṅgacchedo vā’ iti daṇḍaḥ |

śaṅkhalikhitau: “vāpītaḍāgodapānabhedamārgarasadravyadūṣaṇe | adāsīdāsasaṃpradānakaraṇe” |

**[567]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.279] |

> viṣāgnidāṃ striyaṃ caiva puruṣaghnīm agarbhiṇīm |  
> setubhedakaraṃ vāpsu śilāṃ baddhvā praveśayet ||

‘**viṣāgnidām’** patigurunijāpatyapramāpaṇīṃ vikarṇakaranāsoṣṭhīṃ kṛtvā gobhiḥ pramāpayet | ‘**puruṣaghnīm agarbhiṇīm’** puruṣamāriṇīm yā strī bhavet sā yadi garbharahitā bhavati tadā tāṃ jale praveśayen nānyathā |

yamaḥ |

> ulkāgnidāyakāś caurāḥ ghātakāś copaghātakāḥ |  
> svaśarīreṇa daṇḍyāḥ syur manur āha prajāpatiḥ ||

yājñāvalkyaḥ [2.282] |

> kṣetraveśmagrāmavanavivītakhaladāhakāḥ |  
> rājapatnyabhigāmī ca dagdhavyās tu kaṭāgninā ||

kātyāyanaḥ [809] |

> prākāraṃ bhedayed yas tu pātayec chātayet tathā |  
> badhnīyād ambhaso mārgaṃ prāpnuyāt pūrvasāhasam ||

manuḥ [9.289, 275, 272] |

> prākārasyāvabhettāraṃ parikhāṇāṃ ca pūrakam |  
> dvārāṇāṃ caiva bhettāraṃ kṣipram eva pramāpayet ||

**[568]** > rājñaḥ kośāpahartṝṃś ca pratikūleṣv avasthitān |  
> ghātayed vividhair daṇḍair arīṇāṃ copajāpakān ||  
> rāṣṭreṣu rakṣādhikṛtāḥ parasvādāyinaḥ śaṭhāḥ |  
> bhṛtyā bhavanti prāyeṇa tebhyo rakṣed imāḥ prajāḥ ||

tathā [7.124] |

> ye kāryebhyo ‘rtham evaṃ hi gṛhṇīyuḥ pāpacetasaḥ |  
> teṣāṃ sarvasvam ādāya rājā kuryāt pravāsanam ||

tathā [9.231] |

> ye niyuktās tu kāryeṣu hanyuḥ kāryāṇi kāryiṇām |  
> dhanoṣmaṇā pacyamānās tān niḥsvān kāryen nṛpaḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [1.338–39] |

> ye rāṣṭrādhikṛtās teṣāṃ cārair jñātvā viceṣṭitam |  
> sādhūn saṃmānayed rājā viparītāṃs tu ghātayet ||  
> utkocajīvino dravyahīnān kṛtvā vivāsayet |  
> sadānamānasatkārān śrotriyān vāsayet sadā ||

**[569]** tathā [2.243] |

> abadhyaṃ yas tu badhnāti badhyaṃ yaś ca pramuñcati |  
> aprāptavyavahāraṃ ca sa dāpyo damam uttamam ||

viṣṇuḥ [5.195] |

> daṇḍyam unmocayan daṇḍyād dviguṇaṃ daṇḍam āvahet |  
> niyuktaś cāpy adaṇḍyānāṃ daṇḍakārī narādhamaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [955–56] |

> rājakrīḍāsu ye śaktā rājavṛttyupajīvinaḥ |  
> apriyasya tu yo vaktā vadhaṃ teṣāṃ prakalpayet ||  
> pratirūpasya kartāraṃ prekṣaṇāḥ prakarāś ca ye |  
> rājārthamoṣakāś caiva prāpnuyur vividhaṃ vadham ||

hanyād ity anuvṛttau viṣṇuḥ [5.18]: “ye cākulīnā rāṣṭram abhikāmayeyuḥ” |

**[570]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.295] |

> ūnaṃ vāpy adhikaṃ vāpi likhed vā rājaśāsanam |  
> pāradārikacauraṃ vā muñcato daṇḍa uttamaḥ ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: “kūṭaśāsanaprayoge rājaśāsanapratiṣedhe kūṭatulāmānapratimānavyavahāre śārīro ‘ṅgacchedo vā” |

kātyāyanaḥ [954] |

> pramāṇena tu kūṭena mudrayā vāpi kūṭayā |  
> kāryaṃ tu sādhayed yo vai sa dāpyo daṇḍam uttamam ||

manuḥ [9.232] |

> kūṭaśāsanakartṝṃś ca prakṛtīnāṃ ca dūṣakān |  
> strībālabrāhmaṇaghnāṃś ca hanyād dviṭsevinas tathā ||

viṣṇuḥ [3.33–35, 37]: “svāmyamātyadurgakośadaṇḍarāṣṭramitrāṇi prakṛtayaḥ | taddūṣakāṃś ca hanyāt | svarāṣṭrapararāṣṭrayoś ca cāracakṣuḥ syāt | duṣṭāṃś ca hanyāt” ||

punar viṣṇuḥ [5.9–11]: “kūṭaśāsanakṛtṝṃś ca rājā hanyāt |kūṭalekhyakarāṃś ca | garadāgnidaprasahyataskarān strībālapuruṣaghātinaś ca” |

**[571]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.277] |

> śastrāvapāte garbhasya ghātane cottamo damaḥ |

uśanā |

> parikleśena pūrvaḥ syād bhaiṣajyena tu madhyamaḥ |  
> prahāreṇa tu garbhasya pātane daṇḍa uttamaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [799] |

> vyāpādane tu tatkārī vadhaṃ citram avāpnuyāt |

bṛhaspatiḥ [23.9–12] |

> sāhasaṃ pañcadhā proktaṃ vadhas tatrādhikaḥ smṛtaḥ |  
> tatkāriṇo nārthadamaiḥ śāsyāḥ vadhyāḥ prayatnataḥ ||  
> prakāśavadhakā ye tu tathaivopāṃśughātakāḥ |  
> jñātvā samyag dhanaṃ hṛtvā hantavyā vividhair vadhaiḥ ||  
> mitraprāptyarthalobhair vā rājñā lokahitaiṣiṇā |  
> na moktavyāḥ prayatnena sarvabhūtabhayāvahāḥ ||  
> lobhād bhayād vā yo rājā na hanyāt pāpakāriṇaḥ |  
> tasya prakṣubhyate rāṣṭraṃ rājyāt sa parihīyate ||

**[572]** tathā [23.13] |

> bandhāgniviṣaśastreṇa parān yas tu pramāpayet |  
> krodhādinā nimittena naraḥ sāhasikas tu saḥ ||

baudhāyanaḥ: “kṣatriyādīnāṃ brāhmaṇavadhe vadhaḥ sarvasvaharaṇaṃ ca | teṣām eva tulyāpakṛṣṭavadhe yathābalam anurūpadaṇḍaṃ prakalpayet | kṣatriyavadhe gosahasraṃ vṛṣabhaikādhikaṃ rājña utsṛjed vairaniryātanārtham | śataṃ vaiśye daś śūdre vṛṣabhaś cātrādhikaḥ | śūdravadhena strīvadho govadhaś ca vyākhyātaḥ | anyatrātreyyā vadhāt | dhenvanaḍuhoś ca | vadhe dhenvanaḍuhor ante cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret | ātreyyā vadhaḥ kṣatriyavadhena vyākhyātaḥ | haṃsabhāsabarhiṇacakravākabalākākolūkamaṇḍūkaḍiḍḍika-ḍerikāśvababhrunakulādīnāṃ vadhe śūdravat” |

bṛhaspati-kātyāyanau |

> ekasya bahavo yatra praharanti ruṣānvitāḥ |  
> marmaprahārado yaś ca ghātakaḥ sa udāhṛtaḥ ||

**[573]** > marmaghātī tu yas teṣāṃ yathoktaṃ dāpayed damam |  
> ārambhakṛt sahāyaś ca doṣabhājas tadardhataḥ ||  
> kṣatasyālpamahatvaṃ ca marmasthānaṃ ca yatnataḥ |  
> sāmarthyaṃ cānubandhaṃ ca jñātvā cihnaiḥ prasādhayet ||

nāradaḥ [17.9–10] |

> aviśeṣeṇa sarveṣām eṣa daṇḍavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ |  
> vadhād ṛte brāhmaṇasya na vadhaṃ brāhmaṇo ‘rhati ||  
> śiraso muṇḍanaṃ daṇḍas tasya nirvāsanaṃ purāt |
