> lalāṭe cābhiśastāṅkaḥ prayāṇaṃ gardabhena ca ||

sāhacauryayor yamaḥ |

> na śārīro brāhmaṇasya daṇḍo bhavati karhicit |  
> gupte tu bandhane badhvā rājā bhaktaṃ pradāpayet ||  
> atha vā bandhanaṃ rajjvā karma vā kāreyan nṛpaḥ |  
> māsārdhamāsaṃ kurvīta kāryaṃ vijñāya tattvataḥ ||  
> yathāparādhaṃ vipraṃ tu vikarmāṇy api kārayet |  
> rājaduṣṭāni bhāṣeta daṇḍo nirviṣayaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
> avadhyā brāhmaṇā gāvo loke ‘smin vaidikī śrutiḥ |

‘**daṇḍo virviṣayaḥ’** iti | viṣayoddeśān niṣkrāntaḥ kāryaḥ sa eva daṇḍa ity arthaḥ |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.231] |

> yaḥ sāhasaṃ kārayati sa dāpyo dviguṇaṃ damam |  
> yaś caivam uktvāhaṃ dātā kārayet sa caturguṇam ||

**[574]** ‘**ahaṃ dātā’** iti | ‘ahaṃ tubhyaṃ dhanaṃ dāsyāmi tvaṃ kuru’ ity abhidhāya, yaḥ kārayati sa caturguṇaṃ daṇḍya ity arthaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [832–34] |

> ārambhakṛt sahāyaś ca tathā mārgānudeśakaḥ |  
> āśrayaḥ śastradātā ca bhaktadātā vikarmiṇām ||  
> yuddhopadeśakaś caiva tadvināśapradarśakaḥ |  
> upekṣako ‘niyuktaś ca doṣavaktānumodakaḥ ||  
> aniṣeddhā kṣamo yaḥ syāt sarve tatkāryakāriṇaḥ |  
> yathāśaktyanurūpaṃ tu daṇḍam eṣāṃ prakalpayet ||

‘**tadvināśapradarśakaḥ’** tadvināśopāyopadeśakaḥ | ‘**aniyuktaś ca doṣavaktā’** aniyukto rājñāniyukto yo doṣaṃ vadati |

nāradaḥ [4.245–46] |

> ayuktaṃ sāhasaṃ kṛtvā pratyāsattiṃ bhajeta yaḥ |  
> brūyāt svayaṃ vā sadasi tasyāpi vinayaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
> gūhamānas tu dauḥśīlyād yadi pāpaḥ sa jīvati |  
> sabhyāś cāsya na tuṣyanti tīvro daṇḍaś ca pātyate ||

**[575]**

**71 — (ka) atha ghātakānveṣaṇam**

tatra yājñavalkyaḥ [2.280–81] |

> avijñātahatasyāśu kalahaṃ sutabāndhavāḥ |  
> praṣṭavyā yoṣitaś cāsya parapuṃsi ratāḥ pṛthak ||  
> strīdravyavṛttikāmo vā kena vāyaṃ gataḥ saha |  
> tatpradeśasamāsannaṃ pṛcched vāpi janaṃ śanaiḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [23.21, 23–25] |

> hataḥ saṃdṛśyate yatra ghātakas tu na dṛśyate |  
> pūrvavairānumānena jñātavyaḥ sa mahībhujā ||  
> prātiveśyānveśyau ca tasya mitrāribāndhavāḥ |  
> praṣṭavyā rājapuruṣaiḥ sāmādibhir upakramaiḥ ||  
> vijñeyo ‘sādhusaṃsargāc cihnair hoḍhena vā naraiḥ |  
> eṣoditā ghātakānāṃ taskarāṇāṃ ca bhāvanā ||  
> gṛhītaḥ śaṅkayā yas tu na tat kāryaṃ prapadyate |  
> śapathaiḥ sa viśoddhavyaḥ sarvavādeṣv ayaṃ vidhiḥ ||

vyāsaḥ |

> jñātvā tu ghātakaṃ samyak sasahāyaṃ sabāndhavam |  
> hanyāc citrair vadhopāyair udvejanakarair nṛpaḥ ||

**[576]** bṛhaspatiḥ [23.26] |

> divyair viśuddho mocyaḥ syād aśuddho vadham arhati |  
> nigrahānugrahād rājñaḥ kīrtir dharmaś ca vardhate ||

**iti sāhasaparva**

**[577]**

## 72 strīsaṃgrahaṇam
atha strīsaṃgrahaṇam

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ [24.1–5] |

> pāruṣyaṃ dvividhaṃ proktaṃ sāhasaṃ ca dvilakṣaṇam |  
> pāpamūlaṃ saṃgrahaṇaṃ triprakāraṃ nibodhata ||  
> balopadhikṛte dve tu tṛtīyam anurāgajam |  
> tat punas trividhaṃ proktaṃ prathamaṃ madhyam uttamam ||  
> anicchantyā yat kriyate suptonmattapramattayā |  
> pralapantyā vā rahasi balātkārakṛtaṃ tu tat ||  
> chadmanā gṛham ānīya datvā vā madyakārmaṇam |  
> saṃyogaḥ kriyate yasyās tad upādhikṛtaṃ viduḥ ||  
> anyonyacakṣūrāgeṇa dūtīsaṃpreṣaṇena ca |  
> kṛtaṃ rūpārthalobhena jñeyaṃ tad anurāgajam ||

vyāsaḥ |

> saṃgrahas trividhaḥ proktaḥ prathamo madhyamas tathā |  
> uttamaś ceti śāstreṣu tasyoktaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ pṛthak ||  
> adeśakālasaṃbhāṣā araṇye ca parastriyā |  
> apāṅgaprekṣaṇaṃ hāsyaṃ pūrvasaṃgrahaṇaṃ smṛtam ||

**[578]** bṛhaspatiḥ [24.6] |

> apāṅgaprekṣaṇaṃ hāsyaṃ dūtīsaṃpreṣaṇaṃ tathā |  
> sparśo bhūṣaṇavastrāṇāṃ prathamaḥ saṃgrahaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

nāradaḥ [15.63] |

> nadīnāṃ saṃgame tīrtheṣv ārāmeṣu vaneṣu ca |  
> strīpuṃsau yat sameyātāṃ tac ca saṃgrahaṇaṃ smṛtam ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [24.10] |

> preṣaṇaṃ gandhamālyānāṃ phalamadyānnavasasām |  
> saṃbhāṣaṇaṃ ca rahasi madhyamaṃ saṃgrahaṃ viduḥ ||

vyāsaḥ |

> preṣaṇaṃ gandhamālyānāṃ dhūpabhūṣaṇavāsasām |  
> pralobhanaṃ cānnapānair madhyamaḥ saṃgrahaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [24.8] |

> ekaśayyāsanaṃ krīḍā cumbanāliṅganaṃ tathā |  
> etat saṃgrahaṇaṃ proktam uttamaṃ śāstravedibhiḥ ||

**[579]** vyāsaḥ |

> śayyāsane vivikte tu parasparam upāśrayaḥ |  
> keśākeśigrahaś caiva jñeya uttamasaṃgrahaḥ ||

nārado manuś cādyayoḥ |

> upakārakriyā keliḥ sparśo bhūṣaṇavāsasām |  
> saha śayyāsanaṃ caiva sarvasaṃgrahaṇaṃ smṛtam ||  
> striyaṃ spṛśed adeśe yaḥ spṛṣṭo vā marṣayet tayā |  
> parasparasyānumate sarvaṃ saṃgrahaṇaṃ smṛtam ||

nāradaḥ [15.39, 37] |

> darpād vā yadi vā mohāc chalāghayā vā svayaṃ vadet |  
> pūrvaṃ mayeyaṃ bhukteti tac ca saṃgrahaṇaṃ smṛtam ||  
> pāṇau yaś ca nigṛhṇīyād veṇyāṃ vastrāñ cale ‘pi vā |  
> tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti vā brūyāt sarvaṃ samgrahaṇaṃ smṛtam ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.283–84] |

> pumān saṃgrahaṇe grāhyaḥ keśākeśi parastriyā |  
> sadyo vā kāmajaiś cihnaiḥ pratipattau dvayos tathā ||

**[580]** > nīvīstanaprāvaraṇam ūrukeśāvamarśanam |  
> adeśakālasaṃbhāṣaṃ sahāvasthānam eva ca ||

‘**sahāvasthānam’** ityādiṣu kurvāṇa iti śeṣaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ |

> yāni karmāṇy abhilaṣan pumān vai kurute kvacit |  
> ārambhās te tu nirdiṣṭā garhitāḥ kāmasādhakāḥ ||  
> dūtopacārayuktaś ced avelāsthānasṃsthitaḥ |  
> kaṇṭhakeśāmbaragrāhī karṇanāsākarādiṣu ||  
> ekasthānāsanāhāraḥ saṃgraho navadhā smṛtaḥ |  
> na grāhyo hy anyathākārī grāhako daṇḍam arhati ||  
> garbhapāto nakhānāṃ ca darśanaṃ garbhadhāraṇam |  
> dhāraṇaṃ paravastrāṇām alaṅkārāyudhasya ca ||  
> ebhiś cihnaiḥ sadā jñeyā vyabhicāraratāḥ striyaḥ |  
> gandhamālyāmbaraiś cāpi lekhyasaṃpreṣaṇais tathā ||  
> grāhakaṃ sarvam eva syād ārambhakaraṇaṃ hi tat |  
> asmād akāryasaṃsargād grahaṃ saṃgrahaṇaṃ viduḥ ||

**[581]** > kāmī tu saṃsthito yatra ārambhe kāmasādhake |  
> tat tasmād grahaṇaṃ tasya prāhuḥ saṃgrahaṇaṃ yataḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [24.11] |

> trayāṇām api caiteṣāṃ prathamo madhya uttamaḥ |  
> vinayaḥ kalpanīyaḥ syād adhiko draviṇādhike ||

manuḥ [8.358] |

> parasya patnyā puruṣaḥ saṃbhāṣaṃ yojayan rahaḥ |  
> pūrvam ākṣārito doṣaiḥ prāpnuyāt pūrvasāhasam ||

pūrvam eva ‘**doṣaiḥ’** tatstrīprārthanādibhiḥ | ‘**ākṣāritaḥ’** abhiśastaḥ |

āpastambaḥ [2.26.18–19]: “abuddhipūrvam alaṃkṛto yuvā paradāram anupraviśan kumārīṃ vā vācā bādhyaḥ | buddhipūrvaṃ tu [duṣṭabhāvo] daṇḍyaḥ” |

matsyapurāṇe [227.119–20, 125–26] |

> bhikṣuko ‘py atha vā nārī yo ‘pi syāt tu kuśīlavaḥ |  
> praviśet pratiṣiddhas tu prāpnuyād dviśataṃ damam ||  
> yas tu saṃcārakas tatra puruṣaḥ sa tathā bhavet |  
> pāradārikavad daṇḍyo yaś ca syād avakāśadaḥ ||

manuḥ [8.355] |

> yas tv anākṣāritaḥ pūrvam abhibhāṣeta kāraṇāt |  
> na doṣaṃ prāpnuyāt kiṃcin na hi tasya vyatikramaḥ ||

**[582]** nāradaḥ [15.67] |

> nāthavatyā paragṛhe saṃyuktasya striyā saha |  
> dṛṣṭaṃ saṃgrahaṇaṃ tajjñair nāgatāyāḥ svayaṃ gṛhe ||

abhigamanānuvṛttau kātyāyanaḥ |

> ato ‘nyena prakāreṇa pravṛttau grahaṇaṃ bhavet |  
> svayam evāgatāyāṃ tu puṃgṛhe na tu doṣabhāk ||

nārada-kātyāyanau [nā. 15.61] |

> aduṣṭatyaktadārasya klībasyākṣamakasya ca |  
> svecchānupeyuṣo dārān na doṣaḥ sāhase bhavet ||

asyārthaḥ — aduṣṭāḥ praduṣṭās tyaktāḥ svadārā yena tasya | duṣṭān dārān [tathā] klībākṣamayor dārān dārāṇām evecchayopagacchan na daṇḍanīya iti |

manuḥ [8.360–61] |

> bhikṣukā vandinaś caiva dīkṣitāḥ kāravas tathā |  
> saṃbhāṣaṇaṃ gṛhe strībhiḥ kuryur aprativāritāḥ ||>   
> na bhāṣaṇaṃ parastrībhiḥ pratiṣiddhaḥ samācaret |  
> niṣiddho bhāṣamāṇas tu suvarṇaṃ daṇḍam arhati ||

**[583]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.285] |

> strī niṣedhe śataṃ daṇḍyo dviśataṃ tu damaṃ pumān |  
> pratiṣedhe tayor daṇḍo yathā saṃgrahaṇe tathā ||

asyārthaḥ — strī patipitrādibhiḥ saṃbhāṣaṇādiniṣedhe kṛte sati pravartate yadi, tadā paṇaśataṃ daṇḍyā | puruṣaḥ punar evaṃ niṣiddhe pravartamāno dviśataṃ daṇḍyaḥ | dvayos tu strīpuṃsayoḥ pratiṣiddhe pravartamānayoḥ saṃbhāṣaṇe varṇānusāreṇa yo daṇḍaḥ sa eva daṇḍa iti |

manuḥ [8.362–63] |

> naiṣa cāraṇadāreṣu vidhir nātmopajīviṣu |  
> sajjayanti hi te nārīr nirgūḍhāś cārayanti ca ||  
> kiṃcid eva tu dāpyaḥ syāt saṃbhāṣāṃ tābhir ācaran |  
> praiṣyāsu caikabhaktāsu rahaḥ pravrajitāsu ca ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: “sarveṣāṃ svadāraniyamaḥ svakarmapratipattiś ca dharmaḥ | yena yenāṅgenāparādhaṃ kuryāt tad evāsya chettavyam | aṣṭasahasraṃ vā daṇḍaḥ | anyatra brāhmaṇāt | adaṇḍyo hi brāhmaṇaḥ |

**[584]** manuḥ [8.352–53, 359] |

> paradārābhimarśeṣu pravṛttān nṝn mahīpatiḥ |  
> udvejanakarair daṇḍaiś cihnayitvā pravāsayet ||  
> tatsamuttho hi lokasya jāyate varṇasaṃkaraḥ |  
> yena mūlaharo ‘dharmaḥ sarvanāśāya kalpate ||  
> abrāhmaṇaḥ saṃgrahaṇe prāṇāntaṃ daṇḍam arhati |  
> caturṇām api varṇānāṃ dārā rakṣyatamāḥ smṛtāḥ ||

‘**abrāhmaṇaḥ saṃgrahaṇe’** ity atra brāhmaṇyā iti śeṣaḥ |

**[585]**

**72 — (ka) athābhigamanadaṇḍāḥ**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ [24.13] |

> sahasā kāmayed yas tu dhanaṃ tasyākhilaṃ haret |  
> utkṛtya liṅgavṛṣaṇau bhrāmayed gardabhena tu ||

āpastambaḥ [2.26.10]: “saṃnipāte vṛtte śiśnacchedanaṃ savṛṣaṇasya” |

kātyāyanaḥ [830] |

> strīṣu vṛttopabhogaḥ syāt prasahya puruṣo yadā |  
> vadhas tatra pravarteta kāryātikramaṇaṃ hi tat ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [24.14–15] |

> chadmanā kāmayed yas tu tasya sarvaharo damaḥ |  
> aṅkayitvā bhagāṅkena purān nirvāsayet tataḥ ||  
> damo ‘ntimaḥ samāyāṃ tu hīnāyām ardhikas tataḥ |  
> puṃsaḥ kāryo ‘dhikāyāṃ tu gamane saṃpramāpaṇam ||

**[586]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.286] |

> sajātāv uttamo daṇḍa ānulomye tu madhyamaḥ |  
> prātilomye vadhaḥ puṃso nāryāḥ karṇādikartanam ||

viṣṇuḥ [5.40–43]: “pārajāyī savarṇāgamane tūttamasāhasaṃ daṇḍyaḥ | hīnavarṇāgamane madhyamam | gogamane ca | antyāgamane ca vadhyaḥ | uttamāgamane ca” |

śaṅkhalikhitau: “aniveditapraveśe strīgṛheṣu tatrottamam uttamāyām | viparyaye madhyamasāhasam | pratilomaikāntarāvaskandane sarvasvaṃ vadho vā | viparyaye saṃnirodhaḥ sarvasvaṃ ca” |

asyārthaḥ — anivedya strīgṛhaṃ praviśya uttamāṃ brāhmaṇādistriyam abhigacchato brāhmaṇasyottamasāhaso daṇḍaḥ | ‘**viparyaye’** tu brāhmaṇasya kṣatriyādistrīgamane madhyamasāhaso daṇḍaḥ | pratilomasya śūdrāder ekāntaritadvijātistrīgamane vadhaḥ sarvasvāpahārasahito daṇḍaḥ | **vā**śabdaḥ samuccaye | ‘āryastryabhigamane liṅgoddhāraḥ svaharaṇaṃ ca | goptā ced vadho ‘dhikaḥ’ iti gautamavacanāt [12.2–3] | ‘**viparyaye saṃnirodhaḥ’** brāhmaṇasyāguptapatnīgamane vaiśyasya saṃvatsaraṃ bandhanāgāre tirohitasya sarvasvāpahāro daṇḍaḥ — ‘vaiśyaḥ sarvasvadaṇḍaḥ syāt saṃvatsaranirodhataḥ’ iti manuvacanāt [8.375] iti |

**[587]** darpādhikāre manuḥ [8.372] |

> pumāṃsaṃ dāhayet pāpaṃ śayane tapta āyase |  
> abhyādadhyuś ca kāṣṭhāni tatra dahyeta pāpakṛt ||

nāradaḥ [15.73–75] |

> mātā mātṛṣvasā śvaśrūr mātulānī pitṛṣvasā |  
> pitṛvyasakhiśiṣyastrī bhaginī tatsakhī snuṣā ||  
> duhitācāryabhāryā ca sagotrā śaraṇāgatā |  
> rājñī pravrajitā dhātrī sādhvī varṇottamā ca yā ||  
> āsām anyatamāṃ gatvā gurutalpaga ucyate |  
> śiśnasyotkartanaṃ tatra nānyo daṇḍo vidhīyate ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [3.232–33] |

> pituḥ svasāraṃ matuś ca mātulānīṃ snuṣām api |  
> mātuḥ spatnīṃ bhaginīm ācāryatanayāṃ tathā ||  
> ācāryapatnīṃ svasutāṃ gacchaṃs tu gurutalpagaḥ |  
> chitvā liṅgaṃ vadhas tasya sakāmāyāḥ striyās tathā ||

**[588]** vyāsaḥ |

> guptāyāḥ saṃgrahe daṇḍo yathoktaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ |  
> icchantyām āgatāyāṃ tu gacchato ‘rdhaṃ damaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

manuḥ [8.378–79, 382–83] |

> sahasraṃ brāhmaṇo daṇḍyo guptāṃ viprāṃ balād vrajan |  
> śatāni pañca daṇḍyaḥ syād icchantyā saha saṃgataḥ ||  
> mauṇḍyaṃ prāṇāntiko daṇḍo brāhmaṇasya vidhīyate |  
> itareṣāṃ tu varṇānāṃ daṇḍaḥ prāṇāntiko bhavet ||  
> vaiśyaś cet kṣatriyāṃ guptāṃ vaiśyāṃ vā kṣatriyo vrajet |  
> yo brāhmaṇyām aguptāyāṃ tatsamaṃ daṇḍam arhataḥ ||  
> sahasraṃ brāhmaṇo daṇḍaṃ dāpyo gupte tu te vrajan |  
> śūdrāyāṃ kṣatriyaviśoḥ sāhasro vai bhaved damaḥ ||

āpastambaḥ [2.27.8]: “nāśya āryaḥ śūdrāyām” |

‘**āryo’** brāhmaṇādiḥ, ‘**śūdrāyām’** ananyapūrvāyāṃ retaḥ siktvā, ‘**nāśyo’** viṣayān nirvāsya ity arthaḥ |

**[589]** manuḥ [8.385, 373] |

> agupte kṣatriyāvaiśye śūdrāṃ vā brāhmaṇo vrajan |  
> śatāni pañca paṇḍyaḥ syāt sahasraṃ tv antyajastriyam ||  
> saṃvatsarābhiśastasya duṣṭasya dviguṇo damaḥ |  
> vrātyayā saha saṃvāsre cāṇḍālyā tāvad eva tu ||

‘saṃvatsarābhiśastasya duṣṭasya’ iti — saṃvatsaram anenopabhuktā parastrīti yasyābhiśāpaḥ ‘saṃvatsarābhiśastaḥ’, tasya saṃvatsaram upabhuktāyāṃ yo daṇḍa uktaḥ sa dviguṇaḥ syād ity arthaḥ | ‘vrātyā’ atyantadurācārā vadhabandhopajīviprabhṛtayaḥ saptavidhāḥ | ‘vrātyapratipādakaninditakarmācārā ninditā’ ityādihārītavacanānusārāt |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.294] |

> antyābhigamane tv aṅkyaḥ kabandhena pravāsayet |  
> śūdras tathāntya eva syād antyasyāryāgame vadhaḥ ||

‘aṅkyaḥ kabandhena’ aśiraḥskandhanaraśarīrākāreṇāṅkayitvā |

**[590] **baudhāyanaḥ [2.3.53, 2.4.1–3]: “śūdraṃ kaṭāgninā dahet | athāpy udāharanti | abrāhmaṇasya śārīro daṇḍaḥ |

> abrāhmaṇasya śārīro daṇḍaḥ saṃgrahaṇe bhavet |  
> sarveṣām eva varṇānāṃ dārā rakṣyatamā dhanāt ||  
> na tu cāraṇadāreṣu na raṅgāvatare vadhaḥ |  
> saṃsarjayanti tā hy etān niguptāṃś cālayanty api ||

śūdrasyānuvṛttau gautamaḥ [12.2–3]: “āryastryabhigamane liṅgoddhāraḥ sarvasvaharaṇaṃ ca | goptā ved vadho ‘dhikaḥ” |

āpastambaḥ [2.27.9–10]: “vadhaḥ śūdra āryāyām | dāraṃ cāsya karśayet” |

‘brāhmaṇī vṛṣalaṃ seveta’ ity anuvṛttau yamaḥ |

> śūdraṃ tu ghātayed rājā śayane tapa āyase |  
> dahet pāpakṛtaṃ tatra kāṣṭhaiḥ parṇais tṛṇais tathā ||

manuḥ [8.374–77] |

> śūdro guptam aguptaṃ vā daijātaṃ varṇam āvasan |  
> aguptam aṅgasarvasvī gupte sarveṇa hīyate ||

**[591]** > vaiśyaḥ sarvasvadaṇḍyaḥ syāt saṃvatsaranirodhataḥ |  
> sahasraṃ kṣatriyo daṇḍyo mauṇḍyaṃ mūtreṇa cārhati ||  
> brāhmaṇīṃ yady aguptāṃ tu seveyātām iti sthitiḥ |  
> vaiśyaṃ pañcaśataṃ kuryāt kṣatriyaṃ tu sahasriṇam ||  
> ubhāv api tu tāv eva brāhmaṇyā guptayā saha |  
> viplutau śūdravad daṇḍyau dagdhavyau vā kaṭāgninā ||

‘dvaitātaṃ varṇam āvasan’ dvijātistriyam abhigacchann ity arthaḥ | ‘aguptam’ arakṣitam | ‘aṅgasarvasvī’ aṅgasarvasvasahitaḥ, ‘hīyate’ tenāṅgena yenāṅgenāparāddham, sarvasvena ca hīyata ity arthaḥ | rakṣitāṃ tu vrajan ‘sarveṇa’ aṅgena hīyata ity arthaḥ |

tathā [8.384] |

> kṣatriyāyām aguptāyāṃ vaiśye pañcaśato damaḥ |  
> mūtreṇa mauṇḍyam icchet tu kṣatriyo daṇḍam eva vā ||

hārītaḥ: “śreyasaḥ śayanaśāyinaṃ rājā badhvā śvabhiḥ khādayet | kāṣṭhaiś caināṃ dāhayet” |

‘**śreyasaḥ’** brāhmaṇādes tūttamasya | ‘**śayanaśāyinam’** strīgāminam | ‘**enām’** uttamastriyam |

gautamaḥ [23.14–16]: “śvabhiḥ khādayed rājā nihīnavarṇagamane striyam prakāśam | pumāṃsaṃ ghātayet | yathoktaṃ vā” |

**[492]** vasiṣṭhaḥ [21.1–5]: “śūdraś ced brāhmaṇīm abhigacched vīraṇapatrair veṣṭayitvā śūdram agnau prāsyeta | brāhmaṇyāḥ śirasi vāpanaṃ kṛtvā sarpiṣābhyukṣya nagnāṃ kharam āropya mahāpatham anuvrājayet | pūtā bhavatīti vijñāyate | vaiśyaś ced brāhmaṇīm abhigacchel lohitadarbhair veṣṭayitvā vaiśyam agnau prāsyeta | brāhmaṇyāḥ śirasi vāpanaṃ kṛtvā sarpiṣābhyukṣya nagnāṃ kharam āropya mahāpatham anuvrājayet | pūtā bhavatīti vijñāyet | rājanyaś ced brāhmaṇīm abhigachec charapatrair veṣṭayitvā rājanyam agnau prāsyeta | brāhmanyāḥ śirasi vapanaṃ kṛtvā sarpiṣābhyukṣya nagnāṃ khama āropya mahāpatham anuvrājayet | pūtā bhavatīti vijñāyate | evām vaiśyo rājanyāyāṃ maithunam ācaran | śūdras tu rājanyavaiśyayoḥ” |

atha yamaḥ |

> vṛṣalaṃ sevate yā tu brāhmaṇī madamohitā |  
> tāṃ śvabhiḥ khādayed rājā saṃsthāne vadhyaghātinām ||

**[593]** > vaiśyaṃ vā kṣatriyaṃ vāpi brāhmaṇī sevate tu yā |  
> śiraso muṇḍanaṃ tasyāḥ prayāṇaṃ gardabhena tu ||

‘saṃsthāne vadhyaghātinām,’ vadhyān ye ghātayanti caṇḍālādayas teṣāṃ sthāne |

bṛhaspatiḥ [24.16–17] |

> gṛham āgatya yā nārī pralobhya sparśanādinā |  
> kāmayet tatra sā daṇḍyā narasyārdhadamaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
> chinnanāsauṣṭhakarṇāṃ tu paribhrāmyāpsu majjayet |  
> khadeyed vā sārameyaiḥ saṃsthāne bahusaṃsthite ||

‘bahusaṃsthite’ bahavaḥ saṃsthitā yatra catvarādau |

manuḥ [8.371] |

> bhartāraṃ laṅghayed yā tu strī jñātiguṇadarpitā |  
> tāṃ svabhiḥ khādayed rājā saṃsthāne bahusaṃsthite ||

hanyād ity anvṛttau viṣṇuḥ [5.18]: “striyam asaktabhartṛkāṃ tadatikramaṇīṃ ca” |

yājñavalkyaḥ [3.233] |

> liṅgaṃ chittvā badhas tatra sakāmāyāḥ stryās tathā |

**[594]** bṛhaspatiḥ [24.18–19] |

> anicchantī tu yā muktā guptāṃ tāṃ vāseyed gṛhe |  
> malināṅgīm adhaḥśayyāṃ piṇḍamātropajīvinīm ||  
> kārayen niṣkṛtiṃ kṛcchraṃ parākaṃ vā same gatām |  
> hīnavarṇopabhuktā yā tyājyā badhyātha vā bhavet ||

‘**same gatāṃ’** savarṇapuruṣe saṃgatām |

kātyāyanaḥ [488–79] |

> nāsvatantrāḥ striyo grāhyāḥ pumāṃs tatrāparādhyati |  
> prabhuṇā śāsanīyās tā rājā tu puruṣaṃ nayet ||  
> proṣitasvāmikā nārī prāpitā yady abhigrahe |  
> tāvat sā bandhane sthāpyā yāvat pratyāgataḥ prabhuḥ ||

‘**puruṣaṃ nayet’** strīsvāminaṃ puruṣaṃ prāpayed ity arthaḥ |

matsyapurāṇe [227.127–29]

> balāt saṃdūṣayed yas tu parabhāryāṃ naraḥ kvacit |  
> vadhadaṇḍo bhavet tasya nāparādho bhavet striyāḥ ||  
> adravyāṃ mṛtapatnīṃ tu saṃgṛhṇan nāparādhnuyāt |  
> sa tāṃ parigṛhāṇas tu sarvasvaṃ daṇḍam arhati ||

**kṛtyakalpatarau vyavahārakāṇde**

**[abhigamaṇadaṇḍaḥ]**

**[595]**

**72 — (kha) atha kanyādūṣaṇam**

tatra manuḥ [8.364] |

> yo ‘kāmāṃ dūṣayet kanyāṃ sa sadyo vadham arhati |  
> sakāmāṃ dūṣayaṃs tulyo na vadhaṃ prāpnuyān naraḥ ||

matsyapurāṇe [227.124–25] |

> yo ‘kāmāṃ dūṣayet kanyāṃ sa sadyo vadham arhati |  
> sakāmāṃ dūṣayānas tu prāptaḥ paramasāhasam ||

‘saṃnipāte vṛtte’ ity anuvṛttau āpastambaḥ [2.26.21]: “kumāryāṃ tu svāny ādāya nāśyaḥ’ |

manuḥ [8.366] |

> uttamāṃ sevamānas tu jaghanyo vadham arhati |  
> śulkaṃ dadyāt sevamānaḥ samām icchet pitā yadi ||

**[596]** nāradaḥ [15.71–72] |

> kanyāyām asakāmāyāṃ dvyaṅgulasyāvakartanam |  
> uttamāyāṃ vadhas tv eva sarvasvaharaṇaṃ tathā ||  
> sakāmāyāṃ tu kanyāyāṃ savarṇe nāsty atikarmaḥ |  
> kiṃ tv alaṃkṛtya satkṛtya sa evaināṃ samudvahet ||

atha śaṅkhalikhitau: “kanyāyām asakāmāyāṃ dvyaṅgulacchedo daṇḍaś ca | uttamāyāṃ tu vadho jaghanyasya | samānāyāṃ śulkam ābharaṇaṃ dviguṇaṃ ca strīdhanaṃ datvā pratipadyeta kanyām” |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.287–88] |

> alaṃkṛtāṃ haran kanyām uttamāṃ hy anyathādhamam |  
> daṇḍaṃ dadyāt savarṇāsu prātilomye vadhaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
> sakāmāsv anulomāsu na doṣas tv anyathā damaḥ |

**[597]** > dūṣaṇe tu karaccheda uttamāyāṃ vadhas tathā ||

‘**uttamam’** uttamasāhasam | ‘**adhamam’** adhamasāhasam |

manuḥ [8.367–70, 65] |

> abhiṣajya tu yaḥ kanyāṃ kuryād darpeṇa mānavaḥ |  
> tasyāśu kalpyate aṅgulyau daṇḍaṃ cārhati ṣaṭśatam ||  
> sakāmāṃ dūṣayānas tu nāṅgulīcchedam āpnuyāt |  
> dviśataṃ tu damaṃ dāpyaḥ prasaṅgavinivṛttaye ||  
> kanyaiva kanyāṃ yā kuryāt tasyāḥ syād dviśato damaḥ |  
> śulkaṃ ca triguṇaṃ dadyāc chipāś ca prāpnuyād daśa ||  
> yā tu kanyāṃ prakuryāt strī sā sadyo mauṇḍyam arhati |  
> aṅgulyor eva vā chedaṃ khareṇodvahanaṃ tathā ||  
> kanyāṃ bhajantīm utkṛṣṭaṃ na kiṃcid api dāpayet |  
> jaghanyaṃ sevamānāṃ tu saṃyatāṃ vāsayed gṛhe ||

‘**abhiṣajya’** abhibhūya | ‘**kuryāt’** vikuryāt, dūṣayed iti yāvat | ‘**kalpye’** chedye | ‘**śiphā’** atra jaṭārajvādiprahāraḥ |

**[598]**

**72 — (ga) atha bandhakyabhigamanam**

tatra yamaḥ |

> paradāre savarṇāsu daṇḍyāḥ syuḥ pañca kṛṣṇalāḥ |  
> asavarṇāsv ānulomye daṇḍo dvādaśako mataḥ ||

vyāsaḥ |

> bahubhir bhuktapūrvā yā gacched yas tāṃ narādhamaḥ |  
> tasya veśyāvad icchanti daṇḍanaṃ na tu dāravat ||

kātyāyanaḥ [831] |

> kāmārtā svairiṇī yā tu svayam eva prakāmayet |  
> rājādeśena bhoktavyā vikhyāpya janasaṃnidhau ||

nāradaḥ [15.78–79] |

> svairiṇy abrāhmaṇī veśyā dāsī niṣkāsinī ca yā |  
> gamyāḥ syur ānulomyena striyo na pratilomataḥ ||  
> āsv eva tu bhujiṣyāsu doṣaḥ syāt paradāravat |  
> gamyā api hi nopeyā yatas tāḥ saparigrahāḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.290] |

> avaruddhāsu dāsīṣu bhujiṣyāsu tathaiva ca |  
> gamyāsv api pumān dāpyaḥ pañcāśatpaṇikaṃ damam ||

**[599]** vyāsaḥ |

> paroparuddhāgamane pañcāśatpaṇiko damaḥ |  
> prasahya veśyāgamane daṇḍo daśapaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.291] |

> prasahya dāsyā gamane daṇḍo daśapaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ |  
> bahūnāṃ yady akākāmāsau caturviṃśatikaḥ pṛthak ||

tathā [2.293] |

> paśūn gacchan śataṃ dāpyo hīnāṃ gāṃ caiva madhyamam |

nāradaḥ [15.76] |

> paśuyonāv atikrāman vineyaḥ sa damaṃ śatam |  
> madhyamaṃ sāhasaṃ goṣu tad evāntyāvasāyiṣu ||

matsyapurāṇe [227.143–44] |

> tiryagyonau tu govarjaṃ maithunaṃ yo viṣevate |  
> sa paṇaṃ prāpnuyād daṇḍaṃ tasyāś ca yavasodakam ||

**[600]** > suvarṇaṃ tu bhaved daṇḍo gāṃ vrajan manujottamaḥ |  
> veśyāgāmī dvijo daṇḍyo veśyāśulkasamaṃ paṇam ||

nāradaḥ [15.77] |

> agamyāgāminaḥ śāsti daṇḍo rājñā prakīrtitaḥ |  
> prāyaścittavidhānaṃ tu pāpānāṃ syād viśodhanam ||

manuḥ [8.386–87] |

> yasya stenaḥ pure nāsti nānyastrīgo na duṣṭavāk |  
> na sāhasikadaṇdaghnau sa rājā śakralokabhāk ||  
> eteṣāṃ nigraho rājñaḥ pañcānāṃ viṣaye svake |  
> sāmrājyakṛt sajātyeṣu loke caiva yaśaskaraḥ ||

yamaḥ |

> duṣṭāḥ sāhasikāś caṇḍāḥ kitavā vañcakās tathā |  
> yasya rāṣṭre na santīha sa rājā śakralokabhāk ||

**iti strīsaṃgrahaparva |**

**[601]**

## 73 strīpuṃyogaḥ
atha strīpuṃyogaḥ

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ [25.1] |

> etat saṃgrahaṇasyoktaṃ vidhānaṃ vinayaṃ tathā |  
> strīpuṃsavartanopāyaḥ śrūyatāṃ gadato mama ||

nāradaḥ [15.2] |

> vivāhādividhiḥ strīṇāṃ yatra puṃsāṃ ca kīrtyate |  
> strīpuṃsayoga ity etad vivādapadam ucyate ||

tatra vivāhavidhiḥ vivāhakāṇḍe varṇitaḥ \

**atha strīpuṃsadharmāḥ**

tatra ‘puruṣasya striyāṃ vṛttiḥ’ ity atra —

manuḥ [9.1–2] |

> puruṣasya striyāś caiva dharmye vartmani tiṣṭhatoḥ |  
> saṃyoge viprayoge ca darmān vakṣyāmi śāsvatān ||  
> asvatantrāḥ striyaḥ kāryāḥ puruṣaiḥ svair divāniśam |  
> viṣayeṣu ca sajjantyaḥ saṃsthāpyāś cātmano vaśe ||

**[602]** nāradaḥ [16.30] |

> svātantryād vipraṇaśyanti kule jātā api striyaḥ |  
> asvātantryam atas tāsāṃ prajāpatir akalpayat ||

manuḥ [9.3] |

> pitā rakṣati kaumāre bhartā rakṣati yauvane |  
> putrās tu sthavire bhāve na strī svātantryam arhati ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [1.85] |

> rakṣet kanyāṃ pitā vinnāṃ patiḥ putrās tu vārdhike |  
> abhāve jñātayas teṣāṃ svātantryaṃ na kvacit striyāḥ ||

hārītaḥ: “ekavrataskannabhāvāt parendriyopahatatvāc ca duṣṭāḥ kulasaṅkarakāruṇyo bhavanti | jīvati jārajaḥ kuṇḍo mṛte bhartari golakaḥ | tasmād retopaghātāj jāyāṃ rakṣet | jāyānāśe kulanāśaḥ | kulanāśe tantunāśaḥ | tantunāśe devapitṛyajñanāśaḥ | dharmanāśe ātmanāśaḥ | ātmanāśe sarvanāśaḥ” |

‘**ekavrataskannabhāvād’** iti — eka eva patir iti yo ‘yaṃ vrataniyamaḥ tataḥ skhalanād ity arthaḥ | ‘**tantuḥ’** putrapautradisantatiḥ |

**[603]** manuḥ [9.5–7] |

> sūkṣmebhyo ‘pi prasaṅgebhyaḥ striyo rakṣyāḥ prayatnataḥ |  
> dvayor hi kulayoḥ śokam āvaheyur arakṣitāḥ ||  
> imaṃ hi sarvavarṇānāṃ paśyanto dharmam uttamam |  
> yatante rakṣituṃ bhāryāṃ bhartāro durbalā api ||  
> svāṃ prasūtiṃ caritraṃ ca kulam ātmānam eva ca |  
> svadharmaṃ hi prayatnena jāyāṃ rakṣan hi rakṣati ||

varṇasaṃkarānantaraṃ paiṭhīnasiḥ: “tasmād rakṣet bhāryāṃ sarvataḥ | mā sma saṃkaro bhavatv ity āha |

> apramattā rakṣata tantum enaṃ mā vaḥ kṣetre parabījāny avāpsuḥ |  
> bhāryāṃ rakṣata kaumārīṃ bibhyataḥ pararetasaḥ” ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [25.2] |

> sūkṣmebhyo ‘pi prasaṅgebhyo nivāryā strī svabandhubhiḥ |  
> śvaśrvādibhir gurustrībhiḥ pālanīyā divāniśam ||

nāradaḥ [16.28–29] |

> mṛte bhartary aputrāyāḥ patipakṣaḥ prabhuḥ striyāḥ |  
> viniyogātmarakṣāsu bharaṇe tu sa īśvaraḥ ||

**[604]**  
> parikṣīṇe patikule nirmanuṣye nirāśraye |  
> tatsapiṇḍeṣu cāsatsu pitṛpakṣaḥ prabhuḥ striyāḥ ||  
> pakṣadvayāvasāne tu rājā bhartā smṛtaḥ striyāḥ |  
> sa tasyā rakṣaṇaṃ kuryān nigṛhṇīyāt pathaś cyutām ||

manuḥ [9.4] |

> kāle ‘dātā pitā vācyo vācyaś cānupayan patiḥ |  
> mṛte bhartari putras tu vācyo mātur arakṣitā ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [25.5] |

> aprayacchan pitā kāle patiś cānupayann ṛtau |  
> putraś cābhaktado mātur garhyā daṇḍyāś ca dharmataḥ ||

manuḥ [9.14–15, 17–21, 16] |

> naitā rūpaṃ parīkṣante nāsāṃ vayasi niścayaḥ |  
> virūpaṃ rūpavantaṃ vā pumān ity eva bhuñjate ||  
> pauṃścalyāc calacittatvān naisnehyāc ca svabhāvataḥ |  
> rakṣitā yatnato ‘pīha bhartṛṣv etā vikurvate ||  
> śayyāsanam alaṃkāraṃ kāmaṃ krodham anārjavam |  
> drohabhāvaṃ kucaryāṃ ca strībhyo manur akalpayat ||

**[605]**  
> nāsti strīṇāṃ kriyā mantrair iti dharma vyavasthitaḥ |  
> nirindriyā hy amantrāś ca striyo ‘nṛtam iti sthitiḥ ||  
> tathā hi śrutayo bahvyo nigītā nigameṣv api |  
> svālakṣaṇyaparīkṣārthaṃ tāsāṃ śṛṇuta niṣkṛtim ||  
> yan me mātā pralulubhe vicaranty apativratā |  
> tan me retaḥ pitā vṛṅktām ity asyaitan nidarśanam ||  
> dhyāyaty aniṣṭaṃ yat kiṃcit pāṇigrāhasya cetasā |  
> tasyaiṣa vyabhicārasya nihnavaḥ samyag ucyate ||  
> evaṃ svabhāvaṃ jñātvāsāṃ prajāpatinisargajam |  
> paramaṃ yatnam ātiṣṭhet puruṣo rakṣaṇaṃ prati ||

**[606]** ‘**nirindriyā’** nirvīryā dhairyaprajñābalādirahitā ity arthaḥ | ‘**striyo ‘nṛtam’** iti prāyaśo ‘nṛtavadanaśīlatvād ucyate | ‘**śrutayaḥ’** śrutivākyāni | ‘**nigameṣu’** vedeṣu | ‘**svālakṣaṇyam’** svarūpam | **tāsām** ityādi — tāsāṃ śrutīnāṃ madhye yā niṣkṛtirūpā [mānasa]vyabhicāraprāyaścittabhūtāḥ, tāḥ śrutīḥ ‘**śṛṇuta’** strīsvabhāvajānārtham ity arthaḥ | ‘**tan me retaḥ pitā vṛṅktām’** iti, tan mātrā parapuruṣalobhajanitaṃ pāpaṃ pituḥ reto ‘panudatu iti | piteti ṣaṣṭhyarthe prathamā | ‘**prajāpatinisragajam’** prajāpatir hiraṇyagarbhaḥ, tadīyam anisarge sṛṣṭikāle jātam |

dakṣaḥ |

> jalaukavat striyaḥ sarvā bhūṣaṇācchādanāśanaiḥ |  
> subhṛtāp kṛtā nityaṃ puruṣaṃ hy apakarṣati ||  
> jalaukā raktam ādatte kevalaṃ sā tapasvinī |  
> itarā tu dhanaṃ vittaṃ māṃsaṃ vīryaṃ balaṃ sukham ||  
> sāśaṅkā bālabhāve tu yauvane ‘bhimukhī bhavet |  
> tṛṇavan manyate nārī vṛddhabhāve svakaṃ patim ||  
> svākāmye vartamānā sā snehān na ca nivaritā |  
> apathyā tu bhavet paścād yathā vyādhir upekṣitaḥ ||

‘**svākāmye’** svecchāyām |

**[607]** manuḥ [9.9] |

> yādṛśaṃ bhajate hi strī sūte ‘patyaṃ tathāvidham |  
> tasmāt prajāviśuddhyarthaṃ striyo rakṣet prayatnataḥ ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: “yasmin bhāvo ‘rpitaḥ strīṇām ārtave tādṛśaṃ putraṃ janayanti | yathā nīlavṛṣeṇa nīlavatsaprabhavaḥ | śvetena śveta eva jāyate | evaṃ yonir eva balavatī | yasmād varṇāḥ saṃkīryante” |

rāmāyaṇe |

> naivāṅganānāṃ dayito nāpi dveṣyo ‘sti kaścana |  
> sarvam evāvalambante latā gahanajā iva ||

mahābhārate |

> kulīnā rūpavatyaś ca nāthavatyaś ca yoṣitaḥ |  
> na maryādāsu tiṣṭhanti sa doṣaḥ strīṣu nārada ||  
> anarthitvān manuṣyāṇāṃ bhayāt parijanasya ca |  
> maryādāyām amaryādāḥ striyas tiṣṭhanti bhartṛṣu ||  
> yauvane vartamānānāṃ mṛṣṭābharaṇavāsasām |  
> nārīṇāṃ svairavṛttīnāṃ spṛhayanti kulastriyaḥ ||  
> yadi puṃsāṃ gatir brahman kathaṃcin nopapadyate |  
> apy anyonyaṃ pravartante na ca tiṣṭhanti bhartṛṣu ||

**[608]** > alābhāt puruṣāṇāṃ hi bhayāt parijanasya ca |  
> vadhabandhabayāc caiva svayaṃ guptā bhavanti tāḥ ||  
> nāgnis tṛpyati kāṣṭhānāṃ nāpagānāṃ mahodadhiḥ |  
> nāntakaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ na puṃsāṃ vāmalocanā ||  
> kāmānām api dātāraṃ dātāraṃ mānasāntvayoḥ |  
> rakṣitāraṃ na mṛṣyanti yatnatas tāḥ striyaḥ sadā ||

**73 — (ka) atha rakṣāvidhiḥ**

tatra manuḥ [9.10–12] |

> na kaścid yoṣitaḥ śaktaḥ prasahya parirakṣitum |  
> etair upāyayogais tu śakyās tāḥ parirakṣitum ||  
> arthasya saṃgrahe caināṃ vyaye caiva niyojayet |  
> śauce dharme ‘nnapaktyāṃ ca pārināhyasya cekṣaṇe ||  
> arakṣitā gṛhe ruddhāḥ puruṣair āptakāribhiḥ |  
> ātmānam ātmanā yās tu rakṣeyus tāḥ surakṣitāḥ ||

‘pāriṇāhyam’ kuṇḍalakaṭakādi |

bṛhaspatiḥ [25.6] |

> āyavyaye ‘rthasaṃskāre gṛhopaskararakṣaṇe |  
> śaucāgnikārye saṃyojyā rakṣā strīṇām iyaṃ smṛtā ||

**[609]** manuḥ [9.22–24, 26–28, 8] |

> yādṛgguṇena bhartrā strī saṃyujyeta yathāvidhi |  
> tādṛgguṇā sā bhavati samudreṇeva nimnagā ||  
> akṣamālā vasiṣṭhena saṃyuktādhamayonijā |  
> śāraṅgī mandapālena jagāmābhyarhaṇīyatām ||  
> etāśā cānyāś ca loke ‘sminn apakṛṣṭaprasūtayaḥ |  
> utkarṣaṃ yoṣitaś cāptāḥ svaiḥ svair bhartṛguṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ ||  
> prajanārthā mahābhāgā pūjārhā gṛhadīptayaḥ |  
> śriyaḥ striyaś ca geheṣu na viśeṣo ‘sti kaścana ||  
> utpādanam apatyasya jātasya paripālanam |  
> pratyahaṃ lokayātrāyāḥ pratyakṣaṃ strīnibandhanam ||  
> apatyaṃ dharmakāryāṇi śuśrūṣā ratir uttamā |  
> dārādhīnas tathā svargaḥ pitṝṇām ātmanaś ca ha ||  
> patir bhāryāṃ saṃpraviśya garbho bhūtveha jāyate |  
> jāyāyās tad dhi jāyātvaṃ yad asyāṃ jayate punaḥ ||

**[610]** mahābhārate [ānu. 81.15] |

> śriyaḥ etāḥ striyo nāma satkāryā bhūtim icchatā |  
> lālitā nigṛhītā ca strī śrīr bhavati bhārata ||

manuḥ [3.56–59] |

> yatra nāryas tu pūjyante ramante tatra devatāḥ |  
> yatraitās tu pūjyante sarvāś tatrāphalāḥ kriyāḥ ||  
> śocanti jāmayo yatra vinaśyaty āśu tatkulam |  
> na śocanti tu yatraitā vardhate tad dhi sarvadā ||  
> jāmayo yāni gehāni śapanty apratipūjitāḥ |  
> tāni kṛtyāhatānīva vinaśyanti samantataḥ ||  
> tasmād etāḥ sadābhyarcyā bhūṣaṇācchādanāśanaiḥ |  
> bhūtikāmair narair nityaṃ satkāreṇotsaveṣu ca ||

‘**jāmayaḥ’** kulastriyaḥ bhaginīsnuṣādyāḥ |

yājñavalkyaḥ [1.82] |

> bhartṛbhrātṛpitṛjñātiśvaśrūśvaśuradevaraiḥ |  
> bandhubhiś ca striyaḥ pūjyā bhūṣaṇācchādanāśanaiḥ ||

tathā [3.79] |

> dohasasyāpradānena garbho doṣam avāpnuyāt |  
> vairūpyaṃ maraṇaṃ vāpi tasmāt kāryaṃ priyaṃ striyāḥ ||

**[611]** manuḥ [9.74, 95–96] |

> vidhāya vṛttiṃ bhāryāyāḥ pravaset kāryavān naraḥ |  
> avṛttikarṣitā hi strī praduṣyet sthitimaty api ||  
> devadattāṃ patir bhāryāṃ vindate necchayātmanaḥ |  
> tāṃ sādhvīṃ bibhṛyān nityaṃ devānāṃ priyam ācaran ||  
> prajananārthaṃ striyaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ santānārthaṃ ca mānavāḥ |  
> tasmāt sādhāraṇo dharmaḥ śrutau patnyā sahoditaḥ ||

‘**sthitimatī’** kulācārasaṃpattiyuktā | ‘**prajananam’** garbhasaṃgrahaṇam | ‘**santāno’** garbhādhānam |

tathā [9.85–87] |

> yadi svāḥ svāvarāś caiva vinderan yoṣito dvijāḥ |  
> tāsāṃ varṇakrameṇaiva jyaiṣṭhyaṃ pūjā ca veśma ca ||  
> bhartuḥ śarīraśuśrūṣāṃ dharmakāryaṃ ca naityakam |  
> svā caiva kuryāt sarveṣāṃ nānyajātiḥ kathaṃcana ||  
> yas tu tat kārayen mohāt svajātyā sthitayānyathā |  
> yathā brāhmaṇacaṇḍālaḥ pūrvadṛṣṭas tathaiva saḥ ||

**[612]** yājñavalkyaḥ [1.88] |

> satyām anyāṃ savarṇāyāṃ dharmakāryaṃ na kārayet |  
> savarṇāsu vidhau dharme jyeṣṭhayā na vinetarā ||

viṣṇuḥ [27.1–4]: “savarṇāsu bahuṣu bhāryāsu vidyamānāsu jyeṣṭhayaiva saha dharmakāryaṃ kuryāt | miśrāsu kaniṣṭhayāpi samānavarṇayā | abhāve tv anantarayaivāpadi | na tv eva ca svijaḥ śūdrāyāḥ” “

chandogapariśiṣṭe kātyāyanaḥ |

> agniśiṣṭāṃ hi śuśrūṣāṃ bahubhāryaḥ savarṇayā |  
> kārayet tadvad bahutvaṃ cej jyeṣṭhayā garhitā na cet ||  
> yā vā syād vīrasūrāsāmājñāsaṃpādinī ca yā |  
> dakṣā priyaṃvadā śuddhā tām atra viniyojayet ||  
> dinakrameṇa vā karma yathājyaiṣṭhyaṃ svaśaktitaḥ |  
> vibhajya saha vā kuryur yathājñānam aśāṭhyavat ||  
> strīṇāṃ saubhāgyato jyaiṣṭhyaṃ vidyayaiva dvijanmanām |  
> na hi svalpena tapasā bhartā tuṣyati yoṣitām ||

**[613]** > bhartur ādeśavartinyā yoṣayā bahubhir vrataiḥ |  
> agniḥ śuśrūṣito yatra sā strī saubhāgyam āpnuyāt ||

dakṣaḥ |

> prathamā dharmapatnī tu dvitīyā rativardhinī |  
> dṛṣṭam eva phalaṃ tatra nādṛṣṭam upapadyate ||  
> dharmapatnī samākhyātā nirdoṣā yadi sā bhavet |  
> doṣe sati na doṣaḥ syād anyā kāryā gunānvitā ||

‘śūdrā’ ity anuvṛttau manu-viṣṇū |

> saṃtuṣṭo bhāryayā bhartā bhartrā bhāryā tathaiva ca |  
> yasminn etatkule nityaṃ kalyāṇaṃ tatra vai dhruvam ||  
> yadi hi strī na roceta pumāṃsaṃ na pramodayet |  
> apramodāt punaḥ puṃsaḥ prajanaṃ na pravartate ||  
> striyāṃ tu rocamānāyāṃ sarvaṃ tad rocate kulam |  
> tasyām arocamānāyāṃ sarvam eva na rocate ||  
> anyonyasyāvyabhīcāro bhaved āmaraṇāntikaḥ |  
> eṣa dharmaḥ samāsena jñeyaḥ strīpuṃsayoḥ paraḥ ||

**[614]**  
> tathā nityaṃ yateyātāṃ strīpuṃsau tu kṛtakriyau |  
> yathā nāticaretāṃ tau viyuktāv itaretaram ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [1.74] |

> yatrānukūlyaṃ dampatyos trivargas tatra vardhate |

dakṣaḥ |

> gṛhavāsaḥ sukhārtho hi patnīmūlaṃ ca tatsukham |  
> sā patnī yā vijānāti cittajñā vaśavartinī ||  
> anukūlā tv avāgduṣṭā dakṣā sādhvī prajāvatī |  
> ebhir eva guṇair yuktā śrīr eva strī na saṃśayaḥ ||  
> prahṛṣṭamānasā nityaṃ sthānamānavicakṣaṇā |  
> bhartuḥ prītikarī yā tu sā bhāryā itarā jarā ||

vyāsaḥ |

> pūrvotthānaparā dakṣā jaghanyāsanaśāyinī |  
> avāgduṣṭānukūlā strī bhaved vai puṇyakarmaṇaḥ ||

atha dakṣaḥ |

> duḥkhāsikā kalir bhedaś chidraṃ pīḍā parasparam |  
> pratikūlakalatrasya dvidārasya na saṃśayaḥ ||

**[615]** manuḥ [9.77–79] |

> saṃvatsaram udīkṣeta dviṣantīṃ yoṣitaṃ patiḥ |  
> ūrdhvaṃ saṃvatsarād enāṃ dāyaṃ kṛtvā na saṃvaset ||  
> atikrāmet pramattaṃ yā mattaṃ rogārtam eva vā |  
> sā trīn māsān parityājyā vibhūṣaṇaparicchadā ||  
> unmattaṃ patitaṃ klībam abījaṃ pāparogiṇam |  
> na ca dviṣantyās tyāgo ‘sti na ca dāyāpavartanam ||

atha nāradaḥ [15.95] |

> anukūlām avāgduṣṭāṃ dakṣāṃ sādhvīṃ prajāvatīm |  
> tyajan bhāryām avasthāpyo rājñā daṇḍena bhūyasā ||

‘cauravac chāsya’ ity anuvṛttau viṣṇuḥ [5.162–63]: “nirdoṣaṃ parityajan patnīṃ ca” |

yājñavalkyaḥ [1.76] |

> ājñāsaṃpādinīṃ dakṣāṃ vīrasūṃ priyavādinīm |  
> tyajan dāpyas tṛtīyāṃśam adravyo bharaṇaṃ striyāḥ ||

**[616]** devalaḥ |

> svadārāṃs tyajato mohān narasyānyāyamocinaḥ |  
> dharmavaṃśaparityaktur niṣkṛtir na vidhīyate ||  
> kuṣṭhinīṃ patitāṃ vandhyām unmattāṃ vigatārtavām |  
> aduṣṭāṃ labhate tyaktuṃ tīrtān na tv eva karmaṇaḥ ||

‘**anyāyamocinaḥ’** anyāyena moktuḥ | ‘**tīrtād’** yonitaḥ | ‘**karmaṇaḥ’** pāpakarmāditaḥ |

nāradaḥ [15.90, 92–94] |

> anyonyaṃ tyajator āgaḥ (?) syād anyonyaviruddhayoḥ |  
> strīpuṃsayor nigūḍhāyā vyabhicārād ṛte striyāḥ ||  
> strīdhanabhrṣṭasarvasvāṃ garbhavisraṃsinīṃ tathā |  
> bhartuś ca vadham icchantīṃ striyaṃ nirvāsayed gṛhāt ||  
> anarthaśīlāṃ satataṃ tathaivāpriyavādinīm |  
> pūrvāśinī ca yā bhartus tāṃ strīṃ nirvāsayed gṛhāt ||  
> vandhyāṃ strījananīṃ nindyāṃ pratikūlāṃ ca sarvadā |  
> kāmato nābhinandeta kurvann evaṃ na doṣabhāk ||

**[317]** ‘**āgaḥ’** pāpam | ‘**nigūḍhā’** rakṣitā | ‘**strīdhanabhraṣṭasarvasvām’** strīdhanatvena bhraṣṭaṃ bhrāṃśitaṃ sarvasvaṃ yayā sā tathoktā | ‘**bhraṣṭam’** atrāntarbhāvitaṇyartham |

yamaḥ |

> ṛtusnātā tu yā nārī bhartāraṃ nopagacchati |  
> tāṃ grāmamadhye vikhyāpya bhrūṇaghnīṃ tu vivāsayet ||  
> bhartuḥ pratiniveśena yā vṛthā gamayed ṛtūn |  
> tāṃ tu vikhyāpya bandhūnāṃ bhrūṇaghnīṃ tu vivāsayet ||

‘**pratiniveśena’** atidveṣeṇa |

baudhāyanaḥ |

> aśuśrūṣākarīṃ vandhyāṃ bandhakīṃ parihiṃsakīm |  
> tyajanti puruṣāḥ prājñāḥ kṣipram apriyavādinīm ||  
> aprajāṃ daśame varṣe strīprajāṃ dvādaśe tyajet |  
> pretaprajāṃ pañcadaśe sadyas tv apriyavādinīm ||

vasiṣṭhaḥ [21.9–10] |

> vyavāye tīrthagamane dharmebhyaś ca nivartane |

**[618]** > catasras tu parityājyāḥ śiṣyagā gurugā ca yā ||  
> patighnī ca viśeṣeṇa juṅgitopagatā ca yā |

yājñavalkyaḥ [1.72] |

> vyabhicārād ṛtau śuddhir garbhe tyāgo vidhīyate |  
> garbhabhartṛvadhe tāsāṃ tathā mahati pātake ||

hārītaḥ: “garbhaghnīm adhovarṇagāṃ śiṣyasutagāminīṃ ca | pātavyasanasaṃsaktāṃ ca | dhanadhānyakṣayakarīṃ ca varjayet” |

yamaḥ |

> svacchandagā ca yā nārī tasyās tyāgo vidhīyate |  
> na caiva strīvadhaṃ kuryān na caivāṅgavikartanam ||  
> svacchandavyabhicāriṇyāṃ vivasvāṃs tyāgam abravīt |   
> na bandhanaṃ na vairūpyaṃ vadhaṃ strīṇāṃ vivarjayet ||

**[619]** atha yājñavalkyaḥ [1.70] |

> hṛtādhikārāṃ malināṃ piṇḍamātropajīvinīm |  
> paribhūtām adhaḥśayyāṃ vāsayed dvyabhicāriṇīm ||

nāradaḥ [15.91] |

> vyabhicāre striyo mauṇḍyam adhaḥśayanam eva ca |  
> kadannaṃ ca kuvāsaś ca karma cāvaskarojjhanam ||

**73 — (kha) atha strīdharmāḥ**

tatra manuḥ [5.147–49] |

> bālayā vā yuvatyā vā vṛddhayā vāpi yoṣitā |  
> na svātantryeṇa kartavyaṃ kiṃcit kāryaṃ gṛheṣv api ||  
> bālye pitur vaśe tiṣṭhet pāṇigrāhasya yauvane |  
> putrāṇāṃ bhartari prete na bhajet sā svatantratām ||  
> pitrā bhartrā sutair vāpi necched viraham ātmanaḥ |  
> eṣāṃ hi viraheṇa strī garhye kuryād ubhe kule ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [25.9] |

> bhartrā pitrā sutair na strī viyuktānya[gṛhe] vaset |  
> asatsaṅge viśeṣeṇa garhyatām eti sā dhruvam ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [1.86] |

> pitṛmātṛsutabhrātṛśvaśrūśvaśuramātulaiḥ |  
> hīnā na syād vinā bhartrā garhaṇīyānyathā bhavet ||

**[620]** manuḥ [5.150] |

> sadā prahṛṣṭayā bhāvyaṃ gṛhakārye ca dakṣayā |  
> susaṃskṛtopaskarayā vyaye cāmuktahastayā ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [1.83] |

> saṃyatopaskarā dakṣā hṛṣṭā vyayaparāṅmukhī |  
> kuryāc chvaśurayoḥ pādavandanaṃ bhartṛtatparā ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [25.10] |

> pūrvotthānaṃ guror arvāk bhojanābhyañjanakriyā |  
> jaghanyāsanaśāyitvaṃ karma strīṇām udāhṛtam ||

devalaḥ: “asvātantryaṃ patiśuśrūṣā sahadharmacaryā tatpūjyapūjanaṃ taddveṣyadveṣaṇam aduṣṭabhāvatā nityānukūlyaṃ tatkāryaparatvam iti strīdharmaḥ” |

viṣṇuḥ [25.2–8]: “bhartuḥ samānacāritvam | [śvaśrū]śvaśuragurudevatātithīnāṃ pūjanam | susaṃskṛtopaskaratā | amuktahastatā | suguptabhāṇḍatā | mūlakriyāsv anabhiratiḥ | maṅgalācārātatparatā” |

**[621]** mahābhārate |

> yadaiva bhartā jānīyān mantramūlaparāṃ striyam |  
> udvijeta tadaivāsyāḥ sarpād veśmagatād iva ||

pṛthivīṃ prati lakṣmīvākye viṣṇuḥ [99.21.22] |

> nārīṣu nityaṃ śucitbhūṣitāsu pativratāsu priyavādinīṣu |  
> amuktahastāsu prajānvitāsu suguptabāṇḍāsu balipriyāsu ||  
> suśliṣṭaveśmāsu jitendriyāsu kalivyapetāsu vilolupāsu |  
> dharmavyapekṣāsu dayānvitāsu sthitā sadāhaṃ jagatāṃ vidhātrī ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: “śvaḥ śvaḥ pacanabhāṇḍānām anulepanaṃ susaṃmṛṣṭagṛhadvāropalepanaṃ kṛtaśaucānukūlyadadhyakṣatadūrāpravālapuṣpakṛtabalikarma śvaśrūśvaśurābhivādanānantaraṃ gṛhāvaśyakāni kuryāt | na devabhṛtyātithibhyo ‘gre ‘śnīyāt | na bhartur anyatra pratīkārauṣadhāt” |

‘**śvaḥ śvaḥ pacanabhāṇḍānām’** iti, ‘**pacanabhāṇḍānāṃ’** sthālyādīnāṃ āgāmyāgāmidine upalepanaṃ kartavyam ity arthaḥ |

**[622]** ṛṣyaśṛṅgaḥ |

> gṛhamedhā bhaven nityaṃ bhūṣaṇāni ca pūjayet |  
> nityasnānakṛtāṃ veṇīm arcayet puṇyavāsasā ||  
> pūrvam eva raho gacched yāvan nānyaḥ prabudhyate |  
> devatārādhanaṃ kuryād dhūpapuṣpabaliṃ haret ||

‘**gṛhamedhā’** gṛhakṛtyatatparā | ‘**bhūṣaṇāni ca pūjayet’** bhūṣaṇāni mārjanādinā saṃskuryāt |

śaṅkhalikhitau: “strī nānuktā bahir niṣkrāmet | nānantarīyā paridhāvet | nānutsave gandhamālyābharaṇāni vikṛtāni vāsāṃsi bibhṛyāt | na parapuruṣam abhibhāṣeta | anyatra vaṇikpravrajitavṛddhebhyaḥ | na nābhiṃ darśayet | kulavadhūr āgulphābhyāṃ vāsaḥ paridadhyāt | na stanau vivṛtau kuryāt | na hasetānāvṛtam | na mahājane” |

‘**anāvṛtam’** hastābhyāṃ mukham anācchādya |

vyāsaḥ |

> dvāropasevanaṃ nityaṃ gavākṣeṇa nirīkṣaṇam |  
> asatpralāpo hāsyaṃ ca dūṣaṇaṃ kulayoṣitām ||

manuḥ [9.13] |

> pānaṃ durjanasaṃsargaḥ patyā ca viraho ‘ṭanam |

**[623]** > svapno ‘nyahegavāsaś ca nārīsaṃdūṣaṇāni ṣaṭ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [25.11] |

> pānāṭanadivāsvapnam akriyā dūṣaṇaṃ striyaḥ |

‘**akriyā’** gṛhakṛtyānanuṣṭhānam |

śaṅkhalikhitau: “na gaṇikādhūrtacāriṇīpravrajitekṣaṇikāmāyāvinīkuhakaśīlāviplutābhiḥ sahaiva tiṣṭhet | saṃsargeṇa hi cāritryaṃ duṣyet | na bhartuḥ pratikūlam ācaret | na prakīrṇabhāṇḍabhājanopaskaradravyā notthānakhaṭvāsanapādukā syāt” |

‘**īkṣiṇikā’** daivajñā |

hārītaḥ: “atha patnyācāram anukramiṣyāmo gṛhaṃ patnī na hy apatnīkaṃ vidyāt | tasmāt patnī gṛhācāraparā syāt | susaṃsṛṣṭotpāditasaṃskārā (?) sūpaliptārcitaveśmāni **[628]** patitāni pratikuryāt | aguptaṃ gopayet | anyapuruṣekṣaṇaṃ duṣṭakathādibhāṣaṇaṃ duṣṭapravrajitastrīsaṃsargaṃ ca varjayet | paragṛharathyācatvaravīthīpravrajitālayāṃś ca nābhigacchet | kūpapathasthānaṃ sandhivelāsaṃcaraṇaṃ ca varjayet | paraśayanāsanavastrābharaṇāni manasāpi nādhyavasyed ā punaḥsaṃskārāt | tathaikapātryaṃ madyamāṃsāni | ucchiṣṭanirmālyaṃ ca | anyatra gurubhartṛsutebhyaḥ | ananyapuruṣalolupānarthān varjayet | tathā pratyudvadanam ālasyavaiklavyataulyādi | nocchiṣṭā devāgāraṃ praviśet | nāprokṣyāvimṛśyāparyagnikṛtya śrāpayet | nāprakṣālitapāṇir yāvakotpavanagorasadhānā gṛhṇīyāt | sthālyapidhānadarvīḥ prakṣālyopakaraṇāni gupte nidhāpayet | śvobhūte pratiprakṣālya pacanārthān kuryāt | gorasadhānyāni cāsya nirdeśe gṛhṇīyāt | śṛte prakṣālyopalipya parimṛjya taijasāni veśmāvamārjanaṃ pratyupalepanāni kṛtvā vaiśvadevakāla iti pracodanaṃ snānahetoḥ | snātā śukle vāsasī paridhāya pāṇipādaṃ prakṣālyotkramyācamya devāgāraṃ praviśya namaskṛtyāyatane ‘gnim upasamādhāya samiddarbhapuṣpabaliśāntipātrāṇy āhṛtyānnādyam abhighārya yac cānyad āhnikaṃ syāt | hute devebhyaḥ udvāhāgnau devapatnībhyo baliṃ hared bhartṛnirdeśe | kṛte devātithye yathāsvaṃ gṛhiṇas tarpayitvā śiṣyān **[625]** suhṛdaḥ patiṃ ca tadanujñātāvaśeṣaṃ patnī gupte bhuktvā pratisvābhir upaspṛśya śeṣaṃ bhāṇḍāni nirṇijya prakṣālya ca bahir uttarapūrvasyāṃ diśi vāstubhūtapaśupataye rudrāya nama iti nirṇīya | evaṃ sāyaṃ śṛtādi | yathārthaṃ suviśiṣṭeṣu namo bhagavate rudrāya bhasmasade bhasmanā rakṣāṃ karomīti bhasmanādvāram apidhāya svāmisutādīn ātmānaṃ cālabhet | yac cānyad rakṣyaṃ syāt | nāprakṣālitapāṇipādā saṃviśet | na nagnā | nocchiṣṭā | nānamanīyā | nānamasyabhartṛpādā | nāviditotthānā | pūrvotthāyinī | anupasthāyodakadhānā | anusaraṇaveśmārcinī | pradakṣiṇā | praśāntā | saumyārhitā | bhartuḥ priyavādinī | nopariṣṭāt sthitā āsīta | noccair na vitarkasthāne nābhīkṣṇam īkṣeta | parivṛjya saṃvāhayitvā upāsīta | vyajanenoṣṇe varṣe gharmāmbhāṃsy asya gātrebhyaḥ parimṛjyāt | śirasaś cānavasthitasya samādhānam | grāmāntarāhṛtabhārātikrāntam āyāntam upagaccheta hṛṣṭamanā arghyeṇārghayet | vratadhāraṇaṃ devakāryaṃ snānaṃ vānujñātayā kāryam” ||

‘**kūpapathasthānam’** kūpānuyāyivartmāvasthānam | ‘**aikapātryam’** sahabhojanam | ‘**guravaḥ’** śvaśurādayaḥ | ‘**lolupā’** spṛhā | ‘**anarthaḥ’** niṣprayojano ‘rthavyayaḥ | ‘**pratyudvadanam’** pratikūlābhidhānam | ‘**taulyam’** svakulādhyanucitaveṣabhāṣādīti **[626]** jayasvāmī | ‘**avimṛśya’** keśakīṭādikam avicārya | ‘**yāvakaḥ’** piṭakādiḥ | ‘**utpavanam’** cālanī | ‘**asya nirdeśe’** bhartur anujñāne | ‘**snānahetoḥ’** patur iti śeṣaḥ | ‘**yac cānyat’** iti, anyan maṇḍakādi | ‘**āhnikam’** tadaharbhojyam, tac cābhighārya bhartur nirdeśe tiṣṭhed iti śeṣaḥ | ‘**śeṣam’** āhnikaśeṣaṃ aśiṣṭam api | ‘**prasvābhiḥ’** ātmārthopakalpitābhir adbhiḥ | ‘**upaspṛśya’** ācamya | ‘**nirṇijya’** annamalāpakarṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā | ‘**śṛtādi’** śṛte prakṣālyopalipyetyādi rudrabaliparyantam | ‘**ālabhet’** bhasmopaliptena hastena spṛśet | ‘**anupasthāyodakadhānā’** ariktodakapātrā | ‘**pradakṣiṇā’** sotsāhā | kam eṣā vīkṣyata iti yatra lokasya vicāraṇā bhavati tad ‘**vitarkasthānam’** | ‘**parimṛjya’** pādayo rajaḥ | ‘**saṃvāhayitvā’** aṅgamardanaṃ kṛtvā | ‘**vyajanenoṣṇe’** vyajanena uṣṇakāle upāsīta | ‘**anavasthitasya’** ākulitacetasaḥ |

chāndogyapariśiṣṭe kātyāyanaḥ |

> patyur apy abhiyoginyā śuśrūṣyo ‘gnir vinītayā |  
> saubhāgyavad avaidhavyakāmayā bhartṛbhaktayā ||

**[627]** ‘patyur apy abhiyoginyā’ patyur apy ādhikyena satatam agninābhiyuktayā satyāgniḥ śuśrūṣyaḥ |

śaṅkhalikhitau: “na bhartāraṃ dviṣyād yady apy aṣṭīvalaḥ syāt | patito ‘ṅgahīno vyādhito vā | patir hi daivataṃ strīṇām | na vratopavāsaniyamejyādānadharmo vānugrāhakaḥ strīṇām anyatra patiśuśrūṣāyāḥ | kāmaṃ bhartur anujñātāyā vratopavāsaniamejyādīnām abhyāsaḥ strīdharmaḥ” |

patiṭhīnasiḥ: “striyo gṛhadevatāḥ | tāsāṃ na śaucaṃ na vrataṃ nopavāsaḥ | patiśuśrūṣayā gacchanti paramāṃ gatim” |

manuḥ [5.153–54] |

> anṛtāv ṛtukāle tu mantrasaṃskārakṛt patiḥ |  
> sukhasya nityaṃ dāteha paraloke ca yoṣitaḥ ||  
> viśīlaḥ kāmadṛpto vā guṇair vā parivarjitaḥ |  
> upacaryaḥ striyā sādhvyā satataṃ devavat patiḥ ||

manu-viṣṇū [manuḥ 5.155; vi. 25.15] |

> nāsti strīṇāṃ pṛthag yajño na vrataṃ nāpy upoṣaṇam |  
> patiṃ śuśrūṣate yena tena svarge mahīyate ||

**[628]** viṣṇuḥ [25.16] |

> patyau jīvati yā yoṣid upavāsavrataṃ caret |  
> āyur harati sā bhartur narakaṃ caiva gacchati ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [1.77] |

> strībhir bhatṛvacaḥ kāryam eṣa dharmaḥ paraḥ sthitaḥ |  
> āśuddheḥ saṃpratīkṣyo hi mahāpātakadūṣitaḥ ||

gautamaḥ [18.1–3]: “asvatantrā dharme strī | nāticared bhartāram | vākcakṣuhkarmasaṃyutā” |

hārītaḥ: “śucyācārā bhartṛmanāḥ sādhvī bhavati | evam hy āha —

> yasya bhāryā vaśā sādhvī satataṃ priyavādinī |  
> śucyācārā bhartṛmanā sā devī parikīrtyate” ||

manuḥ [5.151, 153] |

> yasmai dadyāt pitā tv enāṃ bhrātā vānumate pituḥ |  
> taṃ śuśrūṣeta jīvantaṃ saṃsthitaṃ na ca laṅghayet ||  
> pāṇigrāhasya sādhvī strī jīvato vā mṛtasya vā |  
> patilokam abhīpsantī nācaret kiṃcid apriyam ||

‘**saṃsthitam’** mṛtam |

**[629]** yājñavalkyaḥ [1.75, 87] |

> mṛte jīvati vā patyau yā nānyam upagacchati |  
> seha kīrtim avāpnoti modate comayā saha ||  
> patipriyahite yuktā svācārā vijitendriyā |  
> iha kīrtim avāpnoti pretya cānuttamāṃ gatim ||

manuḥ [5.154, 165, 166] |

> dānaprabhṛti yā tu syād yāvad āyuḥ pativratā |  
> bhartṛlokaṃ na tyajanti yathā vārundhatī tathā ||  
> patiṃ yā nābhicarati manovāgdehasaṃyatā |  
> sā bhartṛlokam avāpnoti sadbhiḥ sādhvīti cocyate ||  
> anena nārīvṛttena manovāgdehasaṃyatā |  
> iha kīrtim avāpnoti patilokaṃ paratra ca ||

‘patiloko’ atra patyā sahādhikāreṇa yajñādibhir yo loka upārjitaḥ |

chāndogyapariśiṣṭe kātyāyanaḥ |

> patiśuśrūṣayaiva strī sarvān lokān samaśnute |  
> divaḥ punar ihāyātā sukhānāṃ sāvadhir bhavet ||

**[630]** bṛhaspatiḥ [25.12] |

> ārtārte mudite hṛṣṭā proṣite malinā kṛśā |  
> mṛte mriyeta yā patyau sā strī jñeyā pativratā ||

vasiṣṭhaḥ [21.14] |

> pativratānāṃ gṛhamedhinīnāṃ satyavratānāṃ ca śucivratānām |  
> tāsāṃ tu lokāḥ patibhiḥ samānā gomāyulokā vyabhicāriṇīnām ||

manuḥ [9.30] |

> vyabhicārāt tu bhartuḥ strī loke prāpnoti nindyatām |  
> śṛgālayoniṃ prāpnoti pāparogaiś ca pīḍyate ||

chandogapariśiṣṭe kātyāyanaḥ |

> patim ullaṅghya mohāt strī kaṃ kaṃ na narakaṃ vrajet |  
> kṛcchrān mānuṣatāṃ prāpya kiṃ kiṃ duḥkhaṃ na paśyati ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: “surālaśunapalāṇḍugṛñjanakavakādīny abhakṣyāṇi ca varjayet | āhāramayaṃ śarīram | tanmayatvād brāhmaṇaḥ saṃkīryate | mātur aśitapītād dhi garbhaḥ saṃbhavati” |

manuḥ [9.184] |

> pratiṣiddhā pibed yā tu madyam abhyudayeṣv api |  
> prekṣāsamāje gacched vā sā daṇḍyā kṛṣṇalāni ṣaṭ ||

**[631]** vasiṣṭhaḥ [21.11] |

> yā brāhmaṇī syād iha vai surāpī na tāṃ devāḥ patilokaṃ nayanti |  
> ihaiva sā carati kṣīṇapuṇyā śunībhūtā gardabhī sūkarī ca ||

**atha proṣitabhartṛkāyāḥ**

tatra manuḥ [9.75] |

> vidhāya proṣite vṛttiṃ jīven niyamam āsthitā |  
> proṣite tv avidhāyaiva jīvec chilpair agarhitaiḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [1.74] |

> krīḍāśarīrasaṃskārasamājotsvadarśanam |  
> hāsyaṃ paragṛhe yānaṃ tyajet proṣitabhartṛkā ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [25.13] |

> prasādhanaṃ nṛtyagītasamājotsavadarśanam |  
> māṃsamadyābhiyogaṃ ca na kuryāt proṣite patau ||

**[632]** viṣṇuḥ [25.9–11]: “bhartari proṣite ‘pratikarmakriyā | paragṛheṣv anabhigamanam | dvāradeśagavākṣakeṣv anavasthānam” |

śaṅkhalikhitau: “sarvāsāṃ proṣite bhartari brāhmaṇī cāritraṃ rakṣet | itarāsāṃ mātāpitarāv anantaraṃ rājanyo vā | preṅkhātāṇḍavavihāracitradarśanāṅgarāgodyānavivṛtaśayanotkṛṣṭa-pānabhojanakandukakrīḍādhūpagandhamālyālaṃkāradantadhāvanāñjanādarśana-prasādhanādīnām asvatantrāṇāṃ proṣitabhartṛkāṇāṃ kulastrīṇām anārambhaḥ” |

‘sarvāsām’ ityādi, sarvāsāṃ proṣitabhartṛkāṇāṃ madhye brāhmaṇī ātmanā cāritraṃ rakṣet | itarāsāṃ tu proṣitabhartṝṇāṃ mātāpitarau rakṣete | anantaraṃ ca tayor asato rājanyo rakṣet | ekabhartṛkāṇāṃ caitad ucyate | ‘preṅkhā’ doḷā |

hārītaḥ: “na proṣite tv alaṃkuryāt | na veṇīṃ pramuñceta” |

**atha mṛtabhartṛkāyāḥ**

tatra aṅgirāḥ |

> mṛte bhartari yā nārī samārohed dhutāśanam |  
> sārundhatīsamācārā svarge loke mahīyate ||  
> triṃśatkoṭyo ‘rdhakoṭī ca yāni lomāni mānave |  
> tāvanty abdāni sā svarge bhartāraṃ yānugacchati ||

**[633]** > vyālagrāhī yathā vyālaṃ bilād uddharate balāt |  
> tadvad bhartāram ādāya tenaiva saha gacchati ||  
> mātṛkaṃ paitṛkaṃ caiva yatra kanyā pradīyate |  
> punāti trikulaṃ nārī bhartāraṃ yānugacchati ||  
> tatra sā bhartṛparamā parā paramalālasā |  
> krīdate patinā sārdhaṃ yāvad indrāś caturdaśa ||  
> brahmaghno vā kṛtaghno vā mitraghno vāpi yo naraḥ |  
> taṃ vai punāti sā nārī ity āṅgirasabhāṣitam ||  
> sādhvīnām eva nārīṇām agniprapatanād ṛte |  
> nānyo dharmo ‘tra vijñeyo mṛte bhartari karhicit ||  
> yāvan nāgnau dahed dehaṃ mṛte patyau pativratā |  
> tāvan na mucyate nārī strīśarīrāt kathaṃcana ||  
> sadvṛttabhāvārpitabhartṛkāṇāṃ strīṇāṃ viyogakṣatakātarāṇām |  
> tāsāṃ prabhāvas tamite gate kaṃ nāgnipraveśād aparo ‘sti mārgaḥ ||

‘**sadvṛtteti’** | ‘**vṛttam’** ācāraḥ | ‘**bhāvo’** ‘bhiprāyaḥ | tau śobhanāv arpitau yābhis tās tathā | ‘**viyogakṣatakātarāṇāṃ’** viyoga eva ‘**kṣatam’** prarohī vraṇaḥ tatra kātarāṇām | ‘**prabhau’** bhartari | ‘**kaṃ’** svargam |

**[634]** vyāsaḥ |

> dayitaṃ yānyadeśasthaṃ mṛtaṃ śrutvā pativratā |  
> samārohati śīghre ‘gnau tasyāḥ śaktiṃ nibodhata ||  
> yadi praviṣṭo narakaṃ baddhaḥ pāśaiḥ sudāruṇaiḥ |  
> saṃprāpto yātanāsthānaṃ gṛhīto yamakiṃkaraiḥ ||  
> tiṣṭhate vivaśo dīno veṣṭyamānaḥ svakarmabhiḥ |  
> vyālagrāhī yathā sarpaṃ balād gṛhnāty aśaṅkitaḥ ||  
> tadvad bhartāram ādāya divaṃ yāti tapobalāt |  
> tatra sā bhartṛparamā stūyamānāpsarogaṇaiḥ ||  
> krīḍate patinā sārdhaṃ yāvad indrāś caturdaśa |

brahmapurāṇe |

> mṛte bhartari satstrīṇāṃ na cānyā vidyate gatiḥ |  
> nānyad bhartṛviyogāgnidāhasya śamanaṃ kvacit ||  
> deśāntaramṛte tasmin sādhvī tatpādukādvayam |  
> nidhāyorasi saṃśuddhā praviśej jātavedasam ||  
> ṛgvedavādāt sādhvī strī na bhaved ātmaghātinī |  
> tryahāśauce nivṛtte tu śrāddhaṃ prāpnoti śāstravat ||

**[635]** ‘**ṛgvedavādāt’** — ‘imā nārīr avidhavā’ ityādimantrāt | evaṃ ca sakalavacanaparyālocanayā brāhmaṇādisarvabhāryāṇāṃ svagatabhartṛgataphalaviśeṣārthinīnāṃ garbhavatībālāpatyādi-vyatiriktānāṃ sahamaraṇānumaraṇayor adhikāra iti |

bṛhaspatiḥ |

> śarīrārdhaṃ smṛtā nārī puṇyāpuṇyaphale samā |  
> anvārūḍhā jīvantī vā sādhvī bhartṛhitāya sā ||

viṣnuḥ [25.14]: “mṛte bhartari brahmacaryaṃ tadanvārohaṇaṃ vā” |

hārītaḥ: “āhitāgniś cet pramīyeta, aupāsanāvakṣāṇāgniṃ parigṛhya sarpirājñībhiḥ **[636]** sūtrasvanam iṣṭvā nāvaset | anāhitāgniś ced anyam ādadyāt | janāgniṃ vā parigṛhya bhartuḥ pituḥ svajanagṛhavarjaṃ jitajihvāhastapādendriyā svācāravatī divārātraṃ bhartāram anuśocantī vratopavāsaiḥ kṣāntāyuṣo ‘nte patilokaṃ jayati na bhūyaḥ pativiyogam āpnotīti | evaṃ hy āha —

> pativratā tu yā sādhvī niṣṭhāṃ yāti prabhau mṛte |  
> sā hitvā sarvapāpāni patilokam avāpnuyāt” ||

‘**avakṣāṇaṃ’** ardhadagdhadārum ulmukham | ‘āyaṃ gauḥ’ iti tisra ṛcaḥ sarpirājñyaḥ | ‘**anyam’** gṛhyam ādhānavidhinā gṛhṇīyāt | ‘**janāgniḥ’** sabhyaḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ [25.15] |

> vratopavāsaniratā brahmacarye vyavasthitā |   
> damadānaratā nityam aputrāpi divaṃ vrajet ||

manuḥ [5.157–62] |

> kāmaṃ tu kṣapayed dehaṃ puṣpamūlaphalaiḥ śubhaiḥ |  
> na tu nāmāpi gṛhṇīyāt patyau prete parasya tu ||

**[637]** > āsītāmaranāt kṣāntā niyatā brahmacāriṇī |  
> yo dharma ekapatnīnāṃ kaṅkṣantī tam anuttamam ||  
> anekāni sahasrāṇi kumārabrahmacāriṇām |  
> divaṃ gatāni viprāṇām akṛtvā kulasaṃtatim ||  
> mṛte bhartari sādhvī strī brahmacarye vyavasthitā |  
> svargaṃ gacchanty aputrāpi yathā te brahmacāriṇaḥ ||  
> apatyalobhād yā tu strī bhartāram ativartate |  
> seha nindām avāpnoti patilokāc ca hīyate ||  
> nānyotpannā prajāstīha na cāpy anyaparigrahe |  
> na dvitīyaś ca sādhvīnāṃ kvacid bhartopadiśyate ||

**[638]** niyogānantaraṃ yamaḥ |

> yāvajjīvaṃ sadāsīta niyatā brahmacāriṇī |  
> yo dharma ekapatnīnāṃ taṃ dharmam abhikāṅkṣatī ||  
> striyāḥ śrutau vā śāstre vā pravrajyā na vidhīyat |  
> prajā hi tasyā svo dharmaḥ savarṇād iti dhāraṇā ||  
> aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi munīnām ūrdhvaretasām |  
> divaṃ gatāni viprāṇām akṛtvā kulasantatim ||  
> tathaiva kanyā vyāvṛttā brahmacarye vyavasthitā |  
> aputrā prāpnuyāt svargaṃ yathā te brahmacāriṇaḥ ||  
> aputrā jātaputrā vā kanyā patim anuvratā |  
> prāpnuyāt svargam eveti manuḥ svāyambhuvo ‘bravīt ||

‘**ekapatnīnām’** ekapatikānām | ‘**kanyā’** atra ūḍhā |

kātyāyanaḥ [837] |

> anekadoṣaduṣṭe ‘pi mṛte bhartari vā sadā |  
> sādhvācārā ca tiṣṭheta guruśuśrūṣaṇe ratā ||  
> mṛte bhartari yā sādhvī brahmacarye vyavasthitā |  
> sārundhatīsamācārā brahmaloke mahīyate ||

**[639]**

**[73 — [ga] atha niyogaḥ**

tatra manuḥ [9.59] |

> devarād vā sapiṇḍād vā striyā samyaṅ niyuktayā |  
> prajepsayādhigantavyā santānasya parikṣaye ||

nāradaḥ [15.80–82, 86–88] |

> niyuktā gurubhir gacched devaraṃ putrakāmyayā |  
> sa ca tāṃ pratipadyeta tathaivāputramanmanaḥ ||  
> putre jāte nivarteta viplavaḥ syād ato ‘nyathā |  
> ghṛtenābhyajya gātrāṇi tailenāvikṛtena vā ||  
> mukhān mukhaṃ pariharan gātrair gātrāṇi cāspṛśan |  
> kule tadavaśeṣe ca santānārthaṃ na kāmataḥ ||

**[640]** > niyukto gubhir gacched bhrātṛbhāryāṃ yavīyasaḥ |  
> avidyamāne tu gurau rājñe vācyaḥ kulakṣayaḥ ||  
> tatas tadvacanād gacched anuśiṣyāt striyaṃ ca saḥ |  
> pūrvoktena vidhānena snātāṃ puṃsavane śuciḥ ||  
> sakṛd ā garbhadhānāt tu vṛtte garbhe tathaiva sā |  
> ato ‘nyathā vartamānaḥ pumān strī vāpi kāmataḥ ||  
> vineyau subhṛśaṃ rājñā viplavaḥ syād ato ‘nyathā |

yamaḥ |

> ṛtau tu tasyāṃ snātāyāṃ vāgyatas tāmase niśi |  
> svaśmaśrunakharomāṇāṃ gandhasparśāv avedayan ||  
> ekavāsā ghṛtāktāṅgo durgandhaḥ śokadurmanāḥ |  
> mukhān mukhaṃ pariharan gātrair gātrāṇi vāspṛśan ||  
> yatātmā garbham ādadhyād vṛte garbhe tv apavrajet |  
> jātāpatyāṃ nādhigacchej jāte putre tathaiva ca ||

**[641]** > sīmantonnayanādīni sarvakarmāṇi kārayet |  
> bhrātṛsantānam icchadbhiḥ pitṝṇām ūrdhvadehinām ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [1.68–69] |

> aputrāṃ gurvanujñāto devaraḥ putrakāmyayā |  
> sapiṇḍo vā sagotro vā ghṛtābhyakta ṛtāv iyāt ||  
> ā garbhasambhavād gacchet patitaś cānyathā bhavet |  
> anena vidhinā jātāḥ kṣetrajo ‘sya bhavet sutaḥ ||

devalaḥ |

> naṣṭaḥ pravrajitaḥ klībaḥ patito rājakilbiṣī |  
> lokāntaragato vāpi parityājyaḥ patiḥ striyāḥ ||  
> mṛte bhartari jīve vā strī vindetāparaṃ patim |  
> santatyanāśārthatayā na svātantryeṇa yoṣitaḥ ||

nāradaḥ [15:98–102] |

> aṣṭau varṣāṇy udīkṣeta brāhmaṇī proṣitaṃ patim |  
> aprasūtā tu catvāri parato ‘nyaṃ samācaret ||

**[642]** > kṣatriyā ṣaṭsamās tiṣṭhed aprasūtā samātrayam |  
> vaiśyā prasūtā catvāri dve same tv aprasūtikā ||  
> na śūdrāyāḥ smṛtaḥ kālo na ca dharmavyatikramaḥ |  
> viśeṣato ‘prasūtāyāḥ saṃvatsaraparā sthitiḥ ||  
> apravṛttau smṛtaḥ kāla eṣa proṣitayoṣitām |  
> jīvati śrūyamāṇe ca syād eṣa dviguṇo vidhiḥ ||  
> prajāpravṛttau nārīṇāṃ vṛttir eṣā prajāpateḥ |  
> ato ‘nyagamane strīṇāṃ eṣa doṣo na vidyate ||

atha devarasapiṇḍādhikāre manuḥ [9.64–67] |

> nānyasmin vidhavā nārī niyoktavyā dvijātibhiḥ |  
> anyasmin hi niyuñjānā dharmaṃ hanyuḥ sanātanam ||  
> nodvāhikeṣu mantreṣu niyogaḥ kīrtyate kvacit |  
> na vivāhavidhāv uktaṃ vidhavāvedanaṃ punaḥ ||  
> ayaṃ dvijair hi vidvadbhiḥ paśudharmo vigarhitaḥ |  
> manuṣyāṇām api prokto vene rājyaṃ praśāsati ||  
> sa mahīm akhilāṃ bhuñjan rājarṣipravaraḥ purā |  
> varṇānāṃ saṃkaraṃ cakre kāmopahatacetasaḥ ||

**[643]** > tadā prabhṛti yo mohāt pramītapatikāṃ striyam |  
> niyojayaty apatyārthaṃ taṃ vigarhanti sādhavaḥ ||

mṛtapatyadhikāre vasiṣṭhaḥ [17.64–66]: “syāc cen niyoginoḥ | rikthalobhān nāsti niyogaḥ | prāyaścittaṃ vāpy upadiśya niyuñjyād ity eke” |

kātyāyanaḥ |

> niyogāt pāvanaṃ kuryād yathoktaṃ tadviśuddhaye |  
> dvijasya strīṣu dharmo ‘yaṃ śūdrasyaike sadāśrayaḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [saṃskāra 267–69] |

> ukto niyogo manunā niṣiddhaḥ svayam eva tu |  
> yugahrāsād aśakyo ‘yaṃ kartuṃ martyair vidhānataḥ ||  
> tapojñānasamāyuktāḥ kṛte tretāyuge narāḥ |  
> dvāpare ca kalau nṝṇāṃ śaktihānir vinirmitā ||

**[644]** > anekadhā kṛtāḥ putrā ṛṣibhir ye purātanaiḥ |  
> na śakyate ‘dhunā kartuṃ śaktihīnair idantanaiḥ ||

**73 — (gha) atha parapūrvāḥ**

tatra nāradaḥ [15.45–53] |

> parapūrvāḥ striyas tv anyāḥ sapta proktā yathākramam |  
> punarbhūs trividhā tāsāṃ svairiṇī ca caturvidhā ||  
> kanyaivākṣatayonir yā pāṇigrahaṇadūṣitā |  
> punarbhūḥ prathamā proktā punaḥ saṃskārakarmaṇā ||  
> kaumāraṃ patim utsṛjya yā tv anyaṃ puruṣaṃ śritā |  
> punaḥ patyur gṛham iyāt sā dvitīyā prakīrtitā ||  
> asatsu devareṣu strī bāndhavair vā pradīyate |  
> savarṇāya sapiṇḍāya sā tṛtīyā prakīrtitā ||

**[645]** > strī prasūtāprasūtā vā patyau caiva ca jīvati |  
> kāmāt samāśrayed anyaṃ svairiṇī prathamā tu sā ||  
> mṛte bhartari yā tu strī devarādīn apāsya tu |  
> kāmatas tu bhajed enaṃ dvitīyā sā prakīrtitā ||  
> deśāpahṛtavikrītā kṣuttṛṣṇāvyasanārditā |  
> tavāham ity upagatā sā tṛtīyā prakīrtitā ||  
> deśadharmān avekṣya strī gurubhir yā pradīyate |  
> utpannasāhasānyasmai sāntimā svairiṇī smṛtā ||  
> punarbhuvāṃ vidhis tv eṣa svairiṇīnāṃ prakīrtitaḥ |  
> pūrvā pūrvā jaghanyāsāṃ śreyasī tūttarottarā ||

manuḥ |

> patiṃ hitvā nikṛṣṭaṃ svam utkṛṣṭaṃ yā niṣevate |  
> nindyaiva loke bhavati parapūrveti cocyate ||

**[646]** ‘tisraḥ punarbhvaś catasraḥ svairiṇyaḥ’ ity abhidhāya śaṅkhalikhitau: “tatra pūrvā pūrvā jaghanyāḥ | tāsām apatyānām ṛkthapiṇḍodakayajñeṣu yo vikalpaḥ sa matur eva guṇavattayā vyākhyātaḥ” |

yājñavalkyaḥ [1.67] |

> akṣatā ca kṣatā caiva punarbhūḥ saṃskṛtā punaḥ |  
> svairiṇī yā patiṃ hitvā savarṇaṃ kāmataḥ śrayet ||

hārītaḥ |

> svairiṇī ca punarbhūś ca retodhāḥ kāmacāriṇī |  
> sarvabhakṣyā ca vijñeyāḥ pañcaitā śūdrayonayaḥ ||  
> etāsāṃ yāny apatyāni utpadyante kadācana |  
> na tān paṅktiṣu yuñjīta na te paṅktyarhakāḥ smṛtāḥ ||

‘**retodhāḥ’** kuṇḍamātā | ‘**kāmacāriṇī’** caturbhya ūrdhvam anyapuruṣagāminī | ‘**sarvabhakṣyā’** surāpī |

kātyāyanaḥ |

> sukhārthaṃ yā pravṛttā strī na bhartuḥ sutakāmyayā |  
> putraṃ tu janayed eva nindyā pāpā tu sā smṛtā ||  
> bhartṛgotraṃ samutsṛjya nārī yady anyam āśritā |  
> nindyaiva sā smṛtā loke parapūrveti cocyate ||

**[647]** > parapūrvāśritā yatra tatra syān nāśitaḥ prabhuḥ |  
> kramād ṛte tu dharmo ‘yaṃ labdhā vā svāmino bhavet ||  
> niroddhavyā ca tāḍyā ca parapūrvāparādhataḥ |  
> akṣamāṃ vānavekṣantīṃ tāḍayan daṇḍam arhati ||  
> caurahastān nadīvegād durbhikṣād deśaviplavāt |  
> nistārya vāsakāntārāl labdhvā tyaktvā kramāgatā ||  
> āsāṃ bhoge na doṣaḥ syād iti śāstraviniścayaḥ |  
> svāmidattāṃ tu gṛhṇīyād eṣā cen na tato ‘nyathā ||  
> dīyamānām athātmānaṃ yā nārī nānumodate |  
> na sā deyā na ca grāhyā vidhir eṣ smṛto bhṛguḥ ||  
> na cottamāṃ na cākāmāṃ tathā putravatīṃ na ca |  
> īdṛśīṃ tv anurūpeṇa niṣkrayeṇa pramīlayet ||

**iti mahārājādhirājaśrīmadgovindcandradevamahāsāndhivigrahikeṇa**

**bhaṭṭaśrīhṛdayadharātmajena bhaṭṭaśrīmallakṣmīdhareṇa viracite **

**kṛtyakalpatarau vyavahārakāṇḍe strīpuṃyogaparva ||**

**[648]**

## 74 dāyavibhāgaḥ
atha dāyavibhāgaḥ

tatra nāradaḥ [26.2] |

> vibhāgo ‘rthasya pitryasya putrair yatra prakalpyate |  
> dāyabhāga iti proktaṃ tad vivādapadaṃ budhaiḥ ||

manuḥ [9.104] |

> ūrdhvaṃ pituś ca mātuś ca sametya bhrātaraḥ samam |  
> bhajeran paitṛkaṃ riktham anīśās te hi jīvatoḥ ||

devalaḥ |

> pitary uparate putrā vibhajeran pitur dhanam |  
> asvāmyaṃ hi bhaved eṣāṃ nirdoṣe pitari sthite ||

‘**nirdoṣe’** pātityadirahite |

**[649]** nāradaḥ [16.2] |

> pitary ūrdhvaṃ gate putrā vibhajeyur dhanaṃ pituḥ |  
> mātur duhitaro ‘bhāve duhitṝṇāṃ tadanvayaḥ ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: “ata ūrdhvaṃ rikthabhāgaḥ | na jīvati pitari rikthaṃ vibhajeran | yady api syāt paścād adhigataṃ tair anarhā eva putrāḥ | arthadharmayor asvātantryāt” |

‘**yady api paścād adhigatam’** pitṛdhanavyāpāranirapekṣaiḥ putraiḥ paścāt samarthair vidyādibhir upāttam |

manuḥ [9.105–110] |

> jyeṣṭha eva tu gṛhṇīyāt pitryaṃ dhanam aśeṣataḥ |  
> śeṣās tam upajīveyur yathaiva pitaraṃ tathā ||

**[650]**  
> jyeṣṭhena jātamātreṇa putrī bhavati mānavaḥ |  
> pitṝṇām anṛṇaś caiva sa tasmāt sarvam arhati ||  
> yasminn ṛṇaṃ sannayati yena cānantyam aśnute |  
> sa eva dharmajaḥ putraḥ kāmajān itarān viduḥ ||  
> piteva pālayet putrān jyeṣṭho bhrātṝn yavīyasaḥ |  
> putravac cāpi varteran jyeṣṭhe bhrātari dharmataḥ ||  
> jyeṣṭhaḥ kulaṃ vardhayati vināśayati vā punaḥ |  
> jyeṣṭhaḥ pūjyatamo loke jyeṣṭhaḥ sadbhir agarhitaḥ ||  
> yo jyeṣṭho jyeṣṭhavṛttiḥ syān māteva ca piteva ca |  
> ajyeṣṭhavṛttir yas tu syāt sa saṃpūjyas tu bandhuvat ||

tathā [9.214] |

> na cādatvā kaniṣṭhebhyo jyeṣṭhaḥ kurvīta yautukam |

‘**yautukam’** pṛthagbhūtaṃ dravyam gavādi |

nāradaḥ [16.5] |

> bibhṛyād vecchataḥ sarvān jyeṣtho bhrātā yathā pitā |  
> bhrātā śaktaḥ kaniṣṭho vā śaktyapekṣā kule sthitiḥ ||

**[651]** śaṅkhalikhitau: “kāmaṃ vaseyur ekataḥ saṃhatā vṛddhim ācakṣīran” |

manuḥ [9.111] |

> evaṃ saha vaseyur vā pṛthag vā dharmakāmyayā |  
> pṛthag vivardhate dharmas tasmād dharmyā pṛthakkriyā ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26.5] |

> ekapākena vasatāṃ pitṛdevadvijārcanam |  
> ekaṃ bhaved vibhaktānāṃ tad eva syād gṛhe gṛhe ||

hārītaḥ: “jīvati pitari putrāṇām arthādānavisargākṣepeṣu na svātantryam, kāmadāne proṣite cārtiṃ gate vā jyeṣṭha evārthāṃś cintayet” |

śaṅkhalikhitau: “pitary aśakte kuṭumbavyavahāraṃ jyeṣṭhaḥ kuryād anantaro vā kāryajñas tadanumatena | na tv akāme pitari ṛkthavibhāgaḥ | vṛddhe viparītacetasi dīrgharogiṇi vā jyeṣṭha eva pitṛvad arthān pālayed itareṣām | ṛkthamūlaṃ hi kuṭumbam | asvatantrāḥ pitṛmantaḥ | mātary apy evam sthitāyām” |

**[652] **‘**anantaraḥ’** anujaḥ | ‘**tadanumatena’** jyeṣṭhānumatena | ‘**asvatantrāḥ’** putrā iti sambandhaḥ |

**atha jīvatpitṛkavibhāgaḥ**

tatra manu-viṣṇū [manu 9.209; vi. 18.43] |

> paitṛkāt tu pitṛdravyam anavāpyaṃ yad āpnuyāt |  
> na tat putrair bhajet sārdham akāmaḥ svayam ārjitam ||

‘**anavāpyam’** aśaktyādinā pitrā yad upekṣitaṃ tad anyenāptum aśakyam |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.121] |

> bhūr yā pitāmahopāttā nibandho dravyam eva vā |  
> tatra syāt sadṛśaṃ svāmyaṃ pituḥ putrasya cobhayoḥ ||

‘**nibandhaḥ’** ākarādau rājādidattaṃ niyataṃ labhyam |

bṛhaspatiḥ [26.14, 58, 59] |

> dravya pitāmahopātte sthāvare jaṅgame tathā |  
> samam aṃśitvam ākhyātaṃ pituḥ putrasya caiva hi ||  
> paitāmahaṃ hṛtaṃ pitrā svaśaktyā yad upārjitam |  
> vidyāśauryādināvāptaṃ tatra svāmyaṃ pituḥ smṛtam ||

**[653]** > pradānaṃ svecchayā kuryād bhāgaṃ caiva tato dhanāt |  
> tadabhāve tu tanayāḥ samāṃśāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ||

‘atha putrā vibhajeran’ ity adhikākre nāradaḥ [13.3] |

> mātur nivṛtte rajasi prattāsu bhaginīṣu ca |  
> nivṛtte cāpi ramaṇe pitary uparataspṛhe ||

‘**nivṛtte ramaṇe’** ratiśaktau nivṛttāyām |

bṛhaspatiḥ [26.9] |

> pitror abhāve bhrātṝṇāṃ vibhāgaḥ saṃpradarśitaḥ |  
> mātur nivṛtte rajasi jīvator api śasyate ||

śāṅkhalikhitau: “jīvati vā pitari rikthavibhāgo ‘numataḥ | prakāśaṃ vā mitho vā dharmataḥ” |

hārītaḥ: “jīvann eva vā pravibhajya vanam āśrayet | vṛddhāśramaṃ vā gacchet | svalpena vā saṃvibhajya bhūyiṣṭham ādāya vaseta | sa yady upadaśyet punas tebhyo gṛhṇīyāt | kṣīṇāṃś ca vibhajet” |

**[654]** ‘**upadaśyet’** upakṣīyeta |

viṣṇuḥ [17.1]: “pitā cet putrāṇ vibhajet tasya svecchā svayam upātte ‘rthe” |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.114–15] |

> vibhāgaṃ cet pitā kuryāt svecchayā vibhajet sutān |  
> jyeṣṭhe vā śreṣṭhabhāgena sarve vā syuḥ samāṃśinaḥ ||  
> yadi kuryāt samān aṃśān patnyaḥ kāryāḥ samāṃśikāḥ |  
> na dattaṃ strīdhanaṃ yāsāṃ bhartrā vā śvaśureṇa vā ||

nāradaḥ [16.12] |

> dvāv aṃśau pratipadyeta vibhajann ātmanaḥ pitā |

pitradhikāre śaṅkhalikhitau: “sa yady ekaputraḥ syād dvau bhāgāv ātmanaḥ kuryād dvipadacatuṣpadeṣu rūpam adhikam | vṛṣabho jyeṣṭhāya | gṛhaṃ yavīyase | anyatra pitur avasthānāt” |

baudhāyanaḥ [2.3.6–7]: “daśānāṃ caikam uddharej jyeṣṭhaḥ | samam itare vibhajeran” |

‘**daśānām’** gavāśvādirūpāṇām |

**[655]** āpastambaḥ [2.13.12; 2.14.1]: “ekadhanena jyeṣṭhaṃ toṣayitvā | jīvan putrebhyo vibhajet samaṃ klībam unamattaṃ patitaṃ parihāpya” |

‘**ekadhanena’** ekena dhanena gavādinā |

manuḥ [9.215] |

> bhrātṝṇām avibhaktānāṃ yady utthānaṃ bhavet saha |  
> na tatra viṣamaṃ bhāgaṃ pitā dadyāt kathaṃcana ||

nāradaḥ [16.15] |

> pitraiva tu vibhaktā ye samanyūnādhikair dhanaiḥ |  
> teṣāṃ sa eva dharmaḥ syāt sarvasyaiva pitā prabhuḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26.15] |

> samanyūnādhikā bhāgāḥ pitrā yeṣāṃ prakalpitāḥ |  
> tathaiva te pālanīyā vineyās te syur anyathā ||

**atha pramītapitṛkavibhāgaḥ**

**tatroddhāraḥ**

tatra manuḥ [9.112–14] |

> jyeṣṭhasya viṃśa uddhāraḥ sarvadravyāc ca yad varam |  
> tato ‘rdhaṃ madhyamasya syāt turīyaṃ tu yavīyasaḥ ||

**[656]** > jyeṣṭhaś caiva kaniṣṭhaś ca saṃharetāṃ yathoditam |  
> ye ‘nye jyeṣṭhakaniṣṭhābhyāṃ yeṣāṃ syān madhyamaṃ dhanam ||  
> sarveṣāṃ dhanajātānām ādadītāgryam agrajaḥ |  
> yac ca sātiśayaṃ kiṃcid daśataḥ prāpnuyād varam ||

‘**jyeṣṭhasya viṃśa uddhāra’** ityādi — madhyamād dhanād viṃśatitamo bhāgo jyeṣṭhasyoddhṛto adhiko grāhyaḥ syāt | ardhaturīyabhāgau ca viṃśatitamabhāgāpekṣayaiva | tena madhyamād dhanāt catvāriṃśattamo bhāgo madhyamasyoddhṛto ‘dhiko grāhyaḥ | kaniṣṭhasyāśītitama ity uktaṃ bhavati | guṇavajjyeṣṭhādiviṣayaś cāyam uddhāraḥ |

gautamaḥ [28.5–8]: “viṃśatibhāgo jyeṣṭhasya mithunam ubhayatodadyukto ratho govṛṣaḥ | kāṇakhorakūṭavaṇḍā madhyamasyānekāś cet | avir dhānyāyasī gṛham ano yuktaṃ catuṣpadāṃ caikaikaṃ yavīyasaḥ | samadhetarat sarvam” |

‘**kūṭaḥ’** śṛṅgavikalaḥ | ‘**vaṇḍo’** bālāvir ahitaḥ | ‘**anaḥ’** śakaṭam |

**[657]** hārītaḥ: “vibhajiṣyamāṇe gavāṃ samūhe vṛṣabham ekadhanaṃ variṣṭhadhanaṃ vā jyeṣṭhāya dadyuḥ | devatāgṛhaṃ ca | itare niṣkramya kuryuḥ | ekasminn eva vā dakṣiṇaṃ jyeṣṭhāyānupūrvyam itareṣām” |

‘**ekadhanam’** utkṛṣṭadhanam | ‘**devatāḥ’** pūjyaviṣṇvādipratimāḥ | ‘**gṛham’** paitṛkam | ‘**niṣkramya kuryuḥ’** iti, ātmavāsārthaṃ gṛhāntarāṇīti śeṣaḥ | ‘**ekasminn eva’** ityāder ayam arthaḥ — yadā niṣkramya gṛhāntarakaraṇāsaṃbhavas tadā ‘**dakṣiṇam’** pradhānaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ ‘**jyeṣṭhāya’** jyeṣṭhārthaṃ bhaved ity arthaḥ |

āpastambaḥ [2.14.7–8]: “deśaviśeṣe suvarṇaṃ kṛṣṇā gāvaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ bhaumaṃ jyeṣṭhasya | rathaḥ pituḥ paribhāṇḍaṃ ca” |

‘**bhaumam’** bhūmau jātaṃ tilamāṣādi | ‘**paribhāṇḍam’** bhojanapātrādi |

baudhāyanaḥ [2.2.9]: “asati pitari caturṇāṃ varṇānāṃ go’śvājāvayo jyeṣṭhāṃśaḥ” |

devalaḥ |

> putrāṇāṃ madhyamo dāyaḥ samānānām apīṣyate |  
> jyeṣṭhasya daśamaṃ bhāgaṃ nyāyavṛttasya nirdiśet ||

‘**madhyamo dāyaḥ’** madhyamaṃ dhanaṃ viṃśatitamo bhāgaḥ |

**[658]**

**anekamātṛkabhrātṛvibhāgaḥ**

atha manuḥ [9.122–24] |

> putraḥ kaniṣṭho jyeṣṭhāyāṃ kaniṣṭhāyāṃ ca pūrvajaḥ |  
> kathaṃ tatra vibhāgaḥ syād iti cet saṃśayo bhavet ||  
> ekaṃ vṛṣabham uddhāraṃ saṃhareta sa pūrvajaḥ |  
> tato ‘pare ‘jyeṣṭhavṛṣās tadūnānāṃ svamātṛtaḥ ||  
> jyeṣṭhas tu jāto jyeṣṭhāyāṃ hared vṛṣabhaṣoḍaśāḥ |  
> tataḥ svamātṛtaḥ śeṣā bhajerann iti dhāraṇā ||

‘**saḥ’** pūrvasyāṃ jātaḥ | ‘**pūrvajo’** jyaiṣṭhineyaḥ kanīyān ucyate | ‘**tato ‘pare’** iti, tataḥ śreṣṭhavṛṣādye ‘pare ‘śreṣṭhavṛṣās te svamātṛta ūnānāṃ vayasā jyeṣṭhānāṃ bhavantīty arthaḥ | ‘**vṛṣabhaṣoḍaśāḥ’** vṛṣabhāḥ ṣoḍaśa yāsāṃ tās tathā | ‘**śeṣā’** gāvaḥ |

**[659]** gautamaḥ [28.14–16]: “ṛṣabho ‘dhiko jyeṣṭhasya | rṣabhaṣoḍaśā jyaiṣṭhineyasya | samadhā vājyeṣṭhineyena yavīyasām” |

‘**samadhā’** samaprakāreṇa |

śaṅkhalikhitau: “ṛṣabho ‘dhiko jyeṣṭhāya | gṛhaṃ yavīyase | anyatra pitur avasthānāt” |

bṛhaspatiḥ [26.24–25] |

> yady ekajātā bahavaḥ samānā jātisaṃkhyayā |  
> sāpatnyās tair vibhaktavyaṃ mātṛbhāgena dharmataḥ ||  
> savarṇā bhinnasaṃkhyā ye puṃbhāgas teṣu śasyate |

manuḥ [9.115] |

> uddhāro na daśasv asti saṃpannānāṃ svakarmasu |  
> yat kiṃcid eva deyaṃ syāj jyāyase mānavardhanam ||

‘**daśasu’** gavādiṣu iti śeṣaḥ |

**[660]** tathā [9.125–26] |

> sadṛśastrīṣu jātānāṃ putrāṇām aviśeṣataḥ |  
> na mātṛto jyaiṣṭhyam asti janmato jyaiṣṭhyam ucyate ||  
> janmajyeṣṭhena cāhvānaṃ subrahmaṇyāsv ap smṛtam |  
> yamayoś caiva garbheṣu janmato jyeṣṭhatā smṛtā ||

‘**subrahmaṇyā’** nāma mantraviśeṣo jyotiṣṭome chandogair gīyate ‘indra āgaccha’ ityādi |

devalaḥ |

> bahirvarṇeṣu cārityād yamayoḥ pūrvajanmataḥ |  
> yasya jātasya yamayoḥ paśyanti prathamaṃ mukham ||  
> santānaḥ pitaraś caiva tasmin jyaiṣṭhyaṃ pratiṣṭhitam |

manuḥ [9.213] |

> yo jyeṣṭho vinikurvīta lobhād bhrātṝn yavīyasaḥ |  
> so ‘jyeṣṭhaḥ syād abhāgī ca niyantavyaś ca rājabhiḥ ||

‘**vinikurvīta’** vañcayet |

manuḥ [9.116–17] |

> evaṃ samuddhṛtoddhāre samān aṃśān prakalpayet |  
> uddhāre ‘nuddhṛte tv eṣām iyaṃ syād aṃśakalpanā ||

**[661]** > ekādhikaṃ harej jyeṣṭhaḥ putro ‘dhyardhaṃ tato ‘nujaḥ |  
> aṃśam aṃśaṃ yavīyāṃsa iti dharmo vyavasthitaḥ ||

gautamaḥ [28.9–13]: “dvyaṃśaṃ vā pūrvajasya syāt | ekaikam itareṣām | ekaikaṃ vā dhanarūpaṃ kāmyaṃ pūrvaḥ pūrvo labheta | daśataḥ paśūnām | naikaśaphadvipadānām” |

‘**daśataḥ’** paśūnām iti | daśapaśūn labhata ity arthaḥ |

vasiṣṭhaḥ [17.40, 42–45]: “atha bhrātṝṇāṃ dāya[vi]bhāgaḥ | dvyaṃśaṃ harej jyeṣṭhaḥ | gavāśvasya cānudaśamam | ajāvayo gṛhaṃ ca kaniṣṭhasya | kārṣṇāyasaṃ gṛhopakaraṇāni ca madhyamasya” |

‘**gavāśvasya cānudaśamam’** iti — gavāśvānāṃ daśānām ekaikam uddhṛtya jyeṣṭho gṛhṇīyāt ity arthaḥ |

nāradaḥ [16.13–14] |

> jyeṣṭhāṃśo ‘dhiko deyaḥ kaniṣṭhāvāvaraḥ smṛtaḥ |  
> samāṃśabhāgāḥ śeṣāḥ syur aprattā bhaginī tathā ||  
> kṣetrajeṣu ca putreṣu tadvaj jāteṣu dharmataḥ ||

‘**kṣetrajeṣu dharmato jāteṣu’** | ‘**tadvat’** aurasavad bhāgakalpanā kartavyety arthaḥ |

nāradaḥ [13.3] |

> mātur nivṛtte rajasi prattāsu bhaginīṣu ca |  
> nivṛtte cāpi ramaṇe pitary uparataspṛhe ||

**[662]** bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26.21] |

> janmavidyāguṇajyeṣṭho dvyaṃśaṃ dāyam avāpnuyāt |  
> samāṃśabhāginas tv anye teṣāṃ pitṛsamas tu saḥ ||

uśanā |

> varṇānām anulomānāṃ vibhāgo ‘yaṃ prakīrtitaḥ |  
> samatvenaikajātānāṃ vibhāgas tu vidhīyate ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.117] |

> vibhajeran sutāḥ pitror ūrdhvam ṛktham ṛṇaṃ samam |

tathā [2.120] |

> sāmānyārthasamutthāne vibhāgas tu samaḥ kṛtaḥ |  
> anekapitṛkāṇāṃ tu pitṛto bhāgakalpanā ||

‘**sāmānyārthasamutthāne’** iti | yadā sāmānyasyārthasya kṛṣyādinā samyag utthāne vardhanaṃ bhavati, tadā samo vibhāgaḥ | na tatra bahutaram anenopāttam ity apekṣā kartavya ity arthaḥ | ‘**anekapitṛkāṇām’** iti | anekabhrāfṛṇāṃ ye putrāḥ teṣāṃ samaviṣamasaṃkhyākānām api paitāmahe dhane vibhajyamāne tatpitṝṇāṃ yo hy aṃśaḥ sa eva teṣām, na punaḥ pratyekam aṃśakalpanety arthaḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ [26.18] |

> samavetais tu yat prāptaṃ sarve tatra samāṃśinaḥ |  
> tat putrāḥ viṣamasamāḥ pitṛbhāgaharāḥ smṛtāḥ ||

**[663]** kātyāyanaḥ [855–56] |

> avibhakte nije prete tatsutaṃ rikthabhāginam |  
> kurvīta jīvanaṃ yena labdhaṃ naiva pitāmahāt ||  
> labhetāṃśaṃ sa pitryaṃ tu pitṛvyāt tasya vā sutāt |  
> sa evāṃśas tu sarveṣāṃ bhrātṝṇāṃ nyāyato bhavet ||  
> labheta tatsuto vāpi nivṛttiḥ parato bhavet ||

devalaḥ |

> avibhaktavibhaktānāṃ kulyānāṃ vasatāṃ saha |  
> bhūyo dāyavibhāgaḥ syād ā caturthād iti sthitiḥ ||  
> tāvat kulyāḥ sapiṇḍāḥ syuḥ piṇḍabhedas tv anantaram |  
> samam icchanti piṇḍānāṃ dāyārthasy vibhājanam ||  
> vidhir eṣa savarṇānāṃ bahūnāṃ samudāhṛtaḥ |  
> eka eva savarṇaḥ syād dāyo ‘tra na vibhajyate ||

‘avibhaktavibhaktānām’ avibhaktānāṃ vibhaktānāṃ ca |

vasiṣṭhaḥ [17.40–41]: “atha bhrātṝṇāṃ dāyavibhāgaḥ | yāś cānapatyāḥ striyas tāsāṃ cāputralābhāt” |

‘**striyo’** atra bhrātṛbhāryāḥ | ‘**ā putralābhād’** iti — tāś ca yadi saṃbhāvitaputralābhās tadā tāsām api bhāgo deyaḥ | yadi tu putro notpadyate tadāsau bhāgo bhrātṝṇām | tāsāṃ tu bharaṇamātram |

**[664]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.123] |

> pitur ūrdhvaṃ vibhajatāṃ mātāpy aṃśaṃ samaṃ haret |

pitety anuvṛttau bṛhaspatiḥ [26] |

> tadabhāve tu jananī tanayānāṃ samāṃśinī |

tathā |

> samāṃśā mātaras teṣāṃ turīyāṃśā ca kanyakā |

‘**turīyāṃśaḥ’** sajātīyasya bhrātur yāvān aṃśas tadapekṣayā caturtho bhāgaḥ saṃskārārthaṃ pitṛdhane kalpanīyaḥ | yat tu viṣṇuvacanam [18.34–35]: “mātaraḥ putrabhāgānusāreṇa bhāgahāriṇyo anūḍhāś ca duhitaraḥ” iti, tad apy etadvacanānusārāt duhitṝṇāṃ caturthabhāgaparam |

vyāsaḥ |

> asutās tu pituḥ patnyaḥ samānāṃśā prakīrtitāḥ |  
> pitāmahyaś ca tāḥ sarvā mātṛtulyā prakīrtitāḥ ||

atha bṛhaspatiḥ [26.19] |

> pitṛṛkthaharāḥ putrāḥ sarva eva yathāṃśataḥ |  
> vidyākarmayutas teṣām adhikaṃ labdhum arhati ||  
> vidyāvijñānaśauryārthajñānadānakriyāsu ca |  
> yasyeha prathitā kīrtiḥ pitaras tena putriṇaḥ ||

**[665]** nāradaḥ [16.35] |

> kuṭumbārtheṣu yo yuktas tat karyaṃ kurute tu yaḥ |  
> sa bhrātṛbhir bṛhaṇīyo grāsācchādanavāhanaiḥ ||

manuḥ [9.207] |

> bhrātṝṇāṃ yas tu neheta dhanaṃ śaktaḥ svakarmaṇā |  
> sa nirbhājyaḥ svakāḍ aṃśāt kiṃcid datvopajīvanam ||

āpastambaḥ [2.14.14–15]: “sarve hi dharmayuktā bhāginaḥ | yas tv adharmeṇa dravyāṇi pratipādayati jyeṣṭho ‘pi tam abhāgaṃ kurvīta” |

**atha vibhāgānarhāḥ **

tatra gautamaḥ [28.41]: “savarṇāputro ‘py anyāyavṛtto na labhetaikeṣām” |

**[666]** manuḥ [9.214] |

> sarva eva vikarmasthā nārhanti bhrātaro dhanam |

śaṅkhalikhitau: “apapātritasya rikthapiṇḍodakāni nārhanti bhrātaro dhanam” |

bṛhaspatiḥ [26.34–37] |

> savarṇājo ‘py aguṇavān nārhaḥ syāt paitṛke dhane |  
> tatpiṇḍadāḥ śrotriyā ye teṣāṃ tad abhidhīyate ||  
> uttamarṇādhamarṇebhyaḥ pitaraṃ trāyate sutaḥ |  
> atas tadviparītena nāsti tena prayojanam ||  
> tayā gavā kiṃ kriyate yā na dhenur na garbhiṇī |  
> ko ‘rthas tena tu putreṇa yo na vidvān na dhārmikaḥ ||  
> śāstraśauryārtharahitas tapojñānavivarjitaḥ |  
> ācārahīnaḥ putras tu mūtroccārasamas tu saḥ ||

manuḥ [9.201–03] |

> anaṃśau klībapatitau jātyandhabadhirau tathā |  
> unmattajaḍamūkās tu ye ca kecin nirindriyāḥ ||  
> sarveṣām api tan nyāyyaṃ dātuṃ śaktyā manīṣiṇā |  
> grāsācchādanam atyantaṃ patito hy adadad bhavet ||

**[667]** > yady arthitā tu dāraiḥ syāt klībādīnāṃ kathaṃcana |  
> teṣām utpannatantūnām apatyaṃ dāyam arhati ||

‘**nirindriyāḥ’** paṅgvādayaḥ | ‘**klībādīnām’** ity atadguṇasaṃvijñāno bahuvrīhiḥ |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.140–42] |

> patitas tatsutaḥ klībaḥ paṅgur unmattako jaḍaḥ |  
> andho ‘cikitsyarogādyā bhartavyās tu niraṃśakāḥ ||  
> aurasāḥ kṣetrajās teṣāṃ nirdoṣā bhāgahāriṇaḥ |  
> sutāś caiṣāṃ prabhartavyā yāvad vai bhartṛsātkṛtāḥ ||

**[668]** > aputrā yoṣitaś caiva bhartavyāḥ sādhuvṛttayaḥ |  
> nirvāsyā vyabhicāriṇyaḥ pratikūlās tathaiva ca ||

nāradaḥ [16.21] |

> pitṛdviṭ patataḥ ṣaṇḍo yaś ca syād apapātritaḥ |  
> aurasā api naite ‘ṃśaṃ labheran kṣetrajāḥ kutaḥ ||

‘**apapātritaḥ’** rājavadhādinā doṣeṇa bāndhavair yasya ghaṭāpavarjanaṃ kṛtam |

devalaḥ |

> mṛte na pitari klībakuṣṭhyunmattajaḍāndhakāḥ |  
> patitaḥ patitāpatyaṃ liṅgī dāyāṃśabhāginaḥ ||  
> teṣāṃ patitavarjebhyo bhaktavastraṃ pradīyate |  
> tatputrāḥ pitṛdāyāṃśaṃ labheran doṣavarjitāḥ ||

‘**mṛte na pitari’** iti | mṛte pitari klībādayo nāṃśabhāgina iti saṃbandhaḥ |

viṣṇuḥ [15.32–39]: “patitaklībāciktsyarogavikalās tv abhāgahāriṇaḥ | rikthagrāhibhis te bhartavyāḥ | teṣāṃ caurasāḥ putrā bhāgahāriṇaḥ | na tu patitasya | patanīye kṛte **[669]** karmaṇy anantarotpannāḥ | pratilomās tu strīṣu cotpannāś cābhāginaḥ | tatputrāḥ paitāmahe ‘py arthe | aṃśagrāhibhis te bharaṇīyāḥ” |

gautamaḥ [28.44–46]: “jaḍaklībau bhartavyau | apatyaṃ jaḍasya bhāgārham | śūdrāputravat pratilomāsu” |

‘**śūdrāputravat pratilomāsu’** iti, śūdrāputro ‘py anapatyaśuśrūṣuś cel labheta vṛttim antevāsividhinā tatputroktaprakāreṇa | yathā śūdrāputro jīvanamātraṃ labhata evaṃ pratilomāsuto ‘pīti |

kātyāyanaḥ [862–65] |

> akramoḍhāsutaś caiva sagotrādyaś ca jāyate |  
> pravrajyāvasitaś caiva na rikthaṃ teṣu karhicit ||  
> akramoḍhāsutas tv ṛkthī savarṇaś ca yadā pituḥ |  
> asavarṇaprasūtaś ca kramoḍhāyāṃ tu yad bhavet ||  
> pratilomaprasūtā yā tasyāḥ putro na rikthabhāk |  
> grāsācchādanam atyantaṃ deyaṃ tadbandhubhiḥ smṛtam ||  
> bandhūnām apy alābhe tu pitryaṃ dravyaṃ tad āpnuyāt |  
> apitryaṃ tad dhanaṃ prāptaṃ dāpanīyā na bāndhavaiḥ ||

‘**kramoḍāsuto’** atra akramoḍhāyām asavarṇāyāṃ jātaḥ so ‘rikthī | evaṃ kramoḍhāyāṃ savarṇena jātaḥ ṛkthabhāg iti | ‘**sagotrādyaś ca jāyate’** iti — **[670]** sagotrāyāṃ vivāhitāyāṃ sagotrādyo jāyate ‘sau [na] ṛkthabhāg ity arthaḥ | ‘**dāpanīyā na bāndhavaiḥ’** grāsācchādanam api na dāpayitavyā ity anvayaḥ |

**athāsaṃkṛtasṃskaraṇam**

tatra nāradaḥ [16.33–34] |

> yeṣāṃ ca na kṛtāḥ pitrā saṃskāravidhayaḥ kramāt |  
> kartavyā bhrātṛbhis teṣāṃ paitṛkād eva taddhanāt ||  
> avidyamāne pitrye ‘rthe svāṃśād uddhṛtya vā punaḥ |  
> avaśyakāryāḥ saṃskārā bhrātṝṇāṃ pūrvasaṃskṛtaiḥ ||

devalaḥ |

> kanyābhyaś ca pitṛdravyaṃ deyaṃ vaivāhikaṃ vasu |  
> aputrakasya kanyā svā dharmajā putravad dharet ||

**[671]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.124] |

> asaṃskṛtā tu saṃskāryā bhrātṛbhiḥ pūrvasaṃskṛtaiḥ |  
> bhaginyaś ca nijād aṃśād aṃśaṃ kṛtvā turīyakam ||

viṣṇuḥ [15.31]: “anūḍhāyāḥ kanyāyāḥ svavittānusāreṇa saṃskāraṃ kuryāt” |

manuḥ [9.118] |

> svebhyaḥ svebhyas tu kanyābhyaḥ pradadyur bhrātaraḥ pṛthak |  
> svāt svād aṃśāc caturbhāgaṃ patitāḥ syur aditsavaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ [858] |

> kanyakānāṃ tv adattānāṃ caturtho bhāga iṣyate |  
> putrāṇāṃ ca trayo bhāgāḥ svāmyaṃ svalpe dhane smṛtam ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: “vibhajyamāne dāyārthe kanyālaṃkāraṃ vaivāhikaṃ strīdhanaṃ kanyā labhet” |

baudhāyanaḥ [2.3.44]: “mātur alaṃkāraṃ duhitaraḥ sāṃpradāyikaṃ labherann anyad vā” |

**[672]** ‘na dāyam arhati strī’ ity anuvṛttau punar baudhāyanaḥ: “nirindriyā adāyāś ca striyo matā iti śrutiḥ” |

**atha vibhājyam**

tatra kātyāyanaḥ [840, 850] |

> paitāmahaṃ ca pitryaṃ ca yac cānyat svayam arjitam |  
> dāyādānāṃ vibhāge tu sarvam etad vibhajyate ||  
> ṛkthaṃ prītipradattaṃ tu datvā śeṣaṃ vibhāvayet |  
> ā caturthāt tu tad grāhyaṃ krameṇaiva hi tatsutaiḥ ||

‘**ā caturthā’** puruṣāt |

nāradaḥ [16.32] |

> yac chiṣṭaṃ pitṛdāyebhyo datvarṇaṃ paitṛkaṃ ca yat |  
> bhrātṛbhis tad vibhaktavyam ṛṇī syād anyathā pitā ||

kātyāyanaḥ [846–49, 841–42] |

> bhrātrā pitṛvyamātṛbhyāṃ kuṭumbārtham ṛṇaṃ kṛtam |  
> vibhāgakāle dātavyam ṛṇibhiḥ sarvam eva tu ||

**[673]** > tad ṛṇaṃ dhanene deyaṃ nānyathaiva pradāpayet |  
> bhāvitaṃ cet pramāṇena virodhāt parato yadā ||  
> pitryaṃ pitryarṇasaṃbaddham ātmīyaṃ cātmanā kṛtam |  
> ṛṇam evaṃvidhaṃ śodhyaṃ vibhāge bandhubhiḥ saha ||  
> dharmārthaṃ prītidattaṃ ca yad ṛṇaṃ svaniyojitam |  
> tad dṛśyamānaṃ vibhajen na dānaṃ paitṛkād dhanāt ||  
> dṛśyamānaṃ vibhajyeta gṛhaṃ kṣetraṃ catuṣpadam |  
> gūḍhadravyābhiśaṅkāyāṃ pratyayas tv atra kīrtitaḥ ||  
> gṛhopaskaravāhyās tu dohyābharaṇakarmiṇaḥ |  
> dṛśyamānā vibhajyante kośaṃ gūḍhe ‘bravīd bhṛguḥ ||

‘**tad ṛṇaṃ dhane deyam’** ityāder arthaḥ — **vibhāgakāle**, ‘**virodhāt’** parasparavipratipattau, yan na dattaṃ ‘**tad ṛṇam’**, ‘**parataḥ’** uttarakālam, yadā deyaṃ bhavati tadā ‘**pramāṇena cet vibhāvitam’** bhavati tato deyaṃ nāparata iti | ‘**pitryarṇasaṃbaddham’** pitryarṇapariśodhanārthaṃ yat ‘**kṛtaṃ’** ātmīyaṃ kuṭumbārthaṃ parakṛtam api ‘**ātmanā kṛtam’** api kuṭumbārtham eva | ‘**dharmārthaṃ prītidattam’** iti — svayam asādhāraṇyena sādhāraṇadhanaṃ ‘**dharmārtham’** dattam, prītyā ca yad dattam, ‘**ṛṇaṃ yat’** svayam uttamarṇatvenānyasmai dattaṃ tat jñāyamānaṃ vibhaktavyam | yato ‘vibhaktāt paitṛkād dhanād asādāraṇyena dānaṃ nocitam iti |

**[674]** manuḥ [9.119] |

> ajāvikaṃ caikaśaphaṃ na jātu viṣamaṃ bhajet |  
> ajāvikaṃ tu viṣamaṃ jyeṣṭhasyaiva vidhīyate ||

**athāvibhājyam**

tatra manuḥ [9.206] |

> vidyādhanaṃ tu yady asya tat tasyaiva dhanaṃ bhavet |  
> maitram audvāhikaṃ caiva mādhuparkikam eva ca ||

‘**mādhuparkikam’** madhuparkakāle pūjyatayā yal labdham |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.119] |

> kramād abhyāgataṃ dravyaṃ hṛtam abhyuddharet tu yaḥ |  
> dāyādebhyo na tad dadyād vidyayā labdham eva ca ||

**[675]** vyāsaḥ |

> vidyāprāptaṃ śauryadhanaṃ yac ca saudāyikaṃ bhavet |  
> vibhāgakāle tat tasya nānveṣṭavyaṃ svaṛkthibhiḥ ||

‘**saudāyikam’** itthaṃ kātyāyanena lakṣitam [971] |

> ūḍhayā kanyayā vāpi patyuḥ pitṛgṛhād api |  
> bhrātuḥ sakāśāt pitror yal labdhaṃ saudāyikaṃ smṛtam ||

gautamaḥ [28.31]: “svayam arjitam avaidyebhyo vaidyaḥ kāmaṃ na dadyāt” |

‘**vaidyo’** vidvān |

kātyāyanaḥ [875] |

> nāvidyānāṃ tu vaidyena deyaṃ vidyādhanāt kvacit |  
> samavidyādhikānāṃ tu deyaṃ vaidyena tad dhanam ||

nāradaḥ [16.11] |

> vaidyo ‘vaidyāya nākāmo dadyād aṃśaṃ svato dhanāt |  
> pitryaṃ dravyaṃ samāśritya na cet tena tad āhṛtam ||

**[676]** **vibhajed** ity anuvṛttau punar nāradaḥ [16.5–7] |

> śauryabhāryādhane hitvā yat tu vidyādhanaṃ bhavet |  
> trīṇy etāny avibhājyāni prasādo yaś ca paitṛkaḥ ||  
> mātrā ca svadhanaṃ dattaṃ yasmai syāt prītipūrvakam |  
> tasyāpy eṣo vidhir dṛṣṭo mātāpīṣṭe yathā pitā ||

vyāsaḥ |

> pitāmahena yad dattaṃ pitrā vā prītipūrvakam |  
> tasya tan nāpahartavyaṃ mātrā dattaṃ ca yad bhavet ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.115] |

> pitṛdravyāvināśena yad anyat svayam arjitam |  
> maitram audvāhikaṃ caiva dāyādānāṃ na tad bhavet ||

manu-viṣṇū [manu 9.208; vi 18.42] |

> anupaghnan pitṛdravyaṃ śrameṇa yad upārjayet |  
> svayam īhitalabdhaṃ ca nākāmo dātum arhati ||

vyāsaḥ |

> anāśritya pitṛdravyaṃ svaśakyāpnoti yad dhanam |  
> dāyādebhyo na tad dadyād vidyālabdhaṃ ca yad bhavet ||

**[677]** kātyāyanaḥ [867, 870, 873, 871, 872, 876, 878–80] |

> parabhaktapradānena prāptavidyo yadānyataḥ   
> tayā prāptaṃ ca vidhinā vidyāprāptaṃ tad ucyate ||  
> upanyaste ca yal labdhaṃ labdhaṃ prādhyayanāc ca yat |  
> vidyādhanaṃ tu tat prāhuḥ sāmānyaṃ yad ato ‘nyathā ||  
> śiṣyād ārtvijyataḥ praśnāt saṃdhigdhapraśnanirṇayāt |  
> svajñānśaṃsanād vādāl labdhaṃ prādhyayanāc ca yat ||  
> vidyādhanaṃ tu tat prāhur vibhāge na vibhajyate |  
> śilpiṣv api hi dharmo ‘yaṃ mūlyād yac cādhikaṃ bhavet ||
