> vidyāpaṇakṛtaṃ caiva yājyataḥ śiṣyatas tathā |  
> etad vidyādhanaṃ prāhuḥ sāmānyaṃ yad ato ‘nyathā ||  
> paraṃ nirasya yal labdhaṃ vidyayā paṇapūrvakam |  
> vidyādhanaṃtu tad vidyān na vibhājyaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ ||  
> vidyāpratijñayā labdhaṃ śiṣyād āptaṃ ca yad bhavet |  
> ṛtviṅnyāyena yal labdham etad vidyādhanaṃ bhṛguḥ ||

**[678]**  
> āruhya saṃśayaṃ yatra prasabhaṃ karma kurvate |  
> tasmin karmaṇi tuṣṭena prasādaḥ svāminā kṛtaḥ ||  
> tatra labdhaṃ tu yat kiṃcit dhanaṃ śauryeṇa tad bhavet |  
> dhvajāhṛtaṃ bhaved yat tu vibhājyaṃ naiva tat smrtam ||  
> saṃgrāmād āhṛtaṃ yat tu vidrāvya dvaṣatāṃ balam |  
> svāmyarthe jīvitaṃ tyaktvā tad dhvajāhṛtam ucyate ||  
> yal labdhaṃ lābhakāle tu svajātyā kanyayā saha |  
> kanyāgataṃ tu tad vittaṃ śulkaṃ vṛddhikaraṃ smṛtam ||  
> vaivāhikaṃ tu tad vidyād bhāryayā yat samāhṛtam |  
> dhanam evaṃvidhaṃ sarvaṃ vijñeyaṃ karmasādhakam ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: “na vāstuvibhāgo nodapātrālaṃkārānuyuktastrīvāsasām apāṃ pracāravartmanāṃ vibhāgaś ceti prajāpatiḥ” |

manu-viṣṇū [ma. 9.219; vi. 18.44] |

> vastraṃ patram alaṃkāraḥ kṛtānnam udakaṃ striyaḥ |  
> yogakṣemapracāraṃ ca na vibhājyaṃ pracakṣate ||

**[679]** ‘**vastram’** samūlyam aṅgadhṛtam | ‘**patra**’śabdo ‘tra lekhyaniviṣṭadhanaparaḥ | ‘dhanapatraviśiṣṭaṃ tu’ iti kātyāyanavacanānusārāt | ‘**striyaḥ’** saṃyuktāḥ, ‘avibhāgaḥ strīṣu saṃyuktāsu’ [28.48] iti gautamavacanāt | ‘**yogakṣemam’** mantripurohitādi yogakṣemahetutvāt | ‘**pracāraḥ’** gavādīnāṃ pracāraṇamārgaḥ |

vyāsaḥ |

> avibhājyaṃ sagotrāṇām ā sahasrakulād api |  
> yājyaṃ kṣetraṃ ca pātraṃ ca kṛtānnam udakaṃ striyaḥ ||

‘**kṣetram’** vāstukṣetram |

**[680]** kātyāyanaḥ [882–84] |

> dhanaṃ patraniviṣṭaṃ tu dharmārthaṃ yan nirūpitam |  
> udakaṃ caiva dārāś ca nibandho yaḥ kramāgataḥ ||  
> dhṛtaṃ vastram alaṃkāro vānurūpaṃ ca yad bhavet |  
> yathākālopayuktāni tathā yojyāni bandhubhiḥ ||  
> gopracāraś ca rathyā ca vastraṃ yac cāṅgayojitam |  
> prayojyaṃ na vibhajyeta śilpārthaṃ ca bṛhaspatiḥ ||  
> deśasya jāteḥ saṅghasya dharmo grāmasya yo bhṛguḥ |  
> uditaḥ syāt sa tenaiva dāyadharmaṃ prakalpayet ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [26.47, 50, 51, 3, 2, 52] |

> vastrādayo ‘vibhājyā yair uktaṃ tair na vicāritam |  
> dhanaṃ bhavet samṛddhānāṃ patrālaṃkārasaṃsṛtam ||  
> madhyasthitam anājīvyaṃ dātuṃ naikasya śakyate |  
> yuktyā vibhajanīyaṃ tad anyathānarthakaṃ bhavet ||

**[681]** > vikrīya vastrābharaṇam ṛṇam udgrāhya lekhitam |  
> kṛtānnaṃ cākṛtānnena parivartya vibhajyate ||  
> uddhṛtya kūpavāpyambhas tv anusāreṇa gṛhyate |  
> yathābhāgānusāreṇa setuḥ kṣetre vibhajyate ||  
> ekāṃ strīṃ kārayet karma yathāṃśena gṛhe gṛhe |  
> bahvyaḥ samāṃśato deyā dāsānām apy ayaṃ vidhiḥ ||  
> yogakṣemavato lābhaḥ samatvena vibhajyate |  
> pracāraś ca yathāṃśena kartavya ṛṇibhiḥ saha ||

‘**yogakṣemavataḥ’** yogakṣemahetoḥ | atra ca vastrādīnāṃ prakāraviśeṣeṇa vibhājyatvam uktam | ato manvādīnāṃ vastrādyavibhājyatvavacanāni svarūpato vibhājyatāniṣedhaparāṇīty avirodhaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [874] |

> kule vinītavidyānāṃ bhrātṝṇāṃ pitṛto ‘pi vā |  
> śauryaprāptaṃ tu yad vittaṃ vibhājyaṃ tad bṛhaspatiḥ ||

**[682]** asyārthaḥ — [‘kule’] svakule pitāmahapitṛvyādibhyaḥ pitṛta eva vā śikṣitavidyānāṃ bhrātṝṇāṃ yat tu vidyāśauryaprāptaṃ dhanaṃ tadvibhāgakāle vibhaktavyam eveti |

nāradaḥ [16.10] |

> kuṭumbaṃ bibhṛyād bhrātur yo vidyām adhigacchataḥ |  
> bhāgaṃ vidyādhanas tasmāt sa labhetāśruto ‘pi san ||

‘**aśruto’** atra avidyaḥ |

manuḥ [9.204–05] |

> yat kiṃcit pitari prete dhanaṃ jyeṣṭho ‘dhigacchati |  
> bhāgo yavīyasāṃ tatra yadi vidyānupālinaḥ ||  
> avidyānāṃ tu sarveṣām īhātaś ced dhanaṃ bhavet |  
> samas tatra vibhāgaḥ syād apitrya iti dhāraṇā ||

‘**yat kiṃcid’** ityādi — pitṛdravyāvirodhenāpi yato jyeṣṭho dhanam arjayati tatra kaniṣṭhānām api vibhāgo bhavati yadi te vidyābhyāsaratā bhavanti | ‘**īhātaḥ’** kṛṣyādiceṣṭātaḥ |

vasiṣṭhaḥ [17.51]: “yena caiṣāṃ svayam utpāditaṃ syāt tad dvyaṃśam āharet” |

vyāsaḥ |

> sādhāraṇaṃ samāśritya yat kiṃcid vāhanāyudham |  
> śauryādināpnoti dhanaṃ bhrātaras tatra bhāginaḥ ||  
> tasya bhāgadvayaṃ kāryaṃ śeṣās tu samabhāginaḥ |

**atha strīdhanakṛtyam**

tatra manuḥ [9.199] |

> na nirhāraṃ striyaḥ kuryuḥ kuṭumbād bahumadhyagāt |  
> svakād api ca vittād dhi svasya bhartur anājñayā ||

‘**nirhāram’** niṣkṛṣya haraṇam | ‘**kuṭumba**’padena kuṭumbadhanaṃ tatsāhacaryād ihocyate | ‘**svakāt’** svabhartur asādhāraṇāt |

manu-viṣṇū [ma. 9.200; vi. 17.22] |

> patyau jīvati yaḥ strībhir alaṃkāro dhṛto bhavet |  
> na taṃ bhajeran dāyādā bhajamānāḥ patanti te ||

**[684]** āpastambaḥ [2.14.9]: “alaṃkāro bhāryāyā jñātidhanaṃ cety eke” |

nāradaḥ [4.28; nā. ma. saṃ. 2.24] |

> bhartrā prītena yad dattaṃ striyai tasmin mṛte ‘pi tat |  
> sā yathākāmam aśnīyāt dadyād vā sthāvarād ṛte ||

vyāsaḥ |

> dvisahasrapaṇo dāyaḥ striyaṃ deyo dhanasya tu |  
> yac ca bhartrā dhanaṃ dattaṃ sā yathākāmam āpnuyāt ||

kātyāyanaḥ [901, 905–07, 921] |

> ūḍhayā kanyayā vāpi patyuḥ pitṛgṛhe ‘pi vā |>   
> bhrātuḥ sakāśāt pitror vā labdhaṃ saudāyikaṃ smṛtam ||  
> saudāyikaṃ dhanaṃ strīṇāṃ prāpya svātantryam iṣyate |  
> yasmāt tadānṛśaṃsyārthaṃ tair dattaṃ tatparjīvanam ||  
> saudāyike sadā strīṇāṃ svātantryaṃ parikīrtitam |  
> vikraye caiva dāne ca yatheṣṭaṃ sthāvareṣv api ||

**[685]**  
> bhartṛdāyaṃ mṛte patyau vinyaset strī yatheṣṭataḥ |  
> vidyamāne tu saṃrakṣet kṣapayet tatkule ‘nyathā ||  
> aputrā śayanaṃ bhartuḥ pālayantī gurau sthitā |  
> bhuñjītāmaraṇāt kṣāntā dāyādā ūrdhvam āpnuyuḥ ||

‘patyur gṛhe’ iti saṃbandhaḥ | ‘bhrātuḥ pitror vā’ ity upalakṣaṇam, tenānyebhyo ‘pi | svamātāpitṛkulebhyo yal labdhaṃ dhanaṃ tat ‘saudāyikam’ | tatra ca ‘sthāvare’ api striyāḥ dānādiṣu svātantryam | bhartṛdatteṣu tu sthāvarātirikteṣv eva yatheṣṭaṃ dānādiṣv adhikāraḥ |

rājā ṛkthaṃ pālayed ity anuvṛttau manuḥ [8.28–29] |

> vaśāputrāsu caivaṃ syād rakṣaṇaṃ niṣkulāsu ca |  
> pativratāsu ca strīṣu vidhavāsv āturāsu ca ||  
> jīvantīnāṃ tu tāsāṃ ye tad dhareyuḥ svabāndhavāḥ |  
> tāñ chiṣyāc cauradaṇḍena dhārmikaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ ||

‘**vaśā’** vandhyā | ‘**aputrā’** mṛtaputrā | ‘**niṣkulā’** pranaṣṭamātāpitṛkulā |

devalaḥ |

> vṛttir ābaharaṇaṃ śulkaṃ lābhaś ca strīdhanaṃ bhavet |  
> bhoktrī ca svayam evedaṃ patir nārhaty anāpadi ||

**[686]** > mṛṣā mokṣe ca bhoge ca striyai dadyāt savṛddhikām |  
> putrān nirharaṇe cāpi strīdhanaṃ bhoktum arhati ||

kātyāyanaḥ [911–14] |

> na bhartā naiva ca suto na pitā bhrātaro na ca |  
> ādāne vā visarge vā strīdhane prabhaviṣṇavaḥ ||  
> yadi hy ekataras teṣāṃ strīdhanaṃ harate balāt |  
> savṛddhiṃ pratidāpyaḥ syād daṇḍaṃ caiva samāpnuyāt ||  
> tad eva yady anujñāpya bhakṣayet prītipūrvakam |  
> mūlam eva sa dāpyaḥ syād yadā sa dhanavān bhavet ||  
> vyādhitaṃ vyasanasthaṃ ca dhanikaiś copapīḍitam |  
> jñātvā nisṛṣṭaṃ yat prītyā dadyād ātmecchayā ca saḥ ||

**[687]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.147] |

> durbhikṣe dharmakāryārthe vyādhau saṃpratirodhake |  
> gṛhītaṃ strīdhanaṃ bhartā na striyai dātum arhati ||

kātyāyanaḥ [908–10] |

> yadi cet sa dvibhāryaḥ syān na ca tāṃ bhajate punaḥ |  
> prītyā visṛṣṭam api cet pratidāpyaḥ sa tad balāt ||  
> grāsācchādanavāsānām ācchedo yatra yoṣitaḥ |  
> tatra svam ādadīta strī vibhāgaṃ rikthināṃ tathā ||  
> likhitasyeti dharmo ‘yaṃ prāpte bhartṛkula vaset |  
> vyādhitā pretakāle tu gacched bandhukulaṃ tataḥ ||  
> yajñārthaṃ dravyam utpannaṃ tasmād dravyaṃ niyojayet |  
> sthāneṣu dharmajuṣṭeṣu na strīmūrkhavidharmiṣu ||

**[688]** > bhartrā pratiśrutaṃ deyam ṛṇavat strīdhanaṃ sutaiḥ |  
> tiṣṭhed bhartṛgṛhe yā tu na sā pitṛkule vaset ||

**atha strīdhanavibhāgaḥ**

tatra manuḥ [9.192–93, 195] |

> jananyāṃ saṃsthitāyāṃ tu samaṃ sarve sahodarāḥ |  
> bhajeran mātṛkaṃ rikthaṃ bhaginyaś ca sanābhayaḥ ||  
> yās tāsāṃ syur duhitaras tāsām api yathārhataḥ |  
> mātāmahyā dhanāt kiṃcit predeyaṃ prītipūrvakam ||  
> anvādheyaṃ ca yad dattaṃ patyā prītena caiva yat |  
> patyau jīvati vṛttāyāḥ prajāyās tad dhanaṃ bhavet ||

‘**sanābhayo’** atra sodaryāḥ | ‘**yathārhataḥ’** dravyāpatvabahutvādiyogyatādyanusāreṇa | ‘**anvādheyam’** vivāhottarakālaṃ bhartṛkule pitṛkule ca yal labdhaṃ dhanam |

bṛhaspatiḥ [26.31] |

> strīdhanaṃ syād apatyānāṃ duhitā ca tadaṃśinī |  
> aputrā cet samūḍhā tu labhate mānamātrakam ||

**[689]]** manuḥ [9.131] |

> mātus tu yautakaṃ yat syāt kumārībhāga eva saḥ |

‘yautakam’ vivāhakāle pitrādibhiḥ striyai yad dattaṃ dhanam |

gautamaḥ [28.25]: “strīdhanaṃ duhitṝṇām aprattānām apratiṣṭhitānāṃ ca” |

‘**apratiṣṭhitāḥ’** vivāhitā api nirdhanabhartṛkā durbhagā anapatyāś ca |

vasiṣṭhaḥ [17.46]: “mātuḥ pāriṇāhyaṃ striyo vibhajetan” |

‘**pāriṇāhyam’** paricchada ādarśakaṅkaṇādiḥ |

vibhajerann ūrdhvam ity anuvṛttau yājñavalkyaḥ [2.117] |

> mātur duhitaraḥ śeṣam ṛṇāt tābhya ṛte ‘nvayaḥ |

‘**anvayaḥ’** tatputrapautrādiḥ |

vivāhārheṣv ity anuvṛttau viṣṇuḥ [17.20]: “sarveṣv eva prasūtānāṃ tad dhanaṃ duhitṛgāmi” |

manuḥ [9.198] |

> striyās tu yad bhaved vittaṃ pitrā dattaṃ kathaṃcana |  
> brāhmaṇī tad dharet kanyā tadapatyasya vā bhavet ||

**[690]** asyārthaḥ —strīṇām abhartṛkāṇām anapatyānāṃ ca pitrā dattaṃ sapatnīduhitā brāhmaṇi yā kanyā sā haret tadapatyaṃ ceti |

kātyāyanaḥ [918, 917] |

> duhitṝṇām abhāve tu ṛkthaṃ putreṣu tad bhavet |  
> bandhudattaṃ tu bandhūnām abhāve bhartṛgāmi tat ||  
> bhaginyo bāndhavaiḥ sārdhaṃ vibhajeran sabhartṛkāḥ |  
> strīdhanasyeti dharmo ‘yaṃ vibhāgas tu prakalpitaḥ ||

**athāprajāyāḥ**

tatra manuḥ [9.196–97] |

> brāhmadaivārṣagāndharvaprājāpatyeṣu yad dhanam |  
> atītāyām aprajasi bhartur eva tad iṣyate ||  
> yat tv asyāḥ syād dhanaṃ dattaṃ vivāheṣv āsurādiṣu |  
> atītāyām aprajasi mātāpitros tad iṣyate ||

**[691]** devalaḥ |

> sāmānyaṃ putrakanyānāṃ mṛtāyāṃ strīdhanaṃ striyām |  
> aprajāyāṃ hared bhartā mātā bhrātā pitāpi ca ||

gautamaḥ [28.26–27]: “bhaginīśulkaṃ sodaryāṇām ūrdhvaṃmātuḥ | pūrvaṃ caike” |

‘**bhaginīśulkaḥ’** āsurādivivāhoḍhāyā bhaginyāḥ dhanam | ‘**ūrdhvaṃ mātuḥ’** mātari mṛtāyām ity arthaḥ |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.144] |

> bandhudattaṃ tathā śulkam anvādheyakam eva ca |  
> aprajāyām atītāyāṃ bāndhavās tad avāpnuyuḥ ||

manuḥ [9.135] |

> aputrāyāṃ mṛtāyāṃ tu putrikāyāṃ kathaṃcana |  
> dhanaṃ tat putrikābhartā haretaivāvicārayan ||

paiṭhīnasiḥ: “pretāyāṃ putrikāyāṃ na bhartā tad dravyam arhaty aputrāyāṃ kumāryā svasrā vā tad grāhyam” |

**[692]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.146] |

> datvā kanyāṃ haran daṇḍyo vyayaṃ dadyāc ca sodayam |  
> mṛtāyāṃ sarvam ādadyāt pariśodhyobhayavyayam ||

asyārhaḥ — svayam eva vācā **datvā**, ‘**haran’** kāraṇam antareṇa kanyām apaharan, **daṇḍyo** bhavati | yac ca vareṇa dattaṃ hiraṇyadikaṃ tatra samavṛddhikaṃ **dadyād** iti kanyādātur upadeśaḥ | atha kathaṃcid vāgdāttā mṛtā, tasyāṃ ‘**mṛtāyāṃ sarvam ādadyāt’** | yat pūrvaṃ dattam ubhayor api vyayaṃ śodhayitvā yat kanyāpitrā saṃbandhinām upacārārthaṃ paṇyādikaṃ dattam, yac ca saṃbandhināṃ maṅgalārthaṃ dattam aṅgulīyādikam, ubhayaṃ parigaṇayyāvaśiṣṭam **ādadyāt** |

arhatīty anuvṛttau śaṅkhaḥ: “svayaṃ śulkaṃ voḍhā” |

baudhāyanaḥ |

> ṛkthaṃ mṛtāyāḥ kanyāyā gṛhṇīyuḥ sodarāḥ svayam |  
> tadabhāve bhaven mātus tadabhāve pitur bhavet ||

**[693]** bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26.32–33] |

> mātṛṣvasā mātulānī pitṛvyastrī pituḥ svasā |  
> śvaśrūḥ pūrvajapatnī ca mātṛtulyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||  
> yad āsām auraso na syāt suto dauhitra eva vā |  
> tatsuto vā dhanaṃ tāsāṃ svasrīyādyāḥ samāpnuyuḥ ||

**atha strīdhanalakṣaṇam**

tatra manu-kātyāyanau [ma. 9.194’ kā. 894] |

> adhyagnyadhyāhavanikaṃ dattaṃ ca prītitaḥ striyai |  
> bhrātṛmātṛpitṛprāptaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ strīdhanaṃ smrtam ||

nāradaḥ [16.8] |

> adhyagnyadhyāhavanikaṃ bhartṛdāyas tathaiva ca |  
> bhrātṛdattaṃ pitṛbhyāṃ ca ṣaḍvidhaṃ strīdhanaṃ smṛtam ||

viṣnuḥ [17.18]: “pitṛmātṛsutabhrātṛdattam adhyagnyupāgatam ādhivedanikṃ bandhudattaṃ śulkam anvādheyakam iti strīdhanam” |

devalaḥ |

> vṛttir ābharaṇaṃ śulkaṃ lābhaś ca strīdhanaṃ bhavet |

**[694]** kātyāyanaḥ [904]

> prāptaṃ śilpais tu yad vittaṃ prītyā caiva yad anyataḥ |  
> bhartuḥ svāmyaṃ sadā tatra śeṣaṃ tu strīdhanaṃ bhavet ||

[kā. 895–97]

> vivāhakāle yat strībhyo dīyate ky agnisaṃnidhau |  
> tad adhyagnikṛtaṃ sadbhiḥ strīdhanaṃ parikīrtitam ||  
> yat punar labhate nārī nīyamānā hi paitṛkāt |  
> adhyāhavanikaṃ nāma tat strīdhanam udāhṛtam ||  
> prītyā pradattaṃ yat kiṃcit śvaśrvā vā śvaśureṇa vā |  
> pādavandanikaṃ yat tal lāvaṇyārjitam ucyate ||

[kā. 899–900]

> vivāhāt parato yat tu labdhaṃ bhartṛkulāt striyā |  
> anvādheyaṃ tad uktaṃ tu labdhaṃ yat svakulāt tayā ||  
> ūrdhvaṃ labdhaṃ tu yat kiṃcit saṃskārāt prītitaḥ striyā |  
> bhartuḥ pitroḥ sakāśād vā anvādheyaṃ tu tad bhṛguḥ ||

**[695]** [kā. 898]

> gṛhopaskaravāhyānāṃ dohyābharaṇakarmaṇām |  
> mūlyaṃ labdhaṃ tu yat kiṃcit śulkaṃ tat parikīrtitam ||

**athāvaluptavibhāgaḥ**

tatra manuḥ [9.218] |

> ṛṇe dhane ca sarvasmin pravibhakte yathāvidhi |  
> paścāt dṛśyeta yat kiṃcit tat sarvaṃ samatāṃ nayet ||

kātyāyanaḥ [885–88] |

> pracchāditaṃ tu yad yena punar āgatya yat samam |  
> bhajeran bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdham abhāve hi pituḥ sutāḥ ||  
> anyonyāpahṛtaṃ dravyaṃ durvibhaktaṃ ca yad bhavet |  
> yathāprāptaṃ vibhajyeta samabhāgena tad bhṛguḥ ||  
> vibhaktenaiva yat prāptaṃ dhanaṃ tasyaiva tad bhavet |  
> hṛtaṃ naṣṭaṃ ca yal labdhaṃ prāg uktaṃ ca punar bhavet ||

**[696]**  
> bandhuvargahṛtaṃ dravyaṃ balān naiva pradāpayet |  
> bandhūnām avibhaktānāṃ bhogaṃ naiva pravartayet ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26.141–42] |

> sādhāraṇaṛṇanyāsanihnave chadmanā kriyām |  
> pārśvahānikarīṃ kṛtvā paścāc cheṣaṃ pradāpayet ||  
> māyāvino dhṛtadhanāḥ krūrā lubdhāś ca ye narāḥ |  
> saṃprītyā sādhanīyās te svārthahānyā chalena vā ||

**atha nānāvarṇasamavāyavibhāgaḥ **

tatra manuḥ [9.148–54] |

> etad vibhāgaṃ vijñeyaṃ vibhāgasyaikayoniṣu |  
> bahvīṣu caikajātānāṃ nānāstrīṣu nibodhayet ||  
> brāhmaṇasyānupūrveṇa catasras tu yadi striyaḥ |  
> tāsāṃ putreṣu jāteṣu vibhāgo ‘yaṃ vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ||

**[697]** > kīnāśo govṛṣo yānam alaṃkārāś ca veśma ca |  
> viprasyoddhārakaṃ deyam ekāṃśaś ca pradhānataḥ ||  
> tryaṃśaṃ dāyād dhared vipro dvāv aṃśau kṣatriyāsutaḥ |  
> vaiśyājo ‘dhyardham evāṃśam aṃśaṃ śūdrāsuto haret ||  
> sarvaṃ vā rikthajātaṃ tu daśadhā pravibhajya tu |  
> dharmyaṃ vibhāgaṃ kurvīta vidhinānena dharmavit ||  
> caturo ‘ṃśān hared vipras trīn aṃśān kṣatriyāsutaḥ |  
> vaiśyāputro hared dvyaṃśam aṃśaṃ śūdrāsuto haret ||

‘ekayoniṣu’ ekajātīyāsu strīṣu jātānām ity arthaḥ | ‘nānāstrīṣu’ nānājātīyāsu strīṣu | ‘ekāṃśaś ca pradhānataḥ’ ye brāhmaṇasya trayo ‘ṃśās tatraikāṃśaḥ pradhānataḥ sāradravyāt kartavyaḥ |

nāradaḥ [16.14] |

> varṇāvareṣv aṃśahātir ūḍhājāteṣv anukramāt |

**[698]** mahābhārate [anuśāsana, 42.48–56] |

> bhīṣma uvāca —  
> kṣatriyasyāpi bhārye dve vihite kurunandana |  
> tṛtīyā vā bhavec chūdrā na tu dṛṣṭāntataḥ smṛtā ||  
> aṣṭadhā tu bhavet kāryaṃ kṣatriyasvaṃ yudhiṣṭhira |  
> kṣatriyāyā haret putraś caturo ‘ṃśān pitur dhanāt ||  
> yuddhaupacārikaṃ yat tu pitur āsīd dharec ca tat |  
> vaiśyāputras tu bhāgāṃs trīn śūdrāputras tathāṣṭamam ||  
> so ‘pi vittaṃ haret pitror nādattaṃ hartum arhati |  
> ekaiva hi bhaved bhāryā vaiśyasya kurunandana ||  
> dvitīyā vā bhavec chūdrā na tu dṛṣṭāntataḥ smṛtā |  
> pañcadhā vā bhavet kāryaṃ vaiśyasvaṃ bharatarṣabha ||  
> tayor apatyayor vakṣye vibhāgaṃ ca narādhipa |  
> vaiśyāputreṇa hartavyās catvāro ‘ṃśāḥ pitur dhanāt ||  
> pañcamas tu bhaved bhāgaḥ śūdrāputrāya bhārata |  
> so ‘pi dattaṃ haret pitrā nādattaṃ hartum arhati ||

**[699]** ‘**dṛṣṭānto’** atra vedaḥ | ‘**yuddhaupacārikam’** yuddhopakaraṇam |

viṣṇuḥ [18.1–27]: “brāhmaṇasya caturṣu varṇeṣu [cet] putrā bhaveyus te paitṛkam ṛkthaṃ daśadhā vibhajeyuḥ | tatra ca brāhmaṇīsutaś caturo ‘ṃśān ādadyāt | kṣatriyāputras trīn | dvāv aṃśau vaiśyāsutaḥ | sūdrāputras tv ekam | atha cec chūdrāputravarjaṃ brāhmaṇasya putratrayaṃ bhavet tadā navadhā dhanaṃ vibhajeyuḥ | varṇakrameṇa catustridvibhāgīkṛtān aṃśān dadyuḥ | vaiśyavarjam aṣṭadhā kṛtvā caturas trīn ekaṃ ca samādadyuḥ | kṣatriyavarjaṃ saptadhā kṛtvā caturo dvāv ekaṃ ca | brāhmaṇavarjaṃ ṣaḍdhā kṛtvā trīn dvāv ekaṃ ca | kṣatriyasya kṣatriyāvaiśyāśudrāputreṣv ayam eva vibhāgaḥ | atha brāhmaṇasya brāhmaṇakṣatriyau putrau syātām, tadā saptadhā kṛtād dhanāt brāhmaṇaś caturo ‘ṃśān dadyāt | trīn rājanyaḥ | atha brāhmaṇasya brāhmaṇavaiśyau cet putro syātāṃ tadā taddhanāt ṣaḍdhavibhaktān caturo ‘ṃśān brāhmaṇas ev ādadyāt | dvau vaiśyaḥ | atha brahmaṇasya brāhmaṇaśūdrau putrau syātāṃ tadā tadhanaṃ pañcadhā **[700]** vibhajeyātām | caturo ‘ṃśān brāhmaṇas tv ādadyāt | ekaṃ śūdraḥ | atha brāhmaṇasya kṣatriyasya vā kṣatriyavaiśyau dvau putrau syātāṃ tadā taddhanaṃ pañcadhā vibhajeyātām | trīn aṃśān kṣatriyas tv ādadyāt | dvāv aṃśau vaiśyaḥ | atha brāhmaṇasya kṣatriyasya vā kṣatriyaśūdrau putrau syātāṃ tadā taddhanaṃ caturdhā vibhajeyātām | trīn aṃśān kṣatriyas tv ādadyāt | ekaṃ śūdraḥ | atha brāhmaṇasya kṣatriyavaiśyayor vā [vaiśyaśūdrau] putrau syātāṃ tadā taddhanaṃ tridh vibhajeyātām | dvāv aṃśau vaiśyas tv ādadyāt | ekaṃ śūdraḥ” |

atha śaṅkhalikhitau: “anyavarṇastrījātānāṃ dāyād ardhārdhahānir varṇakrameṇa” |

viṣṇuḥ [18.38–40]: “yadi dvau brāhmaṇīputrao syātām ekaḥ śūdrāputras tadā navadhā vibhaktasyārthasya brāhmaṇīputrāv aṣṭau bhāgān ādadyātām ekaṃ śūdrāputraḥ | atha śūdrāputrāv ubhau syātām eko brāḥmaṇīputras tadā ṣaḍdhā vibhaktasya dhanasya caturo ‘ṃśān brāhmaṇas tv ādadyād dvāv aṃśau śūdrāputrau | anena kramenānyatrāpy aṃśakalpanā bhavati” |

punar viṣṇuḥ [18.28–31]: “athaikaputrā brāhmaṇasya [brāhmaṇa]kṣatriyaviśyāḥ sarvaharāḥ | kṣatriyavaiśyau rājanyasya | vaiśyasya vaiśyaḥ | śūdrasya śūdraḥ” |

vasiṣṭhaḥ [17.47, 50]: “yadi brāhmaṇasya brāhmaṇīkṣatriyāvaiśāsu putrāḥ syus tadā tryaṃśaṃ brāhmaṇyāḥ putro haret | dvāv aṃśau rājanyāyāḥ putraḥ | samam itare vibhajeran” |

**[701]** manuḥ [9.156–57] |

> samavarṇāsu vā jātāḥ sarve putrā dvijanmanām |  
> uddhāraṃ jyāyase datvā bhajerann itare samam ||  
> śūdrasya tu savarṇaiva nānyā bhāryā vidhīyate |  
> tatra jātāḥ samāṃśāḥ syur yadi putraśataṃ bhavet ||

baudhāyanaḥ [2.3.12–13]: “savarṇāputrānantarāputrayor anantarāputraś ced guṇavān sa jyeṣṭhāṃśaṃ haret | guṇavān aśeṣāṇāṃ bhartā bhavet” |

bṛhaspatiḥ [vy. 26.120] |

> vipreṇa kṣatriyājāto janmajyeṣṭho guṇānvitaḥ |  
> bhavet samāṃśo vipreṇa vaiśyājātas tathaiva ca ||

gautamaḥ [28.36–39]: “brāhmaṇasya rājanyāputro jyeṣṭho guṇasampannas tulyabhāk | jyeṣṭḥāṃśahīnam anyat | rājanyāvaiśyāputrasamavāye yathā sa brāhmaṇīputreṇa | kṣatriyāc cet tulyabhāk” |

‘**brāhmaṇīputreṇa’** kanīyaseti śeṣaḥ | ‘**jyeṣṭhāṃśahīnam anyat’** jyeṣṭhasya uddhārarūpo viṃśatitamo yo ‘ṃśas tadrahitaṃ ‘**anyat’** dravyaṃ samaṃ vibhaktavyam ity arthaḥ | ‘**yathā sa brāhmaṇīputreṇa’** iti — yathā sa kṣatriyāputro jyeṣṭho brāhmaṇīputreṇa kanīyasā tulyāṃśaḥ | evaṃ vaiśyāputro ‘pi brāhmaṇaja eva **[702]** kṣatriyāputreṇa kanīyasā tulyāṃśaḥ | ‘**kṣatriyāc cet’** iti, kṣatriyāc ced rājanyāvaiśyāputrau bhavataḥ, tadāpi vaiśyāputro jyeṣṭhaḥ kṣatriyāputreṇa kanīyasā tulyāṃśa ity arthaḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26.121] |

> na pratigrahabhūr deyā kṣatriyāya sutāya vai |  
> yady apy asya pitā dadyān mṛte viprāsuto haret ||

vṛddhamanuḥ |

> brahmadāyāgatāṃ bhūmiṃ hareyur brāhmaṇīsutāḥ |  
> gṛhaṃ dvijātayaḥ sarve yathā kṣetraṃ kramāgatam ||

‘**brahmadāyāgatām’** pratigrahayājanādinā labdhām |

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26.122] |

> śūdryāṃ dvijātibhir jāto na bhūmer bhāgam arhati |

devalaḥ [bṛ. vy. 26.123–24] |

> sajātāv āpnuyāt sarvam iti dharmo vyavasthitaḥ ||  
> niṣāda ekaputras tu viprasvasya tṛtīyabhāk |  
> dvau sapiṇḍaḥ sakulyo vā svadhādātātha saṃharet ||

**[703]**  
> kulyābhāve svadhādātā ācāryaḥ śiṣya eva vā |  
> sarvāsv āpatsu tān varṇān svagotrān pratipādayet ||

‘**niṣādaḥ’** śūdrāyāṃ brāhmaṇāj jātaḥ | ‘**dvau’** aṃśāv iti śeṣaḥ | ‘**svadhādātā’** piṇḍadaḥ | ‘**sarvāsv āpatsu’** sarveṣāṃ sapiṇḍādīnām abhāve | ‘**tān varṇān’** niṣādapitṛsavarṇān |

viṣṇuḥ [18.32–33]: “dvijātīnāṃ śūdras tv ekaḥ putro ‘rdhaharaḥ | aputrarikthasya yā gatiḥ sātrārdhasya dvitīyasya” |

‘**dvijātīnāṃ’** brāhmaṇavyatiriktānāṃ kṣatriyavaiśyānāṃ brāhmaṇajāte śūdrāputre devalena tṛtīyāṃśabhāgitvasyoktatvāt |

[manuḥ] [9.154–55] |

> yady api syāt tu satputro ‘py asatputro ‘pi vā bhavet |  
> nādhikaṃ daśamād dadyāc chūdrāputrāya dharmataḥ ||

**[704]**  
> brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ śūdrāputro na rikthabhāk |  
> yad evāsya pitā dadyāt tad evāsya dhanaṃ bhavet ||

yadā pitā prasannaḥ śūdrāputrāya dadāti, tadā daśamam evāṃśaṃ dadyād ityarthaḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26.125] |

> anapatyasya śuśrūṣur guṇavān śūdrayonijaḥ |  
> labhetājīvanaṃ śeṣaṃ sapiṇḍāḥ samavāpnuyuḥ ||

gautamaḥ [28.40]: “śūdrāputro ‘py anapatyasya suśrūṣuś cel labheta vṛttimūlam antevāsividhinā” |

anūḍhāputraviṣayam etat, aparigṛhītāsu ity adhikārāt |

śaṅkhalikhitau: “na śūdrāputro ‘rthabhāgī | yad evāsya pitā dadyāt tad evāsya bhāgaḥ | tasya gomithunaṃ cāparaṃ vā dadyāt | kṛṣṇāyasaṃ kṛṣṇadhānyaṃ tilavarjam” |

gautamaḥ [28.46]: “śūdrāputravat pratilomāsu” |

manuḥ [9.179] |

> dāsyāṃ vā dāsadāsyāṃ vā yaḥ śūdrasya suto bhavet |  
> so ‘nujñāto hared aṃśam iti dharmo vyavasthitaḥ ||

‘**dāsadāsī’** paricārakadāsī |

**[705]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.133–34] |

> jāto ‘pi dāsyāṃ śūdreṇa kāmato ‘ṃśaharo bhavet |  
> mṛte pitari kuryus taṃ bhrātaras tv ardhabhāgikam ||

**atha vibhaktajavibhāgaḥ**

tatra manu-nāradau [ma. 9.216; nā. 16.44] |

> ūrdhvaṃ vibhāgāj jātas tu pitryam eva dhanaṃ haret |  
> saṃsṛṣṭās tena vā ye syur vibhajeta sa taiḥ saha ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 16.54–55] |

> pitrā saha vibhaktā ye sāpatnā vā sahodarāḥ |  
> jaghanyajāś ca ye teṣāṃ pitṛbhāgaharās tu te ||  
> anīśaḥ pūrvajaḥ pitrye bhrātṛbhāge vibhaktajaḥ |

tathā [vya. 26.56–57] |

> putraiḥ saha vibhaktena pitrā yat svayam arjitam |  
> vibhaktajasya tat sarvam anīśāḥ pūrvajāḥ smṛtāḥ ||

**[706]**  
> yathā dhane tatharṇe ‘pi dānādhānakrayeṣu ca |  
> parasparam anīśās te muktvā śaucodakakriyāḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.122] |

> vibhakteṣu suto jātaḥ savarṇāyāṃ vibhāgabhāk |  
> dṛśyād vā tadvibhāgaḥ syād āyavyayaviśodhitāt ||

asyāyam arthaḥ — yo vibhāgakāle garbhastho na jñātaḥ paścāj jātaḥ sa sarvebhyo ‘ṃśaharebhyaḥ sakāśāt svāṃśaṃ tadaṃśasamaṃ labheta |

yad āha viṣṇuḥ [17.3]: “pitṛvibhaktā vibhāgānantarotpannasya bhāgaṃ dadyuḥ” iti |

vibhāgānantarakālaṃ ca yasya garbhādhānaṃ sa pitryam evāṃśaṃ labhate na tu pūrvajād aṃśād api | “anīśaḥ pūrvajaḥ pitrye bhrātṛbhāge vibhaktajaḥ” iti bṛhaspativacanāt [vya. 26.55] | pitṛvibhāgakālaprāptam āyavyayaśodhitaṃ yāvad vidyamānaṃ dhanam upalabhyate tato vā dhanāt svāṃśaṃ labhata iti |

**[707]**

**atha vibhaktāgatavibhāgaḥ**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ [vya.26.63–67, 39] |

> kṛte ‘kṛte vibhāge vā ṛkthī yatra pravartate |  
> sāmānyaṃ ced bhāvayati tatra bhāgaharas tu saḥ ||  
> ṛṇaṃ lekhyaṃ gṛhaṃ kṣetraṃ yasya paitāmahaṃ bhavet |  
> cirakālaproṣito ‘pi bhāgabhāgāgatas tu saḥ ||  
> gotrasādhāranaṃ tyaktvā yo ‘nyadeśaṃ samāśāritaḥ |  
> tadvaṃśasyāgatasyāṃśaḥ pradātavyo na saṃśayaḥ ||  
> tṛtīyaḥ pañcamaś caiva saptamo vāpi yo bhavet |  
> janmanāmaparijñāne labhetāṃśaṃ kramāgatam ||  
> yaṃ paramparayā maulāḥ sāmantāḥ svāminaṃ viduḥ |  
> tadanvayasyāgatasya dātavyā gotrajair mahī ||  
> jātā janiṣyamāṇāś ca garbhasthā ye ca mānavāḥ |  
> sarve kāṅkṣanti tāṃ vṛttim anācchedyā tatas tu sā ||

**[708]**

**atha putrāntaravibhāgaḥ**

tatra manuḥ [9.130] |

> pitrikāyāṃ kṛtāyāṃ tu yadi putro ‘nujāyate |  
> samas tatra vibhāgaḥ syāj jyeṣṭhatā nāsti hi striyāḥ ||

‘**anujāyate’** paścād utpadyate |

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26.70] |

> eka evaurasaḥ putraḥ pitrye svāmī prakīrtitaḥ |  
> tattulyā putrikā proktā bhartavyās tv apare smṛtāḥ ||

manuḥ [9.163] |

> eka evaurasaḥ putro pitryasya vasunaḥ prabhuḥ |  
> śeṣāṇām ānṛśaṃsyārthaṃ pradadyāt tu prajīvanam ||

[tathā] [9.120–21] |

> yavīyāñ jyeṣṭhabhāryāyāṃ putram utpādayed yadi |  
> samas tatra vibhāgaḥ syād iti dharmo vyavasthitaḥ ||

**[709]**  
> upasarjanaṃ pradhānasya dharmato nopapadyate |  
> pitā pradhānaṃ prajane tasmād dharmeṇa taṃ bhajet ||

[tathā] [9.146] |

> dhanaṃ yo bibhṛyād bhrātur mṛtasya striyam eva ca |  
> so ‘patyaṃ bhrātur utpādya dadyāt tasyaiva tad dhanam ||

[tathā] [9.162] |

> yady ekarikthinau syātām aurasakṣetrajau sutau |  
> yady asya paitṛkaṃ rikthaṃ sa tad gṛhṇīta netaraḥ ||

‘**vasunaḥ’** vittasya | ‘**śeṣāṇām’** kṣetrajavyatiriktānām | ‘**upasarjanam’** atra upasarjanatvam | ‘**kṣetrajaḥ’** atrāniyuktāyām utpannaḥ |

viṣṇuḥ [17.23] |

> anekapitṛkāṇāṃ tu pitṛto ‘ṃśaprakalpanā |  
> yasya yat paitṛkaṃ rikthaṃ sa tad gṛhṇīta netaraḥ ||

‘**anekapitṛkāṇām’** [ekasyāṃ yoṣiti] bahubhiḥ saṃgatāyāṃ jātānām |

**[710]** manuḥ [9.164–65] |

> ṣaṣṭhaṃ tu kṣetrajasyāṃśaṃ pradadyāt pitṛkād dhanāt |  
> auraso vibhajan dāyaṃ pitryaṃ pañcamam eva vā ||  
> aurasakṣetrajau putrau pitṛrikthasya bhāginau |  
> daśāpare tu kramaśo gotrarikthāṃśabhāginaḥ ||

ṣaṣṭhapañcamavibhāgavikalpo guṇavatvāguṇavatvena vyavasthitaḥ | ‘**daśāpare’** dattakādayaḥ | ‘**kramaśaḥ’** pūrvapūrvābhāve paraḥ paraḥ ity anena krameṇa | ‘**gotravikthāṃśabhāginaḥ’** gotrabhājaḥ trikthabhājaś ca bhavantīty arthaḥ |

‘putraṃ pratigṛhīṣyam’ ity anuvṛttau vasiṣṭhaḥ [15.9–10]: “tasmiṃś cet pratigṛhīta aurasaḥ putra utpadyate sa caturthabhāgagāmī syāt | yadi nābhyudayikeṣu prayuktaṃ syāt” |

kātyāyanaḥ [857] |

> utpanne tv aurase putre tṛtīyāṃśaharāḥ smṛtāḥ |  
> svarṇās tv asavarṇās tu grāsācchādanabhāginaḥ ||

**[711]** bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26.71] |

> kṣetrajādyā sutāś cānye pañcaṣaṭsaptabhāginaḥ |

hārītaḥ: “vibhajiṣyamāṇam ekaviṃśaṃ kānīyāya dadyāt | viṃśaṃ paunarbhavāya | ekonaviṃśaṃ dvyāmuṣyāyaṇāya | aṣṭādaśaṃ kṣetrajāya | saptadaśaṃ putrikāputrāya | itarān aurasāya putrāya dadyuḥ” |

brahmapurāṇe |

> samagradhanabhoktā syād auraso ‘pi jaghanyajaḥ |  
> tribhāgaṃ kṣetrajo bhuṅkte caturthaṃ putrikāsutaḥ ||  
> kṛtrimaḥ pañcabhāgaṃ tu ṣaḍbhāgaṃ gūḍhasaṃbhavaḥ |  
> saptāṃśaṃ cāpaviddhas tu kānīnaś cāṣṭamāṃśakam ||  
> navabhāgaṃ sahoḍhaś ca krīto daśamam aśnute |  
> paunarbhavas tu parato dvādaśaṃ svayam āgataḥ ||  
> trayodaśaṃ svabhāgaṃ tu śūdro bhuṅkte pitur dhanāt |  
> tadgotrajo vā dharmiṣṭho brahmacāry atha vā punaḥ ||

‘**parataḥ’** daśamāt param ekādaśamaṃ samaśnuta ity arthaḥ |

**[712]** śaṅkhalikhitau: “ṣaḍdāyādeṣu vikalpaḥ | aurasaḥ kṣetrajaḥ pitrikāsutaḥ paunarbhavaḥ kānīno gūḍhotpannaś ceti | ṣaḍvidhā bandhudāyādāḥ | pitṛpitāmahānām ekagotrā rikthapiṇḍodakasāmānyāt | teṣām arthaṃ daśabhāgān kuryāt | dvau bhāgau pitur dvāv aurasasya | trīn kṣetrajaputrikāsutayoḥ | ekaikam itareṣām” |

punaḥ śaṅkhalikhitau: “ṛṣabho ‘dhiko jyeṣṭhasya | tasyābhāve kṣetrajaputrikāputrasutayoḥ | tayor apy abhāve trayāṇām itareṣām | teṣām apy abhāve ṣaṇṇām adāyādānām | apaviddhaḥ sahoṣho dattaḥ krītakaḥ śūdrāputraḥ upanataś ca svayam ity adāyādāḥ ṣaḍ eva putrāḥ | teṣāṃ sārānusārato ‘rtham apekṣya deyam etebhyaḥ prajīvanam” |

gautamaḥ [25.33]: “putrā aurasa-kṣetraja-datta-kṛtrima-gūḍhotpannāpaviddhā rikthabhājaḥ | kānīna-sahoḍha-paunarbhava-putrikāputra-svayaṃdatta-krītā gotrabhājaś caturthāṃśina aurasābhāve” |

**[713]** ‘**gotrabhājaḥ’** gotraṃ bhajante piṇḍodakadānādikriyābhiḥ putrakāryaṃ kurvantīti tathocyante | etac ca kānīnādīnāṃ gotrabhāktvavacanam aurasādīnām ṛkthabhājām ekatarasyāpi sadbhāve ‘ṃśaharatvaniṣedhārtham” |

aurasa-kṣetraja-putrikāputra-paunarbhava-kānīna-gūḍhotpannān abhidhāya vasiṣṭhaḥ [17.25–26]: “ity ete dāyādā bandhavās trātāro mahato bhayād ity āhuḥ | athādāyādabandhūnāṃ sahoḍha eva prathamaḥ” |

idaṃ ca paunarbhava-kānīnayor aṃśaharatvābhidhānaṃ pitṛvarṇapaunarbhavakānīnaviṣayam | gautamīyaṃ caitayor aṃśaharatvaniṣedhanam asavarṇaviṣayam |

> utpanne tv aurase putre tṛtīyāṃśaharāḥ sutāḥ |  
> savarṇāstv asavarṇās tu grāsācchādanabhāginaḥ ||

iti kātyāyanavacanāt [857] | sahoḍha-datta-krīta-svayamupagatāpaviddha-śūdrāputrān abhidhāya, aurasādīn parāmṛśya — punar vasiṣṭhaḥ [17.39]: “yasya pūrveṣāṃ ṣaṇṇāṃ na kaścid dāyādaḥ syād ete tasya dāyaṃ hareyuḥ” |

hārītaḥ: “ṣaḍbandhudāyādāḥ ṣaḍabandhudāyādāḥ | sādhvyāṃ svayam utpāditaḥ kṣetrajaḥ paunarbhavaḥ kānīnaḥ putrikāputro gṛhe gūḍhotpanna iti bandhudāyādāḥ | dattaḥ krīto ‘paviddhaḥ sahoḍhaḥ svayamupāgataḥ sahasā dṛṣṭaś cety abandhudāyādāḥ” |

**[714]** ‘**sādhvyām’** vivāhasaṃskṛtāyāṃ ‘svayamutpāditaḥ’ putra aurasa ity arthaḥ | ‘**sahasā dṛṣṭaḥ’** yo mātāpitrādihīno ‘kasmād dṛṣṭaḥ kenacid apreritena ‘**mama tvaṃ putra’** ity uktaḥ ‘**tathā’** iti pratipadyate | ‘**abandhudāyādāḥ’** bandhudāyān nādadate ye tathoktāḥ |

yamaḥ |

> putrās tu dvādaś proktā munibhis tattvadarśibhiḥ |  
> teṣāṃ ṣaḍ bandhudāyādāḥ ṣaḍ adādādabāndhavāḥ ||  
> dvayamutpāditaś caiko dvitīyaḥ kṣetrajaḥ smṛtaḥ |  
> tṛtīyaḥ putrikāputra iti dharmavido viduḥ ||  
> paunarbhavaś caturthas tu kānīnaś caiva pañcamaḥ |  
> gṛhe ca gūḍha utpannaḥ ṣaḍ ete piṇḍadāḥ sutāḥ ||  
> apaviddhaḥ sahoḍaś ca dattaḥ kṛtrima eva ca |  
> pañcamaḥ krītakaḥ putro yaś copanayate svayam ||  
> ity ete saṃkarotpannaḥ ṣaḍ adāyādabāndhavāḥ |

**[715]** manuḥ [9.158–60] |

> putrān dvādaśa yān āha manuḥ svāyaṃbhuvo nṛṇām |  
> teṣāṃ ṣaḍ bandhudāyādāḥ ṣaḍ adāyādabāndhavāḥ ||  
> aurasaḥ kṣetrajaś caiva dattaḥ kṛttrima eva ca |  
> gūḍhotpanno ‘paviddhaś ca dāyādā bāndhavāś ca ṣaṭ ||  
> kānīnaś ca sahoḍhaś ca krītaḥ paunarbhavas tathā |  
> svayaṃdattaś ca śaudraś ca ṣaḍ adāyādabāndhavāḥ ||

baudhāyanaḥ [2.3.31–32] |

> aurasaṃ putrikāputraṃ kṣetrajaṃ dattakṛttrimau |  
> gūḍhajaṃ cāpaviddhaṃ ca rikthabhājaḥ pracakṣate ||  
> kānīnaṃ ca sahoḍhaṃ ca krītaṃ paunarbhavaṃ tathā |  
> svayaṃdattaṃ niṣādaṃ ca gotrabhājaḥ pracakṣate ||

aurasa-putrikāputra-kṣetraja-kānīna-gūḍhotpannāpaviddha-sahoḍha-paunarbhava-dattaka-dvayamupāgata-kṛttrima-krītān abhidhāya, devalaḥ |

> ete dvādaśaputrās tu santatyartham udāhṛtāḥ |  
> ātmajāḥ parajāś caiva labdhā yādṛcchikās tathā ||  
> teṣāṃ ṣaḍ bandhudāyādāḥ pūrve ‘nye pitur eva ṣaṭ |  
> viśeṣaś cāpi putrāṇām ānupūrvyād viśiṣyate || \
**[716]**  
> sarve hy anaurasasyaite putrā dāyaharāḥ smṛtāḥ |  
> aurase punar utpanne teṣu jyaiṣṭhyaṃ na tiṣṭhati ||  
> teṣāṃ savarṇā ye putrās te tṛtīyāṃśabhāginaḥ |  
> hīnās tam upajīveyur grāsācchādanasaṃbhṛtāḥ ||

aurasa-kṣetraja-putrikāputra-paunarbhava-kānīna-gūḍhotpanna-sahoḍha-datta-krīta-svayamupāgatāpaviddha-yatrakvacanotpāditān abhidhāya, viṣṇuḥ [15.28–30]: “eteṣāṃ pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ śreyān | sa eva dāyaharaḥ | sa cānyān bibhṛyāt” |

aurasa-putrikāsuta-kṣetraja-kānīna-paunarbhava-dattaka-krīta-svayaṃdatta-sahoḍhāpaviddhān abhidhāya, yājñavalkyaḥ [2.132] |

> piṇḍado ‘ṃśaharaś caiṣāṃ pūrvābhāve paraḥ paraḥ |

nāradaḥ [16.45–47, 49] |

> aurasaḥ kṣetrajaś caiva putrikāputra eva ca |  
> kānīnaś ca sahoḍhaś ca gūḍhotpannas tathaiva ca ||  
> paunarbhavo ‘paviddhaś ca dattaḥ krītaḥ kṛtas tathā |  
> svayaṃ copāgataḥ putrā dvādaśaite prakīrtitāḥ ||

**[717]**  
> teṣāṃ ṣaḍ bandhudāyādāḥ ṣaḍ adāyādabāndhavāḥ |  
> pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ smṛtaḥ śreṣṭho jaghanyo yo ya uttaraḥ ||  
> kramād ete pravartante mṛte pitari taddhane |  
> jyāyaso jyāyaso ‘bhāve jaghanyo yas tad āpnuyāt ||

manuḥ [9.185] |

> na bhrātaro na pitaraḥ putrā ṛkthaharāḥ smṛtāḥ |

tathā [9.184] |

> śreyasaḥ śreyaso ‘lābhe pāpīyān ṛktham arhati |  
> bahavaś cet tu sadṛśāḥ sarve ṛkthasya bhāginaḥ ||

śaṅkhalikhitau |

> śreyasaḥ śreyaso ‘lābhe pāpīyān ṛktham arhati |

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26.72–73] |

> datto ‘paviddhaḥ krītaś ca kṛtaḥ śaudras tathaiva ca |  
> jātiśuddhāḥ karmaśuddhā madhyamās te sutā matāḥ ||  
> kṣetrajo garhitaḥ sadbhis tathā paunarbhavaḥ sutaḥ |  
> kānīnaś ca sahoḍhaś ca gūḍhotpannas tathaiva ca ||

**[718]** hārītaḥ [bṛhaspati, vy. 26.74–75] |

> śūdrāputrāḥ svayaṃdattā ye caite krītakāḥ smṛtāḥ |  
> sarve te gotriṇaḥ proktāḥ kāṇḍapṛṣṭhā na saṃśayaḥ ||  
> svakulaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā yo vai parakulaṃ vrajet |  
> tena duścaritenāsau kāṇḍapṛṣṭho na saṃśayaḥ ||

yamaḥ |

> āpadgato ‘bhyupagato yaś ca syād vaiṣṇavīsutaḥ |  
> sarve te manunā proktā kāṇḍapṛṣṭhās trayas tathā ||  
> kulaṃ kāṇḍam it khyātaṃ yasmāt pūrvāṇi te jahuḥ |  
> tatra jyeṣthataro yaḥ syāt taṃ vai kāṇḍeti nirdiśet ||  
> svakulaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā yo vai parakulaṃ vrajet |  
> tena duścaritenāsau kāṇḍapṛṣṭha iti smṛtaḥ ||

‘vaiṣṇavī’ śūdrā |

**atha putralakṣaṇam**

**aurasaḥ**

tatra vasiṣṭhaḥ [17.12–13]: “dvādaśa ity eva putrāḥ putrāṇadṛṣṭāḥ | svayam utpāditaḥ svakṣetre saṃskṛtāyām aurasaḥ” |||

**[719]** viṣṇuḥ [15.1–2]: “atha dvādaśa putrā bhavanti | sve kṣetre saṃskṛtāyām utpāditaḥ svayam aurasaḥ prathamaḥ” |

manuḥ [9.166] |

> sve kṣetre saṃskṛtāyāṃ tu svayam utpadayed dhi yam |  
> tam aurasaṃ vijānīyāt putraṃ prāthamakalpikam ||

devalaḥ |

> saṃskṛtāyāṃ ca bhāryāyāṃ svayam utpādito hi yaḥ |  
> auraso nāma putraḥ sa pradhānaḥ pitṛvaṃśadhṛk ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.128]: “auraso dharmapatnījaḥ”

āpastambaḥ [2.13.1–2]: “savarṇām apūrvāṃ śāstravihitāṃ yathartu gacchataḥ putrās teṣāṃ karmabhiḥ saṃbandhaḥ | dāyenāvyatikramaś cobhayoḥ” |

**[720]** baudhāyanaḥ [2.3.14, 16]: “savarṇāyāṃ saṃskṛtāyāṃ svayam utpāditam aurasaṃ putram vidyāt | athāpy udāharanti —

> aṅgād aṅgāt saṃbhavati hṛdayād abhijāyase |  
> ātmā vai putranāmāsi saṃjīva śaradaḥ śatam” ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: “brāhmaṇas tu savarṇāyāḥ pāṇiṃ gṛhṇīyāt | tasyāṃ hi pitāmahānāṃ tanavo ‘nusūyante | putropacāreṇātmānam anumantrayate | evaṃ hy āha —

> aṅgād aṅgāt saṃbhavati hṛdayād abhijāyase |  
> ātmā vai putranāmāsi saṃjīva śaradaḥ śatam” ||  
> ādhatta pitaro garbhaṃ kumāraṃ puṣkarasrajam |  
> tatheha puruṣasyātmā tasmāt tvam iha jāyase |  
> ātmā putra iti proktaḥ pitur mātur anugrahāt |  
> punnāmnas trāyate yas tatputras tenāsi saṃjñitaḥ ||

**atha kṣetrajaḥ**

tatraurasānantaraṃ vasiṣṭhaḥ [17.18]: “tadalābhe niyuktāyāṃ kṣetrajo dvitīyaḥ” |

**[721]** viṣṇuḥ [15.2]: “niyuktāyāṃ sapiṇḍenottamavarṇena votpāditaḥ kṣetrajo dvitīyaḥ” |

manuḥ [9.167] |

> yas talpajaḥ pramītasya klībasya vyādhitasya vā |  
> svadharmeṇa niyuktāyāṃ sa putraḥ kṣetrajaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.128] |

> kṣetrajaḥ kṣetrajātas tu sagotreṇetareṇa vā |

baudhāyanaḥ [2.3.17–18]: “mṛtasya prasūto yaḥ klībasya vyādhitasya vānyenānumataḥ svakṣetre sa kṣetrajaḥ | sa eṣa dvipitā dvigotraś ca dvayor api svadhārikthabhāg bhavati” |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.127] |

> aputreṇa parakṣetre niyogotpāditaḥ sutaḥ |  
> ubhayor apy asau rikthī piṇḍadātā ca dharmataḥ ||

**[722]** manuḥ [9.53] |

> kriyābhyupagamād etad bījārthaṃ yatra dīyate |  
> tasyeha bhāginau dṛṣṭau bījī kṣetrika eva ca ||

nāradaḥ [15.58] |

> kṣetrikānumate bījaṃ yasya kṣetre prasicyate |  
> tadapatyaṃ dvayor eva bījikṣetrikayor matam ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: “matrasaṃskārakartur apatyam ity āṅgirasaḥ | bījakṣetrayor anumate yad bīkaṃ prakīryate tad dvidhā śasyam ity uśanā” |

kātyāyanaḥ [859] |

> kṣetrikasya matenāpi phalam utpādayet tu yaḥ |  
> tasyeha bhāginau tau tu na phalaṃ hi vinaikataḥ ||

**[723]** hārītaḥ: “jīvati kṣetrajam āhur asvātantryāt | mṛte dvyāmuṣyāyaṇam anūptabijatvāt | nābījaṃ kṣetraṃ phalati, nākṣetraṃ bījaṃ prarohati, ity ubhayadarśanād ubhayor apatyam ity eke | teṣām utpādayituḥ prathamapiṇḍo bhavati dvau piṇḍau nirvapen nirvāpe | atha vaikapiṇḍe dvā anukīrtayet | dvitīye putraṃ tṛtīye pautraṃ lepinaś ca trīn vācakṣāṇa ā saptamād ity apare” |

‘**jīvati’** kṣetapatau | tasyaiva putram ‘**kṣetrajam āhuḥ’** | atra hetuḥ — ‘**asvātantryāt’** striyāḥ | ‘**mṛte’** tu kṣetrapatau, ‘aputrā śayanaṃ bhartuḥ pālayantī vrate sthitā’ iti manuvacanāt | yady api striyā asvātantryaṃ tadavasthaṃ tathāpi na kṣetriṇa eveti | atra hetum āha — ‘**anūptabījatvāt’** kṣetriṇā | ‘**nirvāpe’** nirupyate ‘sminn iti ‘**nirvāpaḥ’** pitṛyajñaḥ | ‘**ekapiṇḍe dvau’** iti — ekaikasmin piṇḍe dvau dvāv iti vīpsāvagantavyā | yadi dvipitā syād ekaikasmin piṇḍe dvau dvāv upalakṣayed iti āpastambavacanānusārāt [āp. śrau. 1.9.7] | ‘**dvitīye putram’** ityādi — dvitīye putram ārabhyed ity arthaḥ | ‘**lepinaś ca trīn vācakṣāṇo’** dvau dvāv anukīrtayed ity arthaḥ |

nāradaḥ [16.23] |

> dvyāmuṣyāyaṇakā dadyur dvābhyāṃ piṇḍodake pṛthak |  
> rikthād ardhaṃ samādadyur bījikṣetrikayos tathā ||

**[724]** baudhāyanaḥ [2.3.19: “athāpy udāharanti —

> dvipituḥ piṇḍadānaṃ syāt piṇḍe piṇḍe ca nāmanī |  
> trayaś ca piṇḍāḥ ṣaṇṇāṃ syur evaṃ kurvan na muhyati || iti”

**atha putrikāputraḥ**

tatra vasiṣṭhaḥ [17.15]: “tṛtīyaḥ putrikā vijñāyate | abhrātṛkā [hi] puṃsaḥ pitṝn abhyeti pratīcīnaṃ gacchati putratvam” |

‘**puṃsaḥ’** patyuḥ sakāśāt | ‘**pratīcīnam’** pratyāvṛttim, pitṛkulābhimukhyam ity arthaḥ |

śaṅkhalikhitau: “putrikā putravad iti pracetasaḥ | tasyāpatyaṃ putrikāsutā mātāmahapitāmahābhyāṃ piṇḍadaḥ |

> putradauhitrayor loke na viśeṣo ‘sty anugrahe |  
> tasmāt tu saṃśayān nehopeyād abhrātṛkāṃ striyam ||

**[725]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.128] |

> auraso dharmapatnījas tatsamaḥ putrikāsutaḥ |

vidyād ity anuvṛttau baudhāyanaḥ [2.3.15]: “abhyupagamya duhitari jātaṃ putrikāputram asyāṃ dauhitram” |

atrānaurasābhiprāyeṇa manuḥ [9.131–32] |

> dauhitra eva tu hared aputrasyākhilaṃ dhanam |  
> dauhitro hy akhilaṃ riktham aputrasya pitur haret ||

aurasānuvṛttau devalaḥ |

> tattulyaḥ putrikāputro dāyadaḥ so ‘tha vā bhavet |  
> sa eva dadyāt piṇḍaṃ tu pitre mātāmahāya ca ||  
> pautradauhitrayor loke na viśeṣo ‘stu dharmataḥ |  
> tayor ‘hi mātāpitarau saṃbhūtau tasya dehataḥ ||  
> akṛtā vā kṛtā vāpi yaṃ vindet sadṛśaṃ sutam |  
> pautrī mātāmahas tena dadyāt piṇḍaṃ hared dhanam ||

kṛtākṛtaduhitradhikāre bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26.133] |

> yathā pitṛdhane svāmyaṃ tasyāḥ satsv api bandhuṣu |  
> tathaiva tatsuto ‘pīṣṭe mātṛmātāmahe dhane ||

**[726]** śaṅkhalikhitau: “strīdhanaṃ ca kanyā labhate | tadapatyasya dhanaṃ kanyābhāga eva” |

‘**tadapatyasya’** tacchabdena putrikāmātuḥ parigrahaḥ | tatsutasyottarakālaṃ jātasya aputrakasyātītasya dhanam ‘**kanyābhāga eva’** putrikābhāga eva | tasyāḥ sodarabhrātṛrūpatvād ity abhiprāyaḥ |

atha manuḥ [9.127–29] |

> aputro ‘nena vidhinā sutāṃ kurvīta putrikām |  
> yadapatyaṃ bhaved asyāṃ tan mama syāt svadhākaram ||  
> anena tu vidhānena purā cakre ‘tha putrikām |  
> vivṛddhyarthaṃ svavaṃśasya svayaṃ dakṣaprajāpatiḥ ||  
> dadau sa daśa dharmāya kāśyapāya trayodaśa |  
> somāya rājñe satkṛtya prītātmā saptaviṃśatim ||

vasiṣṭhaḥ [18.17] |

> abhrātṛkāṃ pradāsyāmi tubhyaṃ kanyām alaṅkṛtām |  
> asyāṃ yo jāyate putraḥ sa me putro bhaved iti ||

**[727]** gautamaḥ [28.18–20]: “pitotsṛjet putrikām anapatyo ‘gniṃ prajāpatiṃ ceṣṭvāsmadartham apatyam iti saṃvādya | abhisandhimātrāt putrikety ekeṣām | tatsaṃśayān nopayacched abhrātṛkām” |

jābāliḥ |

> pitrikāyāḥ pradāne tu sthālīpākena dharmavit |  
> agniṃ prajāpatiṃ ceṣṭvā putradāne tathaiva ca ||

brahmapurāṇe |

> aputreṇa ca yā kanyā manasā putravat kṛtā |  
> rājāgnibāndhavebhyaś ca samakṣaṃ vātha kutracit ||  
> prāggarbham atha vā śulkam uktvā pitrā varāya vai |  
> mṛte pitari vā dattā sā vijñeyā tu putrikā ||  
> pitryād ṛkthāt samaṃ bhāgaṃ labhate tādṛśī tu sā |

**[728]** manuḥ [9.140] |

> mātuḥ prathamataḥ piṇḍaṃ nirvapet putrikāsutaḥ |  
> dvitīyaṃ tu pitus tasyās tṛtīyaṃ tu pituḥ pituḥ ||

**atha paunarbhavaḥ**

tatra vasiṣṭha-viṣṇū [va. 17.18; vi. 14.7] | “paunarbhavaś caturthaḥ” |

manuḥ [9.175] |

> yā tu patyā parityaktā vidhavā vā svecchayā |  
> utpādayet punar bhūtvā sa paunarbhava ucyate ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.130] |

> akṣatāyāṃ kṣatāyāṃ vā jātaḥ paunarbhavaḥ sutaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [860] |

> klībaṃ vihāya patitaṃ yā punar labhate patim |  
> tasyāṃ paunarbhavo jāto vyaktam utpādakasya saḥ ||

**[729]**

**atha kānīnaḥ**

tatra vasiṣṭhaḥ [17.21–23]: “kānīnaḥ pañcamaḥ | yā pitṛgṛhe ‘saṃskṛtā kāmād utpādayet sa kānīno mātāmahasya putro bhavatīty āhuḥ | athāpy udāharanti —

> aprattā duhitā yasya sutaṃ vindeta tulyataḥ |  
> pautrī mātāmahas tena dadyāt piṇḍaṃ hared dhanam || iti |

nāradaḥ [16.18] |

> ajñātapitṛko yas tu kānīno gūḍhamātṛkaḥ |  
> mātāmahāya dadyāt sa piṇḍaṃ rikthaṃ haret tataḥ ||

baudhayanaḥ [2.3.24]: “asaṃskṛtām anatisṛṣṭāṃ yām upagacchet tasyāṃ yo jātaḥ sa kānīnaḥ” |

brahmapurāṇe |

> adattāyāṃ tu yo jātaḥ savarṇena pitur gṛhe |  
> sa kānīnaḥ sutas tasya yasmai sā dīyate punaḥ ||

**[730]** nāradaḥ [16.17] |

> kānīnaś ca sahoḍhaś ca gūḍhāyāṃ yaś ca jāyate |  
> teṣāṃ voḍhā pitā jñeyas te [ca bhāgaharā smṛtāḥ] ||

**atha gūḍhotpannaḥ**

tatra manuḥ [9.170] |

> utpadyate gṛhe yasya na ca jñāyeta kasya saḥ |  
> sa gṛhe gūḍha utpannas tasya syād yasya talpajaḥ ||

**atha sahoḍhaḥ**

tatra viṣṇuḥ [14.15–17]: “sahoḍhaḥ saptamaḥ | garbhiṇī yā saṃskriyate tasyāḥ putraḥ | sa tu pāṇigrāhasya” |

manuḥ [9.173] |

> yā garbhiṇī saṃskriyate jñātājñātāpi vā satī |  
> voḍhuḥ sa garbho bhavati sahoḍha iti cocyate ||

**[731]**

**atha dattakaḥ**

tatra manuḥ [9.168, 141–42] |

> mātā pitā vā dadyātāṃ yam adbhiḥ putram āpadi |  
> sadṛśaṃ prītisaṃyuktaṃ sa jñeyo dattrimaḥ sutraḥ ||  
> upapanno guṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ putro yasya tu dattrimaḥ |  
> sa haretaiva tad rikthaṃ saṃprāpto ‘py anyagotrataḥ ||  
> gotrarikthe janayitur na hared dattrimaḥ sutaḥ |  
> gotrarikthānugaḥ piṇḍo vyapaiti dadataḥ svadhā ||

vasiṣṭhaḥ [15.1–8]: “śoṇitaśukrasaṃbhavaḥ puruṣo mātāpitṛnimittakaḥ | tasya pradānavikrayaparityāgeṣu mātāpitarau prabhavataḥ | na tv ekaṃ putraṃ dadyāt pratigṛhṇīyād vā | sa hi santānāya pūrveṣām | na tu strī putraṃ dadyāt pratigṛhṇīyād vā | anyatrānujñānād bhartuḥ | putraṃ pratigrahīṣyan bandhūn āhūya rājani ca nivedya niveśanasya **[731]** madhye vyāhṛtīḥ hutvādūrebāndhavam asannikṛṣṭam eva pratigṛhṇīyāt | saṃdehe cotpanne dūrebāndhavaṃ śūdram iva asthāpayet | vijñāyate hy ekena bahūṃs trāyata iti” |

‘**adūrebāndhavam’** sannihitamātulādikam | ‘**asannikṛṣṭam eva’** avijñātaguṇadoṣam api | apyarthaḥ evakāraḥ | ‘**saṃdehe’** ityādi — bāndhavānām asannidhānāj jātisaṃdehe śūdratvenādhyavasya saṃskārahīnam eva ‘**sthāpayet’** | śūdro ‘pi hi kila putro bhavatīty abhiprāyaḥ |

**atha krītaḥ**

tatra manuḥ [9.174] |

> krīṇīyād yas tv apatyārthe mātāpitror yam antikāt |  
> sa krītakaḥ sutas tasya sadṛśo ‘sadṛśo ‘pi vā ||

**[733]** baudhāyanaḥ [2.3.26]: “mātāpitror hastāt krīto ‘nyatarasya vā yo ‘patyārthe gṛhyate sa krītakaḥ” |

**atha svayamupāgataḥ**

tatra manuḥ [9.177] |

> mātāpitṛvihīno yas tyakto vā syād akāraṇāt |  
> ātmānaṃ darśayed yasmai svayaṃdattas tu sa smṛtaḥ ||

**athāpaviddhaḥ**

tatra viṣṇuḥ [15.24–26]: “apaviddhas tv ekādaśaḥ | pitrā mātrā ca parityaktaḥ | sa ca yena gṛhītaḥ” |

vasiṣṭhaḥ [17.36–37]: “apaviddhaḥ pañcamaḥ | yaṃ mātāpitṛbhyām apāstaṃ gṛhṇīyāt” |

**[734]**

**atha kṛttrimaḥ**

tatra manuḥ [9.169] |

> sadṛśaṃ yaṃ prakuryātāṃ guṇadoṣavicakṣaṇam |  
> putraṃ putraguṇair yuktaṃ sa vijñeyas tu kṛttrimaḥ ||

**atha śūdrāputraḥ**

[tatra] viṣṇuḥ [15.27]: “yatra kvacanotpāditaś ca dvādaśaḥ” |

vasiṣṭhaḥ [17.38]: “śūdrāputra eva [ṣaṣṭho] bhavatīty āhuḥ” |

manuḥ [9.177] |

> yaṃ brāhmaṇas tu śūdrāyāṃ kāmād utpadeyet sutam |  
> sa pārayann eva śavas tasmāt pāraśavaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

baudhāyanaḥ [2.3.29–30]: “dvijātipravarāc chūdrāyāṃ jātaḥ kāmāt pāraśava iti” |

**[735]** atha manuḥ [9.180–81] |

> kṣetrajādīn sutān etān ekādaśa yathoditān |  
> putrapratinidhīn āhuḥ kriyālopān manīṣibhiḥ ||  
> ya ete vihitāḥ putrāḥ prasaṅgād anyabījajāḥ |  
> yasya te bījato jātās tasya te netarasya tu ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26.77–78] |

> putrās trayodaśa proktā manunā ye ‘nupūrvaśaḥ |  
> santānakāraṇaṃ teṣām aurasaḥ putrikāsutaḥ ||  
> ājyaṃ vinā yathā tailaṃ sadbhiḥ pratinidhiḥ smṛtam |  
> tathaikādaśaputrās tu putrikaurasayor vinā ||

**[736]** brahmapurāṇe |

> dattakaś ca svayaṃdattaḥ kṛttrimaḥ krīta eva ca |  
> apaviddhaś ca ye putrā bharaṇīyāḥ sadaiva hi ||  
> bhinnagotrāḥ pṛthak piṇḍāḥ bhinnavaṃśakarās tathā |  
> sūtake mṛtake vāpi tryahāśaucasya bhāginaḥ ||  
> api vastrānnadārṝṇāṃ kṣetrabījavatāṃ tathā |  
> śūdro dāsaḥ pāraśavo viprāṇāṃ vidyate kvacit ||  
> rājñāṃ tu śāpadagdhānāṃ nityaṃ kṣayavatāṃ tathā |  
> atha saṃgrāmaśīlānāṃ kadācid vā bhavanti te ||  
> auraso yadi vā putras tv atha vā putrikāsutaḥ |  
> vidyate tatra teṣāṃ tu vijñeyāḥ kṣetrajādayaḥ ||  
> ekādaśa pṛthaggotrā vaṃśamātrakarās tu te |  
> śrāddhādi dāsavat sarve teṣāṃ kurvanti nityaśaḥ ||  
> gūḍhotpannaś ca kānīnaḥ sahoḍhaḥ kṣetrajas tathā |  
> paunarbhavaś ca vaiśyānāṃ rājadaṇḍabhayād api ||  
> varjitāḥ pañca dhanināṃ śeṣāḥ sarve bhavanty api |  
> śūdrāṇāṃ dāsavṛttīnāṃ parapiṇḍopajīvinām ||  
> parāyattaśarīrāṇāṃ na kvacit putra ity api |  
> tasmād dāsāc ca dāsyāc ca jāyate dāsa eva hi ||

**[736]**

**atha putratvavicāraḥ**

tatra vasiṣṭhaḥ [18.6]: “kṣetriṇaḥ putro janayituḥ putra iti vivadante” |

āpastambaḥ [2.13.6] |

> apramattā rakṣatha tantum etaṃ mā vaḥ kṣetre parabījāni vāpsuḥ |  
> janayituḥ putro bhavati sāṃparāye modhaṃ pitā kurute tantum enam || iti |

manuḥ [9.35–36] |

> bījasya caiva yonyāś ca bījam utkṛṣṭam ucyate |  
> sarvabhūtaprasūtir hi bījalakṣaṇalakṣitā ||  
> yādṛśaṃ tūpyate bījaṃ kṣetre kālopapāditam |  
> tādṛg rohati tat tasmin bījaṃ svair vyañjanaṃ guṇaiḥ ||

tathā [9.41, 45–46, 48–52, 54–55] |

> tat prājñena vinītena jñānavijñānavedinā |  
> āyuṣkāmena vaptavyaṃ na jātu parayoṣiti ||

**[738]**  
> etāvān eva puruṣo yaj jāyātmā prajeti ca |  
> viprāḥ prāhus tathā caiva yo bhartā sā smṛtāṅganā ||  
> na niṣkrayavisargābhyāṃ bhartur bhāryā vimucyate |  
> evaṃ dharmaṃ vijānīmaḥ prāk prajāpatinirmitam ||  
> yathā yo’śvoṣṭradāsīṣu tv ajāvimahiṣīṣu ca |  
> notpādakaḥ prajābhāgī tathaivānyāṅganāsv api ||  
> ye ‘kṣetriṇo bījavantaḥ parakṣetrapravāpiṇaḥ |  
> te vai sasyasya jātasya na labhante phalaṃ kvacit ||  
> yady anyagoṣu vṛṣabho vatsānāṃ janayec chatam |  
> gominām eva te vatsā moghaṃ skanditam ārṣabham ||  
> tathaivākṣetriṇo bījaṃ parakṣetrapravāpiṇaḥ |  
> kurvanti kṣetriṇām arthaṃ na bījī labhate phalam ||  
> phalaṃ tv anabhisaṃdhāya kṣetriṇāṃ bījināṃ tathā |  
> pratyakṣaṃ kṣetriṇām artho bījād yonir garīyasī ||

**[739]**  
> moghavātāhṛtaṃ bījaṃ yasya kṣetre prarohati |  
> taj jñeyaṃ kṣetrikasyaiva na bījī labhate phalam ||  
> eṣa dharmo gavāśvasya dāsyuṣṭrājāvikasya ca |  
> vihaṅgamahiṣīṇāṃ ca vijñeyaḥ prasavaṃ prati ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: “kṣetrikasyāvijñānena yad bījaṃ prakīryate tat kṣetrikasyaiva | na tatra bījī bhāgam arhati” |

gautamaḥ [18.9–14]: “kṣetriyaḥ pāradāriko na vibhāgam arhati | nātidvitīyaṃ janayitur apatvyam | samayād anyasya | jīvataś ca kṣetre | parasmāt tasya | dvayor vā | rakṣaṇāt tu bhartur eva” |

**[740]** ‘**nātidvitīyaṃ janayitur apatyam’** iti — ‘**dvitīyaṃ’** niyogena ‘**janayituḥ’** dvitīyam atikramya tṛtīyam apatyaṃ na bhavatīty arthaḥ | ‘**samayād anyasya’** ‘mamedam apatyaṃ bhavatu’ it saṅketāt, ‘**anyasya’** bījino bhavati | ‘**jīvataś ca kṣetre** — jīvataḥ prajananāsamarthasya [patyuḥ] ‘**kṣetre’** bhāryāyām, yad apatyaṃ jāyate tat kṣetriṇa eva |

śaṅkhalikhitau: “niyataṃ kṣetriṇām apatyam iti vedavādo mātur apatyam ity eke” |

tathā: “vasiṣṭhakaśyapayor jalagatayor udavāsād uttīryaikaḥ prajām utpādayaty avijñāto lokānām | evaṃ tayor dvidhā santānaḥ | yasmāt kuladharmaparigraharikthapiṇḍodakāni caikataḥ kṛtvā parakṣetrotpannā api prayacchanti” |

**atha putrādideśaḥ**

tatra manuḥ [9.182–83] |

> bhrātṝṇām ekajātānām ekaś cet putravān bhavet |  
> sarve te tena putreṇa putriṇo manur abravīt |  
> sarvāsām ekapatnīnām ekā cet putriṇī bhavet |  
> sarvās tās tena putreṇa prāha putravatīr manuḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26.79–80] |

> yady ekajātā bahavo bhrātaras te sahodarāḥ |  
> ekasyāpi sute jāte sarve te putriṇaḥ smṛtāḥ ||

**[741]**  
> bahvīnām ekapatnīnām eṣa eva vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ |  
> ekā cet putriṇī tāsāṃ sarvāsāṃ piṇḍadas tu saḥ ||

**atha putraniruktādiḥ**

tatra manu-viṣṇū [ma. 9.138; vi. 15.44] |

> punnāmno narakād yasmāt pitaraṃ trāyate sutaḥ |  
> tasmāt putra iti proktaḥ svayam eva svayaṃbhuvā ||

hārītaḥ |

> punnāmā nirayaḥ proktaś chinnatantuś ca nairayaḥ |  
> tatra vai trāyate yasmāt tasmāt putra iti smṛtaḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26.81–82] |

> puṃnāmno narakād yasmāt pitaraṃ trāyate yataḥ |  
> mukhasaṃdarśanenāpi tadutpattau yateta saḥ ||  
> pautro ‘tha putrikāputraḥ svargaprāptikarāv ubhau |  
> rikthapiṇḍapradānena samau saṃparikalpitau ||

**[742]** viṣṇu-vasiṣṭhau [vi. 15.45; vas. 17.1] |

> ṛṇam asmin sannayati amṛtatvaṃ ca vindati |  
> pitā putrasya jātasya paśyec cej jīvito mukham ||

śaṅkhalikhita-pauṭhīnasayaḥ |

> yatra kvacana jātena pitā putreṇa nandati |  
> tena cānṛṇatāṃ yāti pitṝṇāṃ piṇḍadena vai ||

hārītaḥ |

> yasya putraḥ śucir dakṣaḥ pūrve vayasi dhārmikaḥ |  
> niyantā cātmadoṣāṇāṃ sa tārayati pūrvajān ||

śaṅkhalikhitau |

> agnihotraṃ trayo vedā yajñāś ca śatadakṣiṇāḥ |  
> jyeṣṭhaputraprasūtasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm ||  
> putrapautrapratiṣthasya bahuputrasya jīvataḥ |  
> askannavedayajñasya hantaprāptaṃ triviṣṭapam ||

śaṅkhalikhita-viṣṇu-vasiṣṭha-hārītāḥ |

> putreṇa lokañ jayati pautreṇānantyam aśnute |  
> atha putrasya pautreṇa bradhnasyāpnoti viṣṭapam ||

**[743]** yājñavalkyaḥ [1.78] |

> lokānantyaṃ divaḥ prāptiḥ putrapautraprapautrakaiḥ |

vasiṣṭhaḥ [17.2–4]: “anantā putriṇo lokā nāputrasya loko ‘stīti śrūyate | ‘prajāḥ santv aputriṇaḥ’ ity abhiśāpaḥ | ‘prajābhir agne amṛtatvam aśyām’ ity api nigamo bhavati” |

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26.88–90] |

> aputreṇa sutaḥ kāryo yādṛk tādṛk prayatnataḥ |  
> piṇḍodakakriyāhetor nāmasaṃkīrtanasya ca ||  
> kaṅkṣanti pitaraḥ putrān narakāpātabhīravaḥ |  
> gayāṃ yāsyati yaḥ kāścit so ‘smān santārayiṣyati ||  
> yathā jalaṃ kuplavena taran majjati mānavaḥ |  
> tathā pitā kuputrais tu tamasy andhe nimajjati ||

**[744]**

**atha ninditaḥ**

tatra manuḥ [9.143–44] |

> aniyuktāsutaś caiva putriṇyāptaś ca devarāt |  
> ubhau tau nārhatau bhāgaṃ jārajātakakāmajau ||  
> niyuktāyām api pumān nāryāṃ jāto ‘vidhānataḥ |  
> naivārhaḥ paitṛkaṃ rikthaṃ patitotpādito hi saḥ ||

gautamaḥ [28.24]: “devaravatyām anyajātam abhāgam” |

nāradaḥ [16.19–20] |

> jātā ye tv aniyuktāyām ekena bahubhis tathā |  
> ariktabhāgas te sarve bījinām eva te sutāḥ ||  
> dadyus te bījino piṇḍaṃ mātā cec chulkato hṛtā |  
> aśulkopanatāyāṃ ca piṇḍadā voḍhur eva te ||

**[745]** manuḥ [9.191] |

> dvau tu yau vivadeyātāṃ dvābhyāṃ jātau striyāṃ dhane |  
> tayor yady asya pitryaṃ syāt tat sa gṛhṇīta netaraḥ ||

**atha aputradhanavibhāgaḥ**

tatra manuḥ [9.190] |

> saṃsthitasyānapatyasya sagotrāt tantum āharet |  
> tatra yad ṛkthajātaṃ syāt tat tasmai pratipādayet ||

‘**tantum āharet’** sagotrāt puruṣāt santānam utpādayed ity arthaḥ |

vṛddhamanuḥ |

> aputrā śayanaṃ bhartuḥ pālayantī vrate sthitā |  
> patny eva dadyāt tat piṇḍaṃ kṛtsnam arthaṃ labheta ca ||

**[746]** bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26.92–95, 97–98, 105] |

> āmnāye smṛtitantre ca lokācāre ca sūribhiḥ |  
> śarīrārdhaṃ smṛtā jāyā puṇyāpuṇyaphale samā ||  
> yasya noparatā bhāryā dehārdhaṃ tasya jīvati |  
> jīvaty ardhaśarīre ‘rthaṃ katham anyaḥ samāpnuyāt ||  
> sakulyair vidyamānais tu pitṛbhrātṛsanābhibhiḥ |  
> asutasya pramītasya patnī tadbhāgahāriṇī ||  
> pūrvapramītāgnihotraṃ mṛte bhartari taddhanam |  
> vindet pativratā nārī dharma eṣa sanātanaḥ ||  
> jaṅgamaṃ sthāvaraṃ haimaṃ kupyadhānyarasāmbaram |  
> ādāya dāpayec chrāddhaṃ māsaṣāṇmāsikādikam ||  
> pitṛvyagurudauhitrān bhartuḥ svasrīyamātulān |  
> pūjayet kavyapūrtābhyāṃ vṛddhāndhān atithīn striyaḥ ||  
> tatsapiṇḍā bāndhavāś ca ye ‘nye syuḥ paripanthinaḥ |  
> hiṃsyur dhanāni tān rājā cauradaṇḍena śāsayet ||

**[747]** atha nāradaḥ [16.50] |

> putrābhāve tu duhitā tulyasantānadarśanāt |  
> putraś ca duhitā cobhau pituḥ santānakārakau ||

tathā (?) | [manu 9.130]

> yathaivātmā tathā putraḥ putreṇa duhitā samā |  
> tasyām ātmani tiṣṭhantyāṃ katham anyo dhanaṃ haret ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26.132] |

> sadṛśī sadṛśenoḍhā sādhvī śuśrūṣaṇe ratā |  
> kṛtākṛtā vāputrasya pitur dhanaharī tu sā ||

‘kṛtā’ putrikātvena sthāpitā |

tathā [vya. 26.135] |

> bhāryāsutavihīnasya tanayasya mṛtasya ca |  
> mātā ṛkthaharī jñeyā bhrātā vā tadanujñayā ||

**[748]** manuḥ [9.217] |

> anapatyasya putrasya mātā dāyādam āpnuyāt |  
> mātary api ca vṛttāyāṃ pitur mātā hared dhanam ||

gautamaḥ [27.28]: “asaṃsṛṣṭivibhāgaḥ | pretānāṃ jyeṣṭhasya” |

manuḥ [9.185–87] |

> pitā hared aputrasya rikthaṃ bhrātara eva vā |  
> trayāṇām udakaṃ kāryaṃ triṣu piṇḍaḥ pravartate ||  
> caturthaḥ saṃpradātaiṣāṃ pañcamo nopapadyate |  
> ata ūrdhvaṃ sakulyaḥ syād ācāryaḥ śiṣya eva vā ||

paiṭhīnasiḥ: “aputrasya svaryātasya bhrātṛgāmi dravyam | tadabhāve mātāpitarau labhetām | patnī vājyeṣṭhā sagotraśiṣyasabrahmacāriṇaḥ” |

yac ca ‘aputradhanaṃ patnyabhigāmi’ ityādi viṣṇuvacanena [17.4] bhrātṛsadbhāve ‘py aputradhanasya patnyabhigāmitvaṃ pratipāditam, tat ‘aputrā **[749]** śayanaṃ bhartuḥ’ ityādi vṛddhamanuvākyaparyālocanayā bhartṛśayanaparipālanaśrāddhakaraṇādiguṇopetā yā patnī tadviṣayam | yā caivaṃvidhā na bhavati tasyāṃ vidyamānāyām ap bhrātṛgāmy eva tad dhanam | yac ca —

> bharaṇaṃ cāsya kurvīran strīṇām ājīvanakṣayāt |  
> rakṣanti śayyāṃ bhartuś ced ācchidyur itarāsu tat ||

iti bharaṇamātraṃ śaṅkhenoktam | tadvaidhavyavrarahitāvyabhicāriṇīmātraviṣayam | yaś ca yājñavalkyena (2.135) ‘pitarau bhrātaras tathā’ iti bhrātṛsadbhāve pitror evādhikāra uktaḥ; saḥ pitṛpitāmahādyupārjitadhanaviṣayaḥ | yac ca pitṛdrvyāvirodhenopārjitaṃ tat pitroḥ sadbhāve ‘pi bhrātṝṇām eva |

devalaḥ |

> tato dāyam aputrasya vibhajeran sahodarāḥ |  
> kulyā duhitaro vāpi dhriyamāṇaḥ pitāpi vā ||  
> savarṇā bhrātaro mātā bhāryā veti yathākramam |  
> teṣām abhāve gṛhṇīyuḥ kulyānāṃ sahavāsinaḥ ||

**[750]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.135–36] |

> patnī duhitaraś caiva pitarau bhrātaras tathā |  
> tatsuto gotrajo bandhuḥ śiṣyaḥ sabrahmacāriṇaḥ ||  
> eṣām abhāve pūrvasya dhanabhāg uttarottaraḥ |  
> svaryātasya hy aputrasya sarvavarṇeṣv ayaṃ vidhiḥ ||

viṣṇuḥ (19.4–13): “aputrasya dhanaṃ patnyabhigāmi | tadabhāve duhitṛgāmi | tadabhāve mātṛgāmi | tadabhāve pitṛgāmi | tadabhāve bhrātṛgāmi | tadabhāve bhrātṛputragāmi | tadabhāve bandhugāmi | tadabhāve sakulyagāmi | tadabhāve sahādhyāyigāmi | tadabhāve brāhmaṇadhanavaarjaṃ rājagāmi” |

duhitṛdauhitrānantaraṃ bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26.134] |

> tadabhāve bhrātaras tu bhrātṛputrāḥ sanābhayaḥ |  
> sakulyā bāndhavāḥ śiṣyāḥ śrotriyāś ca dhanārhakāḥ ||  
> mṛta ‘napatyo ‘bhāryaś ced abhrātṛpitṛmātṛkaḥ |  
> sarve sapiṇḍās tad dāyaṃ vibhajeran yathāṃśataḥ ||

**[751]**  
> samutpannā dhanād ardhaṃ tadardhaṃ sthāpayet pṛthak |  
> māsaṣāṇmāsikaśrāddhe vārṣikaṃ ca prayatnataḥ ||  
> bahavo jñātayo yatra sakulyā bāndhavās tathā |  
> yo hy āsannataras teṣāṃ so ‘napatyadhanaṃ haret ||

baudhāyanaḥ [1.11.15–12]: “prapitāmahaḥ pitāmahaḥ pitā svayaṃ sodaryā bhrātaraḥ savarṇāyāḥ putrapautrāḥ prapautrās tān avibhaktadāyādān sapiṇḍān ācakṣate | vibhaktādāyādān api sakulyān ācakṣate | asatsv aṅgajeṣu tadgāmī hy artho bhavati | sapiṇḍābhāve sakulyaḥ | tadabhāve pitācāryo ‘ntevāsī ṛtvig vā haret | tadabhāve rājā” |

nāradaḥ [16.51–52] |

> abhāve duhitṝṇāṃ ca sakulyā bāndhavās tathā |  
> tataḥ sajātyāḥ sarveṣām abhāve rājagāmi tat ||  
> anyatra brāhmaṇāt kiṃ tu rājā dharmaparāyaṇaḥ |  
> tat strīṇāṃ jīvanaṃ dadyād eṣa dāyavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ||

devalaḥ |

> sarvatra dāyakaṃ rājā hared brahmasvavarjitam |  
> adāpayaṃ brahmasvaṃ śrotriyabhyaḥ pradāpayet ||

**[752]** baudhāyanaḥ [1.11.14] |

> brahmasvaṃ putrapautraghnaṃ hanyād ekākinaṃ viṣam |  
> [na viṣaṃ viṣam ity āhur brahmasvaṃ viṣam ucyate] ||  
> tasmād rājā brāhmaṇasvaṃ nadadīta kathaṃcana |  
> paramaṃ hy etad viṣaṃ yad brāhmaṇasvam iti ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26.119] |

> ye ‘putrāḥ kṣatraviṭśūdrāḥ patnībhrātṛvivarjitāḥ |  
> teṣāṃ dhanaṃ hared rājā sarvasyādhipatir hi yaḥ ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: “pariṣadgāmi vā śrotriyadravyaṃ na rājagāmi | na hāryaṃ rājñā devabrāhmaṇasaṃsthitam | na nikṣepopanidhikramāgatam | na bālastrīdhanāni | evaṃ hy āha —

> na hāryaṃ strīdhanaṃ rājñā tathā bāladhanāni ca |  
> nāryāḥ ṣaḍāgamaṃ vittaṃ bālānāṃ paitṛkaṃ dhanam ||”

manuḥ [8.27] |

> bāladāyāgataṃ rikthaṃ tāvad rājā tu pālayet |  
> yāvat sa syāt samāvṛtto yāvad vātītaśaiśavaḥ ||

**[753]** viṣṇuḥ [3.65]: “bālānāthastrīdhanāni ca rājā paripālayet” |

śaṅkhalikhitau: “rakṣed rājā bālānāṃ dhanāny aprāptavyavahārāṇāṃ śrotriyaviīrapatnīnām | prahīṇasvāmikāni rājagāmīni bhavanti” |

putrādhikāre baudhāyanaḥ [2.3.37]: “teṣām aprāptavyavahārāṇām aṃśān sopacayān suguptān nidadhyād ā vyavahāraprāpaṇāt” |

kātyāyanaḥ [845] |

> proṣitasya ca yo bhāgo rakṣeyuḥ sarva eva tam |  
> bālaputre mṛte rikthaṃ rakṣyaṃ tatsvaṃ tu bandhubhiḥ ||  
> poganḍāḥ paratas taṃ tu vibhajeran yathāṃśataḥ |

‘**bālaputre’** bālaḥ putraḥ yasya tasmin | ‘**pogaṇḍo’** atibālaḥ vyavahārānabhijñaḥ |

viṣṇuḥ [15.40]: “yaś cārthaharaḥ sa piṇḍadāyī” |

smṛtiḥ: “yo dhanam ādadīta sa tasmai śrāddhaṃ kuryāt | piṇḍaṃ ca tripuruṣaṃ dadyāt” iti |

**[754]** bṛddhaśātātapo bṛhaspatiś ca [vya. 26.139] |

> bhrātā vā bhrātṛputro vā sapiṇḍaḥ śiṣya eva vā |  
> saha piṇḍakriyāṃ kṛtvā kuryād abhyudayaṃ tataḥ ||

vasiṣṭhaḥ [viṣṇu 15.31]: “putraḥ pitṛvittālābhe ‘pi piṇḍaṃ dadyāt” |

atha viṣṇuḥ [17.15]: “vānaprasthadhanam ācāryo gṛhṇīyāc chiṣyo vā” |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.137] |

> vānaprasthayatibrahmacāriṇām ṛkthabhāginaḥ |  
> kremenācāryasacchiṣyadharmabhrātrekatīrthinaḥ ||

**atha saṃsṛṣṭivibhāgaḥ**

tatra manuḥ [9.210–12] |

> vibhaktaḥ saha jīvanto vibhajeran punar yadi |  
> samas tatra vibhāgaḥ syāj jyaiṣṭhyaṃ tatra na vidyate ||  
> yeṣāṃ jyeṣṭhaḥ kaniṣṭho vā hīyetāṃśapradānataḥ |  
> mriyetānyataro vāpi tasya bhāgo na lupyate ||

**[755]**  
> sodaryā vibhajeraṃs taṃ sametya sahitāḥ samam |  
> bhrātaro ye ca saṃsṛṣṭā bhāginyaś ca sanābhayaḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26.106] |

> saṃsṛṣṭau yau punaḥ prītyā tau parasparabhāginau |

tathā [vya. 26.106–08, 112] |

> vibhaktā bhrātaro ye ca saṃprītyaikatra saṃsthitāḥ |  
> punar vibhāgakaraṇe jyaiṣṭhyaṃ teṣāṃ na vidyate ||  
> yadā kaścit pramīyeta pravrajed vā kathaṃcana |  
> na lupyate tasya bhāgaḥ sodarasya vidhīyate ||  
> yā tasya bhaginī sā tu tato ‘ṃśaṃ labdhum arhati |  
> anapatyasya dharmo ‘yam abhāryāpitṛkasya ca ||  
> saṃsṛṣṭānāṃ tu yaḥ kaścid vidyāśauryādinādhikam |  
> prāpnoti tasya dātavyo dvyaṃśaḥ śeṣāḥ samāṃśinaḥ ||

nāradaḥ [16.24] |

> saṃsṛṣṭānāṃ tu yo bhāgas teṣām eva sa iṣyate |  
> ato ‘nyathāṃśabhājas tu nirbījeṣv itarān iyāt ||

**[756]** ‘**ato ‘nyathā’** saṃsṛṣṭinām abhāve | ‘**nirbījeṣu’** santānarahiteṣu | ‘**itarān’** aṃśaharān | ‘**iyāt’** gacchet |

śaṅkhaḥ |

> bhrātṝṇām aprajāḥ preyāt kaścit cet pravrajet vā |  
> vibhajeran dhanaṃ tasya śeṣās tu strīdhanaṃ vinā ||  
> bharaṇaṃ cāsya kurvīran strīṇām ā jīvitakṣayāt |  
> rakṣanti śayyāṃ bhartuś ced ācchindyur itarāsu tat ||  
> yā tasya duhitā tasyāḥ pitraṃśo bharaṇe mataḥ |  
> ā saṃskārād dhared bhāgaṃ parato bibhṛyāt patiḥ ||

‘**itarāsu’** śayyām arakṣantīṣu | ‘**ā saṃskārāt’** vivāham abhivyāpya tāvataṃ bhāgaṃ hared yāvatā vivāhasya niṣpattir ity arthaḥ |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.138] |

> saṃsṛṣṭinas tu saṃsṛṣṭī sodarasya tu sodaraḥ |  
> dadyāc cāpaharec cāṃśaṃ jātasya ca mṛtasya ca ||

**[757]** anantaraṃ yājñavalkyaḥ [2.139] |

> anyodaryas tu saṃsṛṣṭī nāyodaryadhanaṃ haret |  
> asaṃsṛṣṭy api vādadyāt saṃsṛṣṭo nānyamātṛjaḥ ||

‘**saṃsṛṣṭo’** atra ekodarasambaddhaḥ sodaro ‘bhipretaḥ |

kātyāyanaḥ [932] |

> saṃsṛṣṭānāṃ tu saṃsṛṣṭā pṛthaksthānāṃ pṛthaksthitāḥ |  
> abhāve ‘rthaharā jñeyā nirbījānyonyabhāginaḥ ||

‘**abhāve’** strīputrādīnām arthaharāṇām abhāve |

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26.113] |

> vibhakto yaḥ punaḥ pitrā bhrātrā vaikatra saṃsthitaḥ |  
> pitṛvyenātha vā prītyā sa tu saṃsṛṣṭa ucyate ||

**[758]**

**atha vibhāganiścayaḥ**

tatra nāradaḥ [16.36–40] |

> vibhāgadharmasaṃdehe dāyādānāṃ vinirṇayaḥ |  
> jñātibhir bhāgalekhyena pṛthakkāryapravartanāt ||  
> bhrātṝṇām avibhaktānām eko dharma pravartate |  
> vibhāge sati dharmo ‘pi bhavet teṣāṃ pṛthak pṛthak ||  
> dānagrahaṇapaśvannagṛhakṣetraparigrahāḥ |  
> vibhaktānāṃ pṛthag jñeyāḥ pākadharmāgamavyayāḥ ||  
> sākṣitvaṃ prātibhāvyaṃ ca dānaṃ grahaṇam eva ca |  
> vibhaktā bhrātaraḥ kuryur nāvibhaktāḥ parasparam ||  
> yeṣām etāḥ kriyā loke pravartante svarikthataḥ |  
> vibhaktān avagaccheyur lekhyam apy antareṇa tān ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.149] |

> vibhāganihnave jñātibandhusākṣyabhilekhitaiḥ |  
> vibhāgabhāvanā jñeyā gṛhakṣetraiś ca yautakaiḥ ||

**[759]** tathā [2.52] |

> bhrātṝṇām atha dampatyoḥ pituḥ putrasya caiva hi |  
> prātibhāvyam ṛṇaṃ sākṣyam avibhakte na tu smṛtam ||

‘**yautakaiḥ’** pṛthābhūtaiḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26.147] |

> pṛthag āyavyayadhanāḥ kusīdaś ca parasparam |  
> vaṇikpathaṃ ca ye kuryur vibhaktās te na saṃśayaḥ ||

**atha vibhktakṛtyam**

tatra nāradaḥ |

> yady ekajātā bahavaḥ pṛthagdharmāḥ pṛthakkriyāḥ |  
> pṛthakkarmaguṇopetā na cet kāryeṣu saṃmatāḥ ||

**[760]**  
> svabhāgān yadi dadyus te vikrīṇīyur athāpi vā |  
> kuryur yatheṣṭaṃ tat sarvam īśās te svadhanasya vai ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 26]

> yenāṃśo yādṛśō bhuktas tasya tan na vicālayet |

tathā [vya. 26] |

> svecchākṛtavibhāgo yaḥ punar eva visaṃvadet |  
> sa rājñāṃśe svake sthāpyaḥ śāsanīyo ‘nubandhakṛt ||

tathā [vya 26] |

> vibhaktā hy avibhaktā vā dāyādā sthāvare samāḥ |  
> eko hy anīśaḥ sarvatra dānādhamanavikraye ||

**iti mahārājādhirājaśrīgovindcandradevamahāsāndhivigrahikeṇa**

**bhaṭṭaśrīhṛdayadharātmajena bhaṭṭaśrīlakṣmīdhareṇa viracite **

**kṛtyakalpatarau vyavahārakāṇḍe dāyavibhāgaḥ ||**

**[761]**

## 75 dyūtasamāhvayam
atha dyūtasamāhvayam

tatra nāradaḥ [19.1] |

> akṣavadhraśalākādyair devanaṃ jihmakāritam |  
> paṇakrīḍāvayobhiś ca padaṃ dyūtasamāhvayam ||

manuḥ [9.229] |

> aprāṇibhir yat kriyate tal loke dyūtam ucyate |  
> prāṇibhiḥ kriyate yas tu sa vijñeyaḥ samāhvayaḥ ||  
> kākinyo vadhrikāś caiva śalākāḥ sīsam eva ca |  
> akṣāḥ sabījāḥ kuhakā dyūtopakaraṇāni ṣaṭ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 28.1] |

> anyonyaṃ parigṛhītāḥ pakṣimeṣamṛgādayaḥ |  
> praharante kṛtapaṇās taṃ vadanti samāhvayam ||

**[762]** manuḥ [9.221–22, 224, 227–28] |

> dyūtaṃ samāhvayaṃ caiva rājā rāṣṭrād vivāsayet |  
> rāṣṭāntakaraṇāv etau dvau doṣau pṛthivīkṣitām ||  
> prakāśam etat tāskaryaṃ yad devanasamāhvayau |  
> tayor nityaṃ pratīghāte nṛpatir yatnavān bhavet ||  
> dyūtaṃ samāhvayaṃ caiva yaḥ kuryād yaś ca kārayet |  
> tān sarvān ghātayed rājā śūdrāṃś ca dvijaliṅginaḥ ||  
> dyūtam etat purākalpe dṛṣṭaṃ vairakaraṃ mahat |  
> tasmād dyūtaṃ na seveta hāsyārtham api buddhimān ||  
> pracchannaṃ vā prakāśaṃ vā tan niṣeveta yo naraḥ |  
> tasya daṇḍavikalpaḥ syād yatheṣṭaṃ nṛpates tathā ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

> dyūtaṃ naiva tu seveta krodhalobhavivardhanam |  
> asādhujananaṃ krūraṃ narāṇāṃ dravyanāśanam ||

**[763]**  
> dhruvaṃ dyūtāt kalir yasmād viṣaṃ sarpamukhād iva |  
> tasmād rājā nivarteta viṣaye vyasanaṃ hi tat ||  
> varteta cet prakāśaṃtu dvārāvasthitatorṇam |  
> saṃmohārtham āryāṇāṃ kārayet tatkarapradam ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 27.1–2] |

> dyūtaṃ niṣiddhaṃ manunā satyaśaucadhānapam |  
> tatpravartitam anyaiś ca rājabhāgasamanvitam ||  
> sabhikādhiṣṭhitaṃ kāryaṃ taskarajñāpakaṃ hi tat |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.203] |

> dyūtam ekamukhaṃ kāryaṃ taskarajñānakāraṇāt |  
> eṣa eva vidhir jñeyaḥ prāṇidyūtasamāhvaye ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 27.3] |

> sabhiko grāhakas tasya dadyāj jetre nṛpāya ca |

**[764]** kātyāyanaḥ |

> sabhikaḥ kārayed dyūtaṃ deyaṃ dadyāt svayaṃ nṛpe |  
> daśakaṃ tu śate vṛddhiṃ gṛhṇīyāc ca parājayāt ||  
> jetur dadyāt svayaṃ dravyaṃ jitaṃ grāhyaṃ tripakṣakam |  
> sadyo vā sabhikenaiva kitavāt tu na saṃśayaḥ ||

nāradaḥ [19.2, 8] |

> sabhikaḥ kārayed dyūtaṃ deyaṃ dadyāc ca tattvataḥ |  
> daśakaṃ tu śataṃ vṛddhis tataḥ syād dyūtakāritā ||  
> atha vā kitavo rājñe datvā bhāgaṃ yathoditam |  
> prakāśaṃ devanaṃ kuryād evaṃ doṣo na vidyate ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.199–200] |

> glahe śatikavṛddhes tu sabhikaḥ pañcakaṃ śatam |  
> gṛhṇīyād dhūrtakitavād itarād daśakaṃ śatam ||

**[765]** > sa samyak pālito dadyād rājñe bhāgaṃ yathākṛtam |  
> jitam udgrāhayej jetre dadyāt satyavacāḥ kṣamī ||

nāradaḥ [19.3] |

> dvir abhyastāḥ patanty akṣā glahe yasyākṣadevinaḥ |  
> jayaṃ tasyāparasyāhuḥ kitavasya parājayam ||

kātyāyanaḥ [938] |

> ekarūpā dvirūpā vā dyūte yasyākṣadevinaḥ |  
> dṛśyate ca jayas tasya yasminn akṣā vyavasthitāḥ ||

**[766]** bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 28.2] |

> dvandvayuddhe tu yaḥ kaścid avasādam avāpnuyāt |  
> tatsvāminā paṇo deyo yas tatra parikalpitaḥ ||

nāradaḥ [19.5] |

> aśuddhaḥ kitavo nānyad āśrayed dyūtamaṇḍalam |  
> pratihanyān na kitavaṃ dāpayantaṃ svam iṣṭataḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.201] |

> prāpte nṛpatibhāge tu prasiddhe dyūtamaṇḍale |  
> jitaṃ sa sabhike sthānaṃ dāpayed anyathā na tu ||

nāradaḥ [19.7] |

> anirdiṣṭas tu yo rājñā dyūtaṃ kurvīta mānavaḥ |  
> na sa taṃ prāpnuyāt kāmaṃ vinayaṃ caiva so ‘rhati ||  
> parihāsakṛtaṃ yac ca yac cāpy aviditaṃ nṛpe |  
> tatrāp nāpnuyāt kāmam atha vā nāśam āptayoḥ ||  
> bhakṣyabhojyānnapānāni svalpāny anyāni kānicit |  
> prītyā tu sakṛd ājīvet prasaṅgaṃ tu vivarjayet ||

**[767]** kātyāyanaḥ |

> prasahya dāpayed deyaṃ tasmin sthāne na cānyathā |  
> jitaṃ vai sabhikas tatra sabhikapratyayāt kriyā ||  
> anabhijño jito mocyo ‘bhijño vāpi jito rahaḥ |  
> sarvasve ‘pi jite ‘bhijñe na sarvasvaṃ pradāpayet ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 27.6] |

> raho jito ‘nabhijñaś ca kūṭākṣaiḥ kapaṭena vā |  
> mocyo ‘bhijño ‘pi sarvasvaṃ jitaṃ sarvaṃ na dāpyate ||

nāradaḥ [19.6] |

> kūṭākṣadevinaḥ pāpān nirhared dyūtamaṇḍalāt |  
> kaṇṭhe ‘kṣamālām āsajya sa hy eṣāṃ vinayaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 27.7] |

> kūṭākṣadevinaḥ kṣudrā rājabhāgaharāś ca ye |  
> gaṇanāvañcakāś caiva daṇḍyās te kitavāḥ smṛtāḥ ||

‘**gaṇanāvañcakāḥ’** gaṇanāyāṃ vañcakāḥ |

**[768]** tathā [vya. 22.11] |

> glahaḥ prakāśaḥ kartavyo nirvāsyāḥ kūṭādevinaḥ |

‘**glahaḥ’** dyūte paṇaḥ |

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.202] |

> rājñā sacihnaṃ nirvāsyāḥ kūṭākṣopadhidevinaḥ |

viṣṇuḥ [5.134–35]: “dyūte kūṭākṣadevināṃ karacchedaḥ | upadhidevināṃ saṃdaṃśacchedaḥ” |

‘**saṃdaṃśo’** atrāṅguṣṭhatarjanīsaṃyogaḥ |

nāradaḥ [19.4] |

> kitaveṣv eva tiṣṭhetan kitavāḥ saṃśayaṃ prati |  
> ta eva tatra draṣṭāras tatra caite tu sākṣiṇaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

> vigrahe vijaye lābhe karaṇe kūṭadevinām |  
> pramāṇaṃ sabhikas tatra śuciś ca sabhiko yadi ||

**[769]** > mlecchaśvapākadhūrtānāṃ kitavānāṃ tapasvinām |  
> tatkṛtācārabhettṝṇāṃ niścayo na tu rājani ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 27.9–11] |

> ubhayor api saṃdigdhau kitavās tu parīkṣakāḥ |  
> yadā vidveṣiṇas te tu tadā rājā vicāralet ||  
> evaṃ vādikṛtān vādān avekṣet pratyahaṃ nṛpaḥ |  
> nṛpāśrayās tathā cānye vidvadbhir brāhmaṇaiḥ saha ||

manuḥ [8.178–80] |

> anena vidhinā rājā mithyā vivadatāṃ nṛṇām |  
> sākṣipratyayasiddhāni kāryāṇi samatāṃ nayet ||

**[770]**  
> udito ‘yaṃ vistareṇa mitho vivadamānayoḥ |  
> aṣṭādaśasu mārgeṣu vyavahāravinirṇayaḥ ||  
> evaṃ kāryāṇi sarvāṇi kurvan samyaṅ mahīpatiḥ |  
> deśān alabdhaṇ lipseta labdhāṃś ca paripālayet ||

**iti śrībhaṭṭalakṣmīdharaviracit kṛtyakalpatarau**

**dyūtasamāhvayam**

**[771]**

## 76 kriyābhedaḥ
atha kriyābhedaḥ

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 10.56–59] |

> vivādo ‘ṣṭādaśopetaḥ pūrvottaraviśeṣataḥ |  
> vyākhyātas tv adhunā samyak kriyābhedān nibodhata ||  
> pūrvaṃ kṛtā kriyā yā tu pālanīyā tathaiva sā |  
> anyathā kriyate yatra kriyābhedas tadā bhavet ||  
> vihāya karaṇaṃ pūrvaṃ dhaniko vādhamarṇikaḥ |  
> kuryān nyūnādhikaṃ tulyaṃ kriyābhedaḥ sa ucyate ||  
> dvikenārthaṃ samādāya prapannaḥ pañcakaṃ tu yaḥ |  
> lābhaṃ tatra pramāṇaṃ syāt paścimaṃ tad dhi niścitam ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.23] |

> sarveṣv eva vivādeṣu balavaty uttarakriyā |  
> ādhau pratigrahe krīte pūrvā tu balavattarā ||

**[772]** nāradaḥ [4.97] |

> kriyārṇādiṣu sarveṣu balavaty uttarottarā |  
> pratigrahādhikrīteṣu pūrvā pūrvā garīyasī || 

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 10.61–64] |

> kriyā balavatī pūrvā vikrayādhipratigrahe |  
> ṛṇādikeṣu kāryeṣu paścimā tu garīyasī ||  
> uttarottarabandhena prāgbandhaḥ śithilo bhavet |  
> yaḥ paścimaḥ kriyākāraḥ sa pūrvād balavattaraḥ ||  
> nyāsaṃ kṛtvā tataś cārthaṃ gṛhītvādhiṃ karoti yaḥ |  
> vikrayaṃ vā kriyā tatra paścimā balavattarā ||  
> kṛtaṃ ced ekadivase vikryādhipratigraham |  
> trayāṇām api saṃdehe kathaṃ tatra vicāraṇā ||  
> trīṇy eva hi pramāṇāni vibhajeran yathāṃśataḥ |  
> ubhau cārthānurūpeṇa vibhāgena pratigrahaḥ ||

**iti kriyābhedaḥ**

**[773]**

## 77 prakīrṇakam
atha prakīrṇakam

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 29.1] |

> eṣa vādikṛtaḥ prokto vyavahāraḥ samāsataḥ |  
> nṛpāśrayaṃ pravakṣyāmi vyavahāraṃ prakīrṇakam ||

nāradaḥ [20.1–4] |

> prakīrṇakaḥ punar jñeyo vyavahāro nṛpāśrayaḥ |  
> rājñām ājñāpratīghātas tatkarmakaraṇaṃ tathā ||  
> purapradhānasaṃbhedaḥ prakṛtīnāṃ tathaiva ca |  
> pāṣaṇḍinaigamaśreṇigaṇadharmaviparyayāḥ ||  
> pitāputravivādaś ca prāyaścittavyatikramaḥ |  
> pratigrahavilopaś ca lopa āśramiṇām api ||

**[774]** > varṇasaṃkaradoṣaś ca tadvṛttir ahitas tathā |  
> na dṛṣṭaṃ yac ca pūrveṣu sarvaṃ tat syāt prakīrṇakam ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

> pūrvoktād uktaśeṣaṃ syād adhikāracyutaṃ ca yat |  
> āhṛtya paratantrārthanibaddham asamañjasam ||  
> dṛṣṭāntatvena śāstrānte punaruktakriyāsthitam |  
> anena vidhinā yat tu vākyaṃ tat syāt prakīrṇakam ||  
> rājadharmān svadharmāṃś ca saṃdigdhānāṃ viśeṣaṇam |  
> prāguktād uktaśeṣaṃ ca sarvaṃ tat syāt prakīrṇakam ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 29.12–15] |

> ṣaḍbhāgakaraṇaṃ śulkaṃ garte deyaṃ tathaiva ca |  
> saṃgramacaurabhedī ca paradārābhimarśanam ||

**[775]** > gobrāhmaṇajighāṃsā ca sasyavyāghātakṛt tathā |  
> etān daśāparādhāṃs tu nṛpatiḥ svayam aniveṣet ||  
> niṣkṛtīnām akaraṇam ājñāsedhavyatikramaḥ |  
> varṇāśramavilopaś ca varṇasaṃkaralopanam ||  
> nidhir niṣphalavittaṃ ca daridrasya dhanāgamaḥ |  
> etāṃś cāraiḥ suviditān svayaṃ rājā nivārayet ||  
> anāmnātāni kāryāṇi kriyāvādāś ca vādinām |  
> prakṛtīnāṃ prakopaś ca saṃketaś ca parasparam ||  
> aśāstravihitaṃ yac ca prajāyāṃ saṃpravartate |  
> upāyaiḥ sāmabhedādyair etāni śamayen nṛpaḥ ||

**varṇāśramavyavasthāpanam**

yājñavalkyaḥ [1.361] |

> kulāni jātīḥ śreṇīś ca gaṇān jānapadān api |  
> svadharmāc calitān rājā vinīya sthāpayet pathi ||

nāradaḥ [20.5–6] |

> rājā tv avahitaḥ sarvān āśramān paripālayet |  
> upāyaiḥ śāstravihitaiḥ caturbhiḥ prakṛtīs tathā ||  
> yo yo varṇo ‘vahīyet yaś codrekam anuvrajet |  
> taṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā svato mārgāt pracyutaṃ sthāpayet pathi ||

**[776]** śaṅkhalikhitau |

> varṇāśramāṇāṃ saṃsthānam ānupūrvyānupūrvaśaḥ |  
> teṣāṃ hetur avasthāne rājā suprasthito yadi ||  
> rājamūlam idaṃ rāṣṭraṃ brahmakṣatrapurogamam |  
> sthite rājani taddharme durācārān na kurvate ||

manuḥ [9.273; 8.410; 8.418] |

> yaś cāpi dharmasamayāt pracyuto dharmajīvanaḥ |  
> daṇḍenaiva samāploṣet svakād dharmād dhi vicyutam |  
> vāṇijyaṃ kārayed vaiśyaṃ kusīdaṃ kṛṣim eva ca |  
> paśūnāṃ rakṣaṇaṃ caiva śūdraṃ dāsyaṃ dvijanmanām ||  
> vaiśyaśūdrau prayatnena svāni karmāṇi kārayet |  
> tau hi cyutau svakarmabhyaḥ kṣobhayetām idaṃ jagat ||

yamaḥ |

> yat kiṃcit kurute rājā śubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubham |  
> bhṛtyās tad anukurvanti nartakyo nartanaṃ yathā ||  
> tasmāt paurāṇikān dharmān nipuṇair mantribhiḥ saha |  
> praśiṣyād bhūpatiḥ samyag brahmakṣatravivṛddhaye ||

**[777]** gautamaḥ [8.1–3]: “dvau loke dhṛtavratau rājā brāhmaṇaś ca bahuśrutaḥ | tayoś caturvidhasya manuṣyajātasyāntaḥsaṃjñānāṃ calanapatanasarpiṇām āyattaṃ jīvanam | prasūtirakṣaṇam asaṃkaro dharmaḥ” |

vasiṣṭhaḥ [1.40–42]: “trayo varṇā brāhmaṇasy nideśe varteran | brāhmaṇo dharmān prabrūyāt | rājā cānuśiṣyāt” |

hārītaḥ: “nigrahānugrahapālaneṣu sarveṣām unmaryādināṃ maryādābhedināṃ paradāraparadravyāpahāriṇāṃ rājā śāstā bhavaty evety āha |

> gurur ātmavatāṃ śāstā śāstā rājā durātmanām |  
> antaḥpracchannapāpānāṃ śāstā vaivasvato yamaḥ ||  
> gurubhir ye na śāsyante rājñā vā gūḍhakilbiṣāḥ |  
> te narā yamadaṇḍena śastā yānty adhamāṃ gatim ||

āpastambaḥ [2.10.13–16; 2.11.1]: “śāstrair adhigatānām indriyadaurbalyād vipannānāṃ śāstā nirveśam upadiśed yathākarma yathoktam | tasya cec chāstram ativarteran rājānaṃ gamayet | **[778]** rājā purohitaṃ dharmārthakuśalam | sa brāhmaṇān niyuñjyāt | balaviśeṣeṇa paradāsyavarjaṃ niyamair upaśodhayet | itareṣāṃ varṇānām ā prāṇaviyogāt samavekṣya teṣāṃ karmāṇi rājā daṇḍaṃ praṇayet” |

uśanā |

> mohāt pramādāt saṃharṣāt prītyā coktaṃ mayeti yaḥ |  
> nāham evaṃ punar vakṣye daṇḍārdhaṃ tasya kalpayet ||

vākpāruṣyaviṣayam etat |

gautamaḥ [12.48–49]: “puruṣaśaktyaparādhānubandhavijñānād daṇḍaniyogaḥ | anujñānaṃ vā vedavitsamavāyavacanāt” |

vasiṣṭhaḥ [19.6]: “daṇḍas tu deśakālakarmavarṇavayovidyāsthānaviśeṣair hiṃsākrośayoḥ kalpyaḥ, āgamād dṛṣṭāntāc ca” |

‘rājñā’ ity anuvṛttau, śaṅkhaḥ: “daṇḍo yathāsārāpakāraṃ ca vayovidyāvarṇalakṣaṇaguṇānugaḥ” |

**[779]** daṇḍasṛṣṭyanantaraṃ manuḥ [7.16] |

> taṃ deśakālau śaktiṃ ca vidyāṃ cāvekṣya tattvataḥ |  
> yathārhataḥ saṃpraṇayen nareṣv anyāyavartiṣu ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [1.368] |

> jñātvāparādhaṃ deśaṃ ca kālaṃ balam athāpi vā |  
> vayaḥ karma ca vittaṃ ca daṇḍaṃ daṇḍyeṣu pātayet ||

viṣṇuḥ [5.190] |

> āgaḥsu ca yathānyeṣu jñātvā jātiṃ dhanaṃ vayaḥ |  
> daṇḍaṃ prakalpayed rājā saṃmantrya brāhmaṇaiḥ saha ||

punar viṣṇuḥ [3.91–94]: “aparādhānurūpaṃ ca daṇḍaṃ daṇḍyeṣu pātayet | samyagdaṇḍapraṇayanaṃ kuryāt | dvitīye ‘parādhe na sa kasyacit kṣameta | svadharmam apālayan nādaṇḍyo nāmāsti rājñaḥ” |

manuḥ [8.335] |

> pitācāryaḥ suhṛn mātā bhāryā putraḥ purohitaḥ |  
> nādaṇḍyo nāma rājño ‘sti yaḥ svadharme na tiṣthati ||

**[780]** yājñavlkyaḥ |

> ṛtvikpurohitāmātyaputrasaṃbandhibāndhavāḥ |  
> dharmād civalitā daṇḍyā nirvāsyā rājahiṃsakāḥ ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: “adaṇḍyau mātāpitarau snātakapurohitau parivrājakavānaprasthau janmakarmaśrutaśīlaśaucācāravantaś ca | ete hi darmapratikarā rājñaḥ | strībālavṛddhās tapasvinas tebhyaḥ krodhaṃ niyacchet” |

kātyāyanaḥ |

> ācāryasya pitur mātur bāndhavānāṃ tathaiva ca |  
> eteṣām aparādhe tu daṇḍo naiva vidhīyate ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 9.17, 11] |

> gurūn purohitān pūjyān vāgdaṇḍenaiva daṇḍayet |  
> vivādino narāṃś cānyān doṣiṇo ‘rthena daṇḍayet ||  
> mahāparādhayuktāṃś ca vadhadaṇḍena śāsayet |

**[781]** kātyāyanaḥ |

> mitrādiṣu prayuñjīta vāgdaṇḍaṃ dhik tapasvini |  
> yathoktaṃ tasya tat kuryād anuktaṃ sādhukalpitam ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 29.2; 9.12–13] |

> vāgdhigdaṇḍaṃ vadhaṃ caiva caturdhā kalpitaṃ damam |  
> puruṣaṃ doṣavibhavaṃ jñātvā saṃparikalpayet ||  
> svalpe ‘parādhe vāgdaṇḍaṃ dhigdaṇḍaṃ pūrvasāhase |  
> madhye tu rodhanaṃ daṇḍaṃ rājadroheṣu bandhanam ||  
> nirvāsanaṃ virodhe ‘pi kāryam ātmahitaiṣiṇā |  
> yojyāḥ samastāś caikasya mahāpātakakāriṇaḥ ||

manuḥ [8.123] |

> vāgdaṇḍaṃ prathamaṃ kuryād dhigdaṇḍaṃ tadanantaram |  
> tṛtīyaṃ dhanadaṇḍaṃ tu vadhadaṇḍam ataḥ param ||

tathā [8.130] |

> vadhenāpi yadā tv enaṃ nigṛhītuṃ na śaknuyāt |  
> tadaiṣu sarvam apy etat prayuñjīta catuṣtayam ||

‘**vadhenāpi’** tāḍanenāpīty arthaḥ |

**[782]** bṛhaspatiḥ [1.91; 29.6, 9] |

> vāgdaṇḍaś caiva dhigdaṇḍo viprāyattāv ubhau smṛtau |  
> arthadaṇḍavadhāv uktau rājāyattāv ubhāv api ||

manuḥ [8.310; 9.288; 8.124–25] |

> adhārmikaṃ tribhir nyāyair nigṛhṇīta prayatnataḥ |  
> nirodhanena bandhena vividhena vadhena ca ||  
> bandhanāni ca sarvāṇi vamāṅge viniveśayet |  
> duḥkhitā yatra dṛśyeran vikṛtāḥ pāpakāriṇaḥ ||  
> daśasthānāni daṇḍasya manuḥ svāyaṃbhuvo ‘bravīt |  
> triṣu varṇeṣu yāni syū rakṣato brāhmaṇo vrajet ||  
> upastham udaraṃ jihvā hastau pādau ca pañcamam |  
> cakṣur nāsā ca karṇau ca dhanaṃ dehas tathaiva ca ||

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 29.4–5] |

> hastāṅghriliṅganayanaṃ jihvā karṇau ca nāsikā |  
> grīvā pādārdhasaṃdaṃśalalāṭauṣṭhagudaṃ kaṭiḥ ||  
> sthānāny etāni daṇḍasya nirdiṣṭāni caturdaśa |  
> lalāṭāṅko brāhmaṇasya nānyo daṇḍo vidhīyate ||

yamaḥ |

> sarveṣām eva varṇānām anyonyasyāparādhinām |  
> śārīraṃ dhanasaṃyuktaṃ daṇḍaṃ dharmyaṃ prakalpayet ||

**[783]** > jagat sarvam idaṃ hanyād brāhmaṇasya na tatsamam |  
> tasmāt tasya vadhaṃ rājā manasāpi na cintayet ||  
> avadhyān brāhmaṇān āhuḥ sarvapāpeṣv avasthitān |  
> yad yad vipreṣu kuśalaṃ na tad rājā samācaret ||

hārītaḥ |

> na tv aṅgabhedaṃ viprasya pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ |  
> tapasā cejyayā caiva brāhmaṇaḥ pūyate sadā ||

manuḥ [8.380–81] |

> na jātu brāhmaṇaṃ hanyāt sarvapāpeṣv avasthitam |  
> rāṣṭrād enaṃ bahiḥ kuryāt samagradhanam akṣatam ||  
> na brāhmaṇavadhād bhūyān adharmo bhuvi vidyate |  
> tasmād asya vadhaṃ rājā manasāpi na cintayet ||

gautamaḥ [8.4–12]: “sa eva bahuśruto bhavati | lokavedavedāṅgavit | vākovākyetihāsapurāṇakuśalaḥ | tadapekṣas tadvṛttiḥ | catvāriṃśatā saṃskāraiḥ saṃskṛtaḥ | triṣu karmasv abhirataḥ | ṣaṭsu vā | sāmayācārikeṣv abhivinītaḥ | ṣaḍbhiḥ parihāryo rājñā avadhyaś cābandhyaś cādaṇḍyaś cābahiṣkāryaś cāparivādyaś cāparihāryaś ceti” |

‘**triṣu’** dānādhyayanayāgeṣu | ‘**ṣaṭsu’** [anu]pravacanayājanapratigrahādhyayanādiṣu |

**[784]** vasiṣṭhaḥ [1.45–46]: “brāhmaṇo vedam ādyaṃ karoti | brāhmaṇa āpad uddharati | tasmād brāhmaṇo ‘nādyaḥ somo rājā bhavatīti ha pretya cābhyudayikam itīha vijñāyate” |

śaṅkhalikhitau: “sarvatra trayāṇāṃ varṇānāṃ dhanahārakārāvadhabandhāḥ kriyāsu coparodho mahatsv api pātakeṣu vivāso ‘ṅkakaraṇaṃ brāhmaṇasya prāyaścittāni vā śodhanam | apīḍyo hi brāhmaṇaḥ” |

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 9.10] |

> mahāpātakayukto ‘pi na vipro vadham arhati |  
> nirvāsanāṅkane mauṇḍyaṃ tasya kuryān narādhipaḥ ||

manuḥ [9.235–42] |

> brahmahā ca surāpaś ca taskaro gurutalpagaḥ |  
> ete sarve pṛthag jñeyā mahāpātakino narāḥ ||  
> caturṇām api caiteṣāṃ prāyaścittam akurvatām |  
> śārīraṃ dhanasaṃyuktaṃ dharmyaṃ daṇḍaṃ prakalpayet ||  
> gurutalpe bhagaḥ kāryaḥ surāpāne surādhvajaḥ |  
> steye tu śvapadaṃ kāryaṃ brahmahaṇy aśirāḥ pumān ||  
> asaṃbhojyā asaṃyājyā asaṃpāṭhyāvivāhinaḥ |  
> careyuḥ pṛthivīṃ dīnāḥ sarvadharmabahiṣkṛtāḥ ||

**[785]** > jñātisaṃbandhibhis tv ete tyaktavyāḥ kṛtalakṣaṇāḥ |  
> nirdayā nirnamaskārās tan manor anuśāsanam ||  
> prāyaścittaṃ tu kurvāṇāḥ pūrve varṇā yathoditam |  
> nāṅkyā rājñā lalāṭeṣu dāpyās tūttamasāhasam ||  
> āgaḥsu brāhmaṇasyaiṣ kāryo madhyamasāhasaḥ |  
> vivāsyo vā bhaved rāṣṭrāt sadravyaḥ saparicchadaḥ ||  
> itare kṛtavantas tu pāpāny etāni dharmataḥ |  
> sarvasvahānim arhanti kāmatas tu pravāsanam ||

‘**taskaro’** atra suvrṇacoraḥ |

baudhāyanaḥ [1.18.18]: “brāhmaṇasya bhrūṇahatyāgurutalpagamanasvarṇasteyasurāpāneṣu kabandhabhagaśvapadadhvajāṃs taptenāyasā lalāṭe ‘ṅkayitvā viṣayān nirvāsanam” |

nāradaḥ [21.43–45] |

> brāhmaṇasyāparādheṣu caturṣv aṅko vidhīyate |  
> gurutalpe surāpāne steye brāhmaṇahiṃsane ||

**[786]** > gurutalpe bhagaḥ kāryaḥ surāpāne surādhvajaḥ |  
> steye tu śvapadaṃ kṛtvā śikhipittena pūrayet ||  
> aśirāḥ puruṣaḥ kāryo lalāṭe dvijaghātinaḥ |  
> asaṃbhāṣyas tu kartavyas tan manor anuśāsanam ||

yamaḥ |

> brāhmaṇasyāparādheṣu caturṣv evaṃ vidhīyate |  
> śiraso muṇḍanaṃ daṇḍaṃ purān nirvāsanaṃ tathā ||  
> prakhyāpanārthaṃ pāpasya prayāṇaṃ gardabhena tu |  
> lalāṭe vāṅkakaraṇaṃ kuryād rājā yathāvidhi ||

āpastambaḥ [2.27.18–21]: “niyamātikraminam anyaṃ vā rahasi bandhayet | ā samāpatteḥ | asamāpattau nāśyaḥ | ācārya ṛtvik snātako rājeti trāṇaṃ syur anyatra vadhyāt” |

‘**niyamātikramiṇam’** vihitasyākartāram | ‘**anyam’** niṣiddhakāriṇaṃ brāhmaṇam | ‘**rahasi’** rahasyasthāne ‘**bandhayed’** | ‘**ā samāpteḥ’** yāvan na kariṣyāmīti saṃpratipattiṃ kuryāt | anyathā ‘**nāśyo’** nirvāsyaḥ | ācāryādayo daṇḍyānāṃ ‘**trāṇaṃ syuḥ’** trātāro bhaveyuḥ, na kadācid audāsīnyaṃ bhajeyuḥ |

yamaḥ |

> stenāḥ surāpā brahmaghnā gurudārābhigāminaḥ |  
> na santi yasya rāṣṭreṣu sa rājā śakralokabhāk ||

**[787]** manuḥ [9.243–47] |

> nādadīta nṛpaḥ sādhur mahāpātakino dhanam |  
> ādadānas tu tallobhāt tenādharmeṇa lipyate ||  
> apsu preveśya tad daṇḍaṃ varuṇāyopapādayet |  
> śrutividyopasaṃpanne brāhmaṇe pratipādayet ||  
> īśo daṇḍasya varuṇo rājño daṇḍadharo hi saḥ |  
> īśaḥ sarvasya jagato brāhmaṇo vedapāragaḥ ||  
> yatra varjayate rājā pāpakṛdbhyo dhanāgamam |  
> tatra kālena jāyanta mānavā dīrghajīvinaḥ ||  
> niṣpadyante ca sasyāni yathoktāni viśāṃpate |  
> bālāś ca na pramīyante vikṛtiṃ na ca jāyate ||

yamaḥ |

> patitasya dhanaṃ hṛtvā rājā parṣadi dāpayet |  
> sarvasvaṃ ca hared rājā caturthaṃ cāvaśeṣayet |  
> bhṛtyebhyo ‘nnaṃ smaran dharmaṃ prājāpatyam iti śrutiḥ ||

**[788]**

## 78 taraśulkaḥ
atha taraśulkaḥ

tatra vasiṣthaḥ (18.17–22): “saṃyāne daśavāhavāhinī dviguṇakāriṇī syāt | daśapuruṣavatī pratyekaṃ prapāḥ syuḥ | puṃsāṃ cāvarārdhavāhaṃ vahet | adhyardhā striyaḥ syus taro ‘ṣṭau māṣāḥ śaramadhyāyā aśaramadhyāyāḥ pādaḥ kārṣāpaṇasya | nirudakas taro māṣyaḥ” |
