saṃyāti sametyāneneti ‘**saṃyānaḥ’** nadīparaḥ | tatra vāhinī nauḥ| vāhayantīti ‘**vāhāḥ’** || daśa puruṣāḥ yatra sā tathā ‘**daśapuruṣavatī’** vāhakād anye ‘pi daśapuruṣā yasyām ārūḍhāḥ | ‘**prapāḥ syuḥ’** evaṃ daśapuruṣāḥ prativāhakaṃ prakarṣeṇa pālayitāraḥ syuḥ | puṃsām eva ‘**avarārdhaṃ vāhaṃ vahet’** sā nauḥ yāvantaṃ bhāraṃ vahati tadapekṣayā ‘**avarārdham’** avaraṃ nyūnam ardhaṃ yasmin vāhe taṃ bhāraṃ puruṣaiḥ pūrayet | ‘**adhyardhāḥ striyaḥ syuḥ’** puruṣāpekṣayā adhyardhāḥ striyaḥ, tāsām atibhīrutvāt | ‘**taraḥ’** śulkaḥ ‘**māṣaḥ**,’ kārṣāpaṇaviṃśatitamo bhāgaḥ | ‘**śaramadhyāyāḥ’** yasyāṃ nadyāṃ dhanuṣmatā kṣiptaśaro madhye patati **[789]** tasyāḥ ity arthaḥ | ‘**aśaramadhyāyāḥ pādaḥ’** na madhyaṃ yasyāṃ śareṇa lakṣyate [yāṃ śaro laṅghayatīry arthaḥ] ‘**pādaḥ’** caturthāṃśaḥ ‘**kārṣāpaṇasya’** | ‘**nirudakaḥ’** alpodakaḥ | ‘**māṣyaḥ’** māṣaḥ śulko yatra dīyate |

manuḥ [8.404–07] |

> paṇaṃ yāne taraṃ dadyāt pauruṣe ‘rdhapaṇaṃ taram |  
> pādaṃ paśuś ca yoṣic ca pādārdhaṃ riktakaḥ pumān ||  
> bhāṇḍapūrṇāni yānāni tāryaṃ dāpyāni sārataḥ |  
> riktabhāṇḍāni yat kiṃcit pumāṃsaś cāparicchadāḥ ||  
> dīrghādhvani yathādeśaṃ yathākālaṃ taro bhavet |  
> nadītīreṣu tad vidyāt samudre nāsti lakṣaṇam ||  
> garbhiṇī tu dvimāsādis tathā pravrajito muniḥ |  
> brāhmaṇā liṅginaś caiva nādāpyās tārikaṃ tare ||

**[790]** vasiṣṭhaḥ [18.23–25]: “akaraḥ śrotriyo rājā pumān anāthaḥ pravrajito bālavṛddhataruṇaprajātāḥ prāggāmikāḥ kumāryo mṛtapatyaś ca | bāhubhyāṃ taran śataguṇaṃ dāpyaḥ” |

‘**pumān anāthaḥ’** svajanarahito rogārto vā | ‘**taruṇaprajātāḥ’** aciraprasūtāḥ | ‘**prāggāmikāḥ’** [satatagamanaśīlāḥ] lekhahārakādayaḥ | ‘**mṛtapatyo’** vidhavāḥ |

viṣṇuḥ [5.131]: “tarikaś ca sthalaśulkaṃ gṛhṇan daśapaṇān daṇḍyaḥ | brahmacārivānaprasthabhikṣugurviṇītīrthānusāriṇāṃ nāvikaḥ śaulkikaḥ śulkam ādadānaś ca | tac ca teṣāṃ jahyāt” |

‘**ādadānaś ca’** daṇḍya ity anuṣaṅgaḥ |

manuḥ [8.408–09] |

> yan nāvi kiṃcid dāśānāṃ viśīryetāparādhataḥ |  
> tad dāśair eva dātavyaṃ samāgamya svato ‘ṃśataḥ ||  
> eṣa nauyāyinām ukto vyavahāravinirṇayaḥ |  
> dāśāparādhatas toye daivike nāsti nigrahaḥ ||

**[791]**

## 79 nidhiḥ
atha nidhiḥ

tatra manuḥ [8.35–36] |

> mamāyam iti yo brūyān nidhiṃ satyena hetutaḥ |  
> tasyādadīta ṣaḍbhāgaṃ rājā dvādaśam eva ca ||  
> anṛtaṃ tu vadan dāpyaḥ svavittasyāṃśam aṣṭamam |  
> tasyaiva vā nidhānasya saṃkhyayālpīsasīṃ kalām ||

viṣṇuḥ [3.63–64]: “svanihitād rājñe brāhmaṇavarjaṃ dvādaśam amśaṃ dadyuḥ | paranihitaṃ svanihitam iti vadantas tatsamaṃ daṇḍam āvaheyuḥ” |

nāradaḥ [10.8] |

> svam apy arthaṃ tathā naṣṭaṃ labdhvā rājñe nivedayet |  
> gṛhṇīyāt tu tataḥ śuddham asuddhaṃ syāt tv ato ‘nyathā ||

**atha paranihitam**

tatra vasiṣṭhaḥ [3.14–15]: “aprajñāyamānaṃ vittaṃ yo ‘dhigaccheta rājā tad uddhared adhigrantre ṣaṣṭham aṃśaṃ pradāya | brāhmaṇaś ced adhigacchet ṣaṭkarmasu vartamāno mā rājā haret” |

‘aprajñāyamānam’ ajñāyamānasvāmikam asvāmikaṃ ca |

**[792]** nāradaḥ [10.6–7] |

> pareṇa nihitaṃ labdhvā rājany upaharen nidhim |  
> rājagāmī nidhiḥ sarvaḥ sarveṣāṃ brāhmaṇād ṛte ||  
> brāhmaṇo ‘pi nidhiṃ labdhvā kṣipraṃ rājñe nivedayet |  
> tena dattaṃ tu bhuñjīta stenaḥ syād anivedane ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [2.34–35] |

> rājā labdhvā nidhiṃ dadyād dvijebhyo ‘rdhaṃ dvijaḥ punaḥ |  
> vidvān aśeṣam ādadyāt sa sarvasya prabhur yataḥ ||  
> itareṇa nidhau labdhe rājā ṣaṣṭhāṃśam āharet |  
> aniveditavijñātaṃ dāpyas taṃ daṇḍam eva ca ||

viṣṇuḥ [3.56–62]: “nidhiṃ labdhvā tadardhaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo dadyāt | datvā dvitīyam ardhaṃ kośe praveśayet | nidhiṃ labdhvā brāhmaṇaḥ svayam ādadyāt | kṣatriyaś caturtham aṃśaṃ rājñe dadyāt, śeṣaṃ caturtham aṃśaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo dadyād ardham ādadyāt | vaiśyaś caturtham aṃśaṃ rājñe dadyād brāhmaṇebhyo ‘rdham aṃśaṃ svayam ādadyāt  [793]| śūdras tv avāptaṃ dvādaśadhā vibhajya pañcamaṃ rājñe dadyāt | brāhmaṇebhyo ‘ṃśadvayam eva dadyāt | avaśiṣṭaṃ sarvaṃ svayam ādadyāt | aniveditavijñātasya sarvasvam apaharet” |

manuḥ [8.38–39] |

> yaṃ tu paśyen nidhiṃ rājā purāṇaṃ nihitaṃ kṣitau |  
> tasmād dvijebhyo datvārdham ardhaṃ kośe niveśayet ||  
> nidhīnāṃ tu purāṇānāṃ dhātūnām ākarasya ca |  
> rakṣaṇād dharmabhāg rājā bhūmer adhipatir hisaḥ ||

viṣṇuḥ [3.55]: “ākarebhyaḥ sarvam ādadyāt” |

vasiṣṭhaḥ: “udvāhakāriṇaṃ tv āgmayet kasya kena saha vivāho yujyata it varṇavibhāgapratiṣṭhāpanāya saṃpradāyaṃ rakṣet | ākaraśuddhiś ca tadanurūpakaragrahaṇādyarthe jānīyāt | ākarādhpatayo hi prāyeṇa māyāvino bhavanti” |

**[794]**

## 80 daṇḍapraṇayanavivekaḥ
atha daṇḍapraṇayanavivekaḥ

tatra manuḥ [7.14–15, 17–18] |

> tadarthaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ goptāraṃ dharmam ātmajam |  
> brahmatejomayaṃ daṇḍam asṛjat pūrvam īśvaraḥ ||  
> tasya sarvāṇi bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca |  
> bhayād bhogāya kalpante svadharmān na calanti ca ||  
> sa rājā puruṣo daṇḍaḥ sa netā śāsitā ca saḥ |  
> caturṇām āśramāṇāṃ ca dharmasya pratibhūḥ kṛtaḥ ||  
> daṇḍaḥ śāsti prajāḥ sarvā daṇḍa evābhirakṣati |  
> daṇḍaḥ supteṣu jāgarti daṇḍaṃ dharmaṃ vidur budhāḥ ||

tathā [7.25] |

> yatra śyāmo lohitākṣo daṇḍaś carati pāpahā |  
> prajās tatra vivardhante netā cet sādhu paśyati ||

tathā [7.31, 26, 30, 27–29, 19] |

> śucinā satyasandhena yathāśāstrānusāriṇā |  
> daṇḍaḥ praṇayituṃ śakyaḥ susahāyena dhīmatā ||  
> tasyāhuḥ saṃpraṇetāraṃ rājānaṃ satyavādinam |  
> samīkṣyakāriṇaṃ prājñaṃ dharmakāmārthakovidam ||  
> asahāyena mūḍhena lubdhenākṛtabuddhinā |  
> na śakto nyāyato netum ṛktheṣu viṣayeṣu ca ||

**[795]** > taṃ rājā praṇayan samyak trivargenābhivardhate |  
> kāmātmaviṣayaḥ kṣudro daṇḍenaiva nihanyate ||  
> daṇḍo hi sumahatejo durdharaś cākṛtātmabhiḥ |  
> dharmād vicalitaṃ hanti nṛpam eva sabāndhavam ||  
> tato durgaṃ ca rāṣṭraṃ ca lokaṃ ca sacarācaram |  
> antarikṣagatāṃś caiva yatīn devāṃś ca pīḍayet ||  
> samīkṣya subhṛtaḥ samyak sarvā rañjayati prajāḥ |  
> asamīkṣya praṇītas tu vināśayati sarvataḥ ||

‘**sudhṛtaḥ’** yathārhaṃ dhṛtaḥ |

tathā [7.20–21] |

> yadi na praṇayed rājā daṇḍaṃ daṇḍyeṣv atandritaḥ |  
> śūle matsyān ivāpakṣyan durbalān balavattarāḥ ||  
> adyāt kākaḥ puroḍāśaṃ śvā ca lihyād dhavis tathā |  
> svāmyaṃ ca na syāt kasmiṃś cit pravartetādharottaram ||

aṅgirāḥ |

> rājā gurur yamaś caiva śāsan dharmeṇa yujyate |  
> kartā ca mucyate pāpān na ca pāpena lipyate ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [1.359–60] |

> yo daṇḍyān daṇḍayed rājā samyag vadhyāṃś ca ghātayet |  
> iṣṭaṃ syāt kratubhis tena samāptavaradakṣiṇaiḥ ||

**[796]** > iti saṃcintya nṛpatiḥ kratutullyaphalaṃ pṛthak |  
> vyavahārān svayaṃ paśyet sabhyaiḥ parivṛto ‘nvaham ||

tathā [1.357] |

> adharmadaṇḍanaṃ loke dharmakīrtivināśanam |  
> samyak ca daṇḍanaṃ rājñaḥ svargakīrtijayāvaham ||

manuḥ [8.128; 9.247] |

> adaṇḍyaṃ daṇḍayan rājā daṇḍyaṃ caivāpy adaṇḍayan |  
> ayaśo mahad āpnoti narakaṃ caiva gacchati ||  
> yāvān avadhyasya vadhe tāvān vadhyasya mokṣaṇe |  
> adharmo nṛpater dṛṣṭo dharmas tu viniyacchataḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

> rājāno mantriṇaś caiva viśeṣād enam avāpnuyuḥ |  
> aśāsanāt tu pāpānāṃ natānāṃ daṇḍadhāraṇāt ||

‘**natānām’** vinītānām, adaṇḍyānām iti yāvat |

vasiṣṭhaḥ [19.40–43]: “daṇḍotsarge rājaikarātram upavaset | trirātraṃ purohitaḥ | kṛcchram adaṇḍane purohitas trirātraṃ rājā ca” |

**[797]**

**atha daṇḍotkarṣāpakarṣādiḥ**

tatra kātyāyanaḥ |

> sacihnam api pāpaṃ tu pṛcchet pāpasya kāraṇam |  
> tathā daṇḍaṃ niyuñjīta doṣam āropya yatnataḥ ||  
> prāṇātyaye tu yatra syād akāryakaraṇaṃ kṛtam |  
> daṇḍas tatra tu naiva syād eṣa dharmaḥ smṛto bhṛguḥ ||  
> sadvṛttānāṃ tu sarveṣām aparādho yadā bhavet |  
> avaśenaiva daivāt tu daṇḍaṃ tatra na kalpayet ||  
> samyagdaṇḍapraṇetāro nṛpāḥ pūjyāḥ surair api |  
> ārambhe prathamaṃ dadyāt pravṛtte madhyamaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
> yasa yo vihito daṇḍaḥ paryāptasya sa vai bhavet |  
> kalpito yasya yo daṇḍas tv aparādhasya yatnataḥ ||

**[798]** > paṇānāṃ grahaṇaṃ tat syāt tanmūlyaṃ vātha rājani |  
> aparādheṣu niyatam āhur gārgīyamānavāḥ ||  
> daṇḍanīyaḥ sa śauthilyāt prathamaṃ neti gautamaḥ |  
> arthavanto yatas santo yathoktān api te damān ||  
> dadyur naivopaśāmyeyus tasmāt tatra viniścayaḥ |  
> tasmād avyāhatāḥ pāpā yena yena śubhaṃ punaḥ ||  
> na kuryus tat tad evaiṣāṃ kartavyam iti niścayaḥ |  
> samūhasthāḥ pravṛttāś ca pāpeṣu puruṣādhamāḥ ||  
> yathoktaṃ dviguṇaṃ daṇḍam ekaikasya pradāpayet |

nāradaḥ [21.53–56] |

> śārīraś cārthadaṇḍaś ca daṇḍas tu dvividhaḥ smṛtaḥ |  
> śārīro dvividhaḥ prokto hy arthadaṇḍo ‘py anekadhā ||  
> kākiṇyādis tv arthadaṇḍaḥ sarvasvāntas tathaiva ca |  
> śārīras tv avarodhādir jīvitāntakaras tathā ||  
> kākiṇyādis tu yo daṇḍaḥ sa tu māṣaparaḥ smṛtaḥ |  
> māṣāvarārdho yaḥ proktaḥ kārṣāpaṇaparas tu saḥ ||

**[799]** > kārṣāpaṇāvarād yas tu catuḥkārṣāpaṇottaraḥ |  
> dvyavaro ‘ṣṭapaṇās tv anyas tryavaro dvādaśōttaraḥ ||  
> kārṣāpaṇādyā ye proktāḥ sarve te syuś caturguṇāḥ |  
> evam anye ‘pi vijñeyāḥ prāk caite pūrvasāhasāt ||

manuḥ [8.336] |

> kārṣāpaṇaṃ bhaved daṇḍo yatrānyaḥ prākṛto janaḥ |  
> tatra rājñāṃ bhaved daṇḍaḥ sahasram iti dhāraṇā ||

tathā [9.148] |

> brāhmaṇān bādhamānaṃ tu kāmād avaravarṇajam |  
> hanyāc citrair vadhopayair udvegajanakair nṛpaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

> pravrajyāvasitaṃ śūdraṃ japahomaparaṃ tathā |  
> vadhena śasayet pāpaṃ dāpyo vā dviguṇaṃ damam ||

**[800]** > aspṛśyadhūrtadāsānāṃ narāṇāṃ pāpakāriṇām |  
> prātilomyaprasūtānāṃ tāḍanaṃ nārthato damaḥ ||  
> paratantrās tu ye kecid dāsatvaṃ ye ca saṃsthitāḥ |  
> anāthās te tu nirdiṣṭās teṣāṃ daṇḍas tu tādanam ||  
> tāḍanaṃ bandhanaṃ caiva tathaiva ca viḍambanam |  
> eṣa daṇḍo hi dāsasya nārthadaṇḍo bṛhaspatiḥ ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: “śilpinaḥ kāravaḥ śūdrās teṣāṃ vyabhicāreṣv api śilpopakaraṇāni rakṣed rājā | tulamānapratimānasamutthāni vaṇikpathānām | kṣetrabījabhaktagośakaṭakarṣaṇadravyāṇi karṣakāṇām | vādyabhāṇḍālaṅkāravāsāṃsi raṅgopajīvinām | gṛhaśayanālaṅkāravāsāṃsi veśyānām | śastrāṇi cāyudhopajīvinām | sarveṣāṃ karaṇadravyāṇi nāhāryāṇi rājñā dhārmikeṇa | asvā hi puruṣāḥ pāpabahulāś cāvidheyāś ca bhavanti | tebhyaḥ pāpāṃśabhāg rājā | tasmān nādhanānnānupakaraṇān kuryāt | tanmūlā hi vṛttiḥ | vṛttimūlo nivāsaḥ | tair nivasadbhiḥ sphītaṃ rāṣṭram ity ucyate” |

**[801]** bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 9.19] |

> vadhārhaḥ suvarṇaśataṃ damaṃ dapyas tu pūruṣaḥ |  
> aṅgacchedārhakas tv ardhaṃ saṃdaṃśārhas tadardhakam ||

kātyāyanaḥ [964–66] |

> suvarṇaśatam ekaṃ tu vadhārho daṇḍam arhati |  
> aṅgacchede tadardhaṃ tu vivāse pañcaviṃśatim ||  
> kulīnāryaviśiṣṭeṣu nikṛṣṭeṣv anusārataḥ |  
> sarvasvaṃ vā nigṛhyaitān purācchīghraṃ pravāsayet ||  
> nirdhanā bandhane sthāpyā vadhaṃ naiva pravartayet |  
> sarveṣāṃ pāpayuktānāṃ viśeṣārthaś ca śāstrataḥ ||

tathā [967–68, 781, 969] |

> vadhāṅgacchedārhavipro niḥsaṅge bandhane viśet |  
> tadā karmaviyukto ‘sau vṛttasthasya damo hi saḥ ||

**[802]** > kūṭasakṣy api nirvāsyo vikhyāpyo ‘satpratigrahI |  
> aṅgacchedī viyojyaḥ syāt svadharme bandhanena tu ||  
> karṇauṣṭhaghrāṇapādākṣijihvāśiśnakarasya ca |  
> chedane cottamaṃ dadyād bhedane madhyamaṃ bhṛguḥ ||  
> etaiḥ samāparādhānāṃ tatrāpy evaṃ prakalpayet |  
> bālavṛddhāturastrīṇāṃ na daṇḍas tāḍanaṃ damaḥ ||

‘**vadhāṅgacchedārhaḥ’** varṇāntarāṇāṃ yenāparādhena vadho ‘ṅgacchedo vā daṇḍaḥ, tad yukto vipraḥ | ‘**vṛttasthasya’** iti viśeṣaṇena durvṛttasya daṇḍāntaraṃ sūcayati |

manuḥ [9.229–30] |

> kṣatraviṭśūdrayonis tu daṇḍaṃ dātum aśaknuvan |  
> ānṛṇyaṃ karmaṇā gacched vipro dadyāc chanaiḥ śanaiḥ ||  
> strībālonmattavṛddhānāṃ daridrāṇāṃ ca rogiṇām |  
> śiphāvidalarajjvādyair vidadhyān nṛpatir damam ||

**[803]** kātyāyanaḥ [970] |

> strīdhanaṃ dāpayed daṇḍaṃ dhārmikaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ |  
> nirdhanā prāptadoṣā strī tāḍanaṃ daṇḍam arhati ||

nāradaḥ [20.35–38] |

> brāhmaṇasya parīhāro rājñaś cāsanam agrataḥ |  
> prathamaṃ darśanaṃ prātaḥ sarvebhyaś cābhivādanam ||  
> agraṃ navebhyaḥ sasyebhyo mārgadānaṃ ca gacchataḥ |  
> bhaikṣyahetoḥ parāgāre praveśaś cānivāritaḥ ||  
> samitpuṣpakuśādhāneṣv asteyaṃ svaparigrahāt |  
> anākṣepaḥ parebhyaś ca saṃbhāṣas tu parastriyā ||  
> nadīṣv avetanas tāraḥ pūrvam uttāraṇaṃ tathā |  
> tareṣv aśulkadānaṃ ca na ced vāṇijyam asya tat ||

**[804]**

**atha brāhmaṇasy parīhāraḥ**

tatra śaṅkhalikhitau: “indhanodakāgnikāṣṭhatṛṇopalapuṣpamūlaphalaparṇādāneṣv agrāpacayam, daivatīrthābhigamanam, gṛhakoṣṭhapraveśanam, pathi śastradhāraṇam, asaṃbaddham āsanam, prastuteṣv anivāraṇam, asadvāsaś ceti, śiloñchapadayor dhānyarāśigrahaṇam, agrotsargaprasavavṛddhikarṣāpaṇaśulkanadītareṣv anuparodhanam, parastrīsaṃbhāṣaṇam, rājastrīdarśanam, rājñā samāsanam, vyatikramaṇaṃ ca kopāt sarvam arhati brāhmaṇaḥ” |

**atha nagaraparīhāraḥ**

tatra śaṅkhalikhitau: “na vaiṣṭikaṃ jāṅghikaṃ kṣetradravyāpaharaṇaṃ puṣpamūlapracayanaṃ svayamarjitapraveśanaṃ niṣkramaṇapraveśaneṣv anivedanaṃ skandhavāhyeṣu śulko gaṇasamayaśreṇipūgacaraṇavyavahāraniṣṭhā **[805]** svāminaḥ parijñātāro ‘nyatra rājābhidrohāt nagaranivāsināṃ vipretarāṇām api parigrahā anaparādhāḥ” |

bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 9.25] |

> sākṣilekhyānumānena samyag divyena vā jitaḥ |  
> yo na dadyād deyam arthaṃ sa nirvāsyas tataḥ purāt ||

[bṛh. prāya. 84]

> viṣodbandhanaśastreṇa yas tv ātmānaṃ pramāpayet |  
> mṛto ‘medhyena leptavyo nānyaṃ saṃskāram arhati ||

aṅgirāḥ |

> ātmānaṃ ghātayed yas tu rajjvādibhir upakramaiḥ |  
> mṛte ‘medhyena leptavyo jīvec ced dviguṇo damaḥ ||

**[806]** yājñavalkyaḥ [2.307] |

> rājñānyāyena yo daṇḍo gṛhīto varuṇāya tam |  
> nivedya dadyād viprebhyaḥ svayaṃ triṃśadguṇīkṛtam ||

kātyāyanaḥ [971–73] |

> anyāyopārjitaṃ nyastaṃ kośe kośaṃ niveśayet |  
> kāryārthe kāryanāśaḥ syād buddhimān nopapātayet ||  
> datvā dhanaṃ tad viprebhyaḥ sarvaṃ daṇḍasamutthitam |  
> putre rājyaṃ samāsajya kurvīta prāyaṇaṃ vane ||  
> evaṃ varet sadā yukto rājadharmeṣu pārthivaḥ |  
> hiteṣ caiva lokasya sarvān bhṛtyān niyojayet ||

**atha daṇḍasaṃjña**

tatra śaṅkhalikhitau: “caturviṃśatir ekanavatiḥ prathamasāhasaḥ, dviśataṃ pañcaśataṃ caiva madhyamasāhasaḥ, ṣaṭśataṃ sahasraṃ cottamaḥ | yathāsārāpakāraṃ sarveṣām ānupūrveṇa” |

nāradaḥ [21.30–31] |

> caturviṃśāvaraḥ pūrvaḥ paraḥ ṣaṇṇavatir bhavet |  
> śatāni pañca ca tu paro madhyamo dviśatāvaraḥ ||

**[807]**  
> sahasras tūttamo jñeyaḥ sa tu pañcaśatāvaraḥ |  
> trividhaḥ sāhaseṣv evaṃ daṇḍa uktaḥ svayaṃbhuvā ||

atra manuḥ [8.138] |

> paṇānāṃ dve śate sārdhe pathamaḥ sāhasaḥ smṛtaḥ |  
> madhyamaḥ pañca vijñeyaḥ sahasraṃ tv eva cottamaḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [1.366] |

> sāśītipaṇasāhasro daṇḍa uttamasāhasaḥ |  
> tadardhaṃ madhyamaḥ proktas tadardham adhamaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

**atha mānasaṃjñā**

tatra manuḥ [8.131–37] |

> lokasaṃvyavahārārthaṃ yāḥ saṃjñāḥ prathitā bhuvi |  
> tāmraraupyasuvarṇānāṃ tāḥ pravakṣyāmy aśeṣataḥ ||  
> jālāntaragate bhānau yat sūkṣmaṃ dṛśyate rajaḥ |  
> prathamaṃ tat pramāṇānāṃ trasareṇuṃ pracakṣate ||  
> trasareṇavo ‘ṣṭau vijñeyā likṣaikā ca pramāṇataḥ |  
> tā rājasarṣapas tisras te tu dve gaurasarṣapaḥ ||

**[808]**  
> sarṣapāḥ ṣaḍ yavo madhyaḥ triyavaṃ tv ekakṛṣṇalam |  
> pañcakṛṣṇalako māṣas te suvarṇaṃ tu ṣodaśa ||  
> palaṃ suvarṇāś catvāraḥ palāni dharaṇaṃ daśa |  
> dve kṛṣṇale samadhṛte vijñeyo raupyamāṣakaḥ ||  
> te ṣoḍaś syād dharaṇaṃ purāṇaś caiva rājataḥ |  
> kārṣāpaṇas tu vijñeyas tās tisraḥ kārṣikaḥ paṇaḥ ||  
> dharaṇāni daśa jñeyaḥ śatamānaṃ tu rājataḥ |  
> catuḥsuvarṇiko niṣko vijñeyas tu pramāṇataḥ ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [1.364] |

> plaṃ suvarṇāś catvāraḥ pañca vāpi prakīrtitam |

māṣādhikāre viṣṇuḥ [4.8–9]: “taddvādaśam akṣārdham | akṣārdham eva caturmāṣakaṃ suvarṇaḥ” | bṛhaspatiḥ [vya. 8.8, 10] |

> loke saṃvyavahārārthaṃ saṃjñeyaṃ kathitā bhuvi |  
> tāmrakarṣakṛtā mudrā vijñeyaḥ kārṣikaḥ paṇaḥ ||  
> sa eva candrikā proktā nāś catasras tu dhānakāḥ |  
> tā dvādaś suvarṇas tu dīnārākhyaḥ sa eva hi || \
**[809]** nāradaḥ [21.58–60] |

> māṣo viṃśatibhāgas tu jñeyaḥ kārṣāpaṇasya tu |  
> kākinī tu caturbhāgo māṣasya ca paṇasya ca ||  
> pañcanadyāḥ pradeśe tu saṃjñeyaṃ vyāvahārikī |  
> kārṣāpaṇpramāṇaṃ tu tannibaddham ihaiva vā ||  
> kārṣāpaṇo ‘bdhikā jñeyā tās catasras tu dhānakaḥ |  
> te dvādaśa suvarṇas tu dīnāraś citrakaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

tathā [21.57] |

> kārṣāpaṇo dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśi raupyaḥ pravartate |  
> paṇair nibaddhaḥ pūrvasyāṃ ṣoḍaśaiva paṇāḥ sa tu ||

kātyāyanaḥ [491–92] |

> māṣaḥ pādo dvipādo vā daṇḍo yatra prakalpitaḥ |  
> anirdiṣṭaṃ tu sauvarṇaṃ māṣakaṃ tatra kalpayet ||  
> yatrokto māṣako daṇḍo rājānaṃ tatra nirdiśet |  
> kṛṣṇalaiś coktam eva syād uktaṃ daṇḍaviniścaye ||

**[810]**

**atha naigamādisaṃjñā**

tatra kātyāyanaḥ [678–82] |

> nānāpaurasamūhas tu naigamas tu prakīrtitaḥ |  
> nānāyudhadharavrātāḥ samavetāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||  
> samūho vaṇigādīnāṃ pūgaḥ saṃparikīrtitaḥ |  
> brāhmaṇānāṃ samūhas tu gaṇa ity ucyate budhaiḥ ||  
> pravrajyāvasitā ye tu pāṣaṇḍāḥ parikīrtitāḥ |  
> śilpopajīvino ye tu śilpinaḥ parikīrtitāḥ ||  
> ārhatasaugatānāṃ tu samūhaḥ saṅga ucyate |  
> cāṇḍālaśvapacādīnāṃ samūho gulma saṃjñitaḥ ||  
> gaṇapāṣaṇḍapūgāś vrātāś ca śreṇayas tathā |  
> samūhasthāś ca ye cānye vargākhyās te bṛhaspatiḥ ||  
> cāturvarṇyasya yā sūtirasajātyādisaṃbhavā |  
> tasyā dharmāḥ samuddiṣṭā jātiḥ sā parikīrtitā ||

**iti śrīlakṣmīdharakṛte kṛtyakalpatarau**

**vyavahārakāṇḍe prakīrṇakam**

**[811]**

## 81 varṇānulomapratilomāḥ
atha varṇānulomapratilomāḥ

tatra āpastambaḥ [1.1.4–5]: “catvāro varṇā brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyaśūdrāḥ | teṣāṃ pūrvaḥ pūrvo janmataḥ śreyān” |

manuḥ [10.3–4] |

> vaiśeṣyāt prakṛtiśraiṣṭhyān niyamasya ca dhāraṇāt |  
> saṃskārasya viśeṣāc ca varṇānāṃ brāhmaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ||  
> brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyas trayo varṇā dvijātayaḥ |  
> caturtha ekajātis tu śūdro nāsti tu pañcamaḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ |

> viprakṣatriyavaiśyāś ca śūdrāś cāntyās trayo dvijāḥ |  
> pratilomānulomāś ca tair yutā varṇasaṃkarāḥ ||

devalaḥ: “catvāro varṇā brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyaśūdrā iti | anulomāś catvāraḥ savarṇāmbaṣṭhapāraśavogrā iti | pratilokāḥ ṣaḍ āyogavakṣattacaṇḍālamāgadhavaidehakasūtā **[812]** iti | antarālāḥ ṣaṭ kukkuṭapulkasavenakuśīlavabandiśvapākā iti | sarveṣāṃ lakṣaṇāni vidhānānupūrvaṃ vyākyāsyāmaḥ |

> brāhmaṇyāṃ brāhmaṇāj jātaḥ saṃskṛto brāhmaṇo bhavet |  
> evaṃ kṣatriyaviṭśūdrā jñeyās tebhyaḥ svayonijāḥ ||  
> brāhmaṇāt kṣatriyāyāṃ tu samutpannaḥ savarṇakaḥ |  
> vaiśyāyāṃ brāhmaṇāj jātaḥ putro ‘mbaṣṭha iti smṛtaḥ ||  
> viprān niṣādaḥ śūdrāyāṃ jātaḥ pāraśavo ‘pi saḥ |  
> vaiśyāyāṃ kṣatriyāj jātaḥ savarṇaḥ sa ca saṃjñayā ||  
> śūdrāyāṃ kṣatriyāj jātaṃ prāhur ugram iti dvijāḥ |  
> vaiśyāc chūdrasya kanyāyāṃ śūdra eva prajāyate ||”

manuḥ [10.6–10] |

> strīṣv anantarajātāsu dvijair utpāditān sutān |  
> sadṛśān eva tān āhur mātṛdoṣavigarhitān ||  
> anantarāsu jātāyāṃ vidhir eṣa sanātanaḥ |  
> dvyekāntarāsu jātānāṃ dharmyaṃ vidyād imaṃ vidhim ||

**[813]**  
> brāhmaṇād vaiśyakanyāyām ambaṣtho nāma jāyate |  
> niṣādaḥ śūdrakanyāyāṃ yaḥ pāraśava ucyate ||  
> kṣatriyāc chūdrakanyāyāṃ krūtācāravihāravān |  
> kṣatraśūdravapur jantur ugro nāma prajāyate ||  
> viprasya triṣu varṇeṣu nṛpater varṇayor dvayoḥ |  
> vaisyasya varṇe caikasmin ṣaḍ ete ‘pasadāḥ smṛtāḥ ||

tathā [10.14] |

> putrā ye ‘nantarastrījāḥ krameṇoktā dvijanmanām |  
> tān anantaranāmnas tu mātṛdoṣāt pracakṣate ||

yājñavalkyaḥ [1.90–95] |

> savarṇebhyaḥ savarṇāsu jāyante hi sajātayaḥ |  
> anindyeṣu vivāheṣu putrāḥ santānavardhanāḥ ||  
> viprān mūrdhāvasikto hi kṣatriyāyāṃ viśaḥ striyām |  
> jāyate ‘mbaṣṭhaḥ śūdrāyāṃ niṣādaḥ pāraśavo ‘pi vā ||  
> māhiṣyograu prajāyete viṭśūdrāṅganayor nṛpāt |  
> śūdrāyāṃ karaṇo vaiśyād dvijebhyaḥ kṣatriye tathā ||

**[814]** > ambaṣṭho brāhmaṇāc chūdryāṃ jātaḥ pāraśavo ‘pi vā |  
> vaiśyāśūdrayos tu rājanyān māhiṣyograu sutau smṛtau ||  
> vaiśyāt tu karaṇaḥ śūdryāṃ vinnāsv eṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ |

baudhāyanaḥ [1.17.4–6]: “kṣatriyā vaiśyāyāṃ kṣatriyaḥ | śūdrāyām ugraḥ | vaiśyāc chūdrāyāṃ rathakāraḥ” |

uśanā: “utkarṣāpakarṣā varṇā vijñāyante | rathakārāmbaṣṭhasutogramāgadhavenapukkasa-kṣattakukkuṭavaidehavaṇḍālaśvapākavrātyaprabhṛtayaḥ | tatra savarṇāyām eva savarṇaḥ | brāhmaṇāt kṣatriyāyāṃ jāto brāhmaṇa eva saḥ | vaiśyāyām ambaṣṭhaḥ | śūdrāyāṃ pāraśavaḥ | niṣāda ity eke | kṣatriyeṇa vaiśyāyāṃ kṣatriyaḥ, śūdrāyām ugraḥ, vaiśyena śūdrāyāṃ vaiśyaḥ” |

‘**brāhmaṇa va sa’** iti, kṣatriyapūrvanāt kṣatriyād utkṛṣṭo brāhmaṇavad ity arthaḥ |

śaṅkhalikhitau: “tatra brāhmaṇāt kṣatriyāyāṃ kṣatriya eva jāyate | kṣatriyeṇa vaiśyāyāṃ vaiśya eva | vaiśyena śūdrāyāṃ śūdraḥ | brāhmaṇena śūdrāyāṃ niṣādaḥ pāraśavo **[815]** vā jāyata ānulomyena vidhinā | viparyaye brāhmaṇyāṃ sūtaḥ kṣatriyeṇa | kṣatriyāyāṃ māgadho vaiśyena | vaiśyāyām āyogavaḥ śūdreṇa | śūdreṇa brāhmaṇyāṃ caṇḍālo jāyate | ambaṣṭhogrāv ekāntarānulomyena | kṣattṛvaidehakāv ekāntaraprātilomyena | yasmād varṇāḥ saṃkīryante tasmāt pratisaṃskāraḥ” |

gautamaḥ {4.16–21]: “anulomā anantaraikāntaradvyantarāsu jātāḥ savarṇāmbaṣṭhograniṣādadauṣyantapāraśavāḥ | pratilomāḥ sūtamāgadhāyogavakṣattṛvaidehakacaṇḍālāḥ | brāhmaṇy ajījanat putrān varṇebhya ānupūrvyād brāhmaṇasūtamāgadhacaṇḍālān | tebhya eva kṣattriyā mūrdhāvasiktakṣatriyadhīvarapulkasān | tebhya eva vaiśyā bhṛjyakaṇṭhamāhiṣyavaiśyavaidehakān | pāraśavayavanakaraṇaśūdrān śūdrety eke” |

nāradaḥ [14.103–04] |

> anantaraḥ smṛtaḥ putraḥ putra ekāntaras tathā |  
> dvyantaraś cānulomyena tathaiva pratilomataḥ ||  
> ugraḥ pāraśavaś caiva niṣādaś cānulomataḥ |  
> uttamebhyas trayas tribhyaḥ śūdrāputrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||  
> brāhmaṇyām api daṇḍālasūtavaidehakā api |  
> aparebhyas trayas tribhyo vijñeyā pratilomajāḥ ||

**[816]**  
> savarṇo māgadhaś caiva kṣattā ca kṣatriyāsutaḥ |  
> ānulomyena tatraiko dvau jñeyau pratilomajau ||  
> vaiśyāputrās tathāmbaṣṭhayavanāyogavā api |  
> prātilomyena tatraiko dvau jñeyāv anulomajau ||  
> savarṇo brāhmaṇīputraḥ kṣatriyāyām anantaraḥ |  
> ambaṣṭhograu tathā putrāv evaṃ kṣatriyavaiśyayoḥ ||  
> ekāntaras tu dauṣyanto vaiśyāyāṃ brāhmaṇāt sutaḥ |  
> śūdrāyāṃ kṣatriyāt tadvan niṣādo nāma jāyate ||  
> śūdrā pāraśavaṃ sūte brāhmaṇāḍ dvyantaraṃ sutam |  
> ānulomyena varṇānāṃ tathaiva pratilomataḥ ||  
> anantaraḥ smṛtaḥ sūto brāhmaṇyāṃ kṣatriyāt sutaḥ |  
> māgadhāyogavau tadvat sutau dvau vaiśyaśūdrayoḥ ||  
> brāhmaṇy ekāntaraṃ sūte vaiśyād vaidehakaṃ sutam |  
> kṣattāraṃ kṣatriyā śūdrāt putram ekāntaraṃ tathā ||  
> dvyantaraḥ prātilomyena pāpiṣṭhaḥ saṃkare sati |  
> caṇḍālo jāyate śūdrād brāhmaṇī yatra muhyati ||

**[817]** devalaḥ |

> śūdrād āyogakṣattṛvaṇḍālāḥ pratilomajāḥ |  
> vaiśyāyāṃ kṣatriyāyāṃ ca brāhmaṇyāṃ ca yathākramam ||  
> tathaiva māgadho vaiśyāj jāto vaidehako ‘pi ca |  
> brāhmaṇyāṃ kṣatriyāj jātaḥ sūto jātyā svakarmaṇā ||

viṣṇuḥ [16.3–6]: “pratilomāś cāryavigarhitāḥ | tatra vaiśyāputraḥ śūdreṇāyogavaḥ | pulkasamāgadhau kṣatriyāputrau śūdravaiśyābhyām | caṇḍālavaidehakasūtāś ca brāhmaṇīputrāḥ śūdraviṭkṣatriyaiḥ” |

vasiṣṭhaḥ [18.1–6]: “śūdreṇa brāhmaṇyām utpannaś caṇḍālo bhavatīty āhuḥ | rājanyāyāṃ vaiṇaḥ | vaiśyāyām antyāvasāyī | vaiśyena brāhmaṇyām utpanno rāmako bhavatīty āhuḥ | rājanyāyāṃ pulkasaḥ | rājanyena brāhmaṇyām utpannaḥ sūto bhavatīty āhuḥ” |

yamaḥ |

> sarvāś caṇḍālayonayas tu cāturvarṇyād viniḥsṛtāḥ |  
> sūtamāgadhacaṇḍālaśvapacā ugrapulkasāḥ ||  
> ekayonaya evādyās trayas teṣām anantarāḥ |  
> dvāv ekayonijāv eva eka evottaraḥ smṛtaḥ ||

**[818]** > kṣatriyāj jāyate sūto vaiśyāj jāyeta māgadhaḥ |  
> śūdrāj jāyeta caṇḍālo brāhmaṇī yatra muhyati ||  
> kṣatriyāyāṃ tu vaiśyena śvapaco nāma jāyate |  
> śūdreṇa jāyate cograḥ kṣatriyā yatr muhyati ||  
> vaiśyāyām eva śūdreṇa pulkaso nāma jāyate |  
> bījayoniviśiṣṭās te varṇebhyas tv adhamottamāḥ ||

hārītaḥ: “viparītā brāhmaṇyāṃ kṣatriyavaiśyaśūdrāḥ sūtamāgadhamātaṅgān janayanti | kṣatriyāyāṃ vaiśyaśūdrau vandiniṣādau janayataḥ | vaiśyāyāṃ śūdraḥ pulkasaṃ janayati” |

paiṭīnasiḥ: “sūtamāgadhacaṇḍālāś ceti brāhmaṇyāṃ mohād adhovarṇebhyaḥ | ambaṣṭhaś cāyogavaś ceti kṣatriyāyām | vaiśyāyāṃ māgadhaś ceti | pulkaso vaiṇo rathakāraḥ śvapākaḥ kaivarto niṣādaś ceti varṇasaṃkarā jāyante” |

baudhāyanaḥ [1.16.6–15]: “śūdrād vaiśyāyāṃ māgadhaḥ kṣatriyāyāṃ kṣattā brāhmaṇyām caṇḍālaḥ | vaiśyāt kṣatriyāyām āyogavo brāhmaṇyāṃ vaidehakaḥ | kṣatriyād brāhmaṇyām sūtaḥ | tatrāmbaṣṭhograsaṃyoge bhavaty anulomaḥ | kṣattṛvaidehayoḥ pratilomaḥ | ugrāj jātaḥ **[819]** kṣattāyāṃ śvapākaḥ | vaidehakād ambaṣṭhāyāṃ vaiṇaḥ | niṣādāc chrūdrāyāṃ pulkasaḥ | śūdrān niṣādyāṃ kukkuṭaḥ | varṇasaṃkarād utpannāt vrātyān āhur manīṣiṇa iti” |

paiṭhīnasiḥ: “pratilomād avyabhicāre sūtamāgadhāyogavā jāyante | śūdreṇottamāsu śvapākacaṇḍālaniṣādā jāyante | brāhmaṇena kṛṣṇāyāṃ pāraśavaḥ | pāraśavyāṃ kṣattā | kṣatriyeṇa kṣṣṇāyāṃ vandī | vaiśyena vaitālaḥ | pāraśavena kṣatriyāyām ambaṣtho vaiśyāyāṃ dundalādo ‘mbaṣṭhaś ceti | videhāyāṃ venaḥ | vaidehakavandiniṣādāmbaṣṭhāsu brāhmaṇena cūcukamudgupaulkasakukkuṭakā jāyante | vaiśyāyām āyogavaḥ | kṣatriyeṇa kṣattāpulkasavenogreṣu dūtapreṣyakaivartārā jāyante | ugreṇādyāsu mauñjiṣṭhasautapāṇivikalā jāyante | ugrāyāṃ tv ādyaiḥ pauṣṭikaḍombabhiñjaśiṇḍikā jāyante” |

śaṅkhalikhitau: “kṣatryām ugrasaṃge śvapākaḥ | vaidehakāyām ambaṣṭhasaṃyoge venaḥ | śūdrāyāṃ niṣādena pulkasaḥ māgadhena kukkuṭakaḥ” |

**[820]** baudhāyanaḥ [1.13.9]: “ambaṣṭhāt prathamāyāṃ śvapākaḥ | ugrād dvitīyāyāṃ venaḥ | niṣādāt tṛtīyāyāṃ pulkasaḥ | viparyaye kukkuṭakaḥ” |

devalaḥ |

> ugrān niṣādyām utpannas tanayaḥ kukkuṭo bhavet |  
> tato niṣādāc chūdrāyāṃ jāto bhavati pulkasaḥ ||  
> vaidehakena tv ambaṣṭhyāṃ jāto vena iti smṛtaḥ |  
> vaidehakāyām ambaṣṭhād bhavej jātaḥ kuśīlavaḥ ||  
> kṣatryāṃ tathograjaḥ putraḥ śvapāka iti kīrtyate |  
> antarālā bhavanty evam ete cānye ca miśrajāḥ ||

manu-viṣṇū [ma. 10.15, 18–19, 25–40; vi. 16–17] |

> brāhmaṇād ugrakanyāyāṃ āvṛto nāma jāyate |  
> ābhīro ‘mbaṣṭhakanyāyām āyogavyāṃ tu dhigvaṇaḥ ||  
> jāto niṣādāc chūdrāyāṃ jātyā bhavati pulkasaḥ |  
> śūdrāj jāto niṣādyāṃ tu sa vai kukkuṭakaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
> kṣattur jātas tathogrāyāṃ śvapāka iti kīrtyate |  
> vaidehakena tv ambaṣṭhyām utpanno vena ucyate ||  
> saṃkīrṇayonayo ye tu pratilomānulomajāḥ |  
> anyonyavyatiṣaktāś ca tān pravakṣyāmy aśeṣataḥ ||

**[821]**  
> sūto vaidehakaś caiva caṇḍālaś cādhamo nṛṇām |  
> māgadhaḥ kṣatrajātiś ca tathāyogava eva ca ||  
> ete ṣaṭ sadṛśān varṇāñ janayanti svayoniṣu |  
> mātṛjātyāṃ prasūyante pravarāsu ca yoniṣu ||  
> tathā trayāṇāṃ varṇānāṃ dvayor ātmāsya jāyate |  
> ānantaryāt svayonyāṃ ca tathā bāhyeṣv api kramaḥ ||  
> te cāpi bāhyān subahūṃs tato ‘py adhikadūṣitān |  
> parasparasya dāreṣu janayanti vigarhitān ||  
> yathaiva śūdro brāhmaṇyāṃ bāhyaṃ jantuṃ prasūyate |  
> tathā bāhyataraṃ bāhyaś cāturvarṇye prasūyate ||  
> pratikūlaṃ vartamānā bāhyā bāhyatarān punaḥ |  
> hīnā hīnān prasūyante varṇān pañcadaśaiva tu ||  
> prasādhanopacārajñam adāsaṃ dāsyajīvanam |  
> sairindhraṃ vāgurāvṛttiṃ sūte dasyur ayogave ||  
> maitreyakaṃ tu vaideho mādhūkaṃ saṃprasūyate |  
> nṝn praśaṃsaty ajasraṃ yo ghaṇṭātāḍo ‘ruṇodaye ||

**[822]**  
> niṣādo mārgavaṃ sūte dāsaṃ naukarmajīvinam |  
> kaivartam iti yaṃ prāhur āryāvartanivāsinaḥ ||  
> mṛtavastrabhṛtsv anāryāsu garhitānnāśanāsu ca |  
> bhavanty āyogavīṣv ete jātihīnāḥ pṛthak trayaḥ ||  
> kārāvaro niṣādāt tu carmakāraḥ prasūyate |  
> vaidehakād andhramedau bahirgrāmapratiśayau ||  
> caṇḍālāt pāṇḍusopākas tvaksāravyavahāravān |  
> āhiṇḍiko niṣādena vaidehyām eva jāyate ||  
> caṇḍālena tu sopāko mūlavyasanavṛttimān |  
> pulkasyāṃ jāyate pāpaḥ sadā sajjanagarhitaḥ ||  
> niṣādastrī tu caṇḍālāt putram antyāvasāyinam |  
> śmaśānagocaraṃ sute bāhyānām api garhitam ||  
> saṃkare jātayas tv etāḥ pitṛmātṛpradarśitāḥ |  
> pracchannā vā prakāśā vā veditavyāḥ svakarmabhiḥ ||

nāradaḥ [14.105] |

> sūtādyāḥ pratilomās tu ye jātāḥ pratilomataḥ |  
> sasaṃskārāś ca pākādyās teṣāṃ triḥsaptako gaṇaḥ ||

**[823]** śaṅkhalikhitau: [kṣatriyavaiśyānulomāntarotpanno yo rathakāras tasyejyādānopanayanasaṃskārakriyā aśvapratiṣṭhārathasūtravāstuvidyādhyayanavṛttitā ca] |

vasiṣṭhaḥ: “kṣatriyavaiśyānulomāntarajāto rathakāra ity eke | tasyādhyayanejyādhānopanayanasaṃskārāś cāpratiṣiddhāḥ | rathasūtravāstuvidyādhyayanakarmavṛttiś ceti” |

yājñavalkyaḥ [1.95] |

> māhiṣyeṇa karaṇyāṃ tu rathakāraḥ prajāyate |

yamaḥ |

> maryādāyā vilopena jāyate varṇasaṃkaraḥ |  
> bhraṣṭavaṃśās tu patitā bhraṣṭācārā bhavanti te ||

punar yamaḥ |

> prātilomyānulomyena guṇadoṣān nibodhata |  
> ānulomyena varṇatvaṃ prātilomyena pātakam ||

manuḥ [10.66–72] |

> anāryāyāṃ samutpanno brāhmaṇāt tu yadṛcchayā |  
> brāhmaṇyām apy anāryāt tu śreyastvaṃ kveti ced bhavet ||

**[824]**  
> jāto nāryām anāryāyām āryād āryo bhaved guṇaiḥ |  
> jāto ‘py anāryād āryāyām anārya iti niścayaḥ ||  
> ubhāv api tv asaṃskāryāv iti dharmo vyavasthitaḥ |  
> vaiguṇyāj janmataḥ pūrva uttaraḥ pratilomataḥ ||  
> subījaṃ tv eva sukṣetre jātaṃ saṃpadyate yathā |  
> tathāryāj jāt āryāyāṃ sarvaṃ saṃskāram arhati ||  
> bījam eke praśaṃsanti kṣetram eke manīṣiṇaḥ |  
> bījakṣetre tathaivānye tatreyaṃ tu vyavasthitiḥ ||  
> akṣetre bījam utsṛṣṭam antaraiva vinaśyati |  
> ajījakam api kṣetraṃ kevalaṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ bhavet ||  
> yasmād bījaprabhāveṇa tiryagjā ṛṣayo ‘bhavan |   
> pūjitāś ca praśastāś ca tasmād bījaṃ viśiṣyate ||

tathā [10.41–42] |

> svajātijānantarajāḥ ṣaṛsutā dvijadharmiṇaḥ |  
> śūdrāṇāṃ tu sadharmāṇaḥ sarve ‘padhvaṃsajāḥ smṛtāḥ ||  
> tapobījaprabhāvaiś ca te gacchanti yuge yuge |  
> utkarṣaṃ cāpakarṣaṃ ca manuṣyeṣv iha janmataḥ ||

**[825]** tathā [10.64–65] |

> śūdrāyāṃ brāhmaṇāj jātaḥ śreyasā cet prajāyate |  
> aśreyān śreyasīṃ jātiṃ gacchaty āsaptamād yugāt ||  
> śūdro brāhmaṇyam abhyeti brāhmaṇaś caiva śūdratām |  
> kṣatriyāj jātam evaṃ tu vidyād vaiśyāt tathaiva ca ||

baudhāyanaḥ [1.16.13–14]: “niṣādena niṣādyām ā pañcamāj jāto ‘pahanti śūdratām | tam upanayet ṣaṣṭhaṃ yājayet saptamo ‘vikṛto [bhavati] | jīvasaṃjīvakara ity eṣāṃ sajñāḥ krameṇa nipatanti” |

yājñavalkyaḥ [1.96] |

> jātyutkarṣo yuge jñeyaḥ pañcame saptame ‘pi vā |  
> vyatyaye karmaṇāṃ sāmyaṃ pūrvavac cādharottaram ||

**[826]** āpastambaḥ [2.11.10–11]: “dharmacaryayā jaghanyo varṇaḥ pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ varṇam āpadyate jātiparivṛttau | adharmacaryayā pūrvo varṇo jaghanyaṃ varṇam āpadyate varṇam āpadyate jātiparivṛttau” |

manuḥ [10.73] |

> anāryam āryakarmāṇam āryaṃ cānāryakarmiṇam |  
> saṃpradhāryābravīd dhātā na samau nāsamāv iti ||

tathā [10.20–23] |

> dvijātayaḥ savarṇāsu janayanty avratāṃs tu yān |  
> tān sāvitrīparibhraṣṭān vrātyān iti vinirdiśet ||  
> vrātyāt tu jāyate viprāt pāpātmā bhṛjjakaṇṭakaḥ |  
> āvantyavāṭadhānau ca puṣpadhaḥ śaikha eva ca ||  
> jhallo mallaś ca rājanyād vrātyāl licchavir eva ca |  
> naṭaś ca karaṇaś caiva khaso draviṣa eva ca ||  
> vaiśyāt tu jāyate vrātyāt sudhanvācārya eva ca |  
> kāruṣaś ca vijanmā ca maitraḥ sātvata eva ca ||

**[827]** devalaḥ |

> vratahīnā asaṃskārāḥ savarṇāsv api ye punaḥ |  
> utpāditā bhaveyus te vrātyā iva bahiṣkṛtāḥ ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: “triṣu varṇeṣv asaṃskṛtaprasūtaḥ syāt kālābhijñātaḥ patitasāvitrīko brāhmaṇaḥ” |

yamaḥ |

> yas tu pravrajitāj jātaḥ pravrajyāvasitaś ca yaḥ |  
> tāv ubhau brahmacaṇḍālāv āha vaivasvato yamaḥ ||  
> ārūḍhapaitāj jāto hy ārūḍhapatitaś ca yaḥ |  
> dvāv etau brahmacaṇḍālau manuḥ svāyambhuvo ‘bravīt ||  
> yas tu pravratijāputro brāhmaṇyāṃ caiva śūdrajaḥ |  
> dvāv etau brahmacaṇḍālau manuḥ svāyambhuvo ‘bravīt ||

aṅgirāḥ |

> yas tu pravrajitāputro brāhmaṇyāṃ yaś ca śūdrajaḥ |  
> tāv ubhau viddhi caṇḍālau sagotrādyaś ca jāyate ||

**[828]** manuḥ [10.43–44] |

> śanakais tu kriyālokād imāḥ kṣatriyajātayaḥ |  
> vṛṣalatvaṃ gatā loke brāhmaṇādarśanena ca ||  
> pauṇḍrakāś cauḍhradraviḍā kāmbojā yavanāḥ śakāḥ |  
> pāradāḥ pallavāś cīnāḥ kirātā daradāḥ khaśāḥ ||

tathā [10.57–61] |

> varṇāpetam avijñātaṃ naraṃ kaluṣayonijam |  
> āryarūpam ivānāryaṃ karmabhiḥ svair vibhāvayet ||  
> anāryatā niṣṭhuratā krūratā niṣkriyātmatā |  
> puruṣaṃ vyañjayantīha loke kaluṣayonijam ||  
> pitur vā bhajate śīlaṃ mātur vobhayam eva vā |  
> na kathaṃcana kuryoniḥ prakṛtiṃ svāṃ niyacchati ||  
> kule mukhye ‘pi jātasya yasya syād yonisaṃkaraḥ |  
> saṃśrayaty eva tacchīlaṃ naro ‘lpam api vā bahu ||  
> yatra tv ete paridhvaṃsāj jāyante varṇadūṣakāḥ |  
> rāṣṭrīyaiḥ saha tad rāṣṭraṃ kṣipram eva vinaśyati ||

nāradaḥ [14.113] |

> rakṣāpramādān nṛpater jāyate varṇasaṃkaraḥ |  
> tasmād rājñā viśeṣeṇa striyo rakṣyās tu saṃkarāt ||

**[829]** śaṅkhalikhitau: “evaṃ varṇe bhedaḥ | pramādād daurbalyāc ca rājñas tu kilbiṣaṃ kartur yad dāpayet teṣāṃ pratiniyatāni karmāṇi rājñā pratipādanīyāni” |

**atha teṣāṃ karmāṇi**

tatra manuḥ [10.46–50] |

> ye dvijānām apasadā ye cāpadhvaṃsajāḥ smṛtāḥ |  
> te ninditair vartayeyur dvijānām eva karmabhiḥ||  
> sūtānām aśvasārathyam ambaṣṭhānāṃ cikitsitam |  
> vaidehakānāṃ strīkāryaṃ māgadhānāṃ vaṇikpathaḥ ||  
> matsyaghāto niṣādānāṃ tvaṣṭir āyogavasya ca |  
> medāndhracuñcumadgūnām āraṇyapaśuhiṃsanam ||  
> kṣatrugrapulkasānāṃ tu bilaukovadhabandhanam |  
> dhigvaṇānāṃ carmakāryaṃ veṇānāṃ bhāṇḍavādanam ||  
> caityadrumaśmaśāneṣu śailūṣopavaneṣu ca |  
> vaseyur ete vijñātā vartayantaḥ svakarmabhiḥ ||

**[830]** ‘**apadhvaṃsajāḥ’** pratilomajāḥ | ‘**ninditaiḥ’** dvijānām āpadvihitair vāṇijyādibhiḥ | ‘dvijānām upayogibhiḥ preṣyakarmabhir’ iti medhātithiḥ [on MDh 10.46]|

śaṅkhalikhitau: “sūtānām annasaṃskārakriyā keśaśmaśrunakhalomavāpanasnapanavilepāny alaṃkaraṇam aśvadamanayogyāsanaprekṣaṇāni karmāṇi | kṣattuḥ pratīhāradautye | māgadhānāṃ mṛdaṅgaveṇuvīṇāvādanavṛtyagītapuṣpamāṇavakakarmasiddhikopasthānagāthāślokapratyūṣa-pratibodhanāni karmāṇi | ambaṣṭhānāṃ jātiviśeṣāt kāyaśalyaśalākārasāyanaviṣonmādaklība-jvarāpasmārakumāracikitsāśarīrapoṣaṇādikarmāṇi | vaidehakānāṃ patracchedanasīvana-rañjanāvanirṇejanavāpītaṭākodyānārāmāvaskaraśodhanāni karmāṇi | ugrāṇāṃ kuñjaragrahaṇa-rājacchatradhāraṇapurataḥpradhāvanabandhanāgārasaṃyamanāni karmāṇi | veṇānāṃ laṅganavanakṛīḍāniyuddhamāyāśāstraindrajālaprasthāpanapraharaṇāni karmāṇi | kukkuṭānāṃ praharaṇakaraṇacakratomarabhiṇḍipālapāśāsiparaśvathalaguḍalohajālikāsamarasaṃdhāraṇādīni karmāṇi | āyogavānām avaskaraṇakumbhakaraṇasuvarṇarajatamaṇilohādiśilpakaraṇāni carmavṛttitā ceti | pulkasānāṃ nagaravīthīrakṣaṇajāgaraṇānāthamṛtanirharaṇālekhyapatra-cchedamālikatvam iti karmāṇi | niṣādānāṃ vāgurāpāśasaṃdhāraṇamṛgapaśupakṣimatsyadāraṇa-madhupātanavikartanādīni karmāṇi |

**[831]** ‘puṣpamāṇavakakarmasiddhikopasthānam’ puṣpamāṇavakatvena jyotiḥśāstravittvena karmasiddhyupadeśārthaṃ rājasamīpopasthānam iti śabarasvāmī |

viṣṇuḥ [16.7–13]: “raṅgāvataraṇam āyogavānām | vyādhatā pulkasānām | stutikriyā māgadhānām | vadhyaghātitvaṃ caṇḍālānām | strīrakṣātajjīvanaṃ ca vaidehakānām | aśvasārathyaṃ sūtānām” |

hārītaḥ: “teṣāṃ vṛttīr vakṣyāmaḥ aśvarathasūtatvaṃ sūtāya | mṛdaṅgavādopajīvanaṃ māgadhāya | śmaśānamṛtaparicchadopajīvanaṃ caṇḍālāya | naṭayitaryanuvāditvaṃ vandine | potavāhopajīvanaṃ niṣādāya | tūryavādavīthīraṅgavāstuprakṣālanaṃ pulakasāya” |

yamaḥ |

> sūtānām aśvasārathyaṃ māgadhānāṃ cikitsitam |  
> caṇḍālānāṃ vadhyaghātaś cuñcupānāṃ ca vetanam ||  
> āghoṣaṇaṃ ca madgūnāṃ pulkasānāṃ ca saṃtaram |

**[832]** manuḥ [10.51–52, 50, 53–56] |

> caṇḍālaśvacapānāṃ tu bahirgrāmāt pratiśrayaḥ |  
> apapātrāś ca kartavyā dhanam eṣāṃ śvagardabham ||  
> vāsāṃsi mṛtacailāni bhinnabhāṇḍeṣu bhojanam |  
> kārṣṇāyasam alaṅkāraḥ parivrajyā ca nityaśaḥ ||  
> caityadrumaśmaśāneṣu vaneṣūpavaneṣu ca |  
> vaseyur ete vijñātā vartayantaḥ svakarmabhiḥ ||  
> na taiḥ samayam anvicchet puruṣo dharmam ācaran |  
> vyavahāro mithas teṣāṃ vivāhaḥ sadṛśaiḥ saha ||  
> annam eṣāṃ parādhīnaṃ deyaṃ syād bhinnabhājane |  
> rātrau na vicareyus te grāmeṣu nagareṣu ca ||  
> divā careyuḥ kāryārthaṃ cihnitā rājaśāsanaiḥ |  
> abāndhavaṃ śavaṃ caiva nirhareyur iti sthitḥ ||  
> vadhyāṃś ca hanyuḥ satataṃ yathāśāstraṃ mṛpājñayā |  
> vadhyavāsāṃsi gṛhṇīyuḥ śayyādyābharaṇāni ca ||

yamaḥ |

> kārṣṇāyasam alaṃkāras tatpātreṣu ca bhojanam |  
> bahirgrāmanivāsaś ca dhanam eṣāṃ ca gardabhaḥ ||

**[833]** śaṅkhalikhitau: “caṇḍālānām ekāntavāsaḥ śmaśānasaṃrakṣaṇaṃ śvakulaparidhāvanaṃ vadhyaghātitvam iti karmāṇi | śvapacānāṃ caivam | dasyumlecchagaṇānāṃ ca kṛtaśastropajīvanam iti karmāṇi | nāryaḥ sajātīyāḥ sarveṣāṃ śreyasyaḥ syur iti” |

viṣṇuḥ [16.14–16]: “caṇḍālānāṃ bahirgrāmanivasanaṃ mṛtacailadhāraṇam iti viśeṣaḥ | samānajātibhir vāsaḥ sarveṣām | svapitṛvittānuharaṇaṃ ca” |

devalaḥ |

> tatra jātyantarālānāṃ pratilomānulomayoḥ |  
> sve sve ca yonisaṃbandhāṃs tān saṃpādayet pṛthak ||  
> tathaiva caturo varṇān sve sve dharme niyojayet |  
> rājño bhūtir yaśas tuṣṭir dharmaś ca parivardhate ||

manuḥ [10.62–63] |

> brāhmaṇārthe gavārthe ca dehatyāgo ‘nupaskṛtaḥ |  
> strībālābhyupapattau ca bāhyānāṃ siddhikāraṇam ||

**[834]**  
> ahiṃsā satyam asteyaṃ śaucam indriyanigrahaḥ |  
> etaṃ sāmāsikaṃ dharmaṃ caturvarṇye ‘bravīn manu ||

devalaḥ: “svajātijīvanaṃ sarvapramāṇatitikṣā vyavahāraparapramāṇaṃ svabhṛtyapoṣaṇam akarmaparivarjanam ityā (?) caṇḍāladharmaḥ” |

iti vyavahārakāṇḍe varṇānulomapratilomalakṣaṇavṛttidharmāḥ ||

**iti mahārājādhirājaśrīmadgovindcandradevamahāsāndhivigrahika-**

**bhaṭṭahṛdayadharātmajabhaṭṭaśrīlakṣmīdhareṇa viracite **

**kṛtyakalpatarau vyavahārakāṇḍaṃ samāptam ||**
